MAT 18:8 Amana yukani koku dyaku holo kulu dyaku dyakusumunaka, bukunadya amana losadya ku kyana yi ngeyi; bulungi kwena ngeyi wakota mu luzingu yi koku dimosi holo kulu dimosi, ka mboti ku ni wakala yi malu modi holo moku modi amana bakulosa ku mbawu ya mvula yi mvula.
MAT 18:9 Amana yuka ni disu dyaku dyakusumunaka, lokuladya amana losadya ku kyana yi ngeyi; bulungi kwena ngeyi wakota mu luzingu lwakonda tsuka yi disu dimosi, ka mboti ku ni wakala kwaku yi mesu modi amana bakulosa ku bilungi.»
MAT 18:10 «Talenu, lulewulaku mosi wa bana bakhunda baba; mukuma yiluzimbwadi ni banzyo ba bawu muna mazilu bisi tala kosu tangwa mbunzu ya Tata wama wuna wenina mu mazilu.
MAT 18:11 [Mukuma Mwana wa mutu kisa hulula bana bátota.]
MAT 18:12 «Abweti lwisi banza? Yukani mutu mosi kavwa mikoku khama, amana mosi muna kati dya myawu katota, kasísaku makumi vwa yi vwa muna mongu ndangu kenda sanda wuna wátota?
MAT 18:13 Amana yuka ni kasengumunawa, mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi, kasángwala kikuma kya wawu kuluta makumi vwa yi vwa ma mina myakonda tota.
MAT 18:14 Phila mosi, lweku luzolu lwa Tata wenu wuna wenina muna mazilu, ni mosi mu kati dya baleki baba katota.»
MAT 18:15 «Yukani phangi waku kasumuka [kwena ngeyi], ndawenda, mumona, kalenu benu boodi lwesi. Yukani kakuyukila, wumunungini phangi waku.
MAT 18:16 Kaasi yukani kayukiku, bonga hika mutu mosi kondilo boodi ha kimosi yi ngeyi, ndangu mu ndinga ya bambangi boodi kondilo batatu dyambu dyosu dyayilama."
MAT 18:17 Kaasi yukani kabwisa kubayukila, zimbula ku Dibundu; amana yuka ni kabwisa phi kuyukila Dibundu, kakala kikuma kya ngeyi hanga muphakanu yi kalaki ka phaku.
MAT 18:18 «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi, moosu mana lwakása ha tsi makásama ku zilu, amana moosu mana lwakútumuna ha tsi makútumuka ku zilu.
MAT 18:19 «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi hika ni yuka boodi ha kati dya benu bayukana, ha tsi haha, mu kulomba kyosu kima, kyakina kabáheka Tata wama wenina mu mazilu.
MAT 18:20 Mukuma hana henina bodi holo batatu bakhundakana mu khumbu yama, meni yenina hana kati dya bawu.»
MAT 18:21 Hanga buna kábwesuka Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Pfumu, mbala kwa pfwani kulolula kwena phangi wama yandu wuphangi mbi, amana yimúlolula tii yi kuna mbala tsambwadi?»
MAT 18:22 Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Yikuzimbwadiku ni yi kuna mbala tsambwadi, kaasi yi kuna mbala makumi tsambwadi yi tsambwadi.
MAT 18:23 Ihana ni, Kipfumu kya mazilu kifwanakani yi kyamvu mosi wázola kutala mambu ma pfuka zandi kwena basadi bandi.
MAT 18:24 Amana buna káyandika mu kusalabwa, bisa munatina mosi wáfwana kufuta mafunda yi mafunda ma mbongu.
MAT 18:25 Bwosu kakalaku yi kima kya kufuta, pfumu wandi wáhana muswa ndangu bamutekisa yandi yi mukhetu wandi yi bana bandi yi bima byosu bina kákala byawu, ndangu bafuta pfuka yandi.
MAT 18:26 Musadi wábwa muna malu mandi amana wáfukama kuna thwala yandi mu kuzonza: "Sipha mbundu pfumu, kikuma kya meni, yikufuta pfuka yosu!"
MAT 18:27 Kiwayi kyámukwata pfumu wa musadi wuna, wámusula kenda amana wámuyambwadilaya pfuka.
MAT 18:28 Mu kulubuka, musadi wuna bátundakana yi mosi wa banduku ba kisalu wuna wafwana kumufuta mbongu za khunda. Musadi wámukwata, amana wáyandika mu kumukama hana dinga mu kuzimbula: "Futa pfuka yama!"
MAT 18:29 Hanga nduku wa kisalu wubwi muna malu mandi, kakala mubokwadila: "Sipha mbundu kikuma kya meni, yikufuta!"
MAT 18:30 Kaasi yandi kázolaku; wenda mutimbula mu boloku, yi kuna kafútila pfuka yina.
MAT 18:31 Mu kumona mana mabwa, banduku bandi ba kisalu kyadi kyábakwata lawu; hanga bendi menika kwena pfumu wa bawu mosu mana máluta.
MAT 18:32 Hanga pfumu wumutedisi amana wumuzimbwadi: "Musadi wa mbi! Yikuyambwadidiki pfuka yaku kikuma wumbokwadidiki;
MAT 18:33 wulungikiku, ngeyi phi kuyukila nduku waku wa kisalu kiwayi, bwosu yikuyukidiki phi ngeyi kiwayi?"
MAT 18:34 Amana pfumu wandi, mu khabu, wámulambula mu boloku tii yi kuna kafútila byosu bina káfwana mu kufuta.»
MAT 18:35 «Yi bwabuna phi Tata wama wenina ku zilu kalúhanga yukani mosi-mosi wa benu kaloludiku kwena phangi wandi yi mbundu yandi yosu.»
MAT 19:1 Tangwa kámanisa Yesu ndinga zazi, wákatuka ku Ngadidi amana wenda ku milambu mya Yuteya, kuna sambwa dikwawu dya Yolutani.
MAT 19:2 Milumba-lumba mya batu lawu bámulanda, amana kwakuna, wábuka bambefu.
MAT 19:3 Amana ndambu ya Bafwadisi bábwesuka kwena yandi, mu kumuleya yi kumuhyula: «Yakala kenina yi muswa wa kuyambula mukhetu wandi mu kosu kikuma?»
MAT 19:4 Amana yandi mu kuvutula, wuzimbudi: «Lwátangaku ni, "ku luyanduku, kábahanga mukhetu yi yakala",
MAT 19:5 amana kázimbula: "Ihana ni, yakala kasísa tata wandi yi ngudi wandi, amana kakhúndakana yi mukhetu wandi, amana bakítuka, bawu bodi, musuni wumosi".
MAT 19:6 Ndangu bakálaku hika bodi, kaasi mutu mosi. Disongidila, kina kakasi Nzambi, mutu kahambulaku.»
MAT 19:7 Bafwadisi bamuzimbwadini: «Kikuma kya biki Moyize káhanina muswa ni bahana, kwena mukhetu, mukanda wa kufwa kwa longu amana bamukula?»
MAT 19:8 Yandi wubazimbwadi: «Moyize, kikuma kya mbundu ya tadi yina lwenina yawu, káluhekila muswa wa kukula bakhetu benu; ku luyandiku, bwákalaku buna.
MAT 19:9 Kaasi, yiluzimbwadibwa: wuna wayámbula mukhetu wandi, katula kusala kindumba, amana kakwela wa hika, mbongi katini.»
MAT 19:10 Balonguki bandi bámuzimbwala: «Yuka ni yi bwana dyenina dyambu dya yakala yi mukhetu, bulungi kakwelaku kwandi.»
MAT 19:11 Amana yandi wábazimbwala: «Boosu bafwaniyoku kutambwasa ndinga yayi, kaasi kwena bawu bana lwesi bahekaya!
MAT 19:12 Mukuma henina yi bayakala bafwaniku kukwela kikuma bwabuna bábutuka, henina yi bakwawu bátyelabwa kwena batu, amana henina yi bakwawu bábwisa kukwela, kikuma kya Kipfumu kya mazilu. Wuna wufwani kutambwasa, katambwasa!»
MAT 19:13 Hanga bamunatini bana, ndangu kabathetika moku amana kalombila kikuma kya bawu, kaasi balonguki bakala bakaya.
MAT 19:14 Amana Yesu wázimbula: «Yambulenu bana, lubakandisaku mu kukwisa kwena meni, mukuma Kipfumu kya mazilu kyenina kikuma kya bana benina hanga bawu.»
MAT 19:15 Amana wábathetika moku, wákatuka hana.
MAT 19:16 Hanga mutu mosi wisa bwesuka kwena yandi, wuzimbudi: «Mulongi, biki bya bukheti pfwani kuhanga mu kutambula luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula?»
MAT 19:17 Amana yandi wumuzimbwadi: «Kikuma kya biki wungyufwadi mu mambu ma bukheti? Mosi lwesi wenina wa bukheti. Amana yuka ni wazola kukota mu luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula, lunda mitsiku.»
MAT 19:18 Wumuhyudi: «Khi myawu?» Amana Yesu wuzimbudi: «Wahóndaku mvumbi wa khengu; watáku mbongi; wayíbaku; wahúnaku musamu;
MAT 19:19 zitisa tata waku yi ngudi waku; amana wazóla mukwenu khunda hanga ngeyi meni.»
MAT 19:20 Ngunza wumuzimbwadi: «Mambu mana moosu, yisima zitisa, biki hika bikhondi?»
MAT 19:21 Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Yukani wuzodi wakala walungila, ndawenda, tekisa bima byaku, amana wahana mbongu kwena batsukami, amana wátambula kuvwa kumosi mu mazilu, kunima, nzawisa amana wandanda.»
MAT 19:22 Amana mu kayuka, ngunza, ndinga yina, wenda yi kiwayi mukuma kimvwama kya lawu kakala kyawu.
MAT 19:23 Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi: phasi bwenina kwena mvwama mosi mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya mazilu.
MAT 19:24 Amana yiluzimbwadi hika: bweku phasi kwena kamela mu kulobuka ha hundu dya ndongu, kuluta mvwama mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
MAT 19:25 Amana mu kuyuka bwabuna, balonguki báyituka lawu, bakala zimbula: «Nati si wufwani kuhuluka?»
MAT 19:26 Amana Yesu buna kabatala, wubazimbwadi: «Mana misiku lendakana kwena batu, misi lendakana kwena Nzambi.»
MAT 19:27 Hanga Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Tala betu, tusisi bima byetu byosu amana tulandi ngeyi. Abweti dyakála kikuma kya betu?»
MAT 19:28 Amana Yesu wábazimbwala: «Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi: kwena benu lwisa ndanda: mu tsi ya pha, tangwa kazákala Mwana wa mutu hana kiti kyandi kya luyalu lwa khembu, benu phi lwakála bazakala muna biti kumi yi byodi bya luyalu mu kufundisa bikanda kumi yi byodi bya Kiseledi.
MAT 19:29 Amana kosu mutu wuna wásisa nzu holo baphangi ba bayakala holo baphangi ba bakhetu, holo tata holo ngudi holo bana holo mafu kikuma kya khumbu ya meni, katámbula mbala khama kuluta amana kavwa luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula.
MAT 19:30 Lawu bakála batheti, basúkinina amana lawu bakála batsuka, batékila.»
MAT 20:1 «Mukuma, Kipfumu kya mazilu kifwanakani hanga: mutu mosi, pfumu wa kilanga wálubuka muna suka-suka kusanda basadi kikuma kya kilanga kyandi kya vinu.
MAT 20:2 Amana wáyukana yi basadi mu fwalanga dimosi muna kilumbu amana wábatuma mu kilanga kyandi kya vinu.
MAT 20:3 Wálubuka hika mu tangwa dya vwa dya suka, wumoni bahika bakala kuna zandu bakonda kisalu.
MAT 20:4 Kwena batu bana wuzimbudi: "Alwenda benu phi muna kilanga kya vinu, amana yiluheka lufutu luna lufwani."
MAT 20:5 Bawu benda kwakuna. Wálubuka hika mu tangwa dya tsinzi, yi mu tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika, wusadi phila mosi.
MAT 20:6 Amana mu tangwa dya tanu dya masikidika, buna kálubuka, wáwana hika bakwawu bakala batelama hana, amana wubazimbwadi: "Kikuma kya biki luwheniki kilumbu kya muthu konda kisalu?"
MAT 20:7 Bamuzimbwadini: "Kikuma heku mutu wutubongi mu kisalu." Yandi wubazimbwadi: "Ndenu lwenda benu phi mu kilanga kya vinu."
MAT 20:8 «Kuma buna kwáyila, pfumu wa kilanga kya vinu wuzimbudi kwena kaphita kandi: "Tela basadi amana wabafuta lufutu lwa bawu. Wayándikila kwena bana batsuka yi kuna kwa bana batheti."
MAT 20:9 Amana buna bisa bana báyandika mu tangwa dya tanu dya masikidika, bátambula kosu mutu fwalanga dimosi.
MAT 20:10 Amana buna bisa bana batheti, bakala banza ni batámbula kuluta, kaasi batambudi, bawu phi, fwalanga dimosi kosu mutu.
MAT 20:11 Buna bátambula, báyandika mu kubokuta kikuma kya pfumu wa kilanga
MAT 20:12 yi kuzonzaka: "Baba bisiki batsuka, tangwa dimosi lwesi basadini, amana wubafuti kitesu kimosi yi betu tuhyombidi kilumbu kyosu yi mwini wutuwhidi!"
MAT 20:13 Kaasi yandi mu kuvutula kwena mosi wa bawu, wuzimbudi: "Mukwetu, yikuhangiku mbi; tuyukanikiku yi meni kikuma kya fwalanga dimosi?
MAT 20:14 Tambula kina kyenina kya ngeyi amana ndawenda. Yukani nzodi yihana, kwena wuna wenina watsuka, kitesu kimosi yi ngeyi, mana matadi meni-meni.
MAT 20:15 Yeku yi hamu dya kusadila mbongu zama bwosu nzodini? Kondilo kikudi-kudi wungyukidi kikuma kya buna yenina mutu wa mboti?"
MAT 20:16 Ihana ni, bátekila bakála batsuka amana batsuka bakála batheti.»
MAT 20:17 Bwosu kakala tombuka ku Yelusalemi, Yesu wábanata ku phungamu balonguki kumi yi bodi amana muna nzila, wubazimbwadi:
MAT 20:18 «Talenu, ku Yelusalemi tubati tombuka; Mwana wa mutu bamúlambula kwena mbuta wa banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku. Ndola ya lufwa bamúzengila
MAT 20:19 amana bamúlambula kwena baphani, ndangu bamuseya, bamuzyatula, bamukhoka hana kitakani. Amana mu kilumbu kya tatu, kafútumuka.»
MAT 20:20 Hanga ngudi wa bana ba Zebeteya wábwesuka kwena Yesu yi bana bandi ba bayakala amana wáfukama ndangu kamulomba kima kimosi.
MAT 20:21 Amana yandi wumuzimbwadi: «Biki wuzodini?» Mukhetu wámuzimbwala: «Zonza ni bana bama baba bodi bazakala mosi kuna kitata kyaku, amana mosi ku kimama kyaku muna Kipfumu kyaku.»
MAT 20:22 Amana Yesu mu kuvutula, wuzimbudi: «Lwisiku zaya mambu mana lwisi lomba. Lwalénda kunwa mbungu yina yinwa meni?» Bawu bamuzimbwadini: «Twalenda.»
MAT 20:23 Yandi wubazimbwadi: «Mbungu yama lwanwáya. Kaasi kuzakala ku kitata kyama yi ku kimama kyama, ka meni ku yihana muswa; kaasi bizika byenina kikuma kya babana kayidikilabya Tata wama.»
MAT 20:24 Bakwawu bana kumi, ha báyuka bwabuna, hanga babayukidi khabu baphangi bana bawu bodi.
MAT 20:25 Amana Yesu wábatela boosu wubazimbwadi: «Luzayi ni malemba ma makanda bisi yala hana thandu ya batu hanga bapfumu, amana bambuta bisi songila kwena bakwawu hamu dya bawu.
MAT 20:26 Bwakálaku buna ha kati dya benu, kaasi wuna wazóla, ha kati dya benu, kukituka mbuta, kakála musadi wenu,
MAT 20:27 amana wuna wazóla kukala watheti mu kati dya benu kakala muhika wenu:
MAT 20:28 Bwosu Mwana wa mutu, yandi kísaku ndangu bamusadila, kaasi kikuma kya kusadila yi kulambula luzingu lwandi mu phila ya kukatula batu balawu mu kihika.»
MAT 20:29 Buna bálubuka mu Yediko, mulumba-lumba wa batu wámulanda.
MAT 20:30 Amana baphofu bodi bazakala kuna kabeta ka nzila, buna báyuka ni Yesu kakala luta, bákalunga mu kuzonza: «Tuyukila kyadi, Pfumu, Mwana wa Tavidi!»
MAT 20:31 Amana mulumba-lumba wa batu wáyandika kubakandikisa ndangu badibata, kaasi bawu bákalunga hika ngolu: «Tuyukila kyadi, Pfumu, Mwana wa Tavidi!»
MAT 20:32 Amana Yesu buna kátelama, wábatela amana wábahyula: «Biki luzodi ni yilusadila?»
MAT 20:33 Bamuzimbwadini: «Pfumu, mesu metu matemuka!»
MAT 20:34 Amana yi kyadi kya lawu, Yesu wábasimba muna mesu; muna mbala mosi, báyandika kumona hika, amana bámulanda.
MAT 21:1 Tangwa bátula bela-bela yi Yelusalemi, amana bátula ku hata dya Betifasi, bela-bela yi mongu wa Olive, hanga Yesu wátuma balonguki bodi,
MAT 21:2 mu kubazimbwala: «Alwenda kuna hata dina dyenina ku thwala ya benu, amana lwawána ane wa kibuti wakuzitika yi mwana wa ane hakimosi yi yandi; bakutumunenu, amana bandatinenu.
MAT 21:3 Amana yuka ni mutu kaluzimbwala kima, zimbulenu: "Pfumu mupfunu kabavwini." Amana, muna mbala mosi, kabásula.»
MAT 21:4 Amana mambu mana mábwa ndangu dyalungila dyambu dina dyázonzama kwena mbikudi:
MAT 21:5 «Zimbulenu kwena mwana wa mukhetu wa Siyoni: Tala kyamvu waku wisi kwena ngeyi, wabasa yi ngemba, wazanza hana thandu ya ane wa kibuti, yi hana thandu ya mwana wa ane, mwana wa mbisi mosi.»
MAT 21:6 Buna benda balonguki, báhanga phi bwosu kábalongila Yesu.
MAT 21:7 Bisa munata ane wa kibuti yi mwana wandi, amana hana tandu ya bawu, báthetika miledi mya bawu; amana Yesu wázakala hana thandu.
MAT 21:8 Amana mulumba-lumba wa batu bakala yala miledi mya bawu muna nzila; bahika bakala hawula mihandi ku miti yi kuyalakamya muna nzila.
MAT 21:9 Milumba-lumba mya batu bakala kwenda kuna thwala ya yandi amana bana bakala landa yi kukalungaka mu kuzimbula: «Ozana kwena Mwana wa Tavidi! Kasambuka wuna wisi kwisa mu khumbu ya Pfumu! Ozana kwena Nzambi muna bisoka!»
MAT 21:10 Amana buna kakala kota mu Yelusalemi, mbanza yosu yánikana mu kuzimbula: «Nati kenina yandu?»
MAT 21:11 Amana milumba-lumba mya batu bakala vutula: «Yandu kenina mbikudi Yesu, mwisi Nazaleti dya Ngadidi.»
MAT 21:12 Yesu wákota kuna nzu ya Nzambi, wákukwasa boosu bana bakala tekisa yi bana bakala sumba kuna nzu ya Nzambi, amana wámwanga mesa ma bakwa tsyenzya yi biti bya bateki ba baphombu.
MAT 21:13 Amana wubazimbwadini: «Tala mana másonama: "Nzu yama batédikiya nzu ya bisambu." Kaasi benu, lukitudiya saka dya bandwandwa!»
MAT 21:14 Baphofu yi bifwa malu bábwesuka kwena yandi muna nzu ya Nzambi. Amana wábabuka.
MAT 21:15 Kaasi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku buna bámona mambu ma khumbwa mana kahanga, yi bana bakhunda buna bakala kalunga mu nzu ya Nzambi: «Ozana kwena Mwana wa Tavidi!» Hanga báfunga khabu
MAT 21:16 amana bamuzimbwadini: «Wubati yuka mana babati zonza bana baba?» Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Eeh. Lwátangaku kedi ndinga zazi: "Muna munwa mya bana bakhunda yi bana ba lubutu wádiyidikila lukumu?"»
MAT 21:17 Amana buna kábasisa, wálubuka mu mbanza, ndangu kenda ku hata dya Betaniya, wanimba kwakuna.
MAT 21:18 Muna suka, mu kuvutuka ku mbanza, wáyuka nzala.
MAT 21:19 Amana buna kámona miti wa fiki wumosi muna nzila, wábwesuka kwakuna; kaasi wuwani lwesi khaya; amana wázimbula kwena miti wa fiki: «Ka kibundu kimosi ku hika kyabútuka mwena ngeyi, mu kimakulu!» Amana muna tangwa meni dina, mufiki wáyumuka.
MAT 21:20 Buna bámona bwabuna, balonguki báyituka lawu: Abweti miti wa fiki wawu wuyumukini mu mbala mosi?
MAT 21:21 Amana mu kuvutula, Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi, honi lwakala yi lukwikilu, lwisiku banga phi, lwasalaku lwesi mana masalami ku miti wa fiki, kaasi lufwani phi kuzimbula kwena mongu wawu: "Kinduka hana, amana dilosa mu yanga dya mbuta", bwana bwahángama."
MAT 21:22 Kyosu kina lwalómba mu lombilu yi lukwikilu, lwatámbulakya.»
MAT 21:23 Buna kákota mu nzu ya Nzambi, tangwa kakala longa, bapfumu ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta bisa muhyula: «Mu hamu dya nati wubati hangila mambu mana? Amana nati wákuheka hamu meni dina?»
MAT 21:24 Amana mu kuvutula, Yesu wuzimbudi kwena bawu: «Meni phi yiluhyula kyufu kimosi lwesi; yukani lwamvútwala, yilúzimbwala keti mu hamu dya nati yisi sadila mambu mana.
MAT 21:25 Mbotika yina ya Yowani, ku zilu yátuka ho kwena batu?» Kaasi bawu bakala diwinina bawu yi bawu, yi kudizimbwalaka: «Yuka twazimbula: "Ya ku zilu", katúzimbwala: "Amana kikuma kya biki lwakonda sila lukwikilu mwena yandi?"
MAT 21:26 Amana yuka twazimbula: "Kwena batu", tufwani kubanga mulumba-lumba wa batu, mukuma boosu bisi kwikila ni Yowani mbikudi kákala.»
MAT 21:27 Amana mu kuvutula kwena Yesu, bazimbudi: «Tuzayiku.» Yandi phi wubavutwadi: «Meni phi yiluzimbwalaku keti mu hamu dya nati yisi sadila mambu mana.»
MAT 21:28 «Abweti lubanzi? Mutu mosi wákala yi bana ba bayakala bodi; hanga wubwesuki kwena wuna wa tsomi wuzimbudi: "Mwana awenda, lelu, wasala mu kilanga kya vinu."
MAT 21:29 Amana yandi, mu kuvutula, wuzimbudi: "Nzodiku;" kaasi kunima wázosulula, wenda ku kilanga.
MAT 21:30 Amana buna kábwesuka kwena mukwawu, wuzimbudi phila mosi. Amana yandi mu kuvutula wuzimbudi: "Eeh, yikwenda, tata" kaasi kendaku ku kilanga.
MAT 21:31 Nati mu kati dya bawu boodi wásala luzolu lwa tata?» Bavutudi: «Watheti», Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi, bakalaki ka phaku yi bandumba balutekididi mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
MAT 21:32 Mukuma Yowani kisa kwena benu mu kulusongila nzila ya masonga, amana benu lwámukwikilaku. Kaasi bakalaki ka phaku yi bandumba bámukwikila, amana keti buna nana lwámona mambu mana, lwázosululaku kwenu ndangu lwamukwikila.»
MAT 21:33 «Yukenu kingana kya hika: Mutu mosi wákala pfumu wa nzu wákuna kilanga kya vinu. Wukakikya mu luphangu, wáyidika kinyongi kya vinu muna kati, wátunga kinongi kikuma kya kutadikina vinu, kunima wáluwisakya kwena basadi ba vinu, amana wenda mu kitambu.
MAT 21:34 Amana ha dyálungila tangwa dya bibundu, wátuma basadi bandi kwena basadi bana bákala mu kilanga kya vinu ndangu bamubongila ndambu yandi ya bibundu.
MAT 21:35 Kaasi buna bábakwata basadi bandi kwena basadi bana bakala sala mu kilanga kya vinu; mosi bámubeta, mosi hika bámuhonda, amana mukwawu hika bámuzukwamina matadi.
MAT 21:36 Wáhitika hika basadi bakwawu kuluta thalu ya bana batheti, amana bábahanga hika phila mosi.
MAT 21:37 Amana ku tsuka, wábahitika mwana wandi wa yakala, yi kubanzaka: "Bamuzitisa mwana wama."
MAT 21:38 Kaasi tangwa bámumona basadi bana bákala mu kilanga kya vinu, badizimbwadi bawu yi bawu: "Yandi kenina swana! Alwisenu, twamuhonda ndangu twabonga kuvwa kwandi!"
MAT 21:39 Hanga bamukwati, bámutimbula ku phenza ya kilanga kya vinu amana bámuhonda.
MAT 21:40 «Amana tangwa kakwísa mukwa kilanga kya vinu, abweti kabáhanga basadi bana?»
MAT 21:41 Bamuvutwadini: «Batu bana bambi, kabáhonda konda kubayukila kyadi, amana kilanga kya vinu kalúwisakya kwena batu bahika, bana bamúheka bibundu muna tangwa dyandi.»
MAT 21:42 Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Khaku kedi lutanga muna Masonuku:» "Tadi bálosa bana bakala tunga dyadyadi dikituki kisina kya mupfundila; Dyambu dina dyátuka kwena Pfumu, dyena dyambu dya kuyituka ku mesu ma betu!"
MAT 21:43 «Ihana ni, yiluzimbwadi: Kipfumu kya Nzambi bálukatulakya amana báhanakya kwena kanda dya hika dina dyábutilakya bibundu. [
MAT 21:44 Amana wosu wuna wabwa ha tadi dina katóluka; ha thandu ya wuna dyabwíla, dyamúnikumuna.]»
MAT 21:45 Amana buna báyuka bwabuna mbuta wa banganga Nzambi yi bafwadisi bingana byandi, bábakisa ni kikuma kya bawu kakala zonzila.
MAT 21:46 Bakala sanda phila ya kumukwatisila, báyuka bweya bwa milumba-lumba mya batu, kikuma bakala mubongila hanga mbikudi.
MAT 22:1 Yesu wázonzila hika mu bingana; wuzimbudi:
MAT 22:2 «Kipfumu kya mazilu kifwanakani yi kyamvu mosi wáta mukinzi wa longu lwa mwana wandi wa yakala.
MAT 22:3 Amana wátuma basadi bandi benda tela batu bana kátedisa ku mukinzi wa longu; kaasi bázolaku kukwisa.
MAT 22:4 Wátuma hika basadi bakwawu, mu kuzimbula: "Zimbulenu kwena bana thedisiki: Tala, ngidiki kedi madya mama, miluma mya bangombi yi bambisi bahika ba senga babahondi, byosu byayilama; alwisenu ku mukinzi wa longu!"
MAT 22:5 Kaasi bawu bálewula, benda kwabawu, mosi wenda ku kilanga kyandi, mukwawu wenda ku kikhita kyandi;
MAT 22:6 amana bakwawu, bábakwata basadi bandi, bábatukwana, amana bábahonda.
MAT 22:7 Kyamvu wáyuka khabu: amana buna kátuma baphumbulu bandi, wáhondisa bandwandwa bana yi mbanza ya bawu phi wáyokisaya.
MAT 22:8 Hanga wuzimbudi kwena basadi bandi: "Mukinzi wa longu wuyilami, kaasi batu babana bátedisa bákalaku kwatakani kikuma kya wawu.
MAT 22:9 Hangenu lwenda muna phambu za nzila, amana tedisenu, ku mukinzi wa longu, boosu bana lwawána."
MAT 22:10 Buna bálubuka basadi bana mu nzila, bákutikisa batu boosu bana báwana, ba mbi yi ba mboti; nzu ya mukinzi yábasa yi batu.
MAT 22:11 Amana buna kákota kyamvu mu kutala batu bana kátedisa, wámona mwamuna mutu mosi wakonda vwata muledi wa mukinzi wa longu.
MAT 22:12 Amana wumuzimbwadi: "Mukwetu, abweti wukotidi mwamu konda muledi wa mukinzi wa longu?" Kaasi yandi kámonaku kima kya kuvutula.
MAT 22:13 Hanga kyamvu wuzimbudi kwena basadi: "Mukasenu moku yi malu, amana mulosenu ku nzila kwena phipha; kwakuna kwakála bidilu yi makwenzi."
MAT 22:14 Mukuma balawu bátela, kaasi bakhunda básolama.»
MAT 22:15 Hanga bafwadisi bendi kasa kifwandu, bamuleya ndangu bamukwatila mu ndinga.
MAT 22:16 Amana batumini balonguki ba bawu kwena yandi ha kimosi yi ndambu ya batu bana bakala landa Helodi, mu kuzimbula: «Mulongi, tuzayi ni kyedika wisi zonza ngeyi amana wisi longa nzila ya Nzambi mu masonga. Weku yi bweya bwa mambu mana bisi banza batu mukuma wisiku tala mbunzu za batu.
MAT 22:17 Tuzimbwaleti si buna wisi banza ngeyi: bulombi mu kufuta phaku ya Khayisala ho loni?»
MAT 22:18 Kaasi Yesu, bwosu kázaya mabanza ma bawu ma mbi; wuzimbudi: «Kikuma kya biki lubati ndeyila, bakavungalosi?
MAT 22:19 Tsongilenu mbongu zina bisi futa phaku.» Bawu bámusongila fwalanga dimosi,
MAT 22:20 amana wábahyula: «Mbunzu yi khumbu yayi básonika haka, bya nati?»
MAT 22:21 Bamuzimbwadini: «Bya Khayisala». Hanga wubazimbwadi: «Disongidila, hanenu mambu ma Khayisala kwena Khayisala, amana mambu ma Nzambi kwena Nzambi.»
MAT 22:22 Buna báyuka bwabuna, báyituka, amana bámusisa, benda kwa bawu.
MAT 22:23 Muna kilumbu meni kina, ndambu ya Basadise, bana bisi zimbula ni kweku lufutumuku, bábwesuka kwena yandi, amana bámuhyula
MAT 22:24 mu kuzimbula: «Mulongi, Moyize kázimbula: "Yuka ni mutu mosi kafwa konda kubuta mwana, myaki wandi kafweti kwela mufwidi ndangu katombula kikanda kya phangi wandi."
MAT 22:25 Kinga, kwákala kwena betu, yi baphangi ba bayakala tsambwadi; amana watheti wákwela, wáfwa; amana konda kusisa dibuta, wásisa mufwidi wandi kwena myaki wandi.
MAT 22:26 Busalami phila mosi kwena wuna wazodi, yi watatu, yi kuna kwa wuna watsambwadi.
MAT 22:27 Amana kunima dya bawu boosu, mukhetu wáfwa.
MAT 22:28 Mu kilumbu kya lufutumuku, mukhetu wa nani kakala, ha kati dya bawu tsambwadi? Mukuma boosu bámukwela!»
MAT 22:29 Amana mu kuvutula, Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Luditotisi kikuma lwisiku bakisa keti Masonuku keti ngolu za Nzambi.
MAT 22:30 Mukuma, ku lufutumuku lwa bafwa kwakálaku yi bayakala keti bakhetu bakwélana, kaasi bakala hanga banzyo mu zilu.
MAT 22:31 Amana kikuma kya lufutumuku lwa bafwa, lwátangaku mana báluzimbwala kwena Nzambi:
MAT 22:32 "Meni yena Nzambi wa Bulahami yi Nzambi wa Yizaki yi Nzambi wa Yakobi"? Keku Nzambi wa bafwa kaasi wa bana ba moya.»
MAT 22:33 Amana buna báyuka bwana, milumba-lumba mya batu báyituka lawu ku malongi mandi.
MAT 22:34 Buna báyuka Bafwadisi ni Yesu wábatsukisa Basadise, bákutakana.
MAT 22:35 Amana mosi hana kati dya bawu, mulongi wa mitsiku, kakala muleya mu kumuhyula:
MAT 22:36 «Mulongi, khi wawu mutsiku wa mbuta mu mitsiku?»
MAT 22:37 Yandi wumuvutwadi: «"Watónda Pfumu Nzambi waku yi mbundu yaku yosu, yi moya waku wosu yi ngangu zaku zoosu."
MAT 22:38 Wawu wenina mutsiku wa mbuta yi watheti.
MAT 22:39 Amana mutsiku wa zodi, phila mosi yi wuna wa theti: "Tonda khunda waku hanga ngeyi meni."
MAT 22:40 Mitsiku myami myodi mivungi mitsiku yi Bambikudi.»
MAT 22:41 Bwosu bákutakana Bafwadisi, Yesu wábahyula
MAT 22:42 mu kuzimbula: «Biki lwisi banza kikuma kya Kidisitu? Mwana wa nati kenina?» Bamuvutwadini: «Wa Tavidi.»
MAT 22:43 Yandi wubazimbwadi: «Abweti si Tavidi, mu Kitembu kisi mutela ni Pfumu, tangwa kisi zimbula:»
MAT 22:44 "Pfumu kázimbula kwena Pfumu wama": Sikuka ku kitata kyama, yi kuna yibásila bambeni baku ku sina dya bitambi byaku."
MAT 22:45 «Disonga yuka ni Tavidi kisi mutela "Pfumu", abweti kakadila mwana wandi?»
MAT 22:46 Amana ka mutu ku walenda kumuvutwala ndinga mosi. Tuka kilumbu meni kina, ka mutu ku wámeka hika kumuhyula kyufu.
MAT 23:1 Hanga Yesu wázonza kwena milumba-lumba mya batu yi kwena balonguki bandi
MAT 23:2 mu kuzimbula: «Balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi badizakadisi ha kiti kya Moyize.
MAT 23:3 Disongidila ni, mambu moosu mana balúzimbwala, salenu, swekenu phi, kaasi benu luhangaku mihangu mya bawu. Mukuma bisi zonza kaasi bisiku sadila.
MAT 23:4 Amana bisi wongika miteti mya zitu, myena yi phasi mu kunata, mu mahembu ma batu; kaasi bawu meni bisiku zola kuningisa keti ku mulembu.
MAT 23:5 Amana bisalu bya bawu byosu, bisi sala, ndangu badimonikisaka kwena batu. Ihana ni, bisi nata biphakala bya mbuta bya mavwelesi hana mbunzu yi muna moku ma bawu yi miledi mya mbuta amana baleyisi yi misinga.
MAT 23:6 Amana bazodi kuzakala mu bifulu bya theti mu mikinzi yi bifulu bya theti mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta;
MAT 23:7 yi mboti mu mazandu, yi kubatelaka kwena batu ni "Mulongi."
MAT 23:8 Kaasi benu, luzolaku ni balutela "Mulongi", mukuma mosi lwesi wena mulongi wenu, amana benu, benu boosu lwena baphangi.
MAT 23:9 Lutelaku mutu, ha tsi haha, ni "Tata", mukuma mosi lwesi wena tata wenu, Tata wa ku zilu.
MAT 23:10 Luzolukaku ni balutela "Mutwadisi", mukuma mosi lwesi wena Mutwadisi wenu Kidisitu.
MAT 23:11 Amana mbuta mu kati dya benu kakala musadi wenu.
MAT 23:12 Wuna wadítombula yandi meni, bamúkulumuna amana wuna wadíkulumuna yandi meni, bamútombula.»
MAT 23:13 «Amana khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Kikuma lwisi yafikila kyafulu kya Kipfumu kya mazilu ku thwala ya batu; amana lwisimwoku kota benu-benu, lwisiku bayambula phi mu kukota babana bazola kukota.» [
MAT 23:14 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Mukuma lwisi botula kwena bafwidi bima bya bawu amana, mu kudihunikisa, lwisi sala malombilu ma kaleyi; kikuma kya bwabuna, lwatámbula pfundusu mosi yiluti kitesu.]
MAT 23:15 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Kikuma lwisi kangala muna yanga dya mbuta yi muna tsi ndangu lwakotisa muphakanu mosi ku dingumba dyenu, amana buna lwamúnunga, lumukitudi mutu mosi wa bilungi mbala zodi kuluta benu.
MAT 23:16 «Khi kyadi kwena benu bathwadisi baphofu, lwisi zimbula: "Honi mutu kadya ndefi mu khumbu ya nzu ya Nzambi, ka kima ku; kaasi yuka ni mutu kadya ndefi mu wolu dina dyenina mu nzu ya Nzambi, kafweti lungisa ndefi yandi."
MAT 23:17 Bilawu yi baphofu! Biki biluti mupfunu, wolu ho nzu ya Nzambi yina yisi sakumuna wolu?
MAT 23:18 Amana lwisi zimbula hika: "Honi mutu kadya ndefi mu khumbu ya mesa ma kimenga, ka kima ku; kaasi yuka ni mutu mosi kadya ndefi mu khumbu ya kabu dina dyenina ha mesa ma kimenga, kafweti lungisa ndefi yandi."
MAT 23:19 Baphofu! Amana biki biluti mupfunu, kabu ho mesa ma kimenga mana misi sakumuna kabu?
MAT 23:20 Disongidila, wuna wisi dya ndefi mu khumbu ya mesa ma kimenga kisiya dya mu khumbu ya mesa ma kimenga yi mu khumbu ya bima byosu byenina hana thandu;
MAT 23:21 amana wuna wisi dya ndefi mu khumbu ya nzu ya Nzambi, kisiya dya mu khumbu ya nzu ya Nzambi yi mu khumbu ya wuna wisimwa kala.
MAT 23:22 Amana wuna wisi dya ndefi mu khumbu ya zilu, kisiya dya mu khumbu ya kiti kya luyalu kya Nzambi yi mu khumbu ya wuna wenina hana wazakala.
MAT 23:23 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Kikuma lwisi hana kimosi kya kumi kya khaya za tsudi ya kitoku yi bithundu yi miti mya kitoku, kaasi lusisi bima bya mupfunu mu mitsiku: kusungama, khenda yi lukwikilu; byabina biluti mboti mu kusala, konda kusisa bina bisadi.
MAT 23:24 Bathwadisi baphofu, lwisi kenza malafu mu kukatula biyingayinga kaasi lwisi mina Kamela wa muthu!
MAT 23:25 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Kikuma lwisi semisa phenza ya kopha yi dilonga, amana mu kati bya kabasi yi bima bina lwisi yiba yi kukonda kwa kusipha kwa mbundu.
MAT 23:26 Mufwadisi phofu! Semisa theti kati dya kopha ndangu phenza yandi phi yasema.
MAT 23:27 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Kikuma lufwanani yi mazyamu basiti phemba mabati monika kitoku ku phenza, kaasi mu kati mabasa yi mifufwa mya bamvumbi yi bima byosu bya mvindu.
MAT 23:28 Phila mosi phi yi benu, lwisi monika batu ba masonga kwena batu, kaasi mu kati lwabasa yi mvunga yi mambu mambi.
MAT 23:29 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi, bakavungalosi! Lwisi tunga mazyamu ma bambikudi, yi kunenga mazyamu ma batu ba masonga,
MAT 23:30 amana lwisi zimbula: "Wadi betu phi twazingila mu tangwa dya batata betu, wadi twakanaku kala mu kithwadi kya mbi yi bawu kikuma kya kunokisa menga ma bambikudi."
MAT 23:31 Abwabuna lwisi ta kimbangi kwena benu-benu ni lwenina bana ba batu bana báhonda bambikudi.
MAT 23:32 Amana benu, landenu, manisenu mana báyandika batata benu!
MAT 23:33 Banyoka, mbandu ya masawa! Abweti lubati banza kutina kyana pfundusu ya bilungi?
MAT 23:34 Ihana ni tala meni phitiki kwena benu bambikudi yi batu ba nduka yi balongi ba mitsiku. Muna kati dya bawu, bahika, lwabáhonda amana lwabákhoka ha kitakani, bakwawu hika, lwabázyatula muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta zenu amana bakwawu hika phi, lwabányokuniki mbanza muna mbanza;
MAT 23:35 ndangu yalubwila mbesi ya menga moosu ma batu ba masonga mana mátyakana ha tsi tukidila ku menga ma Abelu mutu wa masonga yi kuna menga ma Zakadiya, mwana wa yakala wa Balakiya, wuna lwáhonda ha kati dya nzu ya Nzambi yi mesa ma kimenga.
MAT 23:36 Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi: mambu mana moosu mabwíla kwena batu ba mbandu yayi.»
MAT 23:37 «Yelusalemi, Yesulusalemi, ngeyi wisi honda bambikudi yi kubatimbwala matadi bana bisi kutumina! Mbala kwa nzodi kedi kukutikisa bana baku bwosu kisi kutikisa, ngudi wa khoku, bana bandi ku tsi ya mahela mandi, kaasi lwázolabwoku.
MAT 23:38 Tala buthwena, balúyambwadidiya nzu yenu, yakítuka zumbu!
MAT 23:39 Mukuma, yiluzimbwadi, mu kyedika: Tuka lelu dyadi lwambónaku hika tii yi kuna lwazímbwala: "Kasakumuka wuna wukwisila mu khumbu ya Pfumu!"»
MAT 24:1 Mu kulubuka kwa Yesu mu nzu ya Nzambi, balonguki bandi bábwesuka ndangu bamusongila thungidi ya nzu ya Nzambi.
MAT 24:2 Amana yandi mu kubavutwala, wuzimbudi: «Lwisibyoku tala bima byabi byosu? Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi, hasálaku keti tadi dimosi ha thandu ya tadi dikwawu dyakonda wulumuka.»
MAT 24:3 Amana buna kázakala yandi hana mongu wuna bisi tela ni mongu wa Olive, balonguki bábwesuka kwena yandi, mu kingenga bazimbudi: «Tuzimbwala khi tangwa makála mambu mana amana khi kidimbu kyasóngila ngisilu yaku yi tsuka ya tsi?»
MAT 24:4 Amana mu kubavutwala, Yesu wuzimbudi: «Kebenu, ka mutu ku kalutotisa!
MAT 24:5 Kikuma lawu bakwísa mu khumbu ya meni, mu kuzimbula: "Meni yenina Kidisitu" amana lawu babátotisa.
MAT 24:6 Amana lwayúka kuzonzila mvita yi pfweta-pfweta za mvita: talenu, lukalaku mu bidilu; mukuma mboti mambu mana masalama, kaasi yakálaku kedi tsuka.
MAT 24:7 Mukuma tsi yimosi yanwánisa tsi yikwawu, amana kipfumu kimosi kyanwánisa kipfumu kikwawu; amana nzala yi kunikana kwa mafu byakála muma mwahika.
MAT 24:8 Amana mambu mana moosu makála hanga misongu mya theti.
MAT 24:9 Hanga balulambudi ku kiwayi amana balúhonda amana balúmenga muna makanda moosu kikuma kya khumbu ya meni.
MAT 24:10 Muna tangwa meni dina, kyakála kisinza kikuma kya batu balawu, amana bamosi badílambula bawu yi bawu, amana bahika badímenga bawu yi bawu.
MAT 24:11 Amana bambikudi ba bukamvi lawu batélama, bahukumuna batu balawu.
MAT 24:12 Kikuma kya mambu mambi mana ma lawu; lungongu lwa batu balawu lwakúlumuka.
MAT 24:13 Kaasi wuna wakwámina tii yi kuna tsuka, yandi kahúluka.
MAT 24:14 Musamu wa Bukheti wawu wa Kipfumu kya mazilu basámunawa muna tsi yosu yina bisi zingila, kyakála kimbangi kikuma kya makanda moosu, hanga tsuka yisi.»
MAT 24:15 «Tangwa lwamóna muzangi wanzanzi wakutelamisa muna kizika kyahedila, bwosu kázonza mbikudi Tanyela, mutu wuna wubati tanga kabakula!
MAT 24:16 Hanga bana bakala mu kinzunga kya Yuteya batini muna myongu;
MAT 24:17 wuna wakála ha thandu ya mudilu, katulukaku kikuma kya kulubula bima mu nzu yandi;
MAT 24:18 amana wuna wakala mu kilanga kavutukaku kikuma kya kubonga muledi wandi.
MAT 24:19 Khi kyadi kwena mukhetu wuna wakala ku vumu yi kwena wuna wakala yemika muna bilumbu meni bina!
MAT 24:20 Lombilenu ndangu lutinaku mu tangwa dya kyosi kya lawu, keti mu kilumbu kya sabata!
MAT 24:21 Mukuma, kiwayi kya lawu kyakála, hanga kina kyakonda kedi kala tuka ku luyandiku lwa tsi yi buthwena bwabu, amana zakálaku hika.
MAT 24:22 Wadi ni bilumbu bina byákalaku bya khufi, wadi keti mutu káhulukaku, kaasi kikuma kya bana básolama bákhufikisilabya bilumbu bina.
MAT 24:23 Yuka ni mutu kaluzimbwala: "Kidisitu haha kenina!" Holo: "Kuna kenina!" Lukwikilaku.
MAT 24:24 Mukuma bamasiya ba bukamvi yi bambikudi ba bukamvi balúbuka; basóngila biphadi yi mambu ma kuyituka mukuma, yuka bwalendakana, bahúkumuna keti bana kásola Nzambi.
MAT 24:25 Tala buna thekidi luzimbwala.
MAT 24:26 «Disongidila yuka ni baluzimbwala: "Talenu, mu nganga kenina, lulubukaku; holo, talenu ku suku kenina, lukwikilaku.
MAT 24:27 Kikuma bwosu wisi lubuka mutsyenzya tuka ku malubwakidi amana wukenzudi yi kuna mazyokidi, bwabuna kwakála kukwisa kwa Mwana wa mutu.
MAT 24:28 Kuna kwakála kivundisila, kwakuna bakútakanina bangandwanganga.»
MAT 24:29 «Hanga kunima dya bilumbu bina bya kiwayi, tangwa kaphínda, ngondi kaséngulaku myesi myandi, bathetimbwa babwa tukidila ku zilu, amana ngolu za mazilu zaníkana.
MAT 24:30 Hanga kidimbu kya Mwana wa mutu kimoniki muna zilu; amana bikanda byosu bya tsi mu khondu byakála, bamóna Mwana wa mutu buna kakwísa hana matuti ma zilu yi ngolu yi khembu ya lawu.
MAT 24:31 Katúma banzyo bandi yi phungi ya mbuta, amana bakútikisa batu ba tselu ya bana kásola tukidila tselu ya tsi yi tselu ya zilu.»
MAT 24:32 «Mbandu ya kingana kya mufiki yaluheka dilongi: tangwa lwamóna ni miti wusawakidini, zayenu ni tsungi ya pha yibwesukini.
MAT 24:33 Phila mosi yi kwena benu, tangwa lwamóna bima bina byosu, zayenu ni Mwana wa mutu wekina mu kukwisa.
MAT 24:34 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi: mbandu yayi, yahítaku kedi yi kuna masálamina mambu mana moosu.
MAT 24:35 Zilu yi tsi byatóta, kaasi ndinga zama zalendaku tota.»
MAT 24:36 «Kikuma kya kilumbu meni kina yi tangwa, ka mutu ku wuzayibya, keti banzyo muna mazilu, keti Mwana; kaasi Tata yandi hika.
MAT 24:37 Mukuma bwosu bwákala mu tangwa dya Nowa, yibwana phi bwakála mu kukwisa kwa Mwana wa mutu.
MAT 24:38 Amana bwosu bwákala muna bilumbu meni bina byátekila kithombu, batu bakala dya yi kunwa, bakala kwelana yi kukwedisa, tii yi kuna kilumbu kina kákota Nowa mu nzasa;
MAT 24:39 amana bakalaku bakula kima tii yi kuna kyisila kithombu amana kinati byosu, yibwabuna phi bwakála mu kukwisa kwa Mwana wa mutu.
MAT 24:40 Hanga batu bodi bakála muna kilanga: mosi batámbula amana mosi bamúsisa.
MAT 24:41 Bakhetu bodi bakala toka muna yanda, mosi bamúnata, mukwawu bamúsisa.
MAT 24:42 Disongidila kalenu batemuna, mukuma luzayiku keti khi kilumbu kakwísa Pfumu wenu.
MAT 24:43 Amana zayenu bwabu: Wadi mukwa nzu kazayaka tangwa dina kakwisa mwifi, kakhanaku nimba amana kakhanaku yambwadila ni kalungula nzu yandi.
MAT 24:44 Yihana ni, kalenu bayilama, benu phi, mukuma Mwana wa mutu kakwísa muna tangwa dina lukondi yindula benu.»
MAT 24:45 «Nati si musadi wakwikama yi wa ngangu? Wuna káheka mukwa nzu kiyeka kya basadi bahika ndangu kabahekaka kudya muna tangwa dina difwani?
MAT 24:46 Kyesi kwena musadi wuna, buna kakwísa mukwa nzu, kamuwana bwabuna mu kisalu!
MAT 24:47 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa: kamúheka kiyeka kya bima byandi byosu.
MAT 24:48 Kaasi yuka ni yandina kakala musadi wa mbi amana kadibanzila muna mbundu yandi: "Pfumu wama kalengaku kwisa,"
MAT 24:49 kayandika kubabeta banduku ba kisalu, amana kadyaka, kanwaka phi kumosi yi babana bisi zela malafu,
MAT 24:50 kyedika mukwa nzu wuna katúla muna kilumbu kimosi kina kakalaku wayilama musadi wuna yi mu tangwa dina kakondiku zaya;
MAT 24:51 kamúheka ndola ya mbuta amana kámusya mu ndonga ya bakavungalosi, kuna kwakala bidilu yi makwenzi.»
MAT 25:1 «Kinga Kipfumu kya mazilu kifwanani yi bana ba bandumba kumi bábonga mwinda mya bawu, benda tundakana yi yakala dya longu.
MAT 25:2 Batanu, hana kati dya bawu, báyilamaku amana batanu bahika báyilama.
MAT 25:3 Bana bakonda yilama, buna bábonga mwinda mya bawu, bánataku masi ma bawu.
MAT 25:4 Kaasi batanu bana bayilama bánata masi muna bilekwa yi mwinda mya bawu.
MAT 25:5 Bwosu kázingidila yakala mu kukwisa, boosu bahanga balembwi kwabawu amana bánimba.
MAT 25:6 Amana mu kisuku kya phipha, kindanda kiditi: "Talenu yandu yakala, lubukenu, lwenda mutundakana!"
MAT 25:7 Hanga bandumba bana boosu batokami, amana báyidika mwinda mya bawu.
MAT 25:8 Hanga bana bakonda yilama bazimbudi kwena bana báyilama: "Tuhekenu masi menu, kikuma mwinda mya betu mizimi."
MAT 25:9 Bana ba mayedi bavutudi: "Loni, meku mafwana kikuma kya betu yi benu; mboti lwenda kwena bana bisima tekisa ndangu lwasumba kikuma kya benu."
MAT 25:10 Bwabuna benda bawu mu kusumba, yakala wátula. Amana bana bakala bayilama bakota yi yandi muna nzu ya mukinzi wa longu, hanga bayafikidi mwelu.
MAT 25:11 Amana kunima dya tangwa, bisa bandumba bana bakwawu, mu kuzimbula: "Tata, Tata, tuyafwadila!"
MAT 25:12 Kaasi yandi mu kuvutula, wuzimbudi: "Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi: Yiluzayiku."
MAT 25:13 Disongidila, kalakenu bayilama, kikuma luzayiku keti kilumbu keti tangwa.»
MAT 25:14 «Kipfumu kya mazilu kifwanakani hanga mutu mosi, mu kukwenda mu kitambu: watéla basadi bandi amana wábaheka bima byandi.
MAT 25:15 Kwena mosi, mikuta mitanu mya wolu, kwena mukwawu, mikuta myodi mya wolu, amana kwena wuna wa tatu mukuta wumosi, kwena kosu mutu muna ngolu zandi, amana kunima, wenda kwandi mu kitambu.
MAT 25:16 Buna kenda, musadi wuna wábonga mikuta mitanu, wásadilamya amana wálumbula mitanu myahika.
MAT 25:17 Phila mosi yi wuna wábonga mikuta myodi, wálumbula myodi myahika.
MAT 25:18 Kaasi wuna wátambula mukuta wumosi wenda wawu, wásima muna mafu amana wázikawa mukuta wa wolu wa pfumu wandi.
MAT 25:19 «Amana kunima dya tangwa dya lawu, pfumu wa basadi bana wisa, hanga wubatedi ndangu kazaya mutindu wuna básadiladya wolu.
MAT 25:20 Amana buna kábwesuka wuna wátambula mikuta mitanu, wusongidi hika mitanu mikwawu mu kuzimbula: "Pfumu, mikuta mitanu wápheka, tala mitanu mikwawu ndumbudi."
MAT 25:21 Pfumu wandi wumuzimbwadi: "Bwa bukheti! Ngeyi wenina musadi wa bukheti yi wa bulemvu. Muna bima bya khunda wukadiki mulemvu, yikúyadika ha thandu ya bima bya lawu, kota mu kyesi kya pfumu waku."
MAT 25:22 Buna kábwesuka wuna wátambula mikuta myodi wuzimbudi: "Pfumu, mikuta myodi wápheka, tala, mikwawu myodi mina ndumbudi!"
MAT 25:23 Pfumu wandi wumuzimbwadi: "Bwa bukheti! Musadi wa bukheti yi wa bulemvu, mu bima bya khunda, wisi dikadila wa bulemvu, yikúyadika ha thandu ya bima bya lawu; kota mu kyesi kya pfumu waku.
MAT 25:24 Amana buna kábwesuka wuna wátambula mukuta wumosi, wuzimbudi: "Tata, bwosu yikuzaya ni ngeyi mukwa mathata, wisi hela muna wakonda kunina, amana wisi wongika hana wakonda mwanga;
MAT 25:25 amana mu kubanga, yihanga, tswekiwa mukuta waku mu mafu; tala wawu mukuta waku."
MAT 25:26 Amana pfumu wandi wumuvutwadini: "Musadi wambi, mubolu! Wázayabwa ni yisi hela muna yikonda kunina, yisi wongika muna yikonda mwanga?
MAT 25:27 Wadi wakala kwenda sikula mukuta wa wolu dyama kwena bana bisi sala ku banki, amana mu kuvutuka kwama, khadi tambula bina byenina bya meni yi muluta.
MAT 25:28 Disongidila ni mutambulenu mukuta wuna wa wolu amana hanenu kwena wuna wenina myawu kumi.
MAT 25:29 Mukuma bahána kwena wuna wenina kyawu, ndangu kakala yi bima bya lawu, kaasi kwena wuna wukondi kima, bamútambula keti kina kenina kyawu.
MAT 25:30 Amana musadi wuna wakonda mupfunu, mulosenu ku phenza, muna phipha ya ku phenza; kwakuna kwakala bidilu yi makwenzi."»
MAT 25:31 «Tangwa kakwísa Mwana wa mutu mu khembu yandi yi banzyo boosu ha kimosi yi yandi, hanga wuzakadi hana kiti kyandi kya khembu.
MAT 25:32 Makanda moosu makhúndakana kuna thwala ya yandi, amana kabáhambula bamosi yi bakwawu, bwosu kisi hambula kalema mikoku yi bakhombu:
MAT 25:33 hanga wulongiki mikoku kuna koku dyandi dya kitata, amana bakhombu kuna koku dyandi dya kimama.
MAT 25:34 Hanga kyamvu wuzimbudi kwena bana bakála ku koku dyandi dya kitata: "Alwisa, benu kásambula Tata wama, tambulenu Kipfumu kya mazilu kina báluyidikila tukila buna káhanga tsi.
MAT 25:35 Mukuma, yíkala yi nzala, benu lwápheka bya kudya; yíkala yi kihwinya, benu lwápheka bya kunwa; yíkala munzenza amana benu lwángyamba;
MAT 25:36 yíkala khonga, benu lwámvwatisa; yikala bela, benu lwátsadisa; yíkala mu boloku, amana lwisa thala."
MAT 25:37 Amana batu ba masonga bamúvutwala mu kuzimbula: "Pfumu, khi tangwa twákumona ngeyi wákala yi nzala, amana twákuheka bya kudya, holo wákala yi kihwinya, twákuheka bya kunwa?
MAT 25:38 Khi tangwa twákumona, wákala munzenza amana twákuyamba, holo wákala khonga amana twákuvwatisa?
MAT 25:39 Amana khi tangwa twákumona wakala bela holo mu boloku, amana thwisa kutala?"
MAT 25:40 Kyamvu kabávutwala: "Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi: mbala zoosu zina lwásalabwa kwena mosi wa baphangi bama baba benina bakhunda, kwena meni lwásalabwa!"
MAT 25:41 «Hanga wuzimbudi hika kwena bana bakala ku koku dyandi dya kimama: "Katukenu haha, batu basingama! Alwenda kuna mbawu ya mvula yi mvula yina báyidika kikuma kya kiphidi-mutu yi banzyo bandi.
MAT 25:42 Mukuma, yíkala yi nzala kaasi lwáphekaku bya kudya, yíkala yi kihwinya kaasi lwáphekaku bya kunwa;
MAT 25:43 yíkala munzenza kaasi lwángyambaku; yíkala khonga kaasi lwámvwatisaku; yíkala wabela yi mu boloku kaasi lwáthalaku."
MAT 25:44 Hanga bawu phi bavutudi mu kuzimbula: "Pfumu, khi tangwa si twákumona ngeyi wákala yi nzala holo wákala yi kihwinya, holo munzenza, holo kikhonga, holo wabela, holo mu boloku amana twakonda kusadisa?"
MAT 25:45 Hanga wubavutwadi mu kuzonza: "Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa, mbala zoosu zina lwásadilabwoku kwena mosi wa baleki baba, lwásalabwoku phi kwena meni."
MAT 25:46 Amana baba bákwenda ku ndola ya mvula yi mvula, kaasi batu ba masonga, mu luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula.»
MAT 26:1 Tangwa kámanisa Yesu ndinga zazi zoosu, wuzimbudi kwena balonguki bandi:
MAT 26:2 «Luzayi ni kunima bilumbu byodi mukinzi wa phaki wakála: amana Mwana wa mutu bamúlambula ndangu bamukhoka ha kitakani.»
MAT 26:3 Hanga bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta bakutakani muna kyanzala kya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, wuna bakala tela ni Khayifu;
MAT 26:4 Bakasi kifwandu kya kumukwatisa Yesu mu kitsweki yi kumuhondisa.
MAT 26:5 Bakala zimbula: «Heku ni mu tangwa dya mukinzi, ndangu mvwalangani yikalaku ha kati dya batu.»
MAT 26:6 Yesu ku Betaniya kákala, muna nzu ya Simoni mukwa bwasi,
MAT 26:7 mukhetu mosi wisa bwesuka kwena Yesu, kákala yi mulangi wa mananasi ma thalu ya lawu amana wázunzilama hana mutwa wa yandi bwabuna kákala kuna mesa.
MAT 26:8 Amana balonguki buna bámona bwabuna, bámonaku kyesi, hanga bazimbudini: «Kikuma kya biki kuzanga kwa bwabu?
MAT 26:9 Bufwaniki basumbisama mu thalu ya lawu, amana mbongu bahanaza kwena batsukami!»
MAT 26:10 Kaasi Yesu buna kábakulabwa, wubazimbwadi: «Kikuma kya biki lubati muhekila phasi mukhetu yandu? Mukuma dyambu dya kitoku kasadi kwena meni;
MAT 26:11 mukuma batsukami lwakádiki bawu kosu tangwa, kaasi meni twakádikiku yenu kosu tangwa.
MAT 26:12 Yandi kanzunzidi mananasi mama mu lutu, ndangu katekila yidika kuzika kwama.
MAT 26:13 Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi: kuna basámuna Musamu wa Bukheti wawu, mu tsi yosu, baménikiki phi mambu mama kasadi yandu, kikuma kya kumubambuka yandi.»
MAT 26:14 Hanga mosi wa bawu kumi yi bodi, wuna bakala tela ni Yutasi Sikadyoti, wendi kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi
MAT 26:15 wuzimbudi: «Biki luzodi kupheka, amana meni yilulambwala yandi?» Hanga bawu bamufuti makuta makumatatu.
MAT 26:16 Amana tuka tangwa meni dina, kakala sanda tangwa dya mboti ndangu kamulambula Yesu.
MAT 26:17 Mu kilumbu kya theti kya mukinzi wa mapha makonda kisi dya muvimbu, balonguki bábwesuka kwena Yesu mu kuzimbula: «Ku biki wuzodi ni twakuyidikila madya ma mukinzi wa Phaki?»
MAT 26:18 Hanga yandi wuzimbudini: «Alwenda muna mbanza kwena mutu mosi, amana muzimbwalenu: "Mulongi kazimbudini: Tangwa dyama dibwesukini; ku nzu ya ngeyi yidila madya ma Phaki yi balonguki bama."»
MAT 26:19 Balonguki báhanga bwosu kabalongikila Yesu, amana báyidika madya ma Phaki.
MAT 26:20 Masikidika ha mábwa, ku mesa kákala yi bawu kumi yi bodi.
MAT 26:21 Amana buna bákala mu kudya, yandi wuzimbudi: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi: mosi mu kati dya benu kandámbula.»
MAT 26:22 Hanga báyuki kiwayi kya lawu, báyandika kumuhyula mosi kunima mukwawu: «Ka meni ku, Pfumu, kabwaku?»
MAT 26:23 Yandi, mu kuvutula, wuzimbudi: «Wuna wuvundiki koku ha longa dimosi yi meni, yandi wuna wandámbula.
MAT 26:24 Mwana wa mutu kabati kwenda, tala mana másonama kikuma kya yandi; kaasi khi kyadi kwena mutu wuna wulambudi Mwana wa mutu! Bwálunga ni mutu wuna kabutukaku kwandi!»
MAT 26:25 Amana mu kuvutula, Yutasi, wuna wámulambula wuzimbudi: «Ka meni ku, Mulongi, kabwaku?» Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Ngeyi meni wuzimbudibwa.»
MAT 26:26 Buna bakala dya, Yesu wábonga dipha, wásambuladya amana wábukunadya, wáhanadya kwena balonguki, amana wuzimbudi: «Bongenu, dyenu, lwalu lwena lutu lwa meni.»
MAT 26:27 Amana wábonga mbungu mosi, kunima dya kuvutula matondu, wábahekaya mu kuzonza: «Nwenuya benu boosu,
MAT 26:28 mukuma mama menina menga ma meni, ma bulunda bwa Nzambi, mana matyakani kikuma kya batu lawu mu kuloluka kwa masumu.
MAT 26:29 Amana yiluzimbwadi, mukyedika: tuka buthwena, yinwáku hika vinu dina, tii yi kuna kilumbu kina yinwádya ha kimosi yi benu muna Kipfumu kya Tata wama.»
MAT 26:30 Amana buna báyimbila mikunga mya mukinzi, bálubuka, benda ku mongu wa Olive.
MAT 26:31 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Benu boosu lwathína muna phipha yayi, mukuma tala mana másonama: "Yimúhonda kalema, amana kibuka kya mikoku kyamwángalakana."
MAT 26:32 Kaasi kunima kufutumuka kwama, yilútekidila kuna Ngadidi.»
MAT 26:33 Amana mu kuvutula, Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Yuka ni boosu bakútina, meni, ketibwe, yikútinaku.»
MAT 26:34 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Mu kyedika yikuzimbwadi: mu phipha yayi, khoku kakókulaku kedi, wáthuna mbala tatu.»
MAT 26:35 Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Keti kufwa, yifwa kumosi yi ngeyi, yikútunaku.» Balonguki boosu bazimbudi phi phila mosi.
MAT 26:36 Hanga Yesu wísa yi bawu, homa hamosi bisi tela ni Ngetisemani, amana wuzimbudi kwena balonguki bandi: «Zakalenu hahaha, kithama kina yikwenda lombila meni kuna.»
MAT 26:37 Wánata Phetelu yi bana ba Zebeteya bawu bodi, wáyandika kuyuka kyadi yi kiwayi.
MAT 26:38 Hanga wubazimbwadi: «Mbundu yama mu kiwayi yenina yi kuna lufwa; salenu haha, amana kalenu batokama kumosi yi meni.»
MAT 26:39 Wáhaluka koma, wáfukama, mbunzu mu mafu, mu kulombila yi kuzimbula: «Tata wama, yuka ni bwalendakana, khatwala bungu dyadi; salaku bwosu buna nzodi meni, kaasi bwosu wuzodi ngeyi.»
MAT 26:40 Tangwa kisa vutuka kwena balonguki, kábawana baleka; amana wuzimbudi kwena Phetelu: disongidila lulendiku kutokama keti tangwa dimosi kumosi yi meni?
MAT 26:41 Tokamenu, lombilenu phi, ndangu lubwaku mu kimeka. Kitembu kyazyama kyenina kaasi lutu lwalembwa lwenina.
MAT 26:42 Wáhaluka hika mbala ya zodi mu kulombila bwabu: «Tata wama, bufwaniku ni mbungu yayi ndwayoku, mbatanana buna, yambula luzolu lwaku lwasalama!»
MAT 26:43 Amana wisa vutuka hika, wubawani baleka, mukuma mesu ma bawu zitu mákala.
MAT 26:44 Yesu wábasisa, wáhaluka hika, wulombidi mbala ya tatu mu kulandulula ndinga meni zimosi.
MAT 26:45 Hanga wisi vutuka kwena balonguki amana wubazimbwadi: «Lunimbi hika, lulembwi kwenu! Talenu, tangwa dibwesuki, amana Mwana wa mutu bamulambudi ku moku ma basumuki.
MAT 26:46 Telamenu, thwendenu! Tala, wekina bela-bela wuna ndambudiki!»
MAT 26:47 Muna tangwa meni dina kakala zonza Yesu, Yutasi, mosi wa bawu kumi yi bodi wátula hakana, hakimosi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu bakala yi mbedi za vita yi khindi muna moku. Bwosu bábatuma kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba bayuta.
MAT 26:48 Amana wuna wámulambula, wábasongila kidimbu kimosi mu kuzimbula: «Wuna yibúmbakana, yandi wuna, mukwatenu.»
MAT 26:49 Amana buna kábwesuka kwena Yesu, wuzimbudini: «Mboti, Labuni!» Amana wámubumbakana.
MAT 26:50 Amana Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Mukwetu, kikuma kya dyambu dina wisidi, saladya.» Hanga buna bábwesuka, bamusimbi Yesu amana bamukwati.
MAT 26:51 Amana mosi wa bana bákala yi Yesu, wálubula mbedi ya phoku yandi, hanga wuhuti kutu dya musadi wa mbuta wa banganga Nzambi.
MAT 26:52 Hanga Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Vutula mbedi yaku ya phoku muna kilalu kyandi, mukuma boosu bana banwánina ku mbedi, ku mbedi phi bafwíla.
MAT 26:53 Kondilo wubanzi ni pfwaniku yimubokwadila Tata wama, amana kaphitika bibuka bya banzyo kuluta kumi yi bodi?
MAT 26:54 Abweti si malúngila Masonuku? Mana mabati zonza ni bulungi ni masalama bwabuna.»
MAT 26:55 Muna tangwa meni dina, Yesu wuzimbudi kwena milumba-lumba mya batu: «Lwisi khwata yi mbedi yi khindi, hanga wuna yenina ndwandwa? Kinga yikala zakala bilumbu byosu mu nzu ya Nzambi mu kulonga, amana lwákhwataku.
MAT 26:56 Kaasi mana moosu mabwini ndangu malungila Masonuku ma bambikudi.» Hanga balonguki boosu bamusisi, batini phi.
MAT 26:57 Bana buna bámukwata Yesu, bámunata ku nzu ya Khayifu, mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, kuna bákutakanina balongi ba mitsiku yi bambuta ba Bayuta.
MAT 26:58 Amana Phetelu, yandi, kakala landa muna kyana, yi kuna kyanzala kya mbuta kya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi. Amana buna kákota muna kati, wuzakadi yi batsinzidi ndangu kazaya buna mamánisina.
MAT 26:59 Amana bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku yi kimvuka kyambuta bakala sanda kimbangi kya mbi kikuma kya Yesu, ndangu bamuzengila mukanu wa lufwa.
MAT 26:60 Kaasi bámonaku, mbatanana lawu dya bambangi ba luvunu bisa funda, kaasi ku tsuka, bisa bwesuka bodi,
MAT 26:61 bazimbudi: «Yandu-yandu kakala zimbula: Pfwani yiwulumuna nzu ya Nzambi yayi, amana thunguludiya mu bilumbu bitatu."»
MAT 26:62 Amana mbuta wa banganga Nzambi buna kátelama, wázimbula kwena yandi: «Keti kima wubatiku vutula? Biki wuzonzi kikuma kya bimbangi byabi babati kufundila baba?»
MAT 26:63 Kaasi Yesu wádibata. Amana mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wumuzimbwadi: «Mu khumbu ya Nzambi wa moya mbati zenga, wátuzimbwala yuka ni ngeyi, wenina Kidisitu, Mwana wa Nzambi?»
MAT 26:64 Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Ngeyi meni wuzimbudibwa. Kaasi yiluzimbwadi hika: tuka buthwena, lwamúmona Mwana wa mutu wazakala kuna koku dya kitata dya Mukwa Ngolu zoosu yi mu kukwisa hana thandu ya matuti ma zilu.»
MAT 26:65 Hanga mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wuyati miledi myandi, amana wuzimbudi: «Nzambi kabati tukwana! Kikuma kya biki twasósila hika bambangi? Talenu buthwena luyuki benu-benu ngusi;
MAT 26:66 Abweti lubanzi benu?» Amana boosu mu kuvutula, bazimbudi: «Bulombi kafwa.»
MAT 26:67 Hanga bamuhumi metya kuna mbunzu yandi amana bamuti makufi bahika phi bamuti mbata,
MAT 26:68 mu kuzonza: «Bikuleti, kamba ngeyi Kidisitu wenina, keti nati wukubeti!»
MAT 26:69 Phetelu kákala wazakala kuna phenza, hana kyanzala. Amana musadi wa mukhetu mosi wábwesuka kwena yandi mu kuzimbula: «Ngeyi phi, wákala yi Yesu, mwisi Ngadidi.»
MAT 26:70 Kaasi yandi wátuna ku thwala ya batu boosu, mu kuzimbula: «Nzayimoku mana wubati zimbula.»
MAT 26:71 Buna kakala kwenda kuna mwelu wa kyanzala, wumoni hika musadi wahika wa mukhetu amana yandu-yandu wuzimbudi kwena bakwawu: «Yandu phi kákadikini yi Yesu mwisi Nazaleti.»
MAT 26:72 Amana wutuni hika yi ndefi: «Yimuzayiku mutu yandu.»
MAT 26:73 Kunima dya mwana tangwa, bábwesuka batu bákala hana, bazimbudi kwena Phetelu: «Mu kyedika, ngeyi wenina phi mosi hana kati dya bawu; mukuma nzonzidi yaku yibatibwa songila mboti-mboti.»
MAT 26:74 Hanga Phetelu wuyandiki kudya ndefi: «Yukani meni yimuzayi mutu yandu, Nzambi kapheka ndola!» Amana muna tangwa meni dina, khoku mosi wákokula,
MAT 26:75 Amana Phetelu wáyubuka ndinga yina ya Yesu: «Ku thwala ya kukokula kwa khoku, mbala tatu wathúna meni.» Amana wálubuka, wádila phi lawu.
MAT 27:1 Kuma buna kwakhya, lukutakanu lwásalama, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi boosu yi bambuta Bayuta bákasa fwongu kikuma kya Yesu ndangu bamuhondisa.
MAT 27:2 Amana buna bámukasa, bámunata, bámulambula kwena Philatu, kilolu mwisi Loma.
MAT 27:3 Hanga buna kámona Yutasi, wuna wámulambula, ni bamuzengidi lufwa, wázosuluka, wávutula makuta makumatatu kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta.
MAT 27:4 Wubazimbwadi: «Tsumuki mu kulambula menga ma mutu wakonda sala mbi.» Bawu bazimbudi: «Khi mambu ngeyi yi betu! Makutadi ngeyi meni!»
MAT 27:5 Amana buna kálosa makuta meni mana muna nzu ya Nzambi, wenda, amana wádikudika.
MAT 27:6 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi buna bátonguna makuta meni mana, bazimbudi: «Bulombiku kutimbulama mu sanduku dya nzu ya Nzambi, kikuma thalu ya menga.»
MAT 27:7 Lukutakanu buna lwásalama, makuta mana básumbilama kilanga kya mutu wuna wakala bumba nzungu za tuma, kikuma kya mazyamu ma banzenza.
MAT 27:8 Ihana bátedilakya, «Kilanga kya menga» yi lelu dyadi.
MAT 27:9 Hanga malungidi mana mázonzama mu nzila ya mbikudi Yelemiya: «Bábonga makuta makumatatu, yena thalu yina bázenga bana ba Kiseledi kikuma kya yandi;
MAT 27:10 Hanga bahanima kikuma kya kilanga kya wuna wisi bumba nzungu, bwosu kátsilabwa yandi meni Pfumu.»
MAT 27:11 Yesu buna kákala ku thwala ya Philatu, hanga wumuhyudi: «Ngeyi, kyamvu wa Bayuta wena?» Amana Yesu wuvutudi: «Ngeyi meni wuzimbudibwa.»
MAT 27:12 Kaasi mu tangwa dina bakala mufunda kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta, Yesu kávutulaku kima.
MAT 27:13 Hanga Philatu wumuzimbwadi: «Wubatiku yuka mambu moosu mana babati zonza kikuma kya ngeyi?»
MAT 27:14 Kaasi kávutulaku ndinga keti mu dyambu dimosi, hanga Philatu yituki lawu.
MAT 27:15 Bwosu bwákala mu mukinzi wosu, Philatu kakala yambwadila mutu wa boloku mosi kikuma kya mulumba-lumba wa batu, wosu wuna bakala lomba.
MAT 27:16 Kinga, muna tangwa dina, kwákala yi mutu wa boloku mosi watoma zayakana, khumbu yandi [Yesu] Balabasi.
MAT 27:17 Bwosu bákala bakutakana, hanga Philatu wubahyudi: «Nati luzodi yiluyambwadila, [Yesu] Balabasi ho Yesu yandi bisi tela Kidisitu?»
MAT 27:18 Mukuma wázaya kwandi ni kikuma kya kiphala bámulambwala.
MAT 27:19 Amana buna kázakala ha kiti kya nganda, mukhetu wandi wumutumini ndinga: «Wukotaku mambu ma mutu wa masonga wuna, mukuma lelu, phasi lawu mboni mu ndosi, kikuma kya yandi.»
MAT 27:20 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta bálwengisa milumba-lumba mya batu ndangu balomba Balabasi, amana bámuhondisa Yesu.
MAT 27:21 Amana mu kuvutula, Philatu wubahyudi: «Nati, mu kati dya bawu bodi luzodi ni yiluyambwadila?» Bawu bavutudi: «Balabasi!»
MAT 27:22 Philatu wábazimbwala: «Abweti si yimúhanga Yesu yandi bisi tela Kidisitu?» Boosu bavutudi: «Mukhoka ha kitakani!»
MAT 27:23 Yandi wávutwakila: «Kikuma kya khi mbi kasadi?» Kaasi bawu báyandika kukalunga ngolu mu kuzimbula: «Bamukhoka ha kitakani.»
MAT 27:24 Amana Philatu buna kámona ni heku kima kahanga, kaasi bwosu yálutakana mvwalangani, hanga wubongi mamba, wásukula moku kuna thwala ya mulumba-lumba wa batu, mu kuzonza: «Nzayiku dyambu ditadidi menga mama; benu, malutadi benu-benu!»
MAT 27:25 Amana mu kuvutula, batu boosu bázimbula: «Menga mandi makala hana thandu ya betu yi bana betu!»
MAT 27:26 Hanga wubalubwadi Balabasi; amana Yesu buna kamubetisa fimbu, wumulambudi ndangu bamukhoka ha kitakani.
MAT 27:27 Hanga baphumbulu ba Philatu bamubulumuni Yesu yi muna nganda ya yandi Philatu, amana bákhokika kibuka kya baphumbulu.
MAT 27:28 Bámuwomuna miledi, bámuvwatisa muzaka wumosi wa kabengi.
MAT 27:29 Bátunga mukhonzi wumosi wa tsaku, bámuvwatisaya kuna mutwa yi muswangina kuna koku dya kitata, amana, bwosu báfukama ku thwala ya yandi, bakala museya mu kuzimbula: «Mboti, kyamvu wa Bayuta!»
MAT 27:30 Bakala muhuma metya bábonga muswangina amana beka muzyatula muna mutwa.
MAT 27:31 Kunima dya kumuseya, bámukatulawa muzaka wuna, bámuvwatisa hika miledi myandi, amana bámunata ndangu benda mukhoka ha kitakani.
MAT 27:32 Mu kulubuka, bátundakana mutu mosi, mwisi Sileni, khumbu yandi Simoni; hanga bamulundiki ndangu kanata kitakani kya Yesu.
MAT 27:33 Bátula homa hana bisi tela ni Ngolungota, disongidila: «Kizika kya Kibelengenzi kya mutwa.»
MAT 27:34 Bamuheki kunwa vinu dya kubundikisa yi kisi dya khadi; buna káyedika, kázolaku kunwa.
MAT 27:35 Kunima dya kumukhoka ha kitakani, baphumbulu bákabana miledi myandi mu kubetilamya zeki.
MAT 27:36 Kunima, bázakala hahana mu kumutanikina.
MAT 27:37 Amana báthetika hana thandu ya mutwa wandi bisona bina byákala tendula kikuma kya lufwa lwandi: «Yandu kenina Yesu, kyamvu wa Bayuta.»
MAT 27:38 Hanga bakhokini hana kitakani bandwandwa bodi ha kimosi yi yandi, mosi ku koku dya kitata, mukwawu ku koku dya kimama.
MAT 27:39 Bana bákala mu kuluta, bákala mutukwana yi kunikisaka mutwa mya bawu;
MAT 27:40 amana bazimbudi: «Ngeyi wakala zimbula ni wawúlumuna nzu ya Nzambi amana mu bilumbu bitatu watúngululaya, dihulula ngeyi meni, yuka ni Mwana wa Nzambi wenina, amana tuluka ha kitakani!»
MAT 27:41 Phila mosi phi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku yi bambuta ba Bayuta bakala museya yi kuzonzaka:
MAT 27:42 «Batu bahika kakala hulula, kafwaniku kudihulula yandi meni! Kyamvu wa Kiseledi kenina: katuluka buthwena bwabu ha kitakani amana twakwikila mwena yandi.
MAT 27:43 Kakala dihana kwena Nzambi, buthwena, kamuhulula yuka ni kisi muzola; mukuma kakala zimbula: "Mwana wa Nzambi yenina"!»
MAT 27:44 Amana phila mosi yi bandwandwa bana bámukhoka bawu ha kitakani bákala mutukwana.
MAT 27:45 Tuka tangwa dya tsinzi, phipha yábwa mu tsi yina yosu tii yi kuna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika.
MAT 27:46 Amana bela-bela yi tangwa tatu dya masikidika, Yesu wákalunga mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Diya, Diya, lema sabakatani?» Disongidila: «Nzambi wama, Nzambi wama, kikuma kya biki wungyambwadidi?»
MAT 27:47 Amana bahika, mu kati dya bana bákala hakana, buna báyuka, bazimbudi: «Diya, kabati tela yandu.»
MAT 27:48 Mosi muna kati dya bawu, wenda thinu, wábonga kitini kya dinyuka, wávundikikya muna vinu dya ngani, amana wákasadya ku miti, kamuheka yandi ndangu kanwa.
MAT 27:49 Kaasi bahika bakala zimbula: «Yambulenu, twatala kamba Diya kakwisa muhulula hahana!»
MAT 27:50 Amana Yesu wákalunga hika mu ndinga ya ngolu, wátabula moya.
MAT 27:51 Kutala muledi wa zitu wuna wakala kabisa kizika kyahedila yi kina kyákala kyahedila lawu mu nzu ya Nzambi wuyatukini mu byati byodi tuka ku londi yi kuna banda. Amana mafu mánikana, matadi phi máyatuka,
MAT 27:52 mazyamu másabuka, bamvumbi ba lawu ba batu ba Nzambi báfutumuka.
MAT 27:53 Bálubuka mu mazyamu, kunima dya lufutumuku lwa Yesu, bákota mu Yelusalemi, mbanza yatoma amana bádimonikisa kwena batu ba lawu.
MAT 27:54 Satudiyoni yi bana bakala kengila bawu Yesu, buna bámona ni mafu manikani yi mambu mana máluta; báyuka bweya bwa lawu, bazimbudi: «Mu kyedika, yandu Mwana wa Nzambi kákadi!»
MAT 27:55 Amana hákala hakana bakhetu balawu, babana bámusindikila Yesu tukidila ku Ngadidi mu kumusadila, bakala tala kuna kyana.
MAT 27:56 Ha kati dya bawu, hákala Madiya mwisi Makatala yi Madiya ngudi wa Zyaki yi Yozefu yi ngudi wa bana ba Zebeteya.
MAT 27:57 Masikidika ha mábwa, wisa tula mvwama mosi, mwisi Adimate, khumbu yandi Yozefu, wuna wákala phi mulonguki wa Yesu.
MAT 27:58 Wenda kwena Philatu, wálomba lutu lwa Yesu. Hanga Philatu wáhana muswa ni bamuhekalwa.
MAT 27:59 Amana Yozefu wábonga lutu lwa Yesu, wávungalwa ha muledi wa pha,
MAT 27:60 wásikulalwa muna mazyamu mandi ma pha mana kásima muna ditadi, amana buna kábundumuna kalunga tadi ku mwelu wa mazyamu, wenda kwandi.
MAT 27:61 Madiya mwisi Makatala yi Madiya wuna mukwawu, hana bákala, bazakala kuna thwala ya mazyamu.
MAT 27:62 Kilumbu kyalanda kifwani. Kyákala ku manima ma kilumbu kina bakala yidikila sabata, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi Bafwadisi bákutakana kuna nzu ya Philatu
MAT 27:63 mu kuzimbula: «Mbuta-mutu, tubati bambuka ni mukwa bukamvi wuna, buna kákala wa moya, kázimbula: "Kunima bilumbu bitatu, yifútumuka."
MAT 27:64 Disongidila ni senda bakengidila mboti-mboti mazyamu yi kuna kilumbu kya tatu, kondi lo, balonguki bandi bisa muyiba nana. Hanga bahuna kwena batu: "Wufutumuki ku bafwa." Holoni, bukamvi bwabu bwa tsuka bwalúta buna bwa theti.»
MAT 27:65 Philatu wubazimbwadi: «Talenu baba baphumbulu; ba kitshinzidi. Alwendenu, kengidilenu mboti-mboti mazyamu bwosu luzodidi.»
MAT 27:66 Hanga bendi, mu kukengila mboti-mboti, basya kidimbu kuna tadi dina dyákala fidinga mazyamu amana básisa batsinzidi.
MAT 28:1 Kunima dya sabata, muna suka-suka dya kilumbu kya theti kya phosa, Madiya mwisi Makatala yi Madiya wuna mukwawu benda tala mazyamu.
MAT 28:2 Kutala mafu manikani ngolu; mukuma wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wákulumuka ku zilu, wisa bundumuna tadi amana kákala wazakala hana thandu ya dyawu.
MAT 28:3 Kifwani kyandi kyakala kedyamina hanga mitsyenzya, miledi myandi myákala mya phembi ya lawu.
MAT 28:4 Kikuma kya bwabuna, batsinzidi báyuka bweya bwa lawu. Bakala tekita amana bákituka hanga batu bafwa.
MAT 28:5 Mu kutambula ndinga, wanzyo wázimbula kwena bakhetu: «Lukalaku yi bweya, benu, mukuma nzayi ni Yesu wuna bákhoka ha kitakani lubati sanda;
MAT 28:6 keku haha, wufutumukini bwosu kázimbula. Alwisa, talenu homa hana kakadikini walandalala.
MAT 28:7 Alwenda tswatsu, zimbulenu kwena balonguki bandi: "Wufutumuki ha kati dya bafwa, amana tala wulutekididi kedi mu Ngadidi; kwakuna lwámumona." Tala, mana khádiki mawu mu kuluzimbwala.»
MAT 28:8 Amana bákatuka tswatsu ku mazyamu, bákala bazakama yi kitswi yi kyesi kya lawu amana bakhetu benda thinu kusamuna kwena balonguki bandi.
MAT 28:9 Kutala, Yesu wisi batundakana mu kuzimbula: «Kimboti kyenu!» Bawu bábwesuka, bámubumbakana muna malu mu kumufukamina.
MAT 28:10 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Lukalaku yi bweya. Alwenda, samunenu kwena baphangi bama ni benda kuna Ngadidi: amana bangwána kwakuna.»
MAT 28:11 Tangwa bakala mu nzila, ndambu ya batshinzidi ba mazyamu, bisa mu mbanza, basamuni kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi moosu mosu mana máluta.
MAT 28:12 Buna bákutakana yi bambuta ba Bayuta, lukutakanu lwásalama: bábonga lukanu, amana bahana mbongu za lawu kwena baphumbulu
MAT 28:13 mu kuzimbula: «Zimbulenu: "Balonguki bandi bisi muyibaka muna phipha, bwosu tukadiki betu banimba."
MAT 28:14 Amana yuka ni kilolu mwisi Loma kayukabwa, betu twamúlembika, ndangu benu baluyangisaku.»
MAT 28:15 Batsinzidi bátambula mbongu, báhanga bwosu bábazimbwala. Amana ndinga yayi yámwangana kwena Bayuta tii yi kuna lelu dyadi.
MAT 28:16 Balonguki kumi yi mosi benda ku Ngadidi, kuna mongu wuna kábazimbwala Yesu ni benda.
MAT 28:17 Tangwa bámumona, báfukama, kaasi bahika bákala yi keti-keti.
MAT 28:18 Yesu wábwesuka, wuzimbudi kwena bawu: «Kipfumu kyosu báphekakya muna zilu yi ha tsi.
MAT 28:19 Disongidila alwendenu, kitulenu batu ba makanda moosu balonguki bama; babotikenu mu khumbu ya Tata yi ya Mwana yi Kitembu Kyatoma;
MAT 28:20 balongenu mu kusadila moosu mana yilulongikidi. zayenubwoku, meni yenina yi benu bilumbu byosu tii yi kuna tsuka ya tsi.»
MAR 1:1 Luyandiku lwa Musamu wa Bukheti wa Yesu Kidisitu, Mwana wa Nzambi
MAR 1:2 bwosu bwásonama mwena Mbikudi Yesaya: «Phitikini mbambala wama ku thwala ya ngeyi, kikuma kya kukuyidika nzila.
MAR 1:3 Yi yandi wuna wubati kalunga muna nganga: Yidikenu nzila ya Pfumu, sungikenu mikinda myandi.»
MAR 1:4 Bwabuna kálubuka Yowani, kakala botika muna nganga, amana weka longa mbotika ya kusoba bikalulu kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu.
MAR 1:5 Bisi kinzunga kya Yuteya boosu yi bisi Yelusalemi boosu bakala kwenda kwakuna kwena yandi amana bakala tambula mbotika kwena yandi, muna Yolutani, yi kufungunaka masumu ma bawu.
MAR 1:6 Yowani kákala wavwata muledi wa mwika mya kamela yi mukaba wa tsibu muna mbunda; kakala dya baphasu yi bwiki bwa mu tseki.
MAR 1:7 Kakala longa: «Kabati kwisa kuna manima ma meni, wuna wenina yi ngolu kuluta meni; amana kutu meni ndungiku mu kuzenzama amana yikutumuna musinga wa tsabatu zandi.
MAR 1:8 Meni yikala lubotika mu mamba, kaasi yandi kakwisa lubotika mu Kitembu Kyatoma.»
MAR 1:9 Muna bilumbu meni bina Yesu kátuka ku Nazaleti, hata dya Ngadidi, hanga bamubotiki kwena Yowani muna Yolutani.
MAR 1:10 Buna kálubuka Yesu mu mamba, kámona zilu dikanguki yi Kitembu Kyatoma kukulumuka kwena yandi hanga yembi.
MAR 1:11 Ndinga yáyukalakana kuna zilu: «Ngeyi wenina Mwana wama watondama; mwena ngeyi tsini kyesi kyama.»
MAR 1:12 Muna tangwa meni dina, Kitembu wámunatisa mu nganga.
MAR 1:13 Kánanga bilumbu makumaya muna nganga, bisa muleya kwena Satana. Kakala zinga kumosi yi bambisi ba mu tseki; amana banzyo bakala musadila.
MAR 1:14 Kunima dya kumukwatisa Yowani mu boloku, Yesu wísa kuna Ngadidi, kakala longa Musamu wa Bukheti wa Nzambi.
MAR 1:15 Kakala zimbula: «Tangwa difwani amana Kipfumu kya Nzambi kibwesukini! Balumunenu mbundu amana kwikilenu mu Musamu wa Bukheti!»
MAR 1:16 Buna kakala luta muna kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta dya Ngadidi, wámona Simoni yi Andele, phangi wa Simoni, bakala timbula wanda dya bawu muna yanga, mukuma balobi bákala.
MAR 1:17 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Ndandenu amana yilukitula balobi ba batu.»
MAR 1:18 Muna mbala mosi, básisa mawanda ma bawu amana benda mulanda.
MAR 1:19 Buna káphusana ndambu, wámona Zyaki, mwana wa Zebeteya, yi phangi wandi Yowani, bákala phi muna masuwa ma bawu, beka yidika mawanda.
MAR 1:20 Muna mbala mosi wábatela; bámusisa tata wa bawu Zebeteya muna masuwa yi basadi bandi, amana bámulanda.
MAR 1:21 Bákota mu Kaphedinawuma. Muna kilumbu kya sabata, wákota muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta amana wáyandika mu kulonga.
MAR 1:22 Bakala yituka kikuma kya malongi mandi; mukuma kakala longa hanga mutu wenina yi hamu, heku ni hanga balongi ba mitsiku.
MAR 1:23 Kinga muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta meni yina, mwákala yi mutu mosi wákala yi kitembu kya mbi, hanga wukalungini:
MAR 1:24 «Kikuma kya biki wudikotisidini mu mambu ma betu, Yesu mwisi Nazaleti? Wisini ndangu watuzanga? Nzayi mboti nani ngeyi wenina: Watoma bátuma kwena Nzambi!»
MAR 1:25 Yesu wákayakya, mu kuzimbula: «Dibata amana lubuka mwena mutu yandu!»
MAR 1:26 Kitembu kya mbi kyálubuka mwena yandi mu kumuningisa ngolu yi kukalunga ngolu.
MAR 1:27 Boosu báyituka lawu; bakala dihyula bawu yi bawu: «Biki byabi? Malongi mapha, yi hamu dyosu! Kabati senda kwena bitembu bya mbi, amana bibati mulemvukila!»
MAR 1:28 Amana khululuka yandi yámwangana yi tswatsu muna kinzunga kya Ngadidi kyosu.
MAR 1:29 Mu kulubuka mu nzu ya kimvuka ya bayuta, wénda ha kimosi yi Zyaki yi Yowani ku nzu ya Simoni yi Andele.
MAR 1:30 Buko bwa mukhetu bwa Simoni, walandalala kákala hana thangi, kikhafuma kákala kyawu; muna mbala mosi, bámumenikina yandi Yesu.
MAR 1:31 Yandi wábwesuka amana wumusimbini kuna koku, wumutelamisini phi; kikhafuma kimuhwini, amana wuyandikini mu kubaheka madya.
MAR 1:32 Masikidika ha mábwa, kunima kuzyoka kwa tangwa, bakala munatina bambefu boosu yi bakwa bitembu bya mbi.
MAR 1:33 Mbanza yosu yákhokana kuna thwala ya mwelu wa nzu.
MAR 1:34 Kábelula bambefu balawu bakala bela maladi ma mutindu yi mutindu amana wákukwasa bitembu bya mbi byalawu; Kákalaku sisa tangwa ni bitembu bya mbi byayakula, kikuma byákala muzaya keti nati kákala.
MAR 1:35 Muna suka, bwosu kwákala phipha, Yesu wátokama, wálubuka ndangu kenda ku phungamu amana kwakuna kikuma kya kulombila.
MAR 1:36 Simoni yi bana kákala bawu benda musanda;
MAR 1:37 Tangwa bámusengumuna, bamuzimbwadini: «Boosu babati kusanda.»
MAR 1:38 Yandi wubavutwadini: «Thwendenu kuma kwahika, muna mahata ma kinzunga, ndangu kwakuna phi yisamuna musamu; kikuma kya bwabuna yisidikini.»
MAR 1:39 Amana wénda muna kinzunga kya Ngadidi kyosu; mu kusamuna musamu muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta za bawu yi kukukwasaka bitembu bya mbi.
MAR 1:40 Mukwa bwasi mosi wísa kwena Yesu, wáfukama amana wámubokwadila: «Yuka ni wuzodibwa, fwani watsemisa.»
MAR 1:41 Yesu yi kiwayi kyosu, wálambula koku, wámusimba amana wuzimbudini: «Nzodibwa, sema!»
MAR 1:42 Muna mbala mosi, bwasi bwámuwaluka; wásema.
MAR 1:43 Yesu wámukebisa, wámulubula
MAR 1:44 mu kuzimbula: «Dikenga mu kumenika kwena mutu. Kaasi ndawenda disongila kwena nganga Nzambi, amana tambika kabu dyaku kikuma kya kudisemisa kwaku bwosu kálongabwa Moyize; kyakála kimbangi kikuma kya bawu.»
MAR 1:45 Kaasi yandi, buna kenda, wáyandika mu kumenika mambu mana mámubwila kwena batu mu ndinga ya ngolu yi kikesa yi kuyadingisaka Ndinga mu phila ni Yesu kálendaku hika mu kukota buna bufwani keti mu mbanza yimosi. Kákala watelama kuna phenza, kuna phungamu, amana bakala tuka tselu yi tselu yi kwisaka kwena yandi.
MAR 2:1 Kunima ndambu ya bilumbu, Yesu wávutuka ku Kafadinawumi. Báyuka ni kuna nzu kenina.
MAR 2:2 Amana háwongama thalu ya lawu dya batu, kwásalaku keti homa, keti ku thwala ya mwelu. Kakala balonga Ndinga.
MAR 2:3 Hákala hana kati dya bawu yi batu bisa mu kunata kiwokoku mosi bátikula kwena batu baya.
MAR 2:4 Bwosu bakalaku lenda mu kumutudisa kwena Yesu, kikuma kya mulumba-lumba wa batu, bálungula hana thandu ya mudilu wa nzu yina kákala amana báyidika hundu hahana, bákulumuna kiphoyu kina kákala walandalala kiwokoku.
MAR 2:5 Mu kumona lukwikilu lwa bawu, Yesu wázimbula kwena kiwokoku: «Mwana wama, masumu maku makulolukini.»
MAR 2:6 Hákala hakana yi ndambu ya balongi ba mitsiku, bazakala, bekina dizonzila muna mbundu za bawu meni:
MAR 2:7 «Kikuma kya biki kabati zonzila bwabuna? Nzambi kabati sawula? Nani wufwani kulolula masumu, yuka ni ka yandi meni ku Nzambi lwesi?»
MAR 2:8 Muna mbala mosi, Yesu wábakula, muna kitembu kyandi, mabanza bákala mawu; wubazimbwadini: «Kikuma kya biki lwenina yi mabanza ma bwabuna?
MAR 2:9 Biki byakonda kala phasi, mu kuzimbula kwena kiwokoku: "Masumu maku makulolukini" ho mu kuzimbula: "Telama, bonga thangi yaku amana kangala"?
MAR 2:10 Kaasi bulungi, ndangu lwazayabwa ni Mwana wa mutu kenina yi hamu dya kulolula masumu ha tsi.» Wuzimbudi kwena kiwokoku:
MAR 2:11 «Yikuzimbwadibwa, telema, bonga thangi yaku, amana vutuka ku nzu yaku.»
MAR 2:12 Muna mbala mosi, mutu wuna wátelama, wábonga thangi yandi, wálubuka kuna thwala ya batu boosu, amana báyituka lawu, boosu bakala zatula Nzambi mu kuzimbula: «Khaniku tumona kedi dyambu dya mutindu wawu!»
MAR 2:13 Yesu wálubuka hika ku kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta; mulumba-lumba wa batu wosu wakala kwisa kwena yandi, amana kakala balonga.
MAR 2:14 Mu kuhita, wámona Lefi, mwana wa yakala wa Alufwe, wazakala hana mesa ma kisalu. Wumuzimbwadini: «Ndanda!» Yandu-yandu wátelema amana wámulanda.
MAR 2:15 Bwosu kákala ku mesa kuna nzu ya Lefi, tulaki twa phaku lawu yi basumuki bákala hana mesa hakimosi yi Yesu yi balonguki bandi, mukuma lawu bákala mu kumulanda.
MAR 2:16 Balongi ba mitsiku ba bafwadisi buna bámumona mu kudya hakimosi yi bakalaki ka phaku yi basumuki, beka zimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Kikuma kya biki kabati dila homa hamosi yi bakalaki ba phaku yi basumuki?»
MAR 2:17 Kinga Yesu wáyuka, hanga wubazimbwadini: «Kabanaku benina bakola mu lutu bisi vwa mupfunu wa munganga, kaasi bambefu. Yísaku tela batu ba masonga, kaasi basumuki.»
MAR 2:18 Balonguki ba Yowani yi bafwadisi bakala zila kudya. Batu bahika bisa zimbula kwena Yesu: «Kikuma kya biki balonguki ba ngeyi bisiku zila bawu, kinga balonguki ba Yowani yi balonguki ba bafwadisi bisi zila madya?»
MAR 2:19 Yesu wávutula: «Banduku ba kikwedi bafwani kuzila madya mu tangwa dina kenina kikwedi hakimosi yi bawu, ku mukinzi wa longu? Tangwa dyosu dina kakála kikwedi hakimosi yi bawu, balendaku kuzila madya.»
MAR 2:20 Bilumbu byakwísa bina babákatula yandi kikwedi; hahana nana bazíla kudya, muna kilumbu meni kina.
MAR 2:21 «Heku mutu wisi londa kitemba kya muledi wa pha yi muledi wakhulu; kondilo kitemba kya pha kyayáta muledi wuna wakhulu, amana kuyatuka kwa muledi kwakala kwalawu.
MAR 2:22 Amana kweku mutu wisi longulula vinu dya pha mu bilungu bya khulu; kondilo vinu dyabúla bilungu, yi vinu yi bilungu bizangani; vinu dya pha, difwani mu bilungu bya pha!»
MAR 2:23 Buna kakala hita muna bilanga bya bule kilumbu kimosi kya sabata, balonguki bandi, báyandika kuhela misambu myandi, kinzila-nzila.
MAR 2:24 Bafwadisi bamuzimbwadini: «Tala, kikuma kya biki babati hangila mambu mana mafwaniku kuhanga mu kilumbu kya sabata?»
MAR 2:25 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Benu lwatangaku mambu káhanga Tavidi, tangwa kákala yi lungwa amana wáyuka nzala, yandi yi bana kákala bawu?
MAR 2:26 Bwosu kákota muna kikumbu kya Nzambi mu tangwa dina kákala Abyatadi mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, wádya mapha ma mulambu. Kinga bulombi ni banganga Nzambi lwesi balendama dya, amana wábahekama phi ndambu bana kákala bawu.»
MAR 2:27 Amana wubazimbwadini: «Sabata básaladya kikuma kya mutu, kaasi mutu káhangamaku kikuma kya sabata.
MAR 2:28 Yihana ni Mwana wa mutu kenina kibeni pfumu wa kilumbu sabata.»
MAR 3:1 Yesu wávutuka hika ku nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta. Kwákala kwakuna yi mutu mosi wákala yi koku dyawokumuka.
MAR 3:2 Batu bakala musimbulula Yesu mu kuzaya kinga kamubelula mu kilumbu kya sabata, balenga mufunda
MAR 3:3 Hanga wuzimbudini kwena mutu wuna wákala yi koku dyawokumuka: «Telama hana, ha kati.»
MAR 3:4 Kunima wubazimbwadini: «Biki bilungi mu kusala mu kilumbu kya sabata? Kusala mboti ho mbi? Kuhulula luzingu lwa mutu ho kuzanga?» Kaasi báhwena talala.
MAR 3:5 Hanga wubatadini boosu yi khabu; mu kiwayi kikuma kya mbundu ya ngolu ya bawu. Wuzimbudini kwena mutu wuna: «Yuna koku dyaku.» Wáyunadya, amana koku dyandi dyátoma.
MAR 3:6 Buna bálubuka, bafwadisi, benda kutakana yi bakwa kibuka kya Eloti kikuma kya yandi, kikuma kya kusanda phila yina bamúhondisila.
MAR 3:7 Yesu wenda hunga ku bela-bela yi yanga dya mbuta kumosi yi balonguki bandi. Mulumba-lumba wa batu lawu bámulanda. Bátuka ku kinzunga kya Ngadidi, ku kinzunga Yuteya,
MAR 3:8 ku Yelusalemi, ku kinzunga kya Yitumeya kuna Sambwa dya Yolutani dya kinzunga kya Tidi yi Sitoni. Batu balawu meni bana, bisa kwena yandi mukuma báyuka moosu mana kakala hanga.
MAR 3:9 Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi ni bamuyidikila masuwa mamosi, ndangu mulumba-lumba wa batu wumulundikisaku.
MAR 3:10 Mukuma, bwosu kakala belula batu balawu, boosu bana bákala yi makhasi bakala dilosa kwena yandi ndangu bamusimba.
MAR 3:11 Bitembu bya mbi, tangwa byákala mumona, bakala bwa kuna thwala ya yandi amana bakala kalunga: «Ngeyi wenina Mwana wa Nzambi!»
MAR 3:12 Kaasi yandi wákandisabya ni bamenikaku kwena batu keti nati kenina yandi.
MAR 3:13 Yesu wátombuka ku mongu; wátela bana kázola amana bisa kwena yandi.
MAR 3:14 Kumi yi bodi kábasola, babana káheka khumbu ya bathumwa, ndangu bakala hakimosi yi yandi amana kábatuma mu kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti,
MAR 3:15 yi hamu dya kukukwasila bitembu bya mbi.
MAR 3:16 Kábasola bawu kumi yi bodi: Simoni wuna káheka khumbu ya Phetelu,
MAR 3:17 Zyaki, mwana wa Zebeteya yi Yowani phangi wa Zyaki, kwena bawu káhana khumbu ya Bowanedizi, disongidila: «Mwana wa mubandanu»
MAR 3:18 Andele, Fidiphu, Batolomi, Mathayi, Toma, Zyaki, mwana Alufwe, Thati yi Simoni mwisi kibuka kya bana bisi nwanina diphanda,
MAR 3:19 yi Yutasi Sikadyoti wuna wámulambula Yesu.
MAR 3:20 Kunima, Yesu wávutuka kuna nzu, amana mulumba-lumba wa batu wákhokama hika, mu mutindu wumosi ni bawu balendaku keti kudya.
MAR 3:21 Buna báyuka bwabuna, biwutu byandi bénda ni bamubonga, mukuma bakala zimbula: «Kabatiku dizaya hika!»
MAR 3:22 Balongi ba mitsiku bana bátuka ku Yelusalemi bakala zimbula: «Belezebula kenina yandi, mu ngolu za pfumu wa bitembu bya mbi kisi kukwasila bitembu bya mbi!»
MAR 3:23 Yesu wábatela amana wáyandika mu kubazimbwala mu bingana: «Abweti Satana kalenda kukwasa Satana?
MAR 3:24 Honi kipfumu kimosi kyadikabisa kyawu meni, kipfumu meni kina kyazíluka;
MAR 3:25 amana honi nzu yimosi yadikabisa yawu-meni, nzu meni yina yaléndaku hika kuzyama.
MAR 3:26 Amana yuka ni Satana kadinwanisa yandi meni, wa kudikabisa kenina amana kazyamaku, yimeni wukulukini kwandi.
MAR 3:27 «Ka mutu ku wakóta mu nzu ya yakala-phandi ndangu kamuyiba bima byandi konda katekila mukasa yakala-phandi wuna; amana kunima kalunga tambula byosu mu nzu yandi.
MAR 3:28 Abwabuna yiluzimbwadini: Moosu kalólulama kwena bana ba batu, masumu yi ngusi zina bahitikisini.
MAR 3:29 Kaasi wosu wuna wulewudi Kitembu Kyatoma, kalendaku tambula ndoluka, mukuma wuhodi disumu dimosi dya mvula yi mvula.»
MAR 3:30 Yesu kakala bazonzila bwabuna kikuma bakala zimbula: «Kitembu kya mbi kenina kyawu.»
MAR 3:31 Ngudi wa Yesu yi baphangi bandi batudini. Batelamikini hana phenza, bamutedisini.
MAR 3:32 Batu balawu bakala bazakala mu kabeta ka yandi amana bamuzimbwadini: «Ngudi waku yi baphangi baku ba bayakala yi baphangi baku ba bakhetu ha nzila benina, amana babati kusanda.»
MAR 3:33 Yesu wuvutudi: «Banati ngudi wama yi baphangi bama?»
MAR 3:34 Kunima, wásimbulula kwena babana bákala bazakala mu kabeta ka yandi, wuzimbudini: «Talenu: ngudi wama yi baphangi bama.
MAR 3:35 Kikuma, wosu wuna wisi hanga luzolu lwa Nzambi, yandi wuna phangi wama wa yakala yi phangi wama wa mukhetu yi ngudi wama.»
MAR 4:1 Yesu wáyandika hika mu kulonga kuna khungu ya yanga dya mbuta. Mulumba-lumba wa batu balawu wámuzyeta yandi. Hanga wuzanzi mu masuwa wuzakadini mwamuna. Mulumba-lumba wa batu wosu ku tseki, bela-bela yi yanga dya mbuta.
MAR 4:2 Kakala balonga mambu ma lawu mu bingana amana wekina bazimbwala muna malongi mandi:
MAR 4:3 «Hinikinenu! Mukuni wálubuka mu kwenda mwanga mbutu.
MAR 4:4 Buna kakala mwanga kheni, ndambu yahika yenda bwila mu nzila: banuni bisiya dya.
MAR 4:5 Ndambu ya hika yenda bwila muma mwa matadi, muna mwakonda kala mafu ma lawu. Hanga yibufudi tswatsu, kikuma mafu mákalaku lawu;
MAR 4:6 kaasi ha kwátwa mwini, yáyokama amana yáyumuka mukuma yákalaku yi misodi.
MAR 4:7 Yahika yenda bwila ha kati kya tsaku. Tsaku záleya amana zákakidisaya, amana konda kuha keti kheni.
MAR 4:8 Kaasi kheni yikwawu yábwila mu mafu ma bukheti; yámena, yákola phi, ku tsuka yihe kheni: yimosi yálubula makumatatu, yikwawu makumasambanu, yikwawu hika khama.»
MAR 4:9 Amana kakala zimbula: «Wuna wenina yi matu ma kuyukila, kayuka!»
MAR 4:10 Buna kákala kuna phungamu, bana bámuzyeta, hakimosi yi bawu kumi yi bodi, báyandika mu kumuhyula kikuma kya bingana.
MAR 4:11 Amana kakala bazimbwala: «Kwena benu, kitsweki kya Kipfumu kya Nzambi kyáhanamina; kaasi kwena babana benina ku phenza, moosu misi hitila mu bingana,
MAR 4:12 ndangu: «Basímbulula kwa bawu, kaasi bamónaku kima; bahínikina kwa bawu, kaasi babákulaku kima; hanga bavutukisa nana kumanima amana masumu mabaloluka nana.»
MAR 4:13 Yesu wubazimbwadi hika: «Lubatiku bakula kingana kyaki? Amana abweti lwalenda bakula bingana byosu?
MAR 4:14 Mukuni kabati mwanga Ndinga ya Nzambi.
MAR 4:15 Bana benina mu kati kya nzila, mwena bawu yámwanganina Ndinga, kaasi muna kuyukilaya phi Satana wisi katula Ndinga meni yina bámwangiki mwena bawu.
