MAR 4:16 Amana kwena yina bámwanga muna muma mwa matadi, yi batu babana, buna bisi yuka Ndinga, batambwasiya yi kyesi,
MAR 4:17 kaasi beku yi misodi mwena bawu meni, bisi zyama lwesi mu tangwa dimosi; amana yukani kiwayi kondilo munyanga wisa kikuma kya Ndinga ya Nzambi, kyekina kisinza kikuma kya bawu.
MAR 4:18 Yikwawu yina yábwila ha kati kya tsaku; benina babana bisi yuka Ndinga,
MAR 4:19 kaasi phasi za tsi, byesi bya bimvwama bya luvunu yi mabanza mahika ma mutindu yi mutindu bisiya kakidikisa Ndinga, amana yihesiku.
MAR 4:20 Kaasi yahika yina yámwangana mu mafu ma bukheti; benina babana bisi yuka Ndinga ya Nzambi, batambudiya amana yibuti kheni; yimosi makumatatu, yikwawu makumasambanu, yikwawu khama.»
MAR 4:21 Yesu wábazimbwala hika: «Mwinda, ku sina dya nzungu ya tuma bisiwa sya kondilo ku tsi ya thangi? Keku ha thandu ya muzanga wa mwinda?
MAR 4:22 Mukuma heku kima kyaswamana, kyakonda zayakana, heku kitsweki kyakonda tunguluka mu kati kya mwini.
MAR 4:23 Honi mutu wenina yi matu ma kuyukila, kayuka!»
MAR 4:24 Kakala bazimbwala hika: «Kebenu mu mana lwisi yuka! Bakwisa lutesila muna kitesu kina lwisi tesila benu-benu; amana bayíka hika kikuma kya benu.
MAR 4:25 Mukuma bahána kwena wuna wenina kedi yi kima; kaasi kwena wuna wukondi kima, bamúkatula keti kina kenina kyawu.»
MAR 4:26 Yesu kakala zimbula hika: «Phila mosi yi Kipfumu kya Nzambi, kyenina hanga mutu wubati mwanga kheni mu kilanga kyandi.
MAR 4:27 Kanimba kondilo katokama, phipha yi mwini, kheni yisi mena amana yikodi konda kazaya keti khi mutindu.
MAR 4:28 Mafu mabati menisa kheni mawu meni: theti ngwalengi, kunima misambu, tsuka-tsuka mbongu yikodi.
MAR 4:29 Buna kyisi benga kibundu, batambudi mbedi, mukuma tangwa dya kuhelakya dilungidini.»
MAR 4:30 Yesu kakala zimbula hika: «Yi biki twalenda fwanikisa Kipfumu kya Nzambi? Yi khi mutindu wa kingana twalenda fwanikisakya?
MAR 4:31 Kifwanani yi kheni ya tidi, buna batimbudiya muna mafu, yenina kukeya kuluta kheni zoosu za mu mafu.
MAR 4:32 Kaasi buna bakuniya, yileyi, mihandi mikodi kuluta miti myosu myenina mu masamba amana yilubudi mihandi mya mbuta, keti banuni ba ku zilu bafwani kutunga mazamba ma bawu muna tsya kivula kyandi.»
MAR 4:33 Muna lawu dya bingana bya mutindu meni wuna mwa mwamuna Yesu kakala balongila Ndinga ya Nzambi, bwosu buna báfwana kuyukila.
MAR 4:34 Kakalaku bazonzisa konda ni kata kingana; kaasi mu kingenga, kakala tendula moosu kwena balonguki bandi.
MAR 4:35 Muna masikidika ma kilumbu meni kina, Yesu wubazimbudi kwena balonguki bandi: «Tulabukenu ku sambwa dina.»
MAR 4:36 Kunima dya kusula mulumba-lumba wa batu, bámunata muna masuwa mana kákala. Hákala phi yi masuwa mahika hakimosi yi yandi.
MAR 4:37 Kimbongila kimosi kya ngolu kyátukula, makaka menika dibunda kuna masuwa, hanga masuwa mazodi mabasa yi mamba.
MAR 4:38 Yandi wanimba kákala kuna manima ma masuwa, mutwa hana mbumbi ya mutwa. Bámutokamisa amana bámuzimbwala: «Mulongi, tukulukini amana ngeyi bubatiku kuheka pasi?»
MAR 4:39 Yesu wátokama, wákaya kimbongila, amana wáhana muswa kwena yanga dya mbuta: «Kala talala, dibata!» Kimbongila kyádibata amana talala dya lawu dyákota.
MAR 4:40 Kunima Yesu wábazimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki lwenina yi bweya bwabuna? Lweku kedi yi lukwikilu?»
MAR 4:41 Hanga kitswi kibakwati, bábanga lawu, bakala dizimbwala bawu yi bawu: «Amana nati kenina yandundu, ni keti kimbongila, keti yanga dya mbuta byamulemvukilaka?»
MAR 5:1 Kunima Yesu yi balonguki bandi benda ku sambwa dikwawu dya yanga dya mbuta, ku kinzunga kya bisi Ngelasoni.
MAR 5:2 Buna kátuluka mu masuwa, mutu mosi wálubuka muna mazyamu, kákala phi wazakama yi kitembu kya mbi wísa kuna thwala ya yandi.
MAR 5:3 Kakala zingila hana kati dya mazyamu, amana keti mutu kálendaku hika kumukasa, keti mu muyololu;
MAR 5:4 Mukuma, mbala za lawu bakala muzitikila mitaku kuna malu yi miyololu muna moku, kaasi kákalamya tabula yi kutolulaka mitaku. Kwakalaku keti mutu wakala yi ngolu za kumulembikila.
MAR 5:5 Kosu tangwa, phipha keti mwini, kakala kangala muna mazyamu yi muna mongu, mu kukalungaka yi kudityonunaka yandi meni ku matadi.
MAR 5:6 Buna kámona Yesu muna kyana; wénda thinu, wáfukama kuna thwala ya yandi,
MAR 5:7 amana wákalunga: «Khi dyambu wumvwini ngeyi, Yesu, Mwana wa Nzambi Kahungu? Yikubokwadidini, muna khumbu ya Nzambi, wungyangisaku!»
MAR 5:8 Mukuma Yesu kakala muzimbwala: «Kitembu kya mbi, lubuka mwena mutu yandu!»
MAR 5:9 Kakala muyufula: «Biki khumbu yaku?» Yandi wávutula: «Khumbu yama "Khwingi", mukuma lawu thwenina.»
MAR 5:10 Amana mutu wuna wámubokwadila Yesu yi nziki-nziki ni katumaku bitembu bya mbi ku phenza ya kinzunga.
MAR 5:11 Kinga kwákala kwakuna, bela-bela yi mongu, yi kibuka kimosi kyambuta kya bangulu bakala dya.
MAR 5:12 Bitembu bya mbi byámubokwadila: «Tutuma mwena bangulu bana. Tuyambula thwenda kota mwena bawu!»
MAR 5:13 Yesu wátambwasabwa. Hanga bitembu bya mbi bilubukini mwena mutu, byenda kota mwena bangulu, amana kibuka kyosu kyádidindumuna muna mungulunga yi kuna yanga dya mbuta. Hákala kitesu kya mafunda modi ma bangulu; bázyonda muna yanga dya mbuta.
MAR 5:14 Babana bakala hungula bangulu bátina, benda nata tsangu muna mbanza yi muna mahata amana batu bisa tala mana máhita.
MAR 5:15 Buna bátula bela-bela yi Yesu, bámona mutu wuna wákala yi bitembu bya mbi wazakala, wuvwatikini miledi yi mabanza ma kimutu. Yandi wuna wákala wazakama yi khwingi ya bitembu bya mbi hanga báyuka bweya.
MAR 5:16 Babana bámona mana máhita, bakala bamenika mana mámubwila mutu wuna wákala yi bitembu bya mbi yi meni dya bangulu.
MAR 5:17 Hanga bayandikini mu kubokwadila Yesu ni kakatuka mu kinzunga kya bawu.
MAR 5:18 Buna kakala kota mu masuwa, mutu wuna bálubula bitembu bya mbi wámubokwadila ndangu kakalaka yi yandi.
MAR 5:19 Kaasi Yesu kátambwasaku, wumuzimbwadini: «Vutuka ku nzu yaku, kwena biwutu byaku amana wabámenika moosu mamana kakuhangidini Pfumu yi buna kakuyukidini kiwayi.»
MAR 5:20 Wénda kwandi amana wáyandika mu kusamuna muna Mbanza kumi moosu mana káhanga Yesu kikuma kya yandi. Amana boosu báyituka lawu.
MAR 5:21 Yesu wávutwakisa hika ku sambwa dikwawu dya yanga dya mbuta muna masuwa. Mulumba-lumba wa batu lawu bisa wongama bela-bela yi yandi. Ku khungu ya yanga dya mbuta kákala.
MAR 5:22 Mosi wa bapfumu ba nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, khumbu yandi Zayilusi, wátula. Buna kámona Yesu, wábwa muna malu mandi
MAR 5:23 amana wámubokwadila lawu: «Mwana wama wa mukhetu mu kulakana kenina. Awisa, muthetika moku ndangu kabeluka amana kazinga!»
MAR 5:24 Yesu wénda hakimosi yi yandi. Mulumba-lumba wumosi wa batu balawu bakala mulanda yi kumufitikisaka tselu yi tselu.
MAR 5:25 Kinga hákala hakana yi mukhetu mosi wakala noka menga tukidila mvula kumi yi zodi.
MAR 5:26 Kányokuka lawu mu kukwendaka kwena bandomvi balawu, amana, wámanisa kuvwa kwandi kwosu konda kutambula ndandu; kaasi phasi zakala muvula hika.
MAR 5:27 Buna káyuka kuzonzila Yesu, wísa bwesuka muna mulumba-lumba wa batu, kuna kunda dya Yesu, wásimba muledi wandi.
MAR 5:28 Mukuma kakala dizimbwala: «Yukani yisimba lwesi myawu meni miledi myandi, yíkola.»
MAR 5:29 Muna mbala mosi, menga mámukangama amana wádiyuka muna lutu lwandi, ni wukodi mu makhasi mandi.
MAR 5:30 Muna mbala mosi, Yesu wádiyuka mwena yandi-meni ni ngolu zimosi zimulubukini. Kahanga wubalungini muna mulumba-lumba wa batu amana wuyandikini mu kuzimbula: «Nati wusimbi miledi myama?»
MAR 5:31 Balonguki bandi bamuzimbwadini: «Wubati mona mulumba-lumba wa batu baba babati kufitikisa tselu yi tselu, amana wubati zimbula hika: "Nati wutsimbini?"»
MAR 5:32 Kaasi kakala simbulula muna kabeta ka yandi mu kumona wuna wáhanga bwabuna.
MAR 5:33 Mukhetu wuna, bwosu kázaya mana mámubwila, yi tsula yosu, wisa bwa muna malu mandi hanga wumuzimbwadi kyedika kyosu.
MAR 5:34 Kaasi Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Mwana wama wa mukhetu, lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini. Ndawenda mu ngemba amana kola mu makhasi maku.»
MAR 5:35 Muna tangwa dina kakala zonza bwabuna, kutala batu bátuka ku nzu ya Zayilusi bisi zimbula: «Mwana waku wa mukhetu wufini. Kikuma kya biki wubati muyangisila hika Mulongi?»
MAR 5:36 Kaasi Yesu kálandaku mana bakala zonza, wázimbula kwena Zayilusi: «Wuyukaku bweya, kwikila lwesi.»
MAR 5:37 Kaasi Yesu kátambwasaku ni benda musindikila kwena mutu, kwena Phetelu lwesi, Zyaki yi Yowani phangi wa yakala wa Zyaki.
MAR 5:38 Ha bátula ku nzu ya Zayilusi; kwakuna, wámona mvwalangani, batu babati dila yi kukalungaka mu miboku.
MAR 5:39 Wákota amana wábazimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki mvwalangani yayi yi bidilu byabi? Mwana kafiku, wunimbiki.»
MAR 5:40 Bawu bakala museya. Kaasi yandi wábakukwasa boosu, wutambudi lwesi tata yi ngudi wa mwana, yi balonguki bana bakala musindikila; amana wákota muna kákala mwana.
MAR 5:41 Yesu wámusimba mwana kuna koku amana wumuzimbwadi: «Tadita kum!» Disongidila: «Mwana wa mukhetu, yikuzimbwadibwa, telama!»
MAR 5:42 Muna mbala mosi, mwana wa mukhetu wátelama amana wáyandika kukangala; mvula kumi yi zodi kákala zawu. Mabanza mábavwalangana boosu.
MAR 5:43 Kaasi Yesu wátoma bakandisa ni keti mutu kazayabwoku, amana wuzimbudini: «Muhekenu bima bya kudya.»
MAR 6:1 Ha kákatuka hakana, wenda ku mbanza yina kákodila; amana balonguki bandi bámulanda.
MAR 6:2 Tangwa kyáfwana kilumbu kya sabata, wáyandika mu kulonga muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta. Batu balawu bana bakala hinikina, báyituka lawu. Beka dihyula: «Ku biki mamutukidi mamana? Khi mutindu wa mudimu wana bámuheka? Abweti biphadi bya mutindu wuna bifwani kusalamina mu moku mandi?
MAR 6:3 Ka yandi ku musadi wa mabaya, mwana wa Madiya, phangi wa Zyaki, Zoze, Yuta, yi Simoni? Baphangi bandi ba bakhetu benahoku ha kati dya betu?» Kákala kisinza kikuma kya bawu.
MAR 6:4 Yesu kakala bazimbwala: «Mbikudi bisiku mukanda lukumu, kaasi kisiku lumina mu tsi yandi yi muna kikanda kyandi.»
MAR 6:5 Yesu kalendaku kusala keti kiphadi kimosi kwakuna, kaasi kábuka lwesi ndambu ya bambefu mu kubathetika moku.
MAR 6:6 Kakala yituka kikuma kya kukonda kwa lukwikilu kwa batu ba ku tsi yandi. Kunima kakala kangala muna mahata ma kinzunga mu kulongaka.
MAR 6:7 Buna kátela bawu kumi yi bodi, wáyandika mu kubatuma bodi-bodi yi kubaheka hamu hana thandu ya bitembu bya mbi.
MAR 6:8 Wábaheka mutsiku wawu: «Lunataku kima mu nzila, koka lwesi; keti dipha, keti waba, keti dikuta dya phalata muna khola.
MAR 6:9 Vwatenu tsabatu, kaasi lunataku bikutu byodi.»
MAR 6:10 Kakala bazimbwala hika: «Muna nzu yina lwakóta, kalenu mwamuna kilumbu yi kuna lwakátwakila homa meni hana.
MAR 6:11 Amana yukani batu babusa mu kuluyamba keti mu kuluhinikina, mu kukatuka hana meni, khukumunenu fusyangeni dya bitambi byenu: kyakála kimbangi kikuma kya bawu.»
MAR 6:12 Amana buna bénda balonguki, bálonga kwena batu ni mboti babalumuna mbundu.
MAR 6:13 Bakala kukwasa bitembu bya mbi lawu yi kusita masi kwena bambefu amana bakala kola.
MAR 6:14 Kinga kyamvu Eloti wáyuka buna yakala kwenda khumbu ya Yesu khululuka. Bahika bakala zimbula: «Yowani, wuna wakala botika, wufutumuki ha kati dya bafwa! Hahana kenina yi ngolu za kuhangila biphadi.»
MAR 6:15 Bahika bakala zimbula: «Yandu Diya.» Bahika phi: «Yandu mosi wa bambikudi bana bakhulu.»
MAR 6:16 Kaasi Eloti mu kuyuka bwabuna, kakala zimbula: «Yowani wuna yibukwasa meni mutwa, yandi wufutumukini!»
MAR 6:17 Mukuma yandi-meni Eloti wámukwatisa Yowani, wámukasisa miyololu mu boloku. Kikuma kya Elodyadi, mukhetu wa Fidiphu, phangi wandi wa yakala, wuna kákwela.
MAR 6:18 Kikuma Yowani kakala zimbula kwena Eloti: «Wulungiku mu kukwela mukhetu wa phangi waku!»
MAR 6:19 Elodyadi kikudi-kudi kya Yowani kákala kyawu amana kakala zola ni kamuhondisa. Kaasi kakalaku lenda.
MAR 6:20 Mukuma Eloti bweya bwa Yowani kákala bwawu, bwosu kázaya ni mutu wa masonga yi watoma kákala amana kakala musweka. Tangwa kakala muyuka, kakalaku mona kima kya kuhanga; kinga kakala muhinikina yi tsambu.
MAR 6:21 Kaasi phila yámonika mu kilumbu kya mukinzi wa lubutuku lwa Eloti, kásadisa mukinzi kikuma kya batu bandi ba luzitu yi bapfumu ba baphumbulu yi bapfumu ba mahata ma kinzunga kya Ngadidi.
MAR 6:22 Mwana wandi wa mukhetu, Elodyadi, wákota hana mbasi amana wákina; Eloti yi batu bana kátedisa bwábasephidisa lawu. Kyamvu wázimbula kwena mwana wa mukhetu: «Ndomba kyosu kina wuzodini, amana yikúhekakya.»
MAR 6:23 Hanga wudi ndefi ya mukwandi kwena mwana wa mukhetu: «Kina wandómba, yikuhekakya keti kyati kya kipfumu kyama.»
MAR 6:24 Mwana wa mukhetu wálubuka amana wázimbula kwena ngudi wandi: «Biki yilómba?» Yandu-yandu wávutula: «Mutwa wa Yowani, wuna wakala botika.»
MAR 6:25 Mwana wa mukhetu wénda tswasu kwena kyamvu mu kumulomba: «Nzodi ni wapheka, buthwena meni bwabu, ha dilonga, mutwa wa Yowani Mubotiki.»
MAR 6:26 Kyamvu Eloti wáyuka kiwayi kya lawu; kaasi, kikuma kya ndefi yina kádya ku thwala ya babana kátedisa, kázolaku mu kumutuna.
MAR 6:27 Muna mbala mosi, kyamvu wátuma tsinzidi mosi yi muswa wa kunata mutwa wa Yowani. Tsinzidi wenda mubukuna Yowani mutwa muna boloku.
MAR 6:28 Kunima wisa nata mutwa wandi hana dilonga. Wáhanawa kwena mwana wa mukhetu, amana mwana wa mukhetu wáhanawa kwena ngudi wandi.
MAR 6:29 Buna báyuka musamu wuna, balonguki ba Yowani, bisa bonga mvumbi yandi amana bázikaya muna mazyamu.
MAR 6:30 Bathumwa bákutakana kuna kakala Yesu, bámumenikina mambu moosu mana báhanga yi moosu mana bálonga.
MAR 6:31 Hanga wubazimbwadini: «Alwisenu ku phungamu, homa hamosi hakálaku batu, amana lwalembwa koma.» Mukuma lawu bakala kwisa yi kukwendaka, amana bawu bakalaku keti tangwa dya kudya.
MAR 6:32 Bahanga bakoti mu masuwa ndangu benda ku phungamu, kuma kumosi kwa talala.
MAR 6:33 Balawu bábamona mu kukwenda amana bábabakula mu mahata moosu ma kinzunga muna bakala kwenda. Bakala takula mu malu, amana bakala bakesidila kuna thwala.
MAR 6:34 Tangwa kátuluka Yesu mu masuwa, wámona mulumba-lumba wa batu lawu; kiwayi kyámukwata, kikuma bákala hanga mikoku mikondi kalema. Amana wáyandika mu kubalonga mambu ma lawu.
MAR 6:35 Buna kwáyila kuma, balonguki bandi bisa muzimbwala: «Homa thwenina ha tseki, kuma phi kuyidini.
MAR 6:36 Basula batu, ndangu benda muna mafedime yi muna mahata ma kinzunga, ndangu badisumbila bima bya kudya.»
MAR 6:37 Kaasi Yesu wubavutwadini: «Bahekenu benu-benu madya.» Bawu bamuzimbwadini: «Thwenda sumba mapha ma khama zodi za phata ndangu thwisa badisila?»
MAR 6:38 Yandi wubahyudini: «Alwenda taleti, mapha makwa lwenina mawu?» Kunima dya kuzikisa, bávutula: «Mapha matanu yi batsema bodi.»
MAR 6:39 Hanga wubasendi ni babazakadisa boosu mu bibuka muna mwangu watsi.
MAR 6:40 Amana batu bázakala mu bibuka bya khama yi bya makumatanu.
MAR 6:41 Wátambula mapha mawu matanu yi batsema bawu bodi, wásekula mesu kuna zilu, wuvutudini matondu kwena Nzambi. Wábukuna mapha amana wáhanama kwena balonguki bandi; ndangu bakabisama. Wákabisa phi batsema bawu bodi hana kati dya bawu boosu.
MAR 6:42 Boosu bádya amana báyukuta.
MAR 6:43 Amana balonguki bánata bitunga kumi yi byodi bya bitini bya mapha yi bya batsema.
MAR 6:44 Babana bádya mapha bákala mafunda matanu ma bayakala.
MAR 6:45 Muna tangwa meni dina, kunima wásenda balonguki bandi bakota mu masuwa amana bamutekidilaka kuna sambwa dya Betisayita, kithama kina kasúdila yandi-meni mulumba-lumba wa batu.
MAR 6:46 Kunima dya kubasula, wenda ku mongu kikuma kya kulombila.
MAR 6:47 Ha yábwa phipha, masuwa makala matudi kedi ha kati kya yanga dya mbuta. Yesu yandi buhika kákala muna mafu.
MAR 6:48 Mu kumona ni balonguki bandi mu phasi bakala sabwakila, mukuma pfunzi yakala bakakidikisa; muna khoku wa theti, Yesu wísa kwena bawu mu kukangala hana yanga dya mbuta, hanga wuna wabahita.
MAR 6:49 Tangwa bámumona kukangala ha thandu ya yanga dya mbuta, bakala banza ni kiphedikisa amana báyandika mu kukalunga;
MAR 6:50 mukuma bakala mumona bawu boosu amana mabanza mabavwalangana. Muna mbala mosi, Yesu wázonza kwena bawu: «Kalenu yi kikesa, meni yandu, luyukaku bweya!»
MAR 6:51 Kunima wákota muna masuwa ha kimosi yi bawu, amana pfunzi yálembama. Báyituka lawu, mwena bawu meni
MAR 6:52 mukuma bábakisaku keti kima kikuma kiphadi kina kya mapha: mbundu za bawu zitu zákala.
MAR 6:53 Buna bámanisa mu kusabuka, bátula ku Ngenezaleti amana bátuluka mu mafu.
MAR 6:54 Buna bátuluka mu masuwa, batu bámubakula Yesu.
MAR 6:55 Batu bátuka mu kinzunga meni kina kyosu amana báyandika mu kunata bambefu hana biphoyu, mwosu muna bakala muyukila khululuka.
MAR 6:56 Mwosu muna kakala kota Yesu, mahata, mbanza, keti mu mafedime, batu bakala sikula bambefu muna mbasi yi kumubokwadilaka ni kabayambwadila ndangu balenga simba keti nzenzi ya muledi wandi. Amana bambefu boosu bana bakalaya simba, bákola.
MAR 7:1 Bafwadisi yi ndambu ya balongi ba mitsiku bátuka ku Yelusalemi bisa kutakana kuna kakala Yesu.
MAR 7:2 Babati mona ni ndambu ya balonguki bandi bekina dya yi moku ma mvindu, disongidila ni makonda kusukula.
MAR 7:3 Mukuma Bafwadisi yi Bayuta boosu bisiku dya kedi konda kusukula moku, kikuma bisimya zitisa mikuku mya bakhaka;
MAR 7:4 amana tangwa batukini ku zandu, bisiku dya lwesi kunima dya kudisemisa. Bisi zitisa lawu mikuku myahika mya bakhaka, mu mbandu kusukula kwa makopha, malonga, tulondu, nzungu za bisengu yi [thangi].
MAR 7:5 Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku bámuhyula kwena Yesu: «Kikuma kya biki balonguki baku bisiku landila mikuku mya bakhaka, bawu kudyaka moku yi mvindu?»
MAR 7:6 Yandi wubazimbwadini: «Bakavungalosi, Yesaya mboti kázonza mu kubikula kwena benu! Bwosu bwásonama: "Kanda dyadi dyisi nzitisila ha munwa, kaasi mbundu yandi kyana yenina yi meni.
MAR 7:7 Mu phamba bisi pfukamina, mukuma malongi ma bawu myenina mikuku mya batu."
MAR 7:8 Lwisi losila mitsiku mya Nzambi amana ludihani ku mikuku mya batu.»
MAR 7:9 Kakala bazimbwala: «Benu lwisi toma losila mitsiku mya Nzambi ndangu lwahalaminaka mu kikhaka kyenu!"
MAR 7:10 Moyize kázimbula: "Zitisa tata waku yi ngudi waku", amana phi: "Wuna wasínga tata wandi kondilo ngudi wandi bamuhondisa."
MAR 7:11 Kaasi benu, lwisi zimbula: Wuna wazímbula kwena tata wandi kondilo kwena ngudi wandi: "Kina yikhana mu kukuheka kikuma kya kukusadisa kyenina kyakutambika kikuma kya Nzambi,
MAR 7:12 lwisiku sisa hika kima kya kusala kikuma kya tata wandi kondilo ngudi wandi.
MAR 7:13 Bwabuna lwisi zimbikisila ndinga ya Nzambi kikuma kya kikhaka kina lwásambwakisila kwena batu. Amana mambu mahika lawu lwisi sala mafwanakana yi mamana.»
MAR 7:14 Yesu wátela hika mulumba-lumba wa batu amana wázimbula: «Ngyukenu benu boosu amana bakisenu:
MAR 7:15 Kweku kima kyatuka ku phenza, kyakota mwena mutu kyalenda musumuna. Kaasi kima kina kyisi lubuka mwena mutu, kyakina kyisi musumuna. [
MAR 7:16 Yuka ni matu ma kuyukila lwenina mawu, yukenu mboti.»]
MAR 7:17 Buna kásisa mulumba-lumba wa batu, kávutuka ku nzu, balonguki bandi bámuhyula thendula ya kingana kina.
MAR 7:18 Yandi wubazimbwadini: «Benu phi lweku yi ngangu? Lwisiku zaya ni heku kima kya ku phenza, kikoti mwena mutu kyalenda musumuna,
MAR 7:19 mukuma kyawu kyisiku kota ku mbundu yandi; kaasi mu kundu dyandi, ku thwala kukwenda mu kabini?» Muna ndinga meni zina, mwamuna Yesu kakala zimbwala ni madya moosu ma kasemi menina.
MAR 7:20 Kakala zimbula hika: «Kina kyisi lubuka mwena mutu kyakina kyisi musumuna.
MAR 7:21 Mukuma muna mbundu ya mutu, mwamuna mwisi tuka mabanza mambi: kindumba kya kisaka-saka, bwifi, khengu,
MAR 7:22 mbongi, lukusu, khu, nduka za mbi, bizumba, ngusi, kukenga mesu, kuhuna musamu, lulendu, kukonda kubakisa mambu.
MAR 7:23 Mambu mama moosu mambi myisi lubuka mu kati dya mutu amana myisi sumuna mutu.»
MAR 7:24 Buna kákatuka Yesu hahana, wénda ku kinzunga kya Tidi. Wákota muna nzu yimosi, kátondaku ni bamuzaya kwena mutu; kaasi kálendaku mu kuswama.
MAR 7:25 Muna tangwa meni dina mukhetu mosi, mwana wandi wa mukhetu kákala yi kitembu kya mbi kimosi. Buna káyuka kuzonzila Yesu, wisa dilosa muna malu mandi.
MAR 7:26 Mukhetu meni wuna kákalaku Muyuta, mwisi Silo-Fenisi kákala. Kakala mubokwadila ni kakukwasa kitembu kya mbi kina kya mwana wandi.
MAR 7:27 Kaasi Yesu kakala muzimbwala: «Yambula theti bana bayukuta; mukuma ka mboti ku mu kutambula madya ma bana, amana batimbulama kwena bambwa.»
MAR 7:28 Kaasi mukhetu kámuvutwala: «Pfumu, aketi bambwa phi bisi dya bizotu bina bisi bwisisa bana mu tsya mesa.»
MAR 7:29 Yandi wumuzimbwadini: «Kikuma kya ndinga yina, vutuka ku nzu yaku, kitembu kya mbi kilubukini mwena mwana waku wa mukhetu.»
MAR 7:30 Tangwa kávutuka ku nzu yandi, káwana mwana walandalala hana thangi, kitembu kya mbi kilubuki kedi.
MAR 7:31 Buna kálubuka ku kinzunga kya Tidi, wáhitila ku Sitoni amana wávutwakila ku yanga dya mbuta dya Ngadidi, wáhitila mu kinzunga kya Mbanza Kumi.
MAR 7:32 Bámunatina muhunga mosi wákala babakana mu kuzonza; amana bámubokwadila ni kamusya moku.
MAR 7:33 Yesu wámunata ku kingenga kyana yi mulumba-lumba wa batu; wámusya milembu myandi muna matu, wálokula metya amana wámusimba lulaka yi metya mandi.
MAR 7:34 Kunima wásekula mesu kuna zilu, wáhumwakina amana wázimbula kwena kahuwa: «Efwata!» Disongidila: "Kanguka!"
MAR 7:35 Muna mbala mosi, matu ma mutu wuna mákanguka, lulaka lwandi lwákutumuka, wáyandika mu kuzonza buna bwa bukheti.
MAR 7:36 Yesu wábakandikisa ni bazonzilabwoku kwena mutu; kaasi mbatanana kábakandisabwa, báyadingisawa hika lawu, musamu, kuluta.
MAR 7:37 Batu báyituka lawu, bakala zimbula: «Moosu kabati hanga menina ma bukheti lawu! Kabati yukisa tuhuwa yi kuzonzisa mihunga!»
MAR 8:1 Muna bilumbu meni bina, hákala yi mulumba-lumba wa batu wumosi wambuta bakhokana hika. Bakalaku keti kima kya kudya. Yesu wátela balonguki bandi amana wábazimbwala:
MAR 8:2 «Kiwayi yenina kyawu kikuma mulumba-lumba wa batu wawu. Tala bilumbu byekina bitatu tukidila buna benina hakimosi yi meni amana beku keti kima kya kudya.
MAR 8:3 Yukani yibasula yi nzala, bakwenda lengalakana muna nzila, mukuma bahika hana kati dya bawu kyana batukini.»
MAR 8:4 Balonguki bandi bamuvutwadini: «Kubiki twawana mapha ma kubadisila mu tseki mwamu?»
MAR 8:5 Yesu wubahyudini: «Mapha makwa lwenina mawu?» Bazimbudini: «Tsambwadi.»
MAR 8:6 Kahanga wulombi kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu ni bazakala muna mafu. Kunima wábonga mapha tsambwadi amana wávutula matondu kwena Nzambi. Wábukununama amana wáhanama kwena balonguki bandi ndangu bakabisa kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu. Balonguki phi bahangini bwabuna.
MAR 8:7 Bákala hika yi tuma twa batsema. Kunima dya kubasakumuna, wázimbula ni babakabisa hika.
MAR 8:8 Batu bádya amana báyukuta. Bátonguna bitunga tsambwadi bya kabasi yi bitini bina byásala.
MAR 8:9 Bákala kitesu kya mafunda maya. Kunima Yesu wábasula.
MAR 8:10 Muna mbala mosi, yandi wákota mu masuwa yi balonguki bandi amana bénda muna kinzunga kya Talamanuta.
MAR 8:11 Bafwadisi bátula, báyandika kutendana yi Yesu. Amana, kikuma kya kumuleya, hanga bamulombi kiphadi kimosi kyatuka ku zilu.
MAR 8:12 Yesu wáhumwakina amana wuzimbudini: «Kikuma kya biki batu ba mbandu yayi babati lombila kiphadi? Mukyedika yiluzimbwadini: yamónaku keti kiphadi kimosi, batu ba mbandu yayi!»
MAR 8:13 Kunima wábasisa amana wákota muna masuwa mu kukwenda ku sambwa dikwawu dya yanga dya thibu.
MAR 8:14 Balonguki bázimbakana mu kunata mapha. Dipha dimosi lwesi bákaladyawu mu masuwa.
MAR 8:15 Yesu wábakebisa: «Kebenu! Dikengenu ku muvimbu wa bafwadisi yi muvimbu wa Eloti.»
MAR 8:16 Balonguki bakala tendana bawu yi bawu kikuma bákalaku yi mapha.
MAR 8:17 Yesu wábakulabwa amana wábazimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki lubati tendanina ni lweku yi mapha? Khaniku kedi lubakisa? Khaniku kedi lumona? Mbundu zazitama ziluyenina?
MAR 8:18 Lwenina yi mesu amana lwisiku mona? Lwenina yi matu amana lwisiku yuka? Lwisiku yubuka:
MAR 8:19 ha yíbukuna mapha matanu kikuma kya bayakala mafunda matanu, bitunga bya kabasi bikwa bya bitini bya mapha bina lwátonguna?» Bavutudini: «kumi yi byodi».
MAR 8:20 «Amana tangwa yíbukuna mapha tsambwadi kikuma kya mafunda maya ma bayakala; bitunga bya kabasi bikwa bya bitini bya mapha bina lwatonguna?» Bavutudini: «Tsambwadi.»
MAR 8:21 Amana kakala bazimbwala: «Khaniku kedi lubakisa kwenu?»
MAR 8:22 Buna bátula ku Betisayita, bamunatini phofu mosi, bamubokwadidi ni kamusimba.
MAR 8:23 Yesu wámusimba phofu muna koku amana wámulubula mu hata. Kunima wámusya metya muna mesu amana wámusya moku, wumuhyudini: «Kima wubati mona?»
MAR 8:24 Phofu wátemuna mesu amana wuzimbudini: «Mbati mona batu, mbati bamona hanga miti kaasi babati kangala.»
MAR 8:25 Yesu wámusya hika moku muna mesu; phofu wákola amana wekina mona mboti-mboti bima byosu.
MAR 8:26 Hanga wumusendi ni kavutuka ku nzu yandi, mu kuzimbula: «Vutukaku ku hata.»
MAR 8:27 Yesu yi balonguki bandi bénda ku mahata mana menina bela-bela yi Sezale dya Fidiphu. Muna nzila, wáyandika mu kuhyula kwena balonguki bandi: «Biki bisi zonza batu kikuma kya meni?»
MAR 8:28 Bamuzimbwadini: «Bahika bisi zonza ni ngeyi wenina Yowani Mubotiki, bakwawu ni ngeyi Diya, bakwawu hika phi ni ngeyi wenina mosi hana kati dya bambikudi.»
MAR 8:29 Yandi wubahyudini: «Amana kwena benu, nati lwisi zimbula yenina meni?» Phetelu wumuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi wenina Kidisitu.»
MAR 8:30 Yesu wátomabakandisa ndangu bazimbulaku kima kitadidi yandi kwena mutu.
MAR 8:31 Hanga Yesu wuyandikini kubalonga: «Bulungi ni Mwana wa mutu kanyokuka lawu, bamulosila kwena bambuta ba Bayuta, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku, bamúhondisa amana kafútumuka kunima dya bilumbu bitatu.»
MAR 8:32 Yesu kákalabwa zonza wengele. Hanga Phetelu wumunati ku kabeta wekina mukaya.
MAR 8:33 Kaasi Yesu wábaluka, wábatala balonguki bandi amana wámukaya Phetelu: «Katuka, awenda ku manima ma meni, Satana! Mukuma wisiku banza hanga Nzambi, kaasi hanga batu.»
MAR 8:34 Kunima Yesu kahanga wutedi mulumba-lumba wa batu yi balonguki bandi amana wubazimbwadini: «Yuka ni mutu wuzodini kandanda, kadizimbakana yandi meni, katikula kitakani kyandi amana kandanda.
MAR 8:35 Mukuma, wosu wuna watónda mu kuhulula luzingu lwandi, katótisalwa; kaasi wosu wuna watótisalwa kikuma kya meni yi kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti kahúlulalwa.
MAR 8:36 Amana khi wawu mupfunu kwena mutu wa kuvwila kwandi tsi yosu amana katotisa luzingu lwandi?
MAR 8:37 Mutu, biki kafwani mu kuhana tambwa-tambwa yi luzingu lwandi?
MAR 8:38 Mukuma, wuna wangyúka tsoni yi ndinga zama ku mesu ma batu ba mbandu yayi bakonda kwikama yi ya basumuki, Mwana wa mutu phi tsoni kamúyuka tangwa kakwísa mu khembu ya Tata wandi yi yina ya banzyo ba Nzambi.»
MAR 9:1 Yesu wábazimbwala hika: «Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadini, ndambu ya batu mu kati dya baba benina haha benina haha bafwaku kedi konda kumona Kipfumu kya Nzambi buna kyakwísila yi ngolu.»
MAR 9:2 Kunima dya bilumbu bisambanu, Yesu wábonga Phetelu, Zyaki yi Yowani phangi wandi, hanga wubanati bawu buhika ku phungamu hana mongu wumosi wa kaleyi. Kwakuna, ku phungamu. Yesu wábalumuka hana mesu ma bawu;
MAR 9:3 miledi myandi myakala kedyamina mu phembi yimosi yina kalendaku mu kusemisa kwena mutu wa ha tsi yayi.
MAR 9:4 Diya yi Moyize bádimonikisa kwena bawu, yi kuyambilaka yi Yesu.
MAR 9:5 Phetelu wázimbula kwena Yesu: «Mulongi, bulungi ni twakala kwetu kwakuku. Tutungenu masombolu matatu, dimosi kikuma kya ngeyi, dikwawu kikuma kya Moyize, dikwawu hika kikuma kya Diya.»
MAR 9:6 Kámonaku mayakwadi, mukuma bweya bwábakwata.
MAR 9:7 Hanga kwisi tuti dimosi dyábafidinga yi kivula kya dyawu, amana ndinga yáyukalakana: «Yandu kenina Mwana wama watondama, muyukilenu!»
MAR 9:8 Muna mbala mosi, bátala hana bákala, kaasi bámonaku hika mutu mukwawu; Yesu lwesi yandi buhika yi bawu meni.
MAR 9:9 Mu kukulumuka kwa bawu kuna mongu, Yesu wábakandisa mu kumenika kwena mutu mana bámona yikuna káfutumukina Mwana wa mutu, ku bafwa.
MAR 9:10 Básimbidilaya ndinga meni yayina, kaasi kuna yi kudihyulaka bawu yi bawu: «Biki disongidila dya "kufutumuka ku bafwa"?»
MAR 9:11 Bakala muhyula: «Kikuma kya biki balongi ba mitsiku bisi zimbwala ni Diya fwani mu kutekila kwisa?»
MAR 9:12 Yandi wábavutwala: «Diya kafweti tekila kwisa ndangu kalongika byosu. Amana kikuma kya biki básonikina ni Mwana wa mutu kanyókuka amana kaléwuka?
MAR 9:13 Kaasi yiluzimbwadini ni Diya wísa kedi amana bámuhanga buna bázola, bwosu buna básonika kikuma kya yandi.»
MAR 9:14 Buna bátula bela-bela yi balonguki bahika, bámona mulumba-lumba wa batu lawu babazingiki balongi ba mitsiku bakala tendana yi balonguki.
MAR 9:15 Buna bámumona Yesu, báyituka lawu amana bénda thinu ndangu bamuheka mboti.
MAR 9:16 Yandi wábahyula balonguki bandi: «Biki lukadi tendanina yi bawu?»
MAR 9:17 Yakala mosi, muna mulumba-lumba wámuvutwala: «Mulongi, yikunatini mwana wama wuna wenina yi kitembu kya kamama.
MAR 9:18 Kwosu kuma kimukwatidini, kyisi mulemba ha tsi, hanga mwana wuyandiki kulubuka mafulu-fulu yi kudyaka makwenzi, amana yandi mutu wekina sununu. Yibabokwadidiki balonguki baku mu kukukwasa kitembu kina, kaasi balendikisikikyoku.»
MAR 9:19 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Benu mbandu yakonda lukwikilu! Yi kuna khi tangwa yikadiki yi benu? Yi kuna khi tangwa yilutambwasiki? Mundatinenu.»
MAR 9:20 Bámunatina yandi. Buna kámona Yesu, kitembu kyambi kyámunikisa ngolu; wábwa ha tsi amana weka dibundumuna yi mafulu-fulu kaki-kaki.
MAR 9:21 Yesu wáhyula kwena tata wandi: «Tukidila mvula kwa kedi kisi bela bwabubu?» Tata wandi wávutula: «Tukidila kimwana kyandi.
MAR 9:22 Mbala za lawu, kitembu kyisi mulundika ku mbawu ho loni mu mamba ndangu kyamuhonda. Kaasi yuka ni wufwani mu kuhanga kima, tuyukila kiwayi amana awisa tusadisa.»
MAR 9:23 Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Ho walenda! Moosu malendakana kwena wuna wisi kwikila.»
MAR 9:24 Muna mbala mosi, tata wa mwana wákalunga: «Khwikidini, awisa tsadisa kikuma kya kukonda kwa lukwikilu kwama!»
MAR 9:25 Yesu buna kámona mulumba-lumba wa batu wakala yikama hika; kahanga wukayi kitembu kya mbi mu kuzimbwalakya: «Kitembu kya muhunga yi kahuwa, meni yikuhekini muswa, lubuka mwena mwana yandu amana wuvutukamwoku hika!»
MAR 9:26 Kitembu kyálubuka mu kukalunga yi kukonya kwa lawu. Mwana wekina hanga wuna wufini; muna phila meni yana, batu bahika bakala zimbula: «Mwana wufini.»
MAR 9:27 Kaasi Yesu, buna kámusimba mwana kuna koku, wámutelamisa, mwana phi wekina mutendendi.
MAR 9:28 Tangwa kávutuka Yesu ku nzu, balonguki bandi báyandika mu kumuhyula mu kingenga: «Kikuma kya biki tulendidikiku mu kukukwasakya betu-betu kitembu meni kina?»
MAR 9:29 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Mbandu ya kitembu kina yisi lubukila lwesi mu lombilu.»
MAR 9:30 Buna bákatuka hahana, báhitila mu Ngadidi. Yesu kázolaku ni bamubakula kuna kenina.
MAR 9:31 Mukuma kakala balongisila balonguki bandi yi kubazimbwalaka: «Mwana wa mutu bámulambula ku moku ma batu, bamúhonda amana kunima dya bilumbu bitatu bya lufwa lwandi, kafútumuka.»
MAR 9:32 Kaasi balonguki bakalaku bakisa thendula ya ndinga yina; amana bákala yi bweya bwa kumuhyula byufu.
MAR 9:33 Bátula ku Kafadinawumi. Tangwa bákala muna nzu, Yesu wáhyula kwena balonguki: «Tendu dya biki lukadiki dyawu mu nzila?»
MAR 9:34 Kaasi bawu bádibata, mukuma, mu nzila, bakala tendana bawu yi bawu mu kuzaya keti nati wenina mbuta.
MAR 9:35 Hanga wuzakadini, wátela bawu kumi yi bodi amana wábazimbwala: «Yuka mutu wuzodi kukala watheti, kakala watsuka ha kati dya batu boosu yi musadi wa batu boosu.»
MAR 9:36 Hanga wubongi mwana wakhunda mosi, wámusya hana kati dya bawu amana, kunima dya kumuzangula, wábazimbwala:
MAR 9:37 «Wosu wuna wayámba mwana mosi wakhunda, hanga yandu, mu khumbu ya meni, meni-meni kayambini; amana wosu wuna wungyambini, kayambiku lwesi meni, kaasi wuyambi phi wuna wáthuma.»
MAR 9:38 Yowani kázimbula kwena Yesu: «Mulongi, tumonikini mutu mosi wisi kukwasa bitembu bya mbi mu khumbu ya ngeyi, amana tusandikini mu kumukandisabwa, kikuma kisiku landa betu.»
MAR 9:39 Yesu wuvutudini: «Lumukandisabwoku, mukuma heku mutu wasála kiphadi mu khumbu yama amana muna mbala mosi kenda zonza hika mambu mambi matadidi meni.
MAR 9:40 Kikuma, wuna wisiku tubwisa, hakimosi kenina yi betu.
MAR 9:41 Amana wosu wuna walúheka kopha dya mamba mu khumbu ya buna lwenina kwena Kidisitu; abwabuna, yiluzimbwadini, kalendalwoku totisa lufutu lwandi.»
MAR 9:42 «Wosu wuna wuhukumuni mosi wa bana ba khunda baba bisi kwikila mwena meni, bulungi kwena yandi bamuzitikila kalunga tadi hana tsingu amana bamudibula muna dingu dya yanga dya mbuta.
MAR 9:43 Yukani koku dyaku dyakusumunaka, bukunadya; bulungi kwena ngeyi wakota mu luzingu yi koku dimosi, ka mboti ku ni wakala yi moku maku modi amana wenda ku bilungi, kuna kwisiku zima mbawu. [
MAR 9:44 Kuna, "mimvidya mina misi vukula lutu misiku fwa amana mbawu yisiku zima."]
MAR 9:45 Yukani ni kitambi kyaku kyakusumunaka, bukunakya; bulungi kwena ngeyi wakota mu luzingu yi kitambi kimosi, ka mboti ku ni wakala yi bitambi byaku byodi amana bakulosa ku bilungi. [
MAR 9:46 Kuna, "mimvidya mina misi vukula lutu misiku fwa amana mbawu yisiku zima."]
MAR 9:47 Yuka phi ni disu dyaku dyakusumunaka, vusadya, bulungi kwena ngeyi wakota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi yi disu dimosi; ka mboti ku ni wakala yi mesu modi amana bakulosa ku bilungi.
MAR 9:48 Kwakuna, "mimvidya mina misi vukula lutu misiku fwa, amana mbawu yisiku zima."
MAR 9:49 Kikuma, kosu mutu katwa mungwa wa mbawu.
MAR 9:50 «Mungwa wenina kima kya bukheti; kaasi yuka ni munzenzu wuhwini, yi biki bavútwalawa hika? Kalenu yi mungwa mwena benu-benu, amana zingilakenu mu ngemba benu yi benu.»
MAR 10:1 Yesu buna kákatuka hahana, wisa ku kinzunga kya Yuteya yi kuna sambwa dikwawu dya Yolutani. Milumba-lumba mya batu myákhokama hika bela-bela yi yandi; bwosu kyákala kikalulu kyandi, wáyandika mu kubalonga.
MAR 10:2 Bafwadisi bisa muhyula, ndangu bamuleya. Bámuhyula: «Yakala kenina yi muswa wa kuyambula mukhetu wandi?»
MAR 10:3 Yesu wábavutwala: «Khi mutsiku káluheka Moyize?»
MAR 10:4 Bawu bázimbula: «Moyize wáhana muswa wa kusonikina mukanda wa kufwa kwa longu yi wa kukula.»
MAR 10:5 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Moyize, kikuma kya mbundu ya tadi yina lwenina yawu, káluhekila mutsiku wuna."
MAR 10:6 Kaasi ku luyandiku lwa phangamu, Nzambi kábahanga yakala yi mukhetu.
MAR 10:7 "Kikuma kya bwabuna, yakala kasísa tata wandi yi ngudi wandi amana kadínama yi mukhetu wandi,
MAR 10:8 amana bawu bodi bakítuka mutu mosi." Yihana ni beku hika bodi kaasi mutu mosi.
MAR 10:9 Mutu kahambulaku kina kakhundikisini Nzambi.»
MAR 10:10 Buna bátula ku nzu, balonguki bámuhyula hika byufu kikuma kya dyambu meni dina.
MAR 10:11 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Wuna wayámbula mukhetu wandi amana kakwela wahika, wuti mbongi ku thwala wuna watheti;
MAR 10:12 amana yuka ni mukhetu kadihambula yi yakala dyandi amana kakwela wahika, wuti mbongi.»
MAR 10:13 Batu bakala munatina bana ndangu kabasimba kuna moku, kaasi balonguki bakala bakaya.
MAR 10:14 Mu kumona bwabuna, Yesu wáyuka khabu amana wábazimbwala: «Yambulenu bana bakhunda bisa kwena meni! Lubakandisaku, mukuma Kipfumu kya Nzambi kyenina kikuma kya batu bana benina hanga bawu.
MAR 10:15 Abwabuna, yiluzimbwadi: wosu wuna wakonda yamba Kipfumu kya Nzambi hanga mwana wakhunda, kakótamwoku.»
MAR 10:16 Kunima wábazangula muna moku mandi amana wábasakumuna mu kubathetikaka moku.
MAR 10:17 Bwosu kakala kwenda muna nzila, yakala mosi wísa thinu amana wáfukama kuna thwala ya Yesu mu kumuhyula: «Mulongi wa bukheti, biki pfwani yihanga mu kuvwa luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula?»
MAR 10:18 Yesu wámuzimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki wuthedidini wa bukheti? Heku mutu wenina wa bukheti ho ka Nzambi lwesi ku.
MAR 10:19 Wuzayi mitsiku myami: "Wuhondaku mvumbi ya khengu, wutaku mbongi, wuyibaku, wutaku kimbangi kya bukamvi, wuhunaku musamu, zitisa tata waku yi ngudi waku.»
MAR 10:20 Yandi wumuvutwadini: «Mulongi, mambu mana mosu yisima zitisa tukidila kileki kyama.»
MAR 10:21 Yesu wámutala amana wámutonda, wumuzimbwadini: «Kima kimosi kikukondini: ndawenda, tekisa byosu bina wenina byawu, hanabya kwena batsukamini, amana watámbula kuvwa ku zilu; kunima nzawisa amana ndanda.»
MAR 10:22 Kaasi yandi buna káyuka ndinga meni yina, kiwayi kyámukwata amana wénda mu kyadi, mukuma bima bya lawu kákala byawu.
MAR 10:23 Yesu buna kátala muna kabeta kandi, wuzimbudini kwena balonguki bandi: «Phasi bwenina kwena bana benina yi bimvwama mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi!»
MAR 10:24 Balonguki báyituka lawu kikuma kya ndinga zandi. Kaasi Yesu wávutwakila: «Bana bama, phasi bwenina mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi!
MAR 10:25 Bweku phasi kwena kamela mu kulobuka ha hundu dya ndongu, kaasi phasi lawu kwena mvwama mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
MAR 10:26 Balonguki báyituka hika lawu, bakala dihyula bawu yi bawu: «Amana nati walenda huluka?»
MAR 10:27 Yesu wábatala amana wuzimbudini: «Mana malendakanaku kwena batu, malendakana kwena Nzambi; mukuma heku dyambu dyakonda lendakana kwena Nzambi.»
MAR 10:28 Phetelu wáyandika mu kumuzimbwala: «Tala betu, tusisini bima byetu byosu amana tulandi ngeyi.»
MAR 10:29 Yesu wávutula: «Abwabuna, yiluzimbwadibwa: heku mutu wásisa nzu, baphangi ba bayakala, baphangi ba bakhetu, ngudi, tata, bana kondilo mafu, kikuma kya meni yi kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti;
MAR 10:30 amana kakonda tambula mbala khama buthwena bwabu: nzu, baphangi ba bayakala, baphangi ba bakhetu, bangudi, bana, yi mafu yi munyanga phi; amana muna tsi yina yakwísa, kakonda tambula moya wa mvula yi mvula.
MAR 10:31 Lawu bakala batheti, basúkinina amana lawu bakala batsuka, batékila.»
MAR 10:32 Mu nzila bákala mu kutombuka ku Yelusalemi. Amana Yesu kakala kwenda ku thwala ya bawu. Balonguki mu tsumbi bákala, bana bakala mulanda phi, bweya bakala bwawu. Yesu wábonga hika bawu kumi yi bodi, bela-bela yi yandi, amana wáyandika mu kubazimbwala mambu mama makhana mubwila.
MAR 10:33 Kábazimbwala: «Talenu, ku Yelusalemi tubati tombuka; Mwana wa mutu bamúlambula kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi kwena balongi ba mitsiku. Ndola ya lufwa bamúzengila, bamúlambula kwena baphani.
MAR 10:34 Bamúseya, bamúlokwala metya, bamúzyatula amana bamúhonda. Amana kunima bilumbu bitatu, kafútumuka.»
MAR 10:35 Bana ba Zebeteya bodi, Zyaki yi Yowani, bísa muzimbwala: «Mulongi, twazóla ni wahanga kikuma kya betu mana twakúlomba.»
MAR 10:36 Yandi wubahyudini: «Biki luzodi ni yihanga kikuma kya benu?»
MAR 10:37 Bawu bamuzimbwadini: «Tuheka nzila ni twazakala mosi kuna koku dyaku dya kitata, mukwawu kuna koku dyaku dya kimama muna khembu yaku.»
MAR 10:38 Kaasi Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Lwisiku zaya mambu mana lwisi lomba. Lwalenda kunwa bungu dyadi yinwa meni, kondi loni kutambula mbotika yayi yitámbula meni?»
MAR 10:39 Bawu bamuzimbwadini: «Twalendabwa.» Yesu wubavutwadini: «Bungu dyadi nzodi yinwa meni, lwanwádya, amana balubotika phi mu mbotika yayi yitámbula meni.
MAR 10:40 Kaasi mana matadidini kuzakala ku kitata kyama holo ku kimama kyama, ka meni ku yisima hana; bifulu bina byenina kikuma kya bana báyidikilabya.»
MAR 10:41 Kumi bana bahika báyuka bwabuna, hanga babafungidi khabu Zyaki yi Yowani.
MAR 10:42 Yesu wábatela amana wubazimbwadini: «Luzayi ni malemba ma makanda bisi yala batu hanga bapfumu, amana bambuta bisi songila kwena bakwawu hamu dya bawu.
MAR 10:43 Dyeku buna mu kati dya benu, kaasi wuna wazola, mu kati dya benu, kukituka mbuta, kakála musadi wenu,
MAR 10:44 amana wosu wuna wuzodi kukala watheti mu kati dya benu, kakála muhika wa batu boosu.
MAR 10:45 Mukuma keti yandi meni Mwana wa mutu kísaku ndangu bamusadila, kaasi kikuma kya kusadila yi kulambula luzingu lwandi mu phila ya kukatula batu balawu mu kihika.»
MAR 10:46 Bisi ku Yediko. Amana buna kálubuka Yesu mu Yediko, yi balonguki bandi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu, phofu mosi wakala lomba bima muna nzila, khumbu yandi Balatimeya, mwana wa Timeya, kákala wazakala kuna kabeta ka nzila.
MAR 10:47 Wáyuka ni wuna Yesu mwisi Nazaleti amana wáyandika kukalunga: «Yesu, Mwana wa Tavidi, ngyukila kyadi!»
MAR 10:48 Balawu bakala mukaya ndangu kadibata, kaasi yandi wákalunga hika ngolu: «Mwana wa Tavidi, ngyukila kyadi!»
MAR 10:49 Yesu wátelema amana wuzimbudini: «Mutelenu.» Bámutela phofu yi kumuzimbwalaka: «Sya kikesa, telema, kabati kutela.»
MAR 10:50 Wálosa muzaka wandi, wátelama mbala mosi amana wísa kuna kákala Yesu.
MAR 10:51 Yesu wámuhyula: «Biki wuzodi yikuhangila?» Phofu wámuzimbwala: «Mulongi, nzodi yimona hika.»
MAR 10:52 Yesu wámuzimbwala: «Ndawenda, lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini.» Muna tangwa meni dina, wáyandika kumona, amana wámulanda muna nzila.
MAR 11:1 Amana Tangwa bábwesuka yi Yelusalemi, mu kukwenda ku hata dya Betifasi yi Betaniya, bela-bela yi mongu wa Olive, Yesu wátuma bodi ba balonguki bandi
MAR 11:2 mu kubazimbwala: «Alwenda kuna hata dina dyenina ku thwala ya benu, buna lwakóta, lwawána mwana wa ane wakuzitikila, wuna bakonda kedi zakala kwena mutu; mukutumunenu, amana mundatinenu.
MAR 11:3 Amana yuka ni mutu kaluzimbwala: kikuma kya biki lubati hangila bwabuna?" Zimbulenu: "Pfumu mupfunu kamuvwini." Amana, muna mbala mosi, kamúsula.»
MAR 11:4 Bénda amana báwana mwana wa ane wa kuzitikila hana nzila, bela-bela yi mwelu wumosi, muna nzila. Bamukutumuni.
MAR 11:5 Ndambu ya batu bana bákala hana báyandika mu kubazimbwala: «Biki lubati hanga? Kikuma kya biki lubati mukutwamina mwana wa ane wuna?»
MAR 11:6 Bábavutwala bwosu kázimbulabwa Yesu, amana bábasula.
MAR 11:7 Bámunata mwana wa ane kwena Yesu; báthetika miledi mya bawu hana thandu ya yandi, Yesu wázakala hana thandu.
MAR 11:8 Batu balawu báyala miledi mya bawu muna nzila, amana bahika yi ndala zina bákesa mu bilanga.
MAR 11:9 Bana bakala kwenda ha thwala yi bana bakala landa bakala kalunga: «Ozana! Kasakumuka wuna wubati kwisa mu khumbu ya Pfumu!
MAR 11:10 Lwasakumuka luyalu luna lubati kwisa, luyalu lwa Tavidi tata wetu! Ozana muna bisoka!»
MAR 11:11 Yesu wákota mu Yelusalemi, kuna nzu ya Nzambi. Kunima dya kusimbululaya bima byosu yi bwosu kwáyila kuma, wénda ku Betaniya kumosi yi bawu kumi yi bodi.
MAR 11:12 Kilumbu kyálanda, bwosu kakala lubuka ku Betaniya, Yesu wáyuka nzala.
MAR 11:13 Buna kámona muna kyana mufiki wávwota yi khaya, wenda tala akolu kawanakwa kima; kaasi buna katula hahana, káwanaku keti kima, khaya za khatu, mukuma yákalaku tsungi ya bibundu bya fiki.
MAR 11:14 Hanga wuzimbudi kwena mufiki: «Mvula yi mvula, ka mutu ku wadya hika kibundu kyatúka mwena ngeyi!» Amana balonguki bandi bámuyuka.
MAR 11:15 Bátula ku Yelusalemi. Yesu wákota kuna nzu ya Nzambi, wáyandika mu kukwasa bana bakala tekisa yi bana bakala sumba kuna nzu ya Nzambi, wámwanga mitalaka mya bakwa tsyenzya yi biti bya bateki ba baphombu,
MAR 11:16 konda kusisa mutu kanata kima muna luphangu lwa nzu ya Nzambi.
MAR 11:17 Kakala balonga yi kuzimbulaka: «Bwásonamaku bwabu: "Nzu yama batédikiya ni nzu ya bisambu kikuma kya bikanda byosu?" Kaasi benu, lukitudiya saka dya bandwandwa!»
MAR 11:18 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku bámuyuka; bakala sanda phila ya kumuhondisila; bweya bwa yandi bákala bwawu, kikuma mulumba-lumba wa batu wosu wakala yituka kikuma kya malongi mandi.
MAR 11:19 Ha mabwa masikidika, Yesu yi balonguki bandi bálubuka mu mbanza.
MAR 11:20 Buna bakala hita muna suka, balonguki bámona mufiki wayumuka yi kuna misodi.
MAR 11:21 Phetelu, bwosu káyubuka mana máhita, wumuzimbwadini: «Mulongi, talandi, mufiki wawu wábundila wosu wuyumukini.»
MAR 11:22 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Kwikilenu mwena Nzambi!
MAR 11:23 Abwabuna, yiluzimbwadibwa, wuna wazímbula kwena mongu wawu: "Kinduka hana, dilosa mu yanga dya mbuta," konda keti keti muna mbundu yandi, kaasi kakwikilaka ni mamana kabati zimbula malúngila, mamana mamúhangamina.
MAR 11:24 Yihana yiluzimbwadini: "Kyosu kina lwalómba mu kulombila, kwikilenu ni lutambudikya kedi amana balúhekakya."
MAR 11:25 "Amana buna lutelamikini mu kulombila, yuka ni dyambu lwenina dyawu yi mukwenu, mulolulenu, ndangu Tata wenu wenina muna mazilu kalulolula phi mitsoki myenu. [
MAR 11:26 Kaasi yukani lubaloludiku, Tata wenu wuna wenina mu mazilu, ketibwe kalúlolulaku mitsoki myenu.]»
MAR 11:27 Yesu yi balonguki bandi bávutuka ku Yelusalemi. Bwosu kakala kangala muna luphangu lwa nzu ya Nzambi, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi, balongi ba mitsiku yi bambuta ba dibundu bisa muwana.
MAR 11:28 Amana bamuhyudini: «Mu hamu dya nati wisi hangila bwabuna? Nati wukuhekini hamu dya kuhangilabwa?»
MAR 11:29 Yesu wubavutwadini: «Meni phi yilúhyula kyufu kimosi; yuka ni lwamvutwala, yiluzimbwala keti mu hamu dya nati yisi hangila mambu mana.
MAR 11:30 Mbotika yina ya Yowani, ku zilu yátuka ho kwena batu? Phekenu mvutu.»
MAR 11:31 Kaasi báyandika kutendana bawu yi bawu yi kudizimbwalaka: «Yuka ni twavutula: "Ya ku zilu", kazímbula: "Kikuma kya biki lwakonda mukwikidila?"
MAR 11:32 Kaasi yuka twazimbula: "Kwena batu", hanga...» Bweya bwa mulumba-lumba wa batu bákala bwawu, mukuma boosu bakala mubongila Yowani hanga mbikudi mosi wa kyedika.
MAR 11:33 Hanga bavutudi kwena Yesu: «Tuzayiku.» Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Meni phi yiluzimbwalaku keti mu hamu dya nati yisi hangila mambu mana.»
MAR 12:1 Hanga Yesu wuyandikini mu kubazonzila mu bingana: «Mutu mosi wákuna kilanga kya vinu. Wákakakya mu luphangu, wásima buku dya kinyongi kya vinu, wátunga kinongi kikuma kya kutanikinaka vinu, kunima wáluwisakya kwena batu, amana wénda mu kitambu.
MAR 12:2 Tangwa dya mbongu buna dyálungila, wátuma musadi mosi kwena basadi ba vinu ndangu bamubongila ndambu yandi ya bibundu bya vinu.
MAR 12:3 Bámukwata, bámubeta amana bámukukwasa moku ma khatu.
MAR 12:4 Mukwa kilanga wábahitika hika musadi wahika; bámukhokula muna mutwa amana bámutukwana.
MAR 12:5 Wátuma hika musadi wahika, bámuhonda; kunima balawu bábeta bwabuna, bahika bábahonda.
MAR 12:6 Mwana wandi wa yakala wuna watondama lwesi wásala; ku tsuka, wábahitika yandi mu kudizimbwala: "Bámuzitisa mwana wama wa yakala!"
MAR 12:7 Kaasi basadi babana ba kilanga kya vinu bádizonzila: "Yandu swana! Alwisenu, tumuhondenu, ndangu kuvwa kwasadila betu!"
MAR 12:8 Bámukwata, bámutimbula ku phenza ya kilanga kya vinu amana bámuhonda.
MAR 12:9 «Amana biki kahánga mukwa kilanga kya vinu? Kakwísa, wubahondisini basadi bana, amana kiyeka kya kilanga kya vinu kahánakya kwena basadi bahika.
MAR 12:10 Benu lwátangaku Masonuku mama: "Tadi dina bálosa batungi, dyákituka tadi dya theti dya mupfundila.
MAR 12:11 Mambu mama kwena Pfumu mátuka, dyambu dya ngituka ku mesu metu!"»
MAR 12:12 Bapfumu ba bayuta bakala sanda phila ya kumukwatila, kaasi báyuka bweya bwa mulumba-lumba wa batu. Bábakula ni kikuma kya bawu kátila kingana kina. Bámusisa amana bénda kwabawu.
MAR 12:13 Bamuhitikini ndambu ya bafwadisi yi bakwa kibuka kya Eloti, ndangu bamuleya Yesu muna ndinga zandi.
MAR 12:14 Baba bisa muzimbwala: «Mulongi, tuzayi ni ngeyi kyedika wena amana weku yi bweya bwa mambu mana bisi banza batu kikuma, wisiku tala mbunzu za batu, kaasi wisi longa nzila ya Nzambi buna bufwani. Bulungi mu kufuta phaku ya Khayisala? Tufweti futa ho tufutaku?»
MAR 12:15 Bwosu kázaya bukavungalosi bwa bawu, wábavutwala: «Kikuma kya biki lubati ndeyila? Ndatinenu kuta dimosi, nzodi yimonadya.»
MAR 12:16 Bámunatinadya dimosi, Yesu wábahyula: «Mbunzu yi khumbu yayi básonika haha bya nati?» Bámuvutwala: «Bya Khayisala.»
MAR 12:17 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Hanenu mambu ma Khayisala kwena Khayisala, amana mambu ma Nzambi kwena Nzambi.» Amana báyituka lawu kikuma kya mvutu ya Yesu.
MAR 12:18 Kunima, Basadise bana bisi zimbula ni kweku lufutumuku lwa bafwa, bisa muhyula:
MAR 12:19 «Mulongi, Moyize kátusonikina bwabu: "Yuka ni yakala mosi kafwa konda kubuta mwana, myaki wandi kalunga kwela mufwidi ndangu katombula kikanda kya phangi wandi."
MAR 12:20 Kinga kwákala yi baphangi ba bayakala tsambwadi. Tsomi za bawu wákwela mukhetu amana wáfwa konda kusisa mwana.
MAR 12:21 Wazodi wámukwela mufwidi amana wáfwa konda kusisa keti mwana. Phila mosi yi wuna watatu;
MAR 12:22 amana keti mosi wa bawu tsambwadi kásisaku mwana. Kunima dya bawu boosu, mukhetu phi wáfwa.
MAR 12:23 Muna kilumbu kya lufutumuku lwa bafwa, tangwa batókama, wa nati kakála mukhetu meni wuna? Mukuma bawu tsambwadi bámukwela!»
MAR 12:24 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Taleti! Yi hakana lwisi ditotisila kwenu, lwisiku bakisa keti Masonuku, keti ngolu za Nzambi.
MAR 12:25 Mukuma, ku lufutumuku lwa bafwa, kwakálaku yi bayakala keti bakhetu bakwélana, kaasi bakála hanga banzyo muna mazilu.
MAR 12:26 Kikuma kya kufutumuka kwa bafwa, khaniku kedi lutanga, muna mukanda wa Moyize, mana bámuzimbwala bela-bela yi kivunza kya mbawu? Nzambi kázimbula: "Meni yenina Nzambi wa Bulahami, Nzambi wa Yizaki yi Nzambi wa Yakobi."
MAR 12:27 Disongidila ni keku Nzambi wa bafwa, kaasi wa batu bana benina mu luzingu. Luditotisi kwenu kimakulu.»
MAR 12:28 Mosi wa balongi ba mitsiku, wuna wábayuka buna bakala tendana yi phila kámona ni mboti kábavutwala, wísa hyula kwena Yesu: «Khi wawu mutsiku watheti wuhitini muna mitsiku myosu?»
MAR 12:29 Yesu wuvutudini: «Watheti: "Hinikina, Kiseledi, Pfumu Nzambi wetu, yandi lwesi wenina Pfumu.
MAR 12:30 Amana wazóla Pfumu Nzambi waku, yi mbundu yaku yosu yi moya waku wosu, yi ngangu zaku zoosu, yi ngolu zaku zoosu."
MAR 12:31 Wazodi: "Wazóla mukwenu hanga ngeyi meni." Kweku hika mutsiku wuluti myami myawu myodi.»
MAR 12:32 Mulongi wa mitsiku wumuzimbwadini: «Bwa bukheti, Mulongi! Kyedika wuzimbudini ni Pfumu Nzambi yandi mosi kenina amana heku wahika hanga yandi.
MAR 12:33 Amana ni kumuzola yi mbundu yandi yosu, yi ngangu zandi zoosu, yi ngolu zandi zoosu; yi kuzola mukwenu hanga yandi meni, buluti kimenga kya kuyoka kya muthu yi mikhayilu.»
MAR 12:34 Yesu buna kámona ni kávutula yi mayedi moosu, hanga wumuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi weku kyana yi Kipfumu kya Nzambi.» Amana keti mutu kámekaku hika kumuhyula kyufu.
MAR 12:35 Yesu kakala longa kuna nzu ya Nzambi, kahanga wubahyudini: «Abweti balongi ba mitsiku balenda zonzila ni Masiya kenina mwana wa Tavidi?
MAR 12:36 Yandi meni Tavidi, muna Kitembu Kyatoma, kázimbula: "Pfumu kázimbula kwena Pfumu wama: sikuka kuna kitata kyama, yi kuna yisíla bambeni baku ku sina dya bitambi byaku."
MAR 12:37 Yandi meni Tavidi kabati mutela: "Pfumu" Amana mu biki kalenda kadila hika mwana wandi?» Amana mulumba-lumba wa batu balawu bakala muhinikina yi tsambu.
MAR 12:38 Muna malongi mandi, Yesu kakala bazimbwala: «Dikengenu yi balongi ba mitsiku; bazodi kukangala yi mvwela za kaleyi amana batu babahekaka mboti muna mazandu;
MAR 12:39 bazodi kuzakala mu bifulu bya theti muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta, bazodi phi bifulu bya lukumu mu mikinzi.
MAR 12:40 Bisi botula bima muna nzu za bafwidi, bisi samba malombilu ma kaleyi kikuma kya kudimonikisa. Bawu batámbula pfundusu yina yalúta kitesu.»
MAR 12:41 Kunima Yesu bwosu kákala wasikuka kuna thwala ya mukunzu wa nzu ya Nzambi, kakala simbulula mulumba-lumba wa batu buna bakala sya mbongu. Bamvwama balawu bakala sya lawu.
MAR 12:42 Mufwidi mosi wa phutu wísa, yandi phi wásya makuta modi ma khunda mahitini dikuta dya tsuka.
MAR 12:43 Hanga wubatedi balonguki bandi amana wubazimbwadini: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa, mufwidi yandu wa phutu kasini kuluta boosu bana basini mu mukunzu.
MAR 12:44 Mukuma boosu bana báhani muna kulutuka kwa kuvwa kwa bawu; kaasi yandi, kásini muna kiphutu kyandi, kyosu kina kákadiki kyawu, kyosu kina kafwaniki mu kuzingila.»
MAR 13:1 Bwana kakala lubuka Yesu mu nzu ya Nzambi, mosi wa balonguki bandi wámuzimbwala: «Mulongi! Talandi, khi mutindu wa matadi, khi thungidi!»
MAR 13:2 Yesu wámuvutwala: «Wumoni thungidi zazi za mbuta? Kwasálaku keti tadi dimosi hana thandu ya tadi dikwawu dyakonda wulumuka.»
MAR 13:3 Buna kákala wazakala kuna mongu wa Olive, kuna thwala ya nzu ya Nzambi, Phetelu, Zyaki, Yowani yi Andele bámuhyula mu kingenga:
MAR 13:4 «Tuzimbwala, khi tangwa masálama mambu mama, khi kyawu kidimbu kyasóngila tsuka ya mambu mana moosu?.»
MAR 13:5 Hanga Yesu wuyandiki mu kubazimbwala: «Kebenu, mutu kaluhukumunaku.
MAR 13:6 Lawu bakwísa mu khumbu ya meni, mu kuzimbula: "Meni yenina Kidisitu" amana batu balawu babáhukumuna.
MAR 13:7 Tangwa lwayúka kuzonzila mvita yi pfweta-pfweta za mvita: luvumukaku mbundu; bulungi ni mambu mana masalama, kaasi yakálaku kedi tsuka.
MAR 13:8 Mukuma kanda dimosi dyanwánisa kanda dikwawu, amana luyalu lumosi lwanwánisa luyalu lukwawu; amana kunikana kwa mafu yi nzala byakála muma mwahika. Lwakála luyandiku lwa misongu.
MAR 13:9 Dikengenu benu-benu; balúlambula mu nganda amana balúbeta muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta; lwatélama kuna thwala ya bapfumu ba mbanza yi bakyamvu kikuma kya meni, kyakála kimbangi kikuma kya bawu.
MAR 13:10 Bulungi theti Musamu wa Bukheti basamunawa kwena makanda moosu.
MAR 13:11 Tangwa balúnata mu kululambula, lutekilaku diyangisa kikuma kya mana lwazímbula, kaasi zimbulenu mana balúheka muna tangwa meni dina, mukuma ka benu ku lwazónza, Kitembu Kyatoma.
MAR 13:12 Phangi kalámbula phangi wandi ku lufwa, amana tata kalámbula mwana wandi; bana babáthutukila bibuti bya bawu amana babáhondisa.
MAR 13:13 Balúmenga kwena mutu wosu kikuma kya khumbu yama. Kaasi wuna wakwámina tii yi kuna tsuka, yandi kahúluka.»
MAR 13:14 «Buna lwamóna muzangi wanzanzi wakutelamisa muna kafwaniku kukala, mutu wuna wubati tanga kabakula! Hanga, bana bakála mu Yuteya batína mu myongu;
MAR 13:15 wuna wakála ha mudilu katulukahoku, kavutukaku kikuma kya kutambula kima ku nzu yandi;
MAR 13:16 amana wuna wakála ku bilanga kavutukaku ku manima kikuma kya kutambula muledi wandi.
MAR 13:17 Khi phasi kikuma kya bakhetu bana bakála ku bifundu yi kwena bana bakála mu kuyemika muna bilumbu meni bina!
MAR 13:18 Lombilenu ni mambu mama mabwaku mu tangwa dya kyosi kya lawu!
MAR 13:19 Mukuma, bilumbu meni bina byakála bilumbu bya kiwayi kya lawu, kiwayi kimosi, hanga kina kyakonda kedi kala tukidila ku luyandiku lwa phangamu yina káhangila Nzambi tsi yi buthwena bwabu, amana zakálamwoku hika buna kuluta.
MAR 13:20 Wadi ni Pfumu kákufikisaku bilumbu bina, wadi keti mutu kakhanaku zinga hika, kaasi kákufikisilabya kikuma kya bana básolama.
MAR 13:21 Amana ho mutu kaluzimbwala: "Kidisitu haha kenina!" Holo: "kuna kenina!" Lumukwikilaku.
MAR 13:22 Mukuma bamasiya ba bukamvi yi bambikudi ba bukamvi balúbuka; basóngila biphadi yi mambu ma kuyituka kikuma kya kuhukumuna, yuka bwaléndakana, bana kásola Nzambi.
MAR 13:23 Kebenu kwenu! Thekidi luzimbwala moosu.»
MAR 13:24 «Kaasi muna bilumbu bina, kunima dya kiwayi meni kina, tangwa kaphínda, ngondi kaséngulaku myesi myandi,
MAR 13:25 bathetimbwa babwa tukidila ku zilu, amana ngolu za mazilu zaníkana.
MAR 13:26 Hanga bamoni Mwana wa mutu buna kakwísa muna matuti yi ngolu za lawu, yi khembu.
MAR 13:27 Hanga wutumi banzyo amana bakútikisa batu ba tselu ya bana kásola, tukidila tselu ya tsi yi kuna tselu ya ku zilu.»
MAR 13:28 «Mbandu ya kingana kya mufiki yaluheka dilongi: buna lwamóna ni miti wusawakidini, lwisi zaya ni tsungi ya pha yibwesukini.
MAR 13:29 Phila mosi yi kwena benu, tangwa lwamóna bima bina byosu, zayenu ni Mwana wa mutu wekina bela-bela, muna mwelu.
MAR 13:30 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa: mbandu ya batu baba, yahítaku kedi yi kuna masálamina mambu mana moosu.
MAR 13:31 Zilu yi tsi byatóta, kaasi ndinga zama zalendaku tota.»
MAR 13:32 «Kikuma kya mana matadidini kilumbu yi tangwa, ka mutu ku wuzayibya, keti banzyo muna zilu, keti Mwana; kaasi Tata yandi lwesi.
MAR 13:33 Kebenu, temunenu mesu, mukuma luzayiku mu khi tangwa mabwa.
MAR 13:34 Dyakála hanga mutu mosi wénda mu kitambu: wusisini nzu yandi, wuhanini kiyeka kwena basadi bandi; kosu mutu yi kisalu kyandi, amana wásenda kwena tsinzidi kakala watemuna.
MAR 13:35 Disongidila, kalenu batemuna, mukuma luzayiku keti khi tangwa kakwísa mukwa nzu: mu masikidika, ho mu kati kya kisuku, ho mu khoku wa theti, ho mu suka.
MAR 13:36 Kalenu mu bweya kinga katula mu kithulumukina amana kisa luwana banimba.
MAR 13:37 Mana mbati luzimbwala, nzimbudima kwena batu boosu: "Kalenu batemuna!»
MAR 14:1 Bilumbu byodi byásala mu kuta mukinzi wa Phaki yi mukinzi wa mapha makonda muvimbu. Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku bakala sanda phila ya kumukwata Yesu mu mayedi mambi ndangu bamuhonda.
MAR 14:2 Bakala zimbula: «Heku ni mu tangwa dya mukinzi, hanga kwakala nana mvwalangani mu kati dya batu.»
MAR 14:3 Yesu ku Betaniya kákala muna nzu ya Simoni mukwa bwasi. Buna kákala ku mesa mukhetu mosi wákota amana kákala yi mulangi wabasa yi mananasi ma mukwandi, ma thalu ya lawu. Wábula mulangi amana wázunzila mananasi hana mutwa wa Yesu.
MAR 14:4 Ndambu ya batu bahika báyuka kikudi-kudi, hanga beka dizimbwala bawu yi bawu: «Kikuma kya biki kuzanga mananasi mama bwabu?
MAR 14:5 Wadi bakhanima sumbisa mananasi mana mu thalu ya khama tatu za phata, amana mbongu bahana kwena batsukami!» Amana bakala mukumba mukhetu wuna.
MAR 14:6 Kaasi Yesu wázimbula: «Muyambulenu. Kikuma kya biki lubati muyangisila? Dyambu dya bukheti kahangini kwena meni.
MAR 14:7 Mukuma, batsukami lwakadiki bawu kosu tangwa, amana lufwani kubasadisa tangwa dina lumoni; kaasi meni twakádikiku yenu kosu tangwa.
MAR 14:8 Yandi kahangi buna kálendidini: katekidi zunzila mananasi mu lutu lwama kikuma kya kuyidika kuzika kwa lutu lwama.
MAR 14:9 Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadini: kwosu kuna básamuna Musamu wa Bukheti, muna tsi yosu, baménikiki phi mambu mama kahangini mukhetu yandu, kikuma kya kumubambuka.»
MAR 14:10 Yutasi Sikadyoti, mosi wa bawu kumi yi bodi, wénda kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi ndangu kabalambwala yandi Yesu.
MAR 14:11 Buna bámuyuka, básangwala lawu amana básila ni bamuheka mbongu. Yutasi kakala sanda tangwa dya mboti ndangu kamulambula Yesu.
MAR 14:12 Kilumbu kya theti kya mukinzi wa mapha makonda muvimbu, muna kilumbu kina bakala tambika kimenga kya mukinzi wa Phaki, balonguki bandi bamuzimbwadini: «Kubiki wuzodi ni thwenda kuyidikila madya ma mukinzi wa Phaki?»
MAR 14:13 Hanga Yesu wátuma bodi mu kati dya balonguki bandi amana wubazimbwadini: «Alwenda kuna mbanza, lwatúndakana yakala mosi wubati nata kalondu kenina yi mamba. Mulandenu.
MAR 14:14 Amana muna kakóta, zimbulenu kwena mukwa nzu: "Mulongi kazimbudini: Kubiki wenina mwanza wuna yidíla madya ma Phaki yi balonguki bama?"
MAR 14:15 Kalúsongila mwanza wumosi wenina wambuta kuna zilu, wenina wakuyidika kedi yi bima byosu. Yi mwamuna lwayídikila mambu kikuma kya betu.»
MAR 14:16 Balonguki bénda, buna bátula ku mbanza, báwana phi mambu bwosu kábazimbwala amana báyidika madya ma Phaki.
MAR 14:17 Ha mábwa masikidika, Yesu wátula hakimosi yi bawu kumi yi bodi.
MAR 14:18 Buna bákala kuna mesa yi kudyaka, Yesu wuzimbuni: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadini: mosi mu kati dya benu, wubati dya yi meni, kandámbula.»
MAR 14:19 Kiwayi kyábakwata lawu, báyandika mu kumuzimbwala mosi kunima mukwawu: «Ka meni ku, bweku?»
MAR 14:20 Yandi wábavutwala: «Kenina mosi muna kati dya benu kumi yi bodi, wuna wuvundikini koku ha longa dimosi yi meni, yandi wuna wandámbula.
MAR 14:21 Mwana wa mutu kabati kwenda, bwosu bwásonama kikuma kya yandi; kaasi khi kyadi kwena mutu wuna wamúlambula Mwana wa mutu! Bwálunga ni mutu wuna kabutukaku kwandi!»
MAR 14:22 Buna bákala dya, Yesu wátambula dipha, wásambuladya, wábukunadya amana wáhanadya kwena balonguki mu kuzimbula: «Tambulenu, lwalu lwenina lutu lwama.»
MAR 14:23 Kunima, wátambula bungu dimosi, kunima dya kuvutula matondu, wábahekadya, amana bánwaya boosu.
MAR 14:24 Hanga wubazimbwadini: «Mama menina menga mama, ma bulunda bwa Nzambi, mana matyakani kikuma kya batu lawu.
MAR 14:25 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadini: yinwaku hika vinu dina, tii yi kuna kilumbu kina yinwádya, dya pha, muna luyalu lwa Nzambi.»
MAR 14:26 Kunima dya kuyimbila mikunga, bálubuka, benda ku mongu wa Olive.
MAR 14:27 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Kisinza kyakála kikuma kya benu boosu, mukuma bwásonama bwabu: "Yimúhonda kalema, amana mikoku myamwángalakana."
MAR 14:28 Kaasi kunima dya kufutumuka kwama, yilútekidila kuna Ngadidi.»
MAR 14:29 Phetelu wumuzimbwadini: «Tangwa kyakála kisinza kikuma kya boosu, kyakálaku kikuma kya meni.»
MAR 14:30 Yesu wámuvutwala: «Mu kyedika yikuzimbwadini: lelu, muna phipha meni yayi, khoku kakókulaku kedi mbala zodi, ngeyi watsúwangana mbala tatu.»
MAR 14:31 Kaasi Phetelu wávutula yi ngolu zoosu: «Keti kufwa, yifwa hakimosi yi ngeyi, yikusuwanganaku.» Balonguki boosu bázimbula phi phila mosi.
MAR 14:32 Bisa tula homa hamosi bisi tela mu khumbu ya Ngetisemani, amana Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Zakalenu haha, kithama kina yikwata lombila.»
MAR 14:33 Wábonga ha kimosi yi yandi Phetelu, Zyaki yi Yowani. Amana wáyandika kuyuka kyadi yi kiwayi.
MAR 14:34 Hanga wubazimbwadini: «Mbundu yama mu kiwayi yenina yi kuna lufwa; salenu haha, amana kalenu batokama.»
MAR 14:35 Buna káphusana ndambu, wábwa ha tsi amana wálombila ni, yuka bwalendakana, tangwa meni dina dyahaluka yi yandi.
MAR 14:36 Kakala zimbula: «Aba, Tata, moosu maléndakana kwena ngeyi; halula kwena meni bungu dyadi. Kaasi ka luzolu lwa meni ku kaasi luzolu lwaku lwahangama.»
MAR 14:37 Yesu wísa kwena balonguki bawu batatu amana kábawana banimba; wázimbula kwena Phetelu: «Simoni, wunimbi? Wulendiku mu kutokama keti tangwa dimosi?
MAR 14:38 Kalenu batemuna, lombilenu phi, ndangu lubwaku mu kimeka. Kitembu kyazyama kyenina kaasi lutu lwalembwa lwenina.»
MAR 14:39 Wáhaluka hika amana wálombila mu kulandulula ndinga zimosi meni.
MAR 14:40 Kunima wisa vutuka hika, wubawani ku kilu, mukuma mesu ma bawu zitu mákala. Bámonaku biki bamuzimbwala.
MAR 14:41 Yesu wisa vutuka mu mbala ya tatu amana wábazimbwala: «Lunimbi hika, lulembwiki kwenu? Yimeni, tangwa dibwesukini. Mwana wa mutu bamulambudi ku moku ma basumuki.
MAR 14:42 Telamenu, thwendenu! Tala, wekina bela-bela wuna ndambudini!»
MAR 14:43 Muna tangwa meni dina kakala zonza Yesu, Yutasi, mosi wa bawu kumi yi bodi wátula hahana, hakimosi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu bakala yi mbedi za phoku yi khindi hana moku. Bábatuma kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi, balongi ba mitsiku yi bambuta ba bayuta.
MAR 14:44 Yutasi wuna wakala mulambula, watekila basongila kidimbu kimosi mu kuzimbula: «Wuna yibumbakana, yandi wuna. Mukwatenu amana munatenu buna bwa bukheti.»
MAR 14:45 Buna kátula, wubwesukini kuna kákala Yesu, wuzimbudini: «Labuni!» Amana wámubumbakana.
MAR 14:46 Hanga batu meni bana bamubwidini Yesu amana bamunatini.
MAR 14:47 Mosi wa bana bákala hahana, wáhola mbedi ya phoku, wámutapha musadi wa mbuta wa banganga Nzambi amana wámuhuta kwiti.
MAR 14:48 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Lwisi khwata yi mbedi yi khindi, hanga mbedi ni ndwandwa yenina?
MAR 14:49 Yíkala yenu bilumbu byosu kuna nzu ya Nzambi mu kulongaka, amana lwákhwataku. Kaasi mamana mabwini ndangu malungila Masonuku.»
MAR 14:50 Hanga boosu bamusisini, amana batini kwabawu.
MAR 14:51 Ngunza mosi wakala mulanda, wadivunga muledi wa thangi. Bámukwata,
MAR 14:52 kaasi yandi wásutula muledi amana wátina kikhonga.
MAR 14:53 Yesu, bamunata ku nzu ya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, kuna bákutakanina bambuta ba banganga Nzambi boosu, bambuta ba bayuta yi balongi ba mitsiku.
MAR 14:54 Phetelu kakala mulanda kuna kyana, yi kuna kyanzala kya nzu ya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi. Buna kákota muna kati, wázakala yi batsinzidi, kikuma kya yikuyeta mbawu.
MAR 14:55 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi kimvuka kyambuta bakala sanda kimbangi kya mbi kikuma kya Yesu, ndangu bamuzengila ndola ya lufwa, kaasi bámonakyoku.
MAR 14:56 Mukuma lawu dya bambangi ba luvunu bisa funda, kaasi bimbangi byáfwananaku.
MAR 14:57 Ndambu ya batu bálubuka mu kumutila kimbangi kyaki kya luvunu:
MAR 14:58 «Twámuyuka yandu mu kuzimbula: "Yiwúlumuna nzu ya Nzambi yayi bátunga ku moku ma batu, amana mu bilumbu bitatu, yitúngulula yikwawu yina yakonda tungama ku moku ma batu."»
MAR 14:59 Amana mbatanana buna, bimbangi bya bawu byákalaku fwanana.
MAR 14:60 Hanga mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wutelami hana kati dya lukutakanu, wáyufula kwena Yesu: «Keti kima wubatiku vutula? Biki wuzonzi kikuma kya bimbangi byabi babati kufundila baba?»
MAR 14:61 Kaasi Yesu kakalaku yakula, kakalaku vutula keti ndinga. Mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wámuhyula hika: «Ngeyi wenina Kidisitu, Mwana wa Nzambi wasambuka?»
MAR 14:62 Yesu wávutula: «Meni yandu. Amana lwamóna Mwana wa mutu wazakala kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi mukwa Ngolu zoosu amana kakwísa muna matuti ma zilu.»
MAR 14:63 Hanga mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wuyati miledi myandi, amana wuzimbudini: «Kikuma kya biki twasandila hika bambangi?
MAR 14:64 Luyuki benu-benu ngusi katukwani Nzambi; Abweti lubanzi benu?» Boosu bázimbula ni kufwa muna kufwa.
MAR 14:65 Hanga batu bahika bamuhumi metya kuna mbunzu, bamufidingi mbunzu amana bamuti makufi mu kuzimbula: «Bikuleti, keti nati wukubetini!» Amana batsinzidi bamuti mbata.
MAR 14:66 Buna kákala Phetelu wazakala kuna phenza, hana kyanzala, musadi mosi wa mukhetu wa mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wátula.
MAR 14:67 Buna kámona Phetelu wakala yeta mbawu, wámutala amana wuzimbudini: «Ngeyi phi, wukadikini yi Yesu, mwisi Nazaleti.»
MAR 14:68 Kaasi yandi wásuwangana mu kuzimbula: «Nzayiku, mbatiku bakula mana wuzodi wazimbula, ngeyi.» Kunima wálubuka ndangu kenda ku mwelu wa kyanzala; [hanga khoku mosi wukokuni.]
MAR 14:69 Musadi wa mukhetu wámumona hika amana wáyandikila mu kuzimbula kwena babana bákala hakana: «Yandu phi kenina mosi wa bawu!»
MAR 14:70 Amana yandi wásuwangana hika. Kunima dya tangwa dya khunda, babana bákala hakana bázimbula hika kwena Phetelu: «Kyedika, ngeyi wenina mosi wa bawu, mukuma mwisi Ngadidi phi wenina.»
MAR 14:71 Hanga Phetelu wuyandiki mu kudya ndefi: «Yukani meni yimuzayi mutu yandu, Nzambi kapheka ndola!»
MAR 14:72 Amana muna tangwa meni dina, khoku wákokula mu mbala ya zodi. Phetelu wáyubuka ndinga yina kámuzimbwala Yesu: «Khoku kakókulaku kedi mu ya mbala zodi, ngeyi watsúwangana meni mbala tatu.» Hanga wuyandiki mu kudila.
MAR 15:1 Kuma buna kwákhya, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi bákutakana hakimosi yi bambuta ba bayuta yi balongi ba mitsiku mu kimvuka kya mbuta. Kunima dya kumukasa Yesu, bámunata amana bámulambula kwena Philatu.
MAR 15:2 Amana Philatu wámuhyula: «Ngeyi, kyamvu wa Bayuta wenina?» Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Ngeyi meni wuzimbudibwa.»
MAR 15:3 Bimbangi lawu bakala mutila kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi.
MAR 15:4 Philatu wámuhyula hika: «Wubatiku vutula keti kima? Tala moosu mana babati kufundila!»
MAR 15:5 Kaasi Yesu kávutulaku hika keti kima, amana Philatu wáyituka lawu.
MAR 15:6 Bwosu bwákala ni mu mukinzi wosu wa Phaki, Philatu kakala sula mutu wa boloku mosi, wosu wuna bakala lomba batu.
MAR 15:7 Kinga yakala mosi, khumbu yandi Balabasi, wákala mu boloku hakimosi yi bandwandwa, kikuma kya buna káhonda mutu mu tangwa dya mvwalangani.
MAR 15:8 Mulumba-lumba wa batu bénda kuna nzu ya Philatu amana báyandika mu kumulomba ni kabahangila bwosu kyákala kikalulu kya bawu.
MAR 15:9 Philatu wábahyula: «Luzodi yiluyambwadila kyamvu wa Bayuta?»
MAR 15:10 Mukuma wázaya kwandi ni, bapfumu ba banganga Nzambi, kikuma kya kiphala bámulambwala yandi.
MAR 15:11 Kaasi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi bálundika batu ndangu balenga bayambwadila kaka Balabasi.
MAR 15:12 Philatu wáhyula hika: «Amana biki yihanga buthwena kikuma kya yandu lwisi tela ni kyamvu wa Bayuta?»
MAR 15:13 Bákalunga hika: «Mukhoka ha kitakani!»
MAR 15:14 Philatu wábahyula: «Khi mbi kahangini?» Kaasi bawu bákalunga hika ngolu: «Mukhoka ha kitakani!»
MAR 15:15 Philatu wázola kasephidisa mulumba-lumba wa batu, wábasudila yandi Balabasi. Kunima dya kumuzyatwasa mafimbu Yesu, wámulambula ndangu bamukhoka ha kitakani.
MAR 15:16 Baphumbulu bámubulumuna Yesu yi muna kyanzala kya nganda ya pfumu wa mbanza, amana bákhokika kibuka kya baphumbulu.
MAR 15:17 Bámuvwatisa mvwela ya kabengi amana bátunga mukhonzi wumosi wa tsaku, bávwatisawa kuna mutwa wandi.
MAR 15:18 Kunima báyandika mu kumuheka mboti: «Mboti, kyamvu wa Bayuta!»
MAR 15:19 Bakala muzyatula muswangina muna mutwa, kumuhuma metya yi kufukamaka kuna thwala ya yandi.
MAR 15:20 Tangwa bamanisa mu kumuseya, bámukatulaya mvwela yina ya kabengi amana bámuvwatisa hika miledi myandi. Kunima bámunata ku phenza ndangu benda mukhoka ha kitakani.
MAR 15:21 Mu kunata kitakani kyandi, baphumbulu bálundika mutu mosi wakala hita, wátuka ku bilanga, Simoni mwisi Sileni, tata wa Alekizande yi Lufwi.
MAR 15:22 Amana bámunata Yesu yi hana homa hana bisi tela ni Kolukota, disongidila: «Kizika kya Kibelengenzi kya mutwa.»
MAR 15:23 Bázola ni bamuheka vinu dya kusanga mila, kaasi yandi wábwisadya.
MAR 15:24 Bámukhoka ha kitakani, amana bákabana miledi myandi mu kubetilamya zeki ndangu bazaya kina káfwana kubonga kosu mutu.
MAR 15:25 Dyákala tangwa dya vwa dya suka, ha bámukhoka ha kitakani.
MAR 15:26 Bisona bina bánamika byákala tendula kikuma kya ndola yandi, byákala yi mihowu myami: «Kyamvu wa Bayuta.»
MAR 15:27 Hakimosi yi yandi, bákhoka hana kitakani bandwandwa bodi, mosi ku koku dyandi dya kitata, mukwawu ku koku dyandi dya kimama. [
MAR 15:28 Bwabuna málungila mana básonika mu nzila ya Masonuku: «Bámusya mu kanga dya batu bambi.»]
MAR 15:29 Bana bákala mu kuhita, bákala mutukwana yi kunikisaka mutwa mya bawu; yi kuzimbulaka: «He! Ngeyi wakala zimbula ni wáwulumuna nzu ya Nzambi amana mu bilumbu bitatu wutunguludiya,
MAR 15:30 dihulula ngeyi meni amana tuluka ha kitakani!»
MAR 15:31 Phila mosi phi kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi kwena balongi ba mitsiku bakala museya yi kuzonzaka: «Batu bahika kakala hulula amana kafwaniku kudihulula yandi meni!
MAR 15:32 Kidisitu, kyamvu wa Kiseledi, katuluka buthwena ha kitakani, ndangu twamona amana twakwikila.» Batu bana bámukhoka bawu ha kitakani bákala mutukwana phi.
MAR 15:33 Tuka tangwa dya tsinzi, phipha yábwa muna kinzunga kina kyosu tii yi kuna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika.
MAR 15:34 Muna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika, Yesu wákalunga mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Eloyi, Eloyi, lema sabakatani?» Disongidila: «Nzambi wama, Nzambi wama, kikuma kya biki wungyambwadidini?»
MAR 15:35 Bahika, mu kati dya bana bákala hahana, bámuyuka, bazimbudini: «Talandi, Diya, kabati tela yandu!»
MAR 15:36 Mutu mosi wátyakula thinu, wábonga kitini kya vuya, wávundikikya muna vinu dya ngani, amana wázitikadya ku muswangina, kamuheka yandi ndangu kanwa. Amana wuzimbudini: «Yambulenu, twatala kamba Diya kakwisa mutulula hahana!»
MAR 15:37 Kaasi Yesu wákalunga hika mu ndinga ya ngolu amana wátabula moya.
MAR 15:38 Kutala muledi wa zitu wuna wakala kabisa kizika kyahedila yi kina kyákala kyahedila kuluta mu nzu ya Nzambi wuyatukini mu byati byodi tuka ku londi yi kuna banda.
MAR 15:39 Buna kámona phila yina káfwila, hanga satudiyoni wuna wákala hakana, kuna thwala yandi, wuzimbudini: «Mu kyedika, mutu yandu Mwana wa Nzambi kákadikini!»
MAR 15:40 Hákala phi yi bakhetu bakala tala kuna kyana. Hana kati dya bawu, hákala yi Madiya mwisi Makatala, Madiya ngudi wa Zyaki wakhunda yi Zoze yi mukhetu wahika Salomeyi.
MAR 15:41 Babana bakala mulanda, bakala musadila phi tuka ku Ngadidi. Hákala hika yi bakhetu balawu bana bátombuka hakimosi yi yandi ku Yelusalemi.
MAR 15:42 Masikidika hana mabwi kedi, yi bwosu kyákala kilumbu kina kyatekidila sabata, kina bakala yidikila mukinzi,
MAR 15:43 wisa tula Yozefu, mwisi Adimateya, wuna bakala zitisa phi ku kibuka kyambuta. Kakala hingila yandi phi Kipfumu kya Nzambi. Wenda kwena Philatu mu kulomba lutu lwa Yesu.
MAR 15:44 Philatu wáyituka lawu mu kuyuka ni wutabudiki kedi moya, wátedisa satudiyoni amana wámuhyula yuka ni thama katabwadikini moya.
MAR 15:45 Buna káyuka meni dya satudiyoni, wáhana muswa kwena Yozefu mu kubonga mvumbi.
MAR 15:46 Yozefu wásumba muledi wa thangi, wámutulula Yesu ha kitakani, wámuvunga hana muledi wa thangi amana wámusikula muna mazyamu mana básima muna kitadi. Kunima wákidika kalunga tadi kuna mwelu wa mazyamu.
MAR 15:47 Madiya mwisi Makatala yi Madiya ngudi wa Zoze bakala simbulula bamona homa hana bámusya.
MAR 16:1 Buna dyáhita sabata, Madiya mwisi Makatala, Madiya ngudi wa Zyaki yi Salomeyi básumba mananasi kikuma kya kusita lutu lwa Yesu.
MAR 16:2 Muna kilumbu kyatheti kya phosa, muna kati kya suka tangwa weka lubuka, bénda ku mazyamu.
MAR 16:3 Bakala dihyula bawu yi bawu: «Nati watúbundwamina tadi dina dyenina dyakukidika ku mwelu wa mazyamu?»
MAR 16:4 Kaasi buna bávumbula mesu, bámona ni kalunga ka tadi dina, dyakubundumuna kedi kuna kabeta.
MAR 16:5 Buna bákota muna mazyamu; bámona hakana mwana wa yakala mosi, wasikuka kuna koku dya kitata, wávwata mvwela yimosi ya katoki amana báyuka bweya.
MAR 16:6 Kaasi wubazimbwadini: «Lukalaku yi bweya; Yesu mwisi Nazaleti lubati sanda, wuna bákhokiki ha kitakani. Wúfutumuki ku bafwa, kenahoku haka. Talenu homa hana bámusikudikini.
MAR 16:7 Kaasi alwenda zimbula kwena balonguki bandi yi kwena Phetelu: "Wulutekididini muna Ngadidi; kwakuna lwamúmonina, bwosu káluzimbwalabwa."»
MAR 16:8 Bálubuka mu mazyamu, amana benda thinu, bakala tekita yi kitswi. Amana bámenikinaku keti kwena mutu mukuma bweya bákala bwawu. [
MAR 16:9 Kunima dya lufutumuku lwandi, muna suka-suka dya kilumbu kyatheti kya phosa, Yesu wádimonikisa theti kwena Madiya mwisi Makatala, mwena yandi kálubula bitembu bya mbi tsambwadi.
MAR 16:10 Madiya wenda nata musamu kwena babana bákala yi Yesu. Mu khondu bákala yi kudilaka.
MAR 16:11 Tangwa báyuka kuzimbula ni Yesu mu luzingu kákala amana wámumona, bawu bákwikilaku.
MAR 16:12 Kunima dya bwabuna, Yesu wádimonikisa, mu mutindu wahika kwena balonguki bodi hana kati dya bawu bakala kwenda mu mahata.
MAR 16:13 Bisa vutukisa bawu phi mu kusamunabwa kwena bakwawu, kaasi keti bawu phi bábakwikilaku kaka.
MAR 16:14 Ku tsuka, Yesu wisa disongila kwena balonguki kumi yi mosi buna bákala kuna mesa; amana wábakaya kikuma kya kukonda kwa lukwikilu lwa bawu yi mbundu ya tadi ya bawu, kikuma bákwikilaku mwena batu bana bámumona kunima dya kufutumuka kwandi.
MAR 16:15 Kunima wubazimbwadini: «Alwenda muna tsi yosu amana samunenu Musamu wa Bukheti kwena phangamu yosu.
MAR 16:16 Wuna wakwíkila, watámbula phi mbotika kahúluka; kaasi wuna wakwíkilaku bamúzengila ndola.
MAR 16:17 Talenu bidimbu babázayila bana bakwíkila: bakúkwasa bitembu bya mbi mu khumbu ya meni; bazónza mu ndinga za pha;
MAR 16:18 Bakwáta banyoka kuna moku, honi banwini ndikila, keti ya khi mutindu, yabáhangaku keti kima; bathétika moku kwena bambefu amana bawu phi bakwata kola.»
MAR 16:19 Kunima dya kubazonzisa, Pfumu Yesu bámutombula ku zilu, amana wázakala kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi.
MAR 16:20 Amana balonguki benda mwangisa musamu muma mwosu. Pfumu kákala hakimosi yi bawu amana kakala lungisa Ndinga muna bidimbu bya khumbwa bina kákala byawu.]
LUK 1:1 Muzitu Thyofila, Batu ba lawu bámeka kusonika meni dya mambu mana máluta ha kati kya betu.
LUK 1:2 Básonikama bwosu bátuzimbwala betu, batu bana bámona mambu mana yi mesu ma thona tuka ku luyandiku, amana phi babana basadi ba ndinga ya Nzambi.
LUK 1:3 Ihana ni kwena meni phi, phyudiki bwa bukheti, meni dina dyosu, buna dyálutila, tuka ku luyandiku yi kuna tsuka, ihana mbonibwa bwa bukheti mu kukusonikina ngeyi muzitu Thyofila,
LUK 1:4 tsadibwa ndangu wazaya hika tsikiningi ya malongi mana wátambula.
LUK 1:5 Tangwa dina, Eloti kákala pfumu wa mulambu wa Yuteya. Kwákala yi nganga Nzambi mosi, khumbu yandi Zakadiya, wuna wákala mu mukanzu wa Abiya. Mukhetu wandi kakala mosi muna butuka dya Loni, yi mbuta wa theti, wa banganga Nzambi, bakala tela: Dizebeti.
LUK 1:6 Bákala bawu bodi batu basungama ku thwala ya Nzambi, bakala lemvuka phi buna bufwani ku mitsiku yi malongi moosu ma Pfumu.
LUK 1:7 Kaasi bákalaku yi mwana, mukuma Dizebeti kisita kákala, amana bawu bodi phi binunu bákala.
LUK 1:8 Kilumbu kimosi, Zakadiya kakala sala bisalu byandi bya kinganga ku thwala ya Nzambi mukuma dyákala tangwa dya mukanzu wa yandi mu kusalakya.
LUK 1:9 Bwosu yákala tsadidi ya banganga Nzambi, hanga babetini zeki mu kumusola ndangu kakota mu kikumbu kya Nzambi, kayoka phi pfwabidi.
LUK 1:10 Mulumba-lumba wa batu wosu wakala lombila ku phenza, mu tangwa dya kuyoka pfwabidi.
LUK 1:11 Hanga wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wumulubwakidi Zakadiya: wutelamiki kuna lweka lwa kitata lwa mesa mana ma kuyokila pfwabidi.
LUK 1:12 Zakadiya buna kamúmona, hanga mabanza mamuvwalangani, bweya bumukwatini.
LUK 1:13 Kaasi wanzyo wumuzimbwadi: «Yukaku bweya, Zakadiya, mukuma Nzambi wuyuki lombilu lwaku: mukhetu waku, Dizebeti, mwana wa yakala kakúbutila; wamúheka khumbu, Yowani.
LUK 1:14 Kakála tho ya kyesi kya lawu yi tsambu kikuma kya ngeyi, amana batu balawu phi basángwala kikuma kya lubutuku lwandi.
LUK 1:15 Mukuma yandi kakála mutu wa mbuta ku thwala ya Pfumu. Kanwikiku vinu keti malafu ma kufundika lo. Kakála wabasa yi Kitembu kyatoma tuka mu vumu dya ngudi wandi.
LUK 1:16 Kavútula batu ba lawu ba Kiseledi kwena Pfumu Nzambi wa bawu.
LUK 1:17 Kakwísa hanga mbambala wa Nzambi yi kitembu yi ngolu hanga mbikudi Diya, kikuma kya kukhundikisa batata yi bana ba bawu amana kasádisa batu bana báhakuka, mu kutambula ngangu za batu basungama; ndangu kayidika kikanda kya batu kina kyáyilama kikuma kya Pfumu.»
LUK 1:18 Kaasi Zakadiya wuzonzi kwena wanzyo: «Abweti yizáyila ni mambu mana menina ma kyedika? Mukuma meni yekina mbuta, mukhetu wama phi wekina mbuta.»
LUK 1:19 Wanzyo wumuvutwadi: «Meni yenina Ngabudyela; wuna wisi telama ku thwala ya Nzambi mu kumusadila; yandi kathumini ndangu yikuzimbwala amana yikunatina Musamu wa Bukheti wawu.
LUK 1:20 Kaasi ngeyi, wukwikidiku mu ndinga za meni zina zakwísa lungila mu tangwa dyandi; ihana ni kamama wakítuka, kilumbu yikuna malúngila mambu mama.»
LUK 1:21 Muna tangwa meni dina, batu bakala hingila Zakadiya, hanga bekayituka bwosu kázingidila mu kati dya kikumbu.
LUK 1:22 Kaasi ha kálubuka, kálendaku kubazonzisa amana batu babakisa ni mbona mesu kámoni mu kikumbu. Kakala basongila mu bidimbu, kuna yandi mutu, wusadi kamama.
LUK 1:23 Ha kámanisa, Zakadiya, tangwa dyandi dina kafwana kasala bisalu mu nzu ya Nzambi, hanga wuvutuki ku nzu yandi.
LUK 1:24 Kunima dya matangwa, mukhetu wandi Dizebeti wáyimita vumu amana wuswami ngonda tanu muna nzu. Wudizonzidi yandi meni ni
LUK 1:25 «Tala mambu kasadi Pfumu kikuma kya meni: buthwena, wutambwasini kukhutumuna mu dyambu dina dyakala pheka tsoni ku mesu ma batu.»
LUK 1:26 Muna ngonda ya sambanu, Nzambi wáhitika wanzyo Ngabudyela muna mbanza mosi ya Ngadidi, khumbu ya yawu Nazaleti,
LUK 1:27 kwena ndumba wa mukhetu mosi bázitikila mu kimbayi kwena yakala mosi bakala tela Yozefu. Mutu yandu kákala mosi muna butuka dya kyamvu Tavidi. Khumbu ya ndumba wa mukhetu wuna Madiya.
LUK 1:28 Wanzyo wákota muna nzu yandi, wumuzimbwadi phi: «Mboti Madiya! Pfumu wukusadidi mamboti ma lawu, yandi kenina yi ngeyi.»
LUK 1:29 Madiya buna káyuka mambu mana, wekina yangalakanu; wekadihyula thendula ya mboti meni yina.
LUK 1:30 Hanga wanzyo wumuzimbwadini: «Tekitaku, Madiya, mukuma Nzambi wukusadidi mambu ma bukheti.
LUK 1:31 Ka thama ku, vumu wayímita, wabúta mwana mosi wa yakala amana wamúheka khumbu, Yesu.
LUK 1:32 Kakála mutu wa mbuta amana bamútela ni mwana wa Nzambi wa Phungu wuluti. Pfumu Nzambi kamúheka, yandi, kiti kya kipfumu kya khaka wandi Tavidi
LUK 1:33 amana yandi, kayadiki mu matangwa moosu muna kikanda kya Yakobi, kipfumu kyandi kyakálaku yi tsuka.»
LUK 1:34 Madiya wuhyudini kwena wanzyo: «Abweti mahángamina, mambu mana kikuma meni, nzayiku kedi yakala?»
LUK 1:35 Wanzyo wumuvutwadini: «Kitembu Kyatoma kakúkulumukina amana ngolu za Nzambi wa Phungu wuluti zakúfidinga hanga kivula. Ihana ni Mwana wuna wabútuka, bamútediki: watoma, Mwana wa Nzambi.
LUK 1:36 Kiwutu kyaku Dizebeti, yandi phi ku vumu kenina, mwana wa yakala kabúta, mbatanana kinunu; yandi wuna bakala tela ni kisita, buthwena, vumu dilungisini ngonda sambanu.
LUK 1:37 Mukuma heku kima kyakonda lendakana kwena Nzambi.»
LUK 1:38 Hanga Madiya wuzimbudini: «Meni, yenina musadi wa Pfumu; yambula moosu malungila kikuma kya meni, bwosu wuzimbudibwa.» Amana wanzyo wumusisi.
LUK 1:39 Muna bilumbu byálanda, Madiya wubwi mu nzila wendi tswasu ku malondi ma Yuteya.
LUK 1:40 Wákota muna nzu ya Zakadiya amana wámuheka Dizebeti mboti.
