LUK 1:41 Muna tangwa meni dina káyuka, yandu, mboti ya Madiya, mwana wuzatukini muna vumu dyandi. Dizebeti kákala wabasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma
LUK 1:42 amana wuzimbudi mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Nzambi wukusakumuni kuluta bakhetu boosu, mwana wuna wabúta phi kenina wa kusakumuna.
LUK 1:43 Nani yenina meni ndangu, ngudi wa Pfumu wama, kisa thala?
LUK 1:44 Mukuma, tala, muna tangwa meni dina ngyukiki mboti yaku, mwana wuningani mu kyesi muna kati dya meni.
LUK 1:45 Mu kyedika, mu kyesi wenina, mukuma wukwikidini mambu mana kazonzikini Pfumu kikuma kya ngeyi ni malúngila.»
LUK 1:46 Hanga Madiya wuzonzi: «Yibati mutsikisa Pfumu yi mbundu yama yosu, kikuma kenina wa mbuta,
LUK 1:47 Moya wama, wenina wabasa yi kyesi kikuma kya Nzambi muhuludi wama;
LUK 1:48 Mukuma wuthadi meni musadi wandi wadikulumuna. Yi bwabuna ni, tuka lelu, batu boosu bayándika kuthela ni mukwa kyesi,
LUK 1:49 mukuma Nzambi mukwa ngolu zoosu wutsadidi mambu ma mbuta. Khumbu yandi yenina yatoma,
LUK 1:50 matangwa moosu kisi songila khenda zandi kwena batu bana bisi muzitisa.
LUK 1:51 Wusongidi ngolu za koku dyandi: wukudi batu bana benina yi mbundu za lulendu,
LUK 1:52 Wubakatudi bapfumu mu biti bya bawu bya kipfumu amana wubahingisi kwena batu badikulumuna bakala mu ndonga ya theti.
LUK 1:53 Wuhani mamboti ma lawu kwena batu bana bakala mawu nzala, amana wubakukwasi bamvwama moku ma khatu.
LUK 1:54 Wisa yakidila kikanda kya Kiseledi, musadi wandi: kázimbakanaku mu kusongila khenda zandi
LUK 1:55 kwena Bulahami yi kikanda kyandi, mu matangwa moosu bwosu kásila kwena bakhaka betu.»
LUK 1:56 Madiya wánanga yi Dizebeti, ngonda tatu, ku nima wávutuka kuhata dyandi.
LUK 1:57 Ha dyálunga tangwa dya kubuta, Dizebeti wábuta mwana wa yakala.
LUK 1:58 Bakwa mukombu wandi yi biwutu byandi bu bayuka ni Pfumu, wumusongidi khenda zandi mu mambu ma mbuta, ma bukheti kamusadidini, básangwala lawu ha kimosi yi yandi.
LUK 1:59 Kilumbu kya nana ha kyálunga, ku nima lubutuku, bisa ndangu bamukotisa mwana mukhanda; bazodi bamuheka khumbu ya tata wandi Zakadiya.
LUK 1:60 Kaasi ngudi wandi, kuna kákala, wuzimbudi: «Loni, khumbu yandi yakála Yowani.»
LUK 1:61 Bawu bamuvutwadini: «Muna kikanda kyaku mweku mutu wenina yi khumbu yina!»
LUK 1:62 Hanga bahyudi, mu bidimbu, kwena tata keti khi khumbu kazodi bamuheka mwana.
LUK 1:63 Zakadiya wálomba dibaya wusonikini: «Khumbu yandi Yowani.» Batu boosu báyituka.
LUK 1:64 Muna tangwa meni dina, Zakadiya wávutukila kuzonza: wekamukumisa Nzambi mu ndinga ya ngolu.
LUK 1:65 Bakwa mukombu boosu báyuka bweya amana mu kinzunga kina kyosu kya malondi ma Yuteya, báyandika kudimenika mambu mana másalama.
LUK 1:66 Batu boosu bana bakalama yuka, báyandika kuyindula muna mbundu ya bawu yi kudihyulaka: «Buthwena bwabu, nani kakwisa kituka mwana meni yandu?» Mu kyedika ngolu za Pfumu, wakala zawu mwana wuna.
LUK 1:67 Zakadiya, tata wa mwana meni yandu, kakala wabasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma; wáyandika kubikula bwabu:
LUK 1:68 «Lukumu kwena Pfumu, Nzambi wa kikanda kya Kiseledi, mukuma yandi kisa, ndangu kayakidila kikanda kyandi amana kahululakya phi.
LUK 1:69 Kahangi wisi lubula Muhuludi wa ngolu kikuma kya betu, mu kati kya kikanda kya kyamvu Tavidi, musadi wandi.
LUK 1:70 Mamana katekila zonza kwena bambikudi bandi ba Nzambi:
LUK 1:71 luhulusu lumosi lwisi tukatula kwena bambeni betu yi mu luyalu lwa batu bana bisi tumenga.
LUK 1:72 Wásongila kyadi kyandi kwena bakhaka betu amana kázimbakanaku kuyukana kwandi kwatoma.
LUK 1:73 Ihana ni Nzambi wázenga ndefi kwena Bulahami, tata wetu,
LUK 1:74 ni wátuhulula mu luyalu lwa bambeni, ndangu twamusadila konda bweya,
LUK 1:75 ndangu twalenga kala batu ba Nzambi yi batu ba masonga ku thwala yandi mu bilumbu byosu bya luzingu lwetu.
LUK 1:76 Amana kwena ngeyi mwana wama, bakutediki ni mbikudi wa Nzambi wa Phungu wuluti, mukuma wahíta ku thwala Pfumu mu kwenda muyidikila nzila
LUK 1:77 yi kusamuna kwena kikanda kyandi ni wisi bahulula mu kubalolula masumu ma bawu.
LUK 1:78 Nzambi wa betu, wabasa yi lungongu yi kyadi: katúkenzula mu mwini wandi wuna wisi tuka ku zilu bwosu kisi lubuka tangwa,
LUK 1:79 Kikuma kya kukenzula baba benina mu phipa yi mu kivula kya lufwa, mu kutwadisa bitambi byetu mu nzila ya ngemba.»
LUK 1:80 Mwana kakala kola, kakala phi ngolu mu kitembu. Kakala zingila mu nganga tii yi kuna kilumbu kina kisa disongila kwena batu ba kikanda kya Kiseledi.
LUK 2:1 Muna tangwa meni dina, pfumu wa mbuta wa mulambu wa Loma, Khayisala Okisiti, káhanga wulubudi mutsiku ni batu boosu benda disonikisa khumbu.
LUK 2:2 Yi mbala ya theti ya kusonikisa khumbu, yásalama mu tangwa meni dina kákala Kidinwusi pfumu wa mukombu wa Sidiya.
LUK 2:3 Amana batu boosu bákala kwenda mu kudisonikisa khumbu, kosu mutu, kuna mbanza yandi ya kisina.
LUK 2:4 Yozefu, yandi phi, wutuki ku Nazaleti, mbanza ya Ngadidi, wendi ku Betelemi, mbanza yimosi ya Yuteya, kuna kábutwakila kyamvu Tavidi; mukuma yandi phi kákala mu kikanda kya Tavidi.
LUK 2:5 Kenda disonikisa khumbu yi mbayi wandi, Madiya, wákala ku kifundu.
LUK 2:6 Muna tangwa medina bákala ku Betelemi, hanga kilumbu kya kubuta kifwani.
LUK 2:7 Madiya wubuti mwana wandi wa yakala, mwana wandi wa theti; wumuvungi ha miledi, wumunimbiki muna bangwa dina bidila bambisi, kikuma mwákalaku kizika, mu nzu ya banzenza kikuma kya bawu.
LUK 2:8 Muna kinzunga mekina, mwákala yi bakalema bakala leka mu tseki, mu kukinda bibulu bya bawu.
LUK 2:9 Wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wubalubwakidi, khembu ya Pfumu yibayiniki hana bákala boosu. Hanga bweya bubakwati lawu.
LUK 2:10 Kaasi wanzyo wubasamwani: «Luyukaku bweya, mukuma Musamu wa Bukheti yilunatini, wuna wásephidisa lawu, batu boosu:
LUK 2:11 mu phipha ya lelu, muna mbanza ya Tavidi, mubutukidini Muhuludi kikuma kya benu; yi Kidisitu, Pfumu.
LUK 2:12 Talenu bidimbu lwamúzayila: lwamóna mwana mosi wa khunda, wa kuvunga ha miledi, wa kunimbika phi muna bangwa dimosi.»
LUK 2:13 Muna mbala mosi, khumbi-khumbi ya banzyo ba ku zilu, kumosi yi wuna wa theti, bakala zatula Nzambi, bakala zimbula:
LUK 2:14 «Khembu kwena Nzambi muna kisoka kya mazilu yi ngemba hana tsi kwena batu babana kisi tonda!»
LUK 2:15 Tangwa bávutuka, banzyo, ku zilu, hanga bakalema ba mikoku bazimbudi bawu yi bawu: «Thwendenu tii yi kuna Betelemi, ndangu twamona mambu mana mabwi kuna, mana katusamwani Pfumu, twazaya.»
LUK 2:16 Hanga bakinani kukwenda, bamuwani phi Madiya yi Yozefu yi mwana khunda wa kunimbika muna bangwa.
LUK 2:17 Tangwa bámumona, bayandiki kumenika mambu mana kábasamwana wanzyo, matadidi mwana.
LUK 2:18 Batu boosu bana báyuka meeni dya bakalema, hanga bayituki.
LUK 2:19 Madiya, yandi, kakala zindika mambu mana moosu muna mbundu amana kakala yindula lawu.
LUK 2:20 Ku nima, bakalema bávutuka kwena bawu, báyandika kuzatula yi kukumisa Nzambi kikuma kya mambu mana báyuka yi mana bámona, mukuma moosu máluta bwosu kábasamwana wanzyo.
LUK 2:21 Kilumbu kya nana ha kyálunga, kunima lubutuku, hanga bámukotisa mwana mukhanda, bamuheki phi khumbu ya Yesu, yina káhana wanzyo kwena Madiya, hana khaku kayimita vumu.
LUK 2:22 Amana tangwa ha dyálungila ndangu Yozefu yi Madiya balungisa lukanu lwa kudisemisa bwosu buna myakala lomba mitsiku mya Moyize. Hanga bamunati mwana ku nzu ya Nzambi ya Yelusalemi ndangu bamutambika kwena Pfumu,
LUK 2:23 kikuma básonika mu mitsiku mya Pfumu: «Mwana wosu wa yakala wa theti wabútuka, kakála watoma kikuma kya Pfumu.»
LUK 2:24 Bibuti byandi bisa tambika mukhayilu bwosu bwakala lomba mu mitsiku mya Pfumu, mbwela boodi holo phombu boodi ba matuku.
LUK 2:25 Kwákala, kuna Yelusalemi, mutu mosi khumbu yandi Simeyoni. Kákala mutu wasungama; kákala muzitisa Nzambi, kákala hingila yandi wafwana kwisa mu kuhulula Kiseledi. Kitembu Kyatoma kákala yi yandi.
LUK 2:26 Amana Kitembu Kyatoma kátekila muzimbwala ni kakhanaku fwa kedi, konda kumona Kidisitu wa Pfumu.
LUK 2:27 Kitembu wumunatisi Simeyoni, wénda ku nzu ya Nzambi. Muna tangwa meni dina, bibuti bya Yesu bamunati ndangu balungisa lukanu bwosu milombini mitsiku,
LUK 2:28 Simeyoni wumuzangudi muna moku mandi, wuvutudi matondu kwena Nzambi mu kuzonza bwabu:
LUK 2:29 «Buthwena, Pfumu, wulungisi lusilu lwaku: wufwani wamuyambula muhika waku kafwa mu ngemba.
LUK 2:30 Mukuma mesu mama mamoni luhulusu lwaku,
LUK 2:31 luhulusu luna wátekila yidika ku thwala ya bikanda byosu:
LUK 2:32 lwenina mutemu wa kuzayikisa kwena batu ba tsi yosu; wawuna wákala lukumu lwa kikanda kyaku kya Kiseledi.»
LUK 2:33 Tata yi ngudi wa Yesu báyituka mu mambu mamana kázonza Simeyoni kikuma kya yandi.
LUK 2:34 Simeyoni wábasakumuna, wuzonzi phi kwena Madiya, ngudi wa Yesu: «Nzambi wámusola mwana yandu kikuma kya yandi, batu ba lawu bábwa, bahika phi bátombuka, mu Kiseledi. Kakala kidimbu kya Nzambi kaasi batu ba lawu bamubwisa,
LUK 2:35 amana mabanza ma batu ba lawu máswama mu mbundu, kalúbulama ha tseki. Kwena ngeyi, Madiya, phasi za lawu wáyuka ku mbundu hanga ngumba yikutubudi mbundu.»
LUK 2:36 Kwákala hika yi mbikudi mosi wa mukhetu, khumbu yandi Ana, mwana mukhetu wa Phanuwedi, mukwa kikanda kya Asidi. Wanuna kákala, kázinga yi yakala dyandi wa kingunza, mvula tsambwadi,
LUK 2:37 ku nima, wasala mufwidi, kánanga mvula makumi nana yi ya. Kakalaku tina nzu ya Nzambi, kaasi kakala sadila Nzambi phipha yi mwini mu kuzila kudya yi mu kulombila.
LUK 2:38 Yandi phi wátula mu tangwa medina, yandiki kuvutula matondu kwena Nzambi. Wumuzonzidi mwana kwena batu boosu, bana bakala hingila ni Nzambi kahulula Yelusalemi.
LUK 2:39 Tata yi ngudi wa Yesu, ha bálungisa lukanu lwosu, bwosu milombi mitsiku mya Pfumu, bávutuka yi yandi ku Ngadidi, ku mavula ma bawu ma Nazaleti.
LUK 2:40 Mwana kakala kola yi kikesa, wábasa yi mudimu, khenda za Nzambi zákala yi yandi.
LUK 2:41 Kosu mvula, bibuti bya Yesu bakala kwenda ku Yelusalemi kikuma kya mukinzi wa Phaki.
LUK 2:42 Ha kálungisa Yesu mvula kumi yi zoodi, bamunati bwosu kyákala kikalulu kya bawu.
LUK 2:43 Ha bamanisa kuta mukinzi, bávutuka, kaasi mwana sanda, Yesu, wásala ku Yelusalemi; bibuti byandi bázayaku.
LUK 2:44 Babanza ni Yesu kákala yi bakwawu khunda ba mu nzila, bana bakala kangala bawu amana básala kilumbu kimosi mu nzila. Hanga bayandiki kumusanda hana kati kya biwutu yi banduku ba bawu,
LUK 2:45 Kaasi bámusengumunaku. Bávutuka hika ku Yelusalemi yi kwenda musosaka, kinzila-kinzila.
LUK 2:46 Kilumbu kya tatu, bámusenguna muna nzu ya Nzambi: wasikuka hana kati dya balongi ba mitsiku, mu kubahinikina yi mu kubahyula byufu.
LUK 2:47 Batu boosu bana bakala muhinikina, bakala yituka kikuma kya ngangu zandi yi mvutu zina kakala bavutwala.
LUK 2:48 Ha bámusenguna, bibuti byandi, báyituka lawu amana ngudi wandi wumuzimbwadi: «Mwana wama, kikuma kya biki wutuhangidi bwabuna? Tataku yi meni, mu kiwayi kya lawu tukakusandila.»
LUK 2:49 Yandi wubavutwadini: «Kikuma kya biki lubati tsandila? Lwazayabwoku ni yifweti landila mambu ma Tata wama?»
LUK 2:50 Kaasi bábakulaku mambu mana kakala bazimbwala.
LUK 2:51 Yesu wákulumuka nzila mosi yi bawu ku Nazaleti. Kakala balemvukila. Ngudi wandi kakala sweka mambu mana moosu muna mbundu yandi.
LUK 2:52 Amana Yesu kakala kola yi mu mudimu yi mu malutu, kákala hana phi tsambu kwena Nzambi yi kwena batu.
LUK 3:1 Yákala mvula ya kumi yi tanu, ya luyalu lwa Khayisala Tibela. Hana Phosi Philatu kákala muyadi wa kinzunga kya Yuteya. Eloti yandi káyala ku Ngadidi, amana phangi wandi wa yakala Fidiphu ha kinzunga kya Kitudi yi Talakonititi. Lusanyasi kakala tala kinzunga kya Abileni.
LUK 3:2 Ana yi Khayifu bákala bambuta ba banganga Nzambi. Ndinga ya Nzambi yáyukalakana kwena Yowani, mwana wa yakala wa Zakadiya, muna nganga.
LUK 3:3 Yowani wáyandika kukangala kinzunga kina kyosu kyatalana yi nzadi Yolutani. Weka longa mbotika ya kusoba bikalulu kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu.
LUK 3:4 Bwosu buna bwásonama mu mukanda wa ndinga za mbikudi Yesaya: «Ndinga mutu wubati bekitila muna nganga: Yidikenu nzila ya Pfumu, musungikilenu tuma twa nzila bukheti!
LUK 3:5 Beti dyosu dyazíkama yi mongu yi matunda byosu byasíkunuka; nzila zina za khonda zasúngama, nzila za mabulu baséngwadilaza.
LUK 3:6 Amana mutu wosu kamóna luhulusu kahána Nzambi.»
LUK 3:7 Mulumba-lumba wa batu bakala kwisa kwena Yowani ndangu kababotika. Kakala bazimbwala: «Mbandu ya masawa! Nati wulusongidi ni lwatina khabu za Nzambi zina zibati kwisa?
LUK 3:8 Salenu mambu ma bukheti, hanga miti wuna wisi ha bibundu bya bukheti, mu kusongila ni benu, lusobini bikalulu byenu amana ludizonzilaku: "Betu, khaka wetu Bulahami." Mukuma, yiluzimbwadibwa ni Nzambi kalenda kitula matadi mama, bana ba Bulahami!
LUK 3:9 Amana kisoka bela-bela kyenina mu kukwanga miti tuka ku misodi: miti wosu wuna wisiku buta bibundu bya bukheti bakwángawa, balosiwa phi ku mbawu.»
LUK 3:10 Kibuka kimuhyudi: «Amana biki fwani twahanga?»
LUK 3:11 Wubavutwadi: «Wuna wenina yi miledi myodi, kakabisa yi wuna kondi muledi, mutindu mosi phi yi mutu wuna wenina yi bima bya kudya, kahanga bwabuna.»
LUK 3:12 Bakalaki ba phaku bísa ndangu babotama amana bahyudi kwena Yowani: «Mulongi, biki fwani twahanga?»
LUK 3:13 Yowani wubavutwadini: «Lulutulaku thalu yina bázenga kikuma kya phaku.»
LUK 3:14 Baphumbulu, bawu phi bamuhyudini: «Amana betu, biki twahánga?» Wubavutwadi mvutu: «Lubwotulaku mbongu kwena mutu, keti kumuhunina musamu, kaasi tambwasenu yi kyesi lufutu lwenu.»
LUK 3:15 Batu boosu bakala hingila yi kivuvu kyosu, bekadihyula kuna mbundu ni ngatu Yowani, fwani kakala Masiya.
LUK 3:16 Hanga Yowani wubazimbwadi bawu boosu: «Meni, yibati lubotika mu mamba; kaasi wuna wisi kwisa, wuphiti meni mu ngolu: yeku walunga mu kukutumuna misinga mya tsabatu zandi. Kalubotika mu Kitembu Kyatoma yi mu mbawu.
LUK 3:17 Wusimbi muyungulu muna moku mandi ndangu kasola ngenza za bukheti yi tswala. Kawóngika ngenza za bukheti, wuswekiza muna khila, kaasi, tswala, kayókaza mu mbawu yina yisiku zima.»
LUK 3:18 Yowani kakala basidingisa batu yi milongi mya hika mya lawu.
LUK 3:19 Kaasi Yowani kakala mukaya Eloti, wuna wakala yala ku Ngadidi, kikuma wákwela Elodyadi, mukhetu wa phangi wandi wa yakala; mambu mambi ma lawu hika káhanga.
LUK 3:20 Hanga Eloti wuyiki hika dyambu dimosi dya mbi lawu: wumukwatisi, mu boloku, Yowani.
LUK 3:21 Batu ba lawu bakala botama, Yesu phi wábotama. Muna tangwa medina kakala lombila, zilu dyákanguka,
LUK 3:22 amana Kitembu Kyatoma wákulumuka kwena yandi mu kimwesa mutu kya Phombu. Amana ndinga yimosi yituki ku zilu, yizonzi: «Ngeyi wenina Mwana wama watondama; mwena ngeyi mwena kyesi kyama.»
LUK 3:23 Bela-bela yi mvula makumatatu Yesu káyandika kisalu kyandi. Bwosu bakala mubanzila, batu, ni mwana Yozefu; tala mulonga wa butuka dya bakhaka bandi: Hedi;
LUK 3:24 Mathata, Lefi, Meleki, Yanayi, Yozefu,
LUK 3:25 Matatyasi, Amosi, Nawumi, Esidi, Nakhayi,
LUK 3:26 Mati, Matatyasi, Semeyini, Yoseki, Yota,
LUK 3:27 Yowana, Lesa, Zolubabedi, Salasyedi, Nedi,
LUK 3:28 Mediki, Adi, Kosami, Edimatami, Elu,
LUK 3:29 Yesu, Edyezedi, Yodimi, Mathata, Lefi,
LUK 3:30 Simeyoni, Yuta, Yozefu, Yonami, Edyakimi
LUK 3:31 Meleya, Mena, Mathata, Natani, Tavidi,
LUK 3:32 Yese, Obedi, Bozi, Sala, Nasoni,
LUK 3:33 Aminatabi, Adimini, Adini, Hesiloni, Phelesi, Yuta,
LUK 3:34 Yakobi, Kizaki, Bulahami, Tela, Nahodi,
LUK 3:35 Seluki, Lewu, Pheleki, Hebedi, Syela,
LUK 3:36 Kayinami, Alipakisati, Semi, Nowa, Lameki,
LUK 3:37 Matusalemi, Enoki, Yaleti, Maleleyedi, Kayinami,
LUK 3:38 Enosi, Seti, Atamu wuna kahanga Nzambi.
LUK 4:1 Yesu, ha kálubuka mu nzadi Yolutani, wubasi yi Kitembu kyatoma, yandi wumunatisi mu nganga.
LUK 4:2 Kwakuna, kasala bilumbu makumaya, Satana wendi ndangu kamuhukumuna. Kakalaku dya keti kima, bilumbu meni byabina byosu, amana kunima nzala yimukwati.
LUK 4:3 Hanga kiphidi-mutu wumuzimbwadi: «Kamba ngeyi Mwana Nzambi wena, zimbula kwena tadi dyadi dyakituka dipha!»
LUK 4:4 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Básonika mu mukanda wa Nzambi: "Mutu kazingilaku lwesi mu mapha."»
LUK 4:5 Kiphidi-mutu wumunati ha tunda, mu tangwa dimosi, wumusongidi bipfumu bya tsi byosu,
LUK 4:6 amana kiphidi-mutu wumuzimbwadi: «Yikuheka ngolu zoosu yi khembu ya luyalu lwa tsi yayi. Mu kyedika, meni báheka kiyeka kya bima bina byosu, yihánabya phi kwena mutu wuna thondi meni-meni.
LUK 4:7 Honi wapfukamina, byabi byosu bya ngeyi byakituka.»
LUK 4:8 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Básonika mu mukanda wa Nzambi: "Fukamina lwesi Pfumu Nzambi waku, yandi, yandi mosi lwesi wasadila."»
LUK 4:9 Kiphidi-mutu wumunati hika ku Yelusalemi, wumunenginiki kuna kisoka kya mudilu wa nzu ya Nzambi amana wumuzimbwadi: «Honi ngeyi, wu Mwana wa Nzambi, ditsusula tuka haha yi hana tsi;
LUK 4:10 Mukuma básonika mu mukanda wa Nzambi: "Nzambi kahána muswa kwena banzyo bandi ndangu bisa kulema."
LUK 4:11 Amana phi "bakulela muna moku ma bawu ndangu kulu dyaku didikhukulaku ku tadi dimosi."»
LUK 4:12 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Básonika mu mukanda wa Nzambi: "Wamekaku Pfumu Nzambi waku."»
LUK 4:13 Ha kásanda kuhukumuna Yesu, mitindu myosu, kunima, kiphidi-mutu wumusisi kikuma kya tangwa dya hika.
LUK 4:14 Yesu, wabasa yi ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma, wávutuka ku Ngadidi. Khululuka ya khumbu ya Yesu, yáyalangana muna mulambu wa Ngadidi wosu.
LUK 4:15 Kwakuna, kakala longa mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta amana mutu wosu kakala muzatula.
LUK 4:16 Yesu wénda ku Nazaleti, kuna kátsatsukila. Kilumbu kya sabata, wákota mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta bwosu kyákala kikalulu kyandi. Telami kikuma kya kutanga masonuku
LUK 4:17 amana bamuheki mukanda wa kuvunga kásonika mbikudi Yesaya. Hanga vungumuniwa, wumoni homa hana básonika:
LUK 4:18 "Kitembu kya Pfumu kyenina ha thandu ya meni, wátsita masi ndangu yinata Musamu wa Bukheti kwena baphutu. Wáthuma ndangu yisamuna kwena batu ba boloku ni lulubuki, kwena baphofu, ni bamóna hika wanga, kiphwanza kwena batu bena mu kihika,
LUK 4:19 kikuma yisamuna mvula ya mamboti ma Pfumu kwena batu."
LUK 4:20 Kunima Yesu wávungawa mukanda, wuhekiwa kwena musadi amana wuzakadi. Batu boosu bakala mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, bahungudi mesu kwena yandi.
LUK 4:21 Hanga wuyandiki kubasamwana: «Masonuku mama, tutangi mu kitini kyaki, kwena benu, lelu malungidi.»
LUK 4:22 Boosu báyandika kuta kimbangi kya bawu kikuma kya Yesu amana báyandika kuyituka ku mambu ma bukheti kakala zonza. Bakala zonza: «Yandu, ka mwana Yozefu ku?»
LUK 4:23 Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Mu kyedika, kilumbu, lwathíla kingana kyaki: "Munganga, dibuka ngemeni." Lwanzímbwala hika: "Twáyuka mambu moosu wáhanga ku Kaphedinawuma, hangeti mambu mana, buthwena, mu mbanza ya ngemeni yayi."»
LUK 4:24 Kunima, wukosikidini: «Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi ni kweku mbikudi wisi lumina mu tsi yandi.
LUK 4:25 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi ni mu tangwa dya mbikudi Diya, bafwidi lawu bákala mu Kiseledi; zilu dyánokisaku mvula, mu mvula tatu yi ngonda sambanu, nzala lawu yákota muna mulambu wosu.
LUK 4:26 Kinga, Nzambi, kámutumaku Diya kwena mosi wa bawu, kaasi kwena mufwidi mosi lwesi wuna wakala zingila ku hata dya Salepita, mu kinzunga kya Sitoni.
LUK 4:27 Kwákala phi yi bakwa bwasi balawu mu tangwa dya mbikudi Disa, mu Kiseledi; kinga keti mosi wa bawu kásemaku lutu, kaasi Namani, lwesi, mwisi Sidya wásema lutu.»
LUK 4:28 Ha báyuka ndinga meni zina, boosu bákala muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, bahanga, bamingi.
LUK 4:29 Bátelema, bamulubudi, Yesu, kufula dya mbanza amana bamunati ku londi dya mongu wuna bátunga Nazaleti, ndangu bamununguna ha tsi.
LUK 4:30 Kaasi wubalwetuki hana kati wenda kwandi.
LUK 4:31 Hanga, Yesu wénda ku Kaphedinawuma, mbanza ya Ngadidi; kakala longa malongi mandi mu kilumbu kya sabata.
LUK 4:32 Batu bakala yituka mu phila kulonga kwandi, kikuma kakala zonza yi hamu.
LUK 4:33 Mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, mwákala yi mutu mosi bakala yangisa kwena kitembu kya mbi. Wakala kalunga:
LUK 4:34 «Ah! Yesu mwisi Nazaleti! Khi mambu ngeyi yi betu? Wisi ndangu watuzanga? Nzayi mboti keti nani wenina ngeyi: Watoma bátuma kwena Nzambi!»
LUK 4:35 Yesu wákayakya kitembu kina yi ngolu. Wuzonzi: «Dibata! Lubuka phi mwena mutu yandu!» Kitembu kya mbi kimubwisi ha tsi mutu wuna ku mesu ma batu boosu, amana kilubuki kwena yandi, konda kumuhanga kima kya mbi.
LUK 4:36 Amana batu boosu bákala hana báyituka lawu bekadihyula bawu yi bawu: «Khi mutindu wa ndinga yana? Mutu yandu kabati hana muswa yi ngolu yi hamu amana bitembu bya mbi bilubuki!»
LUK 4:37 Amana khululuka ya Yesu yámwangana muna mulambu meni wawuna wosu.
LUK 4:38 Yesu wulubuki muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, wendi ku nzu ya Simoni. Buko bwa mukhetu wa Simoni kákala wabela yi kikhafuma amana balombi kwena Yesu ndangu kahanga dyambu kikuma kya yandi.
LUK 4:39 Wuzenzamini kwena mukhetu wuna, amana muna ndinga ya ngolu, wukayikya kikhafuma kina. Muna mbala mosi, kimukatukini, wutelamini wuyandikini phi kubaheka madya.
LUK 4:40 Ha kwáyila kuma, boosu bana bákala yi bambefu ba bawu bana bákala yi makhasi ma mutindu yi mutindu, babanati kwena Yesu, yandi weka bathetika moku amana wubabuki.
LUK 4:41 Amana bitembu bya mbi bilubuki kwena bambefu balawu, mu kukalunga: «Ngeyi wenina Mwana wa Nzambi!» Kaasi Yesu wáyandika kukayabya yi kukandikisabya ndangu bizonzaku hika, mukuma byawu phi byazaya ni Yesu, Masiya kákala.
LUK 4:42 Buna kwákhya kuma, Yesu wálubuka mu mbanza, wenda hunga mu tseki. Mulumba-lumba wa batu wáyandika kumusosa; ha bámumona, bázola kazakala yi bawu.
LUK 4:43 Kaasi Yesu kábazimbwala: «Bufwani kwena meni yenda samuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa kipfumu kya Nzambi ku mbanza za hika, kikuma kya bwabuna báthumina.»
LUK 4:44 Amana Yesu kakala longa mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta za Yuteya.
LUK 5:1 Kilumbu kimosi, Yesu wátelama kuna kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta dya Ngenezaleti amana kibuka kya batu bakala lundakana mu kuwongama kikuma kya kuyuka ndinga ya Nzambi.
LUK 5:2 Yesu wámona midimba myodi kuna khungu ya mamba: balobi ba batsema bátuluka mu midimba, bekasukula mawanda ma bawu.
LUK 5:3 Yesu wázanza muna mudimba wumosi, wuna wákala wa Simoni, wumulombi ni kanunguna koma ku mamba, kakatuka mu tsenga. Yesu wázakala muna mudimba, wáyandika kulonga malongi mandi kwena kibuka kya batu.
LUK 5:4 Tangwa kámanisa kulonga, wázimbula kwena Simoni: «Phusana kuna dingu dya ndindi amana losenu mawanda menu ndangu lwaloba.»
LUK 5:5 Simoni wumuvutwadini: «Mulongi, tunyokuki phipha yosu mu kuloba, keti kima tukwatiku. Kaasi muna ndinga ya ngeyi, yitímbula mawanda.»
LUK 5:6 Buna bátimbulama, bákwata mbumba yi mbwiti ya batsema: mawanda máyandika kutheta.
LUK 5:7 Hanga batekudi bakwawu khunda bana bákala mu mudimba wahika ndangu bisa basimbisa. Ha bísa bawu, bámona amana mu kimosi bawu boosu, bábasisa midimba myodi, hanga miyandiki kuzyonda.
LUK 5:8 Simoni Phetelu, ha kámona bwabuna, wáfukama kuna mesu ma Yesu, wuzonzi phi: «Haluka, kwena meni, Pfumu, mukuma yenina musumuki!»
LUK 5:9 Amana Simoni yi boosu bana bákala bawu, hanga kitswi kibakwati lawu, kikuma kya mbumba yi mbwiti ya batsema yina bákwata.
LUK 5:10 Phila mosi phi kwena bakwawu khunda ba kisalu bana bákala bawu Simoni, Zyaki yi Yowani bana ba Zebeteya. Bawu phi kitswi kyábakwata lawu. Kaasi Yesu wuzimbudi kwena Simoni: «Yukaku bweya; tuka lelu, ngeyi, batu walobiki.»
LUK 5:11 Bazakudini midimba mya bawu ku tseki, basisi bima bya bawu byosu, bendi landa Yesu.
LUK 5:12 Amana Yesu kákala muna hata dimosi, mutu mosi, wákala lutu yi bwasi, wutudini. Yandi ha kámona Yesu, wudilosi kuna mesu mandi, mbunzu mu mafu, wuyandiki kumubokwadila: «Pfumu, yuka ni wuzodibwa, fwani watsemisa.»
LUK 5:13 Yesu wálambula koku, wámusimba, wuzonzi phi: «Nzodibwa, sema!» Muna mbala mosi bwasi bumuwaluki.
LUK 5:14 Yesu wumuheki mulongi wawu: «Wuzimbulaku kwena mutu, mambu mama. Kaasi ndawenda disongila kwena banganga Nzambi amana hana makabu ma kudisemisa bwosu kásilabwa Moyize, kyakála kimbangi kikuma kya bawu.»
LUK 5:15 Muna tangwa medina, khululuka ya Yesu yáyalangana muma mwosu; milumba-lumba mya batu myakala khokana mu kumuyuka yi kubeluka mu makhasi ma bawu.
LUK 5:16 Kaasi Yesu kakala hunga mu tseki yi kulombilaka.
LUK 5:17 Amana kilumbu kimosi, Yesu kakala longa ha mesu ma Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku; bakala tuka mu mahata ma lawu ma Ngadidi yi ma Yuteya yi ma Yelusalemi. Ngolu za Pfumu zákala kumosi yi Yesu, zazina kakala bukilaka bambefu.
LUK 5:18 Batu bisa nata kiphoyu kyákala mukwa khonzu; bakala sanda phila ya kumukotisila mu nzu ndangu bamutulula kuna mesu ma Yesu.
LUK 5:19 Kaasi bakalaku lenda kikuma kya mulumba-lumba wa batu. Hanga bazanzi yandi ha mudilu wa nzu, batubudi hundu hana kati dya matolu amana bamukulwamini hana kiphoyu kyandi hana kati dya lukutakanu kuna mesu ma Yesu.
LUK 5:20 Buna kámona lukwikilu lwa bawu, Yesu wuzimbudi kwena mbefu: «Yakala, masumu maku makulolukini.»
LUK 5:21 Balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi báyandika kudihyula: «Nati kenina mutu yandu wubati lewula Nzambi? Nani fwani kalolula masumu, yukani ka yandi meni ku Nzambi lwesi!»
LUK 5:22 Kaasi Yesu wázaya mabanza ma bawu, hanga wubazimbwadi phi: «Kikuma kya biki lwenina yi mabanza ma buna mu mbundu zenu?
LUK 5:23 Biki byakonda phasi mu kuzonza?: "Masumu maku malolukini", ho "Telama, kangala"?
LUK 5:24 Ndangu lwazayabwa ni Mwana wa mutu kenina yi hamu ha tsi haha, dya kulolula masumu.» Hanga wuti ndinga kwena mukwa khonzu: «Yikuzimbwadi, telama, bonga kiphoyu kyaku, vutuka ku nzu yaku!»
LUK 5:25 Muna mbala mosi, mutu wátelema ku mesu ma batu boosu, wázangula kiphoyu kyandi, hana kakala waleka amana wendi ku nzu yandi yi kuzatulaka Nzambi.
LUK 5:26 Boosu báyituka lawu, bámuzatula Nzambi, báyuka bweya bwa lawu, bazonzi phi: «Lelu, tumoni mambu ma kuyituka!»
LUK 5:27 Kunima dya mambu mana, Yesu wálubuka, wámona phi kalaki ka phaku mosi, khumbu yandi Lefi, wasikuka muna nzu ya kisalu ya yandi. Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Ndanda!»
LUK 5:28 Amana Lefi wátelama, wásisa byosu, wenda mulanda phi.
LUK 5:29 Ku nima, Lefi wámuyidikila lawu dya madya muna nzu yandi; tulaki twa phaku lawu yi batu bahika bakala kuna mesa.
LUK 5:30 Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku bakala hana, kuna dingumba dya bawu, báyandika kubakumba; bendi zonza kwena balonguki ba Yesu: «Kikuma kya biki lubati dila yi kunwa ha kimosi yi tulaki twa phaku yi batu bahika basumuki?»
LUK 5:31 Yesu wubavutwadi: «Batu bana bena mu malutu yi ngolu, bisiku kala yi mupfunu wa munganga; kaasi bambefu bisi kala yi mupfunu wa munganga.
LUK 5:32 Meni yisaku tela batu basungama, kaasi basumuki yisa tela ndangu basoba bikalulu.»
LUK 5:33 Bafwadisi báhyula kwena Yesu: «Balonguki ba Yowani yi bana ba betu bayikana kuzila kudya yi kulombila; Kaasi balonguki ba ngeyi, bawu, bisi dya yi kunwa.»
LUK 5:34 Yesu wubavutwadini: «Pfwani lwabazidisa kudya, banduku ba kikwedi mu tangwa dina kenina kikwedi hakimosi yi bawu? Bwalendaku salama!
LUK 5:35 Kaasi tangwa dyakwísa dina babakatula yandi kikwedi, hahana nana bazíla kudya.»
LUK 5:36 Yesu wubatidi kingana kyaki: «Kweku mutu wayata muledi wa pha, kitemba kalondila muledi wa khulu, kondilo, kayata muledi wandi wa khatu, mukuma kitemba kya muledi wa pha kisiku kwelana yi sengi dya khulu.
LUK 5:37 Amana ka mutu ku wulongulula vinu dya pha mu bilungu bya khulu; kondilo, vinu dya pha dyabula bilungu, vinu dityakani amana bilungu bizangani.
LUK 5:38 Kaasi loni! Vinu dya pha, mboti mu bilungu bya pha!
LUK 5:39 Ka mutu ku wátonda kunwa hika vinu dya pha yukani wunwi kedi mulala. Mukuma, bisi zonza: "Mulala wenina wa bukheti."»
LUK 6:1 Amana kilumbu kimosi kya sabata, Yesu kakala luta mu bilanga bya ngenza zimosi zenina hanga losu. Balonguki bandi bakala hela misambu, báyandika kunika ngenza zandi muna moku yi kudyaka.
LUK 6:2 Ndambu ya Bafwadisi bákala hakana hanga bazimbudi: «Kikuma kya biki lubati hangila mambu mafwaniku mu kuhanga, mu kilumbu kya sabata?»
LUK 6:3 Yesu wubavutwadini: «Benu lwátangaku mambu káhanga Tavidi tangwa káyuka nzala yandi yi batu bana bákala yi yandi?
LUK 6:4 Kakota mu kikumbu kya Nzambi, wubongi mapha bahana mikhayilu kwena Nzambi, wudima amana wubaheki phi bakwawu bana kákala bawu, mbatanana bizila bizonzi ni, kaka banganga Nzambi batu lwesi bafwani kudya mapha mana bahani kwena Nzambi.»
LUK 6:5 Yesu wubazimbwadi hika: «Mwana wa mutu yandi wenina pfumu wa kilumbu kya sabata.»
LUK 6:6 Kilumbu kikwawu kya sabata, Yesu wákota mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, wáyandika kulonga. Mwakala mwamuna yi mutu mosi wákala koku dya kitata dyayumuka.
LUK 6:7 Balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi bakala mulandila Yesu mu kiswiswiswi, batala ho mutu kakhana belula mu kilumbu kya sabata, mukuma phila bakala sanda ya kumufunda.
LUK 6:8 Kaasi Yesu wázaya mabanza ma bawu. Hanga wuzimbudi kwena mutu yandu wákala koku dyayumuka: «Telama, awisa haha, ha mbasi.» Mutu, kahanga wutelami, wendi kwakuna.
LUK 6:9 Kunima Yesu wázimbula: «Yiluhyudibwa ni abweti milombi mitsiku myetu, mu kilumbu kya sabata? Kuhanga bukheti ho mbi? Kuhulula moya wa mutu ho kutotisawa?»
LUK 6:10 Kahanga, batadi boosu, kunima wázimbula kwena mutu wuna: «Yuna koku dyaku.» Mutu wuna wáyuna, koku dimutomini.
LUK 6:11 Kaasi balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi báfunga khabu, bekatendana bawu yi bawu keti bweti bafwana muhanga Yesu.
LUK 6:12 Muna tangwa meni dina, Yesu wátombuka ku mongu wumosi kikuma kya kulombila Nzambi, kásala phipha ya muthu, mu kulombila.
LUK 6:13 Kuma ha kwákhya, wubatedi balonguki bandi amana wusodini kumi yi bodi, wubahekini khumbu ni bathumwa.
LUK 6:14 Simoni wuna káheka, yandi, khumbu ya Phetelu yi myaki wandi wa yakala Andele, Zyaki yi Yowani, Fidiphu yi Batolomi,
LUK 6:15 Mathayi yi Tomasi, Zyaki mwana Alufwe yi Simoni wuna wákala mu kibuka kya batu bana bakala wila diphanda,
LUK 6:16 Yuta mwana wa Zyaki yi Yutasi Sikadyoti, wuna wálambula Yesu.
LUK 6:17 Yesu kákulumuka ku mongu yi bathumwa bandi, hanga wutelami ha musenzi, hana hákala kibuka kya balonguki bandi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu bátuka ku mulambu wa Yuteya dyosu yi ku Yelusalemi yi ku mahata ma Tidi yi Sitoni;
LUK 6:18 Bísa ndangu bamuyuka amana kababuka, bana bákala yi bisambu bya maladi. Batu bana bakala yangisa kwena bitembu bya mbi, bawu phi bákola.
LUK 6:19 Batu boosu bakala sanda tswetswa ya kumusimba kikuma ngolu zimosi zakala lubuka mu lutu lwandi, zakala babuka boosu.
LUK 6:20 Yesu wubatadini balonguki bandi amana wuzonzi: «Kyesi, kwena benu baphutu, mukuma kipfumu kya Nzambi kyenina kwena benu!
LUK 6:21 Kyesi kwena benu lubati fwa nzala buthwena, mukuma lwavwa madya ma lawu! Kyesi kwena benu lubati dila buthwena, mukuma lwaséya!»
LUK 6:22 «Kyesi kwena benu bisi menga, bisi kukwasa, bisi sawula amana bisi kumba khumbu zenu kwena batu kikuma kya Mwana wa mutu!
LUK 6:23 Sangwalenu mu kilumbu kina malúngila mambu mana amana kinenu makinu ma muzandu mukuma lufutu lwa mbuta lubati luhingila kuna zilu. Mukuma, bwabuna, bakhaka ba bawu, bakala nyokuna bambikudi.»
LUK 6:24 Kaasi kyadi kwena benu bamvwama, kikuma lutambudi kedi mamboti menu, lwahíngilaku hika kima!
LUK 6:25 Kyadi kwena benu ludiyukwatidi kedi, buthwena, kikuma nzala lwayúka! Kyadi kwena benu lubati seya, buthwena, mukuma mu khondu yi matsanga lwakála!
LUK 6:26 «Kyadi kwena benu bisi zatula kwena batu mukuma bwabuna bakhaka ba bawu bakala zatula bambikudi ba bukamvi!»
LUK 6:27 «Kaasi nzimbudi kwena benu lubati ngyuka ni tondenu bambeni benu, hangenu bukheti kwena batu bana bisi lumenga,
LUK 6:28 sambulenu batu bana bisi lusinga amana lombilenu kikuma kya batu bana bisi lunyokuna.
LUK 6:29 Honi mutu kakuta mbata ku tama dimosi, musila hika dikwawu; honi mutu katambula muzaka waku, muyambula katambula hika kikutu kyaku.
LUK 6:30 Wosu wuna wakulomba kima, muheka. Futisaku kima kwena mutu wuna wukubwotudikya.
LUK 6:31 Hangenu kwena bakwenu bwosu lwisi tya benu phi baluhangila.
LUK 6:32 Honi lwatondaka lwesi batu bana bisi lutonda, biki hika lwatánikina kwena Nzambi? Phila mosi yi basumuki bana bisi tonda batu bana bisi batya bawu phi.
LUK 6:33 Amana yuka ni lwahangaka bukheti lwesi kwena batu bana bisi luhanga mboti, biki hika lwatánikina kwena Nzambi? Phila mosi yi basumuki bana bisibwa hanga!
LUK 6:34 Amana ho ni lwalefisaka lwesi kwena batu bana lwisi sya mbundu ni baluvutwala, biki hika lwatanikina kwena Nzambi? Phila mosi yi basumuki bisi dilefisa bawu yi bawu amana badivutwadi!
LUK 6:35 Kaasi benu, tondenu bambeni benu, bahangilenu bukheti, balefisenu phi konda kusya mbundu ni kima balúvutwala. Amana lufutu lwenu lwákala lwa mbuta, benu lwakála phi bana ba Nzambi wa Phungu, mukuma yandi wamboti kikuma kya bakonda-kabanzi yi bakholwa.
LUK 6:36 Kalenu babasa yi khenda bwosu kábasa tata wenu yi khenda.
LUK 6:37 «Lufundisaku amana benu phi balúfundisaku; luzengilaku bakwenu ndola amana benu phi balúzengilaku ndola; lolulenu bakwenu, bawu phi balúlolula.
LUK 6:38 Kabilenu bakwenu amana Nzambi kalúkabila benu phi: kabásisa mawaba menu yi kuvwa kwa lawu. Kasómama, wuningisima ndangu masomama yi hana thandu. Nzambi katésa makabu menu bwosu lwisi tesila benu phi bakwenu.»
LUK 6:39 Yesu wubazonzidi hika mu kingana: «Phofu kafwaniku kusongila mukwawu phofu nzila, Kondilo, babwa mu dibulu babodi. Kabwaku?
LUK 6:40 Kweku mulonguki wuluti mulongi wandi; kaasi mulonguki wuna baswaniki bwa bukheti, kafwánana hanga mulongi wandi.
LUK 6:41 Kikuma kya biki wisi tadila kitswala kyenina mu disu dya phangi waku amana wubatiku mona mudikita miti wenina mu disu dyaku?
LUK 6:42 Abweti walenda zimbula kwena phangi waku: "Mukwetu, yambula yikukatula kitswala kyaki kyenina mu disu", ngeyi wusiku mona mudikita miti wenina mu disu dya ngeyi meni? Kavungalosi, katula theti miti wena mu disu dyaku amana wamona wanga mu kukatula kitswala kyenina mu disu dya phangi waku.»
LUK 6:43 «Miti wamboti wisiku ha bibundu bya mbi, mutindu mosi yi miti wambi, wisiku ha bibundu bya mboti.
LUK 6:44 Miti wosu bisiwa zayila ku bibundu byandi: kibundu kya fiki bisiku helakya mu minzumbila amana phi bisiku hela kibundu kya vinu mu miti mya tsaku.
LUK 6:45 Mutu wamboti kisi hola mambu mamboti mu kimvwama kya bukheti kina kyenina mu mbundu yandi; mutu wambi phi kisi hola mambu mambi mu kimvwama kya mbi kina kyenina mu mbundu yandi; mukuma mutu wosu kisi lubula mu munwa, mambu moosu mana mabasa muna fuka dya mbundu yandi.»
LUK 6:46 Kikuma kya biki lwisi thedila: «Pfumu, Pfumu, kaasi lwisiku hanga mambu mana yisiluzimbwala?
LUK 6:47 Yilúsongila yi nati kafwanani mutu yandu wisi kwena meni, wuyuki ndinga za meni amana wusiza mu bisalu:
LUK 6:48 yandi kenina hanga mutu mosi wátunga nzu; kahanga simi lawu mumbulu-mbulu amana wutungi mupfundila hana thandu ya tadi. Ha kisa dinata kizalu, mamba ma nzadi maditi kuna nzu kaasi konda kunikana kikuma kitoku bátungaya.
LUK 6:49 Kaasi wosu wuna wuyuki ndinga za meni, kalundizoku phi, fwanani yi mutu wuna mukwawu wátunga nzu yandi ha thandu ya fusyangeni, yakonda mupfundila. Ha mísa mamba ma nzadi, maditi kuna nzu, yosu yiwulumukini: yimwangani.»
LUK 7:1 Ha kámanisa, Yesu, kuzonza mambu mana kwena batu bákala hana, wénda ku mbanza ya Kaphedinawumi.
LUK 7:2 Kwakuna, kwákala yi satudiyoni mosi kákala yi musadi wandi wuna kakala tonda lawu. Musadi meni wuna kákala wabela mu kulakana.
LUK 7:3 Mu tangwa káyuka, kaphiteni, khululuka ya Yesu, hanga wutumi ndambu ya bambuta ba Bayuta ndangu benda mubokwadila Yesu, kisa mubuka musadi wandi.
LUK 7:4 Ha bátula kwena Yesu, báyandika kumubokwadila yi nziki-nziki: «Mutu wuna bulungi wenda musadisa.
LUK 7:5 Mukuma kisi tonda kikanda kyetu, yandi phi wátutungila nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta.»
LUK 7:6 Hanga Yesu wendi bawu nzila mosi. Kakalaku kyana yi nzu, tangwa kámutumina, satudiyoni, banduku bandi ndangu bamuzimbwala: «Pfumu, diyangisaku. Yeku walungila mu kukutambwasa ni wakota mu nzu ya meni;
LUK 7:7 hahana khondi kwisilaka meni-meni, mu kimwesa mutu, kwena ngeyi. Kaasi zonza ndinga mosi amana musadi wama kábeluka.
LUK 7:8 Mukuma, meni-meni yenina mu sina dya hamu dya bapfumu bama amana yena yi baphumbulu bama bisi ndemvukila. Ho ni yizimbula kwena mosi: "Ndawenda!", wendi; ho ni yizimbula kwena mukwawu wa hika: "Nzawisa!" amana wisi; amana kwena musadi wama: "Hanga bwabu!" amana wuhangibwa.»
LUK 7:9 Ha kayuka mambu mana, ma Kaphiteni, Yesu wáyituka. Kahanga wubaluki kwena kibuka kina kyakala mulanda amana wuzonzi: «Yiluzimbwadibwa ni keti mu Kiseledi, khaku kedi mbona kikumbwala kya mbuta, kya mutindu wawu.»
LUK 7:10 Ha bisa vutuka bambambala, bana bátuma, ku nzu ya Kaphiteni, bisa wana musadi wuna wukodi kedi.
LUK 7:11 Hanga Yesu wendi ku hata dimosi bisi tela Nayini; balonguki bandi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu bakala kwenda nzila mosi.
LUK 7:12 Tangwa kátula ku fula dya hata dina, bekanata mvumbi mosi ku mazyamu: kákala mwana yakala wa mufwidi mosi, yandi hika. Batu balawu ba hata medina bákala yi ngudi wuna.
LUK 7:13 Pfumu, ha kámumona mufwidi, kiwayi kimukwati kikuma kya yandi amana wumuzimbwadi: «Wudilaku!»
LUK 7:14 Kahanga wubwesuki, wusimbi phi mukunzu; batu bana bakalawa nata batelami. Yesu wuzonzi: «Mwana yakala, yikuzimbwadi: tokama!»
LUK 7:15 Amana mvumbi wásikuka, wáyandika phi kuzonza. Yesu wámuhana kwena ngudi wandi.
LUK 7:16 Batu boosu bweya bwábakwata, báyandika kumuzatula Nzambi mu kuzonza: «Mbikudi wambuta wulubukini ha kati kya betu!» Amana phi «Nzambi wisi yakidila batu bandi!»
LUK 7:17 Amana muna tsi ya Yuteya yi binzunga byandi byosu báyuka khululuka ya mambu mana káhanga Yesu.
LUK 7:18 Balonguki ba Yowani bázimbula, kwena mulongi wa bawu, mambu mana moosu buna málutila. Yowani wátela bodi muna kati kya balonguki ba bawu;
LUK 7:19 amana wábatuma kwena Pfumu benda muhyula: «Ngeyi, yi Masiya wuna wakwísa, ho twahingila mutu wa hika?»
LUK 7:20 Ha bátula kwena Yesu, bamuzimbwadini: «Yowani Mubotiki wututumi twakuhyula: "Ngeyi, Masiya wuna wufwani mu kukwisa, ho twahingila mutu wa hika?»
LUK 7:21 Muna tangwa medina, Yesu wábuka batu balawu bákala yi bisambu bya maladi, minyanga, wákukwasa bitembu bya mbi bákala byawu yi kutemuna mesu kwena baphofu ba lawu.
LUK 7:22 Kahanga bavutwadi mvutu, batu babana kátuma Yowani: «Ndalwenda, lwamusamwana, Yowani, mambu mana lumoni yi mana luyuki ni baphofu babati mona hika, bakwa khonzu babati kangala, bakwa bwasi basemi, tuhuwa tuyuki, bamvumbi bafutumuki, Musamu wa Bukheti balongiwa kwena baphutu.
LUK 7:23 Kyesi kwena mutu wuna wakonda yambula kikumbwala kyandi mwena meni!»
LUK 7:24 Tangwa bávutuka bathumwa ba Yowani, Yesu wáyandika kuzonzila kikuma kya Yowani kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu: «Biki lwendi talaka mu nganga? Koma ka muswangina kana kabati ningana ku muphephi, kabwaku? Loni?
LUK 7:25 Amana biki lwendi talaka? Mutu mosi wuvwatiki miledi mya kitoku? Kaasi batu baba bisi vwata miledi mya kitoku, bisi zinga luzingu lwa lukumu, mu nzu za bathotila bisi kala.
LUK 7:26 Biki lwendi talaka? Mbikudi mosi? Bwana, bwosu yiluzimbwadi, yandi wuluti mbikudi.
LUK 7:27 Kikuma kya yandi básonika mu mukanda wa Nzambi»: «Yitúma mbambala wama ha thwala ngeyi, mu kukuyidikila nzila.»
LUK 7:28 Yesu yiki hika: «Yiluzimbwadibwa ni heku mutu, ha kati dya baba bábutuka kwena mukhetu, wuluti Yowani; kinga wuna wena wa khunda mu kipfumu kya Nzambi wumuluti.
LUK 7:29 Batu boosu bana bámuyuka yi tulaki twa phaku, boosu bákwikila ni Nzambi kenina wasingama amana babaludi mbundu, batambwasi phi kutambula mbotika kwena Yowani.
LUK 7:30 Kinga Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku bana bákala hana, hanga babwisi mambu kazola kubahangila Nzambi; bábwisa kutambula mbotika ya Yowani.»
LUK 7:31 Yesu wuzonzi hika: «Yi banani pfwani yifwanikisa batu ba buthwena bwabu? Bafwanani yi banani?
LUK 7:32 Bafwanakani yi bana baba bazakadi hana zandu, babati dizonzila: "Tulusikidi mahongi ma kyesi kaasi lukiniku! Tulusidi biwolu, ludidiku!
LUK 7:33 Kikuma, Yowani Mubotiki wisi, kisiku dya dipa keti kunwa vinu, amana benu yikuzonzaka: "Kitembu kya mbi kena kyawu!"
LUK 7:34 Ha yisi meni Mwana wa mutu, yibati dya yi kunwaka, amana benu yikuzimbulaka: "Talenu mutu yandu wisi banza lwesi kudya yi kunwaka vinu, yameni nduku wa tulaki twa phaku yi basumuki.
LUK 7:35 Kaasi boosu bana bisi landa mudimu wa Nzambi bisi songila ni zasungama zenina.»
LUK 7:36 Mufwadisi mosi wálomba kwena Yesu ndangu kenda dya ku nzu yandi. Yesu wákota muna nzu, wubongi homa phi kuna mesa.
LUK 7:37 Kinga mwákala yi mukhetu mosi muna mbanza meni yayina, musumuki. Ha káyuka ni Yesu ku mesa kena muna nzu ya Mufwadisi, wisi nata nganza yimosi ya kabasi yi mananasi ma tsunga ma thalu ya lawu.
LUK 7:38 Wisi telama kuna kunda dya Yesu, kuna bitambi byandi. Wekadila, kitsanga kyandi kiyandiki kunoka muna bitambi bya Yesu; kunima, wuphangusibya yi khambu zandi, wunukibya amana phi wusitibya mananasi.
LUK 7:39 Buna kamona bwabuna, Mufwadisi wuna wámutedisa, wáyandika kudizonzila kuna mbundu: «Wadi mutu yandu kákala mbikudi, kakhani bakula keti nati kenina mukhetu yandu wubati musimba yi buna kenina: musumuki.»
LUK 7:40 Amana Yesu wátambula ndinga, wuzimbudi kwena Mufwadisi: «Simoni, dyambu yena dyawu thondi yikuzimbwala.» Simoni wumuvutwadi: «Zonza Mulongi.»
LUK 7:41 Hanga Yesu wuzonzi: «Batu bodi bafwana kufuta pfuka za makuta ma lawu kwena mukwa zawu. Mosi kafwana kavutula khama tanu za mafwalanga amana mukwawu makumatanu.
LUK 7:42 Babodi, bwosu bakalaku yi kima kya kufuta pfuka zina, hanga mukwa pfuka wábayambwadilaza. Nati, hana kati kya babodi wahita kumutonda?»
LUK 7:43 Simoni wumuvutwadi: «Meni mboni ni wuna káyambwadila yi pfuka ya lawu.» Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Mboti wuzengi.»
LUK 7:44 Yesu kábaluka kwena mukhetu wuna, wuzimbudi phi kwena Simoni: «Wumoni mukhetu yandu? Meni khoti mu nzu yaku, kaasi wuphekiku keti mamba kikuma kya bitambi byama; kaasi yandi wutsukudi bitambi yi matsanga mandi kusumunima phi yi khambu zandi.
LUK 7:45 Wungyambiku, tangwa khotiki mu nzu yaku; kaasi yandi kabatiku lembwa kunuka bitambi byama, tuka buna khotidiki.
LUK 7:46 Wutsitikiku masi ku mutwa wama, kaasi yandi wutsiti mananasi ma tsunga ku bitambi byama.
LUK 7:47 Ihana yikuzimbwadi ni masumu mandi ma lawu, mamuloluki kikuma tonda dyandi dya lawu kasongidi. Kaasi mutu wuna baloludi masumu ma khunda, kisi songila phi tonda dya khunda.»
LUK 7:48 Amana Yesu wázimbula kwena mukhetu: «Masumu maku malolukini.»
LUK 7:49 Bana kákala bawu ku mesa báyandika kudizonzila: «Nati kenina mutu yandu, walenda lolula yi masumu ma batu?»
LUK 7:50 Kaasi Yesu wázimbula kwena mukhetu: «Lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini: ndawenda mu ngemba.»
LUK 8:1 Kunima, Yesu wénda mu mbanza yi mu mahata kikuma kya kulonga, mwamuna, yi kusamunaka Musamu wa Bukheti wa Kipfumu kya Nzambi ha kimosi yi bawu Kumi yi bodi,
LUK 8:2 yi ndambu ya bakhetu bahika bana bábeluka mu bitembu bya mbi yi mu bisambu bya maladi: hanga Madiya wuna bisi tela: Makatala, mwena yandu mwálubuka bitembu bya mbi tsambwadi;
LUK 8:3 Zyani mukhetu wa Kuza, yandu wákala pfumu wa bakalaki mu nzu ya kisalu ya thotila Eloti; Suzani yi bakhetu bahika balawu, boosu, bakala hana bima bya bawu ndangu byamusadisaka Yesu yi bathumwa bandi.
LUK 8:4 Batu balawu bakala tuka mu mbanza za mutindu yi mutindu, bisi kutakana kuna kakala Yesu, wubatidi kingana kyaki:
LUK 8:5 «Mukuni mosi wenda kuna kheni, kuna kilanga kyandi. Ha kakala mwanga kheni, ndambu yahika yenda bwila mu nzila: hanga batu bamaniya dyatikisa, banuni bátuka ku zilu, bisiya dya.
LUK 8:6 Ndambu ya hika yenda bwila mu mafu ma matadi: ha yamena, miti myáyumuka kikuma myákalaku mu mafu ma tsimina.
LUK 8:7 Ndambu yahika yenda bwila ha kati kya tsaku. Tsaku ziyandiki kukola ha kimosi yi ngwalengi ya bukheti; hanga zikakidikisiya.
LUK 8:8 Kaasi kheni yikwawu, yábwila mu mafu ma bukheti, yákola, yihe phi kheni khama ku khama.» Kunima dya kuzonza bwabuna, Yesu yiki hika: «Wuna wenina yi matu ma kuyuka, kayuka!»
LUK 8:9 Balonguki bandi bámuhyula, biki kisongidila kya kingana kyaki.
LUK 8:10 Yandi wubavutwadi: «Nzambi wáluheka, benu, mbakisilu ya kubakula bitsweki bya Kipfumu kya Nzambi; kaasi kwena bahika, wábazimbwalama mu bingana, ihana»: "Bafwani kumona kaasi bisiku mona kima, bafwani kuyuka kaasi bisiku bakula."
LUK 8:11 «Yukenu kisongidila kya kingana kyaki: mbutu, yenina ndinga ya Nzambi.
LUK 8:12 Yina yábwila mu kabeta ka nzila: yenina batu bana bisi yuka ndinga ya Nzambi, kunima kiphidi-mutu wisi katulaya muna mbundu za bawu ndangu bakwikilaku hanga bahuluka nana.
LUK 8:13 Bahika benina hanga mafu ma matadi: bisi yuka ndinga ya Nzambi amana bisiya tambula yi kyesi kyosu. Kaasi yisiku zika misodi, kikumbwala kya bawu kyenina mu tangwa dya khunda, mu tangwa dya phasi, balosikya.
LUK 8:14 Kheni yina yábwila ha kati kya tsaku, benina babana bisi yuka Ndinga, kaasi kunima mayanu yi kimvwama yi byesi bya luzingu, bisiya kakidikisa ndangu yihaku bibundu byakola.
LUK 8:15 Kheni yina yábwila mu mafu ma bukheti, benina batu babana bisi yuka Ndinga ya Nzambi, balundiya muna mbundu yafwana yi ya bukheti; amana yibuti kheni yi kusipha kwa mbundu.»
LUK 8:16 «Ka mutu ku wisi lemisa mwinda amana kendawa fidinga katini kondilo kendawa sweka ku tsi ya thangi. Kaasi bisiwa tudika hana thandu ya muzanga wa mwinda ndangu batu boosu bakóta mu nzu bamona mutemu.
LUK 8:17 Mukuma kweku kima kyaswamana, kyakonda zayakana, kweku kitsweki kyakonda tunguluka amana byosu byámonika ha kitelengeni.
LUK 8:18 Kebenu mu mana lwisi yuka, mukuma bakósikila kwena mutu wuna wenina kedi yi kima kyandi kaasi kwena mutu wuna weku yi kima, bamúbwotula keti koma kana kasi sila mbundu.»
LUK 8:19 Ngudi wa Yesu yi baphangi bandi bisa bamumona; kaasi bálendaku kutula kuna kákala yandi kikuma kya mulumba-lumba wa batu.
LUK 8:20 Bendi muzibwala Yesu bwabu: «Ngudi waku yi baphangi baku, ha nzila benina, bazodi ni bakumona.»
LUK 8:21 Kaasi Yesu wázimbula kwena bawu boosu: «Ngudi wama yi baphangi bama, benina batu bana bisi yuka ndinga ya Nzambi, bisiya sadila phi.»
LUK 8:22 Kilumbu kimosi, Yesu wákota mu mudimba yi balonguki bandi, kahanga wubazimbwadi: «Tulabukenu ku sambwa dina dya yanga.» Amana bénda.
LUK 8:23 Ha bakala labuka, Yesu wánimba. Muna kithulumukina, kimbongila kyátukula hana mukanda wa mamba; masuwa máyandika kukota mamba, mu kihonza bákala.
LUK 8:24 Balonguki bábwesuka kwena Yesu, bámutokamisa mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Mulongi, mulongi tukuluki betu!» Yesu wátokama, wákayaya pfunzi yi mamba, byádibata. Talala dyávutuka.
LUK 8:25 Yesu wábazimbwala balonguki bandi: «Akweti kyenina kikumbwala kyenu?» Kaasi bweya bwábakwata, báyituka lawu, amana bekazonza: «Nati kenina mutu yandu? Kabati hana muswa kwena pfunzi yi mamba amana byosu, bimuyukidi!»
LUK 8:26 Yesu yi balonguki bandi bátula mu tsi ya bisi Ngelasoni, yina yenina ku sambwa dyatalana yi Ngadidi.
LUK 8:27 Tangwa kátuluka Yesu ha tsi, mutu mosi wa ku mbanza meni yana, kákala yi bitembu bya mbi wísa kuna thwala ya yandi. Tuka thama kakalaku vwata hika miledi, amana kakalaku nimba hika mu nzu yandi, kaasi muna mazyamu.
LUK 8:28 Tangwa kámona Yesu, wákalunga, wádilosa muna malu mandi, wuzonzi phi yi ngolu zoosu: «Biki wisi kotila mambu ma meni, Yesu Mwana Nzambi wa ku zilu? Yikubokwadidi, ngyangisaku!»
LUK 8:29 Mukuma Yesu kakala kukwasa kitembu kya mbi kwena mutu ndangu kyalubuka mwena yandi, kyamusisa. Kitembu kina tangwa dya lawu kyákala mu kati dya yandi, kyámukotila tuka thama; kakala zingila wakukasa mu miyololu yi bisengu kuna malu yi ku moku yi kumutanikina, kaasi kakala tabulamya, amana phi kitembu kyákala mutuma katinaka mu tseki.
LUK 8:30 Hanga Yesu wumuhyudi: «Biki khumbu yaku?» Yandi wuvutudi: «Khumbu yama "Khwingi".» Mukuma bitembu bya mbi lawu byákota mwena yandi.
LUK 8:31 Hanga bitembu bimubokwadidi Yesu ndangu kabatumaku mu kalunga.
LUK 8:32 Hakana, hákala yi kibuka kya bangulu bakala sosa madya muna mongu. Bitembu bina byámubokwadila Yesu ni kabatuma benda kota muna bangulu meni babana. Hanga Yesu wubaheki muswa.
LUK 8:33 Bitembu bya mbi byálubuka mwena mutu, byákota mu bangulu. Hanga kibuka kya bangulu kyosu kikatuki ku mongu, kyendi kota mu yanga dya thibu, báfwa phi.
LUK 8:34 Batu bana bakala hungula bangulu, buna bámona mambu mana, bátina, bendi nata tsangu mu mbanza yi mu mahata.
LUK 8:35 Hanga batu balubuki mu kutala mana máhita. Bísa kuna kákala Yesu, báwana phi mutu wuna bálubula bitembu bya mbi: wuzakadiki muna malu ma Yesu, wuvwatiki miledi, mabanza ma kimutu mamuvutwakisi. Hanga batu, bweya bubakwati.
LUK 8:36 Babana bámona mambu moosu mana máhita, bámenika buna kábelukila mutu wuna wákala yi bitembu bya mbi.
LUK 8:37 Bakwa kinzunga kina kya Ngelasoni bálomba kwena Yesu ni kakatuka ku mulambu wa bawu, kikuma bweya bwa lawu bákala bwawu. Yesu wákota mu mudimba, wávutuka phi.
LUK 8:38 Mutu wuna bálubula bitembu bya mbi wámubokwadila Yesu ndangu kakalaka yi yandi. Kaasi Yesu wámukula, wuzimbudi phi:
LUK 8:39 «Vutuka ku nzu yaku, ndawenda samuna mambu moosu mana kasadi Nzambi kikuma kya ngeyi.» Mutu wuna wénda, wásamuna phi mambu mana moosu kámusadila Yesu.
LUK 8:40 Tangwa kávutwakisa, Yesu, ku sambwa dya yanga dya thibu, bámuyamba kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu, mukuma boosu bakala muhingila.
LUK 8:41 Mutu mosi, khumbu yandi Zayilusi, wátula. Yandi kákala pfumu wa nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta. Hanga wudilosi muna malu ma Yesu, wumubokwadidi ndangu kenda ku nzu yandi,
LUK 8:42 kikuma kákala yi mwana wandi yandi mosi wa mukhetu, wekalungisa mvula kumi yi zodi, kakala lakana. Mu tangwa kakala kwenda, Yesu, mulumba-lumba wa batu wakala mukakidikisa, tselu yi tselu.
LUK 8:43 Kinga hákala hana meni, yi mukhetu mosi wakala noka menga tukila mvula kumi yi zodi. Wámanisa kuvwa kwa luzingu lwandi kwosu kwena bandomvi, kaasi keti mutu kálendaku kumubelula.
LUK 8:44 Kahanga wisi bwesuka kuna kunda dya Yesu, amana wusimbi nzenzi ya muledi wa Yesu. Muna mbala mosi, menga mámukangama.
LUK 8:45 Hanga Yesu wuhyudi: «Nati wutsimbi?» Boosu báyandika kutuna ni basadibwoku, Phetelu wuzonzi phi: «Mulongi, mulumba-lumba wa batu wawu wukuzyetiki, yi babana babati kufitikisa tselu zoosu.»
LUK 8:46 Kaasi Yesu wuvutudini: «Mutu wutsimbi, mukuma ngyuki ni ngolu zimosi zilubuki kwena meni.»
LUK 8:47 Mukhetu kádimona ni wutunguluki, hanga wisi yi tsula zoosu, wádilosa kuna bitambi bya Yesu. Wáyandika kuzimbula, hana mesu ma batu boosu, kikuma kina kámusimbila Yesu yi buna kábeluka mu mbala yimosi.
LUK 8:48 Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Mwana wama wa mukhetu, lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini. Awenda mu ngemba.»
LUK 8:49 Muna tangwa dina kakala zonza Yesu, bwabuna, mutu mosi wátuka ku nzu ya Zayilusi wisa muzimbwala: «Mwana waku wa mukhetu wufini. Wumuyangisaku hika Mulongi.»
LUK 8:50 Kaasi Yesu wámuyuka, amana wuzimbudi kwena Zayilusi: «Yukaku bweya! Kwikila lwesi, amana mwana waku wa mukhetu kahúluka.»
LUK 8:51 Tangwa kátula Yesu ku nzu, wábwisa batu bakotaku mu nzu. Hanga kotisi lwesi Phetelu yi Yowani yi Zyaki yi tata yi ngudi wa mwana.
LUK 8:52 Batu boosu bakala dila yi kuyanana kikuma kya mwana wa mukhetu. Hanga Yesu wuzimbudi: «Loni, ludilaku. Mwana kafiku, wanimba kenina.»
LUK 8:53 Kaasi batu bayandiki kumuseya mukuma bázaya ni mwana wufiki kedi.
LUK 8:54 Kaasi Yesu wumusimbi mu koku, wuzonzi phi mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Tokama kwaku mwana!»
LUK 8:55 Moya wandi wuvutuki, wutokami, muna mbala mosi. Yesu wubazimbwadi ni bamuheka bima bya kudya.
LUK 8:56 Tata yi ngudi wa mwana wa mukhetu báyituka lawu, kaasi Yesu wábakandisa ni bazimbulaku kwena mutu mambu mana máluta.
LUK 9:1 Yesu wátela bawu Kumi yi bodi, amana wábaheka ngolu yi hamu hana thandu ya bitembu bya mbi byosu yi mu kubuka bisambu bya kubela.
LUK 9:2 Amana wábatuma kusamuna Kipfumu kya Nzambi yi kubuka bambefu.
LUK 9:3 Wubazimbwadi: «Lunataku kima mu nzila: keti koka, keti waba, keti kudya, keti makuta, amana mutu kakalaku yi miledi myodi.
LUK 9:4 Amana yosu nzu yina lwakóta, kalenu mwamuna yi kuna lwalubwakilamwa.
LUK 9:5 Amana muma mwosu muna baluyambiku batu, mu kulubuka mu mbanza, khukumunenu fusyangeni dya bitambi byenu: ndangu kyakala kambangu kikuma kya bawu.»
LUK 9:6 Amana bwana bálubuka; báyandika kuluta hata muna hata; mu kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti yi kubuka kwa bambefu muma mwosu.
LUK 9:7 Eloti wuna wákala mosi wa bakyamvu baya, wuna wakala yala ku Ngadidi wuyuki mosu mana makala luta, amana mabanza mamuyekina yangalakanu, kikuma bahika bakala zonza: «Yowani wufutumuki ku bafwa.»
LUK 9:8 Bahika bakala zimbula: «Diya wuna wulubukini». Bakwawu phi: «Mosi wa bambikudi bakhulu wufutumuki.»
LUK 9:9 Kaasi Eloti kakala zimbula: «Yowani, meni-meni yímubukwasa mutwa. Amana nati kenina, yandu mbati yuka kuzonzila mambu mana?» Amana kakala sanda kumumona.
LUK 9:10 Amana bathumwa, mu kuvutuka kwa bawu, bámuzimbwala Yesu moosu mana báhanga. Wubabongi amana wendi ku phungamu, ku sambwa dya mbanza yimosi bisi tela ni Betisayita.
LUK 9:11 Amana milumba-lumba mya batu ha bábakulabwa, hanga bamulandi. Yandi wubayambi, wuyandiki kubazonzila Kipfumu kya Nzambi, amana wubuki batu, bana bákala yi mupfunu wa kubeluka.
LUK 9:12 Kaasi kuma kwáyandika kuyila; bawu Kumi yi bodi bisa bwesuka, bámuzimbwala: «Kula mulumba-lumba wa batu, ndangu benda sanda bizika mu mahata yi mafedime ma bela-bela ndangu bamona muma mwa kuleka yi bima bya kudya, mukuma homa thwena ku phungamu, ha kati kya tseki».
LUK 9:13 Kaasi wubazimbwadi: «Bahekenu kudya benu-benu!» Bavutudi: «Thweku yi mapha maluti matanu yi batsema bodi. Akolu ni thwenda sumba madya, betu-betu kikuma kya batu baba boosu.»
LUK 9:14 Mu bwana, hákala kitesu kya mafunda matanu ma bayakala. Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Bazakadisenu mu bibuka bya batu makumatanu.»
LUK 9:15 Bahangi bwabuna, amana bábazakadisa boosu.
LUK 9:16 Yesu wábonga mapha matanu yi batsema bodi, wásekula mesu ku zilu amana wásakumunabya. Kunima, wábukununabya amana wáhanabya kwena balonguki ndangu bakabisabya kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu.
LUK 9:17 Boosu bádya amana báyukuta. Bánata bitunga kumi yi byodi bya bitini bina byásala.
LUK 9:18 Amana kilumbu kimosi, Yesu kakala lombila ku phungamu amana balonguki bákala kumosi yi yandi. Hanga wubahyudi: «Biki misi zonza milumba-lumba mya batu kikuma kya meni?»
LUK 9:19 Bawu bavutudi: «Bahika bisi zonza ni ngeyi wena Yowani Mubotiki, bakwawu hika ni ngeyi, wena Diya, bakwawu bana bahika ni ngeyi, wenina mosi hana kati kya bambikudi bana ba khulu, wuna wufutumukini.»
LUK 9:20 Yesu wubahyudi: «Amana kikuma kya benu, nati yenina?» Phetelu wuvutudi: «Ngeyi wena Kidisitu wa Nzambi.»
LUK 9:21 Yesu kábasidingisa ni bazimbulabwoku kwena mutu;
LUK 9:22 wuyiki: «Bulungi, Mwana wa mutu kanyokuka lawu; bamulosila kwena bambuta ba Bayuta, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku; bamúhonda amana kilumbu kya tatu, kafútumuka.»
LUK 9:23 Amana kakala zimbula kwena boosu: «Yuka ni mutu wuzodini kandanda, kadizimbakana yandi meni, katikula kitakani kyandi kosu kilumbu amana kandanda.
LUK 9:24 Mukuma wuna watónda kuhulula moya wandi, mu kyedika katótisawa; kaasi wuna watótisa moya wandi kikuma kya meni, yandi kahúlulawa.
LUK 9:25 Amana khi mupfunu kwena mutu kavwa tsi yosu, ho kaditotisa kwandi yandi wosu, kondilo kadizanga?
LUK 9:26 Mukuma wuna wangyúka tsoni yi ndinga zama, Mwana wa mutu tsoni kamúyuka, tangwa kakwisa vutuka muna khembu yandi yi mu khembu ya Tata yi yina ya banzyo ba Nzambi.
LUK 9:27 Amana, mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi, ndambu ya batu, mu kati dya babana benina haha, badifwilaku, konda kumona Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 9:28 Amana bilumbu keti nana byáluta, kunima ndinga zina, Yesu wábonga Phetelu, Yowani yi Zyaki, amana wátombuka yi bawu ku mongu kikuma kya kulombila.
LUK 9:29 Amana tangwa kakala lombila, mbunzu yandi yásoba, amana miledi myandi myekina mya phembi yimosi yakala kedyamina.
LUK 9:30 Amana, kutala, batu bodi bákala hahana, yi kuyambilaka yandi: bakala Moyize yi Diya,
LUK 9:31 bakala monika mu kati dya khembu yi kuzonzilaka kwenda kwa yandi, kuna kwafwana kusalama ku Yelusalemi.
LUK 9:32 Phetelu yi bakwawu khunda ku kilu kya ngolu bákala; kaasi ha bátokama, bámona khembu ya yandi yi batu bodi bana bákala yi yandi.
LUK 9:33 Tangwa bakala hambwasana batu bana yi Yesu, Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Mulongi, bwena mboti ni twakalenu kwetu haka. Tutungenu masombolu matatu, dimosi dya ngeyi, dimosi dya Moyize yi dimosi dya Diya.» Kakalaku zaya mana kakala zonza.
LUK 9:34 Buna kakala zonza bwana, tuti dimosi dyisi bafidinga ku kininga kyandi. Hanga balonguki bweya bubakwati, tangwa dyábafidinga tuti.
LUK 9:35 Amana ndinga yimosi yálubuka muna tuti: «Yandu-yandu kenina Mwana wa meni, wuna yisola. Muyukilenu!»
LUK 9:36 Tangwa yáyukalakana ndinga, Yesu yandi hika kakala. Balonguki badibati, amana konda kuzimbula kwena mutu mosi, mu bilumbu meni byabina, mu mana bamona.
LUK 9:37 Kilumbu kyálanda, tangwa bakulumuka ku mongu, mulumba-lumba wa batu wisa mutundakana.
LUK 9:38 Hana kati dya mulumba-lumba wa batu, mutu mosi wákalunga: «Mulongi, yikubokwadidi, mutala mwana wama wa yakala, mukuma mwana wama yandi mosi lwesi.
LUK 9:39 Kosu tangwa kitembu kimosi kisi mukwata, mu mbala mosi, wáyandika kukalunga, kyámuningisa ngolu yi kumulubwasa mafulu-fulu, amana kisi mukatuka mu phasi, kunima dya kumuzokisa yandi wosu.
LUK 9:40 Yíbabokwadila balonguki baku ndangu bakukwasakya kaasi bálendaku.»
LUK 9:41 Yesu wáhumwakina: «Mbandu yakonda lukwikilu yi yavwalangana! Yi kuna khi tangwa yikwata kadiki yi benu yi kulutambwasaka? Mutwala mwana waku kwaku.»
LUK 9:42 Bwana kakala bwesuka, kitembu kya mbi kyámubwisa ha tsi amana kyáyandika kumuningisa hika lawu. Kaasi Yesu, wákayakya kitembu kyambi, wámubelula mwana, wámuvutula phi kwena tata wandi.
LUK 9:43 Amana boosu báyituka kikuma kya kineni kya Nzambi. Bwosu bakala yituka boosu mu mana kakala hanga, wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi:
LUK 9:44 «Kwena benu, tekikenu mboti matu ku ndinga zazi: Mwana wa mutu sanda bamulambula ku moku ma batu.»
LUK 9:45 Kaasi balonguki bábakisayoku ndinga yina: yákala yakububika kikuma kya bawu, ndangu babakulaku ntendula yandi, amana bweya bákala bwawu mu kumuyufula kikuma kya dyambu medina.
LUK 9:46 Balonguki bekatendana bawu yi bawu ndangu bazaya keti nati mbuta mu kati dya bawu.
LUK 9:47 Amana Yesu bu kázaya kutendana kwákala mu mbundu za bawu, wátambula mwana, wámusya bela-bela yi yandi,
LUK 9:48 amana wábazimbwala: «Wuna wamúyamba mwana yandu, mu khumbu ya meni, meni-meni kayambini; amana wuna wangyámba meni, wumuyambi wuna wáthuma. Mukuma, wuna wenina wakhunda kuluta benu boosu, yandi wuna phi wenina mbuta.»
LUK 9:49 Kaasi Yowani wuzimbudi: «Mulongi, betu tumoniki mutu mosi wukakukwasaka bitembu bya mbi mu khumbu ya ngeyi, amana tusosiki kumukandisa, kikuma kisiku landa ngeyi ha kimosi yi betu.»
LUK 9:50 Kaasi Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Lumukandisabwoku, mukuma wuna kisiku lumenga, ha kimosi lwena yandi.»
LUK 9:51 Bwosu byákala kwisalungila bilumbu bina kakala zanguka ku zilu, Yesu wábonga lukanu lwa ngolu lwa kukwenda ku Yelusalemi.
LUK 9:52 Amana wátuma bambambala ku thwala yandi. Baba babwa mu nzila amana bákota ku hata dimosi dya bisi Samadiya ndangu bamuyidikila kutula kwandi.
LUK 9:53 Kaasi bámuyambaku, kikuma ku Yelusalemi kakala kwenda.
LUK 9:54 Buna bámona bwana, balonguki bandi, Zyaki yi Yowani, bazonzi: «Pfumu, wuzodi ni twalomba kwena mbawu yatuka ku zilu ndangu yabazinisa?»
LUK 9:55 Yesu wábaluka kwena bawu amana wábakaya.
LUK 9:56 Amana benda ku hata dya hika.
LUK 9:57 Buna bákala muna nzila, mutu mosi wázimbula kwena Yesu: «Yikúlanda kwosu kuma kuna wakwénda.»
LUK 9:58 Yesu wávutula: «Mikengi myena yi binzenzi, banuni, ku zilu, bena phi yi mazamba, kaasi Mwana wa mutu, keku yi homa kazenza mutwa wandi.»
LUK 9:59 Amana wázimbula kwena mutu wa hika: «Ndanda.» Mutu yandu wávutula: «Pfumu, pheka muswa yenda zika theti tata wama.»
LUK 9:60 Kaasi Yesu kámuzimbwala: «Yambula bamvumbi badizika bawu yi bawu, kaasi ngeyi ndawenda samuna Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 9:61 Mukwawu kázimbula: «Pfumu, yikúlanda meni; kaasi pheka muswa yenda bonga theti ndenga kwena biwutu bya mu nzu yama.»
LUK 9:62 Yesu wámuvutwala: «Wuna wusimbi tsengu mu kubundula, amana katala ku manima, kafwaniku mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 10:1 Kunima dya bwabuna, Pfumu wásola balonguki makumi tsambwadi yi boodi bahika, amana kábatuma bodi-bodi, ku thwala yandi, muna kosu mbanza yi kosu homa hana kafwana kenda yandi meni.
LUK 10:2 Kakala bazimbwala: «Mbutu ya lawu yenina, kaasi basadi, bakhunda. Mulombenu pfumu wa mbutu kahitika basadi mu mbutu yandi.
LUK 10:3 Ndalwenda! Yilutumi hanga bana ba mikoku hana kati dya bambwa-ngongu.
LUK 10:4 Lunataku keti dikuta, keti waba, keti tsabatu; luhekaku mutu mboti mu nzila.
LUK 10:5 Muna nzu yosu yina lwakóta, samunenu theti: "Ngemba yakala mu nzu yayi."
LUK 10:6 Amana yukani mwakala mutu mosi wa ngemba, ngemba ya benu yakála yi yandi; kondilo, yalúvutwakila.
LUK 10:7 Nangenu muna nzu meni yayina, dyenu, nwenu phi bina balúheka; kikuma bulungi musadi katambula lufutu lwandi. Lwendaku nzu muna nzu.
LUK 10:8 Muna mbanza yosu yina lwakóta yi muna balúyamba, dyakenu bina balúheka;
LUK 10:9 bukenu bambefu bana bakala muna, amana bazimbwalenu: "Kipfumu kya Nzambi kibwesukini kwena benu."
LUK 10:10 Kaasi muna kosu mbanza yina lwakóta, yuka baluyambiku, ndalwenda muna mabala-bala, zimbulenu:
LUK 10:11 "Keti fusyangeni dya mbanza yenu dina dinamiki ku bitambi byetu, tukhukumunidya ndangu twaluvutwaladya. Zayenu phi ni Kipfumu kya Nzambi kibwesuki."
LUK 10:12 Yiluzimbwadi ni mu kilumbu kina, phasi za Sotomu, za khunda zakála kuluta mbanza meni yina.»
LUK 10:13 «Khi kyadi kwena ngeyi, Kolazini! Khi kyadi kwena ngeyi, Betisayita! Mukuma wadi biphadi bina byásalama theti kwena benu wadi ni byásalama ku Tidi yi ku Sitoni, tuka thama, wadi batu ba bawu, bákala bábalula bifu bya bawu, bavwata tsaki amana badifuba mu mbombi!
LUK 10:14 Ihana ni mu kilumbu kya pfundusu, phasi za Tidi yi Sitoni za khunda zákala kuluta benu.
LUK 10:15 Amana ngeyi Kaphedinawuma, wadíthumba yi kuna zilu? Loni! Wakúlumuka yi kuna kalunga.»
LUK 10:16 Yesu wuzimbudi hika kwena balonguki: «Wuna wuluyukidi benu, wungyukidi meni, wuna wulubusi benu, wumbusi phi meni; amana wuna wumbusi meni, wumubusi phi wuna wáthuma.»
LUK 10:17 Balonguki bana makumi tsambwadi yi boodi bávutuka yi kyesi, amana bázimbula: «Pfumu, keti bitembu bya mbi bitulemvwakidiki mu khumbu ya ngeyi!»
LUK 10:18 Yesu wábavutwala: «Yikala mumona Satana kubwa ku zilu hanga mutsyenzya.
LUK 10:19 Talenu: yíluheka hamu dya kudyatikisa banyoka yi bikhala-khala yi ha thandu ya ngolu zoosu za mbeni, amana ka kima ku kyáfwana kuluhanga mbi.
LUK 10:20 Ihana ni lusangwalaku kikuma kya bitembu bya mbi bilulemvwakidi; kaasi sangwalenu kikuma khumbu zenu zisonami mu mazilu.»
LUK 10:21 Muna tangwa meni dina, Yesu wázakama yi kyesi, mu lusadisu lwa Kitembu kyatoma, amana wázimbula: «Yikukumisi, Tata, Pfumu wa zilu yi tsi, kikuma wásweka mambu mama kwena batu badimuka yi batu ba ngangu, amana wásongilama kwena bana bakhunda. Yibwabuna Tata, kikuma bwabuna wátya mu tonda dyaku.»
LUK 10:22 «Byosu Tata wama wáphekabya. Amana ka mutu ku wuzayi nani kenina Mwana ho ka Tata ku, ka mutu ku phi wuzayi nati kenina Tata ho ka Mwana ku yi kwena mutu wuna kazodi, Mwana, kumusengwamina.»
LUK 10:23 Wubaluki kwena balonguki, wábazimbwala mu kingenga: «Kyesi kwena mesu mana misi mona mambu mana lubati mona!
LUK 10:24 Mukuma yiluzimbwadi ni bambikudi lawu yi bakyamvu bázola kumona mana lubati tala benu, kaasi bámonamoku, bázola kuyuka phi mana lubati yuka, kaasi báyukamoku.»
LUK 10:25 Mulongi mosi wa mitsiku wátelama amana wámuhyula, ndangu kamumeka: «Mulongi, biki pfwani yihanga mu kutambula luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula?»
LUK 10:26 Yesu kámuzimbwala: «Biki básonika mu mitsiku? Abweti wisi tanga?»
LUK 10:27 Yandi wuvutudi: «"Watónda Pfumu Nzambi waku, yi mbundu yaku yosu, yi moya waku wosu, yi ngolu zaku zoosu, yi ngangu zaku zoosu". Amana khunda waku hanga ngeyi meni.»
LUK 10:28 Amana Yesu wámuzimbwala: «Bwabuna wuvutudi. Hanga bwabuna, amana wazínga.»
LUK 10:29 Kaasi yandi kázola kadinungisa, hanga wuhyudi kwena Yesu: «Amana nani wenina khunda wama?»
LUK 10:30 Yesu wávutwakila: «Mutu mosi wátuka ku Yelusalemi, wákulumuka ku Yediko; wábwa ha moku ma bandwandwa, bámutambula bima byosu, bámubeta amana bénda, bámusisa mu kulakana.
LUK 10:31 Nganga Nzambi mosi wakala kulumuka, bwana lwesi, muna nzila meni yina; wámumona, amana wutembi ku kyana.
LUK 10:32 Amana mutindu mosi, mulefi mosi wátula hakana, wámumona amana wátemba ku kyana.
LUK 10:33 Kaasi Musamadiya mosi wákala mu kitambu, wátula bela-bela yi yandi amana wámuyukila kiwayi kya lawu, buna kámumona.
LUK 10:34 Wábwesuka, wámuzunzila masi yi vinu muna phuta amana wámukasaza. Kunima, wámuzanzisa hana thandu ya Phunda wa yandi meni, wámunata ku nzu ya banzenza amana wámusadisa.
LUK 10:35 Amana kilumbu kyálanda, wálubula mafwalanga modi, wáhanabya kwena mukwa nzu ya banzenza, amana wámuzimbwala: "Musadisa mutu yandu; amana byosu bina walútikisa, yíkuvutwalabya ha yikwisa vutwakisa."»
LUK 10:36 «Khi mutu, mu kati dya bawu batatu, fwani kakala khunda wa mutu wuna babeta kwena bandwandwa?»
LUK 10:37 Mulongi wa mitsiku wuvutudi: «Wuna wámuyukila kyadi.» Yesu wámuzimbwala: «Ndawenda, amana ngeyi phi, sala bwabuna.»
LUK 10:38 Amana tangwa bákala muna nzila, Yesu yi balonguki bandi, wákota mu hata dimosi, amana mukhetu mosi, khumbu yandi Malata, wámuyamba kuna nzu yandi.
LUK 10:39 Myaki wandi wa mukhetu, bakala tela Madiya, kákala wasikuka ha kabeta muna malu ma Pfumu, yi kuhinikinaka phi ndinga yandi.
LUK 10:40 Malata yandi wudisakikiki mu bisalu bya lawu. Wisa kota amana wázimbula: «Pfumu, wubatiku mona kyadi bwana katsudikidiki, myaki wama wa mukhetu, kisalu meni hika? Muzimbwala ni katsadisa.»
LUK 10:41 Pfumu wámuvutwala: «Malata, Malata, wubati nyengalakana yi kudiyangisa kikuma kya bima bya lawu,
LUK 10:42 kaasi dyambu dimosi lwesi diluti mupfunu. Madiya wusodi dyambu dya bukheti dina bafwaniku bamubwotula.»
LUK 11:1 Kilumbu kimosi, Yesu kakala lombila homa ha mosi. Tangwa kámanisa, mosi wa balonguki bandi wámuzimbwala: «Pfumu, tulonga kulombila, bwosu kálongabwa Yowani kwena balonguki bandi.»
LUK 11:2 Yandi wábazimbwala: «Tangwa lubati lombila, zimbulakenu bwabu»: "Tata, khumbu yaku batomisaya; Kipfumu kyaku kyisa.
LUK 11:3 Tuheka, lelu, madya metu ma kosu kilumbu.
LUK 11:4 Tulolula mitsoki myetu, mukuma betu phi, tuloludi kwena batu boosu bana bisi tukota mitsoki. Amana tusadisa ndangu tubwaku mu phukumunu."
LUK 11:5 Kábazimbwala hika bwabu: «Nati muna kati dya benu, wakála yi nduku wandi, amana kamuyendila muna kati dya kisuku, mu kumuzimbwala: "Nduku, ndefisa khwanga tatu;
LUK 11:6 mukuma mosi wa banduku bama wutuki mu kitambu, wuthudidi kuna nzu, amana yeku yi kima yimúheka."
LUK 11:7 Amana yuka ni, muna kati, mukwawu kamuvutwala: "Yambula kutsya malokosi! Mwelu wakubindika wenina, bana bama yi meni-meni ha thangi thwenina; pfwaniku yivumbuka kikuma kya kukuheka khwanga."
LUK 11:8 Yiluzimbwadibwa ni, yuka kavumbukiku mu kumuhekama, kikuma nduku wandi kenina, kavúmbuka kikuma kya nziki-nziki yina kasikhokwatila amana kamúheka kyosu kina kavi mupfunu.
LUK 11:9 Amana meni, yiluzimbwadi ni lombenu, amana balúheka, sandenu amana lwaséngumuna, khokwatilenu amana balúyafwadila.
LUK 11:10 Mukuma mutu wosu wuna wisi lomba, bisi muheka; wuna wisi sanda, kisi sengumuna; amana phi kwena wuna wisi khokwatila, bayáfulula.
LUK 11:11 Khi tata mu kati dya benu, yukani mwana wandi kamulomba tsema, amana kamuheka nyoka ha kifulu kya tsema?
LUK 11:12 Kondilo, yuka kalomba dyaki, kamuheka kikhala-khala?
LUK 11:13 Yukani benu bakholwa, lwazayaka kuheka bima bya bukheti kwena bana benu, Tata wenina kuna zilu, kahána phi Kitembu Kyatoma kwena bana bisikya mulomba!»
LUK 11:14 Yesu kakala kukwasa kitembu kya mbi kyáhonda mutu kamama. Ha kyálubuka kitembu kya mbi, mukwa kamama wázonza. Amana mulumba-lumba wa batu wáyituka.
LUK 11:15 Kaasi batu bahika bázimbula bwabu: «Mu hamu dya Belezebula, pfumu wa biphidi-mutu, kabati kukwasila biphidi-mutu.»
LUK 11:16 Amana bahika, mu kumuleya, hanga bamulombi kiphadi kyatuka ku zilu.
LUK 11:17 Amana bwosu kázaya mabanza ma bawu, wábazimbwala: «Kipfumu kyosu kina kyadíkabisa kyawu meni, kyazíluka, nzu zawúlumuka zimosi ha thandu ya zikwawu.
LUK 11:18 Honi Satana kakala wadikabisa yandi meni, abweti kipfumu kyandi kyazyamina? Kikuma lubati zonza ni mu hamu dya Belezebula mbati kukwasila biphidi-mutu.
LUK 11:19 Amana yukani meni, mu hamu dya Belezebula mbati kukwasila biphidi-mutu, bana benu, mu hamu dya nati bisi kukwasilabya? Ihana bakádila bawu meni bazusi benu!
LUK 11:20 Kaasi yukani mu mulembu wa Nzambi yisi kukwasila biphidi-mutu, kisongidila ni Kipfumu kya Nzambi kyisa kedi yi kuna kwa benu.
LUK 11:21 «Yukani mutu wa ngolu, wenina yi binwaninu, muna kati dya nzu yandi, bima byandi byosu byenina bya kusweka mboti-mboti.
LUK 11:22 Kaasi yukani mosi wahika wumuluti yandi mu ngolu kisa tula, amana kamubeta, kamúbotula binwaninu byosu bina kakala sila mbundu, fwani phi kabisibya bima bina kamubongi.»
LUK 11:23 «Wuna weku yi meni, yandi mutendi wama; amana wuna kisiku khoka yi meni, kisi mwanga.»
LUK 11:24 «Tangwa kilubuki kitembu kya mbi mu kati dya mutu, kisi luta mu kati dya tseki, kyasanda homa ha kulembwila. Amana bwosu kimonihoku, kidizimbwadini: "Yikwenda vutuka, muna nzu yama, muna yílubuka."
LUK 11:25 Amana ha kyatúla, kiwani nzu ya kukombula bukheti yi yakunenga.
LUK 11:26 Hanga, kyendi amana kitambudi bitembu bikwawu tsambwadi bya mbi kuluta kyawu. Bikoti mwamuna amana bisikidi. Tsuka-tsuka, khadidi ya mutu wuna yekina hika ya mbi lawu, kuluta yina yatheti.»
LUK 11:27 Buna kakala zonza bwana, mukhetu mosi wáthuta ndinga hana kati dya mulumba-lumba wa batu amana wámuzimbwala: «Kyesi kwena kundu dina dyákuyimita yi mayeni mana mákuyemika!»
LUK 11:28 Kaasi yandi wávutula: «Kyesi, kaasi kyesi kya lawu kwena bana bisi yuka ndinga ya Nzambi amana bisiya sadila.»
LUK 11:29 Bwosu wakala basa mulumba-lumba wa batu, yandi wáyandika kuzimbula: «Mbandu yayi, ya mbi yenina! Yibati lomba kidimbu. Batámbulaku kidimbu kya hika, kaka kyakina kya Yonasi.
LUK 11:30 Mukuma, bwosu kákala, Yonasi, kidimbu kikuma kya bisi Ninive, phila mosi Mwana wa mutu kakála kidimbu kikuma kya mbandu yayi.
LUK 11:31 Pfumu wa mukhetu wa ku banda katélama, mu kilumbu kya pfundusu, ha kimosi yi batu ba mbandu yayi, amana kabáfunda, kikuma yandi, mu binzunga bya kyana bya tsi kátuka kikuma kya kuyuka mudimu wa Solumoni. Kinga yandi wenina haha, wuluti Solumoni.
LUK 11:32 Batu ba ku Ninive batélama, kilumbu kya pfundusu, ha kimosi yi mbandu yayi, amana bafúndaya, kikuma bawu básoba bikalulu, mu malongi ma Yonasi. Kinga yandu wenina haha, wuluti Yonasi.»
LUK 11:33 «Ka mutu ku walemisa mwinda kikuma kya kuswekawa holo kusyawa ku tsi ya nzungu ya tuma; kaasi bisiwa sya hana muzanga; ndangu bana bakóta bamona kyesesi.
LUK 11:34 Disu dyaku dyena mwinda wa lutu; yukani disu dyaku dyakala bukheti, lutu lwaku lwosu lwakuyinika lwenina; kaasi yukani dyakukala dyafwa, lutu lwaku phi mu phipha lwenina.
LUK 11:35 Ihana ni zaya kulunda kyesesi kina kyenina mwena ngeyi ndangu kikalaku phipha.
LUK 11:36 Honi lutu lwaku lwosu lwena lwa kuyinika, konda kukala keti kitini kimosi mu phipha, lwakála lwosu mu mwini, hanga mwinda wukulemini mu mitsyenzya myandi.»
LUK 11:37 Buna kakala zonza, mufwadisi mosi mutedisi kenda dya ku nzu yandi. Yesu wákota, wénda hana mesa.
LUK 11:38 Mufwadisi wáyituka mu kumona ni Yesu kadisukudiku, bwosu buna myakala lomba mitsiku mya bawu, ku thwala kudya.
LUK 11:39 Kaasi Pfumu kámuzimbwala: «Benu, Bafwadisi, lwisi semisa phenza ya kopha yi ya longa, kaasi ku tsya mbundu, lwabasa yi nzala bwifi yi khu.
LUK 11:40 Batu bakonda ngangu! Wuna wáhanga phenza, ka yandi ku phi wáhanga kati?
LUK 11:41 Kaasi hanakenu hanga makabu ma khenda, bina byena mu kati, amana byosu byakála bya kasemi kikuma kya benu.
LUK 11:42 «Kaasi khi kyadi kwena benu, Bafwadisi, kikuma lwisi futa kimosi kya kumi kya khaya za tsudi ya kitoku yi zina za mu musitu yi ndunda zoosu za khunda-khunda. Kaasi lwisi lenza masonga yi lungongu lwa Nzambi. Mamana mambu mafwani kusalaka, konda kuzimbakana mana masadini.
LUK 11:43 «Khi kyadi kwena benu, Bafwadisi, kikuma lwisi tonda kuzakala ha kiti kya theti, mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta yi kubongaka mboti mu mazandu.
LUK 11:44 Khi kyadi kwena benu! Kikuma lwena hanga mazyamu malamba amana batu bisi dyatama hana thandu konda kuzaya.»
LUK 11:45 Mosi wa balongi ba mitsiku wámuzimbwala: «Mulongi, mu kuzonza bwabuna, wututukwani betu phi!»
LUK 11:46 Amana yandi wávutula: «Khi kyadi kwena benu phi balongi ba mitsiku! Mukuma lwisi longidila, kwena batu, bizitu bya phasi mu kunata, amana lwisibyoku simba, benu-benu, keti ku mulembu wumosi.
LUK 11:47 Khi kyadi kwena benu! Lwisi tunga mazyamu ma bambikudi, kinga batata benu bábahonda!
LUK 11:48 Ihana lubati ta kimbangi, amana lubati sikununa mihangu mya batata benu, mukuma bawu báhonda bambikudi, amana ihana benu lwisima batungila!
LUK 11:49 Ihana ni mudimu wa Nzambi wuzimbudi: "Mbati hitika bambikudi yi bathumwa; amana bahika hana kati dya bawu, babáhonda, babányokuna phi."
LUK 11:50 Ndangu bafutisa, kwena mbandu yayi, menga ma bambikudi boosu, mana mátyakana tuka ku luyanduku lwa tsi,
LUK 11:51 tuka ku menga ma Abelu tii yikuna menga ma Zakadiya, wuna báhonda ha kati dya mesa ma kimenga yi nzu ya Nzambi. Kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa, bafútisama kwena mbandu yayi.
LUK 11:52 «Khi kyadi kwena benu balongi ba mitsiku! Kikuma lwákatula tsabi ya mazaya; benu-benu lukotiku, amana bana bazola kukota, lwábakandikisa.»
LUK 11:53 Tangwa kálubuka kwakuna, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bafwadisi báyandika kumulundika yi kumuhyula mambu ma phila yi phila;
LUK 11:54 bámuleya ndangu bamukwata mu dyambu dimosi dyalubuka mu munwa wandi.
LUK 12:1 Muna tangwa meni dina, mulumba-lumba wa batu wáwongama mu mafunda kumi-kumi, hanga batu bekadidyatikisa bawu yi bawu. Yesu wáyandika kuzimbula, theti, kwena balonguki bandi: «Dikengenu yi muvimbu wa Bafwadisi, wuna wa disu ku tsi ya lukaya.
LUK 12:2 Amana heku kima kyáswamana, kyakonda sengumuka; ka kima ku kya kitsweki kyakonda zayakana.
LUK 12:3 Yi hakana ni mambu moosu lwazónza mu kisuku, mayúkalakana mu kati dya mwini; amana mana lwafwéta mu matu, mu masuku ma kuphata, mayúkalakana mu ndinga ya ngolu, mu midilu mya nzu.»
LUK 12:4 «Yiluzimbwadibwa, kwena benu banduku bama ni lubangaku bana bisi honda lutu kaasi kunima dya bwana, bafwaniku kusala kima kiluti.
LUK 12:5 Yilúsongila nani lufwani kubanga: Bangenu mutu wuna wena ti kunima dya kuhonda, kena yi hamu dya kululosa ku bilungi. Yi bwabuna, yiluzimbwadibwa ni yandi lufwani kubanga!»
LUK 12:6 «Luzayibwoku ni makyokya matanu balendama tekisa mu mafwalanga modi? Kinga keti mosi hana kati dya mawu, kazimbakaniku ku thwala ya Nzambi.
LUK 12:7 Keti tsuki za mutwa myenu, zoosu za kutanga zenina. Lubangaku, lwena mupfunu, kuluta lawu dya banuni ba khunda!»
LUK 12:8 «Yiluzimbwadibwa ni wuna wathámbwasa ku thwala ya batu, Mwana wa mutu kamútambwasa phi ku thwala ya banzyo ba Nzambi.
LUK 12:9 Kaasi wuna wathúna ku thwala ya batu, bamútuna ku thwala banzyo ba Nzambi.
LUK 12:10 Wosu wuna wazónza mbi kikuma kya Mwana wa mutu, kalóluka; kaasi kwena wuna wasáwula Kitembu Kyatoma, kalólukaku.»
LUK 12:11 «Amana tangwa balúnata mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta, keti ku thwala ya bapfumu yi bambuta, mu kulusambisa, ludiyangisaku kikuma kya phila yina lwadíthatumuna, keti buna lwazímbula,
LUK 12:12 mukuma, Kitembu Kyatoma kalúlonga, muna tangwa medina, mana mafwani kuzimbula.»
LUK 12:13 Mutu mosi, muna kati dya mulumba-lumba, wámuzimbwala: «Mulongi, muzimbwala phangi wama twakabana yi meni kuvwa kwetu.»
LUK 12:14 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Mukwetu, nati wungyadiki meni zusi dya benu holo mukabudi wa kuvwa kwenu?»
LUK 12:15 Hanga wubazimbwadi: «Dikengenu mu lukusu lwa mbongu, mukuma keti mu kuvwa kwa lawu, luzingu lwa mutu lweku mu bima byandi.»
LUK 12:16 Kahanga wubatidi kingana kimosi: «Mafu ma mutu mosi wa mvwama hanga malubudi mbutu ya lawu.
LUK 12:17 Kakala yindula amana wudizonzidi: "Biki yihánga? Mukuma yeku yi homa hafwani mu kulumbika mbutu yama."
LUK 12:18 Hanga wuzonzi hika: "Tala buna yihánga: Yimwanga khila zama, amana thungi za hika za mbuta; ndangu yilumbika ngenza zama zoosu yi bima byama bya hika.
LUK 12:19 Amana yidizonzidi: Moya wama, bima bya lawu wenina byawu bya kusweka kikuma kya mvula za lawu; lembwa kwaku, dya, nwa amana ta mukinzi."
LUK 12:20 Kaasi Nzambi wumuzimbwadi: "Zoba dya mutu! Mu phipha meni yayi bakúlombalwa luzingu lwaku. Amana bima byabi wulumbiki, byana byákala?»
LUK 12:21 «Phila mosi bwena kwena mutu wuna wisi lumbika kimvwama kikuma kya yandi meni; kaasi keku mvwama kikuma kya Nzambi.»
LUK 12:22 Kunima Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Ihana yibati luzimbwala: Ludiyangisakaku kikuma kya luzingu lwenu ni biki lwadya, keti kikuma kya lutu lwenu, ni biki lwavwáta.
LUK 12:23 Mukuma, luzingu luluti kudya, amana lutu luluti muledi.
LUK 12:24 Simbululenu Bangandwanganga: bisiku kuna, bisiku hela; beku keti fuka, keti khila, amana Nzambi kisi badisa! Kinga benu, lwenina yi mupfunu wa lawu, kuhyoka banuni!
LUK 12:25 Nati muna kati dya benu, mu nyengi dyandi, fwani kaleyisa keti koma ka luzingu lwandi?
LUK 12:26 Yuka ni lubatiku lenda keti dyambu dya khunda, kikuma kya biki lubati diyangisila mu mambu mana masadini?
LUK 12:27 Simbululenu bithundu buna bisi lubuka: byawu byisiku sala, bisiku tunga muledi; kaasi yiluzimbwadibwa ni keti Solumoni, muna khembu yandi yosu, kávwataku hanga bithundu bina.
LUK 12:28 Yukani Nzambi kavwatisaka bwana mwangu wenina lelu mu bilanga amana mbasi balosiwa ku mbawu, mukyedika, kahángabwa kikuma kya benu phi, batu ba lukwikilu lwakhunda!
LUK 12:29 Amana benu, lusandaku bina lwadya keti bina lwanwa, lukalaku phi yi kiwayi.
LUK 12:30 Kikuma yibyana bima bisi sanda, konda kulembwa, batu ba tsi yosu bana bakondi zaya Nzambi. Kaasi benu, Tata wenu wuzayi ni mupfunu biluyenina.
LUK 12:31 Sandenu benu theti Kipfumu kya Nzambi, amana balúkosikila bikwawu.»
LUK 12:32 «Bangaku, koma ka kibuka kya mikoku! Mukuma busephidisi kwena Tata wenu mu kuluheka Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
LUK 12:33 Tekisenu kuvwa kwenu amana hanenukwa mu makabu ma khenda. Diyidikilenu benu-benu tsaki za makuta mana misiku zangana, kimvwama kina kisiku mana mu mazilu, kuna keti mwifi mosi kisiku tula, amana keti tseledi mosi kadyakyoku.
LUK 12:34 Mukuma, hana henina kimvwama kyenu, hahana hakála mbundu yenu.»
LUK 12:35 «Kalakenu bayilama, mukaba muna luketu amana mwinda myenu mya kulemisa.
LUK 12:36 Amana kalenu hanga batu babati hingila ni pfumu wa bawu, kavutuka ku mukinzi wa longu; ndangu bamukangwala ha kakwisa khokwatila.
LUK 12:37 Kyesi kwena basadi bana kawána pfumu, mu kutula kwandi, bakála batokama! Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa ni kavwáta yameni miledi mya kisalu, kabáheka kifulu ha mesa, amana kakwisa basila bima.
LUK 12:38 Kisa mu kisuku holo mu khoku watheti, yukani kabawana bwabuna, khi kyesi kwena bawu!»
LUK 12:39 «zayenubwoku mboti ni wadi mukwa nzu kazayaka khi tangwa kakwísa mwifi, kakhanaku yambwadila bakota mu nzu yandi.
LUK 12:40 Benu phi, kalenu bayilama, mukuma Mwana wa mutu kakwísa mu tangwa dina lukondi yindula.»
LUK 12:41 Hanga Phetelu wáhyula: «Pfumu, wuti kingana kina kikuma kya betu lwesi ho kikuma kya batu boosu?»
LUK 12:42 Amana Pfumu wávutula: «Nati kalema wa ngangu yi wuna bisi sila mbundu? Wuna kenda sanda pfumu wandi amana wámuheka kiyeka kya kutadikilaka nzu yi basadi bahika mukusya ni kabahekaka ndambu ya bawu ya madya mu tangwa dina difwani.
LUK 12:43 Kyesi kwena musadi wuna yukani pfumu, mu kutula kwandi, kisa muwana muna kisalu meni kina!
LUK 12:44 Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadi: kamúswanika kalenga talaka bima byandi byosu.
LUK 12:45 Kaasi ho musadi wuna kadizonzila: "Pfumu wama zingididi mu kukwisa", kayandika kubabetaka basadi ba bayakala yi basadi ba bakhetu; kadyaka, kanwaka amana kazelaka malafu,
LUK 12:46 pfumu wa musadi meni yayina kakwísa kilumbu kimosi kina kamuhingidiku yandi yi mu tangwa dina kazayiku; amana pfumu kamúheka ndola yiluti kitesu kunima, kamúsya mu kanga dya bana bisiku lemvuka.
LUK 12:47 Musadi wuna wisi dizayila luzolu lwa pfumu wandi, kaasi konda kuyidika kima holo konda kusala luzolu lwa pfumu wandi, bamuzyatwasa mafimbu ma lawu.
