LUK 12:48 Kaasi, musadi wuna wukondibwa zaya amana kisi hanga mambu mana mafwani mamuzyatwasa, katámbula mafimbu ma khunda. Kwena wuna báheka lawu, bámulomba phi lawu; kwena wuna báswekisa lawu, bamúlomba hika kuluta.»
LUK 12:49 «Yisa sya mbawu ha tsi; bwosu thondibwa ni yatekila lema!
LUK 12:50 Yena yi mbotika yimosi mu kutambula amana mbundu ha thandu yingyena tii yi kuna bwalungila!
LUK 12:51 Benu lubanzi ni ngemba yisa nata ha tsi? Loni, kaasi yiluzimbwadibwa ni ngyengu.
LUK 12:52 Mukuma tuka buthwena, batu batanu, muna nzu yimosi bahámbana, batatu mu kimbeni yi bodi amana bodi mu kimbeni yi batatu.
LUK 12:53 Bakala badihambula: tata mu kimbeni yi mwana wa yakala, amana mwana wa yakala mu kimbeni yi tata, ngudi mu kimbeni yi mwana wandi wa mukhetu amana mwana wa mukhetu mu kimbeni yi ngudi, buko bwa mukhetu mu kimbeni yi mukhetu wa mwana wandi amana mukhetu wa mwana mu kimbeni yi buko bwandi bwa mukhetu.»
LUK 12:54 Yesu kázonza hika kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu: «Tangwa lwisi mona tuti dimosi tungamu kuna mazyokidi ma tangwa, lwisi zonza: "Mvula wisi," amana bwana bulungidi.
LUK 12:55 Amana tangwa yisi fula pfunzi ya ku banda, lwisi zonza: "Mwini lawu kwakála", amana bwana bulungidi.
LUK 12:56 Bakavungalosi! Luzayi kubanguna mitindu mya tsi yi mya zilu; amana abweti lwisiku lenda kubakula mutindu wa tangwa dyadi?»
LUK 12:57 «Amana kikuma kya biki lwisiku zengila mwena benu-benu mambu mana mena masungama?
LUK 12:58 Tangwa lwendi mu kibangi yi mbanda waku ku nganda, dikasikisa lwayukana yandi buna lwenina mu nzila. Sandaku ni mbanda waku kakunata ku thwala banganzi, amana nganzi wukulambudi kwena baphumbulu, baphumbulu ndangu bakutimbula mu luzumu.
LUK 12:59 Yikuzimbwadibwa ni mwamuna walúbukamwoku yuka ni khaku kedi wufuta pfuka yina yi kuna dikuta dya tsuka.»
LUK 13:1 Muna tangwa medina, ndambu ya batu bámenika kwena Yesu buna kátuma mbala yimosi Philatu batu mu kuhonda bisi Ngadidi bamosi bana bakala yoka mikhayilu.
LUK 13:2 Yandi wubavutwadi: «Benu lubanzi ni bakwa Ngadidi meni babana, basumuki bákala kuluta bisi Ngadidi bahika, kikuma kya buna banyokuki mu mutindu wuna?
LUK 13:3 Loni, yiluzimbwadibwa; kaasi ho ni lubaludiku bikalulu byenu, lwazíluka benu boosu hanga bawu.
LUK 13:4 Ho phi lo, batu bana kumi yi nana bábwila kibaka kya kaleyi kya Silowe kina kyábahonda phi, lubanzi basumuki bákala kuluta batu boosu bahika ba ku Yelusalemi?
LUK 13:5 Loni, yiluzimbwadibwa; kaasi ho ni lubaludiku bikalulu byenu, phila mosi lwafwa benu boosu.»
LUK 13:6 Yesu wábatila kingana kyaki: «Mutu mosi kákala yi miti, wafwanana yi mumanga, bisi tela ni mufiki kákuna muna kilanga kyandi kya vinu. Wisa sanda kibundu kya fiki kwakuna, kaasi káwanakyoku.
LUK 13:7 Hanga wuzonzi kwena musadi wa vinu: "Tala, mvula tatu kedi yisi kwisa sanda kibundu kya fiki ku mufiki wawu, amana yisikyoku wana. Kisongidila, kwangawa! Kikuma kya biki wisa tambula mafu ma khatu konda kikuma?
LUK 13:8 Musadi wa vinu wumuvutwadi: "Pfumu, yambwadilawa hika mvula yayi; tangwa yisíma hika mu kabeta amana yimana sya mvumvu.
LUK 13:9 Mbanzi, walenda ha bibundu mvula yakwísa; holo, wakwángawa.»
LUK 13:10 Kilumbu kimosi kya sabata, Yesu kakala longa muna mosi ya nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta.
LUK 13:11 Kinga mukhetu mosi wa mbefu wákala hana, báloka mulumba kwena kitembu kya mbi, tuka mvula kumi yi nana; wavwembama kákala amana kakalaku lenda kuvumbuka buna bufwani.
LUK 13:12 Tangwa kámumona Yesu, wámutela amana wázimbula: «Mukhetu, wukutumuki mu kimbefu kyaku.»
LUK 13:13 Amana wámuthetika moku. Muna mbala mosi mukhetu wásungama amana wuyandiki kuzatula Nzambi.
LUK 13:14 Kaasi pfumu wa nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, kásephilaku kikuma Yesu wálungisa kubelula kuna, mu kilumbu kya sabata. Wuzimbudi kwena kibuka kya batu kina kyákala hakana: «Hena yi bilumbu bisambanu bya kisalu, alwisa dibukisaka muna bilumbu meni byabina, kaasi lwisaku mu kilumbu kya sabata.»
LUK 13:15 Pfumu wumuvutwadini: «Ha lwenina benu bakavungalosi, kosu mutu wa benu kisiku kutumuna ngombi kondilo ane wandi muna dinda, mu kilumbu kya sabata, mu kumunata ndangu benda munwisa mamba?
LUK 13:16 Amana mukhetu yandu, mwana kena muna butuka dya Bulahami, amana Satana wámukasa tuka mvula kumi yi nana, kisongidila bulungiku ni bamukutumuna misinga myandi, mu kilumbu kya sabata?»
LUK 13:17 Buna kakala zonza bwabuna, bana bakala mutendisa tsoni zábakwata; amana kibuka kyosu basephidi kikuma kya mambu moosu ma khembu kakala hanga.
LUK 13:18 Yesu kakala zimbula: «Yi biki kifwanakani Kipfumu kya Nzambi? Yi biki pfwani yifwanikisakya?
LUK 13:19 Kifwanakani yi ngenza ya tidi kábonga mutu mosi amana wátimbulaya muna masamba mandi; yimeni, yákituka miti, amana banuni ba ku zilu bisa tunga mazamba ma bawu muna mihandi myandi.»
LUK 13:20 Yesu wuzimbudi hika: «Yi biki pfwani yifwanikisa Kipfumu kya Nzambi?
LUK 13:21 Kifwanakani yi muvimbu kábonga, mukhetu mosi, amana wákotisa muna ndambu ya pfuba tii yi kuna kyáthutumuka kithoba kyosu.»
LUK 13:22 Yesu kakala luta mavula yi mahata yi kwendalongaka musamu wa Nzambi kinzila-nzila mu kukwenda ku Yelusalemi.
LUK 13:23 Mutu mosi wámuhyula: «Pfumu, batu ba khunda lwesi bahúluka?» Yesu wábavutwala:
LUK 13:24 Syenu khwakasu lwakotila ku mwelu wafitakana; mukuma, yiluzimbwadi ni, balawu basánda mu kukota amana baléndabwoku.
LUK 13:25 «Buna katelama mukwa nzu amana kayáfikila mwelu, kuna benu, lwasala ku nzila, lwayándika kukhokwatila kuna mwelu yi kuzonzaka: "Pfumu, tuyafwadila!" Kalúvutwala: "Benu, nzayiku keti ku biki lutuki!"
LUK 13:26 Hanga luyandiki kuzimbula: "Twakala dya yi kunwa ku thwala ngeyi, amana ngeyi wakala longa muna nzila za mbuta za mavula ma betu."
LUK 13:27 Amana kalúvutwala: "Nzayiku keti ku biki lutuki. Halukenu yi meni, benu boosu lwisi hanga mbi!"
LUK 13:28 Hahana kwakála bidilu yi makwenzi, tangwa lwamóna Bulahami, Kizaki, Yakobi yi bambikudi boosu muna Kipfumu kya Nzambi, amana balúkukwasa ku nzila!
LUK 13:29 Batúka ku tsosu yi ku ndamba, ku londi yi ku banda mu kutambula kifulu ku mesa mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
LUK 13:30 Amana, hakála yi batu batsuka batékila, amana batu batheti, basúkinina.»
LUK 13:31 Muna tangwa medina, ndambu ya Bafwadisi bisa muzimbwala: «Ndawenda, katuka haha, mukuma Eloti kabati tonda kukuhonda.»
LUK 13:32 Wubavutwadi: «Ndenu lwenda zimbula kwena mukengi wuna wa nduka za mbi: "Yikúkwasa biphidi-mutu amana mbeludi lelu yi mbasi; kilumbu kya tatu mbanisibya."
LUK 13:33 Kaasi bufwani yilanda nzila yama lelu, mbasi yi kilumbu kyalanda; mukuma bufwaniku ni mbikudi bamuhondila kuma kwahika ho ka ku Yelusalemi ku.»
LUK 13:34 «Yelusalemi, Yesulusalemi, ngeyi wisi honda bambikudi yi kuhondila ku matadi bana bisi kuhitika! Mbala kwa nzodi kedi kukutikisa bana baku bwosu kisi kutikisa, ngudi wa khoku, bana bandi ku tsi ya mahela mandi, kaasi lwázolabwoku!
LUK 13:35 Yi bwabuna, nzu yenu yikituki yamba. Yiluzimbwadibwa ni lwambónaku kedi tii yi kuna dyakwísila tangwa dina lwazímbula: Kasakumuka wuna wukwisa mu khumbu ya Pfumu!»
LUK 14:1 Kilumbu kimosi kya sabata, Yesu wisa dya ku nzu ya mosi wa bapfumu ba Bafwadisi, amana bawu bakala musimbulula yi tsikiningi.
LUK 14:2 Mukwa maladi ma zatu mosi wákala kuna thwala yandi.
LUK 14:3 Yesu wuhyudi kwena Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku: «Mitsiku mibati hana muswa ho lo, wa kubuka mutu mu kilumbu kya sabata?»
LUK 14:4 Kaasi báhwena talala. Hanga wumubongi mbefu, wámubuka amana wámusula kenda.
LUK 14:5 Kunima, wábazimbwala: «Nati ha kati dya benu, yukani mwana wandi ho lo ngombi wandi kabwa mu buku dimosi, kakonda mulubula yi tswatsu, mu kilumbu kya sabata?»
LUK 14:6 Kaasi bálendaku kuvutula ku kyufu kina.
LUK 14:7 Yesu wáta kingana kwena batu bana bátedisa, kikuma kámona buna bakala sola bifulu bya theti. Kábazimbwala:
LUK 14:8 «Yukani bakutela, kwena mutu, ku mikinzi mya longu, wendaku dizakadisa ha kifulu kya theti. Hakala nana ni mutu mosi kuhyoki ngeyi mu lukumu kátedisiki;
LUK 14:9 amana, wuna wulutedisiki benu boodi, kisa kuzimbwala: "Sisila yandi kifulu." Tsoni wayúka mu kwenda dizakadisa ku kifulu kya tsuka.
LUK 14:10 Kaasi tangwa bákutedisi, ndawenda sikuka ku kifulu kya tsuka, ndangu mu tangwa dina kakwísa wuna kutedisiki, kakuzimbwala: "Nduku wama, tombuka ku thwala." Amana bwakála kikuma kya ngeyi lukumu ku thwala batu boosu bana bakála ku mesa ha kimosi yi ngeyi.
LUK 14:11 Kikuma, "wuna wadítombula bamukulumuna; amana wuna wadíkulumuna, bamútombula.»
LUK 14:12 Yesu wázimbula phi kwena wuna wámutedisa: «Tangwa wisi hana madya ma mu suka keti ma mu masikidika, wutedisaku banduku baku, keti baphangi baku, keti bakwa kikanda kyaku, keti bamvwama babana lwabandakana bawu; bakuvutwala nana, kilumbu kina kyakála kya bawu, hanga bakuvutwadi ngeyi phi buna wubasadidi.
LUK 14:13 Kaasi yuka ni wuzodi kuta mukinzi, tedisa baphutu yi bakwa bifu bya mutindu yi mutindu yi bifwa malu yi moku phi yi baphofu.
LUK 14:14 Wakála yi kyesi, kikuma beku yi kima bakuvutwala. Mukuma, wafútama tangwa bafútumuka batu basungama.»
LUK 14:15 Buna káyuka bwabuna, mosi wa batu bana bakala ku mesa wázimbula kwena Yesu: «Kyesi kwena mutu wuna wadya mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi!»
LUK 14:16 Yandi wámuvutwala: «Mutu mosi wáta mukinzi wa mbuta, amana wátedisa lawu dya batu.
LUK 14:17 Mu tangwa dya kudya, wátuma musadi wandi kenda bazimbwala batu bana kátedisa yandi: "Alwisenu! Bima byosu bya kuyidika kedi byena."
LUK 14:18 Kaasi bawu boosu, mutu yi mutu, kakala lomba ndoluka. Watheti kámuzimbwala: "Kilanga kimosi thuki mu kusumba, buluti mboti, yenda talakya; ndolula."
LUK 14:19 Mukwawu kámuzimbwala: "Bangombi kumi thuki mu kusumba, yendi bameka phi; Yikulombibwa, wandolula."
LUK 14:20 Wahika wuzimbudi: "Buthwena khwediki, pfwaniku kwisa."
LUK 14:21 Musadi, mu kuvutuka, wázimbula mambu mana kwena pfumu wandi. Hanga pfumu wa nzu, mu khabu, wuzimbudi kwena musadi wandi: "Awenda tswatsu muna mabala-bala ma mbuta keti mana ma khunda, ma mbanza, amana nata kwaku baphutu yi batu bana bena yi bifu bya lutu, mutindu yi mutindu yi bifwa mesu yi bana bisi tinguna."
LUK 14:22 Hanga kunima, musadi wisa zimbula: "Pfumu, buna wulombiki busalami, kaasi bizika bisadi hika bya khatu."
LUK 14:23 Hanga pfumu wuzimbudi kwena musadi: "Awenda muna nzila yi mu mikinda mya bilanga, balundika batu mu kukota ndangu nzu yama yabasa.
LUK 14:24 Mukuma, yiluzimbwadibwa: ka mosi ku, wa batu bana bátedisa wayédika madya ma meni."»
LUK 14:25 Milumba-lumba mya batu myakala kangala yi Yandi. Yandi wubaluki amana wubazimbwadi:
LUK 14:26 «Yuka mutu wisi kwena meni amana konda kabwisa tata wandi yi ngudi wandi yi mukhetu wandi yi bana bandi yi baphangi bandi ba bayakala yi baphangi ba bakhetu, keti luzingu lwa yandi meni, kafwaniku kukala mulonguki wa meni.
LUK 14:27 Wuna wukondi nata kitakani kyandi amana kandanda, kafwaniku kukala mulonguki wa meni.
LUK 14:28 Amana nati hana kati dya benu, wázola katunga nzu ya musyetebengi, wakonda zakala theti kikuma kya kutala ho mbongu zafwana kena zawu mu kumanisina kisalu.
LUK 14:29 Kondilo, kunima dya kusikula mupfundila, konda kalenda kumanisaya, amana bana boosu bakwisa mumona bakonda museya
LUK 14:30 mu kuzimbula: "Mutu yandu wáyandika kutunga kaasi kálendaku mu kumanisa!"
LUK 14:31 Holo, khi pfumu, yuka ni kendanwana yi pfumu wahika, kazakalaku theti mu kudihyula yuka wufwani, yi bayakala mafunda kumi, kunwanisa wuna wubati kwisa ku thwala yandi yi mafunda makumodi?
LUK 14:32 Yuka loni, buna kenina hika wuna kyana, kamútumina mbambala mu kulomba ngemba.
LUK 14:33 Yi bwabuna ni, ha kati dya benu, wuna wukondi kudibwisa yi bima byandi byosu kapfwaniku kala mulonguki wa meni.»
LUK 14:34 «Mungwa kima kya mboti. Kaasi honi munzenzu wukondi, yi biki bavútwalawa?
LUK 14:35 Weku hika mboti keti kikuma kya mafu, keti kikuma kya mvumvu; bisiwa losa ku nzila. Wuna wena yi matu ma kuyuka, kayuka!»
LUK 15:1 Bakalaki ba phaku yi basumuki boosu, bábwesuka kwena Yesu ndangu bamuyuka.
LUK 15:2 Bafwadisi yi balongi ba mitsiku bázimbula mu kumukumba: «Kisi yamba basumuki, kisi dya ha kimosi yi bawu!»
LUK 15:3 Hanga Yesu wábatila kingana kyaki:
LUK 15:4 «Khi mutu ha kati dya benu, yuka kákala yi mikoku khama, amana katotisa wumosi, kasísaku makumi vwa yi vwa mahika muna nganga ndangu kenda sanda wuna wutotiki, tii yi kuna kaséngumunawa?
LUK 15:5 Amana buna kaséngumunawa, kasyáwa ha mahembu mandi yi kyesi kyosu.
LUK 15:6 Amana mu kuvutuka ku nzu yandi, kátela banduku yi bana kábandakana bawu mu kubazimbwala: "Sangwalenu yi meni, mukuma tsengumuniwa mukoku wama wuna wátota!"
LUK 15:7 Yiluzimbwadi: "Phila mosi, kyesi kya lawu kyakála mu zilu, kikuma kya musumuki mosi wubaludi mbundu, kuluta batu bana basungama makumi vwa yi vwa bana beku yi mupfunu wa kubalula mbundu.»
LUK 15:8 «Holo, khi mukhetu, yuka kakala yi bibendi kumi amana katotisa kibendi kimosi, kakwikaku yi mwinda, kakombulaku nzu amana wusandi bukheti-bukheti, yi kuna kamónikya?
LUK 15:9 Buna kamónakya, katédisa kuna nzu yandi, banduku yi bakhetu bana kábandakana bawu, amana mu kabázimbwala: "Sangwalenu yi meni kikuma tsengumunikya kibendi kya makuta kina yítotisa!"
LUK 15:10 Phila mosi, yiluzimbwadibwa, kyesi bwena ku thwala banzyo ba Nzambi kikuma kya musumuki mosi wubaludi mbundu.»
LUK 15:11 Yesu kázimbula hika: «Mutu mosi wákala yi bana bodi ba bayakala.
LUK 15:12 Amana wuna wa muleki kuluta wázimbula kwena tata wandi: "Tata, pheka ndambu ya kimvwama yina pfwani yibonga." Hanga tata wukabisi kuvwa kwandi kwena bawu.
LUK 15:13 Amana kunima koma ka bilumbu, mwana wuna wa muleki, wábalula mu makuta bima byosu bina kakala byawu, amana wénda ku tsi yimosi ya kyana. Kwakuna, wázanga kimvwama kyandi mu luzingu lwa kisaka-saka.
LUK 15:14 Buna kámanisa byosu, nzala ya lawu yákota muna tsi meni yana, amana wáyandika kukonda mu byosu.
LUK 15:15 Wádikotisa ku kisalu kya mutu mosi, wa ku tsi meni yayina, wámutuma muna bilanga byandi mu kuhungula bangulu.
LUK 15:16 Amana kázola bwabuna ndangu kayukutaka mu bibundu bina bakala dya bangulu, kaasi keti mutu kámuhekabyoku.
LUK 15:17 Muna kati dya yandi meni, kádizimbwala: "Bakwa, basadi ba tata wama, benina yi mapha malutuki, amana meni, haha, mbati fwa ku nzala?
LUK 15:18 Yitélama, yikwénda kwena tata wama amana yimúzimbwala: Tata, yísumuka ku thwala Nzambi yi ku thwala ngeyi.
LUK 15:19 Pfwaniku hika mu kuthela mwana waku. Mbongila hanga mosi wa basadi baku."
LUK 15:20 Amana wátelama mu kukwenda kwena tata wandi. «Buna kákala kuna kyana, tata wandi mumoni amana wuyuki kiwayi kya lawu: wénda thinu, wámubumbakana amana wámuyamba phi.
LUK 15:21 Mwana kámuzimbwala: "Tata, yísumuka ku thwala Nzambi yi ku thwala ngeyi. Pfwaniku hika kukala hanga mwana waku wa kubuta."
LUK 15:22 Kaasi tata wázimbula kwena basadi bandi: "Natenu tswatsu mvwela yina yiluti bukheti amana muvwatisenuya; musyenu ndamba yimosi kuna mulembu yi tsabatu kuna malu.
LUK 15:23 Natenu mwana ngombi wa senga, muhondenu phi; tudyenu, twata mukinzi,
LUK 15:24 mukuma, mwana wama yandu kadikini wafwa, amana wuvutwakidi luzingu; kákadiki wátota, amana wusengumuki." Amana báyandika kuta mukinzi.
LUK 15:25 «Kinga, mwana wa tsomi, ku bilanga kákala. Buna kávutuka, amana wátula bela-bela yi nzu, wáyuka kizamba yi makinu.
LUK 15:26 Wátela mosi wa basadi mu kumuhyula mambu mana mákala luta.
LUK 15:27 Amana yandu wámuzimbwala: "Myaki waku wuvutuki, amana tata waku wumuhondisidi mwana ngombi wa mafuta, kikuma kamuvutwakidi yi lutu lwa ngolu."
LUK 15:28 Kaasi mbuta wáfunga khabu; kázolaku kukota. Tata wandi wálubuka mu kumubokwadila.
LUK 15:29 Hanga wuvutudi kwena tata wandi: "Mvula za lawu kedi tsadi kikuma kya ngeyi hanga musadi, yisalaku kolama ku mitsiku myaku. Amana wasalaku pheka keti mwana phunda ndangu yita mukinzi yi banduku bama.
LUK 15:30 Kaasi tangwa kisi vutuka, mwana waku yandu wénda fwasa kuvwa kwaku yi bakhetu ba bandumba; kikuma kya yandi wumuhondisidi mwana ngombi wa mafuta!"
LUK 15:31 Tata wámuzimbwala: "Ngeyi, mwana wama, wenina bilumbu byosu yi meni, amana kyosu kyenina kya meni, kyenina phi kya ngeyi.
LUK 15:32 Kaasi bulungiki twata bukheti mukinzi yi kusangwala, mukuma myaki waku yandu wumoni, kákadiki wafwa, amana wuvutwakidi luzingu; kákadiki watota amana wusengumuki!"»
LUK 16:1 Yesu kakala zimbula hika kwena balonguki: «Mutu mosi wa mvwama wákala yi kalema mosi; wuna bátungulula, wakala fwasa bima byandi.
LUK 16:2 Hanga mvwama wumutedi amana wumuzimbwadi: "Biki mbati yuka kuzonzila kikuma kya ngeyi? Tsongila phila yina wukasadilaka kisalu kyaku; mukuma wufwaniku hika kukala kalema ka meni."
LUK 16:3 Kaphita wudizonzidi yandi meni: "Biki yihánga, kikuma pfumu wama mbotudikya kisalu kya kalema? Kusala bilanga? Yeku yi ngolu za kudima. Kulomba-lomba? Yiyúka tsoni."
LUK 16:4 Nzayi buna yihánga, ndangu kwakala batu bana bangyámba, kwena bawu, tangwa bakhátula mu kisalu kyama kya kalema!"
LUK 16:5 Hanga wutedisi kosu mutu wuna wákala yi pfuka ya pfumu wandi. Wuhyudi kwena watheti: "Thalu kwa wufwani kufuta kwena pfumu wama?"
LUK 16:6 Yandi wávutula: "Mindungu khama mya masi." Amana Kalema wámuzimbwala: "Bonga mukanda waku wa pfuka; zakala tswasu, sonika: makumatanu."
LUK 16:7 Kunima wáhyula kwena mukwawu wahika: "Amana ngeyi thalu kwa wufwani kufuta?" Yandi wávutula: "Tsaki khama za bule." Kalema wámuzimbwala: "Bonga mukanda waku wa pfuka sonika: makumi nana.
LUK 16:8 Amana pfumu wámuzatula kalema wuna wa bikwaki kikuma kásala mambu hanga mutu wadimuka mukuma batu ba tangwa dyadi, benina badimuka lawu mu mambu ma batu bana bafwanana bawu, kuluta bana benina mu mwini.»
LUK 16:9 Yesu wáyika: «Amana meni yiluzimbwadi: lakamenu kikhunda yi bimvwama bya mbi bya tsi yayi, ndangu tangwa byafwa, baluyamba mu bifulu bya luzingu lwakonda tsuka.
LUK 16:10 Wuna wena mwani mu bima bya khunda, kakála phi mwani mu bima bya mbuta. Amana wuna wukondi masonga mu bima bya khunda, keku phi yi masonga mu bima bya mbuta.
LUK 16:11 Yuka ni lwakálaku masonga mu kimvwama kya mwani kya tsi yayi, nati walúheka bimvwama bya kyedika?
LUK 16:12 Amana yukani lweku yi mwani ku kima kya mukwenu, nati walúheka kima kya benu-benu?
LUK 16:13 «Ka musadi mosi ku wufwani kakala muhika wa bapfumu bodi: holo kaménga mosi amana katónda mukwawu; kondilo kadínama yi mosi amana wumumengi mukwawu. Lufwaniku kusadila Nzambi yi mbongu.»
LUK 16:14 Bafwadisi, bázoluka mbongu, bakala yuka mambu mana mosu amana báyandika kuseya Yesu.
LUK 16:15 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Benu lwisi dimonikisa batu ba bukheti, ku thwala batu, kaasi Nzambi wuzayi mbundu zenu. Mukuma, mambu mana menina ma mbuta ku mesu ma batu, mena nzanzi ku mesu ma Nzambi.
LUK 16:16 «Yi kuna tangwa dya Yowani, mitsiku yi Bambikudi kwákala. Tuka buna, Kipfumu kya Nzambi básamunakya hanga Musamu wa Bukheti; amana kosu mutu kisi sya ngolu mu kukotamwa.
LUK 16:17 Kinga bweku phasi kikuma kya zilu yi tsi mu kuhyoka, kuluta kwa kisona kimosi kya mitsiku mu kubwa.
LUK 16:18 «Wosu wuna wukatudi mukhetu wandi, amana kakwela wahika, mbongi kati. Amana wuna wukwedi mukhetu wuna bákatula ku longu kwena yakala dyandi, mbongi kati.»
LUK 16:19 «Hákala yi mutu mosi wa mvwama; wakala vwata miledi mya bukheti yi mya thalu kuluta; amana wakala ta kizamba yi kunata luzingu lwa khembu.
LUK 16:20 Phutu mosi wákala lutu yi bitoni-bitoni, khumbu yandi Lasalu, kákala wanimba muna mwelu wa yandi.
LUK 16:21 Kakala zola kuyukuta bizotu bina byákala bwa mu tsi ya mesa ma mvwama. Bambwa bakala henda bitoni byandi.
LUK 16:22 Phutu wáfwa amana bámunata kwena banzyo bela-bela yi Bulahami. Mvwama phi wáfwa amana bámuzika.
LUK 16:23 Muna kalunga, kávumbula mesu, yi minyanga myandi, wámona kuna kyana Bulahami yi Lasalu hana kabeta ka yandi.
LUK 16:24 Hanga wubekitidi: "Tata Bulahami, ngyukila kyadi! Mutuma Lasalu kavundika tsongi ya mulembu wandi muna mamba, ndangu kandokisina ha lulaka mukuma mbati nyokuka mu mbawu yayi."
LUK 16:25 Kaasi Bulahami wámuvutwala: "Mwana wama, bambuketi ni ngeyi wátambula mboti yaku mu luzingu lwaku, kaasi Lasalu, yandi, munyanga kávwa. Buthwena bwabu, kwaku, yandi kena walembwa, kaasi ngeyi wubati nyokuka.
LUK 16:26 Amana mu byana byosu, mbenga mosi ya mbuta basya ha kati dya betu yi benu, ndangu bana bazóla kuluta tuka kwaku yi kuna lwena benu, balendaku salabwa; amana ni balábukaku phi tuka kuna lwena benu yi kwena betu."
LUK 16:27 Mvwama wázimbula: "Yikubokwadidi ngeyi tata mu kutuma Lasalu muna nzu ya tata wama;
LUK 16:28 mukuma yena yi baphangi batanu. Kenda banatina kimbangi kyandi ndangu bisaku, bawu phi, kuma kwaku kwena yi minyanga."
LUK 16:29 Kaasi Bulahami kázimbula: "Bena yi Moyize yi Bambikudi: babayukila!"
LUK 16:30 Mvwama wulanduludini: "Loni, tata Bulahami. Kaasi yuka ni mutu mosi wa ku bafwa kenda kwena bawu, babálumuna mbundu."
LUK 16:31 Kaasi Bulahami wámuzimbwala: "Yukani bayukidiku Moyize yi Bambikudi, bakwíkilaku, keti mwena mutu wafútumuka ha kati dya bafwa."»
LUK 17:1 Yesu wázimbula kwena balonguki bandi: «Bwalendaku salama ni kukalaku mambu mana misi hukumuna; kaasi kyadi kwena mutu wuna mabwidi!
LUK 17:2 Bulungi kwena yandi bamuzitikila, muna tsingu, kalunga tadi amana bamudibula muna yanga dya mbuta, ndangu kahukumuna nana mosi wa baleki baba.
LUK 17:3 Dikengenu! «Yuka ni phangi waku kasumuki, musongila mbi yandi. Honi kabalula mbundu, mulolula.
LUK 17:4 Yukani kasumuki, kwena ngeyi, mbala tsambwadi muna kilumbu, amana ni mbala tsambwadi wisi vutuka kwena ngeyi, mu kuzimbula: "Yibálula mbundu", wamúlolula.»
LUK 17:5 Bathumwa bázimbula kwena Pfumu: «Tuyika lukwikilu lwa lawu.»
LUK 17:6 Pfumu wávutula: «Wadi lwakala yi lukwikilu hanga ngenza ya tidi, lukhani zonza kwena kalamba ka miti wawu: "Divusa, awenda dikuna muna yanga dya mbuta", amana wululemvukidi.»
LUK 17:7 «Nati ha kati dya benu, yukani kakala yi musadi wisi bundula holo wisi hungula kibuka kya mikoku, tangwa kisi vutukisa ku bilanga, kamúzimbwala: "Awisa tswatsu wasikuka ha mesa"?
LUK 17:8 Kaasi kamúzimbwalaku bwabu: "Ndambila kudya kwa meni, vwata miledi mya kisalu kikuma kya kungidikila mesa, yi kuna yidya amana ndwi, kunima, ngeyi phi wafwana dya, wanwa phi"?
LUK 17:9 Yandi, keku yi mupfunu wa kumuvutwala matondu musadi wuna tangwa kamuhangidi bwosu kámulomba?
LUK 17:10 Phila mosi yi benu phi tangwa lwasála mosu mana kalúlomba, zimbulenu: "Betu, basadi kwetu thwenina; twásala lwesi mana twáfwana kusala."»
LUK 17:11 Bwosu kakala kwenda ku Yelusalemi, kakala hyokila hana kati dya Samadiya yi Ngadidi.
LUK 17:12 Amana mu kukota kwandi mu hata dimosi, bakwa bwasi kumi bisa mutundakana. Bátelama kuna kyana,
LUK 17:13 báthuta ndinga amana bázimbula: «Yesu, Mulongi, tuyukila kyadi!»
LUK 17:14 Amana tangwa kábamona, wábazimbwala: «Ndenu lwenda disongila kwena banganga Nzambi.» Buna bakala kwenda kwakuna, básema.
LUK 17:15 Mosi wa bawu, buna kádimona ni wusemi, wisa vutukisa, mu kuzatula Nzambi mu ndinga ya ngolu.
LUK 17:16 Wábwa mbunzu mu mafu muna bitambi bya Yesu amana wámuvutwala matondu. Mwisi Samadiya kákala.
LUK 17:17 Amana Yesu wáhyula: «Ka boosu ku bawu kumi basemi? Amana vwa dyahika, ku biki dyenina?
LUK 17:18 Kaka munzenza meni yandu lwesi wudimonikisi mu kwisa vutuka kuhana khembu kwena Nzambi?»
LUK 17:19 Kunima, wámuzimbwala: «Telama, ndawenda. Lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini.»
LUK 17:20 Bamuhyudi kwena Bafwadisi ndangu bazaya ho mu khi tangwa kyakwísa Kipfumu kya Nzambi. Yandi wábavutwala: «Kipfumu kya Nzambi kisiku kwisa mu phila yina bafwani bamoninakya.
LUK 17:21 Bazímbulaku ni "Talenu, haka kyenina!" Holo "Kuna kyenina!" Mukuma Kipfumu kya Nzambi, hana kati dya benu kyenina.»
LUK 17:22 Amana wázimbula hika kwena balonguki: «Bilumbu byakwísa bina lwasánda ndangu lwamóna keti kimosi kya bilumbu bya Mwana wa mutu, kaasi lwamónakyoku.
LUK 17:23 Balúzimbwala: "Kuna kenina!" Holo, "Kwaku kenina!" Kaasi lwendakwoku, lutsyakulakwoku.
LUK 17:24 Mukuma, bwosu wisi kenya munyenya, tselu yi tselu ya zilu, yibwana buna kakála Mwana wa mutu mu kilumbu kyandi.
LUK 17:25 Kaasi buluti theti, kanyokwama lawu; amana bamulosila kwena mbandu yayi.
LUK 17:26 Mana máluta mu bilumbu bya Nowa; phila mosi malúta mu bilumbu bya Mwana wa mutu.
LUK 17:27 Batu bakala dya, bakala nwa, bayakala yi bakhetu bakala kwela yi ku dikwela tii yi kuna kakótila Nowa mu nzasa: hanga kithombu kisi zaluka, kibatotisi boosu.
LUK 17:28 Bwana, bwabuna bwákala phi hanga mu bilumbu bya Loti: batu bakala dya, bakala nwa, bakala sumba, bakala sumbisa, bakala kuna amana bakala tunga phi;
LUK 17:29 kaasi kilumbu kina kalubuka Loti mu Sotomu, mvula mosi wanoka wa mbawu yi bupfundu bwakala lema ku zilu, amana wábatotisa boosu.
LUK 17:30 Phila mosi malúta kilumbu kina kakwisa sengumuka Mwana wa mutu.
LUK 17:31 «Muna kilumbu kina, wuna wakála ku nzila hana mudilu, wakála yi bima byandi mu nzu, katulukaku kikuma kya kubongabya; amana wuna wakála phi ku bilanga, kavutukaku mu manima.
LUK 17:32 Bambukenu mukhetu wa Loti!
LUK 17:33 Wuna wásanda kusweka luzingu lwandi, katótisalwa, kaasi wuna watótisalwa, kahúlulalwa.
LUK 17:34 "Yiluzimbwadibwa ni, muna phipha meni yina, ha kati dya batu bodi bakála ha thangi yimosi, mosi bamútambula amana mukwawu kasála.
LUK 17:35 Mu kati dya bakhetu bodi bakwata toka mu kindundu, mosi bamúnata, mukwawu kasála.
LUK 17:36 Bayakala bodi bakála mu kilanga kimosi, mosi bamúnata, mukwawu kasála.»
LUK 17:37 Balonguki bámuzimbwala: «Ku biki, Pfumu?» Amana yandi wávutula: «Kuna kwakála mvumbi, yi kwakuna phi bakútakanina bangandwanganga.»
LUK 18:1 Yesu kakala batila kingana kyaki mu kusongila ni bulungi, kulombila bilumbu byosu amana konda kulembwa.
LUK 18:2 Kázimbula bwabu: «Kwákala, ku mbanza mosi, yi zusi mosi, wákalaku banga Nzambi amana kakala lewula mutu woosu.
LUK 18:3 Mwákala phi, muna mbanza meni yana, yi mukhetu mosi wa mufwidi wuna wakala kwisa mu kumuzimbwala: "Nzengila mukanu wawu, kikuma baphangi mbi."
LUK 18:4 Tuka thama, zusi kázolaku; kaasi kunima, wádizimbwala: "Ketibwe yisiku banga Nzambi amana yisi lewula batu,
LUK 18:5 kaasi kikuma mufwidi yandu kabati ngyangisa, yimúzengila mukanu ndangu kisaku ngyata mutwa."»
LUK 18:6 Pfumu wáyika: «Yukenu buna kazimbudi zusi wa mbi.
LUK 18:7 Amana Nzambi, kakonda zengila, batu bandi kásola, mukanu, tangwa babati mutela phipha yi mwini? Kabáhingidisa?
LUK 18:8 Yiluzimbwadibwa, kabázengila mukanu yi tswatsu. Kaasi tangwa kakwísa Mwana wa mutu, lukwikilu kakwisa wana ha tsi?»
LUK 18:9 Yesu wáta hika kingana kyaki, kikuma kya batu bahika bisi dibanzila ni basungama kaasi bisi lewula bakwawu:
LUK 18:10 «Bayakala bodi bakala kwenda ku nzu ya Nzambi mu kulombila; mosi kákala mufwadisi, mukwawu, kalaki ka phaku.
LUK 18:11 Mufwadisi wátelama, wálombila bwabu yandi meni: "Ah! Nzambi, yikuvutwadi matondu kikuma yeku hanga bayakala bahika, bena befi yi batu bakonda sungama, bita-mbongi; holo hanga kalaki ka phaku yandi.
LUK 18:12 Yisi zila kudya, mbala zodi muna phosa, yisi futa kimosi kya kumi kya bima byama byosu."
LUK 18:13 Kalaki ka phaku, yandi, kákala watelama kuna kyana; kálendaku kuvumbula mesu ku zilu, kaasi kákala bunda hana thulu yi kuzonzaka: "Ah! Nzambi, ngyukila kyadi, musumuki yenina."
LUK 18:14 Kyedika yiluzimbwadibwa, yandu-yandu wákulumuka hika ku nzu yandi, mu ndonga yi Nzambi; kaasi ka wuna ku mukwawu. Mukuma wuna wadítombula, kakúlumuka; kaasi wuna wadíkulumuna, katómbuka.»
LUK 18:15 Batu bakala nata kwena Yesu keti bana bakhunda ba lubutu, ndangu kabasimba yi koku. Balonguki, mu kumona bwabuna, báyandika kubakaya.
LUK 18:16 Kaasi Yesu wáhana muswa ni bamunatina bawu amana wázimbula: «Yambulenu bana bisa kwena meni. Lubakandisaku, mukuma Kipfumu kya Nzambi kyenina kikuma kya bana bena hanga bawu.
LUK 18:17 Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadi: wuna wakonda yamba Kipfumu kya Nzambi hanga mwana wa khunda, kakótamwoku, swa!»
LUK 18:18 Pfumu mosi wáhyula kwena Yesu: «Mulongi wa bukheti, biki pfwani yihanga mu kubonga luzingu lwakonda tsuka?»
LUK 18:19 Yesu wámuzimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki wuthedidi wa bukheti? Heku mutu wenina wa bukheti ho ka Nzambi lwesi ku.
LUK 18:20 Wuzayi mitsiku: "Taku mbongi, hondaku, yibaku; taku kimbangi kya luvunu, zitisa tata waku yi ngudi waku.»
LUK 18:21 Mutu wuna wávutula: «Yisi lemvukilamya myana myosu tukidila kileki kyama.»
LUK 18:22 Yesu buna kámuyuka bwabuna, wázimbula: «Kima kimosi hika kikukondi; tekisa byosu bina wena byawu, kabisabya kwena baphutu amana watámbula kimvwama mu mazilu. Kunima, nzawisa ndanda.»
LUK 18:23 Kaasi buna káyuka bwabuna, wekina mu kiwayi kya lawu, mukuma mvwama wambuta kákala.
LUK 18:24 Yesu buna kámumona bwabuna mu kiwayi, wázimbula: «Phasi bwena kwena bana benina yi kimvwama mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
LUK 18:25 Mukuma bweku phasi kwena Kamela mu kulobuka ha hundu dya ndongu, kuluta mvwama mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 18:26 Bana bakala muyuka bázimbula: «Amana nati wufwani kahuluka?»
LUK 18:27 Yesu wávutula: «Mambu mana maléndakanaku kwena batu, maléndakana kwena Nzambi.»
LUK 18:28 Phetelu wázimbula: «Talandi, betu twásisa bima byákala bya betu, mu kukulanda ngeyi.»
LUK 18:29 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadibwa, heku mutu wásisa, kikuma kya Kipfumu kya Nzambi, nzu yi mukhetu yi baphangi, yi tata yi ngudi wandi, holo bana,
LUK 18:30 kakonda tambula, bya lawu kuluta mu tangwa dyadi yi muna tsi yina yisi kwisa, luzingu lwakonda tsuka.»
LUK 18:31 Yesu wábonga bawu Kumi yi bodi amana wábazimbwala bwabu «Tubati tombuka ku Yelusalemi. Mambu moosu mana másonama mu nzila ya bambikudi kikuma kya Mwana wa mutu, malúngila.
LUK 18:32 Mukuma bamúlambula ku moku ma baphani, bamúseya, bamútukwana, bamúlokwala metya.
LUK 18:33 Bamúzyatula, kunima bamúhonda. Amana kilumbu kya tatu, kafútumuka.»
LUK 18:34 Kaasi bawu bábakisaku keti kima mu moosu mana; thendula ya ndinga yina yabákadila yakufidinga, bázayaku keti biki bwazola kuzonza.
LUK 18:35 Bwosu kakala phusana bela-bela yi Yediko, phofu mosi kakala wasikuka kuna kabeta ka nzila yi kulombaka.
LUK 18:36 Wáyuka mulumba-lumba wa batu wákala hyoka amana wáhyula keti biki byabina.
LUK 18:37 Bámuvutwala: «Yesu mwisi Nazaleti wubati luta.»
LUK 18:38 Kahanga wukalungi: «Yesu, Mwana Tavidi, ngyukila kyadi!»
LUK 18:39 Bana bákala ku thwala, báyandika kumukaya ndangu kadibata. Kaasi wákalunga hika ngolu: «Mwana wa Tavidi ngyukila kyadi!»
LUK 18:40 Yesu wátelama, amana wásenda ni bamunatina yandi. Tangwa kábwesuka, Yesu wámuhyula:
LUK 18:41 «Biki wuzodi yihanga kikuma kya ngeyi?» Yandi wávutula: «Pfumu, nzodi yimona hika.»
LUK 18:42 Hanga Yesu wumuzimbwadi: «Mona hika. Lukwikilu lwaku lukuhuludini.»
LUK 18:43 Muna tangwa meni dina, wáyandika kumona amana wámulanda mu kuzatula Nzambi. Batu boosu, mu kumona bwabuna, báyandika mu kukumisa Nzambi.
LUK 19:1 Yesu wákota mu Yediko amana wáhyokila muna mbanza.
LUK 19:2 Kwákala kwakuna yi mutu mosi, khumbu yandi Zakhayi; wákala pfumu wa bakalaki ka phaku, mvwama phi kákala.
LUK 19:3 Kakala sanda mu kumona keti nati kákala Yesu, kaasi kikuma kya mulumba-lumba wa batu, kálendaku kumumona, mukuma wakhufi kákala.
LUK 19:4 Hanga wénda thinu kuna thwala amana wázanza muna miti mosi ndangu kamumona, kikuma mwamuna kafwana kulutila.
LUK 19:5 Amana buna kátula Yesu homa meni yayina, wáthuta mesu ku zilu amana wámuzimbwala: «Zakhayi, tuluka tswatsu, bulungi, yikala lelu ku nzu yaku.»
LUK 19:6 Zakhayi wátuluka tswasu mu kumuyamba yi kyesi kyosu.
LUK 19:7 Amana mu kumona bwabuna, boosu bányengalakana: «Wendi kala ku nzu ya musumuki.»
LUK 19:8 Kaasi Zakhayi, wamutendendi, wuzimbudi kwena Pfumu: «Pfumu, yihána kwena batsukami kati-kati dya kuvwa kwama, amana yukani yihuna mu kulutula thalu ya kosu kima kina kwena mutu, yimúvutwala mbala ya.»
LUK 19:9 Yesu kámuzimbwala: «Lelu luhulusu lwisi kikuma kya nzu yayi, mukuma yandi phi kenina mwana mosi wa Bulahami.
LUK 19:10 Mukuma, Mwana wa mutu kisa sanda yi kuhulula kina kyátota.»
LUK 19:11 Bwosu bakala yuka bima bina, Yesu wáyika hika kingana kimosi kikuma bela-bela yi Yelusalemi kákala, amana bakala banza ni Kipfumu kya Nzambi fwani kyamonika muna tangwa meni dina.
LUK 19:12 Hanga wuzimbudi bwabu: «Mutu mosi wa kikanda kya lukumu wénda ku tsi ya kyana, mu kumuyadika kipfumu kya hata dyandi; ku nima dya kuvutuka.
LUK 19:13 Amana kahanga wutedi kumi dya basadi bandi, wubaheki mafwalanga kumi ma wolu. Amana wábazimbwala: "Sadilenuzoku bikhita tii yi kuna yikwisa vutwakila."
LUK 19:14 Kaasi bakwa mulambu wandi bakala mumenga, amana bátuma kibuka kimosi kya bambambala ku manima ma yandi, ndangu benda zimbula kuna mbanza yina kenda: "Betu tuzodiku: mutu yandu katuyala."
LUK 19:15 "Buna kávutuka, kunima dya kumuyadika kipfumu, hanga wutedisi basadi bana káheka makuta, ndangu kazaya keti bweti básadilama.
LUK 19:16 Watheti wísa amana wázimbula: "Pfumu, fwalanga dyaku dya wolu dilumbudi makwawu kumi."
LUK 19:17 Pfumu wámuzimbwala: "Bwa bukheti, wenina musadi mosi wa bukheti kikuma wuhwidi mwani mu mambu ma khunda; watámbula kipfumu ha thandu ya mbanza kumi."
LUK 19:18 Wazodi wísa amana wázimbula: "Pfumu, fwalanga dyaku dya wolu dilumbudi matanu makwawu."
LUK 19:19 Pfumu wámuvutwala: "Ngeyi, phila mosi, wakála pfumu wa mbanza tanu."
LUK 19:20 Wahika wísa, amana wázimbula: "Pfumu, tala di, fwalanga dyaku dya wolu dina yízindika ha kitemba.
LUK 19:21 Mukuma ngeyi mbangiki, kikuma ngeyi wena mutu wa mathata. Wisi bonga bima bina wusikudiku amana wisi hela bina wukuniku."
LUK 19:22 Pfumu wámuzimbwala: "Muna ndinga zaku meni zina yi mwana yikúfundisila, musadi wa mbi! Wázaya ni meni mukwa mathata. Yisi bonga bima bina tsikudiku; yisi hela phi bina khuniku.
LUK 19:23 Amana kikuma kya biki wakonda sila mbongu zama mu nzu yina bisi vudisila mbongu? Mu kuvutuka kwama yikakwenda bongaza yi muluta."
LUK 19:24 Kunima wázimbula kwena batu bana bákala hana: "Mubotulenudyoku fwalanga dya wolu amana hekenudya kwena wuna wena yi mafwalanga kumi."
LUK 19:25 Bámuzimbwala: "Pfumu, yandi mafwalanga ma wolu kumi kenina mawu kedi!"
LUK 19:26 Yandi wávutula: "Yiluzimbwadibwa: bayíka kwena wuna wena yi bima; kaasi wuna kondi kima, bamúbwotula keti kina kena kyawu.
LUK 19:27 Kaasi kwena bambeni bama, bana bazodikiku ni yibayala, banatenu kwaku amana bazengenu tsingu ha mesu mama."»
LUK 19:28 Kunima dya kuzimbula bwabuna, Yesu wénda ku thwala bawu amana wátombuka ku Yelusalemi.
LUK 19:29 Tangwa kátula bela-bela yi mahata mama: Betifasi yi Betaniya, bela-bela yi mongu wa Olive, wátuma bodi ba balonguki bandi,
LUK 19:30 wubazimbwadi: «Alwenda kuna hata dina dyenina kuna sambwa; ha lwakóta, lwamóna mwana wa ane mosi wuna bisi zanza batu, wakuzitikila; wuna bakonda zanza kedi keti mbala mosi kwena mutu. Mukutumunenu amana munatenu.
LUK 19:31 Yukani mutu kaluhyula: "kikuma kya biki lubati mukutwamina?", lwamúzimbwala bwabu: "Pfumu mupfunu kamuvi."»
LUK 19:32 Bana kátuma benda amana báwana mambu bwosu kábazimbwala.
LUK 19:33 Tangwa bakala kutumuna mwana ane, bakwa yandi bábazimbwala: «Kikuma kya biki lubati kutwamina mwana wa ane?»
LUK 19:34 Bávutula: «Pfumu mupfunu kamuvi.»
LUK 19:35 Amana bámunata mwana wa ane kwena Yesu, kunima bátimbula miledi mya bawu hana kunda dya mwana wa ane, amana bámuzanzisa Yesu.
LUK 19:36 Tangwa kakala kwenda, batu bakala yala mizaka mya bawu muna nzila.
LUK 19:37 Amana kakala bwesuka ku khulumuka ya mongu wa ba Olive tangwa bakala sangwala kibuka kya balonguki, bakala zatula Nzambi mu ndinga ya ngolu, kikuma kya biphadi byosu bina bámona.
LUK 19:38 Bakala zimbula: «Kasakumuka wuna wisi kwisila mu khumbu ya Pfumu! Ngemba mu zilu yi khembu muna bisoka!»
LUK 19:39 Amana ndambu ya Bafwadisi, muna mulumba-lumba wa batu, bámuzimbwala: «Mulongi, bakaya balonguki baku.»
LUK 19:40 Yandi wábavutwala: «Yiluzimbwadibwa, yukani bawu badibata, matadi makálunga!»
LUK 19:41 Amana mu kubwesuka, Yesu wámona mbanza amana wádila kikuma kya yawu,
LUK 19:42 mu kuzimbula: «Wadi ngeyi phi wázaya, mu kilumbu kyaki, abweti kutambula ngemba! Kaasi buthwena moosu makusweka mena ku mesu maku.
LUK 19:43 Mukuma bilumbu byakwísa, kwena ngeyi, bina bakúzyeta buna bufwani kwena bambeni baku amana bakúzinga yi kukufitikisa muma mwosu.
LUK 19:44 Bakúbula, ngeyi yi bana baku mu kati dya ngeyi, amana basísaku mu kati dya ngeyi keti tadi ha thandu ya tadi, kikuma wázayidilaku tangwa dina kisi kutala Nzambi!»
LUK 19:45 Amana buna kákota mu nzu ya Nzambi, wáyandika kukula batu bana bakala tekisa bima.
LUK 19:46 Mu kubazimbwala: «Básonika bwabu: "Nzu yama, yakála nzu yimosi ya bisambu." Kaasi benu, lukitudiya saka dya bandwandwa.»
LUK 19:47 Yesu kakala longa bilumbu byosu muna nzu ya Nzambi. Amana bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku yi bapfumu ba bikanda bakala sanda phila ya kumuhondila.
LUK 19:48 Kaasi bázayaku ketibwe bahanga, mukuma batu boosu bákangama yi yandi mu kumuyuka.
LUK 20:1 Mosi kya bilumbu meni byabina, bwosu kakala longa batu mu nzu ya Nzambi yi kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku yi bambuta bátula hakana
LUK 20:2 amana bámuzimbwala: «Tuzimbwala, mu hamu dya nati wubati sadila bwana; nati kena wuna kuheki hamu meni wuna?»
LUK 20:3 Yesu wábavutwala: «Meni phi, yiluyufula kyufu kimosi. Nzimbwalenu:
LUK 20:4 Mbotika ya Yowani, ku zilu yátuka ho kwena batu?»
LUK 20:5 Kaasi bawu báyandika kudiwinina bawu yi bawu bazimbudi: «Yuka twavutula ni "Ya ku zilu", kazimbula bwabu: "Biki lwakonda mukwikidila?"
LUK 20:6 Yuka phi twazimbula: "Ya batu", batu boosu batuhonda ku matadi, mukuma bwa kyedika ni Yowani mbikudi kákala.»
LUK 20:7 Hanga bavutudi: «Tuzayiku keti nati wámutuma.»
LUK 20:8 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Meni phi yilúzimbwlaku keti mu hamu dya nati yisi sadila bwabuna.»
LUK 20:9 Kunima, Yesu wáyandika kuta kingana kyaki kwena batu: «Yakala mosi wákuna kilanga kya vinu, wáluwisakya kwena batu, amana yandi wénda kuma kwa kyana, wázingidila kwakuna.
LUK 20:10 Tangwa ha dyalungila, wátuma musadi mosi kwena batu bana bakala tala kilanga kya vinu, ndangu bawu bahitika ndambu yandi ya vinu. Kaasi batu bana bakala tala kilanga bámubeta musadi wuna amana bámuvutula moku ma khatu.
LUK 20:11 Wátuma hika musadi mukwawu, kaasi bámubeta, bámutukwana, kunima bámukukwasa moku ma khatu.
LUK 20:12 Wátuma hika musadi wa tatu; yana phi bámulweka amana bámukukwasa.
LUK 20:13 Hanga mukwa kilanga kya vinu wuzimbudi: "Bweti yihanga? Yitúma mwana wama wazolwa; ngatu bamúzitisa."
LUK 20:14 Kaasi tangwa bámumona, batu babana bákala futila mu kilanga, bádizonzila: "Tala yandu swana! Tumuhondenu ndangu kuvwa kwakituka kwa betu."
LUK 20:15 Hanga bamulosi ku manima ma kilanga kya vinu amana bámuhonda. «Amana bweti kakwisa bahanga mukwa kilanga kya vinu?
LUK 20:16 Kakwísa, hanga bahondi batu bana bisi futila mu kilanga kya vinu amana kilanga kahánakya kwena batu bahika.» Buna báyuka ndinga zazina, batu bázimbula: «Mambu mama fwaniku masalama!»
LUK 20:17 Kaasi Yesu wábatala, wubazimbwadi: «Biki disongidila dya ndinga yayi básonika»: "Tadi dina bálosa batungi ba nzu dikituki tadi dya mupfundila wa nzu."
LUK 20:18 «Wosu wuna wabwa hana tadi medina, dyamana mutolula; amana wuna dyabwíla tadi dina, dyamúfukumuna.»
LUK 20:19 Muna tangwa medina, balongi ba mitsiku yi Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi, bakala sanda ni bamukwata Yesu, kaasi báyuka bweya bwa batu. Bábakula ni bawu kátila kingana kina.
LUK 20:20 Báyandika kumukengidila. Bátuma batu bana bakala disongila hanga batu basungama. Batu bana bazodi bamuleya Yesu mu kyufu kimosi, ndangu bamulambula kwena bayadi ba kinzunga.
LUK 20:21 Bámuhyula: «Mulongi, tuzayi ni wisi zonza, wisi longa phi yi singu. Wisiku hambula mbunzu, kaasi wisi songila mu kyedika nzila ya Nzambi.
LUK 20:22 Tufwani kufuta phaku ya Khayisala ho loni?»
LUK 20:23 Amana bwosu kábakula mabanza ma bawu ma mbi, wábavutwala:
LUK 20:24 «Tsongilenu fwalanga dimosi. Mbunzu yi khumbu yayi básonika haka, bya nati?» Bawu bávutula: «Bya Khayisala.»
LUK 20:25 Amana Yesu wábazimbwala: «Ho yi bwabuna, hanenu kwena Khayisala bina byena bya yandi amana kwena Nzambi bina byena bya Nzambi.»
LUK 20:26 Balendaku kumukwata keti mu ndinga yandi mosi ku thwala batu. Kaasi mvutu yandi yábayitwakisa amana bádibata.
LUK 20:27 Ndambu ya Basadise bana bisi kwikila ni kweku lufutumuku, hanga bisi muhyula:
LUK 20:28 Bazonzi: «Mulongi, Moyize kátuheka mutsiku wawu básonika: "Yukani yakala mosi, wena yi myaki wandi honi kafwa amana kasisa mukhetu kaasi konda kubuta mwana yi yandi, bulungi kakwela mufwidi wuna ndangu kabuta bana ba thayi wandi."
LUK 20:29 Kinga, kwákala yi baphangi ba bayakala tsambwadi. Watheti wákwela mukhetu, wáfwa konda mwana.
LUK 20:30 Wazodi,
LUK 20:31 kunima, wuna wa tatu wákwela mukhetu; bwásalama phila mosi kwena bawu tsambwadi, báfwa konda kusisa bana.
LUK 20:32 Kunima, mukhetu phi wáfwa.
LUK 20:33 Kilumbu kya lufutumuku, mukhetu wuna wa nati kakála? Mukuma boosu tsambwadi, bámukwela hanga mukhetu wa bawu!»
LUK 20:34 Yesu wábavutwala: «Mu bulunda bwabu, bakhetu yi bayakala bisi dikwela;
LUK 20:35 kaasi bana bázengila ni bafwana kukota mu bulunda buna yi ku lufutumuku lwa bafwa, bawu, badíkwelaku hika.
LUK 20:36 Bafwánaku hika mu kufwa, kikuma bafwanani yi banzyo amana bekina bana ba Nzambi, hanga bana ba lufutumuku.
LUK 20:37 Bafwa bafútumuka, bwosu katekila zimbula Moyize kikuma kya zanga dya mbawu dyákala mu miti, tangwa kámutela Pfumu: "Nzambi wa Bulahami, Nzambi wa Kizaki yi Nzambi wa Yakobi."
LUK 20:38 Kinga keku Nzambi wa batu bafwa, kaasi wa batu bana bena mu luzingu, mukuma boosu bisi zinga kikuma kya yandi.»
LUK 20:39 Ndambu ya balongi ba mitsiku bahika bávutula: «Mulongi, mboti wuzonzi.»
LUK 20:40 Amana bámekaku hika kumuhyula keti kyufu kimosi.
LUK 20:41 Yesu wábazimbwala: «Abweti bafwani kuzimbula ni Kidisitu kenina mwana wa Tavidi?
LUK 20:42 Mukuma yandi meni Tavidi, bwabu kásonika muna mukanda wa mikunga»: "Pfumu kázimbula kwena Pfumu wama: "Sikuka ku kitata kyama;
LUK 20:43 Yikuna yikítwala bambeni baku, kidyatilu kyaku."
LUK 20:44 «Amana Tavidi kisi mutela ni "Pfumu"; amana abweti kafwani kukala hika mwana wandi?»
LUK 20:45 Buna bakala muyuka batu boosu, Yesu wázimbula kwena Balonguki bandi:
LUK 20:46 «Kebenu yi balongi ba mitsiku. Bazodi kukangala yi malophu ma kaleyi. Bisi zola ni batu babahekaka mboti mu mazandu. Bisi zola kuzakala ha bifulu bya theti mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta, bazodi phi bifulu bya lukumu mu mafeti.
LUK 20:47 Bisi botula bima mu nzu za bafwidi, bisi samba malombilu ma kaleyi kikuma kya kudimonikisa. Bawu batámbula pfundusu yina yalúta kitesu.»
LUK 21:1 Yesu wáthuta mesu; wumoni bamvwama bana bakala sya kuvwa kwa bawu mu mukunzu wa nzu ya Nzambi,
LUK 21:2 wumoni phi mufwidi mosi wa phutu, wásyamwa ndisu zodi.
LUK 21:3 Amana wuzimbudi: «Mu kyedika, yiluzimbwadibwa: mufwidi yandu wa phutu kasini kuluta boosu.
LUK 21:4 Mukuma, boosu bana báhani muna kulutuka kwa kuvwa kwa bawu; kaasi yandi, kahani muna kiphutu kyandi, kyosu kina kafwaniki mu kuzingila.»
LUK 21:5 Bwosu bakala zonzila ndambu ya batu kikuma kya nzu ya Nzambi yi buna bátungilaya mu matadi ma kitoku yi makabu mana bánenginaya. Hanga Yesu wuzimbudi:
LUK 21:6 «Bilumbu byakwísa, mu byosu byabi lubati mona, kwasálaku keti tadi ha thandu ya dikwawu, dina bakonda wulumuna.»
LUK 21:7 Amana bámuhyula: «Mulongi, khi tangwa malúta mambu mana? Khi kidimbu kyatékidila mu kusongila mambu meni mana?»
LUK 21:8 Yandi wávutula: «Kebenu, luhunakanaku. Mukuma balawu bakwísa mu khumbu ya meni, bazónza: "Meni yenina Kidisitu!" bathétika hika: "Tangwa dibwesuki!" Kaasi lubalandaku.
LUK 21:9 Tangwa lwayúka: kuzonzila mvita yi mvwalangani, lubangaku; mukuma bulungi mambu mana maluta theti, kaasi tsuka yeku kikuma kya tangwa dyadi.»
LUK 21:10 Yesu kakala zimbula hika: «Kanda dimosi dyanwánisa kanda dikwawu amana kipfumu yi kipfumu kikwawu;
LUK 21:11 kwakála yi kunikana kwa lawu kwa mafu amana mu binzunga bya lawu, nzala yi kiphuphu byakóta. Mambu ma lawu ma bweya makála yi bidimbu bya mbuta byatúka ku zilu.
LUK 21:12 Kaasi ku thwala bina byosu, balúkwata, balúnyokuna, balúlambula mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta, amana balúsya mu boloku; balúnata ku thwala bakyamvu ba tsi yi bapfumu ba binzunga kikuma kya khumbu ya meni.
LUK 21:13 Yakála nzila kikuma kya benu ndangu lwata kimbangi kya khumbu ya meni.
LUK 21:14 Zayenu mboti ni lufwaniku kudiyangisa kikuma kya phila yina lwakwenda sambila.
LUK 21:15 Mukuma meni-meni, yilúheka ndinga mosi yi mudimu wumosi wuna balendaku kunanama kwena bambeni benu keti kubalumuna.
LUK 21:16 Balúlambula kwena batata benu yi bangudi benu, baphangi benu, biwutu byenu yi banduku benu phi; amana balawu babáhondisa ha kati kya benu.
LUK 21:17 Balúmenga kwena batu boosu kikuma kya khumbu ya meni.
LUK 21:18 Kaasi keti lusuki lumosi lwa mutwa wenu lwatótaku.
LUK 21:19 Muna kikwamina kyenu, lwatámbula luzingu.»
LUK 21:20 «Tangwa lwamóna basuta bazingidya Yelusalemi, zayenu ni kuzangana kwandi kubwesuki.
LUK 21:21 Amana bana bakála ku Yuteya, batína mu malondi; bana bakála ha kati dya mbanza, balúbuka; amana bana bakála mu bilanga, bakotaku mu mbanza.
LUK 21:22 Mukuma byakála bilumbu bya ndola, ndangu malungila moosu mana menina ma kusonika.
LUK 21:23 Khi kyadi kwena bakhetu bana bakála ku mavumu, yi bana bakala yemika muna bilumbu meni byabina! Phasi lawu zakála mu tsi, khabu zamónika kwena batu ba tsi meni yana.
LUK 21:24 Babwa ku mbedi ya phoku, babánata hanga bakwa boloku mu tsi zoosu, amana Yelusalemi badyátadya kwena tsi zoosu za baphani, yi kuna byamánisina bilumbu bina bábaheka.»
LUK 21:25 «Bikhwidimba byamónika kuna tangwa yi kuna ngondi yi muna bambweteti. Ha tsi, batu bawókumuka yi tsula ya lawu kikuma kya malokosi ma pfunzi ya yanga dya mbuta yi kimbongila.
LUK 21:26 Batu balawu badímina ku bweya bwa mambu mana mabwíla tsi, mukuma ngolu za mazilu, zaníkana lawu.
LUK 21:27 Amana bamóna Mwana wa mutu kabati kwisa hana thandu ya dituti, yi ngolu za lawu yi khembu.
LUK 21:28 Tangwa mayandiki kusalama mambu mana, vumbukenu, thutenu mutwa kuna zilu, kikuma luhulusu lwenu lubwesukini.»
LUK 21:29 Kunima, Yesu wábatila kingana kyaki: «Talenu mufiki yi miti myosu:
LUK 21:30 Buna misi yandika kulubula khaya, muna kutala kwa khatu, lwisi bakula ni tsungi ya bukheti yibwesuki.
LUK 21:31 Phila mosi yi benu phi, tangwa lwamóna mambu mana kuluta, zayenu ni Kipfumu kya Nzambi kibwesuki.
LUK 21:32 Mu kyedika yiluzimbwadibwa: mbandu ya batu baba yahítaku kedi yi kuna masálamina mana moosu.
LUK 21:33 Zilu yi tsi byátota, kaasi ndinga zama zalendaku tota.»
LUK 21:34 «Dikebisenu! Mbundu yenu yikalaku mu tsumbi ya mikinzi yi kuzela kwa malafu, yi mu kikuma kya luzingu, ndangu kilumbu kina kiluwanaku mu kithulumukina,
LUK 21:35 hanga wanda; mukuma kyakwísa hana thandu ya boosu bana bisi zinga ha tsi yosu.
LUK 21:36 Kalenu batemuna amana lombilakenu kosu tangwa, ndangu lwakala yi ngolu za kutinina mambu moosu mana malúta, lwalenda telama phi ku thwala Mwana wa mutu.»
LUK 21:37 Amana kosu kilumbu, mu mwini, Yesu kakala longa muna nzu ya Nzambi, amana kakala lubuka ndangu kenda nimba, mu phipha, ku mongu wuna bisi tela ni wa ba Olive.
LUK 21:38 Amana muna suka batu boosu bakala kwisa kwena yandi, muna nzu ya Nzambi, ndangu bamuyuka.
LUK 22:1 Mukinzi wa mapha makonda muvimbu, wuna bisi tela ni Phaki, hanga wákuma belabela.
LUK 22:2 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku beka sanda phila ndangu bamuhondisa, mukuma bweya bwa batu bákala bwawu.
LUK 22:3 Hanga Satana wukoti mwena Yutasi wuna bakala tela ni Sikadyoti, wákala phi ha kati dya bawu Kumi yi bodi.
LUK 22:4 Hanga yandi, wendi yukana yi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bapfumu ba batsinzidi ba nzu ya Nzambi mu phila yina káfwana kubalambwala yandi.
LUK 22:5 Básangwala lawu, báyukana phi ni bamuheka mbongu.
LUK 22:6 Yutasi wátambwasa, wáyandika phi kusanda tangwa dya bukheti ndangu kabalambwala yandi, mu kitsweki, konda bazayabwa kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu.
LUK 22:7 Kilumbu kya mukinzi wa mapha makonda muvimbu, wuna bafwana kutambika kimenga kya Phaki, wálungila.
LUK 22:8 Hanga Yesu wutumi Phetelu yi Yowani, wubazimbwadi: «Alwenda tuyidikila Phaki ndangu twenda dyaya.»
LUK 22:9 Bawu bamuzimbwadini: «Ku biki wuzodi thwenda yidikilaya?»
LUK 22:10 Yandi wubavutwadi: «Tangwa lwakóta mu mbanza, mutu mosi lwatúndakana yi kalondu kandi ka mamba; mulandenu yi muna nzu muna kakóta,
LUK 22:11 amana lwazímbula kwena mukwa nzu: "Mulongi kabati kuhyula ni khi mwanza pfwani yidila Phaki, meni yi balonguki bama?"
LUK 22:12 Kalúsongila mwanza wumosi wena wa mbuta kuna zilu, wena wakuyidika kedi. Yi mwamuna lwayídikila mambu.»
LUK 22:13 Hanga bendi, bawani phi mambu bwosu kábazimbwala, bayidika phi mukinzi wa Phaki.
LUK 22:14 Amana tangwa ha dyalungila, Yesu kakala kuna mesa, amana bathumwa bákala kumosi yi yandi.
LUK 22:15 Wubazimbwadi: «Yi mbundu yama yosu thondikini kudya mukinzi wawu wa Phaki kumosi yi benu, ku thwala kunyokuka,
LUK 22:16 mukuma yiluzimbwadibwa ni yidya woku hika tii yi kuna bwalúngila mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 22:17 Hanga wubongi mbungu yimosi, kunima kumuvutwala Nzambi matondu wuzimbudi hika: «Bongenu yayi, kabulenuyoku muna kati dya benu;
LUK 22:18 mukuma, yiluzimbwadibwa: tukila lelu, yinwáku hika malafu ma vinu, tii yikuna kyakwísila Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
LUK 22:19 Kunima, wubongi dipha; kunima kuvutula matondu, wubukunidya amana wubahekidya mu kuzimbula: «Lwena lutu lwama, luna lulambuki kikuma kya benu. Salakenu bwabuna mu kumbambukaka meni.»
LUK 22:20 Wáhanga bwabuna phi kima kya mbungu, kunima dya kudya, wuzimbudi: «Mbungu yayi yena kuyukana kwa pha kwa Nzambi, mu nzila menga ma meni, mana matyakani kikuma kya benu.
LUK 22:21 Kaasi talenu: wuna wuzodi kathekisa haha kena, ha mesa yi meni!
LUK 22:22 Mukuma, Mwana wa mutu kabati kwenda, bwosu buna bwáyilama; kaasi kyadi kwena mutu wuna wamúlambula!»
LUK 22:23 Amana báyandika kudihyula bawu yi bawu keti nati wufwani kasala dyambu dya buna.
LUK 22:24 Hanga balonguki bayandiki kutendana hana kati dya bawu ndangu bazaya keti nati wufwani batela mbuta.
LUK 22:25 Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Bakyamvu ba tsi za baphani bisi bayala mu kingolu-ngolu amana batu bana bena phi yi kiyeka kya kudyatisa tsi bisi zola: batu bahika babatelaka basadi basadi ba mamboti.
LUK 22:26 Kaasi benu, kabunaku. Wuna wena mbuta ha kati dya benu, kakala hanga muleki wa benu, amana wuna wisi yidika ndonga kakala hanga wuna wubati sadila.
LUK 22:27 Amana, nati wena mbuta? Wuna wena ha mesa ho wuna wubati musadila? Ka wuna ku wena ha mesa? Amana meni yena ha kati dya benu hanga wuna wisi sadila!
LUK 22:28 Benu lwena batu bana bakwamini yi meni, mu bimeka byama;
LUK 22:29 amana meni yiluheki Kipfumu kya Nzambi, bwosu káhanakya tata kwena meni,
LUK 22:30 ndangu lwadya, lwanwa phi ha mesa mama muna Kipfumu kyama, ndangu lwazakala mu biti bya kipfumu mu kusambisa bikanda kumi yi byodi bya Kiseledi.»
LUK 22:31 «Simoni, Simoni! Tala: Satana wululombidi nzila mu kuluhenga bwosu bisi hengula losu yi tswala.
LUK 22:32 Kaasi meni ndombidiki kikuma kya ngeyi, ndangu lukwikilu lwaku lumanisaku. Amana ngeyi, tangwa wavútukisa, basyamisa baphangi baku.»
LUK 22:33 Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Pfumu, yena wayilama mu kukwenda kumosi yi ngeyi yi mu boloku, yi ku lufwa.»
LUK 22:34 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Yikuzimbwadibwa, Phetelu, khoku kakókulaku kedi, lelu, ngeyi wathúna mbala tatu ni wunzayiku.»
LUK 22:35 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi hika: «Tangwa yílutuma konda makuta keti waba, keti tsabatu, Kima kyahika kyálukonda?» Bawu bavutudi: «loni, ka kima ku.»
LUK 22:36 Hanga yandi wubazimbwadi: «Kaasi buthwena, wuna wena yi makuta, kanata, wuna wena phi yi waba, kanata, phila mosi yi wuna wukondi mbedi ya phoku, katekisa muzaka wandi ndangu kasumba mbedi ya phoku.
LUK 22:37 Mukuma yiluzimbwadibwa ni bulungi ni buna básonika, bwalungila mwena meni: "bamukotisi mu ndonga ya bandwandwa." Mukuma, mana mathadi meni malungila.»
LUK 22:38 Balonguki bazimbudi: «Ah Pfumu, tala zazi mbedi zodi.» Amana yandi wubavutwadi: «Zazina zifwani.»
LUK 22:39 Bwosu kálubuka, hanga wénda ku mongu wa ba Olive, bwosu buna kayikana. Balonguki bandi bamulandi.
LUK 22:40 Buna katula homa meni hana, wubazimbwadi: «Lombilenu, ndangu lubwaku mu phukumunu.»
LUK 22:41 Kunima, wádihambula kwena bawu kitesu kya thambi makumatatu. Amana bwosu kafukama, wáyandika phi kulombila,
LUK 22:42 mu kuzimbula: «Tata, yuka ni wuzodi, thinisina kyana mbungu yayi. Kaasi ka luzolu ku lwa meni, yambula luzolu lwaku lwahangama.»
LUK 22:43 Hanga wanzyo mosi wátuka ku zilu, wumulubwakidi, ndangu kamuheka kikesa.
LUK 22:44 Yesu wuyuki kiwayi kya lawu, kahanga wusi hika ngolu mu kulombila. Kyusa kyandi kiyandiki kuhoma muna mafu hanga matonzi ma menga.
LUK 22:45 Buna katelama mu lombilu, wávutukisa kuna bakala balonguki, wubawani baleka kikuma kya kyadi kina bákala kyawu.
LUK 22:46 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi: «Abweti lubati leka buna? Tokamenu, lombilenu phi ndangu lubwaku mu phukumunu.»
LUK 22:47 Buna kakala zonza bwana, kibuka kya batu kitudi. Yutasi wuna wákala ha kati dya bawu Kumi yi bodi, yandi wakala natisakya. Wábwesuka kwena Yesu mu kumuyamba.
LUK 22:48 Kaasi Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Yutasi, mu kuyamba wuzodi wamutekisila Mwana wa mutu?»
LUK 22:49 Buna bámona mana mázola kubwa, bana bakala yi yandi bamuhyudini: «Pfumu, tufwani mu kubeta yi mbedi?»
LUK 22:50 Amana, mosi wa bawu, wubeti musadi mosi wa bambuta ba banganga Nzambi amana wámuhuta kutu dya kitata.
LUK 22:51 Kaasi Yesu wuzimbudi: «Yambulenu, bwana bufwani.» Kunima wusimbi kutu dya mutu wuna, wumubeludi phi.
LUK 22:52 Kunima, hanga Yesu wuzimbudi kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi kwena pfumu wa batsinzidi ba nzu ya Nzambi yi bambuta ba dibundu bana bisa mukwata: «Lwisi ndatina mbedi yi miti hanga mbedi yena ndwandwa.
LUK 22:53 Bilumbu byosu khadiki yi benu mu nzu ya Nzambi, amana lwásandaku ni lwakhwata. Kaasi tangwa dyadi dyena dya benu yi ngolu za phipha.»
LUK 22:54 Kunima dya kumukwata, bamunati, bamukotisi phi mu nzu ya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi. Phetelu kakala landa muna kyana.
LUK 22:55 Hanga balemisi mbawu mu kati dya kyanzala amana bazakadi. Phetelu wendi zakala hana kati dya bawu.
LUK 22:56 Musadi mosi wa mukhetu wumumoni kuna kyesesi kya mbawu, wumusimbuludi yi kiswiswiswi, wuzimbudi: «Yandu phi kákadiki yi yandi.»
LUK 22:57 Kaasi Phetelu wutuni, wuzonzi phi: «Mukhetu, yimuzayiku!»
LUK 22:58 Kunima dya koma ka tangwa, mutu wahika wumumoni amana wuzimbudi hika: «Ngeyi phi wena mosi hana kati dya bawu!» Kaasi Phetelu wumuvutwadi: «Loni, ka meni ku!»
LUK 22:59 Ku nima dya tangwa dimosi, mutu mosi wahika wumuzimbwadi yi singu dyosu: «Mu kyedika, mutu yandu phi kákadiki yi yandi mukuma mwisi Ngadidi kenina yandi phi.»
LUK 22:60 Kaasi Phetelu wuvutudi: «Buna wubati zola kuzonza, nzayibwoku meni.» Muna tangwa meni dina kákala zonza, khoku wákokula.
LUK 22:61 Hanga Pfumu wábaluka amana wámutala Phetelu, hana Phetelu wuyubuki ndinga yina kámuzimbwala Pfumu: «Khoku kakókulaku kedi, lelu, ngeyi wathúna mbala tatu.»
LUK 22:62 Hanga Phetelu wálubuka, amana wádihonda kudila.
LUK 22:63 Bayakala bana bakala mutadikila Yesu, bakala museya yi kumubetaka.
LUK 22:64 Bakala mufidinga mbunzu, mu kumuhyula: «Bikuleti, nati wukubeti?»
LUK 22:65 Amana bákala mutukwana yi kumutangaka mambu ma mbi ma mutindu yi mutindu.
LUK 22:66 Buna kwakhyela kuma, bambuta ba Bayuta, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku bákutakana. Bamunatisi Yesu ku thwala kimvuka kya mbuta kya Bayuta
LUK 22:67 amana bazimbudi: «Yukani ngeyi wena Masiya, tuzimbwalabwa.» Yandi wubavutwadi: «Yukani yiluzimbwalabwa, lwakúmbwalabwoku.
LUK 22:68 Amana yukani yiluhyula kyufu, lwamvútwalaku.
LUK 22:69 Kaasi tuka buthwena, Mwana wa mutu kasíkuka kuna kitata dya ngolu za Nzambi wa Phungu.»
LUK 22:70 Boosu bazimbudi: «Kisongidila, ngeyi Mwana wa Nzambi wena?» Yandi wubavutwadi: «Benu-benu luzimbudibwa ni yeninabwa.»
LUK 22:71 Hanga bawu bazimbudi: «Ni mupfunu wa bimbangi hika thwena wawu betu? Tumuyuki betu-betu muna munwa wandi.»
LUK 23:1 Bátelama boosu ha kimosi amana bámunata ku thwala Philatu.
LUK 23:2 Báyandika kumufunda mu kuzimbula: «Tumuwani mutu yandu, kabati hukumuna batu ba betu; kabati bazimbwala ni bafutaku phaku kwena pfumu wa mbuta Khayisala, wudikitudi yandi meni Masiya, thotila.»
LUK 23:3 Philatu wumuyufudi: «Ngeyi, pfumu wa Bayuta wenina?» Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Ngeyi meni wuzimbudibwa.»
LUK 23:4 Hanga Philatu wuzimbudi kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi milumba-lumba mya batu: «Mboniku kima kya muzengila ndola mutu yandu.»
LUK 23:5 Kaasi bawu balaphikisi ndinga, bazimbudi phi: «Khabu kabati heka batu mu kulonga mu Yuteya dyosu, tuka ku Ngadidi, kuna káyandikila, yi kwaku.»
LUK 23:6 Tangwa káyuka Philatu mambu mana, wuhyudi: «Mutu yandu, mwisi Ngadidi kenina?»
LUK 23:7 Buna káyuka ni Yesu ku kinzunga kina kakala yala Eloti kátuka, kahanga wumuhitiki kwena yandi, mukuma ku Yelusalemi kákala muna bilumbu meni bina.
LUK 23:8 Amana Eloti buna kámona Yesu hanga kyesi kimukwati lawu. Kikuma, kakala sanda ni kamumona tuka thama; mukuma kázola kamumona kikuma kya mambu mana kakala yuka kuzonzila kikuma kya yandi, amana kákala yi kivuvu kya kumumona kusala ndambu ya biphadi.
LUK 23:9 Kahanga wumuhyudi byufu bya lawu kaasi Yesu kámuvutwalaku keti kima.
LUK 23:10 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku hana bákala amana bakala mufunda ngolu.
LUK 23:11 Hanga Eloti yi batsinzidi bandi, wuyandiki kumulewula. Amana kunima kumuseya yi kumuvwatisa muledi wumosi wa kitoku, hanga wumuhitiki hika kwena Philatu.
LUK 23:12 Muna kilumbu meni kina, Eloti yi Philatu bakítuka banduku, bawu batekila kala bambeni.
LUK 23:13 Philatu wákhokisa bambuta ba banganga Nzambi, bathwadisi yi batu bahika,
LUK 23:14 hanga wubazimbwadi: «Benu lwisi ndatina mutu yandu, mu kuzonza ni batu kabati hukumuna. Kinga meni yimuhyudi ku thwala benu boosu kaasi mboniku kima mwena yandi kifwani muzengila ndola, ka kikuma ku muna mamana lubati mufundila.
LUK 23:15 Eloti phi, lo kwandi, mukuma wutulambwadi yandi hika. Kahangiku kima kifwani bamuhondila.
LUK 23:16 Yimusula, kunima dya kumubetisa fimbu.»
LUK 23:17 [Kosu mukinzi wa Phaki, Philatu kafwana kubalubwala mutu mosi mu boloku.]
LUK 23:18 Kaasi báyandika kukalunga boosu: «Muhonda mutu yandu, tulubwala Balabasi!»
LUK 23:19 Balabasi, bámusila mu boloku kikuma kya mvwalangani yina bábusila bisi Loma, yina yáluta mu mbanza yi buna káhonda mutu.
LUK 23:20 Hanga Philatu wázonza hika mbala yikwawu, mukuma kázola kalubula Yesu.
LUK 23:21 Kaasi bawu bakala kalunga: «Mukhoka ha kitakani! Mukhoka ha kitakani!»
LUK 23:22 Philatu wubazimbwadi mu mbala ya tatu: «Khi mbi kasadi mutu yandu? Mboniku kima mwena yandi kilungi kumunatina lufwa. Yimusula, ku nima dya kumubetisa fimbu.»
LUK 23:23 Kaasi bakalungi hika ngolu, mu kulomba ni Yesu kakhokama ha kitakani. Hanga malokosi ma bawu mábanungisa.
LUK 23:24 Philatu wubongi lukanu lwa kubasadila bwosu buna bakala lomba.
LUK 23:25 Wuyambwadidi wuna bákwata mu boloku kikuma kya mvwalangani yi buna káhonda mutu, wuna bakala lomba. Wubalambwadi Yesu ndangu bamuhanga buna bázola.
LUK 23:26 Bwosu bakala munata Yesu, bakwati mutu mosi zina dyandi Simoni, mwisi Sileni, wátuka ku bilanga. Hanga bamukwati ndangu kamunatisa Yesu kitakani kuna manima.
LUK 23:27 Mulumba-lumba wa batu wakala mulanda yi bakhetu mu bidilu yi miyananu mya lawu kikuma kya yandi.
LUK 23:28 Hanga Yesu wubaluki kwena bakhetu wubazimbwadi: «Bakhetu ba ku Yelusalemi, ludilaku kikuma kya meni! Kaasi dilenu kikuma kya benu-benu yi kikuma kya bana benu!
LUK 23:29 Mukuma bilumbu byakwísa, bina bazímbula: "Kyesi kwena bakhobu, kyesi kwena makundu mana mábutaku yi mayeni mana máyemikaku!"
LUK 23:30 Hanga batu báyandika kuzimbula kwena mongu mya mbuta: "Tubwilenu" yi kwena mina mya khunda: "Tufidingenu!"
LUK 23:31 Mukuma, yukani bahanga bwabu kwena miti wa tsi amana miti waloka abweti bahángawa?»
LUK 23:32 Bakala nata muna tangwa medina bayakala bodi bahika bákala bandwandwa ndangu babahonda ha kimosi yi yandi.
LUK 23:33 Buna bátula homa hana bisi tela: «Kibelengenzi kya mutwa», bamukhoki Yesu ha kitakani; phila mosi yi bandwandwa bana, mosi ku koku dya kitata, mukwawu, ku koku dya kimama.
LUK 23:34 [Yesu kakala zimbula: «Tata, balolula mukuma bazayimoku mana babati sala.»] Basanzani miledi myandi mu kubetilamya phi zeki.
LUK 23:35 Batu batelamiki hakana yi kutalaka mambu buna makala luta. Bapfumu ba Bayuta báyandika kumuseya, mu kuzimbula: «Batu bahika kakala hulula, kadihulula phi yandi meni yuka yandi kena Masiya wa Nzambi, wuna kásola!»
LUK 23:36 Basuta phi bakala museya; babwesuki, bamunwisi phi vinu dya ngani,
LUK 23:37 yi kuzimbulaka: «Yukani ngeyi pfumu wa Bayuta wena, dihulula ngeyi meni!»
LUK 23:38 Ha thandu ya mutwa wandi hákala yi bisona byabi: «Yandu kenina pfumu wa Bayuta.»
LUK 23:39 Mosi wa bandwandwa bana bákala ha kitakani, hanga wumutukwani mu kuzimbula: «Ka ngeyi ku Masiya? Dihulula ngeyi meni, amana watuhulula betu!»
LUK 23:40 Kaasi mukwawu, wumusongisi, mu kuzimbula: «Weku yi bweya bwa Nzambi? Ngeyi wubongi ndola mosi yi yandi?
LUK 23:41 Betu, ndola yayi yifwanani yi mbi yina twasadi kaasi yandu kasadiku kima kya mbi.»
LUK 23:42 Amana kakala zimbula: «Yesu, ngyubuka bawu tangwa wakwísa mu Kipfumu kyaku.»
LUK 23:43 Yesu wumuvutwadi: «Yikuzimbwadibwa, mu kyedika: lelu dyadi, wakála yi meni muna Phaladisu.»
LUK 23:44 Amana tangwa ha kátula ha kisosi, kuma kwabwa phipha mu mulambu wosu yi kuna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika.
LUK 23:45 Tangwa wátota. Muledi wa kikumbu kya nzu ya Nzambi wáyatuka ha kati.
LUK 23:46 Yesu wákalunga: «Tata, mvutudi moya wama mu moku maku.» Kunima kuzonza bwabuna, wutabudi.
LUK 23:47 Mu kumona mana maluta, hanga satudiyoni wázatula Nzambi mu kuzimbula: «Mu kyedika, mutu yandu kákadiki mutu wasungama!»
LUK 23:48 Amana milumba-lumba mya batu bakala hana, bisa tala mambu buna máhitila, ku nima kumona mana máhita, bávutuka yi kudibundaka thulu kikuma kya kiwayi.
LUK 23:49 Boosu bana bámuzaya, yi bakhetu bana bisa musindikila tuka ku Ngadidi, bátelama muna kyana ndangu bamona mambu buna makala luta.
LUK 23:50 Hákala yi mutu mosi wa kimvuka kya bukheti, khumbu yandi Yozefu, mutu wa mboti yi wasungama.
LUK 23:51 Yandi kátambwasalwoku lukanu luna bátambula mu kimvuka yi bakwawu, kákala mwisi Adimate mbanza ya Bayuta, amana kakala hingila Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
LUK 23:52 Kahanga wenda kwena Philatu amana wálomba lutu lwa Yesu.
LUK 23:53 Wutuludilwa ha kitakani, wuvungilwa ha muledi, wusikudilwa phi mu mazyamu ma kitadi mana bakonda zika kedi mutu.
LUK 23:54 Kyákala kilumbu kya kuyilama, amana sabata dyázola kuyandika.
LUK 23:55 Bakhetu bana meni bámusindikila tuka ku Ngadidi, bakala landila, bámona mazyamu yi phila yina básikula lutu lwa Yesu.
LUK 23:56 Amana kunima, bávutuka mu kuyidika masi yi mananasi kikuma kya mvumbi. Amana mu kilumbu kya Sabata, bálembwa bwosu buna wakala lomba mutsiku.
LUK 24:1 Kilumbu kya theti kya phosa, bakhetu bénda ku mazyamu muna suka-suka, mu kunata mananasi mana báyidika.
LUK 24:2 Bawani ditadi dyakubundumuna ku thwala mazyamu;
LUK 24:3 bákota, kaasi báwanalwoku lutu lwa Pfumu Yesu.
LUK 24:4 Bwosu bákala mu kitswi kikuma kya mambu meni mana; batu bodi bámonika hakana, bavwatiki miledi myákala kédyamina.
LUK 24:5 Bwosu bákala yi bweya, bázenzika mbunzu muna mafu; kaasi batu bana babazimbwadi: «Kikuma kya biki lwisi sosila mutu wena mu luzingu mu kati dya bafwa?
LUK 24:6 Keku haka, kaasi wufutumuki. Banzenu buna kázimbula kwena benu ha kákala hika ku Ngadidi:
LUK 24:7 Bulungi, Mwana wa mutu bamulambula kwena basumuki amana kakhokama ha kitakani, amana kafútumuka mu kilumbu kya tatu.»
LUK 24:8 Amana báyubuka ndinga meni zina.
LUK 24:9 Bakhetu bákatuka ku mazyamu, kikuma kya kuyadingisa mana mosu kwena Bawu kumi yi mosi yi kwena bakwawu.
LUK 24:10 Hákala yi Madiya mwisi Makatala yi Zyani yi Madiya ngudi wa Zyaki. Bakhetu bahika phi bákala hakana, bazimbudibwa kwena bathumwa.
LUK 24:11 Kaasi ndinga zina bámonaza hanga zina za bilawu bákwikilaku kwena bakhetu.
LUK 24:12 Kaasi Phetelu wátelama, wénda thinu ku mazyamu; amana buna kazenzama, wumoni lwesi bitemba bya miledi bya khatu. Amana wávutuka ku nzu yandi, wuyituki lawu kikuma kya mambu mana maluta.
LUK 24:13 Kinga, muna kilumbu mekyana, boodi hana kati dya balonguki, bakala kwenda ku hata dimosi khumbu ya dyawu: Emawusu; tuka Yelusalemi yi kuna, bafwana kusala tangwa zodi.
LUK 24:14 Muna nzila, bekazonzila mambu mana moosu buna málutila.
LUK 24:15 Tangwa bakala zonza yi kuyambilaka bwabuna, yameni Yesu wábawana, wénda nzila mosi yi bawu.
LUK 24:16 Kaasi mesu ma bawu máfwanaku mu kumusengumuna.
LUK 24:17 Hanga wubahyudi: «Biki lubati zonzila mu nzila?» Hanga batelami yi kyadi kyosu.
LUK 24:18 Mosi hana kati dya bawu, khumbu yandi Kolofasi, wumuvutwadi: «Ngeyi lwesi wunangi bilumbu ku Yelusalemi, wukondi zaya mambu mana málutiki mu bilumbu byabi?»
LUK 24:19 Yandi wáhyula: «Khi dyambu?» Hanga bamuvutwadini: «Mambu mana matadidi Yesu mwisi Nazaleti, wuna wakadi mbikudi wa ngolu mu bisalu yi ndinga zandi ku mesu ma Nzambi yi ku mesu ma batu boosu.
LUK 24:20 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bapfumu betu bamulambudi ndangu kafwa amana bamukhoki ha kitakani.
LUK 24:21 Twakadi yi kivuvu ni yandi wálubula mu kihika Kiseledi. Kaasi bilumbu byekina bitatu, tuka buna mabwidiki mambu mana.
LUK 24:22 Mu kyedika, bakhetu bahika hana kati dya betu batuyitwakisi. Lelu, bendiki muna suka ku mazyamu
LUK 24:23 kaasi bwosu bamoniyoku mvumbi yandi, bisi zimbula ni banzyo babalubwakidi, amana babaheki tsikiningi ni mu luzingu kenina.
LUK 24:24 Batu bahika ha kati dya betu bendiki ku mazyamu, bamoni mambu bwosu buna bazimbudiki bakhetu, kaasi yandi bamumonikiku.»
LUK 24:25 Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Batu bakonda ngangu, mbundu zenu zisiku lenga kwikila mambu mana básamuna bambikudi!
LUK 24:26 Bwáfwanaku ni Masiya kanyokuka bwabuna ku thwala kukota mu khembu yandi?»
LUK 24:27 Wábatendwala mambu moosu mana mamutadidi muna masonuku moosu, tuka ku mikanda mya Moyize yi kuna mikanda mya bambikudi boosu.
LUK 24:28 Buna bátula ku hata dina bakala kwenda, Yesu wuhangi hanga mutu wuzodi kuluta.
LUK 24:29 Kaasi bawu bamubokwadidi mu kuzimbula: «Zakala yi betu; kuma kuyidini, phipa yekina bwa.» Hanga yandi wendi zakala yi bawu muna nzu yina bákota.
LUK 24:30 Yesu wázakala kuna mesa ha kimosi yi bawu; wátambula dipha, wusambudidya; kunima, wábukunadya amana wábahekadya.
LUK 24:31 Hanga mesu ma bawu makanguki, bawu bamutunguludi kaasi yandi wátota hana kati dya bawu.
LUK 24:32 Amana báyandika kudizimbwala bawu yi bawu: «Abweti yikondi tuphumwakina mbundu hanga mbawu, tangwa kakatuzonzisaka mu nzila yi kututendwala masonuku?»
LUK 24:33 Hanga bátelama muna tangwa meni dina, bávutuka phi ku Yelusalemi. Bawani bawu kumi yi mosi mu kimvuka yi banduku ba bawu,
LUK 24:34 beka zimbula: «Mukyedika Pfumu wufutumuki! Mukuma kadimonikisi kwena Simoni!»
LUK 24:35 Hanga balonguki bana bawu bodi babatendwadi mana mábalutila mu nzila mu tangwa bakala kwenda yi buna kadisengumuna Yesu kwena bawu mu tangwa dya kubukuna dipha.
LUK 24:36 Buna bakala zimbula bwabuna, hanga yandi meni Yesu wubalubwakidi, wátelama hana kati dya bawu amana wubazimbwadi: «Ngemba yakala yi benu!»
LUK 24:37 Bweya bubakwati balonguki, bayandiki phi kubanga lawu, kikuma bámona hanga kiphedikisa.
LUK 24:38 Kaasi yandi wubazimbwadi: «Bweya bwa biki lwena bwawu? Biki lubati findila phaka muna mbundu zenu?
LUK 24:39 Talenu moku yi malu mama: mu kyedika, meni yandu; babatenu lutu lwama, talenu phi; kiphedikisa kisiku kala yi musuni keti mufufwa; bwosu lubati mona yenina byawu.»
LUK 24:40 Buna kázimbula bwabuna, hanga wubasongidi moku mandi yi malu mandi.
LUK 24:41 Bwosu kyábalutila kyesi, bafwanaku kedi kukwikila, mu kuyituka bákala. Hanga Yesu wubazimbwadi hika: «Kima kya kudya lwena kyawu haka?»
LUK 24:42 Bámuheka kitini kya tsema wa kukadinga.
LUK 24:43 Wutambudikya amana wudikya phi muna mesu ma bawu.
LUK 24:44 Hanga wubazimbwadi hika: «Tagwa yikala theti ha kimosi yi benu, yikala luzimbwala ni mana básonika kikuma kya meni, mu mitsiku mya Moyize, mu mikanda mya bambikudi yi mu mikunga, mafwana masalama.»
LUK 24:45 Hanga yandi wubakangudi mabanza ndangu babakisa masonuku,
LUK 24:46 amana wubazimwadi: «Básonika bwabu ni Masiya kanyókuka, amana kafútumuka ku tsi ya bafwa mu kilumbu kya tatu,
LUK 24:47 bufwani bayandikila ku Yelusalemi, mu kulonga malongi mu khumbu ya yandi; kusamuna kwena batu ba tsi ni basoba bikalulu ndangu babonga ndoluka ya masumu.
LUK 24:48 Benu lwenina bambangi ba mambu mana.
LUK 24:49 Amana meni phitiki kwena benu, kina kásila Tata wama. Benu, zakalenu mu mbanza tii yikuna lwavwátila ngolu za ku zilu.»
LUK 24:50 Amana, Yesu wábalubula mu mbanza, wábanata tii yi kuna bela-bela yi hata dya Betaniya, Hanga wátombula moku ku zilu, wubasambudi.
LUK 24:51 Buna kakala basambula, wudihambudi yi bawu amana bámutombula ku zilu.
LUK 24:52 Bawu kunima dya kufukama ku thwala yandi, bávutuka phi ku Yelusalemi yi kyesi kya lawu.
LUK 24:53 Bilumbu byosu bakala kutakana mu nzu ya Nzambi yi kukumisaka Nzambi.
JOH 1:1 Muna luyandiku, Ndinga wádikadila amana Ndinga kákala hakimosi yi Nzambi; amana Ndinga kákala Nzambi.
JOH 1:2 Yandi kákala muna luyandiku hakimosi yi Nzambi.
JOH 1:3 Byosu, mwena yandi byáhangamina amana kweku kima kyáhangama konda yandi; muna byabina byisi monika;
JOH 1:4 mwena yandi mwákala luzingu. Amana luzingu lwákala mwini wa batu.
JOH 1:5 Mwini wukenzudini muna phipha, kaasi phipha yálendaku mu kukwatawa.
JOH 1:6 Hátula mutu mosi, bátuma kwena Nzambi, mu khumbu ya Yowani.
JOH 1:7 Kisa hanga mbangi, mu kuta kimbangi kitadidini mwini. Ndangu, mwena Yowani, boosu bakwikila.
JOH 1:8 Ka yandi ku wákala mwini, kaasi kyisa ta kimbangi kwena mwini.
JOH 1:9 Ndinga yákala mwini wakyedika, wuna wisi temuna mutu wosu, Ndinga yísa muna tsi.
JOH 1:10 Ndinga yákala muna tsi. Amana tsi yáhangama mwena yawu, kaasi tsi yámubakulaku.
JOH 1:11 Yísa kwena biwutu byandi, kaasi biwutu byandi bámutambwasaku.
JOH 1:12 Kaasi kwena boosu babana bámutambwasa, wábaheka hamu dya kukituka bana ba Nzambi; kwena babana bisi kwikila muna khumbu yandi.
JOH 1:13 Babana bábutukaku mu menga, keti mu luzolu lwa lutu, keti mu luzolu lwa mutu, kaasi mwena Nzambi.
JOH 1:14 Ndinga yákituka mutu, amana yisa zingila hana kati dya betu, amana betu twámona khembu yandi, khembu ya Mwana wa yakala yandi mosi wuna wábutukila mwena Tata; Ndinga yábasa yi khenda yi kyedika.
JOH 1:15 Yowani wámutila kimbangi; kákalunga mu kuzimbula: «Kikuma kya yandi yízimbwala: "Wuna wubati kwisa ku manima ma meni, kenina mupfunu wa lawu kuluta meni, mukuma, wádikadila kedi ku thwala ya meni."»
JOH 1:16 Kikuma, muna kuvula kwa kuvwa kwandi twátambwala, betu boosu, khenda hana thandu ya khenda.
JOH 1:17 Mukuma mitsiku myáhanama mwena Moyize; kaasi khenda yi kyedika byísila mwena Yesu Kidisitu.
JOH 1:18 Heku mutu wámona kedi Nzambi; kaasi Mwana yandi mosi wenina Nzambi, yandi wisi nangina bela-bela yi Tata, yandi wámuzayikisa Tata.
JOH 1:19 Tala kimbangi kya Yowani, tangwa bámutumina banganga Nzambi yi balefi kwena Bayuta tuka ku Yelusalemi, mu kumuhyula: «Ngeyi nani wenina?»
JOH 1:20 Wátambwasabwa, kátunabwoku, wátambwasa mu kuzimbula: «Meni yeku Kidisitu.»
JOH 1:21 Bámuhyula: «Amana nani wenina? Ngeyi wenina Diya?» Yowani wábavutwala: «Yeku phi yandi.» Bámuhyula: «Mbikudi wenina?» Wuzimbudini: «Loni»,
JOH 1:22 Hanga bamuzimbwadini: «Amana nati wenina? Ndangu twahana mvutu mosi kwena babana bátutuma! Biki wuzimbudini kikuma kya ngeyi meni?»
JOH 1:23 Yowani wávutula: «Meni yenina "wuna wubati kalunga muna nganga: sungikenu nzila kikuma kya Pfumu!"» – Bwabuna kázimbula mbikudi Yesaya. –
JOH 1:24 Batu babana bátuma kwena bafwadisi mu kwenda mumona Yowani;
JOH 1:25 bamuhyudini: «Yuka ni weku Masiya, weku phi Diya, keti mbikudi, amana kikuma kya biki wubati botikila?»
JOH 1:26 Yowani wubavutwadini: «Meni, mbati lubotika mu mamba; hana kati dya benu henina yi mosi wuna luzayiku benu.
JOH 1:27 Kabati kwisa hana manima ma meni. Ndungiku mu kukutumuna misinga mya tsabatu zandi.»
JOH 1:28 Mamana moosu makala hitila ku Betaniya, kuna sambwa dikwawu dya Yolutani, kuna kakala botikila Yowani.
JOH 1:29 Kilumbu kyálanda, Yowani wámona Yesu kukwisa kwena yandi, amana wuzimbudini: «Tala Mwana wa mukoku wa Nzambi wuna wisi katula masumu ma tsi.
JOH 1:30 Kikuma kya yandi yízonzila tangwa yízimbula: "Mutu mosi wubati kwisa ku manima ma meni, kaasi kenina mupfunu kuluta meni, mukuma kakala dizingila kedi ku thwala ya meni."
JOH 1:31 Yikalaku zaya keti nati káfwana kukala, kaasi ho yisa botika mu mamba ndangu yimuzayikisa kwena kanda dya Kiseledi.»
JOH 1:32 Amana Yowani wáta kimbangi kyaki: «Mboni Kitembu kya Nzambi kukulunga tukila ku zilu hanga yembi amana wuzakadini hana thandu ya yandi.
JOH 1:33 Meni-meni yízayaku keti nati kákala, kaasi Nzambi, wuna wáthuma mu kubotika mu mamba, kánzimbwala: "Wamóna Kitembu kukulunga yi kuzakala hana thandu ya mutu mosi; yandi wuna wabótika mu Kitembu Kyatoma."
JOH 1:34 Bwabuna mbonini meni-meni amana thini kimbangi ni mutu yandu kenina Mwana wa Nzambi.»
JOH 1:35 Kilumbu kyálanda, Yowani hana kákala hika, yi boodi ba balonguki bandi.
JOH 1:36 Buna kámona Yesu wakala hita, wuzimbudini: «Tala Mwana wa mukoku wa Nzambi!»
JOH 1:37 Balonguki boodi babana báyuka ndinga zina, hanga balandi Yesu.
JOH 1:38 Yesu wábaluka, wumoni ni bakala mulanda amana wubahyudini: «Biki lubati sanda?» Bawu bamuvutwadini: «Kubiki wisi zingila, Labuni?» -Disongidila: «Mulongi». -
JOH 1:39 Yandi wubazimbwadini: «Alwisa amana lwamóna.» Bénda amana bámona kuna kakala zingila; bánanga kilumbu mekina kwakuna, hakimosi yi yandi. Dyákala hanga tangwa dya kumi yi sambanu dya masikidika.
JOH 1:40 Andele, phangi wa yakala wa Simoni Phetelu, kákala mosi wa bodi babana báyuka ndinga za Yowani amana bálanda Yesu.
JOH 1:41 Mutu watheti katekila tundakana kákala phangi wandi Simoni; amana wumuzimbwadini: «Tumumoni Masiya.» -Disongidila «Kidisitu» -
JOH 1:42 Wámunata Simoni yi kuna kákala Yesu. Yesu wámutala amana wuzimbudini: «Ngeyi wenina Simoni, mwana wa Yowani; bakutediki Sefwasi.» -Disongidila «Tadi». -
JOH 1:43 Kilumbu kyálanda, Yesu wázola ni kenda ku Ngadidi. Amana wátundakana Fidiphu, hanga wumuzimbwadini: «Ndanda!»
JOH 1:44 Fidiphu kákala mwisi Betisayita, mbanza ya Andele yi Phetelu.
JOH 1:45 Fidiphu wátundakana Natanayedi amana wumuzimbwadini: «Tumumoni wuna bázonzila kwena Moyize yi muna Mitsiku yi bambikudi. Kenina Yesu mwisi Nazaleti, mwana wa Yozefu.»
JOH 1:46 Natanayedi wámuzimbwala: «Kuna Nazaleti, kufwani kwalubuka kima kya bukheti?» Fidiphu wumuzimbwadini: «Awisa amana wamóna»
JOH 1:47 Yesu wámona Natanayedi mu kukwisa kwena yandi, hanga wumuzimbwadini kikuma kya yandi: «Tala mwisi Kiseledi wa kyedika; muna mwa yandi mweku bukamvi.»
JOH 1:48 Natanayedi wumuzimbwadini: «Ku biki wunzayidini?» Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Yikumoniki kedi tangwa wukadikini hana sina dya mufiki, hana Fidiphu khaku kakutela.»
JOH 1:49 Natanayedi wávutwakila: «Mulongi, ngeyi wenina Mwana wa Nzambi, ngeyi wenina kyamvu wa Kiseledi!»
JOH 1:50 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Wukhwikidini kikuma kya buna yikuzimbwadini ni yikumoniki muna sina dya mufiki? Wamóna hika mambu ma mbuta-mbuta kuluta mama.»
JOH 1:51 Hanga wumuzimbwadini: «Kyedika, kyedika yibatibwa luzimbwala: lwamóna zilu dyakanguka amana banzyo ba Nzambi kutombuka yi kukulunga hana thandu ya Mwana wa mutu!»
JOH 2:1 Muna kilumbu kya tatu, mukinzi wa longu wákala kuna Kana, muna kinzunga kya Ngadidi. Ngudi wa Yesu hana kákala,
JOH 2:2 Yesu phi bámutedisa kuna longu meni luna hakimosi yi balonguki bandi.
JOH 2:3 Amana bwosu dyákonda vinu, muna tangwa dimosi, hanga ngudi wa Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Beku hika yi vinu.»
JOH 2:4 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Ngudi, biki ngeyi yi meni mu mambu mama? Tangwa dyama khaniku kedi dilungila.»
JOH 2:5 Ngudi wandi wuzimbudini kwena basadi: «Hangenu kyosu kina kalúzimbwala.»
JOH 2:6 Hákala hahana yi mindungu sambanu mya tuma myákala kikuma kya kudisemisa kwa Bayuta. Kosu mundungu yakala kota kitesu kya milangi khama.
JOH 2:7 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Basisenu mindungu myami yi mamba.» Babasisimya yi hana thandu.
JOH 2:8 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Buthwena, tékunenu amana natenumoku kwena muyidiki wa mukinzi.» Amana bawu bámunatinama.
JOH 2:9 Tangwa káyedika, muyidiki wa mukinzi, mamba mákituka vinu, kázayaku kubiki dyátuka vinu meni dina. Kaasi basadi babana bálongulula mamba bázayabwa. Muyidiki wa mukinzi wámutela yakala wuna wákwela
JOH 2:10 amana wumuzimbwadini: «Mutu wosu kisi tekila hana vinu dya bukheti, yuka batu bazedini, wuhani nana mulala. Ngeyi wuswekiki vinu dya bukheti yi buthwena bwabu!»
JOH 2:11 Luna lwákala luyandiku lwa bidimbu bya biphadi bya Yesu. Kásadilakya kuna mbanza ya Kana dya Ngadidi; wásongila khembu yandi, amana balonguki bandi bákwikila mwena yandi.
JOH 2:12 Kunima dya bwabuna, wákulunga ku mbanza ya Kafadinawumi yi ngudi wandi yi baphangi bandi yi balonguki bandi. Amana bilumbu bya khunda lwesi bánangakwa.
JOH 2:13 Mukinzi wa Phaki ya Bayuta wábwesuka amana Yesu wátombuka ku Yelusalemi.
JOH 2:14 Kuna nzu ya Nzambi, káwana bateki ba bangombi, ba mikoku yi ba mayembi; yi bakwa tsyenzya bákala basikuka.
JOH 2:15 Kahanga wuyidiki fimbu dya misinga amana wábakukwasa boosu kuna phenza ya kyanzala kya nzu ya Nzambi, yi mikoku yi bangombi; wámwanga makuta ma bakwa tsyenza, wázanga phi mesa ma bawu;
JOH 2:16 hanga wuzimbudini kwena babana bakala tekisa mayembi: «Katulenu byabina byosu haka! Lukitulaku Nzu ya Tata wama hanga nzu yimosi ya kikhita!»
JOH 2:17 Balonguki bandi báyubuka ni básonika bwabu: «Kitya kya lawu kina yenina kyawu kikuma kya Nzu yaku, kyanzínisa.»
JOH 2:18 Bayuta bámuzimbwala: «Khi kidimbu wutusongidini mu kuhanga bwabuna?»
JOH 2:19 Yesu wábavutwala: «Mwangenu nzu ya Nzambi yayi, amana mu bilumbu bitatu yitúngululaya.»
JOH 2:20 Bayuta bamuzimbwadini: «Kwáfwana mvula makumaya yi sambanu mu kutunga nzu ya Nzambi yayi, amana ngeyi, mu bilumbu bitatu, watúngululaya?»
JOH 2:21 Kaasi nzu ya Nzambi yina kakala zonzila yandi yákala lutu lwandi.
JOH 2:22 Amana tangwa káfutumuka ku bafwa, balonguki bandi báyubuka ni wázimbulabwa bwabuna; amana bákwikila mu Masonuku yi ndinga yina kázimbula Yesu.
JOH 2:23 Buna kákala Yesu ku Yelusalemi, kuna mukinzi wa Phaki, balawu bákwikila mu khumbu yandi, mu kumona bidimbu bya biphadi bina kakala hanga.
JOH 2:24 Kaasi Yesu, yandi, kákwikilaku mwena bawu, kikuma wábazaya boosu.
JOH 2:25 Kákalaku phi yi mupfunu ni bamutila kimbangi kya mutu, mukuma yandi meni wázaya mana mákala mwena mutu.
JOH 3:1 Mutu mosi wákala muna mukanzu wa Bafwadisi khumbu yandi Nikundimu, kákala phi mosi hana kati dya bapfumu ba Bayuta.
JOH 3:2 Wisa muwana Yesu muna phipha yimosi, amana wumuzimbwadini: «Mulongi, tuzayi ni Nzambi wákutuma ndangu wisa tulonga; mukuma ka mutu ku wufwani mu kuhanga bidimbu bya biphadi bwosu wisibya hanga ngeyi, yuka ni Nzambi keku hakimosi yi yandi.»
JOH 3:3 Yesu wámuvutwala: «Mu kyedika, yikuzimbwadibwa: ka mutu ku walenda mona Kipfumu kya Nzambi yuka ni kabutukiku lubutuku lwa pha.»
JOH 3:4 Nikundimu wámuhyula: «Khi phila, mutu yandu wukodi kedi kafwani mu kubutuka hika mbala yikwawu? Wufwani hika ni kavutuka mu kundu dya ngudi wandi, amana kabutuka hika mbala ya zodi?»
JOH 3:5 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Kyedika, kyedika, yikuzimbwadibwa: yuka ni mutu kabutukiku mu mamba yi mu Kitembu, kafwaniku mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
JOH 3:6 Kina kibutukidini mu kimutu, kyenina kya kimutu; amana kina kibutukidini mu kitembu kyenina Kitembu.
JOH 3:7 Yitukaku kikuma kya buna yikuzimbwadini: "Bulungi kwena benu ni lwabutuka mu mbala yikwawu."
JOH 3:8 Muphephi wisi fula kuna wuzodini; wisiwa yuka, kaasi wazáyaku kuna wisi tuka yi kuna wisi kwenda. Phila mosi bwenina yi wuna wubutukini mu Kitembu.»
JOH 3:9 Nikundimu wumuhyudini: «Abweti bwalenda salamina bwabuna?»
JOH 3:10 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Ngeyi wenina mulongi mu Kiseledi, amana wuzayibwoku bwabuna?
