JOH 16:24 Yi bwa buthwena bwabu, khaku kedi lumulomba kima mu khumbu ya meni. Lombenu amana lwatámbula, ndangu kyesi kyenu kyakala kyalungila.»
JOH 16:25 «Moosu mana, mu bingana yisima luzimbwala. Tangwa dyakwísa dina yilúzonzilaku hika mu bingana, kaasi dina yilúsamwana wengele mambu mana matadidini Tata.
JOH 16:26 Muna kilumbu meni kyakina, lwalómba mu khumbu ya meni, amana yiluzimbwadiku ni meni yilómba kwena Tata kikuma kya benu,
JOH 16:27 kikuma, yandi-meni Tata wama kisi luzola, mukuma benu phi lwisi nzola meni, amana lwisi kwikila ni meni kwena Nzambi yítuka.
JOH 16:28 Kwena Tata yítuka amana yisi ha tsi. Buthwena, mbati katuka ha tsi amana yendi kwena Tata.»
JOH 16:29 Balonguki bandi bazimbudini: «Buthwena wekatuzonzila wengele, konda wasadila hika bingana.
JOH 16:30 Buthwena tuzayi ni mambu moosu wuzayima, amana weku yi mupfunu ni mutu kakuhyula. Yi hana tukwikididi ni kwena Nzambi wátuka.»
JOH 16:31 Yesu wubavutwadini: «Buthwena, lukwikidini?
JOH 16:32 Talenu, tangwa dyakwísa, amana dilungidi kedi, dina lwahúmbalakana, kosu mutu yi nzila yandi, amana lwasala nzukula meni hika. Kaasi yeku meni hika kikuma Tata kenina yi meni.
JOH 16:33 Yiluzonzidini bwabuna ndangu lwavwa ngemba mwena meni. Kiwayi kya lawu lwamóna ha tsi yayi. Kaasi kalenu yi kikesa! Meni yínungaya tsi!»
JOH 17:1 Kunima dya kuzonza bwabuna, Yesu wávumbula mesu ku zilu amana wuzimbudini: «A Tata, tangwa dilungidini. Monikisa khembu ya Mwana waku, ndangu Mwana yandi phi kamonikisa khembu ya ngeyi,
JOH 17:2 amana bwosu wámuheka hamu ha thandu ya mutu wosu, kisi hana luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula kwena batu babana wámuheka.
JOH 17:3 -Kinga luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula, lwenina ni bakuzaya ngeyi Nzambi mosi wakyedika, yi wuna wátuma ngeyi, Yesu Kidisitu. -
JOH 17:4 Meni yímonikisa khembu ya ngeyi hana tsi; ndungisini kisalu kina wáthuma mu kusala.
JOH 17:5 Amana buthwena bwabu, Tata, pheka khembu yina yíkala yawu ku mesu ma ngeyi hana tsi khaku kedi yihangama.
JOH 17:6 Ngyadikisiya khumbu yaku kwena batu bana wálubula mu tsi amana wábapheka. Bákala batu ba ngeyi amana wábahana kwena meni, bálunda phi ku ndinga yaku.
JOH 17:7 Buthwena, bazayini ni byosu bina wápheka, kwena ngeyi byátuka.
JOH 17:8 Mukuma yíbaheka ndaka zina wápheka ngeyi; bátambulaza. Bázayabwa ni kyedika, kwena ngeyi yítuka amana bákwikila ni ngeyi wáthuma.
JOH 17:9 «Kikuma kya bawu mbati lombila meni. Mbatiku lombila kikuma kya batu ba tsi, kaasi kikuma kya babana wápheka, kikuma benina ba ngeyi.
JOH 17:10 Kyosu kina kyenina kya meni, kya ngeyi kyenina, amana kina kya ngeyi, kyenina phi kya meni; amana mwena bawu yisi monikina khembu yama.
JOH 17:11 Yenamwoku hika muna tsi, kaasi bawu mu tsi benina; meni yekina mu kukwisa kwena ngeyi. Tata watoma, balema muna khumbu yaku, khumbu yina wápheka, ndangu bákala kima kimosi hanga ngeyi yi meni.
JOH 17:12 Tangwa khadikini yi bawu, yikala balunda muna ngolu za khumbu yaku, ngolu zina wápheka. Yikala balema amana, hana kati dya bawu, keti mosi kátotaku, katula lwesi wuna wáfwana mu kuditotisa, ndangu Masonuku malungila.
JOH 17:13 Buthwena yekina mu kwisa kwena ngeyi. Kima nzonzidini bwabuna buna yenina hika mu tsi, ndangu bavwa mwena bawu-meni kyesi kyama; kyesi kina kyalungila.
JOH 17:14 Meni yíbaheka ndinga yaku, kaasi batu ba tsi bábamenga kikuma beku bisi tsi yayi, bwosu yeku meni phi wa tsi yayi.
JOH 17:15 Yikulombiku ni wabakatula ha tsi, kaasi wabalunda ku Mbi.
JOH 17:16 Beku batu ba ha tsi, bwosu yeku meni phi mutu wa tsi.
JOH 17:17 Batambika muna kyedika; ndinga yaku yenina kyedika.
JOH 17:18 Yíbatuma muna tsi bwosu wáthuma ngeyi phi mu tsi.
JOH 17:19 Amana meni yiditambikini meni wosu kwena ngeyi kikuma kya bawu, ndangu bawu phi bakala ba kutambika kwena ngeyi mu kyedika.
JOH 17:20 «Ndombidiku lwesi kikuma kya bawu, kaasi kikuma phi kya babana bakwíkila mwena meni ku ndinga ya bawu;
JOH 17:21 ndangu boosu bakala kima kimosi, bwosu wenina ngeyi, Tata, mwena meni, yi meni mwena ngeyi, bawu phi bakala mwena betu, ndangu tsi yakwikila ni ngeyi wáthuma.
JOH 17:22 Amana meni yibahekini khembu yina wápheka ngeyi, ndangu bakala kima kimosi bwosu thwenina betu kima kimosi.
JOH 17:23 Meni mwena bawu amana ngeyi mwena meni; ndangu balungila muna kithwadi, amana tsi yazaya ni ngeyi wáthuma, wábazola phi bwosu buna wánzola meni.
JOH 17:24 Tata, bana wábapheka, amana nzodi ni kwosu kuna yenina meni, bawu phi bakala kwakuna hakimosi yi meni ndangu bamona khembu yama, khembu yina wápheka, kikuma watekila nzola hana tsi khaku yihangama.
JOH 17:25 Tata wa masonga, tsi yákuzayaku, kaasi meni yíkuzaya, amana baba-baba babakudi ni ngeyi wáthuma.
JOH 17:26 Yízayikisaya khumbu yaku kwena bawu amana yibázayikisaya hika, ndangu zola dina wenina dyawu kikuma kya meni, dyakala mwena bawu, hanga meni mwena bawu.»
JOH 18:1 Tangwa kámanisa mu kuzonza bwabuna, Yesu wálubuka yi balonguki bandi ndangu benda ku sambwa dya mwana mamba ma Setoni, kwakuna kwákala yi masamba mamosi; Yesu yi balonguki bandi bákota mwamuna.
JOH 18:2 Yutasi, wuna wámulambula, wázaya phi homa hahana; kikuma Yesu yi balonguki bandi bakala kwenda kutakaninaka mbala za lawu kwakuna.
JOH 18:3 Amana Yutasi wisa tula kwakuna, wánata kibuka kya baphumbulu yi batsinzidi bana bámuheka kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bafwadisi. Bákala yi binwaninu amana basimbiki mwinda mya mbweta yi masoka.
JOH 18:4 Yesu wázaya mambu moosu makhana mubwila, wábwesuka kuna thwala amana wubazimbwadini: «Nati lubati sanda?»
JOH 18:5 Bamuvutwadini: «Yesu mwisi Nazaleti.» Yandi wubazimbwadini: «Meni yandu.» Amana Yutasi, wuna wakhana mulambula, watelama kákala hakimosi yi bawu.
JOH 18:6 Buna kábazimbwala: «Meni yandu», bávutwakisa kinima-nima amana bábwa ha tsi.
JOH 18:7 Yesu wábahyula hika: «Nati lubati sanda?» Bawu phi bamuvutwadini: «Yesu mwisi Nazaleti.»
JOH 18:8 Yesu wuvutudini: «Yiluzimbwadikibwa kedi ni meni yandu; amana yuka ni meni lubati sanda, yambulenu baba-baba benda kwabawu.»
JOH 18:9 Kázimbula bwabuna ndangu yalungila ndinga yina katekila zonza: «Thotisikiku keti mosi wa babana wápheka.»
JOH 18:10 Kinga Simoni Phetelu, mbedi ya phoku kákala yawu, wáholaya, wáhuta kutu dya kitata dya musadi wa mbuta wa banganga Nzambi. Khumbu ya musadi wuna yákala Malukusu.
JOH 18:11 Yesu wázimbula kwena Phetelu: «Vutula mbedi yaku ya phoku muna kilalu kyandi. Ngeyi wubanzi ni bungu dya phasi dyadi kaphekini Tata ndwadyoku?»
JOH 18:12 Kibuka kya baphumbulu yi bapfumu ba bawu yi batsinzidi ba Bayuta bámukwatidila Yesu amana bámukasa.
JOH 18:13 Hanga bamunatini theti kwena Ana, yandi, buko bwa Khayifu kákala, wuna wákala mbuta wa banganga Nzambi muna mvula meni yayina.
JOH 18:14 Khayifu meni wuna, yandi wáhana ndongisila yayi kwena Bayuta: «Bulungi ni mutu mosi kafwa kikuma kya kanda dya batu.»
JOH 18:15 Simoni Phetelu yi mulonguki wahika bakala mulanda Yesu kuna manima. Mulonguki meni wuna wázayasana yi mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, yihakana kákotila nzila mosi yi Yesu muna kati dya kyanzala kya nzu ya mbuta wa banganga Nzambi;
JOH 18:16 Phetelu, yandi sadikini hana phenza, bela-bela yi mwelu. Hanga mulonguki wuna wázayakana yi mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wulubukini amana wendi zonza yi tsinzidi wa mukhetu wuna wakala tadikina mwelu, kunima, wámukotisa Phetelu.
JOH 18:17 Hanga musadi wa mukhetu meni yana wakala tsinzidi ku mwelu wuzimbudi kwena Phetelu: «Ngeyi phi weku mosi wa balonguki ba mutu wuna?» Yandi wumuvutwadini: «Loni, ka meni ku.»
JOH 18:18 Basadi yi batsinzidi hana bákala; báwika mbawu amana bekina yeta mukuma kuma kyosi kwákala. Phetelu phi hana kákala yi kuyetaka mbawu hakimosi yi bawu.
JOH 18:19 Mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wumuhyudini Yesu mu mambu mana matadidini balonguki bandi yi malongi mandi.
JOH 18:20 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Meni yikala zonza phwelele kwena mutu wosu. Yikala longa kosu tangwa muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta yi muna nzu ya Nzambi, muna bisi kutakanina Bayuta boosu. Amana yízonzaku keti kima kimosi mu kitsweki.
JOH 18:21 Kikuma kya biki wubati phyudila? Mambu mana nzonzini, hyulama kwena batu babana bángyuka; bawu bazayi bukheti mana yízonza meni.»
JOH 18:22 Yesu buna kázimbula bwabuna, mosi wa batsinzidi bana bákala hakana, hanga wumuti mbata mu kuzimbula: «Yibwabuna wubati vutula kwena mbuta wa banganga Nzambi?»
JOH 18:23 Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Yuka ni mbi nzonzini, songilaya; kaasi yuka ni bukheti nzonzini, kikuma kya biki wubati mbetila?»
JOH 18:24 Hanga Ana wumuhitikini, wakukasa, kwena Khayifu, mbuta wa banganga Nzambi.
JOH 18:25 Simoni Phetelu hana kákala yi kuyetaka mbawu. Bamuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi phi weku mosi wa balonguki bandi?» Kaasi yandi wátuna mu kuzimbula: «Ka meni ku.»
JOH 18:26 Mosi wa basadi ba mbuta wa banganga Nzambi, wuna wákala kiwutu kya mutu wuna káhuta Phetelu kutu, wuzimbudini: «Meni yikumonikiku muna masamba, hakimosi yi yandi?»
JOH 18:27 Kaasi Phetelu wátuna hika. Muna tangwa meni dina, khoku wákokula.
JOH 18:28 Hanga muna suka, bapfumu ba banganga Nzambi bamunatini Yesu tukidila ku nzu ya Khayifu yi kuna nganda ya pfumu wa mbanza wa Loma. Bawu-meni bákotamwoku mu nganda hanga badisumuna nana, ndangu balenga ta mukinzi wa Phaki.
JOH 18:29 Philatu wálubuka kuna bákala bawu amana wuzimbudini: «Khi dyambu lubati mufundila mutu yandu?»
JOH 18:30 Bamuvutwadini: «Wadi ni mutu yandi kákadikiku mutu wambi, wadi tukhaniku kulambwala yandi.»
JOH 18:31 Hanga Philatu wubazimbwadini: «Mubongenu benu-benu amana mufundisenu bwosu milombi mitsiku myenu.» Bayuta bamuzimbwadini: «Betu thweku yi muswa wa kuhondisa mutu.»
JOH 18:32 Bwáhangama bwabuna ndangu yalungila ndinga yina kázimbula Yesu, mu kusongila phila ya lufwa luna kálunga mu kufwila.
JOH 18:33 Philatu wávutuka mu nganda, wámutedisa Yesu amana wumuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi wenina kyamvu wa Bayuta?»
JOH 18:34 Yesu wuvutudini: «Dyambu dina wubati phyula, kwena ngeyi-meni ditukini ho batu bahika bakuzimbwadibwa?»
JOH 18:35 Philatu wumuhyudini: «Disongidila ni meni Muyuta yenina? Kanda dyaku yi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi bisi kulambula kwena meni; biki wuhangi ngeyi?»
JOH 18:36 Yesu wuvutudini: «Luyalu lwama lweku lwa ha tsi yayi. Wadi ni lwákala lwa ha tsi yayi, wadi basadi bama bakhani ndwanina ndangu bandambulaku kwena Bayuta. Mu kuzonza kwamboti, luyalu lwama lweku lwa tsi yayi.»
JOH 18:37 Philatu wumuzimbwadini: «Disongidila ni ngeyi kyamvu wenina?» Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Ngeyi-meni wuzonzibwa ni kyamvu yenina. Meni yuka ni yíbutuka, yisa phi mu tsi, ndangu yita kimbangi kwena kyedika. Wosu wuna wenina mu kyedika, kisi yuka ndinga yama.»
JOH 18:38 Philatu wumuhyudini: «Biki kyedika?» Kunima dya kuzimbula bwabuna, Philatu wálubuka hika mu kumona Bayuta amana wubazimbwadini: «Kikuma kya meni, mboniku keti kikuma kimosi kya kumubedisila mukanu mutu yandu.
JOH 18:39 Bwosu lwáyikana kedi ni kosu mvula, yiluyambwalaka mutu wa boloku mosi mu mukinzi wa Phaki; zengenuti buthwena bwabu, yiluyambwala kyamvu wa Bayuta?»
JOH 18:40 Hanga boosu bayandikini mu kukalunga: «Ka yandi ku! Kaasi Balabasi!» Kinga, Balabasi ndwandwa kákala.
JOH 19:1 Hanga Philatu wutumi ni bamubonga Yesu amana bamuzyatula mafimbu.
JOH 19:2 Baphumbulu bátunga mukhonzi wa tsaku wuna bámuvwatisa kuna mutwa, amana bámuvwatisa muzaka wa kabengi.
JOH 19:3 Bakala kwisa kwena yandi yi kuzimbulaka: «Mboti, kyamvu wa Bayuta!» Amana bakala muta mbata.
JOH 19:4 Philatu wálubuka hika amana wázimbula kwena Bayuta: «Yilunatini yandi ku phenza, ndangu lwazaya ni mboniku keti kikuma kimosi, mwena yandi, kya kumubedisila mukanu.»
JOH 19:5 Yesu phi wálubuka; wuvwatiki mukhonzi wa tsaku yi muzaka wa kabengi. Amana Philatu wubazimbwadini: «Yandi-wu mutu!»
JOH 19:6 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi batsinzidi, buna bámumona, hanga bakalungini: «Mukhoka ha kitakani! Mukhoka ha kitakani.» Philatu wubazimbwadini: «Mubongenu benu-benu amana mukhokenu ha kitakani; mukuma meni mboniku kwama kikuma, mwena yandi, kya kumubedisila mukanu.»
JOH 19:7 Bayuta bamuvutwadini: «Betu thwenina yi mitsiku amana mitsiku meni mina mibati lomba ni kafweti fwa, kikuma wudikitudi Mwana wa Nzambi.»
JOH 19:8 Tangwa káyuka Philatu ndinga yina, wáyuka hika bweya lawu.
JOH 19:9 Wávutuka hika muna nganda amana wáhyula kwena Yesu: «Kubiki wutukini ngeyi?» Kaasi Yesu kámuvutwalaku mvutu.
JOH 19:10 Hanga Philatu wumuzimbwadini: «Abweti wubatiku ngyakula? Wuzayiku ni meni yenina yi kiyeka kya kukuyambwadila holo kya kukukhokisa ha kitakani?»
JOH 19:11 Yesu wuvutudini: «Weku yi kiyeka kimosi hana thandu ya meni yuka ni kakuhekikyoku Nzambi. Ihana ni mutu wuna wisi ndambula kwena ngeyi, disumu dyandi dilutini dina dya ngeyi.»
JOH 19:12 Tukidila bwabuna, Philatu kákala sanda phila ya kumusudila Yesu. Kaasi Bayuta bakalungini: «Yuka ni wamusula, weku nduku wa Khayisala. Kosu mutu wuna wudikitudini kyamvu, kipfumu kabati nwanina yi Khayisala!»
JOH 19:13 Philatu, buna káyuka mihowu meni mina, hanga wumulubudini Yesu kuna nzila amana yandi wendi zakala hana kiti kyandi kya pfundusu, hana batedini: «Homa bákunga mu matadi, amana mu ndinga ya Bahebelu bisiha tela ni "Ngabata".»
JOH 19:14 Kyákala kilumbu kya kuyidika mukinzi wa Phaki, bela-bela yi tsinzi; Philatu wázimbula kwena Bayuta: «Ayanduwu kyamvu wenu!»
JOH 19:15 Kaasi bawu bakalungini: «Kafwa! Kafwa! Mukhoka hana kitakani!» Philatu wubahyudini: «Fwani yimukhoka ha kitakani kyamvu wenu?» Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi bamuvutwadini: «Betu thweku yi kyamvu wahika, kaka Khayisala.»
JOH 19:16 Hanga wubaheki yandi Yesu ndangu bamukhoka ha kitakani. Amana bámunata Yesu.
JOH 19:17 Bwosu kakala nata yandi-meni kitakani kyandi, wálubuka mu hata amana wénda homa hana bisi tela: «Kibelengenzi kya mutwa»; mu ndinga ya Bahebelu, bisiha tela: «Kolukota».
JOH 19:18 Hahana bámukhokila ha kitakani. Hakimosi yi yandi, bakhoki hika batu bodi ha kitakani, mosi ku koku dya kitata dya Yesu, mukwawu ku koku dya kimama; yandi bamusi ha kati.
JOH 19:19 Philatu wáyidikisa koma ka dibaya, bánamikadya hana thandu ya kitakani kya Yesu; dyákala dyakusonika: «Yesu mwisi Nazaleti, kyamvu wa Bayuta.»
JOH 19:20 Bayuta balawu bakala tanga bisona byabina, kikuma homa hana bámukhokila ha kitakani Yesu hákala bela-bela yi mbanza. Masonuku mana makala mu ndinga tatu: yimosi ndinga ya Bahebelu, yikwawu ndinga ya bisi Loma yi ya Bangeleki.
JOH 19:21 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi ba Bayuta bázimbula kwena Philatu: «Wusonikaku buna: "Kyamvu wa Bayuta" kaasi sonika: "Mutu yandu kázimbula: Yenina kyamvu wa Bayuta".»
JOH 19:22 Philatu wuvutudini: «Mana tsonikini, tsonikima kedi.»
JOH 19:23 Kunima dya kumukhoka ha kitakani Yesu, baphumbulu bátambula miledi myandi, bákabisamya mu ndambu ya, ndambu mosi-mosi kikuma kya kosu phumbulu. Bátambula hika mvwela yandi yina bakonda nunga mu bitini, kaasi bátungaya yi muledi wamuthu, tukidila ku londi yi kuna banda.
JOH 19:24 Baphumbulu badizimbwadini bawu yi bawu: «Tuyatayoku mvwela yayi, kaasi tubetilenuyoku zeki ndangu twazaya keti nati watámbulaya.» Bwabuna malungidila Masonuku: «Badikabisidini miledi myama, amana lophu dyama, babetididya zeki.» Bwabuna báhanga baphumbulu.
JOH 19:25 Hana kabeta ka kitakani kya Yesu hákala yi ngudi wandi yi phangi wa mukhetu wa ngudi wandi, Madiya mukhetu wa Kolophasi yi Madiya mwisi Makatala.
JOH 19:26 Yesu buna kámona ngudi wandi, amana hana kabeta ka yandi, hákala yi mulonguki wuna kakala zola lawu, hanga wuzimbudi kwena ngudi wandi: «Ngudi, tala mwana waku.»
JOH 19:27 Kunima wuzimbudi hika kwena mulonguki: «Tala ngudi waku.» Amana tukidila thangwa meni dyadina, mulonguki wámubonga ku nzu yandi.
JOH 19:28 Kunima dya bwabuna, Yesu bwosu kázaya ni moosu malungidi kedi; mu kusya ti Masonuku malungila, wuzimbudini: «Kihwinya yenina kyawu.»
JOH 19:29 Hákala hakana yi kilekwa kimosi kyákala kyabasa yi vinu dya ngani. Bátambula vuya, bázitikiladya kuna tsongi ya luswaswa lwa Yizophi, bávundikadya muna vinu dya ngani, amana báthutadya yi kuna munwa wandi.
JOH 19:30 Yesu, buna káfiya vinu dya ngani, wuzimbudini: «Moosu malungidini!» Kunima wázenzika mutwa amana wátabula moyu.
JOH 19:31 Kilumbu mekina kyákala kitanu, kilumbu kina bakala yidikila sabata amana Bayuta bisa lomba kwena Philatu ndangu bakatula bamvumbi mu bitakani kunima dya kubatolula malu, ndangu mvumbi zinangaku ha kitakani mu kilumbu kya sabata -kikuma kyákala kilumbu kyambuta. -
JOH 19:32 Hanga baphumbulu bisini amana batoludini malu ma mutu watheti, kunima ma wuna mukwawu wuna bákhoka ha kitakani yi Yesu.
JOH 19:33 Tangwa bátula kwena Yesu, bámona ni wufiki kedi; amana bámutolulaku malu.
JOH 19:34 Kaasi mosi wa basuta kahanga wumukubi ngumba muna luhati; muna mbala mosi, menga yi mamba málubuka.
JOH 19:35 Mutu wuna wubati ta kimbangi meni kyakina, yandi wámonakya phi amana kimbangi kyandi kyenina kya kyedika; yandi wuzayi ni kyedika kabati zonza, ndangu benu phi lwakwikila.
JOH 19:36 Mamana mábwa ndangu Masonuku malungila: «Keti mufufwa wandi wumosi watólukaku.»
JOH 19:37 Amana Mukanda wukwawu wuzimbudini hika: «Batála kwena wuna bátubula.»
JOH 19:38 Kunima dya bwabuna, Yozefu, mwisi Adimate, wuna wákala mulonguki wa Yesu, kaasi mu kitsweki, kikuma kya bweya bwa Bayuta, wenda lomba nzila kwena Philatu ndangu kakatula lutu lwa Yesu. Philatu wámuheka nzila. Yozefu wisa amana wákatula mvumbi.
JOH 19:39 Nikodemi, mutu wuna wenda mumona Yesu, kilumbu kimosi muna phipha, wisa nata phi mananasi ma mila ma kubundikisa yi aluwesi, kitesu kya kilo makumatatu.
JOH 19:40 Yozefu yi Nikundimu bátambula mvumbi ya Yesu amana bávungaya ha muledi, yi mananasi ma tsudi, bwosu bisi zika bamvumbi mu kikalulu kya Bayuta.
JOH 19:41 Kinga kwákala yi kilanga kimosi kwakuna bámukhokila ha kitakani, amana muna kilanga meni kyakina, mwákala yi mazyamu mamosi mapha bakonda kedi zika keti mutu.
JOH 19:42 Amana bwosu kyákala kilumbu kya kuyidikila sabata dya Bayuta, mazyamu phi bela-bela mákala, hanga Yozefu yi Nikodemi benda muzesa Yesu muna mazyamu meni mana.
JOH 20:1 Kilumbu kyatheti kya phosa muna suka-suka, Madiya mwisi Makatala wenda kuna mazyamu, kinga kuma mwa phipha hika kwákala, amana wumoni ni ditadi dyakukatula ku mwelu wa mazyamu.
JOH 20:2 Wenda thinu katela Simoni Phetelu yi mulonguki mukwawu wuna kakala zola lawu Yesu amana wubazimbwadini: «Pfumu bamukatudini mu mazyamu, tuzayiku phi keti kubiki bamusini.»
JOH 20:3 Hanga Phetelu yi mulonguki wuna mukwawu bálubuka ndangu benda kuna mazyamu.
JOH 20:4 Thinu bakala kwenda bawu bodi; kaasi mulonguki wuna mukwawu thinu za lawu kákala kuluta Phetelu, amana yandi wáditudila theti ku mazyamu.
JOH 20:5 Kahanga wuzenzamini amana wumonini bitemba bya miledi hana tsi, kaasi kákotaku.
JOH 20:6 Simoni Phetelu, wakala mulanda ku manima, wisa tula amana wákota muna mazyamu, wumoni bitemba bya miledi hana tsi,
JOH 20:7 yi muledi wuna bámukasa ku mutwa. Muledi meni wuna wákalaku homa hamosi yi bitemba bya miledi; kaasi wákala wakuvunga mu kingenga.
JOH 20:8 Hanga mulonguki wuna mukwawu wáditudila theti ku mazyamu, wákota yandi phi. Wámona amana wákwikila.
JOH 20:9 Mukuma yi kuna kilumbu meni kina, balonguki bábakisaku kedi Masonuku mana básonika ni Yesu wáfwana kafutumuka hakati dya bafwa.
JOH 20:10 Hanga balonguki bawu bodi bavutuki kwabawu ku nzu.
JOH 20:11 Madiya wutelamikini kuna phenza, bela-bela yi mazyamu, yi kudilaka. Bwana kakala dila, wuzenzami mu kutala muna mazyamu;
JOH 20:12 hanga wumoni banzyo bodi mu miledi mya phembi, bazakadikini hana hákala theti lutu lwa Yesu, mosi kuna mutwa amana mukwawu kuna malu.
JOH 20:13 Bamuzimbwadini: «Mukhetu, biki wubati didila?» Yandi wubavutwadini: «Kikuma Pfumu wama bamukatudini, nzayiku phi keti kubiki bamusini.»
JOH 20:14 Buna kázimbula bwabuna, wábaluka kumanima amana wumoni Yesu wutelamikini, kaasi kázayaku ni Yesu yandina.
JOH 20:15 Yesu wumuhyudini: «Mukhetu, biki wubati didila? Nati wubati sanda?» Madiya kábanza ni musadi wa bilanga wuna, hanga wumuzimbwadini: «Pfumu, yuka ni ngeyi wumunatini, nzimbwala kuna wumusini, amana yenda mubonga.»
JOH 20:16 Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Madiya!» Yandi wábaluka kwena yandi amana wuzimbudi muna ndinga ya Bahebelu: «Labuni!» disongidila: «Mulongi.»
JOH 20:17 Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Wutsimbaku, mukuma khaku kedi thombuka kwena Tata. Kaasi awenda kwena baphangi bama amana bazimbwala ni thombuki kwena Tata wama wuna wenina phi Tata wenu, Nzambi wama yi Nzambi wenu.»
JOH 20:18 Madiya mwisi Makatala wendi samuna kwena balonguki: «Yimumonini Pfumu!» Amana wábamenikina mamana kámuzimbwala.
JOH 20:19 Muna masikidika mamana ma kilumbu kyatheti kya phosa, balonguki bákala bawongama muna nzu. Bábindika mwelu yi tsabi, kikuma kya bweya bwa Bayuta. Yesu wisa, hanga wutelami hana kati dya bawu, wubazimbwadini: «Ngemba yakala yi benu!»
JOH 20:20 Buna kázimbula bwabuna, wábasongila moku mandi yi luhati lwandi. Balonguki bákala mu kyesi kya lawu mu kumona Pfumu.
JOH 20:21 Yesu wubazimbwadi hika: «Ngemba yakala yi benu! Bwosu buna káthuma Tata, meni phi yilutumini.»
JOH 20:22 Kunima dya kuzimbula bwabuna, wáfula lwanda hana thandu ya bawu amana wubazimbwadini: «Tambulenu Kitembu Kyatoma!
JOH 20:23 Kwena bana lwálolula masumu ma bawu, bátambula ndoluka; kwena bana lwakonda lolula, balólukaku.»
JOH 20:24 Tangwa kisa Yesu, mosi wa bawu kumi yi bodi, khumbu yandi Tomasi, wuna bisi tela ni diphasa, kákalahoku.
JOH 20:25 Hanga balonguki bahika bamuzimbwadini: «Tumumoni Pfumu.» Kaasi yandi wubavutwadini: «Yuka ni mboniku bidimbu bina bamukhokidikini tsosu muna moku mandi, yuka ni khotisiku mulembu wama muna bidimbu meni bina, yuka ni khotisiku phi koku dyama muna luhati lwandi, yikwíkilabwoku keti bweti.»
JOH 20:26 Kunima dya bilumbu nana, balonguki bandi bákala hika badiphatila muna nzu, Tomasi phi hana kákala hakimosi yi bawu. Mwelu myosu mya kukangisa, hanga Yesu wisi telama hana kati dya bawu, wubazimbwadini: «Ngemba yakala yi benu!»
JOH 20:27 Kunima wuzimbudini kwena Tomasi: «Kotisa haha mulembu waku, tala phi moku mama; thuta koku dyaku amana syadya muna luhati lwama. Yambula phaka, kwikila!»
JOH 20:28 Tomasi wumuvutwadini: «Pfumu wama yi Nzambi wama!»
JOH 20:29 Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Kikuma wumboni, yihana wukwikididi? Kyesi kwena babana bisi kwikila konda kumona!»
JOH 20:30 Yesu wata hika bidimbu bya biphadi byalawu, ku thwala ya balonguki bandi, bina bakonda sonika mu mukanda wawu.
JOH 20:31 Kaasi byabi básonikabya ndangu lwakwikila ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu, Mwana wa Nzambi, amana muna lukwikilu meni luna, lwatambula luzingu mu khumbu ya yandi.
JOH 21:1 Kunima dya ndambu ya bilumbu, Yesu wádimokisa hika kwena balonguki, kuna yanga dya mbuta dya Tibediyadi. Tala buna kádimonikisina:
JOH 21:2 Simoni Phetelu, Tomasi wuna bisi tela ni diphasa, Natanayedi mwisi mbanza ya Kana, kuna kinzunga kya Ngadidi, bana ba Zebeteya yi balonguki bahika bodi muna kati dya balonguki bandi, boosu bákala homa hamosi.
JOH 21:3 Simoni Phetelu wubazimbwadini: «Yendi loba.» Bawu phi bamuzimbwadini: «Betu phi twakwénda yi ngeyi.» Bálubuka amana bákota mu masuwa. Phipha meni yina yosu bákwataku keti kima.
JOH 21:4 Kuma buna kwákhya, Yesu hana sambwa kákala watelama; kaasi balonguki bákalaku zaya ni yandi wuna Yesu.
JOH 21:5 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Bana bama, tsema lukwatini?» Bawu bamuvutwadini: «Loni»,
JOH 21:6 Yandi wubazimbwadini: «Timbulenu wanda kuna koku dya kitata kya masuwa amana lwakwáta.» Bátimbuladya phi, amana bálendaku mu kuthutadya kikuma dyábasa yi batsema balawu.
JOH 21:7 Hanga mulonguki wuna kakala zola lawu Yesu, wuzimbudini kwena Phetelu: «Wuna, Pfumu!» Simoni Phetelu buna káyuka: «Pfumu wuna!» wákasa muledi wandi muna mbunda, mukuma kikhonga kákala, amana wáditimbula muna yanga dya mbuta.
JOH 21:8 Balonguki bahika bisa yi masuwa, kuna yi kukokaka wanda dyakabasi yi batsema, mukuma bákalaku kyana yi mafu, kitesu kya metele khama.
JOH 21:9 Buna bátula ku tseki, báwana mbawu yi batsema hana ziku, yi dipha.
JOH 21:10 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Natenu ndambu ya batsema babana lukwatini.»
JOH 21:11 Simoni Phetelu, wázanza muna masuwa amana wákoka yi kuna tseki, wanda dyakabasi yi batsema ba mbuta-mbuta: kitesu kya khama mosi yi makumatanu yi tatu. Mbatanana bákala batsema lawu, wanda dyáyatukaku.
JOH 21:12 Yesu wubazimbwadini: «Alwisa dya.» Keti mulonguki wandi mosi kálendaku mu kumuhyula: «Nati wenina ngeyi?», Mukuma bakala zaya ni wuna Pfumu.
JOH 21:13 Yesu wábwesuka, wátambula dipha amana wábahekadya; wábaheka hika phi tsema.
JOH 21:14 Yayina yákala mbala ya tatu, Yesu wáfutumuka ku bafwa mu kudimonikisa kwena balonguki bandi.
JOH 21:15 Buna bámanisa kudya, Yesu wázimbula kwena Simoni Phetelu: «Simoni, mwana wa Yowani, keti lungongu lwa meni wenina lwawu kuluta baba?» Phetelu wumuvutwadini: «Yibwana, Pfumu, wuzayi bukheti ni yisi kuzola.» Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Disa bana bama ba mikoku.»
JOH 21:16 Wumuzimbwadi hika mu mbala ya zodi: «Simoni, mwana wa Yowani, ngeyi lungongu lwa meni wenina lwawu?» Yandi wumuvutwadini: «Yibwana Pfumu, wuzayi ni yisi kutya.» Yesu wumuvutwadini: «Kala muhungudi wa mikoku myama.»
JOH 21:17 Wumuzimbwadi hika mu mbala ya tatu: «Simoni, mwana wa Yowani, keti wisi thya meni?» Phetelu wáyuka kyadi kikuma kya buna kámuhyula mu mbala ya tatu: «Keti wisi thya meni?» Yandi wumuvutwadini: «Yibwana Pfumu, wuzayi moosu! Wuzayi phi ni yisi kuzola.» Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Disa mikoku myama.
JOH 21:18 Mu kyedika yikuzimbwadibwa: tangwa wákala sanda, wakala dikasa ngeyi meni tsibu yaku, amana wakala kwenda kwosu wakala zola; kaasi tangwa wanúna, wayála moku, mutu wahika wakúzika tsibu yaku mu kukunata kuna wuzodiku.»
JOH 21:19 Yesu kázimbula bwabuna mu kusongila mutindu wa lufwa luna káfwila Phetelu kikuma kya kuhana khembu kwena Nzambi. Kunima dya kuzonza bwabuna, Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Ndanda!»
JOH 21:20 Phetelu buna kábaluka, wumoni mulonguki wuna kakala zola Yesu, kakala balanda, wuna wáyekamina ha thulu ya Yesu tangwa bákala ku mesa, wámuhyula phi: «Pfumu, nati yanduna wukulambuni?»
JOH 21:21 Phetelu buna kámumona, wuzimbudi kwena Yesu: «Pfumu, yandu biki byamúbwila?»
JOH 21:22 Yesu wumuzimbwadini: «Yuka yizola ni kazinga tii yikuna yikwísila, makutadini? Ngeyi landa meni!»
JOH 21:23 Amana musamu wáyalangana ha kati dya baphangi ni mulonguki wuna kafwáku. Kinga Yesu kámuzimbwalaku: «Yandi kafwáku», kaasi kázimbula: «Yuka yizola ni kazinga tii yikuna yikwísila, makutadini?»
JOH 21:24 Yandi wuna mulonguki meni wuna wubati ta kimbangi kya mambu mana, yandi wásonikama, amana tuzayi ni kimbangi kyandi kyenina kyedika.
JOH 21:25 Henina hika yi mambu makwawu ma mbuta káhanga Yesu. Wadi ni básonikakama dimosi-dimosi, mbanzi ni yameni tsi yosu yakhanaku lungila mu mikanda mina bakhana sonika.
ACT 1:1 Muzitu Thyofila, Muna mukanda wama wuna watheti, yízonzila moosu mana káhanga Yesu yi mana kálonga tukidila ku luyandiku
ACT 1:2 yi kuna kilumbu kina kátombwakila ku zilu. Ku thwala ya kunyokuka kwandi ku zilu, wáhana milongi, mu ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma, kwena bathumwa bana kásola.
ACT 1:3 Kwena bawu phi kámonika wamoya, ku manima ma lufwa lwandi, yi mitindu mya lawu mina kádisongila, mu bilumbu makumaya ndangu kabasongila ni mukyedika, mu luzingu kenina: kakala monika yi kubazonzilaka mambu matadidi Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
ACT 1:4 Kilumbu kimosi kakala dya ha kimosi yi bawu, wábaheka mulongi wawu: «Lwendaku kyana yi Yelusalemi, kaasi hingilenu kilangi kina kásila Tata, bwosu yílumenikinabwa.
ACT 1:5 Yowani kábotika yi mamba, kaasi benu, mu bilumbu bya khunda, lwabótama yi Kitembu Kyatoma.»
ACT 1:6 Bana bakala bakutakana bámuyufula bwabu: «Pfumu, buthwena wavutulula Kipfumu kya Kiseledi?»
ACT 1:7 Yandi wábavutwala: «Malutadiku mu kuzaya tangwa holo kilumbu kina kázenga tata mu hamu dyandi.
ACT 1:8 Kaasi tangwa kalúkulwamukina Kitembu Kyatoma, lwatámbula ngolu zandi amana lwakítuka bambangi bama mu Yelusalemi yi mu Yuteya dyosu yi mu Samadiya yi kuna tsuka ya tsi.»
ACT 1:9 Buna kázonza ndinga meni zina, bwosu bakala tala, Yandi wátombuka ku zilu, tuti dimosi dyámufídinga amana bámumonaku hika.
ACT 1:10 Bwosu bakala tala ku zilu kuna kénda yandi, batala bwabu, batu bodi, mu miledi mya phembi, bábatelamina
ACT 1:11 bazonzi phi: «Bisi Ngadidi, kikuma kya biki lutelaminiki haka mu kutala ku zilu? Yesu wuna dihambudi yi benu, wendi ku zilu, kakwisa vutuka kaka bwosu lumumoni kendi ku zilu.»
ACT 1:12 Hanga bavutuki ku Yelusalemi, buna bátuka ku mongu wa Olive. Wuna wakala bela-bela yi Yelusalemi, muna nzila yina bákangala kitesu kya kilometele dimosi.
ACT 1:13 Amana tangwa bákota, bazanza ku mwanza wambuta wa ku zilu kuna bakala kutakanina theti. Kwákala: Phetelu, Yowani, Zyaki, Andele, Fidiphu, Toma, Batolomi, Mathayi, Zyaki mwana wa Alufwe, Simoni wuna wákala theti mu dingumba dya bana bisi nwanina diphandasi, yi Yuta mwana wa Zyaki.
ACT 1:14 Bawu boosu bákwamina mu kimvuka mu kulombilaka homa ha mosi, kumosi yi bakhetu, yi Madiya ngudi wa Yesu, yi baphangi ba Yesu.
ACT 1:15 Kilumbu kimosi muna bilumbu meni bina, Phetelu wátelama hana kati dya bakwikidi, thalu ya batu bana bákala mu kimvuka yakala kitesu kya khama mosi yi makumodi hanga wuzimbudi:
ACT 1:16 «Baphangi bama, bwáfwana malungila Masonuku ma Kitembu Kyatoma, muna munwa wa Tavidi, mana katekila zonza kikuma kya Yutasi, wuna wásongila nzila kwena batu bana bamukwata Yesu.
ACT 1:17 Mukuma kákala mosi mu kati dya betu, amana wátambula kiyeka kyandi mu kisalu meni kyaki.»
ACT 1:18 Kunima kusumba kilanga kimosi yi mbongu zina bámufuta kikuma kya mbi yandi, wabwa wabukama, kundu dyámuyatuka ha kati-kati, mitsyobu myosu mimulubuki.
ACT 1:19 Amana tsangu záyalangana kwena bisi Yelusalemi, tii yi kuna bátedilakya kilanga meni kina mu ndinga ya bawu ni «Hakheditama», disongidila: «Kilanga kya menga».
ACT 1:20 Amana Phetelu wávutwakila hika: "Kinga básonika mu mukanda wa mikunga: nzu yamúkituka yamba, amana keti mutu kazíngilahoku." Amana: "Ni mutu wa hika katambula kiyeka kyandi."
ACT 1:21 «Bulungi ni mu kati dya batu bana bisi tusindikila tangwa dyosu dina kakala kwenda yi kukwisa, Pfumu Yesu ha kati dya betu,
ACT 1:22 tuka ku mbotika ya Yowani tii yi kuna kilumbu kina kátombwakila ha kati dya betu, mosi wa batu meni bana kakituka mbangi wa lufutumuku lwandi ha kimosi yi betu.»
ACT 1:23 Amana bálubula bayakala bodi: Yozefu wuna bakala tela Badisaba, bakala mutela hika ni Yusitusi, yi Matyasi.
ACT 1:24 Kunima balombidi bwabu: «Pfumu, ngeyi wisi zaya mbundu za batu boosu, songila keti nati, ha kati dya bawu bodi, wusodi ngeyi,
ACT 1:25 ndangu kahingana mu kisalu kyaki, kya kithumwa kina kásisa Yutasi mu kukwenda kuna kwámufwana.»
ACT 1:26 Bahanga babeti zeki hana kati dya bawu bodi, amana zeki dyábwila kwena Matyasi, wuna báyika kwena bathumwa kumi yi mosi.
ACT 2:1 Tangwa kyáfwana kilumbu kya Phandikoti, boosu bákala mu kimvuka homa hamosi.
ACT 2:2 Mu kithulumukina, malokosi mamosi mátuka ku zilu, hanga pfunzi ya ngolu yibasisi phi nzu yosu yina bákala bazakala.
ACT 2:3 Kutala mileku mibamonikini hanga mina mya mbawu; midihambudi amana myábwila hana thandu ya kosu mutu wa bawu.
ACT 2:4 Boosu bábasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma amana báyandika kuzonza mu ndinga za hika, bwosu buna kakala batwadisila Kitembu Kyatoma mu kuzonza.
ACT 2:5 Kinga Bayuta bakwikama, ba makanda moosu menina mu tsya zilu bakala zingila ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 2:6 Amana muna malokosi mana máyukalakana, mulumba-lumba wa batu wisa thinu amana bákala mabanza vwalanganu, kikuma kosu mutu kakala bayuka kuzonza muna ndinga yandi.
ACT 2:7 Báyituka lawu, básaluka phi, bakala zimbula: «Batu bana babati zonza, boosu beku bisi Ngadidi?
ACT 2:8 Abweti ni kosu mutu, mu kati dya betu, kabati bayuka muna ndinga yandi ya kisina?
ACT 2:9 Ha kati dya betu henina yi batu batukini ku tsi ya Phaditi, ya Mediya yi ya Elami. Henina yi bana bisi zingila ku Mezophotamiya, ku Yuteya yi ku Kaphatosi, ku Phoni yi kuna mulambu wa Aziya,
ACT 2:10 bátuka ku Fizi yi ku Phafidiya, dya ku Ngiphiti yi kinzunga kya Sileni mu Dibya; henina yi bana bátuka ku Loma,
ACT 2:11 Bayuta yi Bakwa-kwisa bana bákwikila mu malongi ma bayuta, Bakheleti yi Bisi Alabiya; tubati bayuka kuzimbula muna ndinga zetu, mihangu mya mbuta mya Nzambi!»
ACT 2:12 Amana boosu báyituka, bámonaku hika kima kya kuzonza; bakala dizimbwala: "Biki disongidila dya bwabubu?"
ACT 2:13 Kaasi bahika bakala baseya mu kuzimbula: «Malafu ma pha mabazedini!»
ACT 2:14 Hanga Phetelu wátelama yi bawu Kumi yi mosi; wáthuta ndinga amana wázimbula bwabu kwena mulumba-lumba wa batu: «Batu ba mu Yuteya yi benu boosu lwisi zingila mu Yelusalemi, hinikinenu ndinga zama, zayenu bwabu:
ACT 2:15 batu baba bazediku malafu bwosu lubatibwa banza benu, mukuma mu tangwa dya vwa dya mu suka thwenina.
ACT 2:16 Kaasi buthwena, malungidi mana kázimbula mbikudi Yowedi:
ACT 2:17 "Tala mu bilumbu bya tsuka, kázimbula Nzambi; yimwánga Kitembu kyama kwena mutu wosu; bana benu ba bakhetu yi ba bayakala babíkula, bangunza benu bamóna mbona mesu, amana binunu byenu balóta ndosi.
ACT 2:18 Mukyedika, yimwanga Kitembu kyama mwena basadi bama ba bakhetu yi basadi bama ba bayakala muna bilumbu meni bina, amana babíkula.
ACT 2:19 Amana yihána bidimbu bya khumbwa mu londi dya zilu yi biphadi muna banda dya ha tsi, yi menga yi mbawu yi kyungila kya mwisi;
ACT 2:20 tangwa kabáluka mu phipha; amana ngondi kabénga hanga menga, ku thwala kukwisa kwa kilumbu kya Pfumu, kilumbu meni kina kya mbuta yi kya khembu.
ACT 2:21 Hanga wosu wuna watéla khumbu ya Pfumu, kahúluka."
ACT 2:22 «Bisi Kiseledi, hinikikenu ndinga zazi: Yesu mwisi Nazaleti, mutu wuna kásikununa Nzambi kwena benu mu biphadi yi bidimbu bya khumbwa yi bidimbu bina kásala mu nzila ya yandi ha kati dya benu, bwosu luzayibwa benu-benu,
ACT 2:23 mutu wuna, bámulambula bwosu bwádikadila kedi mu luzolu lwa Nzambi, lwámuhondisa mu kumukhoka ha kitakani kwena bandwandwa.
ACT 2:24 Yandi wuna káfutumuna Nzambi, mu kumukatula mu phasi za lufwa, kikuma lufwa lwáfwanaku ni lwamukwata.
ACT 2:25 Mukuma Tavidi bwabu kázimbula kikuma kya yandi: "Yikala mona Pfumu tangwa dyosu ku thwala ya meni; kikuma ku kitata kyama kena ndangu yinikanaku.
ACT 2:26 Ihana ni mbundu yama yenina mu kyesi; amana ndinga zama zabasa mu kyesi kya lawu; lutu lwama phi lwazíngila mu kivuvu,
ACT 2:27 mukuma wayámbwadilaku moya wama mu kalunga, wayámbulaku lutu lwa musadi waku watoma lwavunda.
ACT 2:28 Wátsongila nzila za luzingu, yimóna mamboti ma lawu bwosu wakwataha kadiki ngeyi.
ACT 2:29 «Baphangi bama, yena yi muswa wa kuluzimbwala yi tsikiningi, mu mambu matadidi khaka wa betu Tavidi: yandi wáfwa, bámuzika; amana mazyamu mandi, yi lelu dyadi menina kwena betu.
ACT 2:30 Bwosu kákala mbikudi, wázaya phi ni Nzambi wázenga ndefi mu kuyadika mosi wa butuka dyandi ha kiti kya kipfumu kyandi.
ACT 2:31 Watekilalwa lota lufutumuku lwa Masiya amana wázonzilabwa, mu kuzimbula: "Bámuyambwadilaku mu kalunga, amana lutu lwandi lwávundaku."»
ACT 2:32 «Nzambi wámufutumuna ku lufwa, Yesu wuna yibati zonzila, amana betu boosu thwenina bambangi ba lufutumuku lwandi.
ACT 2:33 Bámutombula kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi, wátambula kwena Tata Kitembu Kyatoma kina kásila, amana wututyakidi mana lubati mona yi mana lubati yuka.
ACT 2:34 Mukuma yandi meni Tavidi kátombukaku ku zilu, kaasi kázonza bwabu: "Pfumu kázimbula kwena Pfumu wama: sikuka ku kitata kyama,
ACT 2:35 kilumbu yikuna yikitwala bambeni baku kidyatilu kya bitambi byaku."
ACT 2:36 Batu boosu ba Kiseledi bafweti zayabwa mboti-mboti ni Nzambi wámukitula Pfumu yi Masiya, Yesu wuna lwákhoka ha kitakani!»
ACT 2:37 Amana ku nima dya kuyuka bwabuna, mbundu zábalwala, bázimbula phi kwena Phetelu yi kwena bathumwa bahika: «Baphangi, biki twahanga si?»
ACT 2:38 Phetelu wubavutwadi: «Sobenu bikalulu, amana kosu mutu mu kati dya benu katambula mbotika mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu, kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu menu. Amana lwátambula kabu dya Kitembu Kyatoma.
ACT 2:39 Mukuma lusilu lwena kikuma kya benu yi kikuma kya bana benu yi kikuma kya boosu bana bena ku kyana, boosu bana katéla Pfumu Nzambi wetu.»
ACT 2:40 Amana Phetelu, mu ndinga za hika za lawu, kakala ta kimbangi yi kubaheka kikesa, mu kuzonza: «Dihululenu kwena mbandu yayi yátota nzila!»
ACT 2:41 Bana bakala kwikila mu ndinga zandi, bakala tambula mbotika. Muna kilumbu meni kina, batu, bela-bela yi mafunda ma tatu báyikama.
ACT 2:42 Boosu bakala sya ngolu mu kuhinikinaka malongi ma bathumwa, kuzingilaka mu kiphangi, mu kudyaka homa ha mosi yi kusambilaka homa hamosi.
ACT 2:43 Bweya bwakala mukwata kosu mutu, amana bidimbu bya khumbwa bya lwawu yi biphadi byákala hangama muna nzila ya bathumwa.
ACT 2:44 Batu boosu bákala yi lukwikilu, bakala zingila mu kimvuka, bima byosu phi bákala byawu mu kimvuka.
ACT 2:45 Bakala tekisa mafu yi bima bya bawu amana bakala dikabisila mbongu mu kati dya bawu boosu, bwosu buna wena mupfunu wa kosu mutu.
ACT 2:46 Kosu kilumbu, bakala vukana kuna nzu ya Nzambi, mu kimosi yi kudyaka mapha muna nzu, amana bakala dya bima bya bawu yi kyesi yi ngemba kuna mbundu.
ACT 2:47 Bakala kumisa Nzambi, batu boosu phi bákala yi kitya kikuma kya bawu. Amana kosu kilumbu, Pfumu, kakala yika batu muna kimvuka kya bawu, bana kakala hulula.
ACT 3:1 Amana Phetelu yi Yowani bakala tombuka ku nzu ya Nzambi mu tangwa dya bisambu (dyakala tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika).
ACT 3:2 Kinga bakala nata mutu mosi wákala yi khonzu tuka lubutuku lwandi, kakala wasikuka bilumbu byosu muna mwelu wa nzu ya Nzambi wuna bakala tela: «Mwelu wa kitoku», ndangu kalombaka kabu dya khenda kwena bana bakala kota mu nzu ya Nzambi.
ACT 3:3 Buna kámona Phetelu yi Yowani bakala kota mu nzu ya Nzambi, wábalomba kabu dya khenda.
ACT 3:4 Phetelu yi Yowani bámutala amana Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Tutala.»
ACT 3:5 Amana yandi wábatala yi kivuvu ni kima katambula kima kwena bawu.
ACT 3:6 Hanga Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Yeku yi phalata, keti wolu; kaasi kina yenina kyawu, yikuhekikya: mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu mwisi Nazaleti, telama amana kangala!»
ACT 3:7 Amana buna kámusimba kuna koku dya kitata, wámutelamisa. Muna mbala mosi kaka, bitambi byandi yi tsingini byázyama.
ACT 3:8 Wádithumba mbala mosi phi wekina mutendendi, wáyandika phi kukangala. Wákota kuna nzu ya Nzambi nzila mosi yi bawu. Kakala kangala, weka sotuka yi kuzatulaka Nzambi.
ACT 3:9 Batu boosu bámumona mu kukangala yi mu kuzatulaka Nzambi;
ACT 3:10 bakala muzaya ni yandi wuna wakala wasikuka ha Mwelu wa Kitoku wa nzu ya Nzambi, wakala lomba phi makabu ma khenda. Batu báyituka lawu, kikuma kya mana mámubwila.
ACT 3:11 Bwosu kányanginina kwena Phetelu yi Yowani, hanga batu boosu báyituki lawu, bénda thinu kuna bákala bawu, muna mbalanda yina bakala tela: «Mbalanda ya Solumoni.»
ACT 3:12 Tangwa kámona bwabuna, Phetelu wázimbula kwena batu bana: «Bisi Kiseledi, kikuma kya biki lubati yitwakila mu mambu mana? Biki lubati tutadila, hangambe ti betu tumukangadisi mutu yandu mu ngolu za betu-betu holo mu kukangama kwetu kwena Nzambi?
ACT 3:13 Nzambi wa Bulahami, Nzambi wa Yizaki, Nzambi wa Yakobi, Nzambi wa batata betu, yandi wuzatudi musadi wandi Yesu, wuna lwálambula, lwátuna phi benu-benu yi kuna thwala ya Philatu, kinga yandi mboti kázenga ni kamusula.
ACT 3:14 Benu lwámutuna wuna Watoma yi Wamasonga, hanga lulombini ni baluyambwadila ndwandwa mosi.
ACT 3:15 Amana wuna wáyandika luzingu, benu lwámuhondisa, kaasi Nzambi wámufutumuna ku bafwa; betu thwena bambangi ba mambu mana.
ACT 3:16 Amana mu lukwikilu lwa khumbu ya yandi meni, khumbu yandi yivutudi ngolu kwena mutu yandu lubati mona, luzayi phi; mu lukwikilu, mu khumbu ya Yesu, lumukodisi kimakulu ku thwala benu boosu.»
ACT 3:17 «Amana buthwena, baphangi bama, nzayi ni mu kukonda kwa kuzaya lwahangila mambu mana, phila mosi yi bapfumu benu.
ACT 3:18 Kaasi muna phila meni yina, yi mwamuna kálungisila, Nzambi, mambu mana kátekila samuna mu munwa wa bambikudi boosu ni Masiya wandi kanyókuka.
ACT 3:19 Ihana ni sobenu bikalulu byenu, bulukenu kwena Nzambi, ndangu masumu menu makumuka.
ACT 3:20 Yi bwana kalúhitikila, Pfumu, matangwa ma kulembwa, amana kahítika Yesu, Masiya wuna katekila sola ku thwala benu.
ACT 3:21 Yandi, wuna wáfwana ku kuzingila ku zilu tii yi kuna tangwa dina kayílulula Nzambi moosu mana kázimbula, tukidila thama, kwena bambikudi bandi ba Nzambi.
ACT 3:22 Moyize kázimbula bwabu: "Pfumu, Nzambi wenu, katélamisa kikuma kya benu, mbikudi mosi hanga meni, hana kati dya baphangi benu; lwamuyukidiki mu mambu moosu mana kakala luzimbwala.
ACT 3:23 Kaasi wuna wakonda mulemvukila mbikudi wuna, bamúzanga amana bamúkatula mu ndonga ya batu ba Nzambi.
ACT 3:24 Bambikudi boosu, yandikila kwena Samwela, yi bilandi byandi, bázonzila bilumbu bina amana básamunabya phi.
ACT 3:25 Benu, lwenina bana ba bambikudi yi muna bulunda buna káta Nzambi mu nzila ya batata benu mu kuzonza kwena Bulahami: "Mwena mosi wa butuka dyaku mwasákumukina bikanda byosu bya ha tsi."
ACT 3:26 Nzambi, kunima dya kulubula musadi wandi, kwena benu katekila muhitika, kikuma kya kulusakumuna, mu kukatula mosi-mosi wa benu ku mabanza mandi mambi.»
ACT 4:1 Tangwa bakala zonza, Phetelu yi Yowani, kwena batu, banganga Nzambi yi kaphita wa batsinzidi ba nzu ya Nzambi yi Basadise bátula.
ACT 4:2 Básidika mu kubamona, bathumwa bawu bodi, mu kulonga kwena batu yi mu kubasamwana kikuma kya Yesu, lufutumuku lwandi ha kati dya bafwa, mu kusongila ni kilumbu kimosi batu bafútumuka.
ACT 4:3 Hanga babakwati, babakotisi phi mu boloku muna phipa meni yana yi kuna kilumbu kyalanda, mukuma kuma kwayila kwákala.
ACT 4:4 Amana batu lawu hana kati dya bana bayuka malongi, hanga bakituki bakwikidi; amana thalu ya bayakala yátombuka bela-bela yi mafunda ma tanu.
ACT 4:5 Amana kilumbu kyalanda, bapfumu ba bawu yi bathwadisi ba nzu ya Nzambi yi balongi ba mitsiku bákutakana kuna Yelusalemi.
ACT 4:6 Hákala hika yi nganga Nzambi wa mbuta Ana yi Khayifu yi Yowani yi Lekizandi yi boosu bana bákala mu kikanda kya bambuta ba banganga Nzambi.
ACT 4:7 Amana buna bábanata Phetelu yi Yowani ku thwala ya bawu, bábahyula phi bwabu: «Mu ngolu za nati yi mu khumbu ya nati wuluhangidi bwabuna?»
ACT 4:8 Hanga Phetelu, wabasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma, wubazimbwadi: «Balemba yi bathwadisi ba nzu ya Nzambi:
ACT 4:9 batufundisidi lelu kikuma kya dyambu dya mboti dimosi tusadi kwena mukwa khonzu yi buna kabelukidi.
ACT 4:10 Zayenubwoku mboti, benu boosu, yi bisi Kiseledi ni mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu mwisi Nazaleti, wuna lwákhoka ha kitakani, amana Nzambi wámufutumuna ha kati dya bafwa, mwena yandi katelamini mutu yandu yi lutu lwa kitoku ku thwala ya benu.»
ACT 4:11 «Yandi: "Yi tadi dina lwálosa benu batungi ba nzu, amana dyákituka tadi dya sina dya mupfundila."»
ACT 4:12 «Luhulusu lweku mwena mutu wahika yuka ka mwena Yandi ku, mukuma mweku khumbu ya hika, mu sina dya zilu, yina bahana kwena batu yina tufwani twahulukila.»
ACT 4:13 Mu kumona kikumbwala kya Phetelu yi Yowani, báyituka lawu, mukuma bakala bazayila ni bawu batu bakonda longuka, bábakula phi ni babana bázinga yi Yesu.
ACT 4:14 Kaasi bwosu bakala mona, hana kabeta ka bawu, mutu wuna wábeluka, wutelamiki, bámonaku hika kima kya kuzonza.
ACT 4:15 Bábasenda batelama ha mbasi, amana báyandika kutendana bawu yi bawu,
ACT 4:16 yi kuzimbulaka: «Biki twabáhanga batu baba? Kikuma, batu boosu ba Yelusalemi bazayi ni kiphadi kyaki kya mbuta, mu nzila ya bawu kisalamini amana twalendakyoku mu kutuna.
ACT 4:17 Kaasi tubakandisenu ndangu dyambu dina diyalanganaku lawu ha kati dya batu, bazonziladyoku keti kwena mutu mosi mu khumbu yina.»
ACT 4:18 Amana bábatela, bábakandisa phi mu kuzonzila keti kulonga hika mu khumbu ya Yesu.
ACT 4:19 Kaasi Phetelu yi Yowani babavutwadi: «Bwalunga bwenina ku mesu ma Nzambi yukani twalemvukila benu hana tufwani kulemvukila Nzambi? Zengenu benu-benu.
ACT 4:20 Mukuma betu, tufwaniku kubusa kuzonzila mambu mana twámona yi mana twáyuka.»
ACT 4:21 Malemba bábayangisa hika kunima bábayambwadila, bámonaku phila ya kubahekila ndola; kikuma batu boosu Nzambi bakala zatula mu kumona mambu mana máluta.
ACT 4:22 Mukuma mutu wuna wábeluka mu kiphadi kina kákala yi mvula ziluti makumaya.
ACT 4:23 Kunima dya kubasula, Phetelu yi Yowani benda menika kwena banduku ba bawu mambu mana moosu bábazimbwala kwena malemba yi banganga Nzambi.
ACT 4:24 Buna báyuka bwabuna, boosu báthuta ndinga mu kimosi, kwena Nzambi amana bázimbula: «Mulongi, ngeyi wáhanga tsi yi zilu yi mayanga yi bina byosu byenamwa.
ACT 4:25 Ngeyi wázonza, mu ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma, mu munwa wa khaka wetu Tavidi musadi waku: "Kikuma kya biki bibati vwalanganina bikanda byosu? Amana kikuma kya biki batu bakasi mafwongu makonda kima?
ACT 4:26 Bakyamvu ba tsi batelami, amana bapfumu phi bakutakani kikuma kya kunwanisa Pfumu yi Kidisitu wandi."
ACT 4:27 Mukuma, mu kyedika, ni kikuma kya kunwanisa musadi waku watoma wuna wáyadika Yesu bakasidi fwongu Eloti yi Phosi Philatu mu mbanza yayi, kumosi yi makanda yi batu ba Kiseledi.
ACT 4:28 Kikuma kya kulungisa lwesi byosu bina wátekila zola mu ngolu zaku.
ACT 4:29 Amana buthwena, Pfumu, tala tsokisila za bawu amana hana ngolu kwena basadi baku mu kulonga malongi maku yi kikumbwala.
ACT 4:30 Lambula koku dyaku ndangu kubeluka kwakala, bidimbu bya khumbwa yi biphadi bya phila yi phila byamónika mu khumbu ya musadi waku watoma Yesu.»
ACT 4:31 Tangwa bálombila, homa hana bákala, háningana. Boosu bábasa yi Kitembu kyatoma, bakala longa phi ndinga ya Nzambi yi kikumbwala.
ACT 4:32 Kibuka kya batu bana bákwikila kyákala yi mbundu mosi yi moya mosi. Hákalaku mutu wakala zimbula ni bima byandi kikuma kya yandi buhika; kaasi kosu kima kyákala mu kimvuka.
ACT 4:33 Amana yi ngolu za lawu, bathumwa, bakala ta kimbangi kya lufutumuku lwa Pfumu Yesu; amana phi khenda za lawu zákala bawu boosu.
ACT 4:34 Amana ha kati dya bawu, ka mutu ku wákala yi mupfunu wa kima. Mukuma boosu bana bákala yi bilanga holo yi nzu, bakalabya tekisa, banati thalu yina bátekisila,
ACT 4:35 bazesibya muna malu ma bathumwa; amana bawu bakala kabisa kwena kosu mutu, bwosu bwákala mupfunu wandi.
ACT 4:36 Bwabuna Yozefu, wuna bakala tela Balanabasi kwena bathumwa, disongidila: «Mutu wisi hana kikesa», mulefi, mwisi Siphe,
ACT 4:37 wátekisa mafu mamosi mana kavwa, wánata makuta amana wásikulama muna malu ma bathumwa.
ACT 5:1 Kinga mutu mosi khumbu yandi Ananiya, yi Safila mukhetu wandi, wátekisa mafu ma bawu.
ACT 5:2 Wásweka ndambu yandi ya makuta, buna báyukana yi mukhetu wandi, amana wenda nata ndambu yina yásala, wásikulaya phi muna malu ma bathumwa.
ACT 5:3 Hanga Phetelu wumuhyudi: «Ananiya, kikuma kya biki kabasisidi Satana mbundu yaku ndangu wahuna Kitembu Kyatoma mu kusweka ndambu ya hika ya makuta mana wutekisidi kilanga?
ACT 5:4 Tangwa wúkadiki mawu, wufwanikiku waswekama? Ata tangwa mátekamiki, thalu ya makuta ma mawu yikadikiku mu hamu dya ngeyi? Kikuma kya biki wubanzidiki dyambu dya phila yina muna mbundu yaku? Wuhuniku kwena batu kaasi kwena Nzambi.»
ACT 5:5 Tangwa káyuka Ananiya bwabuna, wábwa, wáfwa phi. Amana bweya bwa lawu bwábakwata boosu bana báyukabwa.
ACT 5:6 Bangunza bátelama, bávungaya mvumbi ha muledi amana bámunata, bámuzika phi.
ACT 5:7 Kitesu kya matangwa matatu máhita, mukhetu wandi wákota, konda kuzaya mana mábwa.
ACT 5:8 Phetelu wumuhyudi: «Nzimbwala, mu thalu meni yina lutekisidiki kilanga?» Amana yandi wuvutudi: «Mu kyedika, muna thalu meni yina.»
ACT 5:9 Hanga Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Abweti lufwaniki kuyukana ndangu lwasokisila Kitembu kya Pfumu? Zayabwa ni bana bamuziki yakala dyaku, mu mwelu benina; bakúnata ngeyi phi.»
ACT 5:10 Muna tangwa meni dina, wábwa muna malu mandi wátabula phi. Mu kukota kwa bangunza, bámuwana watabula; bámunata, bámuzika phi hana kabeta ka yakala dyandi.
ACT 5:11 Amana Dibundu dyosu bweya bwábakwata lawu boosu bana báyuka mana maluta.
ACT 5:12 Biphadi yi bidimbu bya khumbwa bya lawu byákala hangama kwena batu ku moku ma bathumwa. Bakwikidi bakala kutakana boosu, yi mbundu yimosi muna mbalanda ya Solumoni.
ACT 5:13 Amana muna kati dya batu bahika, keti mosi kanyotaku kukhundakana kwena bawu; kaasi batu bakala bazola lawu.
ACT 5:14 Kaasi kosu tangwa batu bakala kwikila mwena Pfumu, lawu dya bakhetu yi bayakala bakala yikama ku dingumba.
ACT 5:15 Bakala nata bambefu muna mabala-bala; bakala balubula ha biphoyu yi thangi za bawu, ndangu Phetelu ha kahita, kininga kyandi kyafidinga ndambu batu hana kati dya bawu.
ACT 5:16 Batu lawu bátuka mu mbanza zina zákala bela-bela yi Yelusalemi, mu kunata bambefu yi batu bana bakala yangisa kwena bitembu bya mbi, boosu phi bakala beluka.
ACT 5:17 Amana bwosu bábasa yi kiphala, mbuta wa banganga Nzambi yi boosu bana bákala kumosi yi yandi, disongidila kibuka kya basadusi, bazodi bawakula.
ACT 5:18 Babakwatisi bathumwa, babakotisi phi mu boloku dya batu boosu.
ACT 5:19 Kaasi muna phipha, wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wáyafulula mwelu mya boloku amana wábalubula, wubazimbwadi:
ACT 5:20 «Alwenda, telamenu kuna nzu ya Nzambi, amana zimbulenu kwena batu mambu moosu mana matadidi luzingu lwalu lwa pha.»
ACT 5:21 Buna báyuka bwabuna, benda ku nzu ya Nzambi muna kati kya suka, báyandika phi kulonga. Mbuta wa banganga Nzambi yi bana bákala kumosi yi yandi bátula; bákutikisa malemba yi kimvuka kyosu kya bambuta ba bisi Kiseledi amana babatumi kusosa bathumwa muna boloku.
ACT 5:22 Kaasi batsinzidi mu kutula kwa bawu, bábawanamwoku mu boloku. Hanga bavutuki kwabawu, bahani phi meni dya bawu mu kuzimbula:
ACT 5:23 «Tuwani boloku dya kuphata buna bufwani; amana batsinzidi bazakala phi muna bifulu bya bawu kuna thwala mwelu. Kaasi tangwa tuyafuludi, tuwaniku keti mutu mosi mu kati.»
ACT 5:24 Buna báyuka bwabuna, bapfumu ba batsinzidi ba nzu ya Nzambi yi bambuta ba banganga Nzambi báyituka lawu kikuma kya dyambu dina, bakala dihyula keti bweti máhwila mambu mana.
ACT 5:25 Muna tangwa meni dina, mutu mosi wisa bazimbwala: «Batu bana lusiki mu boloku, kuna nzu ya Nzambi benina, babati longa phi batu.»
ACT 5:26 Hanga pfumu wa batsinzidi yi batsinzidi bendi basanda bathumwa. Bábanata konda kubayangisa, mukuma bweya bakala bwawu ni babahonda nana ku matadi kwena batu.
ACT 5:27 Tangwa bábanata, bábasya ku thwala kimvuka, amana mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wábasambisa.
ACT 5:28 Wuzimbudi: «Aketi tulukandisiki ni lulongilaku hika mu khumbu meni yina? Amana talenu buna lubasisi Yelusalemi mu malongi menu! Luzodi hika lwanokisina ha thandu ya betu, menga ma mutu wuna.»
ACT 5:29 Phetelu wávutula, kumosi yi bathumwa bahika: «Bulungi kulemvuka kwena Nzambi kaasi ka batu ku.
ACT 5:30 Nzambi wa batata betu wámufutumuna Yesu wuna lwáhondisa benu, mu kumukhoka ha kitakani.
ACT 5:31 Nzambi wámutombula kuna kitata kyandi, kakala Pfumu yi Muhuludi, ndangu kahana kwena Kiseledi kubalula kwa mbundu yi kuloluka kwa masumu.
ACT 5:32 Betu thwenina bambangi ba mambu mana, kumosi yi Kitembu Kyatoma kina kahana Nzambi kwena bana bisi mulemvukila.»
ACT 5:33 Amana bawu buna báyuka bwabuna, khabu zábakwata, bázola phi babahondisa.
ACT 5:34 Kaasi Mufwadisi mosi khumbu yandi Ngamadyedi, mulongi wa mitsiku wuna bakala zitisa lawu kwena batu, wátelama hana kati dya kimvuka, wásenda ni babalubula koma bathumwa.
ACT 5:35 Kunima wuzimbudi phi: «Bisi Kiseledi, kebenu kikuma kya mambu mana lwahánga kwena batu bana.
ACT 5:36 Mukuma mu mvula zilutuki, kátelamiki mutu mosi wukaditsikisa ni yandi lwesi, Thetasi; amana batu bela-bela yi khama ya bakotiki mu dingumba dyandi. Kaasi bamuhondikini, batu bana bakamulandaka, boosu bamwangalakani, keti kima kisadikihoku hika.
ACT 5:37 Ku manima ma yandi kutelamiki hika Yutasi mwisi Ngadidi, mu tangwa dya kusonikisa khumbu, amana batu ba lawu bamulandiki ku manima kaasi yandi phi wufwiki, batu boosu phi hangi bamwangalakaniki.
ACT 5:38 Amana buthwena, yibatibwa luzimbwala, lulandaku hika batu baba, bayambulenu phi benda. Yukani mu lukanu lwa batu holo tsadidi ya batu, lwatóta.
ACT 5:39 Kaasi yuka ni kwena Nzambi matuki mamana, lwalendaku kubatotisa. Kebenu, lwakota nana mu mvita yi Nzambi.» Bátambwasa dibanza dyandi.
ACT 5:40 Bábatela bathumwa, bababetisi phi, amana bababwisisi ni bazonzilaku hika mu khumbu ya Yesu, kunima bábasula.
ACT 5:41 Bathumwa bálubuka mu kimvuka kya mbuta, yi kyesi kyosu mu kumona ni Nzambi wubatambwasi ni bawu balungidi mu kulewuka kikuma kya Khumbu ya Yesu.
ACT 5:42 Kosu kilumbu, kuna nzu ya Nzambi yi kuna nzu za batu, bakalaku lembwa mu kulonga yi kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa Yesu wuna wenina Kidisitu.
ACT 6:1 Muna bilumbu bina, bwosu bakala vula balonguki, bayuta bana bakala zonza ndinga ya ngeleti bakala nyengalakana kikuma kya bayuta ba tsi yina: bakala zimbula ni kosu kilumbu, mu tangwa dya kukabisa madya, bafwidi ba bawu bakala balewula.
ACT 6:2 Hanga bawu Kumi yi bodi batedisi balonguki boosu, babazimbwadi: «Bulungiku ni twayambula kulonga ndinga ya Nzambi kikuma kya kusadila ku mesa.
ACT 6:3 Yihana ni, ba phangi, solenu bayakala tsambwadi hana kati dya benu, bisi tila kimbangi kya bukheti, bábasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma yi mudimu, amana twabáhekakya kina.
ACT 6:4 Amana betu twadihana lwesi mu lombilu yi kisalu kya Ndinga ya Nzambi.»
ACT 6:5 Dibanza dina dyásephidisa kibuka kyosu. Hanga basodi Kitsyeni, mutu wabasa yi lukwikilu yi Kitembu Kyatoma, Fidiphu, Phokolu, Nikanolu, Timoni, Phadimenasi yi Nikolasi wuna mwisi Atyoki wuna wákota mu dingumba dya Bayuta.
ACT 6:6 Benda basongila ku mesu ma bathumwa, bawu, kunima kulombila, bábasya moku.
ACT 6:7 Amana ndinga ya Nzambi yáyalangana kosu tangwa, thalu ya balonguki yakala vula tswasu ku Yelusalemi, amana mulumba-lumba wa banganga Nzambi ba bayuta bakala lemvuka ku lukwikilu mwena Yesu.
ACT 6:8 Kitsyeni wábasa yi makabu yi ngolu, kakala sala bidimbu bya khumbwa yi biphadi bya mbuta ha kati dya batu.
ACT 6:9 Kaasi bayakala bahika, bana bakala mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta yina bisi tela: «Ya bana balubuka mu kihika», yi bayuta ba mbanza za Sileni yi Alekizandi, yi bisi Sidisi yi bisi kinzunga kya Aziya báyandika kuyumana yi Kitsyeni.
ACT 6:10 Kaasi balendaku mu kumubedisa mukuma kakala zonza yi mudimu yi Kitembu.
ACT 6:11 Hanga bafuti batu bazimbula: «Tumuyukiki mu kuzonzila mambu mabati tukwana Moyize yi Nzambi!»
ACT 6:12 Babalundiki batu yi malemba yi balongi ba mitsiku; kunima bátula kuna kakala, bámukwata, bámunata phi mu kimvuka kya mbuta.
ACT 6:13 Amana báfwonda bambangi ba bukamvi bakala zimbula: «Mutu yandu kisiku yambula mu kuzonza ndinga zibati tukwana homa haha hatoma yi mitsiku mya Moyize.
ACT 6:14 Mukuma tumuyukiki kuzimbula ni Yesu, mwisi Nazaleti, kazánga homa haha, amana kabálumuna mikuku mina twatambula kwena Moyize.»
ACT 6:15 Hanga boosu bana bákala bazakala ha mbasi bakala mutala, bámona mbunzu yandi hanga yina ya wanzyo.
ACT 7:1 Mbuta wa banganga Nzambi wuzimbudi: «Buna babati zimbula kikuma kya ngeyi, bwa kyedika bwenina?»
ACT 7:2 Kitsyeni wávutula: «Baphangi bama yi batata bama hinikinenu! Nzambi wa khembu kádimonikisa kwena Bulahami, tata wetu, tangwa kákala ku Mezophotamiya, hana khaku kenda zakala ku Halani,
ACT 7:3 amana kámuzimbwala: "Katuka ku tsi yaku yi kikanda kyaku, awenda ku tsi yina yikúsongila."
ACT 7:4 Hanga wulubuki mu tsi ya bisi Kaditeni, wendi kala ku Halani. Kwakuna, kunima lufwa lwa tata wandi, Nzambi wamuhitisa mu tsi yayi lwisi kala buthwena.
ACT 7:5 Kámuhekaku keti kuvwa kumosi muna tsi meni yina, keti mafu ma kuthetika bitambi; kaasi kásila ni kamúhekama mafu yi kwena batekulu bandi kinga, muna tangwa meni dina, kákalaku kedi yi mwana.
ACT 7:6 Nzambi kázonza bwabu: "Kanda dyandi dyakádila mu kinzenza mu tsi ya kinzenza, bakwátadya mu kihika amana banyókunadya mu mvula khama ya.
ACT 7:7 Kaasi muna tsi yina yabákwata mu kihika, meni yifúndisaya, ku manima ma bwabuna, balúbuka amana bakwata tsambila ha kati dya homa haha."
ACT 7:8 Kunima Nzambi wáta bulunda yi Bulahami, amana mukhanda wenina kidimbu kya kuyukana; yihana kabutila Yizaki amana wámuyotisa mukhanda mu kilumbu kya nana; bwabuna káhanga Yizaki kwena Yakobi, amana Yakobi phi kwena bana bandi kumi yi bodi, bakhaka ba bikanda byetu.
ACT 7:9 Bakhaka betu, bana ba Yakobi, bámuyukila kiphala phangi wa bawu Yozefu amana bámutekisa ndangu bamunata ku Ngiphiti. Kaasi Nzambi kákala kumosi yi yandi;
ACT 7:10 amana wámutabula mu biwayi byandi kyosu, wámuheka phi khenda yi mudimu ku thwala Fwalawo kyamvu wa Ngiphiti, wuna wámuyadika pfumu mu Ngiphiti yi muna nzu yandi yosu.
ACT 7:11 Hanga nzala yifwebuki lawu mu Ngiphiti yosu yi muna tsi ya Kanana. Kiwayi lawu kyákala, amana bakhaka betu bakalaku mona keti kima kya kudya.
ACT 7:12 Yakobi, buna kayuka ni ngenza za bule zákala mu Ngiphiti, wátuma bakhaka betu mu mbala ya theti.
ACT 7:13 Amana mu mbala ya zodi, Yozefu wádizayikisa kwena baphangi bandi, kisina kya Yozefu phi kyázayakana kwena Fwalawo.
ACT 7:14 Kunima Yozefu wátuma benda musanda tata wandi Yakobi yi kikanda kyandi kyosu; batu makumi tsambwadi yi tanu bákala.
ACT 7:15 Yakobi wákulumuka ku Ngiphiti. Yi kwakuna káfwila yandi yi bakhaka betu.
ACT 7:16 Bábanata ku Sikemi amana bábazika muna mazyamu mana kásumba Bulahami yi mbongu kwena bana ba Amoni kuna Sikemi.
ACT 7:17 «Bwosu dyakala bwesuka tangwa dya lusilu luna kásila Nzambi kwena Bulahami, kanda dyávula lawu mu Ngiphiti,
ACT 7:18 yi kuna tangwa dina kisa yadila kyamvu wahika, mu Ngiphiti, wuna wakonda muzaya Yozefu.
ACT 7:19 Kyamvu meni wuna kakala huna kanda dyetu mu mayedi mambi, wábanyokuna bakhaka betu, wábadindamisa mu kulosa bana ba bawu ba lubutu ndangu bazingaku.
ACT 7:20 Muna tangwa meni dina yi mwamuna kábutuka Moyize, wuna wákala kitoku ku mesu ma Nzambi. Kátsatsuka ngonda tatu muna nzu ya tata wandi.
ACT 7:21 Buna bámuyanika, mwana ndumba wa Fwalawo wámutonguna, amana wámutsasa phi hanga mwana wandi.
ACT 7:22 Moyize katsasukila muna mudimu wosu za bisi Ngiphiti. Kákala yi hamu dya kuzonza yi muna mihangu myandi.
ACT 7:23 Buna kalungisa mvula makumaya, wábonga lukanu lwa kwenda kinda biwutu byandi, bisi kiseledi.
ACT 7:24 Buna kámona mutu mosi bakala yangisa, Moyize wámunwanina amana wávutula mbela ya mutu wuna bánwanisa; wámuhondyanga mwisi Ngiphiti.
ACT 7:25 Kabanza ni biwutu byandi babákula ni Nzambi wuzodi kabaheka luhulusu mu nzila ya yandi; kaasi bábakulabwoku.
ACT 7:26 Kilumbu kyalanda, wádimonikisa kwena bana bákala nwana, wuzodi ni kavutula ngemba ha kati kya bawu mu kuzimbula: "Lwenina baphangi, biki lubati nwanina benu yi benu?"
ACT 7:27 Kaasi wuna wakala yangisa mukwawu, hanga wumununguni Moyize amana wuzimbudi: "Nati wukusi pfumu yi zusi kwena betu?
ACT 7:28 Wuzodi waphonda bwosu wuhondiki mukolu mwisi Ngiphiti?"
ACT 7:29 Buna káyuka bwabuna, Moyize watina, wenda mu kinzenza muna tsi ya Madyani. Kwakuna, wabuta bana ba bayakala bodi.
ACT 7:30 «Buna zalunga mvula makumaya, wanzyo mosi wámumonikina, muna nganga yina ya mongu wa Sinayi, muna muleku wa mbawu hana kivunza.
ACT 7:31 Mu kumona bwabuna, Moyize wáyituka kikuma kya mbona mesu yina. Amana bwosu kakala bwesuka mu kutala, ndinga ya Pfumu yáyukalakana:
ACT 7:32 "Meni yenina Nzambi wa bakhaka baku, Bulahami, Yizaki yi Yakobi". Moyize kuna yi tsula, kálendaku mu kutala.
ACT 7:33 Pfumu wumuzimbwadi: "Womuna tsabatu zaku, mukuma homa haka wutelamiki, mena mafu matoma.
ACT 7:34 Mboni phasi za kanda dyama dyenina mu Ngiphiti, ngyuki bibimu bya bawu, khulumukini ndangu yibahulula. Buthwena awisa, yikútuma ku Ngiphiti."
ACT 7:35 «Moyize yandu básuwangana, mu kuzimbula: "Nati wukuyadikini pfumu yi zusi?", yandi wuna kátuma Nzambi hanga pfumu yi muhuludi, mu lusadisu lwa wanzyo wuna wámulubwakila ha kivunza kya mbawu.
ACT 7:36 Yandi wábalubula, wásala phi biphadi yi bidimbu bya phila yi phila mu tsi ya Ngiphiti, ku yanga dya Kabengi yi mu nganga, mu mvula makumaya.
ACT 7:37 Moyize meni wuna wázimbula kwena bisi Kiseledi: "Nzambi kalúhitika hana kati dya baphangi benu, mbikudi mosi hanga meni.
ACT 7:38 Mu lukutakanu, yandi wákala hakimosi yi wanzyo wuna wakala muzonzila ha mongu wa Sinayi yi bakhaka betu; kátambula ndinga za luzingu ndangu katuhekaza.
ACT 7:39 Bakhaka betu bábwisa kumulemvukila; kaasi bámusuwangana, yi sunga dya kuvutuka ku Ngiphiti.
ACT 7:40 Bazimbudi kwena Loni: "Tuyidikila banzambi bana bakala kwenda ku thwala betu, mukuma Moyize meni wawuna wátulubula mu tsi ya Ngiphiti, tuzayiku mana mamubwidi."
ACT 7:41 Muna bilumbu meni bina, báhala nzambi wa kiteki kya mwana wa ngombi, bámunatina phi mukhayilu wumosi amana báta mukinzi yi kihangwa kya moku ma bawu.
ACT 7:42 Kaasi Nzambi wábafwila kunda, wábayambula ni bafukamina bihangwa bya ku zilu, bwosu básonika mu mikanda mya bambikudi: "Kanda dya Kiseledi, kwena meni lwátambika bibulu yi makabu mahika mu mvula makumaya muna nganga?
ACT 7:43 Loni, kaasi sombolu dya nzambi wenu wa kiteki Moloki lwázangula yi katumbwa ka nzambi wenu wa kiteki Lefwani, bifwanisu meni bina lwáhala mu kubafukamina. Ihana ni yisenda ni balunata kyana kuluta mbanza ya Babiloni."»
ACT 7:44 «Muna nganga, bakhaka betu, bákala yi sombolu dya kimbangi, hanga dina kásongila Nzambi wuna wázonza kwena Moyize ni kayidika, bwosu kifwanisu kina kámona.
ACT 7:45 Sombolu meni dina báhanadya kwena bakhaka betu bana bálanda ku manima yi Yosuwe bákotisadya muna tsi ya makanda mana kákukwasa Nzambi ku thwala ya bawu. Dyásala hana tii yi kuna tangwa dya Tavidi.
ACT 7:46 Tavidi wámona khenda za Nzambi amana wálomba homa hamosi ndangu katungila nzu kikuma kya Nzambi wa Yakobi.
ACT 7:47 Kaasi Salomoni wámutungisila nzu.
ACT 7:48 Kaasi Kahungu kisiku zingila mu nzu zina bátunga mu moku ma batu. Bwosu kazonza mbikudi:
ACT 7:49 "Zilu dyenina kiti kya luyalu lwama, amana mafu menina kidyatilu kya bitambi byama. Khi nzu lwathúngila, kázimbula Pfumu, holo khi homa pfwani yilémbwila?
ACT 7:50 Ka koku dyama ku dyáhanga mana moosu?"
ACT 7:51 «Benu batu ba mutwa ngolu yi mbundu za matadi yi bizika matu, lwisi bwisa kaka Kitembu Kyatoma! Lwenina hanga bakhaka benu.
ACT 7:52 Khi mbikudi bákonda nyokuna bakhaka benu? Báhonda bana batekila samuna kukwisa kwa mutu wa masonga; wuna lwalambudi, buthwena, benu amana lumuhondi.
ACT 7:53 Benu lwátambula mitsiku mina báluheka banzyo kaasi, lwázitisamyoku!»
ACT 7:54 Buna bayuka mambu mana, bafunga khabu yi kukwekisaka menu kikuma kya Kitsyeni.
ACT 7:55 Kaasi yandi, wabasa yi Kitembu kyatoma, buna katala ku zilu, wámona khembu ya Nzambi; amana Yesu watelama kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi.
ACT 7:56 Wuzimbudi: «Mbati mona zilu dya kukangula yi Mwana wa mutu watelema kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi.»
ACT 7:57 Hanga bakalungi ngolu, baziki matu ma bawu, boosu bamubwidi;
ACT 7:58 bámubulumuna ku phenza ya mbanza amana báyandika kumuta matadi. Bambangi básisa miledi mya bawu kwena ngunza mosi, bakala tela Sawulu ndangu kasimbululakamya.
ACT 7:59 Kuna yi kumutimbwalaka matadi, Kitsyeni kakala lombila mu kuzimbula: «Pfumu Yesu, yamba moya wama!»
ACT 7:60 Kunima wábwa muna makungulu amana wákalunga: «Pfumu, wubafutisaku disumu dyadi!» Buna kázimbula bwabuna, wátabula.
ACT 8:1 Sawulu wátambwasa ni bamuhonda Kitsyeni. Yandika kilumbu meni kina, báyandika kunyokuna batu mu Dibundu dina dyákala ku Yelusalemi. Bakwikidi boosu bámwangana muna binzunga bya Yuteya yi Samadiya, katula lwesi bathumwa.
ACT 8:2 Kaasi batu bakwikama bámuzika Kitsyeni, bawu phi bámudila lawu.
ACT 8:3 Sawulu, yandi, kakala sanda kuzanga Dibundu; kakala kota muna nzu, mu kukwata bakhetu yi bayakala yi kubakotisaka mu boloku.
ACT 8:4 Batu bana bámwangana, bakala kwenda muma mwa phila yi phila yi kusamunaka Musamu wa Bukheti wa Ndinga ya Nzambi.
ACT 8:5 Fidiphu, yandi wákulunga ku mbanza ya Samadiya, wásamuna kwakuna Kidisitu.
ACT 8:6 Milumba-lumba mya batu, bázitama mu kuhinikinaka mana kakala zonza Fidiphu, mu kulonguka yi mu kumona bidimbu bya khumbwa bina kakala sala.
ACT 8:7 Mukuma bitembu bya mbi byákala lubuka mwena batu ba lawu yi kukalungaka, amana bakwa khonzu yi babana bawokumuka bákola.
ACT 8:8 Kyesi kya lawu kyákala muna mbanza meni yina.
ACT 8:9 Tuka thama, mutu mosi wákala muna mbanza meni yina, khumbu yandi Simoni. Kakala nika mikisi; kakala yitwakisa batu ku Samadiya amana yi kuditombulaka,
ACT 8:10 tukidila kwena bambuta yi kuna baleki, boosu bakala khundakana kwena yandi, yi kuzimbulaka: «Mutu yandu kenina ngolu za Nzambi, zina bisi tela: "Za mukwandi".»
ACT 8:11 Bakala bandakana kwena yandi kikuma kya buna kakala bayitwakisa, tuka thama, ku mikisi myandi.
ACT 8:12 Kaasi tangwa bákwikila mwena Fidiphu, wuna wakala basamwana Musamu wa Bukheti wa Kipfumu kya Nzambi yi mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu, yi bakhetu yi bayakala bátambula mbotika.
ACT 8:13 Simoni, yandi-meni wákwikila amana wátambula mbotika; kákala tangwa dyosu bela-bela yi Fidiphu amana kakala yituka lawu kikuma kya bidimbu bya khumbwa yi biphadi bya mbuta bina byákala hangama.
ACT 8:14 Bathumwa bana bakala ku Yelusalemi, tangwa báyuka ni bisi Samadiya batambwasiya ndinga ya Nzambi, hanga babahitiki Phetelu yi Yowani.
ACT 8:15 Phetelu yi Yowani buna bátula kwena bawu, bálombila kikuma kya bawu ndangu batambula Kitembu Kyatoma.
ACT 8:16 Mukuma yandu-yandu kabwilaku kedi keti mosi hana kati dya bawu; bátambula lwesi mbotika mu khumbu ya Pfumu Yesu.
ACT 8:17 Hanga Phetelu yi Yowani wubasi moku, amana bátambula Kitembu Kyatoma.
ACT 8:18 Tangwa kámona Simoni ni Kitembu kihanami kwena bakhidisitu, mu kusya kwa moku kwena bathumwa, kahanga wubanatini sunga dya mbongu
ACT 8:19 amana wuzimbudi: «Phekenu bawu hamu meni dyadi, ndangu kwena bana yisya moku, batambula Kitembu Kyatoma.»
ACT 8:20 Kaasi Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Mbongu zaku zazangana kumosi yi ngeyi meni, kikuma wubanzi ni wufwani kusumba kabu dya Nzambi yi mbongu!
ACT 8:21 Weku keti homa, keti muswa mu dyambu dyadi dyenina haha, mukuma mbundu yaku yeku yasungama ku thwala ya Nzambi.
ACT 8:22 Talulula hika dibanza dyaku dya mbi amana lombila Pfumu ndangu, yukani kazola, kalolula sunga dyaku dina dya mbi dyenina ku mbundu yaku.
ACT 8:23 Mukuma meni mboni ni ngeyi wenina wabasa yi mbundu ya kiphala amana wenina muhika wa masumu.»
ACT 8:24 Hanga Simoni wuzimbudi kwena Phetelu yi Yowani: «Bokwadilenu Pfumu kikuma kya meni, ndangu, muna mana luzimbudini, dimbwilaku keti dyambu dimosi.»
ACT 8:25 Ku manima ma kuta kimbangi yi kulonga ndinga ya Pfumu, bávutuka ku Yelusalemi, mu kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti muna mahata ma lawu ma Samadiya.
ACT 8:26 Wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wázimbula kwena Fidiphu: «Telama amana wenda ku banda, muna nzila yina yakulumuka tuka ku Yelusalemi yi kuna Ngaza.» Nzila meni yina bisiyoku lutila lawu.
ACT 8:27 Buna káyuka bwabuna, Phidiphu wátelama amana wenda. Muna nzila, wátundakana mutu mosi, mwisi Etsyophi, mutu meni wuna, yandi wákala pfumu wa mbuta, wisi sweka phi mbongu yi bima byosu bya Kandasi pfumu wa mukhetu wa Etsyophi; hana khaku kedi batundakana yi Fidiphu, kátekila kwisa ku Yelusalemi kikuma kya kufukamina Nzambi,
ACT 8:28 amana kakala vutuka ku nzu yandi, wazakala hana thandu ya mutukumbila wa phunda, yikutangaka mukanda wa mbikudi Yesaya.
ACT 8:29 Kitembu Kyatoma wázimbudi kwena Fidiphu: «Bwesuka amana wátundakana yi mutukumbila wa phunda wuna.»
ACT 8:30 Fidiphu wenda thinu amana wámuyuka mwisi Etsyophi buna kakala tanga mukanda wa mbikudi Yesaya. Yandi wumuzimbwadi: «Wubati bakisa mana wubati tanga?»
ACT 8:31 Yandi wuvutudi: «Abweti yilenda bakisa, yuka ni heku mutu wathendwadilawa?» Kahanga wumubokwadidi Fidiphu ni kazanza ndangu kazakala kumosi yi yandi.
ACT 8:32 Nzila ya Masonuku kakala tanga, yákala yayi: «Bakala munata hanga mukoku banati homa hana bisi bakila mbisi, hanga mwana wa mukoku kisiku meka ku thwala ya wuna wisi mukulula mwika. Kayakudiku keti ndinga.
ACT 8:33 Muna kulewuka kwandi, bábwisa kumunungisa. Nati wálenda mu zonzila kilumbu butuka dyandi? Kikuma luzingu lwandi bákatulalwa ha tsi.»
ACT 8:34 Mwisi Etsyophi wáhyula kwena Fidiphu: «Yikubokwadidi, nzimbwala bawu: kikuma kya nati kabati zonzila mbikudi bwabuna? Kikuma kya yandi meni ho kikuma kya mutu wahika?»
ACT 8:35 Fidiphu wátambula ndinga amana, muna nzila meni yayina ya Masonuku, wáyandika mu kumusamwana Musamu wa Bukheti wa Yesu.
ACT 8:36 Kinzila-kinzila, bátula homa hamosi hakala yi mamba, mutu wuna wázimbula kwena Fidiphu: «Tala mama mamba; biki bikhwati mu kubotama?» [
ACT 8:37 Fidiphu wumuzimbwadini: «Yukani wakwikila yi mbundu yaku yosu, wufwani mu kubotama.» Yandi wuvutudini: «Khwikidini ni Yesu Kidisitu, Mwana wa Nzambi.»]
ACT 8:38 Wásenda mu kutelamisa mutukumbila wa phunda, bákulumuka bawu bodi muna mamba, Fidiphu yi mwisi Etsyophi, amana wámubotika.
ACT 8:39 Ha bálubuka mu mamba, Kitembu kya Pfumu kyámutombula Fidiphu. Mwisi Etsyophi wuna kamumonaku hika, kahanga wusimbi nzila wenda yi kyesi kyosu.
ACT 8:40 Fidiphu, yandi, wisa monikina mu mbanza ya Azoti, kakala samuna Musamu wa Bukheti muna mbanza zoosu muna kakala luta, yi kuna katudila ku Sezale.
ACT 9:1 Muna tangwa meni dina, Sawulu kakalaku lembwa mu kuheyisa balonguki ba Pfumu. Wenda kwena mbuta wa banganga Nzambi,
ACT 9:2 amana wámulomba mikanda kikuma kya nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta muna mbanza ya Tamasi, kinga kawanakwa ndambu ya batu, bayakala holoni bakhetu, bana bakala landa nzila ya Pfumu, kamana bakwata amana kabanata ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 9:3 Buna kakala muna nzila ya Tamasi, hana wekatula bela-bela yi mbanza meni yina, muna kithulumukina, mutsyenzya wumosi wátuka ku zilu, wákenzula hosu hana kákala yandi.
ACT 9:4 Wábwa ha tsi amana wáyuka ndinga yimosi yakala muzimbwala: «Sawulu, Sawulu, biki wubati ngyangisila?»
ACT 9:5 Yandi wávutula: «Nati wenina, Pfumu?» Yandi wuvutudi: «Meni, yenina Yesu wuna wubati yangisa.
ACT 9:6 Kaasi telama, kota muna mbanza amana bakúzimbwala buna wufwani mu kuhanga.»
ACT 9:7 Batu bana kakala kangala bawu, bátelama konda kuyakula; bakala yuka ndinga kaasi bakalaku mona mutu.
ACT 9:8 Sawulu wávumbuka mu mafu, mbatanana kákala ku mesu watemuna, kakalaku mona keti kima. Hanga bamusimbi kuna koku, bámunata ku mbanza Tamasi.
ACT 9:9 Kánanga bilumbu bitatu konda kumona, konda kudya keti kunwa kima.
ACT 9:10 Kinga kuna Tamasi kwákala yi mulonguki mosi khumbu yandi Ananiya. Pfumu kámulubwakila muna mbona mesu amana kámuzimbwala: «Ananiya!» Yandi wávutula: «Awu meni, Pfumu.»
ACT 9:11 Pfumu wumuzimbwadi: «Ndawenda muna mukhidi wuna bisi tela ni Wasingama, amana sanda muna nzu ya Yutasi, mutu mosi, khumbu yandi Sawulu mwisi Talasi. Mukuma mu kulombila kenina
ACT 9:12 amana kámoniki muna mbona mesu, mutu mosi khumbu yandi Ananiya wákota amana wámuthetika moku ndangu kamona hika.»
ACT 9:13 Ananiya wávutula: «A Pfumu, batu balawu yíyuka kuzonzila mutu wuna, bánzimbwala mbi yosu yina káhanga kwena batu ba Nzambi baku kuna Yelusalemi.
ACT 9:14 Amana kisini kwaku yi muswa wa bambuta ba banganga Nzambi mu kukwata batu boosu bana batéla khumbu yaku.»
ACT 9:15 Kaasi Pfumu wumuzimbwadi: «Awenda, mukuma, mutu wuna, yimusodi hanga kilekwa mu kunata khumbu yama kwena makanda, kwena bakyamvu yi kwena bisi Kiseledi.
ACT 9:16 Yimúsongila meni-meni moosu mana kafwani kunyokwakina mu khumbu yama.»
ACT 9:17 Hanga Ananiya wendi, wákota muna nzu, wámusya moku amana wázimbula: «Phangi wama Sawulu, Pfumu Yesu, wuna wukulubwakidiki mu nzila yina wukakwisilaka, káthumini ndangu wamona hika, amana wabasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma.»
ACT 9:18 Muna mbala mosi, mwábwa, muna mesu mandi, bima hanga bibalaka, amana wáyandulula mu kumona. Wátelama, wátambula phi mbotika.
ACT 9:19 Amana ku manima ma kubotama, wádya, wávutwakila phi ngolu. Sawulu wánanga hika ndambu ya bilumbu kumosi yi balonguki bana bakala ku Tamasi.
ACT 9:20 Amana muna mbala mosi wándika mu kusamuna muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta ni Yesu kenina Mwana wa Nzambi.
ACT 9:21 Boosu bana bakala muyuka, báyituka, bakala zimbula: «Ka yandi ku wuna wakala nyokuna batu, ku Yelusalemi, bana bakala tela khumbu yina? Amana, kisiku haka kikuma kya kubakwata amana kabanata ku thwala ya bambuta ba banganga Nzambi?»
ACT 9:22 Kaasi Sawulu, yandi, hamu dyámulutakana kuluta Bayuta bana bakala zingila ku Tamasi kikuma bamonaku kima kya kumuvutwala, kakala basongila yi ngolu ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu.
ACT 9:23 Kunima ya ndambu ya bilumbu, Bayuta báyukana mu kumuhondisa,
ACT 9:24 hanga Sawulu yandi bamulukisi mu kifwandu kya bawu. Phipha, mwini, bawu bakala kengila mwelu myosu mina bakala kotila yi kulubwakila ku mbanza ndangu balenga muhondisila Sawulu.
ACT 9:25 Kaasi, muna phipha, balonguki bandi bámusya mu kitunga amana bámukulumuna yi kuna phenza ya kibaka kya luphangu.
ACT 9:26 Buna kátula ku Yelusalemi, Sawulu kameka kukota mu ndonga ya balonguki, kaasi boosu bweya bakala bwawu kikuma kya yandi, kikuma bákwikilaku ni yandi phi mu kyedika mulonguki kakala.
ACT 9:27 Hanga Balanabasi wumubongi, wámunata kwena bathumwa amana wábatendwala buna kámona, Sawulu, Pfumu muna nzila yi mana kámuzimbwala Pfumu. Wubatendwadi hika phila yina kalongila yi tsikiningi yosu malongi mu khumbu ya Yesu, ku Tamasi.
ACT 9:28 Tukidila tangwa meni dina, Sawulu kakala kwenda yi kuvutuka ku Yelusalemi kumosi yi bawu mu kulonga yi tsikiningi khumbu ya Pfumu.
ACT 9:29 Kakala solula phi yi bayuta bana bakala zonza ndinga ya ngeleti, kufindaka phaka yi bawu; kaasi bawu bakala sanda ni bamuhondisa.
ACT 9:30 Baphangi buna báyuka bwabuna, bámusindikila yi kuna Sezale amana bámuhitika ku Talasi.
ACT 9:31 Dibundu mu ngemba dyákala mu Yuteya dyosu, mu Ngadidi yi mu Samadiya; dyakala tungama yi kuzingila mu bweya bwa Pfumu amana dyakala vula mu lusadisu lwa Kitembu Kyatoma.
ACT 9:32 Phetelu yandi kakala kangala mu binzunga byosu. Kilumbu kimosi, wákulumuka phi kwena bakwikidi bana bakala ku mbanza ya Dita.
ACT 9:33 Káwana kwakuna mutu mosi, khumbu yandi Eneyi, wakala walandalala hana thangi tukidila mvula nana mukuma kikata kákala.
ACT 9:34 Phetelu wumuzimbwadi: «Eneyi, Yesu Kidisitu wukubeludi! Telama amana yidika ngeyi-meni thangi yaku.» Muna mbala mosi, wátelama.
ACT 9:35 Boosu bana bákala ku Dita yi Salo bámona amana bábalumuna mbundu za bawu kwena Pfumu.
ACT 9:36 Mulonguki wa mukhetu mosi wakala ku Zophe, khumbu yandi Tabita, disongidila: «Tolukasi,» disongidila: «tsetsi». Kakala sala mihangu mya mboti lawu yi lusadisu kwena baphutu.
ACT 9:37 Muna bilumbu meni bina, kahanga wubedi amana wufini. Ku nima kusukula lutu lwandi, basikulalwa kuna mwanza wa ku zilu dya nzu.
ACT 9:38 Balonguki ba ku Zophe, bwosu báyuka ni Phetelu ku Dita kenina, dyenina bela-bela yi Zophe, hanga batumini batu bodi benda mubokwadila bwabu: «Wuzingidilaku mu kukwenda kwena betu.»
ACT 9:39 Phetelu wátelama amana wenda yi bawu. Buna kátula, bámuzanzisa yi kuna mwanza wa ku zilu. Bafwidi boosu bábwesuka kwena yandi mu kudila; bakala musongila miledi yi mizaka mina kakala tunga Tolukasi tangwa kákala kumosi yi bawu.
ACT 9:40 Phetelu wálubula batu boosu, kunima wafukama amana wálombila. Ku nima wabaluka kuna kwakala lutu amana wuzonzi: «Tabita telama!» Hanga mukhetu wutemuni mesu, amana buna kamona Phetelu, wasikuka.
ACT 9:41 Yandi wámulambwala koku amana wámutelamisa. Ku manima wátela bakwikidi yi bafwidi, wábasongila yandi, Tabita, yi moya.
ACT 9:42 Tsangu záyalangana mu Zophe dyosu, batu lawu phi bákwikila mwena Pfumu.
ACT 9:43 Wánangakwa hika kuna Zophe ndambu ya bilumbu, kwena mutu mosi, Simoni muyidiki wa mikanda mya bambisi.
ACT 10:1 Kwákala kuna mbanza ya Sezale, yi mutu mosi khumbu yandi Kodineyi, satudiyoni, muna kibuka kina bakala tela: «baphumbulu ba Kitadi.»
ACT 10:2 Mutu meni wuna kákala mutu wakwikama. Yandi yi nzu yandi yosu kakala zitisa Nzambi. Kakala hana makabu ma kihomba lawu kikuma kya batu yi kulombilaka Nzambi kosu tangwa.
ACT 10:3 Kilumbu kimosi, muna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika, hanga mu mbona mesu, kámona wengele. Wanzyo mosi wa Nzambi wákota muna nzu yandi amana wumuzimbwadi: «Kodineyi!»
ACT 10:4 Yandi wumutadi swii yi kadingu-dingu kamukwati amana wumuzimbwadi: «Biki, Pfumu?» Wanzyo wumuvutwadi: «Nzambi wutambudi bisambu byaku yi makabu maku ma kihomba kwena baphutu amana kakuzimbakaniku.
ACT 10:5 Buthwena bwabu, tuma bayakala kuna Zophe amana mutedisa mutu mosi, Simoni, bisi tela: Phetelu.
ACT 10:6 Yandi kuna nzu ya Simoni mukwawu, muyidiki wa mikanda mya bambisi, kisi nimba, nzu yandi yenina ku kabeta ka yanga.»
ACT 10:7 Buna kenda wanzyo wuna wámuzonzisa, Kodineyi wátuma basadi bandi bodi yi phumbulu mosi wuna wakakala zitisa Nzambi hana kati dya baphumbulu bana bakala bela-bela yi yandi.
ACT 10:8 Buna kábamenika moosu, wábatuma ku Zophe.
ACT 10:9 Kilumbu kyalanda, bwosu bákala muna nzila amana bátula bela-bela yi mbanza, Phetelu wázanza hana mudilu wa nzu, mu kati kya mwini, kikuma kya kulombila.
ACT 10:10 Wáyuka nzala amana wásanda kadya. Buna bakala mulambila bima, wámona mbona mesu.
ACT 10:11 Kámona zilu dyakanguka amana kima kimosi hanga kitemba kyambuta kya muledi, kyakala tuluka, bázitikila mu tsongi ya, amana kyáthetama yi hana tsi.
ACT 10:12 Amana mwamuna, mwákala yi bambisi ba malu maya boosu, yi bina bisi landanda mu mafu yi banuni ba ku zilu.
ACT 10:13 Ndinga mosi yimuzimbwadi: «Telama, Phetelu, honda amana wadya!»
ACT 10:14 Amana Phetelu wuzimbudi: «Loni, Pfumu, khaku kedi ndya kima kya khengu, keti kya mukuku.»
ACT 10:15 Ndinga yáyukalakana hika mu mbala ya zodi: «Kina kasemisi Nzambi, ngeyi wumonakyoku mvindu.»
ACT 10:16 Bwabuna bwásalama mbala tatu, kunima kitemba kyátombuka ku zilu.
ACT 10:17 Phetelu, mabanza mámuvwalangana, wáyandika mu kudihyula keti biki disongidila dya mbona mesu yina kámona. Kutala, batu bana bátuma kwena Kodineyi, bakala hyula nzu ya Simoni, bátula muna mwelu.
ACT 10:18 Hanga bátela amana báhyula: «Kwaku kisi nimba, Simoni wuna bisi tela Phetelu»
ACT 10:19 Phetelu buna kakala banza hika mbona mesu yina, Kitembu Kyatoma wámuzimbwala: «Tala batu batatu babati kusanda.
ACT 10:20 Telama, tuluka amana awenda yi bawu konda keti-keti, mukuma meni yibatumi.»
ACT 10:21 Phetelu wátuluka amana wábazimbwala batu bana: «Meni yandu lubati sanda. Biki lwisidi haka?»
ACT 10:22 Bávutula: «Satudiyo Kodineyi, wututumi. Mutu walungila, kisi zitisa Nzambi. Amana kanda dyosu dya Bayuta dyisi mutambwasa. Wanzyo mosi watoma kámuzimbwadiki ni kakutedisa kuna nzu yandi ndangu kayuka buna wenina bwawu mu kumuzimbwala.»
ACT 10:23 Phetelu wábakotisa amana wábayamba phipha meni yana. Kilumbu kyalanda, wásimba nzila amana wenda hakimosi yi bawu. Baphangi bahika ba ku Zophe benda basindikila.
ACT 10:24 Kilumbu kyalanda, Phetelu wátula ku Sezale. Kodineyi kakala bahingila amana wátedisa kuna nzu yandi biwutu byandi yi banduku bandi.
ACT 10:25 Buna kátula Phetelu, Kodineyi wenda mukhikila, wábwa muna malu mandi amana wámufukamina.
ACT 10:26 Kaasi Phetelu kámutelamisa, mu kuzimbula: «Telama, mukuma meni phi mutu yenina hanga ngeyi.»
ACT 10:27 Kuna yi kuyambilaka yi yandi, wákota amana káwana lawu dya batu bana bisa khokana.
ACT 10:28 Kábazimbwala: «Luzayi ni mitsiku myetu myisiku tambwasa ni Muyuta mosi kadikasa yi munzenza kondilo kukota mu nzu yandi. Kaasi Nzambi kátsongidiki ni pfwaniku yimona mutu hanga wuna wakonda lunga kondilo wakuhunga.
ACT 10:29 Yihana ni tangwa lutumiki mutu mu kuthela, yisiki konda tendu. Nzodi yizaya keti kikuma kya biki luthedisidiki.»
ACT 10:30 Kodineyi wuzimbudi: «Bilumbu bitatu kedi bilutini tukidila buna yikala lombila kuna nzu yama, muna tangwa dya tatu dya masikidika, muna mbala mosi, kutala mutu mosi yi miledi mya katoki myakala kedyamina, wuthelamini kuna thwala,
ACT 10:31 amana wunzimbwadini: "Kodineyi, Nzambi wutambudi lombilu lwaku yi makabu maku ma kihomba kwena baphutu.
ACT 10:32 Tuma mutu kuna Zophe mu kutedisa Simoni wuna bisi tela Phetelu. Yandi kisi nimba muna nzu ya Simoni, muyidiki wa mikanda mya bambisi, kuna kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta."
ACT 10:33 Muna mbala mosi, yikutumini bayakala bamosi, amana wutambwasi mu kukwisa. Buthwena bwabu, ku thwala ya Nzambi thwenina betu boosu, kikuma kya kuyuka moosu mamana kakulongikidi Pfumu mu kutuzimbwala.»
ACT 10:34 Phetelu wátambula ndinga amana wuzimbudi: «Mu kyedika, mbakudi ni Nzambi kisiku yekula.
ACT 10:35 Kaasi muna kanda dyosu, wuna wisi muzitisa yi kusadila masonga, kisi mutambwasa.
ACT 10:36 Káhitika ndinga kwena bisi Kiseledi, mu kubasamwana Musamu wa Bukheti wa ngemba mu nzila ya Yesu Kidisitu, yandi wenina Pfumu wa boosu.
