ACT 10:37 Benu, luzayi mana mábwa mu Yuteya dyosu, tukidila ku luyandiku muna Ngadidi, kunima mbotika yina kásamuna Yowani.
ACT 10:38 Luzayi buna káfwebula Nzambi ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma kwena Yesu mwisi Nazaleti. Mwosu muna kakala hita, kakala hanga makheti yi kubuka boosu bana bákala mu kihika kya kiphidi-mutu, mukuma Nzambi kákala kumosi yi yandi.
ACT 10:39 Amana betu, thwenina bambangi ba mambu moosu mana káhanga mu tsi ya Bayuta yi kuna Yelusalemi. Wuna báhonda mu kumukhoka hana kitakani.
ACT 10:40 Kaasi, Nzambi wámufutumuna mu kilumbu kya tatu; yandi wámulubula ndangu bamumona,
ACT 10:41 heku ni kwena kanda dyosu, kaasi kwena bambangi bana katekila sola Nzambi yi kwena betu bana twádya amana twánwa kumosi yi yandi ku manima ma kufutumuka kwandi ha kati dya bafwa.
ACT 10:42 Amana wátutuma mu kusamuna kwena kanda yi kuta kimbangi ni yandi wuna katekila sola Nzambi zusi dya batu bana bisi zinga yi bana bafwa.
ACT 10:43 Bambikudi boosu bisi ta kimbangi ni wosu wuna wukwikidi mwena yandi, muna khumbu yandi, wutambudi ndoluka ya masumu.»
ACT 10:44 Buna kakala zonza Phetelu bwabuna, Kitembu Kyatoma kyábakulumukina batu boosu bana bakala hinikina Ndinga yandi.
ACT 10:45 Bakwikidi boosu ba bayuta bana bísa kumosi yi Phetelu, báyituka lawu mu kumona kabu dya Kitembu Kyatoma kukulumuka kwena baphani.
ACT 10:46 Mukuma bakala bayuka batu bana mu kuzonza mu ndinga zina bakondi zaya, yi kuzatulaka kineni kya Nzambi. Hanga Phetelu wuzonzi:
ACT 10:47 «Tufwani mu kukandikisa mbotika kwena batu bana, bawu batu batambudi Kitembu Kyatoma hanga betu?»
ACT 10:48 Wásenda ni babotika mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu. Hanga bamulombi ni kananga hika ndambu ya bilumbu kwakuna.
ACT 11:1 Bathumwa yi baphangi bana bakala mu Yuteya báyuka ni baphani, bawu phi bátambudiki ndinga ya Nzambi.
ACT 11:2 Buna kátombuka Phetelu ku Yelusalemi, bakwikidi ba bayuta báyandika mu kumuyumanisa:
ACT 11:3 mu kuzimbula: «Wúkotiki mu nzu ya batu bana bakonda yotisa amana wúdiki homa hamosi yi bawu!»
ACT 11:4 Hanga Phetelu wuyandiki mu kubatendwadila yi tsikiningi mana máluta. Wubazimbwadi:
ACT 11:5 «Meni, ku mbanza ya Zophe yikadi mu kulombila, tangwa mbonikini mbona mesu: kima kimosi kyakala kulumuka, hanga kitemba kyambuta kya muledi, kyakuzitikila muna tsongi ya, kyakala kulumuka tukidila ku zilu amana kyisi yi hana yíkala meni.
ACT 11:6 Mu kusimbululakya, mboni ni hákala yi bambisi ba malu maya ba ha tsi yi bambisi ba mu musitu yi bana bisi landanda yi banuni ba ku zilu.
ACT 11:7 Kunima ngyuki ndinga mosi yánzimbwala: "Telama, Phetelu, honda amana dya!"
ACT 11:8 Hanga mvutudi: "Yilendaku, Pfumu, khaku kedi mukota kima kyasumuka, keti kya tsiku muna munwa wama."
ACT 11:9 Mu mbala yazodi, ndinga yátuka tukidila ku zilu yinzimbwadi: "Kina kasemisi Nzambi, ngeyi wumonakyoku mvindu."
ACT 11:10 Bwabuna bwásalama mbala tatu, ku manima byosu byávutuka ku zilu.
ACT 11:11 Muna tangwa meni dina, bayakala bamosi batatu bana báthumina ku Sezale, bátula hana thwala ya nzu yina twákala.
ACT 11:12 Kitembu kinzimbwadi ni yenda yi bawu konda keti-keti. Baphangi basambanu baba lubati mona benda tsindikila, amana twákota muna nzu ya mutu meni wuna.
ACT 11:13 Yandu-yandu wátumenika buna kámonika wanzyo muna nzu yandi, mu kuzimbula: "Tuma mutu kuna Zophe, kenda mutela Simoni wuna bisi tela Phetelu,
ACT 11:14 Yandi wakúzimbwala ndinga mwena zina wahúlwakila, ngeyi yi nzu yaku yosu."
ACT 11:15 Buna yíyandika mu kuzonza, Kitembu Kyatoma kikulumukini, kwena bawu bwosu kyakulumuka kwena betu ku luyandiku.
ACT 11:16 Hanga ngyubuki ndinga yina kázonza Pfumu: "Yowani kábotika yi mamba, kaasi benu, lwatámbula mbotika ya Kitembu Kyatoma."
ACT 11:17 Amana yuka ni Nzambi kabahangila kabu dimosi yi betu kikuma kya buna twákwikila mwena Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu. Nati yenina meni mu kukakidila Nzambi?»
ACT 11:18 Kunima kuyuka bwabuna, bádibata amana bámuzatula Nzambi, mu kuzimbula: «Nzambi wáhana phi kwena Baphani tsobuka ya bikalulu yina yisi nata ku luzingu lwa mukwandi.»
ACT 11:19 Bana bámwangalakana kikuma kiwayi kina kyákala kunima lufwa lwa Kitsyeni, báhitila ku Fenisi, ku Siphe yi ku Atyoki, kaasi bakalaku longa batu bahika, kwena Bayuta lwesi.
ACT 11:20 Kinga, hana kati dya bawu, hákala yi bakwikidi bahika bisi Siphe yi bisi Sileni, bisa ku Atyoki amana bakala zonzila kwena baphani ba ndinga ya ngeleti yi kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa Pfumu Yesu.
ACT 11:21 Koku dya Pfumu dyákala kumosi yi bawu, amana batu balawu bákwikila, bábalula phi mbundu za bawu kwena Pfumu.
ACT 11:22 Musamu wátula kwena Dibundu dya Yelusalemi. Amana bátuma Balanabasi ndangu katula yi kuna Atyosi.
ACT 11:23 Mu kutula kwandi, buna kámona mamboti ma Nzambi, wásangwala lawu, wábaheka kikesa boosu ndangu bakangama kwena Nzambi yi mbundu yimosi.
ACT 11:24 Mukuma kákala mutu wa bukheti, wabasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma yi lukwikilu. Hanga mulumba-lumba wa batu balawu bákhundakana kwena Pfumu.
ACT 11:25 Kunima, wénda sanda Sawulu ku Tadisi.
ACT 11:26 Kunima dya kumusengumuna, wámunata ku Atyosi. Banangi kwakuna mvula muthu, mu kuwaphama mu lukutakanu lwa Dibundu amana bakala longa mulumba-lumba wa batu balawu. Balonguki, ku Atyosi bábongilaya khumbu ya bakidisitu, mu mbala ya theti.
ACT 11:27 Muna bilumbu meni bina, bambikudi bamosi bákulumuka tukidila ku Yelusalemi yi kuna Atyosi.
ACT 11:28 Mosi hana kati dya bawu, khumbu yandi Hakabusi, kátelama amana wásamuna mu ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma ni nzala ya lawu yakóta mu tsi yosu ya bisi Loma. Nzala yákota, muna tangwa dina kákala Koloti pfumu wa mbuta wa mbanza.
ACT 11:29 Hanga balonguki babongi dibanza dya kuhitika lusadisu, kosu mutu muna kitesu kya kuvwa kwandi, kwena baphangi bana bakala zingila ku Yuteya.
ACT 11:30 Bwabuna bahanga amana báhitikalwa kwena bambuta ba dibundu mu nzila ya Balanabasi yi Sawulu.
ACT 12:1 Muna tangwa meni dina, kyamvu Eloti wáyandika kuyangisa ndambu ya baphangi ba Dibundu.
ACT 12:2 Kamuhondisa Zyaki phangi wa Yowani ku mbedi ya phoku.
ACT 12:3 Mu kumona ni mambu mana mábasephidisa Bayuta, wábonga dibanza dya kumukwatisa phi Phetelu. Máluta mu tangwa dya mukinzi wa mapha makonda muvimbu.
ACT 12:4 Kunima dya kumukwata yi kumukotisa mu boloku, wámulambula mu moku ma bibuka biya bya baphumbulu ndangu bamukengilaka. Yandi yi mabanza ma kumusambisa ha mesu ma batu ku manima ma mukinzi wa Phaki.
ACT 12:5 Amana Phetelu kákala wakukwata muna boloku kaasi dibundu dyakala lombila Nzambi, kikuma kya yandi konda kulembwa.
ACT 12:6 Muna phipha, kinga Eloti kákala yi sunga dya kamusambisa mu mwini, ku mesu ma batu, Phetelu wakukasa mu miyololu myodi, wanimba hana kati dya baphumbulu bodi. Ku mwelu batsinzidi bamosi bakala tanikina boloku.
ACT 12:7 Muna mbala mosi, wanzyo wa Pfumu wísa, mitsyenzya mikenzudi suku. Wanzyo mosi wámutokamisa Phetelu mu kumutekula muna luhati ndangu kamutokamisa, amana wumuzimbwadi: «Telama tswatsu!» Miyololu myáwongumuka mu moku mandi.
ACT 12:8 Wanzyo wámuzimbwala: «Vwata mukaba waku amana zitika tsabatu zaku.» Phetelu wusadi bwabuna, ku manima Wanzyo wumuzimbwadi: «Vwata muzaka waku amana ndanda.»
ACT 12:9 Phetelu wálubuka mu kumulanda. Kakalaku zaya ni lusadisu lwa wanzyo lwa kyedika lwakala; kábanza ni mbona mesu.
ACT 12:10 Buna báluta mukanzu watheti yi wazodi, bátula ku mwelu wa bisengu wuna walubwakila ku mbanza. Wádikangwakila wawu-meni kuna thwala ya bawu, bálubuka amana bakala phusana muna balabala dimosi, kutala, wanzyo wutoti.
ACT 12:11 Buna kadibakisa, Phetelu wuzimbudi: «Buthwena, nzayi ni mu kyedika Pfumu wutumiki wanzyo wandi amana wundubudi ku moku ma Eloti yi mu moosu mana bakanzodilaka bayuta.»
ACT 12:12 Tangwa kábakula, wénda ku nzu ya Madiya ngudi wa Yowani wuna bakala tela ni Malaku. Kwakuna bákutakanina ndambu ya lawu ya batu yi kulombilaka.
ACT 12:13 Tangwa kákhokwatila ku mwelu wa luphangu, musadi wa mukhetu mosi khumbu yandi Lodi wábwesuka mu kuhinikina.
ACT 12:14 Buna kábakula ndinga ya Phetelu, sangu-sangu, konda kuyafulula, wátakula thinu mu kusamuna ni Phetelu mu mwelu wa luphangu kenina.
ACT 12:15 Bamuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi wu kilawu!» Kaasi yandi kakala sidingisa ni bwa kyedika. Bawu bakala zimbula: «Wuna wanzyo wandi.»
ACT 12:16 Kuna phi Phetelu yi kukhokwatilaka. Báyafulula amana báyituka lawu mu kumumona.
ACT 12:17 Phetelu wásongila kidimbu kuna koku dyandi ni badibata, wábamenika buna kámulubula Pfumu mu boloku amana wuzimbudi: «Menikenubwa kwena Zyaki yi kwena baphangi.» Kunima wálubuka, amana wénda kuma kwahika.
ACT 12:18 Tangwa kwakhyela kuma, baphumbulu tsula yabakwata: bekadihyula keti biki byámubwila Phetelu.
ACT 12:19 Eloti wátuma ni bamusanda, kaasi kámumonaku. Kábafungwasisa batsinzidi, amana wáhana nzila ni babazunduna mutwa. Kunima, wákulumuka ku Yuteya ndangu kenda ku Sezale kuna kánangina ndambu ya bilumbu.
ACT 12:20 Eloti mu kimbeni kákala yi bisi Tidi yi bisi Sitoni. Kaasi bawu báyukana mu kwenda mutala amana bisa. Bátundakana yi Balasitusi tsinzidi wa mwanza wa kyamvu, ndangu kabasadisa amana bálomba ngemba mukuma madya ma bawu makala tuka ku tsi yina ya kyamvu.
ACT 12:21 Báyukana, kilumbu kimosi amana Eloti wávwata mukonzu wandi, wázakala hana kiti kya luyalu, wáyandika mu kuzonza ku thwala ya batu boosu,
ACT 12:22 batu bakala mutsikisa mu kukalunga: «Yeku ndinga ya mutu kaasi yina ya nzambi mosi!»
ACT 12:23 Kaasi muna tangwa medina, wanzyo mosi wa Pfumu wámubeta, kikuma kahanaku lukumu kwena Nzambi, hanga bamudi kwena mimvidya amana wáfwa.
ACT 12:24 Kaasi ndinga ya Nzambi yámwangana amana yáyalangana.
ACT 12:25 Balanabasi yi Sawulu, kunima kulungisa kisalu kya bawu ku Yelusalemi, bávutuka, bámunata Yowani wuna bakala tela ni Malaku.
ACT 13:1 Muna Dibundu dina dyákala ku Atyosi, mwákala yi bambikudi yi balongi bwosu: Balanabasi, Simeyoni wuna bakala tela Kaphindi, Lukyusi mwisi Sileni, Manayena wuna wakola kumosi yi Eloti wuna wakala yala ku Ngadidi yi Sawulu.
ACT 13:2 Muna tangwa dina bakala zatula Pfumu yi kuzila madya, Kitembu Kyatoma wuzimbudini: «Ngyekwalenu Balanabasi yi Sawulu kikuma kya kisalu kina yíbatedila.»
ACT 13:3 Hanga ku manima ma kuzila madya yi kulombila, babasya moku amana bábasula ni benda.
ACT 13:4 Disongidila, bawu bátuma kwena Kitembu Kyatoma, bákulumuka ku Selesi; amana kwakuna, bákota mu masuwa ndangu benda ku zawala dya Siphele.
ACT 13:5 Buna bátula ku Salamini, básamuna ndinga ya Nzambi muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta. Bákala yi Yowani-Malaku wuna wákala waphamu dya bawu.
ACT 13:6 Kunima dya kulabuka zawala dyosu yi kuna Phafwosi, báwana nganga-ngombu mosi, Muyuta mosi khumbu yandi Badi-Yesu wakala dimonikisa hanga mbikudi.
ACT 13:7 Kakala zingila mu mukombu wa pfumu wa zawala Seluyusi Phawulusi, mutu mosi wa mayedi. Yandi wátedisa Balanabasi yi Sawulu, mu kusanda kayuka Ndinga ya Nzambi.
ACT 13:8 Kaasi nganga-ngombu Edimasi (bwosu buna bakala mutela mu ngeleti), kakala batendisa amana kakala sanda mu kumuhukumuna pfumu wa zawala mu lukwikilu.
ACT 13:9 Hanga Sawulu (wuna bisi tela hika Pholu), wábasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma, wámutala Edimasi
ACT 13:10 amana wuzimbudi: «Ngeyi mutu yandu wabasa yi bukamvi yi mayedi mambi, mwana wa kiphidi-mutu, mbeni wa masonga! Wayambulaku kuzanga nzila za bukheti za Pfumu?
ACT 13:11 Buthwena, koku dya Pfumu dyakúzyatula ngeyi: wakítuka phofu, amana mu tangwa dimosi, wamónaku hika mwini wa tangwa.» Muna tangwa meni dina, phipha yámubwila, wáyandika mu kubabata ndangu kasanda mutu wamúsimba.
ACT 13:12 Tangwa kámona, pfumu wa zawala mana mabwa, wákwikila, wáyuka tsambu lawu kikuma kya malongi ma Pfumu.
ACT 13:13 Pholu yi banduku bandi bákota mu masuwa ma Phafosi, bénda phi ku mbanza ya Pheleze dya Phafidiya. Yowani-Malaku yandi wádihambula yi bawu amana wávutuka ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 13:14 Tuka ku mbanza Pheleze, bálanda nzila ya bawu amana bátula ku Atyosi wa Phisidi. Kilumbu kya sabata, bákota mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta amana bázakala.
ACT 13:15 Ku manima ma kutanga Mitsiku yi Bambikudi mu ndinga ya ngolu, bapfumu ba nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta bátuma benda bazimbwala: «Baphangi, yukani ndinga lwenina yawu kikuma kya kusyamisa batu, zonzenu.»
ACT 13:16 Pholu wátelama, wusongidi kidimbu ku koku amana wuzimbudi: «Bisi Kiseledi yi benu lwisi muzitisa Nzambi, yukenu!
ACT 13:17 Nzambi wa kikanda kyaki, Nzambi wa Kiseledi kásola batata betu amana wávudisa kikanda mu tangwa dina kyákala mu kinzenza ku tsi ya Ngiphiti, kunima wálubulakya mu ngolu za koku dyandi.
ACT 13:18 Wábadisa kitesu kya mvula makumaya muna nganga.
ACT 13:19 Amana ku manima kuzilula makanda tsambwadi muna tsi ya Kanana, wábaheka tsi ya bawu hanga kimvwama
ACT 13:20 moosu mana másalama mu kitesu kya mvula khama ya yi makumatanu. «Ku manima ma bwabuna, wábaheka bazusi tii yi kuna tangwa dya mbikudi Samwela.
ACT 13:21 Ku manima, bálomba kyamvu, Nzambi wábaheka Sawulu, mwana Kisi, wuna wábayala mu mvula makumaya. Mukwa kikanda kya Benzyame kákala.
ACT 13:22 Ku manima ma kumukatula, wábasodila kyamvu Tavidi ndangu kakala pfumu wa bawu. Wáta kimbangi kikuma kya yandi: "Yimusodi Tavidi mwana wa Yese: mutu yandu wufwanani yi mabanza mama, kalúngisa bwosu buna nzodi."
ACT 13:23 Muna kikanda kyandi, Nzambi, muna lusilu lwandi kátedisila Yesu hanga muhuludi kikuma kya Kiseledi.
ACT 13:24 Ku thwala kukwisa kwandi, Yowani wábekitila kikuma kya mbotika ya tsobuka ya bikalulu ya kanda dyosu dya Kiseledi.
ACT 13:25 Amana Yowani buna kákala manisa kisalu kyandi, kákala zimbula: "Kwena benu, nati yenina meni? Meni yenabwoku! Ku manima ma meni kabati kwisila wuna yiléndaku mu kutumuna tsabatu zandi."
ACT 13:26 «Baphangi bama ba kikanda kya Bulahami yi benu lwisi muzitisa Nzambi, Musamu wa luhulusu wuna, kwena betu báhitikawa.
ACT 13:27 Mukuma, bisi Yelusalemi yi bapfumu ba bawu bámubakulaku Yesu, bábakisaku phi ndinga za bambikudi zina bisi tanga mu kosu kilumbu kya sabata. Kaasi bálungisaza mu kumusambisa.
ACT 13:28 Mbatanana bakonda mona kikuma kya kumuzengila lufwa, bálomba kwena Philatu ni kamuhondisa.
ACT 13:29 Ku manima ma kulungisa moosu mana básonika mu Masonuku kikuma kya yandi, bámukulumuna ha kitakani amana bámuzesa muna mazyamu.
ACT 13:30 Kaasi Nzambi wámufutumuna ha kati dya bafwa.
ACT 13:31 Kádimonikisa bilumbu bya lawu kwena bana bámusindikila tuka ku Ngadidi yi kuna Yelusalemi, amana buthwena bákituka bambangi bandi ku thwala ya bisi Kiseledi.
ACT 13:32 Amana betu, tulusamwani Musamu wa Bukheti wawu: lusilu luna kásila kwena batata betu,
ACT 13:33 Nzambi wulungisima buthwena kikuma kya betu bana ba bawu, mu kufutumuna Yesu. Bwosu buna básonika mu mukanda wazodi wa mikunga: "Wenina Mwana wama, meni, khituki tata waku lelu.
ACT 13:34 Nzambi kázimbula: kamúfutumuna ku bafwa ndangu kavutukaku hika mu bivundisila. Bwabuna kázonzila: "Yilúheka bima byatoma bya Tavidi bina bilungini mu lukwikilu."
ACT 13:35 Ihana kázonzila muna mukunga wahika: "Wayámbwadilaku ni Watoma waku kavundila mu mazyamu."
ACT 13:36 Kinga, ku manima ma kusadisa mu makula mandi bwosu buna kázola Nzambi; Tavidi wáfwa, bámuzika hana kabeta ka batata bandi amana wávunda.
ACT 13:37 Kaasi wuna káfutumuna Nzambi, kávundaku.
ACT 13:38 Zayenubwoku, baphangi bama: mwena yandi bisi lulongila ndoluka ya masumu; muna moosu mana myáfwanaku kululolula mitsiku mya Moyize,
ACT 13:39 muna moosu meni mamana, wosu wuna wukwikidi mwena yandi kakútumuka.
ACT 13:40 Disongidila ni kebenu, malubwilaku mana básonika Bambikudi:
ACT 13:41 "Talenu, benu lwabasa yi kilenza, yitukenu amana totenu! Mukuma meni, yilúngisa muhangu wumosi muna tangwa dyenu, muhangu wumosi wuna lwakonda kwikila, yuka ni balumenikawa!»
ACT 13:42 Mu kulubuka kwa Pholu yi Balanabasi, bábabokwadila mu kuzonzila hika dyambu dina mu kilumbu kya sabata kina kyálanda.
ACT 13:43 Tangwa kyámwangana kimvuka, Bayuta balawu yi baphani bana bakwikila mu malongi ma Bayuta bana bisi kumisa Nzambi, bálanda Pholu yi Balanabasi. Baba-baba, muna ngyambila za bawu kumosi yi bawu, bakala basyamisa mu kukangama ku khenda za Nzambi.
ACT 13:44 Sabata dina dyálanda, mbanza yosu kwandi bákutakana mu kuyuka ndinga ya Nzambi.
ACT 13:45 Mu kumona milumba-lumba mya batu, Bayuta bahika báyuka kiphala; bákala mufindisa phaka Pholu yi ngusi.
ACT 13:46 Hanga Pholu yi Balanabasi bakala bazimbwala yi kikumbwala kyosu: «Bwálunga ni baluzimbwalaya, ndinga ya Nzambi, theti kwena benu. Kaasi bwosu lulewudiya amana lumoniki ni lufwaniku mu kutambula luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula, tubaluki kwetu kwena Baphani.
ACT 13:47 Mukuma Pfumu wátuheka muswa wawu: "Yíkukitula, ngeyi, mwini wa makanda, ndangu, mu lusadisu lwa ngeyi, luhulusu lwatula tii yi muna mwatsukila tsi!"»
ACT 13:48 Buna báyuka bwabuna, Baphani básangwala lawu, bázatula Pfumu kikuma kya ndinga yandi. Amana boosu bana káyidika Nzambi kikuma kya luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula bákwikila.
ACT 13:49 Ndinga ya Pfumu yámwangana mu mulambu wosu.
ACT 13:50 Kaasi Bayuta bábalundika bakhetu ba luzitu bana bakala kumisa Nzambi yi bambuta ba mbanza amana bábasosila munyanga Pholu yi Balanabasi amana bábakukwasa mu mulambu wa bawu.
ACT 13:51 Bawu, bábakhukwamina fusyangeni dya bitambi bya bawu amana bénda ku Kikonyumi.
ACT 13:52 Kaasi balonguki ba ku Atyoki wa Phisidi, bawu, bábasa yi kyesi yi Kitembu Kyatoma.
ACT 14:1 Ku Kikonyumi, Pholu yi Balanabasi bakala kota phi mu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta yi kuzonzilaka mu phila yimosi ni Bayuta balawu yi bisi Ngeleti bákwikila.
ACT 14:2 Kaasi Bayuta bana bábwisa mu kukwikila, bakala sanda ni bavwadingisa mbundu za Baphani tii yikuna kuyenguna baphangi.
ACT 14:3 Mbatanana buna, Pholu yi Balanabasi báyika bilumbu bya bawu ku Kikonyumi. Bakala zonza yi kikumbwala kikuma bakala yekamina mwena Pfumu, yandi wuna wakala ta kimbangi kya ndinga ya mamboti mandi mu kuhana bidimbu yi biphadi muna moku ma bawu.
ACT 14:4 Muna mbanza, batu bádikabisa; bahika kikuma kya Bayuta, bakwawu kikuma kya bathumwa.
ACT 14:5 Kaasi bwosu bakala yilama, Baphani yi Bayuta yi bapfumu ba bawu, mu kubanyokuna yi kubahondila ku matadi,
ACT 14:6 bawu buna bábakulabwa, bátina ku mbanza ya Lisiti yi Delebi muna nzunga za kinzunga kya Dikawoni.
ACT 14:7 Kwakuna, báyandika kulonga Musamu wa Bukheti.
ACT 14:8 Kwákala, kuna Lisiti, yi mutu mosi wawokumuka malu; tuka lubutuku lwandi, kákangalaku keti mbala mosi. Wazakala kákala.
ACT 14:9 Kakala yuka mana kakala zonza Pholu. Yandu-yandu wumutadi amana bwosu kámona ni kákala yi lukwikilu lwalenda mubelula,
ACT 14:10 hanga wuzimbudi mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Telama, singika bitambi byaku!» Mutu wuna wásotuka amana wáyandika mu kukangala.
ACT 14:11 Bwosu bámona mambu mana kásala Pholu, milumba-lumba mya batu báthuta ndinga amana bázimbula mu ndinga ya bawu ya Dikawonye: «Banzambi bavwati lutu lwa kimutu amana bakulungi kwena betu!»
ACT 14:12 Balanabasi bakala mutela: «Zewusi» amana Pholu: «Helemesi», kikuma yandi wákala ngenzi.
ACT 14:13 Kikumbu kya nzambi Zewusi kyákala kuna fula dya mbanza amana nganga wa kikumbu mekina, kumosi yi mulumba-lumba wa batu, wánata miluma mya bangombi yi bithundu bya kunenga, kázola ni katambikabya kimenga kwena Pholu yi Balanabasi.
ACT 14:14 Tangwa báyukabwa bathumwa, Pholu yi Balanabasi, báyata miledi mya bawu amana bénda thinu mu mulumba-lumba mu kukalunga:
ACT 14:15 «Bakwetu, biki lubati hangila bwabuna? Betu phi thwenina batu hanga benu. Yuka ni tubati lusamwana Musamu wa Bukheti, ndangu lwayambula mambu makonda mupfunu amana lwabaluka kwena Nzambi wa moya wuna wáhanga zilu yi tsi yi yanga dya mbuta, yi bima byosu bina bisimwa zingila.
ACT 14:16 Muna makula máluta, yandi wáhana nzila kwena makanda moosu mu kulanda nzila za bawu-meni.
ACT 14:17 Kaasi kálembwaku mu kuta kimbangi, mu kuhangaka mambu ma mamboti; mu kulunokisinaka mvula tukidila ku zilu, amana lwisi hela phi bibundu muna tangwa dya byawu, mu kuluhekaka madya yi kyesi kya ku mbundu.»
ACT 14:18 Mbatanana bakala zonza bwabuna, phasi bámona mu kukandikisa kwena milumba-lumba mya batu mu kubatambikila kimenga.
ACT 14:19 Kunima, Bayuta bana bátuka ku Atyosi yi ku Kikonyumi bábalongisila milumba-lumba mya batu. Hanga bamutimbwadi matadi Pholu amana bámubulumuna ku phenza ya mbanza, bábanza ni wafwa kákala.
ACT 14:20 Kaasi tangwa bámuzyeta balonguki, wátokama amana wávutuka mu mbanza. Kilumbu kyalanda, wénda yi Balanabasi ku Delebi.
ACT 14:21 Kunima dya kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti mu mbanza meni yayina yi kuyika balonguki balawu, Pholu yi Balanabasi mu kuvutuka kwa bawu, báhitila ku Lisiti ku Kikonyumi yi ku Atyosi.
ACT 14:22 Bakala syamisa balonguki yi kubaheka kikesa ndangu bazyama mu lukwikilu, mu kuzimbula: «Bulombi kwena betu, twamona kiwayi kya lawu mu kukota mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.»
ACT 14:23 Muna kosu Dibundu, bakala basodila malemba, amana ku manima ma kulombila yi kuzila kudya, bábatambika kwena Pfumu mwena wuna bakala sila lukwikilu lwa bawu.
ACT 14:24 Kunima, báhyokila ku Phisidiya amana bátula ku Phafidiya.
ACT 14:25 Ku manima ma kulonga ndinga ya Nzambi ku Phelezi, bákulumuka ku Atadi.
ACT 14:26 Tangwa bákatuka kwakuna, bálabuka ku Atyosi wa Sidiya, kuna bábatambikila mu khenda za Nzambi, kikuma kya kisalu kina básala.
ACT 14:27 Buna bátula, bákhundikisa Dibundu amana bátendula mambu moosu mana kábasadila Nzambi, yi buna kákangula mwelu wa lukwikilu kwena Baphani.
ACT 14:28 Amana bánanga bilumbu bya lawu kumosi yi balonguki.
ACT 15:1 Ndambu ya batu bana bátuka ku Yuteya, bisa ku Atyosi, bwabu bakala longa kwena baphangi: «Yukani ludiyotisiku, bwosu bulombi mu mikuku mya Moyize, lwalendaku huluka.»
ACT 15:2 Pholu yi Balanabasi bátendana lawu yi bawu. Hanga kunima babongi lukanu ni Pholu, Balanabasi yi ndambu ya batu ba bisi Atyosi batombuka ku Yelusalemi, ku thwala ya bathumwa yi malemba ndangu benda zonzila dyambu dina.
ACT 15:3 Dibundu bábaheka bina bákalabyawu mupfunu kikuma kya mu nzila. Bwosu bakala hitila mu nzila ya Fenisi yi ya Samadiya, yi kumenikaka buna bábalwamina mbundu Baphani; amana bwakala hana kyesi kya lawu kwena baphangi.
ACT 15:4 Mu kutula kwa bawu ku Yelusalemi, bathumwa yi bambuta ba dibundu, bábayamba ku Dibundu amana bábatendwala moosu mana káhanga Nzambi mu nzila ya bawu.
ACT 15:5 Ndambu ya batu bana bákala mu kibuka kya bafwadisi amana bákituka phi bakwikidi, hanga batelami mu kuzimbula: «Bulungi ni babayotisa bakwikidi bana ba Baphani amana babatuma ndangu balemvuka mu mitsiku mya Moyize.»
ACT 15:6 Bathumwa yi malemba bákutakana ndangu bazonzila dyambu dina.
ACT 15:7 Tangwa dya lawu kyábonga kinzonzi. Kunima, Phetelu wátelama amana wubazimbwadi: «Baphangi bama, luzayibwa ni tuka thama, Nzambi wasola ha kati dya benu, ndangu mu munwa wa meni Baphani bayuka ndinga ya Musamu wa Bukheti amana bakwikila.
ACT 15:8 Amana Nzambi, yandi wuzayi mbundu, wubatidi kimbangi mu kubaheka Kitembu Kyatoma hanga kwena betu;
ACT 15:9 kásyaku keti diswaswanu dimosi ha kati kya betu yi bawu, mukuma wásemisa mbundu za bawu mu lukwikilu.
ACT 15:10 Buthwena bwabu, kikuma kya biki lubati musokila Nzambi mu kubanatisa balonguki zitu dina bakonda lenda bakhaka betu yi betu-betu mu kunata?
ACT 15:11 Thwisi kwikila ni mu khenda za Pfumu Yesu twáhulwakila betu yi bawu.»
ACT 15:12 Kibuka kyosu kyahwena talala, amana bakala hinikina Balanabasi yi Pholu kutendula bidimbu byosu yi biphadi bina kásala Nzambi, mu nzila ya bawu, ha kati dya Baphani.
ACT 15:13 Buna bámanisa kuzonza, Zyaki wábonga ndinga, wázonza: «Baphangi, ngyukenu!
ACT 15:14 Simoni kátendula phila yina kábongila Nzambi, mbala ya theti, hana kati dya makanda, kanda dimosi kikuma kya khumbu yandi.
ACT 15:15 Ndinga za bambikudi zifwanakani yi mambu meni mamana, bwosu básonika:
ACT 15:16 "Ku manima ma bwabuna yikwisa hika, mu kutungulula sombolu dya Tavidi dina dyabwa, yitélamisadya hika mu kuzangana kwandi, amana yisúngikadya.
ACT 15:17 Ndangu batu bana basadi balenga sanda Pfumu, abwabuna, makanda moosu mana menina yi khumbu yama,
ACT 15:18 mamana kázimbula Pfumu, yandi wuna wázayikisa mabanza mandi, tukidila thama."
ACT 15:19 Yihana, meni mboni ni babayangisaku Baphani bana babaluki kwena Nzambi.
ACT 15:20 Kaasi tubasonikinenu: bayambula mu kudyaka mbisi basadidi mu nzila za biteki, bayambula mbongi yi bambisi bana bisi zeka tsingu yi bana ba khengu.
ACT 15:21 Kikuma, tuka makula ma thama, muna kosu mbanza, mwena yi batu bisi tanga mitsiku mya Moyize yi muna kosu sabata muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta.»
ACT 15:22 Hanga bathumwa yi malemba yi Dibundu dyosu bamonibwa mboti mu kusola bayala hana kati dya bawu ndangu benda basindikila Pholu yi Balanabasi ku Atyosi. Yuta wuna bakala tela phi Balasabasi, yi Silasi, batu bákala yi kitya mu kati dya baphangi.
ACT 15:23 Bábaheka mukanda wawu: «Bathumwa, malemba yi baphangi bahitiki mboti kwena baphangi Baphani bana benina kuna mbanza ya Atyosi, muna Sidiya yi muna Sidisi!
ACT 15:24 Tuyukikini ni ndambu ya batu batukini kwena betu, bana twakondi senda, baluvwadingisiki mabanza amana baluyukisiki kiwayi muna ndinga za bawu.
ACT 15:25 Ihana, dyambu dina twámonidya bukheti betu boosu mu kusola bayakala amana twabahitika kwena benu ha kimosi yi batya betu Balanabasi yi Pholu,
ACT 15:26 bawu bátambika luzingu lwa bawu kikuma kya khumbu ya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu.
ACT 15:27 Tuluhitiki Yuta yi Silasi, bawu báluzimbwala ndinga meni zina muna munwa mya bawu.
ACT 15:28 Ihana ni, mboti bwenina kwena Kitembu Kyatoma yi kwena betu-betu ni tuluyekikaku keti kizitu kyahika, kaka mihangu mina miluti mupfunu:
ACT 15:29 kudikenga ku bima bina balambudi kwena biteki yi menga yi bambisi bana ba bithitu, yambulenu kindumba; yuka ni lwazitisa mambu mana mosu, mboti lwahánga. Salenu mboti!»
ACT 15:30 Hanga bawu babasisi amana bakulungi ku Atyosi, kwakuna, bákutikisa kibuka kya bakwikidi amana báhana mukanda.
ACT 15:31 Bátangawa amana básangwala kikuma kya kusyamisa kuna.
ACT 15:32 Yuta yi Silasi, bawu meni bakala bambikudi, báhana kikesa kwena baphangi yi kubasyamisa mu ndinga za bawu za lawu .
ACT 15:33 Kunima dya ndambu ya tangwa, baphangi bábazodila kuvutuka kwa ngemba kwena bana bábahitika. [
ACT 15:34 Kaasi Silasi wámonabwa bukheti mu kusala kuna Atyosi kaasi Yuta wávutuka yandi buhika ku Yelusalemi].
ACT 15:35 Pholu yi Balanabasi, bázinga kuna Atyosi, mu kulonga yi kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa ndinga ya Pfumu, kumosi yi batu bakwawu balawu.
ACT 15:36 Kunima ndambu ya bilumbu, Pholu wázimbula kwena Balanabasi: «Tuvutukisa mu kutala baphangi muna mbanza zoosu, muna twásamuna ndinga ya Pfumu, ndangu twazaya keti bweti benina.»
ACT 15:37 Balanabasi kázola ni bamunata Yowani, wuna bakala tela Malaku;
ACT 15:38 Kaasi Pholu kámona ni ka mboti ku banata mutu wuna wábatina kedi tuka ku Phafidiya amana wakonda basindikila mu kisalu kya bawu.
ACT 15:39 Bánanama lawu, ku tsuka badihambula. Balanabasi wámubonga Malaku amana bákota mu masuwa ndangu benda ku Siphe,
ACT 15:40 Pholu, yandi, wásola Silasi amana benda, ku manima ma kubasya ha moku ma Pfumu, kwena baphangi.
ACT 15:41 Wálutila ku binzunga bya Sidiya yi Sidisi mu kusyamisa Mabundu.
ACT 16:1 Pholu wátula ku Delebi, kunima wenda ku Disiti. Kinga kwákala kwakuna yi mulonguki mosi khumbu yandi Thimoti; kákala mwana wa Muyuta wa mukhetu mosi wa mukwikidi yi mwisi Ngeleti mosi.
ACT 16:2 Baphangi ba bisi Lisiti yi bisi Kikonyumi bakala ta kimbangi kya mboti kikuma kya yandi.
ACT 16:3 Pholu kázola ni kamunata kumosi yi yandi, hanga wumubongi amana wumuyotisi kikuma kya Bayuta ba kinzunga mekyana; kikuma boosu bakala zaya ni tata wandi mwisi Ngeleti kákala.
ACT 16:4 Muna mbanza zina bakala hitila, bakala samuna mana bázenga kwena bathumwa yi bathwadisi kuna Yelusalemi, ndangu balundama.
ACT 16:5 Mabundu makala syama mu lukwikilu yi kukolaka kilumbu muna kilumbu.
ACT 16:6 Kitembu Kyatoma wábakandisa Pholu yi Silasi mu kulonga Ndinga ya Nzambi mu kinzunga kya Aziya, hanga báluta ku Fizi yi tsi ya Ngalati.
ACT 16:7 Buna bátula bela-bela yi kinzunga kya Misiya, bámeka mu kukwenda ku kinzunga kya Bitini; kaasi Kitembu kya Yesu kábahekaku nzila.
ACT 16:8 Hanga bahitidi ku Misiya amana bákulunga ku mbanza ya Thowasi.
ACT 16:9 Muna phipha, Pholu wámona mbona mesu. Mwisi Masetwani mosi wákala hana, watelama, kakala mubokwadila bwabu: «Luta ku Masetwani, awisa tusadisa!»
ACT 16:10 Buna kámonina mbona mesu yina, twásanda mu kukwenda ku Masetwani; kikuma twázaya ni Nzambi kátutela ndangu twasamuna Musamu wa Bukheti kwakuna.
ACT 16:11 Buna twábonga masuwa tukidila ku Thowasi, hanga thwendi mbala mosi yi kuna zawala dya Samothalasi; kilumbu kyalanda thwénda ku mbanza ya Neyaphodisi.
ACT 16:12 Ha twákatuka kwakuna, thwénda ku Fidiphu; mbanza yimosi, muna kinzunga kyatheti kya Masetwani amana bisi Loma bakalamwa zingila. Twánanga ndambu ya bilumbu kwakuna.
ACT 16:13 Mu kilumbu kya sabata, twálubuka mu mwelu wa mbanza, kuna khungu ya mamba mosi, homa hana twakala banzila ni twawana kizika kya lombilu. Twázakala hakana amana twáyambila yi bakhetu bana bisaha kutakana.
ACT 16:14 Hakala yi mukhetu mosi khumbu yandi Didya; kikhita kya miledi mya thalu kakala sala, mwisi mbanza ya Thiyatidi, kakala kumisa Nzambi. Kakala yuka, amana Pfumu wámukangula mbundu ndangu kadihana mu ndinga za Pholu.
ACT 16:15 Kunima dya kutambula mbotika yi nzu yandi yosu, wátutedisa kuna nzu yandi, kátubokwadila mu kuzimbula: «Yuka lumoni ni meni yenina wakwikama kwena Pfumu, alwisenu ku nzu yama amana zakalenu kwakuna.» Amana wátubokwadila ndangu twatambwasa.
ACT 16:16 Bwana twákala kwenda ha kizika kya lombilu, musadi wa mukhetu mosi wakala yi mukisi wa nyoka, wakala mutuma mu kubikula mana mabwa ku thwala, muna phila meni yina, mwamuna bapfumu bandi bakala bongila mbongu, hanga wututundakani.
ACT 16:17 Wayandika mu kutulanda, betu yi Pholu, yi kukalungaka: "Batu baba benina basadi ba Nzambi wa phungu! Babati lulonga nzila ya luhulusu!"
ACT 16:18 Bwosu kakala sala bwabuna bilumbu bya lawu, ku tsuka, Pholu wávwalangana, amana wábaluka mu kuzonza kwena kitembu kina: «Mu khumbu ya Yesu Kidisitu, yikuheki muswa ni wálubuka mu lutu lwa mukhetu yandi!» Amana kyálubuka muna tangwa medina.
ACT 16:19 Buna bamona ni kivuvu kya bawu bakala bongila mbongu kitotini, hanga bapfumu ba mwana mukhetu wuna babakwati Pholu yi Silasi amana bababulumuni hana mbasi, kuna thwala ya bapfumu ba mbanza.
ACT 16:20 Babasongidi kwena bazusi ba Loma amana bazimbudi: «Batu baba babati kotisa mvwalangani mu mbanza yetu. Bayuta benina,
ACT 16:21 amana babati longa mikuku mya pha mina batulombiku keti mu ku tambwasa, keti kusadila kwena betu thwenina bisi Loma.»
ACT 16:22 Mulumba-lumba wa batu phi wábabalukila. Hanga bazusi babawomwasi miledi amana bahani muswa ni babadiphula mafimbu.
ACT 16:23 Ku manima ma kubadiphula lawu dya mafimbu, bábatimbula mu boloku, balombi kwena tsinzidi ni kabatalaka mboti-mboti.
ACT 16:24 Buna kabonga muswa wuna, wábakotisa mu suku dina dyákala kuna tsuka ya boloku amana wábakotisa malu muna phophu.
ACT 16:25 Muna kisuku, Pholu yi Silasi bakala lombila yi kuyimbila kikuma kya kuzatula Nzambi; batu bahika ba boloku bakala bayuka.
ACT 16:26 Muna mbala mosi, mafu máningana ngolu, mipfundila mya boloku myáningana. Muna tangwa meni dina, mwelu myosu mya batu ba boloku myákanguka, amana misinga myosu myátabuka.
ACT 16:27 Tsinzidi wátokama, amana buna kámona ni mwelu mya boloku mya kukangula, wáhola mbedi ya phoku yandi; kázola ni kadihonda, kikuma kákabanza ni bakwa boloku bátina.
ACT 16:28 Kaasi Pholu wákalunga: «Wudihekaku phasi! Hatwenina betu boosu!»
ACT 16:29 Hanga tsinzidi wulombi mwinda, wákota thinu amana wábwa kuna thwala ya Pholu yi Silasi, kuna yi kutekitaka.
ACT 16:30 Wabanata ku nzila amana wuzimbudi: «A bapfumu, biki pfwani yihanga ndangu yihuluka?»
ACT 16:31 Bamuvutwadini: «Kwikila mwena Pfumu Yesu, wahúluka ngeyi yi nzu yaku.»
ACT 16:32 Bámulonga ndinga ya Pfumu, yi kwena boosu bana bákala mu nzu yandi.
ACT 16:33 Muna tangwa meni dina, muna phipha, wábabonga yandi meni amana wásukula phuta za bawu. Wátambula mbotika, yandi yi boosu bana bákala mu nzu yandi.
ACT 16:34 Wábatombula ku nzu yandi, wábaheka bima bya kudya amana wásephila kumosi yi nzu yandi yosu kikuma kya buna bákwikila mwena Nzambi.
ACT 16:35 Tangwa kwakhya kuma, bazusi ba Loma bátuma basuta benda zimbula kwena tsinzidi: «Bayambwadila batu bana.»
ACT 16:36 Tsinzidi wátudisa muluwa kwena Pholu mu kuzimbula: «Bazusi bazimbudi ni balubula; buthwena, lubukenu amana lwenda mu ngemba.»
ACT 16:37 Kaasi Pholu kábavutwala bwabu: «Ku manima ma kutubetisa fimbu mu mesu ma batu, konda kutusambisa, betu batu thwena bakwa mbedi ya Loma! Batutimbudi mu boloku. Amana buthwena, bazodi ni batukula mu kitsweki? Loni! Bisa tulubula bawu meni!»
ACT 16:38 Basuta bánata ndinga zina kwena bazusi ba Loma, bawu, bweya bwábakwata mu kuyuka ni bisi mbedi ya Loma bákala.
ACT 16:39 Bisa babokwadila amana bábasula, yi kubalombaka ni bakatuka mu mbanza.
ACT 16:40 Tangwa bálubuka mu boloku, Pholu yi Silasi, bénda ku nzu ya Didya. Buna bábamona, babasyamisa baphangi amana bénda.
ACT 17:1 Kunima kulutila mu nzila ya Afiphodisi yi Apholoniya, bátula ku Tesalonika kuna kwákala nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta.
ACT 17:2 Pholu wénda kwakuna, bwosu buna kayikana. Kitesu kya masabata matatu kakala zonzila, kumosi yi bawu, mambu mana matadidi Masonuku,
ACT 17:3 kákalama babangwamina mu kusongila ni Kidisitu káfwana kunyokuka amana kafutumuka ha kati dya bafwa. Wuzimbudini: «Yesu wuna yibati lusamwana, yandi wuna Kidisitu.»
ACT 17:4 Ndambu ya bayuta hana kati dya bawu bátambwasama amana bákhundakana kwena Pholu yi Silasi. Phila mosi yi bisi Ngeleti balawu bana bakala kumisa Nzambi yi bakhetu bahika ba luzitu.
ACT 17:5 Kaasi Bayuta báyuka kiphala, bábonga ndambu ya bayakala bambi, bana bisi telama muna balabala, hanga balubudi mathata muna kibuka yi mvwalangani muna mbanza. Bénda kuna nzu ya Yasoni mu kusanda Pholu yi Silasi ndangu babanata ku mesu ma batu.
ACT 17:6 Kaasi bábawanaku; hanga babanati Yasoni yi ndambu ya baphangi bahika bakala hana ku thwala ya bazusi ba mbanza, amana báyandika kukalunga: «Batu baba bavwadingisini tsi yosu, buthwena, batudi haka!
ACT 17:7 Amana Yasoni wubayambiki kuna nzu yandi! Boosu babati sala mambu mafwananiku yi mitsiku mya Khayisala, mukuma babati zimbula ni henina yi kyamvu wahika, Yesu!»
ACT 17:8 Ndinga meni zina zibavwadingisi mulumba-lumba wa batu yi bazusi ba mbanza.
ACT 17:9 Kunima dya kubafutisa mbongu, Yasoni yi batu bahika, bábayambwadila.
ACT 17:10 Buna yabwa phipha, hanga baphangi babahitiki Pholu yi Silasi ku Bele. Mu kutula kwa bawu, bénda ku nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta.
ACT 17:11 Baba-baba bákala yi tsambu ya kubayamba kuluta bana bákala ku Tesalonika; báyambaya Ndinga ya Nzambi yi luzolu lwa mboti mu kulongukaka kosu kilumbu Masonuku, ndangu bazaya yukani mambu mana babati balonga ma kyedika menina.
ACT 17:12 Balawu hana kati dya bawu, bákituka bakwikidi. Phila mosi yi bisi Ngeleti ba bakhetu ba luzitu yi bayakala balawu.
ACT 17:13 Kaasi tangwa báyuka, Bayuta ba ku Tesalonika, ni Pholu kabati samuna hika ndinga ya Nzambi ku Bele, bísa hika kwakuna, ndangu bavwadingisa milumba-lumba mya batu.
ACT 17:14 Hanga baphangi bámuhitika Pholu ku sabu dya yanga dya mbuta; kaasi Silasi yi Thimoti básala kuna Bele.
ACT 17:15 Bana bakala munata Pholu, bénda yandi yi kuna Ateni, kunima dya kuvutuka kwa bawu ku Bele, batu meni babana bisa yi muswa wuna kábaheka Pholu kikuma kya Silasi yi Thimoti ndangu bamulanda tswalu.
ACT 17:16 Muna tangwa medina, Pholu kakala bahingila Silasi yi Thimoti kuna Ateni, kámona ni mbanza yina yabasa yi banzambi ba biteki, hanga wuyuki phasi lawu ku mbundu.
ACT 17:17 Kakala solula yi Bayuta yi bana bakala kumisa Nzambi mu nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, amana kosu kilumbu, kakala solula yi bana kakala wana mu mazandu.
ACT 17:18 Ndambu ya batu ba mayedi ba ephikidiye yi ba sitoyisye bayandika mu kuyambila yi yandi. Bahika bakala zimbula: «Biki disongidila dya malokosi mama?» Bakwawu bazimbudi: «Ngatu mulongi mosi wa banzambi ba banzenza wubati longa.» Mukuma Pholu kakala samuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa Yesu yi wuna wa lufutumuku.
ACT 17:19 Hanga bamubongi, bamunati ku Ayelophazi amana bamuzimbwadini: «Fwani twazaya keti khi mawu malongi mapha mana wubati zonzila?
ACT 17:20 Mukuma mambu ma kuyituka wubati zonzila mu matu ma betu. Tuzodi twazaya thendula ya mawu.»
ACT 17:21 Kikuma, bisi Ateni yi banzenza bana bakala zingila ha kati dya bawu bakala lutisa tangwa dya bawu dyosu mu kumenika holo kuyuka mambu mana mapha.
ACT 17:22 Pholu wátelama hana kati dya Ayelophazi, wuzimbudi: «Bisi Ateni, mboni ni batu ba kinzambi lwenina muna mambu moosu.
ACT 17:23 Kikuma mu kuluta khadikini, mboni bima byenu bya bisambu, amana mboni phi yi mesa ma kimenga básonika bwabu: "Kwena nzambi wuna kazayakaniku." Disongidila ni lwisi mufukamina konda kumuzaya, yandi wuna mbati lusamwana meni.
ACT 17:24 Nzambi wuna wáhanga tsi yi byosu bina byeninamwa, yandi wenina Pfumu wa zilu yi wa tsi, kisiku zingila mu nzu za Nzambi zina bátungila mu moku ma batu;
ACT 17:25 bisiku muheka bima bituki mu moku ma batu, hanga wuna wisi konda kima, yandi wisi baheka luzingu kwena boosu, mwela yi bima byosu.
ACT 17:26 Muna nzila ya mutu mosi káhangila makanda moosu ma batu, baba bisi zingila mu tsi yosu, amana wáyidika matangwa yi muma muna bafwani kuzingila,
ACT 17:27 ndangu bamusanda Nzambi, ngatu bafwani kumumona mu kubabata. Kinga yandi kisiku kala kyana yi mosi yi mosi wa betu.
ACT 17:28 Mukuma: "Mwena yandi thwisi zingila, thwisi ninganina amana thwenina; Bwabuna bázimbula phi ndambu ya basoniki benu: "Betu phi thwenina khuna ya yandi."
ACT 17:29 Yukani kikanda kya Nzambi thwenina, twalendaku banza ni bunzambi bwenina hanga wolu, hanga ndisu holo hanga matadi mana bisi hala kwena batu yi mabanza ma kimutu.
ACT 17:30 Kaasi Nzambi, kisiku tala hika tangwa dina dya kukonda mazaya, buthwena, kabati tela batu boosu, muma mwosu, ndangu basoba bikalulu.
ACT 17:31 Kikuma wásya kilumbu kina kasámbisa tsi ya batu yosu mu masonga; mu nzila ya mutu wuna kásola, amana wáhana kambangu kwena batu boosu, mu kumufutumuna ha kati dya bafwa!»
ACT 17:32 Buna báyuka kuzonzila lufutumuku lwa bafwa, bahika bámuseya, bakwawu bazimbudi: «Mbala yahika nana twayúka mambu mana.»
ACT 17:33 Bwabuna kálubukila Pholu ha kati dya bawu.
ACT 17:34 Mbatanana buna, ndambu ya batu bahika, bákhundakana kwena yandi amana bákituka bakwikidi. Muna kati dya bawu, mwákala yi Tenisi, mukwa kibuka kya Ayelophazi, yi ngudi mosi khumbu yandi Tamadiya yi batu bahika.
ACT 18:1 Ku manima ma bwabuna, Pholu wákatuka ku Ateni, wénda ku Khoditu.
ACT 18:2 Káwana kwakuna, Muyuta mosi khumbu yandi Akilasi, mwisi kizunga kya Photi, wisi tula nana tukidila ku Kitadi yi mukhetu wandi Phisikila, kikuma Kodi káhana muswa ni Bayuta boosu bakatuka ku Loma. Hanga Pholu wendi kuna bákala;
ACT 18:3 bwosu kakala sala kisalu kimosi yi bawu, wázakala kuna nzu ya bawu mu kusala kisalu: bákala bayidiki ba masombolu.
ACT 18:4 Kosu sabata, kakala bonga ndinga muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta amana kakala sanda mu kukwikisa Bayuta yi bisi Ngeleti.
ACT 18:5 Kaasi buna bákulumuka, Silasi yi Thimoti tukidila ku Masetwani, Pholu wádihana kimakulu mu kulonga Ndinga ya Nzambi; kakala tendula kwena Bayuta ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu.
ACT 18:6 Kaasi bwosu bakala bwisa Bayuta malongi mandi yi kumutukwanaka, wákhukumuna miledi myandi amana wábazimbwala: «Menga menu makala hana thandu ya mutwa myenu! Meni mathadiku! Buthwena bwabu, yikwénda kwena Baphani.»
ACT 18:7 Wákatuka kuna amana wénda ku nzu ya mutu mosi, khumbu yandi Titiyusi Yusitusi, wakala kumisa Nzambi, nzu yandi yákala hana kabeta ka nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta.
ACT 18:8 Khisiphusi, pfumu wa nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, wákwikila mwena Pfumu yi nzu yandi yosu. Amana bisi Khoditu lawu bana bakala yuka, bákwikila amana bábotama.
ACT 18:9 Muna phipha mosi, Pfumu kámulubwakila Pholu mu mbona mesu, wumuzimbwadi: «Yukaku bweya! Zonzaka, wudibataku,
ACT 18:10 mukuma meni yenina kumosi yi ngeyi. Ka mutu ku wakúhanga kima, kikuma batu balawu yenina bawu mu mbanza yayi.»
ACT 18:11 Kánanga kwakuna, mvula mosi yi ngonda sambanu hana kati dya bawu, mu kulonga ndinga ya Nzambi.
ACT 18:12 Muna tangwa dina kákala Kadiyoni, pfumu wa Loma kuna kinzunga kya Akayi, Bayuta bákutakana, bábonga lukanu lwa mbi kikuma kya Pholu amana bámunata ku nganda ya bazusi,
ACT 18:13 bazimbudi: «Mutu yandu, kabati kwikisa batu ndangu bakumisaka Nzambi muna phila yina milombidiku mitsiku.»
ACT 18:14 Pholu, buna kázola katambula ndinga, Kadiyoni wázimbula kwena Bayuta: «Wadi ni mutsiku kakuludi kondilo dyambu dyahika diluti kitesu, wadi yiluyukidi buna bufwani, benu Bayuta.
ACT 18:15 Kaasi hadyena dyambu ditadi mihowu, khumbu yi mitsiku mya benu-benu, mana matadi benu-benu. Meni, nzodiku kukala zusi dya mambu mana!»
ACT 18:16 Hanga wubakudi ku nganda ya bazusi.
ACT 18:17 Hanga boosu bamukwati Sositeni, pfumu wa nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, amana báyandika kumubeta hana thwala ya nganda ya bazusi, konda bwamuheka phasi Kadiyoni.
ACT 18:18 Pholu wázakala hika kwakuna ndambu ya bilumbu. Kunima, wábasisa baphangi amana wákota mu masuwa ndangu kenda ku Sidiya, kumosi yi Phisila yi Akilasi. Wádikulula tsuki ku mutwa, kuna Sakhe, mukuma lusilu kásila.
ACT 18:19 Tangwa bátula ku Efesu, yandi wábasisa Phisila yi Akilasi. Wenda ku nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta amana wáyambila yi Bayuta.
ACT 18:20 Bámulomba ni kánanga hika ndambu ya bilumbu kwakuna; kaasi yandi kazolaku.
ACT 18:21 Wábasisa mu kuzimbula: «Yikwisa vutuka kwena benu, yukani Nzambi kazolabwa.» Tukidila ku Efesu, wákota mu masuwa.
ACT 18:22 Amana ha kátula, ku Sezale katulukila, wátombuka theti ku Yelusalemi ndangu kahana mboti ku Dibundu, kunima wákulunga ku Atyosi.
ACT 18:23 Ku manima ma ndambu ya tangwa, wénda amana wáhyokila mu nzila ya Ngalati yi Fizi, mu kusyamisa balonguki boosu.
ACT 18:24 Kinga Muyuta mosi, khumbu yandi Apholosi, mwisi Alekizandi, nganzi wa mbuta kákala amana wátoma zaya mambu matadidi Masonuku, wátula kuna Efesu.
ACT 18:25 Yandi, nzila ya pfumu bámulonga, yi ngolu mu kitembu, amana kakala longa yi tsikiningi mambu matadidi Yesu, kaasi mbotika ya Yowani lwesi kázaya.
ACT 18:26 Kákala zonza yi tsikiningi yosu muna nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta. Ku manima ma kumuyuka, Phisila yi Akilasi bámubonga mu kwenda musongila mboti-mboti nzila ya Nzambi.
ACT 18:27 Bwosu kákanina mu kuhyokila ku Akayi, baphangi bámuheka kikesa amana bábasonikina balonguki ndangu bamuyamba mboti-mboti. Mu kutula kwandi kuna, mupfunu wa lawu kákala kwena bana bákituka bakwikidi mu khenda za Nzambi,
ACT 18:28 mukuma, kakala batungulula, Bayuta, yi ngolu zoosu hana mesu ma batu, yi kubasongila muna nzila ya Masonuku ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu.
ACT 19:1 Tangwa kákala Apholosi ku khoditu, Pholu wálutila ku kinzunga kya myongu, wákulumuka yi kuna Efesu. Káwana kwakuna ndambu ya balonguki,
ACT 19:2 amana wubayufudi: «Lwátambula Kitembu Kyatoma tangwa lwákituka bakwikidi?» Bawu bamuvutwadini: «Khaku kedi tuyuka kuzonzila Kitembu Kyatoma».
ACT 19:3 Yandi wábayufula hika: «Amana khi mbotika lwatambula?» Bawu bamuvutwadini: «Mbotika ya Yowani.»
ACT 19:4 Hanga Pholu wuzimbudi: «Yowani kábotika mbotika mosi ya kubalumuna mbundu, kakala zimbula kwena batu ni bakwikila mwena wuna wakala kwisa ku manima ma yandi, disongidila ni Yesu.»
ACT 19:5 Muna ndinga meni zina, bátambula mbotika mu khumbu ya Pfumu Yesu.
ACT 19:6 Pholu wábathetika moku, amana Kitembu Kyatoma wábakulwamukina. Báyandika kuzonza mu ndinga zina zizayakaniku yi kubikulaka mambu mana kakala bazimbwala Nzambi.
ACT 19:7 Bayakala bana bákala kitesu kya kumi yi boodi.
ACT 19:8 Pholu kakala kwenda ku nzu ya kimvuka ya Bayuta, kwakuna kakala zonzila yi kikumbwala; kitesu kya ngonda tatu kakala zonzila yi kukwikisaka batu bana bakala muyuka mu mana matadidi Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
ACT 19:9 Kaasi batu bahika, bwosu bábwisa mu kuyuka yi mu kukwikila. Bakala lewula Nzila yina, mu mesu ma batu boosu. Hanga Pholu wubasisi, wénda yi balonguki ku kabeta, kakala solula yi bawu kosu kilumbu muna nzu ya malongi ya Tilanusi.
ACT 19:10 Bwabuna bwázinga mvula zoodi, mu phila ni batu boosu bakala zingila mu kinzunga kya Aziya, keti Bayuta keti bisi Ngeleti, báyuka ndinga ya Pfumu.
ACT 19:11 Nzambi kakala sala bidimbu bya kuyituka mu nzila ya Pholu.
ACT 19:12 Bwabuna bakala kusilaka kwena bambefu miledi kondilo bitemba bina byákala khundakana ku lutu lwandi; bimbefu byákala beluka amana bitembu bya mbi byákala lubuka.
ACT 19:13 Ndambu ya Bayuta bakala kwenda muma yi muma bakala meka kukula bitembu bya mbi mwena bana bakala byawu, yi kutumbulaka khumbu ya Pfumu Yesu; yi kuzonzaka: «Yiluheki muswa wa kulubuka mu khumbu ya Yesu wuna kabati longila Pholu!»
ACT 19:14 Hákala yi bana ba bayakala tsambwadya ba mosi wa bapfumu ba banganga Nzambi ba Bayuta, khumbu yandi Sevwa bakala sala bwabuna,
ACT 19:15 kaasi kitembu kya mbi kyábavutwala: «Yesu, yimuzayini, nzayi mboti phi keti nani kena Pholu; kaasi benu, banani lwenina?»
ACT 19:16 Amana mutu wuna wákala yi kitembu kya mbi wubabwidi, ngolu kákala kuluta bawu; watoma babeta boosu, bálubuka mu nzu yina, thinu, kikhonga yi phuta muna lutu.
ACT 19:17 Kindanda kiditi kwena boosu bana bisi zingila ku Efesu, Bayuta yi bisi Ngeleti; bweya bwábakwata boosu amana bazimbudi ni khumbu ya Pfumu Yesu yambuta yenina.
ACT 19:18 Balawu ha kati dya bana bákituka bakwikidi bakala kwisa mu kufunguna mihangu mya bawu ha mesu ma batu boosu.
ACT 19:19 Batu balawu bana bakala sadila mikisi, bakala nata mikanda mya bawu amana bayokimya kuna thwala ya batu boosu. Bátanga thalu ya mbongu ya mikanda meni, yákala makumatanu ma mafunda ma bibendi bya mbongu.
ACT 19:20 Bwabuna Ndinga ya Pfumu yakala mwanganina yi ngolu.
ACT 19:21 Kunima dya kusalama kwa mambu mana, Pholu wábonga lukanu, lwa kukwenda ku Yelusalemi mu kulutila mu nzila ya Masetwani yi Akayi. Kakala zimbula: «Buna yikatuka kuna, bwálunga ni yitula hika ku Loma.»
ACT 19:22 Kahanga wutumi bodi ba batu bandi bana bakala musadila ku Masetwani, Thimoti yi Elasiti, kaasi yameni wásala ndambu ya tangwa ku kinzunga kya Aziya.
ACT 19:23 Muna tangwa medina, mvwalangani za lawu zálubuka ku Efeso, kikuma kya Nzila ya Pfumu.
ACT 19:24 Mutu mosi, wakala yidika bima bya phalata, khumbu yandi Temethiyusi. Kakala yidika nzu za Nzambi za khunda-khunda za phalata kikuma kya nzambi wa mukhetu, Atedimisi amana mbongu za lawu kyakala balumbwala, yandi yi basadi bana bakala sala kisalu kimosi yi yandi.
ACT 19:25 Kábakhundikisa boosu kumosi yi batu bahika bana bakala sala yandi kisalu kimosi, amana wuzimbudi: «Bakwetu, luzayi ni kimvwama kyetu mu kisalu kyaki kyisi tuka.
ACT 19:26 Kinga lubati mona amana lubati yuka mana mabati hita; ka ku Efesu lwesi ku, kaasi mu kinzunga kya Aziya kyosu, Pholu meni wawuna kákwikisikini mulumba-lumba wa batu mu kuzimbula ni banzambi bana bahadi ku moku ma batu beku banzambi ba kyedika.
ACT 19:27 Mana mafwaniku lwesi kuzanga kisalu kya betu, kaasi mafwani phi kubebisa mambu ma ngolu ku nzu ya nzambi ya nzambi wa mukhetu Atedimisi yi kukulumuna kipfumu kyandi kina bisi fukamina mu kinzunga kya Aziya yi muna tsi yosu ndangu batu bamufukaminaku hika!»
ACT 19:28 Tangwa báyuka bwabuna, khabu zábakwata lawu amana báyandika mu kukalunga: «Wambuta kenina Atedimisi wa bisi Efeso!»
ACT 19:29 Mvalangani yákota muna mbanza yosu. Boosu, mu kimosi, benda ku tsaka amana bábakwata Kayosi yi Adisitadiki, bisi Masetwani bana bisa musindikila Pholu mu nzila amana bababulumuna yi kuna tsaka.
ACT 19:30 Pholu wázola kenda lubuka ku mesu ma mulumba-lumba wa batu kaasi balonguki bámukandisa.
ACT 19:31 Amana basadi ba leta bana bakala banduku bandi, bámuhitika ndinga mu kumubokwadila ni kendaku ku tsaka.
ACT 19:32 Bahika bakala kalunga kima kimosi, bakwawu kyahika; kikuma, mvwalangani lawu yakala ha kati dya kibuka. Batu balawu bázayaku kikuma kina báwongamina.
ACT 19:33 Ndambu ya batu, muna kibuka, bámutendwala Alekizande mana makala luta, amana bámulundika ndangu kahyoka ku thwala. Alekizande wáthuta koku ndangu kadikutumuna ku thwala ya kibuka.
ACT 19:34 Kaasi tangwa bámutungulula ni Muyuta kákala, boosu báyandika mu kukalunga mu kimosi, kitesu kya matangwa modi: «Wambuta kenina Atedimisi wa bisi Efeso!»
ACT 19:35 Kaasi musoniki wa pfumu wa mbanza wálenda mu kukandisa mulumba-lumba wa batu amana wuzimbudi: «Bayakala ba ku Efeso, nati wukondi zaya ni mbanza ya Efeso yena tsinzidi wa nzu ya nzambi ya nzambi wa mukhetu Atedimisi yi kiteki kyandi kina kyátuka ku zilu?
ACT 19:36 Mambu mana, heku mutu wufwani kuketyakisama. Bulungi ni lwalembama amana luhangaku dyambu konda kuyindula.
ACT 19:37 Kikuma, bayakala baba lwisi bawu, basawudiku, batukwaniku phi nzambi ya betu wa mukhetu.
ACT 19:38 Yukani Temethiyusi yi banduku bandi ba kisalu benina yi dyambu dya mutu, bazusi benina, nganda phi yenina, ndangu benda funda!
ACT 19:39 Amana yukani dyambu dyahika lwenina dyawu, mboti lwanatadya ku nganda yina yifwani kuzengadya bwosu buna milombini mitsiku.
ACT 19:40 Kikuma, fwani batufunda ni mavwanga tulubudi kikuma kya mambu mana malutini lelu, mukuma heku kima kibati tuheka muswa wa kukhokama kwaku.»
ACT 19:41 Kunima kuzonza bwabuna, wámwangakya kibuka kyosu.
ACT 20:1 Buna yámanisa mvwalangani, Pholu wátedisa balonguki; kunima dya kubasyamisa, wábaheka mboti ya tsuka ndangu kenda ku Masetwani.
ACT 20:2 Buna kálutila muna kinzunga meni kina, wátomasyamisa batu kwakuna, kunima wénda ku Ngelesi.
ACT 20:3 Kázakala ngonda tatu kwakuna, muna tangwa dina kázola kukota mu masuwa ndangu kalabuka ku Sidiya, wáyuka ni Bayuta bámukasidi kifwandu; amana wábonga lukanu lwa kuvutukila muna nzila ya Masetwani.
ACT 20:4 Hákala yi batu benda musindikila: Sophatela, mwana Philusi, mwisi Bele, Adisitadiki, Sekundusi mwisi Tesalonika, Kayusi mwisi Telebi, Thimoti, Tisiki yi Thofima bisi Aziya.
ACT 20:5 Baba-baba batekila kwenda, amana bátuhingila kuna Thowasi.
ACT 20:6 Kwena betu phi, kunima kilumbu kya mapha makonda muvimbu, twálabuka tukidila ku Fidiphu. Kunima bilumbu bitanu, tubawani kuna Thowasi, kwakuna, twánanga bilumbu tsambwadi.
ACT 20:7 Muna kilumbu kyatheti kya phosa, twákala bakutakana muna masikidika kikuma kya kubukuna dipha. Pholu, yandi mutu wákana ni kenda mu kilumbu kyalanda, kakala yambila yi batu bákala mu kimvuka. Amana wáleyisa kinzonzi tii yi muna kati kya phipha.
ACT 20:8 Mwinda mya lawu myákala ku mwanza wa ku zilu kuna twákala bakutakana.
ACT 20:9 Kaasi ngunza mosi wákala hana wazakala hana thandu ya nela, khumbu yandi Etiki. Hanga kilu kyamuluku-luku kimukwati muna tangwa dina kakala zonza Pholu; wáhukumuka ku kilu, wátukidila kuna nzu ya tatu ya ku londi, wudilembini hana tsi. Buna benda ni bamuvumbula, bámuwana wufi kedi.
ACT 20:10 Hanga Pholu wukulumukini, wázenzama hana kákala amana wámuzangula muna moku mandi; kunima wuzimbudi: «Lubangaku! Wamoya kenina!»
ACT 20:11 Tangwa kátombuka, wábukuna dipha kikuma kya kudya, kunima kázonza hika tangwa dya kaleyi yikuna kwakhyela kuma, kunima dya bwana, wénda.
ACT 20:12 Bámunata ngunza wuna wamoya, bwáhana kikesa kya lawu.
ACT 20:13 Kikuma kya betu, hanga thwendi theti mu masuwa yi kuna Asosi, kuna twafwana ni twamubongila Pholu. Yibwana káyidika, kikuma kazola ni kendila mu nzila ya mukhidi.
ACT 20:14 Buna katuwana ku Asosi, twámukotisa mu masuwa amana thwénda ku Miteleni.
ACT 20:15 Tuka kwakuna, twákangala mu yanga dya mbuta amana kilumbu kyálanda, twátula ku thwala Kiyo. Kilumbu kyalanda tutudi ku Samosi, amana ha kilumbu kyálanda, twátula ku Mile.
ACT 20:16 Kikuma, Pholu kákana ni kalutila ku kabeta ka Efesu, ndangu kalutisaku tangwa dyakhatu mu Aziya. Tswalu kakala kwenda ndangu katula ku Yelusalemi mu kilumbu kya Phandikoti.
ACT 20:17 Buna bákala hana Mile, Pholu wátuma ni babatedisa malemba ku Efesu.
ACT 20:18 Buna bátula kuna kákala yandi, wubazimbwadi: «Luzayibya mboti, benu, bikalulu byama ku thwala ya benu, tangwa dyosu, tuka kilumbu kyatheti, tangwa yidyata mu kinzunga kya Aziya.
ACT 20:19 Yímusadila Pfumu, mu kudikulumuna, mu matsanga, ha kati dya bimeka bina byándatina bifwandu bya Bayuta.
ACT 20:20 Konda kusweka kima, yílusamwana amana yílulonga moosu mana menina mupfunu, ku thwala ya batu boosu yi muna nzu zenu.
ACT 20:21 Yíbatendwala Bayuta yi Bangeleki ndangu basoba bikalulu, badihana kwena Nzambi amana bakwikila mwena Pfumu Yesu.
ACT 20:22 Buthwena, meni wakukasa yenina kwena Kitembu, yendi ku Yelusalemi, konda kuzaya mana makwenda mbwila kwakuna.
ACT 20:23 Kaasi nzayi kwama ni muna kosu mbanza yina, Kitembu kyatoma kisi tekilatsongila ni miyololu yi kiwayi bibati phingila kwakuna.
ACT 20:24 Kaasi meni luzingu lwama luhitiku mupfunu lawu. Kima kingyenina mupfunu lawu kutula yi kuna tsuka ya kisalu kyama yi kiyeka kápheka Pfumu Yesu: mu kuta kimbangi kya Musamu wa Bukheti wa khenda za Nzambi.
ACT 20:25 «Buthwena nzayi mboti ni, meni, lwambonaku hika, benu boosu muna yíhitila mu kulonga Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
ACT 20:26 Ihana ni thambwasibwa lelu kwena benu: wakasemi kwama yenina muna menga ma benu boosu.
ACT 20:27 Mukuma yílusamwana moosu mana kázenga Nzambi, konda kuluswekila kima.
ACT 20:28 Dikengenu benu-benu yi kwena kibuka kya mikoku mina káluhekila Kitembu Kyatoma khumbu ya bamvungi ba mikoku. Lundenu Dibundu dya Nzambi, dina kásumba mu menga mandi.
ACT 20:29 Nzayi mboti meni, ni kunima dya kwenda kwama, bakwisa kota hana kati dya benu bambwa-ngongu ba nganzi bana banyókuna kibuka kya mikoku.
ACT 20:30 Amana mu kati dya benu, batélama batu bahika bakwata zonza mambu ma luvunu ndangu bahungula balonguki kwena bawu.
ACT 20:31 Yihana ni kengilenu, lwabambuka phi ni mu mvula tatu, phipha yi mwini, mu matsanga, yikalaku lembwa mu kululwengisa, kosu mutu, mana makwísa ku thwala.
ACT 20:32 «Amana buthwena, yilusisi mu moku ma Nzambi yi muna ndinga ya khenda zandi. Yina yenina yi ngolu za kutunga yi kuhana bima bya bukheti kwena bana benina ba yandi.
ACT 20:33 Yínekaku keti mbongu, keti wolu keti miledi mya mutu.
ACT 20:34 Luzayibwa benu-benu: moku mama matsadisini mu kuvwa bima byosu yíkala byawu mupfunu yi kwena banduku bama.
ACT 20:35 Mu moosu, yílulonga ni mu kusala bwabuna lwabásadisila baphutu, mu kuyindulaka ndinga za Pfumu Yesu, yandi wázimbula yandi meni: "Kyesi kya lawu kyisi kala mu kukaba, keku ni mu kubonga!"»
ACT 20:36 Kunima kuzonza bwabuna, wáfukama kikuma kya kulombila ha kimosi yi bawu boosu.
ACT 20:37 Boosu mu bidilu, bámubumbakana Pholu amana bámuyamba.
ACT 20:38 Kyadi kya lawu bákala kyawu, kikuma kábazimbwala ni bamúmonaku hika. Kunima bénda musindikila yikuna masuwa.
ACT 21:1 Bwosu twáhambwasana yi bawu, twásabuka, amana twátadisa ku zawala dya Khosi; kilumbu kyalanda, twátula ku Lodi, amana ha twákatuka kwakuna, thwénda ku Phatala.
ACT 21:2 Buna twáwana kwakuna masuwa mana makala kwenda ku Fenisi; hanga tukoti mwamuna amana thwendi.
ACT 21:3 Buna twátula bela-bela yi Siphe, twásisadya ku koku dya kimama, amana twálanda sambwa dya Sidiya, ndangu twatula ku Tidi kuna máfwana masuwa mu kutulula bima.
ACT 21:4 Bwosu twáwana balonguki, twánanga kwakuna bilumbu tsambwadi. Baphangi, bálwengisa kwena Kitembu Kyatoma amana bázimbula kwena Pholu ni katombukaku ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 21:5 Kaasi tangwa yáhita phosa meni yina, twálanda nzila yetu. Bénda tusindikila boosu yi bakhetu yi bana ba bawu yi kuna phenza ya mbanza; twáfukama kuna kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta amana twásambila.
ACT 21:6 Kunima dya kudiheka mboti za tsuka, twákota mu masuwa, bawu bávutuka kwabawu.
ACT 21:7 Amana betu buna twámanisa kitambu kyetu mu mamba, thwénda tuka ku Tidi yikuna Tholemayasi. Kwakuna twábaheka baphangi mboti, hanga tunangi hika kilumbu kimosi yi bawu.
ACT 21:8 Kilumbu kyálanda, twákatuka, thwénda ku Sezale. Hanga thwendi ku nzu ya Fidiphu wuna wákala musamuni wa Musamu wa Bukheti, yandi kákala mosi hana kati dya bayakala tsambwadi bana básola ku Yelusalemi, twánanga kuna nzu yandi.
ACT 21:9 Kákala yi bandumba baya bana bakala bikula.
ACT 21:10 Bwosu twánanga kuna bilumbu byalawu, mbikudi mosi, khumbu yandi Hakabusi; wátuka ku Yuteya, wisa tula hakana.
ACT 21:11 Hanga wisi kuna twákala betu, wubongi mukaba wa Pholu, amana wudikasi malu yi moku, kunima wuzimbudi: «Tala mana kázimbudini Kitembu Kyatoma: Mutu yandu wuvwi mukaba wawu, Bayuta, kuna Yelusalemi, yi bwabubu bamúkasa, ndangu bamulambula kwena baphani.»
ACT 21:12 Buna twáyuka bwabuna, betu yi bana bákala hakana, twámubokwadila Pholu ndangu katombukaku ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 21:13 Hanga Pholu wuvutudi: «Kikuma kyabiki lubati didila yi kuphumuna mbundu? Meni yenina wayilama, ka kikuma kya kukhasa ku lwesi kaasi yi kikuma kya kufwila kuna Yelusalemi kikuma kya khumbu ya Pfumu Yesu.»
ACT 21:14 Bwosu kázolaku mu kutambwasa mana twakala muzimbwala betu, twákosikilaku hika ndinga amana tuzimbudini: «Yambula luzolu lwa Pfumu lwahangama!»
ACT 21:15 Ku manima ma kulutisa ndambu ya bilumbu kwakuna, twáyilama amana thwénda ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 21:16 Ndambu ya balonguki ba ku Sezale bisa tusindikila yi kuna twafwana kuleka, kuna nzu ya Nasoni mwisi Siphe; wákala mukwikidi tukidila thama.
ACT 21:17 Mu kutula kwetu ku Yelusalemi, baphangi bátuyamba yi kyesi.
ACT 21:18 Kilumbu kyálanda, Pholu wátunata ku nzu ya Zyaki; amana malemba moosu mísa kwakuna.
ACT 21:19 Wábaheka mboti amana wáyandika mu kutangumuna moosu mana káhanga Nzambi, mu nzila kisalu kyandi, ha kati dya baphani.
ACT 21:20 Ku manima ma kumuyuka, bámuzatula Nzambi. Hanga bamuzimbwadini: «Wumoni, phangi, keti makumi ma mafunda makwa ma Bayuta bakitukini bakwikidi; boosu babasi yi tsambu ya kuzitisa mitsiku.
ACT 21:21 Kamba báyuka ni muna malongi maku, ngeyi wubati tuma Bayuta boosu bana bisi zingila mu kati dya makanda ndangu babwisa mitsiku mya Moyize; kamba bayótisaku hika bana, balundaku phi hika mikuku mya kikanda.
ACT 21:22 Biki bifwani? Bayúka kaka ni wísikini.
ACT 21:23 Disongidila, sala kaka mana tukuzimbwadi. Henina ha kati dya betu yi bayakala baya básidiki lusilu.
ACT 21:24 Babonga, disemisa ha kimosi yi bawu amana bafutila mbongu, ndangu badikulula mutwa. Hanga boosu bazáya ni heku kima kya kyedika muna khululuka yina báyukiki kikuma kya ngeyi, kaasi ngeyi phi wisi lunda mitsiku.
ACT 21:25 Kikuma kya Baphani bana bakituki bakwikidi, betu, tumoniki ni mboti twabasonikina ni bayambula kudya mbisi batambiki kwena biteki, keti ba menga, yi bambisi ba bithitu, bayambula phi kindumba.»
ACT 21:26 Kilumbu kyalanda, Pholu wábonga batu meni babana, wádisemisa ha kimosi yi bawu amana wákota kuna nzu ya Nzambi mu kusamuna keti khi tangwa byamánisa bilumbu bya kudisemisa, keti khi tangwa phi batámbika kabu dya mosi yi mosi wa bawu.
ACT 21:27 Ku tsuka ya bilumbu bina tsambwadi, Bayuta ba ku kinzunga kya Aziya, bana bámumona mu nzu ya Nzambi, bálundika mulumba-lumba wa batu wosu amana bámukwata.
ACT 21:28 Bakala kalunga: «Bisi Kiseledi, tusadisenu! Mutu yandi, yandi wisi longa kwena boosu yi muma mwosu, mambu ma mbi matadidi betu Bayuta kikuma kya mitsiku mya Moyize yi kizika kyaki! Wukotisi phi bisi Ngeleki muna nzu ya Nzambi yi kusumunaka kizika kyaki kyatoma!»
ACT 21:29 Mukuma ku luyandiku bámona Thofimi mwisi Efeso ha kimosi yi yandi muna mbanza ya Yelusalemi, amana bakala yindula ni Pholu wámukotisa mu nzu ya Nzambi.
ACT 21:30 Mbanza yosu yekina mu mvwalangani, amana batu bálubuka muma mwosu. Bámukwata Pholu amana bámulubula mu nzu ya Nzambi, kunima dya bwabuna, báyafikila mwelu.
ACT 21:31 Bwosu bakala sanda mu kumuhonda, kindanda kiditi kwena tudibeni ni mvwalangani yikoti mu Yelusalemi dyosu.
ACT 21:32 Muna mbala mosi, yandi wábonga baphumbulu yi basatudiyoni amana wákulumuka thinu. Buna bámona tudibeni yi baphumbulu, báyambula kumubeta Pholu.
ACT 21:33 Hanga tudibeni wubwesuki amana wásenda ni bamukwata amana bamukasa mu miyololu myodi. Kunima wáhyula keti nani kákala yi biki káhanga.
ACT 21:34 Muna mulumba-lumba wa batu, kosu mutu kakala kalunga muna phila yandi amana pfumu wa baphumbulu funda ba Loma, kálendaku mu kuzaya kikuma kya kyedika muna mambu mana, wásenda ni bamunata ku Kaa dya baphumbulu.
ACT 21:35 Buna kátula Pholu mu sikadiye, baphumbulu bámuthuta, kikuma kya mvwalangani ya mulumba-lumba wa batu,
ACT 21:36 kikuma kibuka kya batu kyakala mulanda yi kukalungaka: «Kafwa!»
ACT 21:37 Buna bázola kumukotisa mu Kaa dya basuta, Pholu wázimbula kwena tudibeni: «Pfwani yikuzimbwala dyambu?» Pfumu wa baphumbulu wumuvutwadi: «Wuzayiya kuzonza Ngeleki?
ACT 21:38 Ka ngeyi ku mwisi Ngiphiti wuna wákotisa mvwalangani mu bilumbu bilutiki amana wátini mu nganga yi bandwandwa mafunda maya kikuma kya kunwanisa ngemba ya ku Loma?»
ACT 21:39 Pholu wumuvutwadi: «Meni yenina Muyuta wa ku Talasi dya ku kinzunga kya Sidisi, yíbutukila mu mbanza yina yizayakani. Yikubokwadidi, pheka muswa wa kuzonza kwena batu.»
ACT 21:40 Pfumu wa baphumbulu funda ba Loma wámuheka muswa. Pholu, wátelama muna sikadiye, wusongidi kidimbu kuna koku kwena batu. Talala dyákota. Hanga wuzimbudi kwena bawu mu ndinga ya Bayuta:
ACT 22:1 «Baphangi bama yi batata bama, yukenu buthwena mana yenina mawu mu kuluzimbwala kikuma kya kudikutumuna kwama.»
ACT 22:2 Buna báyuka ni kakala bazonzila mu ndinga ya Bayuta, talala dyekina hika dya lawu. Pholu wuzimbudini:
ACT 22:3 «Meni, yenina Muyuta. Yíbutwakila ku Talasi muna kinzunga kya Sidisi; kaasi muna mbanza meni yayi tsatsukidini, ndongwakidi phi, muna malu ma Ngamadyedi, yandi wuna wándonga mboti-mboti mitsiku mya batata betu. Yíkala mutu wabasa yi tsambu yiluti kitesu kikuma kya Nzambi, bwosu lweninabwa benu boosu lelu.
ACT 22:4 Yínyokuna yi kuna lufwa bana bakala landa Nzila yayi, mu kukwatisaka bakhetu yi bayakala yi kubakotisa mu boloku.
ACT 22:5 Keti mbuta wa banganga Nzambi yi kibuka kya mbuta kya malemba bafwani mu kuta kimbangi kyama. Yítambula phi kuna moku ma bawu mikanda mya nzila kikuma kya baphangi ba bayuta bana bisi landa Nzila yayi kuna Tamasi. Yenda kwakuna ndangu yikwata bana bákala kuna amana yibanata ku Yelusalemi ndangu babaheka ndola.»
ACT 22:6 «Mu nzila yíkala amana yikala bwesuka ku Tamasi, muna mbala mosi, muna mwinyakati, mitsyenzya mya lawu myátuka kuna zilu, myákyenzula homa hosu hana yíkala.
ACT 22:7 Hanga mbwini ha tsi amana ngyuki ndinga yimosi yakala nzimbwala: "Sawulu, Sawulu, kikuma kya biki wubati ndyokwanina?"
ACT 22:8 Hanga mvutudini: "Nati wenina ngeyi Pfumu?" Yandi wunzimbwadini: "Meni, yenina Yesu mwisi Nazaleti, wuna wubati nyokuna ngeyi."
ACT 22:9 Bana bákala yi meni bámona mitsyenzya, kaasi bábakulayoku ndinga ya wuna wakala nzonzisa.
ACT 22:10 Hanga nzimbudini: "Biki pfwani mu kuhanga, Pfumu?" Pfumu wunzimbwadini: "Telama, ndawenda kuna Tamasi, amana kwakuna bakúzimbwala moosu mana wufwana mu kuhanga."
ACT 22:11 Bwosu yikalaku mona hika, kikuma kya khembu ya mitsyenzya mina, bana bákala kumosi yi meni bátsimba kuna koku mu kundatisa, amana yítula ku Tamasi.
ACT 22:12 «Kinga hákala yi mutu mosi khumbu yandi Ananiya, mutu wakwikama mu mitsiku, wuna bakala hanina kimbangi kya mboti kwena Bayuta boosu bana bisi zingila kwakuna,
ACT 22:13 wísa kwena meni amana wunzimbwadi: "Sawulu, phangi wama, mona hika!" Muna tangwa medina, ngyandiki kumona hika, amana yimumoni.
ACT 22:14 Amana wunzimbwadi hika: "Nzambi wa batata betu wákusola mu kuzaya luzolu lwandi, ndangu wamona mutu wa Masonga amana wayuka ndinga yandi.
ACT 22:15 Mukuma wakála mbangi kikuma kya yandi, ku thwala boosu, muna mambu mana wumonini yi mana wuyukini.
ACT 22:16 Amana buthwena, biki wahánga? Telama, tambula mbotika, tumbula zina dya Pfumu ndangu wasukuka mu masumu maku."»
ACT 22:17 «Mu kuvutuka ku Yelusalemi, tangwa yikala lombila muna nzu ya Nzambi, mboni mbona mesu.
ACT 22:18 Amana yimumoni Pfumu, wuna wánzimbwala: "Hanga tswatsu, katuka tswatsu ku Yelusalemi, mukuma batu bana batámbwasakyoku kimbangi kyaki wathíla."
ACT 22:19 Meni mvutudini: "Pfumu, bazayi mboti ni yikala kwenda muna kosu nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta mu kusya yi kubetisa bana bisi kwikila mwena ngeyi.
ACT 22:20 Amana tangwa bánokisa menga ma mbangi waku Kitsyeni, hana yíkala meni-meni, yíbatambwasa, yikala simba miledi mya batu bana bámuhonda."
ACT 22:21 Hanga wunzimbwadini: «Ndawenda, meni yikútuma kwena baphani!"»
ACT 22:22 Bámuhyinikina tii yi kuna ndinga yayi; kaasi hanga bathuti ndinga amana bazimbudi: «Kafwa! Ka mboti ku mu kusisa mutu wa mutindu wawu ni kazinga mu tsi yayi!»
ACT 22:23 Bakala kalunga, kulosa miledi mya bawu yi kutimbulaka mufututu muna zilu.
ACT 22:24 Tudibeni wásenda ni bamukotisa mu kaa dya baphumbulu amana bamubeta kikuma kya kumuzonzisa, ndangu bazaya kikuma kina bakala mukalwangina bwabuna kikuma kya yandi.
ACT 22:25 Bwosu bakala mukasa yi tsibu, Pholu wázimbula kwena satudiyoni wuna wákala hana: «benu, lufwani kubetisa fimbu mwisi mbedi ya Loma yandu bakondi sambisa?»
ACT 22:26 Tangwa káyuka bwabuna, satudiyoni wenda menika kwena tudibeni, wumuzimbwadi: «Biki wahánga? Mudyambu mutu yandu kenina mwisi Loma!»
ACT 22:27 Tudibeni wísa kwena Pholu amana wumuzimbwadi: «Nzimbwala, ngeyi, mwisi Loma wenina?» «Eeh», wuvutudi bwabuna.
ACT 22:28 Tudibeni wuvutwakidi hika: «Meni, mu mbongu za lawu yíbongila muswa wawu!» Pholu wuvutudini: «Meni, tukidila lubutuku lwama.»
ACT 22:29 Muna tangwa medina, batu bana bázola mu kumuzonzisa, báhaluka kyana; amana tudibeni wáyuka bweya, kikuma kya buna kábakula ni mwisi Loma wuna kakasisikini.
ACT 22:30 Kilumbu kyalanda, mu kusanda kazaya kyedika kina bakala mufundila, Pholu, kwena Bayuta, wámukutwamisa misinga amana wásenda kwena bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi kimvuka kyosu mu kukutakana; kunima, wámukulumuna Pholu amana wámusya kuna thwala ya bawu.
ACT 23:1 Pholu wábatala kuna mbunzu batu bákala ha mbasi, wuzimbudi: «Baphangi bama, kikuma kya meni, yi katsatsa ka bukheti kosu yisi zingila ku mesu ma Nzambi, yi kuna lelu dyadi.»
ACT 23:2 Mbuta wa banganga Nzambi Ananiya wásenda kwena bana bákala bela-bela yi yandi ni bamubetila ku munwa.
ACT 23:3 Hanga Pholu wumuzimbwadi: «Nzambi wakúbeta ngeyi, kibaka basiti phemba! Ngeyi wenina wasikuka haka kikuma kya kupfundisa buna bulombi mitsiku yi mana matadidiku mitsiku, wubati senda ni bambeta!»
ACT 23:4 Bana bákala bela-bela yi yandi bázimbula: «Wubati tukwana mbuta wa banganga Nzambi!»
ACT 23:5 Pholu wuvutudi: «Nzayikiku, baphangi bama, ni mbuta wa banganga Nzambi kákadiki. Kikuma, básonika bwabu muna Masonuku: "Wazónzilaku mbi ya pfumu wa kanda dyaku!"»
ACT 23:6 Bwosu kázaya ni ha kati dya kimvuka kyambuta hákala yi Basadise yi Bafwadisi, hanga Pholu wuyandiki kukalunga: «Baphangi bama, meni yenina Mufwadisi, mwana wa Bafwadisi! Yukani meni babati pfundisa, kikuma kya kivuvu mu lufutumuku lwa bamvumbi.»
ACT 23:7 Tangwa kázonza bwabuna, ngyuma zábwa hana kati dya Bafwadisi yi Basadise, amana kimvuka kyádikabisa.
ACT 23:8 Kikuma Basadise, bawu, bisi zimbula ni kweku lufutumuku, keti wanzyo, keti kitembu kaasi Bafwadisi, bawu, bisi kwikila muna byosu bina.
ACT 23:9 Báthuta hika ndinga, hanga ndambu ya balongi ba mitsiku bana bákala ku mukanzu wa Bafwadisi bátelama amana bábwisa mu ndinga ya ngolu: «Tumoniku keti mbi mwena mutu yandu. Amana yukani kitembu kondilo wanzyo wumuzonzidikini!»
ACT 23:10 Bwosu zakala vula ngyuma, tudibeni wáyuka bweya ni bamubukununa nana Pholu, hanga wusendi kwena baphumbulu bandi ni bakulumuka amana bamukatula Pholu ha kati dya bawu amana bamukotisa mu kati dya kaa dya baphumbulu.
ACT 23:11 Phipha yalanda, Pfumu wisa mulubwakila amana wuzimbudi: «Kikesa! Bwosu buna wuthidi kimbangi ku Yelusalemi, bwabuna phi wánata kimbangi ku Loma.»
ACT 23:12 Tangwa kwakya kuma, Bayuta bákasa kifwandu amana balabi ni badyáku, banwáku phi keti kima yukani khaku kedi bamuhonda Pholu.
ACT 23:13 Bakasi ba kifwandu kina bákala thalu kuluta makumaya.
ACT 23:14 Bénda bamona bapfumu ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba dibundu ndangu babazimbwala: «Tudikini thiti ni twadyáku kedi kima yukani khaku bamuhonda Pholu.
ACT 23:15 Buthwena, benu, yukanenu yi bakwa mukanzu wambuta ndangu balomba kwena tudibeni, ni bamukulumuna Pholu ku thwala ya benu. Hanga mbedi ni lubati zola lwalonguka yi masingitini dyambu dyandi. Amana betu, hanga tuswamini ndangu twamuhonda konda katula kedi.»
ACT 23:16 Kaasi mwana khasi wa Pholu wáyuka kuzonzila kifwandu mekina amana wénda kuna kaa dya baphumbulu, wákota kwakuna mu kumuzimbwala Pholu.
ACT 23:17 Pholu wátela mosi wa basatudiyoni amana wumuzimbwadi: «Munata mwana yakala yandi kwena tudibeni, mukuma kenina yi ndinga ya kumuzimbwala.»
ACT 23:18 Satudiyoni wuna wámubonga, wámunata phi kwena tudibeni amana wuzimbudi: «Pholu wuna wenina mu boloku, káthedini amana wundombi ni yisa kunatina mwana yakala yandi wenina yi ndinga ya kukuzimbwala.»
ACT 23:19 Tudibeni wámusimba muna koku, wénda ku phengu amana wámuhyula: «Biki wuzodi wanzimbwala?»
ACT 23:20 Yandi wávutula: «Bayuta báyukani ndangu bakulomba ni mbasi wamúkulumuna Pholu ku thwala kimvuka kyambuta, hanga mbedi ni yandi zodi kalonguka mboti dyambu dyandi.
ACT 23:21 Kaasi ngeyi, wubayukilaku, mukuma, batu kuluta makumaya, hana kati dya bawu, bamúleka mutambu. Bádikini thiti ni badyaku kima keti kunwa yuka ni khaku kedi bamuhonda Pholu. Buthwena, bayilama benina amana dibanza dya ngeyi babati hingila.»
ACT 23:22 Kunima dya kumukandikisa mwana yakala wuna ni kamenikinaku kwena mutu, mambu mana kámuzimbwala, hanga tudibeni wumuvutudini.
ACT 23:23 Kunima, tudibeni wátedisa basatudiyoni boodi amana wubazimbwadi: «Bongenu baphumbulu khama zoodi yi bakwawu makumi tsambwadi bana bisi zanza ha thandu ya baphunda yi bakwawu hika khama zoodi bana benina yi madyonga ndangu bayilama mu kukwenda ku Sezale mu tangwa dya vwa dya phipha.
ACT 23:24 Yidikenu phi baphunda kikuma kya kumunatina Pholu kwena pfumu wa kinzunga Fidikisi.»
ACT 23:25 Hanga wusoniki kisyati bwabu:
ACT 23:26 «Kodiyusi Dizyasi, kwena mutu wa mayedi pfumu wa kinzunga Fidikisi, mboti.
ACT 23:27 Mutu yandu, Bayuta bámukwati, amana bázodikini ni bamuhonda wadi yendiku yakidilaka yi kibuka kya baphumbulu bama; ngyukiki ni mwisi mbedi ya Loma kenina.
ACT 23:28 Bwosu nzodikini mu kuzaya kikuma kina bakamufundilaka, yímukulumuna kuna thwala ya kimvuka kya bawu kyambuta.
ACT 23:29 Mbakisi ni muna mambu matadidi mitsiku mya bawu bakadi mufundila, kaasi hákalaku keti kima kifwani kumunatina lufwa holo miyololu.
ACT 23:30 Buna bándwengisiki ni bakasi kifwandu kikuma kya mutu yandu, yikuhitiki yandi mbala mosi, yibazimbwadiki bana bamufundiki, ni benda mufunda kwena ngeyi.»
ACT 23:31 Baphumbulu báhanga bwosu kituma kina bátambula, bámubonga Pholu amana bámunata phipha-phipha yikuna Atiphatisi.
ACT 23:32 Kilumbu kyálanda, bávutuka ku kaa dya baphumbulu básisa lwesi bakwa baphunda mu kukwenda yi Pholu.
ACT 23:33 Buna bátula ku Sezale, hanga bahani mukanda kwena pfumu wa mbanza amana bamusongidi yandi Pholu.
ACT 23:34 Kunima dya kutanga mukanda, pfumu wa kinzunga wumuhyudi Pholu keti mwisi khi kinzunga kákala. Buna káyuka ni mwisi Sidisi kákala,
ACT 23:35 hanga wumuzimbwadini: «Yikuyuka nana tangwa bakwísa bana bákufundikini.» Amana wásenda ni bamuphatila mu nganda ya Eloti.
ACT 24:1 Kunima bilumbu bitanu, nganga Nzambi wa mbuta Ananiya wákulumuka ku Sezale ha kimosi yi ndambu ya malemba yi nganzi mosi, khumbu yandi Teditulusi. Bámufunda Pholu kwena pfumu wa kinzunga Fidikisi.
ACT 24:2 Bámutedisa Pholu amana Teditulusi wáyandika mu kumufunda bwabu: «Pfumu, kikuma kya kisalu kyaku yi buna wubati yidikila mambu ma tsi yayi, hahana thwenina yi ngemba ya singu yayi.
ACT 24:3 Thwisibya zaya kosu tangwa yi muma mwosu yi mbundu yimosi, pfumu wambuta Fidikisi.
ACT 24:4 Kaasi, mukusya ni yikuhitisaku tangwa ngeyi, yikubokwadidi ni watambwasa mu kutuhinikina yi kyesi kyosu muna koma ka tangwa.
ACT 24:5 Kikuma tumoniki ni, mutu yandu kenina mvwanzi. Ngyuma kisi sanda hana kati dya Bayuta boosu, hana tsi yina bisi zingila; kenina mutwadisi wa dingumba dya bisi Nazaleti.
ACT 24:6 Kázodiki phi ni kasumuna nzu ya Nzambi, hahana twámukwatidini. [Tuzodiki ni twamufungwasa bwosu mibati lombila mitsiku myetu,
ACT 24:7 kaasi Dizyasi pfumu wa baphumbulu wisi yakidila amana wumubotudi mu moku ma betu,
ACT 24:8 hangi tutumi thwisa mufunda ku thwala ya ngeyi.] Wufwani kumuhyula ngemeni, ndangu wazikisa moosu mana tubati mufundila.»
ACT 24:9 Bayuta boosu bátambwasa hanga mbedi ni bwa bukheti bwákala bwabuna.
ACT 24:10 Kunima dya kumusongila mu kidimbu ndangu kazonza kwena pfumu wa kinzunga, Pholu wátambula ndinga, wuzimbudini: «Nzayibwa ni tukidila ndambu ya mvula za lawu wenina zusi wa tsi yayi, yi kivuvu kyosu yisámbila ku mesu ma ngeyi.
ACT 24:11 Bwosu wufwani wazikisabwa ngeyi-meni, khaku kedi hahita bilumbu kumi yi byodi, tukidila buna yitombukidi ku Yelusalemi mu kufukamina Nzambi.
ACT 24:12 Bángwanaku keti muna nzu ya Nzambi, keti muna nzu za kimvuka za Bayuta, keti muna mbanza ni mbati finda phaka yi mutu kondilo kulundika mulumba-lumba wa batu.
ACT 24:13 Baléndaku, buthwena bwabu, mu kukusongila kima kina babati pfundila.
ACT 24:14 Kaasi, nzayibwa ku thwala ya ngeyi ni muna Nzila meni yayina, babati tela bawu ni yambi, mwamuna phi yisi sambidila Nzambi wa batata betu; yisi kwikila phi muna mambu mana básonika mu Mitsiku yi Bambikudi.
ACT 24:15 Yenina yi kivuvu mwena Nzambi, bawu meni phi bazayibwa ni lufutumuku lwakála kikuma kya batu ba masonga yi batu ba mbi.
ACT 24:16 Yihakana, meni phi, yisi sila ngolu ni yikala yi katsatsa ka bukheti, ku mesu ma Nzambi keti kwena batu.
ACT 24:17 «Kunima mvula za lawu yísa ku Yelusalemi mu kuhana mulambu wa khenda kikuma kya batu ba tsi yama yi kutambika makabu kwena Nzambi.
ACT 24:18 Hahana bángwana mu nzu ya Nzambi. Wakasemi, konda kulumbika batu keti mvwalangani.
ACT 24:19 Kaasi ndambu ya Bayuta lwesi bátuka ku Aziya bákala hana, bawu bafwaniki kwisa telama ku thwala ngeyi mu kupfunda, yukani kima benina kyawu kitadidi meni.
ACT 24:20 Kondilo, baba bazimbula keti khi kifu bakhwatiki kyawu tangwa batsambisiki ku thwala ya kibuka kyambuta.
ACT 24:21 Akolu yakala ndinga yina yíthuta, wa mutendendi kuna thwala bawu: "Kikuma kya lufutumuku lwa bafwa, meni, tsambidi lelu, ku thwala ya benu!"»
ACT 24:22 Fidikisi, yandi, wátekila dizayila mambu mana matadidi Nzila, wávutulakya kinzonzi mu kilumbu kyahika. Wubazimbwadi: «Tangwa kakwísa tudibeni Dizyasi, hanana yítaladya dyambu dya benu.»
ACT 24:23 Kásenda kwena satudiyoni ni kamutalaka amana kamusisila ndambu ya tangwa dya kusala luzolu lwandi, konda kukandikisa ni bakwawu khunda bamusadisa.
ACT 24:24 Kunima dya ndambu ya bilumbu, Fidikisi wísa yi mukhetu wandi Thusila, wuna wákala muyuta. Amana wátuma ni benda mubonga Pholu. Wámuhinikina buna kakala zonzila mambu matadidini lukwikilu mwena Yesu Kidisitu.
ACT 24:25 Kaasi bwosu kakala zonzila, pholu, mu mambu matadidi khadidi ya masonga yi kusipha kwa mbundu yi pfundusu yina yakwísa, Fidikisi, bweya bwámukwata, wumuzimbwadi: «Buthwena, awenda kwaku; Ha yimóna tangwa, yikútedisa.»
ACT 24:26 Kakala yi kivuvu ni ngatu Pholu makuta kamuheka; yihana kakala muzyetisila ndangu basolulaka yi yandi.
ACT 24:27 Mvula zodi záhita bwabuna, kunima Fidikisi bámuhingana kwena Phokuyusi Fesitusi. Bwosu kázola ni kabasephidisa Bayuta, Fidikisi wámusisa Pholu muna boloku.
ACT 25:1 Tangwa káyandika Fesitusi kisalu muna kinzunga, bilumbu bitatu byáhita. Wákatuka ku Sezale mu kukwenda ku Yelusalemi.
ACT 25:2 Bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bapfumu ba Bayuta bisa mufunda Pholu kwena yandi. Bakala mubokwadila
ACT 25:3 mu kulomba lusadisu lwa kumutedisa ku Yelusalemi. Bakala mukasila fwongu balenga muhondila mu nzila.
ACT 25:4 Kaasi Fesitusi wávutula ni Pholu mu boloku dya ku Sezadi kákala amana ka thama ku, yandi meni kákhana vutukisa kuna Sezadi.
ACT 25:5 Hanga wuyikini: «Bambuta, hana kati dya benu, bakulumuka yi meni; amana yukani mutu meni wuna dyambu dya mbi káhanga, bamufunda.»
ACT 25:6 Fesitusi kánangaku bilumbu nana keti kumi kwena bawu, kunima wávutuka ku Sezale. Kilumbu kyalanda, wásikuka kuna nganda ya bazusi amana wásenda ni bisa yandi Pholu.
ACT 25:7 Buna kátula Pholu, Bayuta bana bátuka ku Yelusalemi bámuzyeta amana bámukasila misamu mya lawu mya mbi mina balendaku keti bawu meni mu kubangumuna.
ACT 25:8 Kaasi Pholu wádikutumuna mu kuzimbula: «Tsumuniku kima, keti mu mutsiku wa Bayuta, keti mana matadidi nzu ya Nzambi, keti mana matadidi Khayisala.»
ACT 25:9 Bwosu kázola Fesitusi mu kusephidisa Bayuta, hanga wuhyudi kwena Pholu: «Wutambwasi mu kutombuka ku Yelusalemi ndangu wenda samba dyambu meni dina ku thwala ya meni?»
ACT 25:10 Pholu wuvutudini: «Watelama yenina ha mbasi ya bazusi ya Khayisala, amana kwakuku kwa fwani batsambisila. Phangiku kima kyambi kwena Bayuta, bwosu wuzayididibwa ngeyi-meni.
ACT 25:11 Yukani mu kibela yenina, kina kifwani kundatina lufwa, mbwisiku kufwa. Kaasi yukani mweku dyambu dya mukwandi muna moosu mana babati pfundila batu baba, heku mutu wenina yi muswa wa kundambula kwena bawu. Ihana ni ndombi mu kukwenda samba kwena Khayisala.»
ACT 25:12 Hanga Fesitusi, kunima kuyambila yi batu bandi, wuvutudi: «Bwosu wulombikibwa ngeyi meni mu kukwenda samba kwena Khayisala, wakwénda phi kuna thwala Khayisala.»
ACT 25:13 Kunima ndambu ya bilumbu, kyamvu Angidipha yi Belenisi bátula kuna Sezale ndangu bamuheka mboti Fesitusi.
ACT 25:14 Bwosu bálutisa ndambu ya bilumbu kwakuna, Fesitusi wámenika dyambu dya Pholu kwena kyamvu, mu kuzimbula: «Fidikisi mutu mosi kasala kwatisa muna boloku.
ACT 25:15 Buna yenda ku Yelusalemi, bambuta ba banganga Nzambi yi bambuta ba Bayuta bámufunda mu kulomba ndola ya yandi.
ACT 25:16 Yíbavutwala ni bisi Loma bisiku kala yi kikalulu kya kulambula mutu mosi, konda kukhundikisa musambi yi bafundi amana kabonga tangwa dya kudikutumuna ku mambu ma bawu mana mabati muyangisa.
ACT 25:17 Hanga bísa yi kwaku nzila mosi yi meni. Konda kuhitisa tangwa, kilumbu meni kina kyalanda, nzakadi kuna nganda ya bazusi, amana tsendi ni bamunata mutu wuna.
ACT 25:18 Tangwa bátelama bafundi bandi, bamufundaku keti mu dyambu dimosi dya mbi dina yikala mubanzila meni.
ACT 25:19 Phaka lwesi bakala findana kikuma kya mambu ma bunzambi bwa bawu yi kikuma kya mutu mosi wuna bisi tela Yesu, wáfwa amana Pholu kisi tambwasa ni moya kenina.
ACT 25:20 Kwena meni, yíkala tsukungu ku thwala ya dyambu dya mutindu wuna, yímuhyula ni yuka katónda mu kukwenda ku Yelusalemi ndangu benda musambisila dyambu meni dina kwakuna.
ACT 25:21 Kaasi Pholu wálomba, ndangu dyambu dyandi bazengiladya kwena pfumu wa mbuta wa Loma. Hangi phani muswa ni bamusya mu boloku yikuna yimúhitikila kwena Khayisala.»
ACT 25:22 Angidipha wuzimbudi kwena Fesitusi: «Meni phi, yitonda kumuhinikina mutu meni wuna.» Fesutusi wumuvutwadini: «Mbasi wamúhinikina.»
ACT 25:23 Kilumbu kyalanda, Angidipha yi Belenisi bátula yi lukumu lwosu amana bákota muna suku dya nganda, kumosi yi batudibeni yi batu ba luzitu ba mu mbanza. Bisa yandi Pholu, bwosu kásenda Fesitusi.
ACT 25:24 Hanga Fesitusi wuzimbudini: «Kyamvu Angidipha, yi benu boosu lwenina haka kumosi yi betu, talenu mutu yandu bisa funda kwena meni! Kibuka kyosu kya Bayuta, kwakala ku Yelusalemi, kwakala kwaku, boosu babati kalunga ni káfwanaku hika mu kuzinga.
ACT 25:25 Kwena meni, yímona ni kahangiku keti kima kafwani kufwila. Kaasi bwosu kálombi yandi meni ni pfumu wa mbuta wa Loma kenda musambisa, meni phi yímonibwa bukheti mu kumuhitika yandi.
ACT 25:26 Bwosu yeku yi dyambu dya tsikiningi pfwani yimusonikina pfumu wa mbuta mu mana mamutadi; yimutelamisi ku thwala ya benu, theti kwena ngeyi kyamvu Angidipha, ndangu kunima dya byufu byaku, yibonga kima kya kusonika.
ACT 25:27 Mukuma, mbonibwoku bukheti mu kuhitika mutu wa boloku konda kutendula dyambu dina babati mufundila.»
ACT 26:1 Angidipha wázimbula kwena Pholu: «Tendula dyambu dyaku.» Hanga Pholu wáthuta koku kuna zilu, amana wáyandika mu kusamba:
ACT 26:2 «Mu kyesi yenina, kyamvu Angidipha, mu kusamba lelu ku thwala ya ngeyi kikuma kya mambu moosu mana bisi pfundila Bayuta,
ACT 26:3 mukuma wuzayimya bukheti, mikiku mya Bayuta yi phaka za bawu. Yikubokwadidi ni wangyuka yi sipha dya mbundu.
