GAL 4:25 Kinga Akadi, yandi mongu wa Sinayi kuna Alabiya; amana lelu, wufwanakani yi mbanza ya Yelusalemi, mukuma mu kihika yenina yi bana bandi boosu.
GAL 4:26 Kaasi Yelusalemi dina dya ku zilu dyeku mu kihika, amana phi yandi ngudi wetu.
GAL 4:27 Kikuma masonuku mazimbudi bwabu: «Zatuka, ngeyi mukhetu yandu wakonda buta! Sika biyekiyeki, ngeyi wakonda yuka misongu mya kubutila! Mukuma, bana ba mukhetu wuna bálosila bahitakani lawu kuluta babana ba mukhetu wuna wenina yi yakala dyandi.»
GAL 4:28 Kwena benu, baphangi bama, lwenina bana ba kilangi kya Nzambi hanga Yizaki.
GAL 4:29 Kaasi bwosu bwákala mbala yikwawu, mwana wuna wábutukila bwosu bwisi butuka mwana wosu kakala yangisa wuna wábutukila bwosu kyenina Kitembu kya Nzambi. Bwabuna bubati salama phi buthwena.
GAL 4:30 Kaasi biki mazonzi Masonuku? Bwabu: «Mukula muhika yi mwana wandi; mukuma, mwana muhika kalungiku mu kukala swana hakimosi yi mwana wa mukhetu wa longu.»
GAL 4:31 Yibwana, baphangi bama, betu thweku bana ba muhika, kaasi bana ba mukhetu wa longu.
GAL 5:1 Kidisitu watulubula kedi mu kihika ndangu katuheka kiphwanza. Zyamenu mboti, amana ludivutulaku hika ku sina dya muteti wa kihika.
GAL 5:2 Yukenu! Meni Pholu, mukyedika mbati luzimbwala bwabu: ho lwadiyotisisa, Kidisitu kakálaku hika mupfunu kwena benu.
GAL 5:3 Amana thambwasibwa hika kwena mutu wosu wuna wuzodi ni kadiyotisisa: kenina yi pfuka ya kulemvuka ku mitsiku myosu.
GAL 5:4 Benu lwisi sanda ni lwadinungisaka ku mesu ma Nzambi, mu nzila ya mitsiku, bahakuka lwenina yi Kidisitu; lwatámbulazoku khenda za Nzambi.
GAL 5:5 Kwena betu, thwisi sya kivuvu kyetu kyosu mwena Nzambi, wuna watúkitula batu ba masonga ku mesu mandi; yibwana thwisi hingila, mu ngolu za Kitembu Kyatoma wuna wisi sala mu nzila ya lukwikilu lwetu.
GAL 5:6 Mukuma, mwena Kidisitu Yesu, kima kilutini mupfunu kyeku ni kukota mukhanda holo ngulungu: Kima kilutini mupfunu, kyenina lukwikilu luna lwisi monikina mu lungongu.
GAL 5:7 Lwakala takalala kwenu mboti! Nati wulukandisini ndangu lulemvukaku ku kyedika?
GAL 5:8 Kukwikisa meni kwakuna kutukiku kwena Nzambi wuna wisi lutela.
GAL 5:9 Bwosu bisi zonza: «Muvimbu wa mapha wuna wisi thutumuna kithoba kyosu, wa khunda wisi kala».
GAL 5:10 Yihana yisi sila mbundu mwena Pfumu kikuma kya mambu mana malutadidini: yenina yi kikumbwala ni lwabánzaku hika mu mutindu wahika wuna wuswaswani yi wuna wa meni. Kaasi mutu wuna wisi luvwadingisa, kakala nani, katámbulaya ndola.
GAL 5:11 Kwena meni, baphangi, yuka ni yilongaka hika kukota kwa mukhanda; kikuma kya biki bisi ndyokwana hika? Yuka yibwabuna dyenina, kusamuna mambu matadi kitakani meku hika kisinza kya kubwisisa.
GAL 5:12 Yambulenu babana babati luvwadingisa, benda hika kyana mu mambu ma bawu: badizotununa hika lawu!
GAL 5:13 Kaasi benu baphangi, bálutela lwazingila mu kiphwanza. Kima kimosi lwesi, kiphwanza kina kiluhekaku nzila ya kuzingila mu lutu. Kaasi, yambulenu lungongu lwaludyatisa ndangu lwadisadisaka benu yi benu.
GAL 5:14 Mukuma mitsiku myosu myálungila kedi muna ndinga yimosi: «Wazóla khunda waku hanga ngeyi-meni.»
GAL 5:15 Kaasi yukani lwadilunzaka holo lwadivukulaka benu yi benu, kebenu lwadizanga nana benu yi benu.
GAL 5:16 Nzodi yiluzimbwala: yambulenu Kitembu kaludyatisa ndangu lulemvukaku hika ku nzoluka ya lutu.
GAL 5:17 Mukuma lutu lwenina yi nzoluka yandi yina yisi tendana yi nzoluka ya Kitembu, amana Kitembu kenina yi nzoluka yandi yina yibati tendana yi yina ya lutu: lutu yi Kitembu bisi tendana bawu bodi; mu phila ni lulendaku mu kulungisa mana luzodi mu kusala.
GAL 5:18 Kaasi yukani Kitembu wuludyatisini, lweku hika ku sina dya mitsiku.
GAL 5:19 Kinga mihangu mya lutu myisi monika: mbongi, mvindu, kisakasaka,
GAL 5:20 kufukamina banzambi ba biteki, kiloki, tsita, batu kudimenga bawu yi bawu, kiphala, khabu, kudimonikisa ku thwala batu, kudihambula mu bimvuka yi ngyengu,
GAL 5:21 kuzoluka, kuzela malafu, kudya kwa pfita, yi mambu mahika ma lawu mambi. Yiluzimbwadini bwosu yitekila luzimbwala: batu babana bisi hanga mambu ma buna, bakálaku yi kizika mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi.
GAL 5:22 Kaasi kibundu kya Kitembu kyenina: lungongu, kyesi, ngemba, kuvibidila, lutondu lwa bakwenu, buweti, lukwikilu,
GAL 5:23 ndembamu, kukanga kwa mbundu. Heku mutsiku wubwisima mambu ma mutindu wuna!
GAL 5:24 Amana babana benina mwena Kidisitu Yesu, bákhokalwa ha kitakani lutu yi mambu ma lwawu yi nzoluka ya lwawu.
GAL 5:25 Yukani twazingilaka mu Kitembu, tudyatilenu phi mu Kitembu.
GAL 5:26 Tukatulenu kimvunya, tuyumanakaku betu yi betu, tuzolukakaku phi bima betu yi betu.
GAL 6:1 Baphangi bama, ho ni mutu mosi bamukwata mu kifu, benu lwisi zingila mu kitembu, muvutulenu mu nzila yi ndembamu yosu. Kaasi kebenu benu phi, lwabwanana mu kimeka.
GAL 6:2 Natenu bizitu benu yi benu; yibwana lwalungisila mitsiku mya Kidisitu.
GAL 6:3 Amana mutu wuna wisi divuninika, kinga keku yi kima, kisi dihuna yandi-meni.
GAL 6:4 Kosu mutu katala miza mya yandi-meni; ndangu kamona yuka ni kyesi myamúheka. Kaasi kaditesaku yi mukwawu.
GAL 6:5 Mukuma, kosu mutu kiyeka kyandi kanáta.
GAL 6:6 Mutu wuna bisi longa Ndinga ya Nzambi, kakabisa bima byandi yi wuna wisiya mulonga.
GAL 6:7 Luditotisaku, mukuma Nzambi bisiku museya. Kyosu kina kakuni mutu, kyakina kahéla.
GAL 6:8 Wuna wisi kuna kikuma kya lutu lwa yandi-meni, kahéla phi bina lwisi buta lutu, disongidila lufwa; kaasi wuna wisi kuna kikuma kya Kitembu, kahéla phi bina kisi buta Kitembu, disongidila luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula.
GAL 6:9 Tulembwaku mu kusala mambu mamboti; mukuma yuka ni tukatudiku kikesa, twahéla bibundu byetu muna tangwa dya bukheti.
GAL 6:10 Yihana ni buna thwenina yi tangwa, tusadilenu kikuma kya mamboti ma batu boosu, kuluta kikuma kya mamboti ma batu babana thwenina bawu mu kimvuka kimosi kya lukwikilu.
GAL 6:11 Talenu tulamba twa bisona byabi yilusonikini ku koku dya meni-meni!
GAL 6:12 Boosu bana bisi lulundika mu kukota mukhanda, babana bisi zola kudisongila ku thwala ya batu ni ba mboti benina. Kima kimosi lwesi bábwisa bawu, banyokukaku kikuma kya kitakani kya Kidisitu.
GAL 6:13 Kikuma bawu-meni bana bisi kota mukhanda, bisimyoku zitisa mitsiku; kaasi bisi zola ni benu lwakota mukhanda ndangu balenga ditsikisilaka mu lutu lwa benu.
GAL 6:14 Kwena meni, bwalendakanaku ni yisya lulendu lwama mu phamba yuka ni lweku mu kitakani kya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu. Mwamuna muna bákhokilaya tsi kikuma kya meni, hanga meni kikuma kya tsi.
GAL 6:15 Mukuma kima kilutini mupfunu, kyeku ni kukota mukhanda kondilo kukonda kota mukhanda, kaasi kubutuka mutu wa pha.
GAL 6:16 Amana boosu bana balánda dilongi dyadi: ngemba yi khenda za Nzambi byakala kwena bawu bwosu mu Kiseledi kya Nzambi.
GAL 6:17 Tukidila lelu, ka mutu ku kangyangisa; mukuma meni yenina yi bidimbu bya phasi za Yesu muna lutu lwama.
GAL 6:18 Yambula khenda za Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu zakala yi kitembu kyenu, baphangi bama. Abwabuna!
EPH 1:1 Meni Pholu, thumwa wa Kidisitu Yesu, muna luzolu lwa Nzambi. Kwena bakwikidi ba Nzambi benina [ku Efesu]; babana básila mbundu, benina mwena Kidisitu Yesu:
EPH 1:2 Yambula Nzambi Tata wetu yi Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu baluheka khenda yi ngemba!
EPH 1:3 Lukumu kwena Nzambi, Tata wa Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu! Yandi kátusakumuna muna lusakumunu lwosu lwa kitembu muna bizika bya mazilu, mwena Kidisitu.
EPH 1:4 Mwena yandi, Nzambi wátusola ku thwala ya kuhangama kwa tsi, ndangu twakala batu ba Nzambi amana bakonda kifu ku mesu ma yandi. Muna lungongu lwandi,
EPH 1:5 Nzambi wázenga tuka thama mu kutusola ni twakala hanga bana bandi ba kutsasa, muna nzila ya Yesu Kidisitu. Kázola bwabuna muna buweti bwandi;
EPH 1:6 ndangu betu twalumisa khembu ya khenda zina kátuheka mwena Mwana wandi wuna watondama.
EPH 1:7 Mwena Kidisitu, muna nzila ya menga mandi, twábongila luhulusu yi ndoluka ya masumu bwosu kwenina kuvula kwa khenda zandi.
EPH 1:8 Bwabuna kátufwebwalaza mu kutuheka mudimu walungila yi ngangu zalungila.
EPH 1:9 Wátusengwamina diswekamu dya dibanza dyandi dina kázenga tuka thama, muna buweti bwandi, mwena Kidisitu.
EPH 1:10 Dibanza meni dina, kalungisa Nzambi mu tsuka ya matangwa, ditadidi kukhundikisa kwa bima byosu bina byenina mu zilu yi ha tsi amana wusibya mu kiyeka kya Kidisitu.
EPH 1:11 Mwena yandi, twátambula ndambu ya kimvwama kyetu kina kátuzengila tuka thama; betu babana kátekila sola Nzambi tuka ku luyandiku, bwosu buna dyákala dibanza dya wuna wisi lungisa mambu moosu, bwosu buna lwenina lukanu lwa luzolu lwandi.
EPH 1:12 Tuzatulenu khembu ya Nzambi, betu babana twátekila sya kivuvu kyetu mwena Kidisitu!
EPH 1:13 Mwena yandi, benu phi, tangwa lwáyuka musamu wa kyedika, Musamu wa Bukheti wuna wálunatina luhulusu, lwákwikila mwena Kidisitu; amana bálunamika kidimbu kya Kitembu Kyatoma wuna kálusila kilangi.
EPH 1:14 Kitembu meni wuna kenina thuka ya kuvwa kwetu; kithama kina dyakútumukina mu kimakulu kanda dya Nzambi. Hahana ni tuyimbilenu khembu ya Nzambi!
EPH 1:15 Yi hakana ni meni phi, buna yíyuka mu kuzonzila mambu matadidi lukwikilu lwenu mwena Pfumu Yesu yi lungongu lwenu kwena bakwikidi,
EPH 1:16 yisiku lembwa muna lombilu lwama mu kuvutula matondu kwena Nzambi kikuma kya benu.
EPH 1:17 Amana ndombini kwena Nzambi wa Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu, yandi wenina Tata wa khembu, kaluheka kitembu kya mudimu yi kina kya tsengumuka, ndangu lwalenga muzayila.
EPH 1:18 Ndombini phi kalutemuna mesu ma mbundu yenu ndangu lwabakisa mutindu wa kivuvu kina kyákangama ku mbila yandi, kuvwa kwa lawu kwa khembu yina kálusila hakati dya bakwikidi,
EPH 1:19 yi kutoka kwa ngolu zandi zina zilutini kenina zawu kikuma kya betu babana thwisi kwikila. Ngolu meni zina kásongilaza muna ngolu zandi zoosu;
EPH 1:20 tangwa kámufutumuna Kidisitu ha kati dya bafwa amana wumuzakadisi kuna koku dyandi dya kitata, muna mazilu.
EPH 1:21 Kidisitu wábonga kifulu hana thandu ya kipfumu kyosu, ngolu zoosu, hamu dyosu, luyalu lwosu yi khumbu yosu yina yisi tangama lwesi ha tsi haha yi muna tsi yina yakwísa.
EPH 1:22 Nzambi wátulula byosu muna malu ma Kidisitu, wámuhana hanga Pfumu wa mbuta hana thandu ya Dibundu.
EPH 1:23 Dibundu dyenina Lutu lwa Kidisitu; mwena yandi, mwamuna kisi zingila Nzambi wa muthu, yandi wábasisa byosu mwena boosu.
EPH 2:1 Amana benu lwákala theti bafwa kikuma kya mbi zenu yi kikuma kya masumu menu.
EPH 2:2 Mwamuna lwakala dihana theti muna ndyatidi yenu ku luzingu lwa tsi yayi. Amana lwakala lemvwakila pfumu wa bitembu bya mbi byisi yala hakati kya tsi yi zilu. Kitembu meni wuna wubati hanga muhangu mwena batu babana bisiku lemvuka kwena Nzambi.
EPH 2:3 Betu boosu phi, twákala theti muna mukanzu wa batu babana, amana twakala zingila muna tsambu za mbi za kimutu kyetu yi kitembu kyetu. Amana, kikuma kya bifu byetu twátangamina mu pfundusu ya Nzambi hanga batu bahika.
EPH 2:4 Kaasi kheni ya Nzambi yilutini kitesu, kikuma kya lungongu lwa mbuta luna kátutyela,
EPH 2:5 amana betu bana twákala bafwa mu moya kikuma kya mitsoki myetu, yandi wátuvutula hika mu luzingu ha kimosi yi Kidisitu. Mu khenda luhulukidini benu.
EPH 2:6 Nzambi kátufutumuna ku lufwa ha kimosi yi Kidisitu Yesu amana wátuzakadisa ha kimosi yi yandi muna bizika bya mazilu;
EPH 2:7 ndangu kasongila, muna matangwa makwísa, buweti bwandi buna buhitini kitesu kwena betu mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
EPH 2:8 Kikuma mu khenda za Nzambi lwáhulwakila benu, mu nzila ya lukwikilu. Luhulusu luna lutukiku kwena benu-benu, dyenina kabu dya Nzambi;
EPH 2:9 ditukiku ku mihangu myenu, yi hana ni ka mutu ku wufwani kaditsikisa.
EPH 2:10 Mukuma betu thwenina bihangwa byandi; mwena Kidisitu Yesu twáhangamina, kikuma kya mihangu mya bukheti mina kátekila yidika Nzambi, ndangu twasadilamya.
EPH 2:11 Yi hana ni yindulenuti buna lwákala theti! Benu lwákala batu bakondi kala Bayuta; Bayuta bakala lubongila hanga batu bakonda kota mukhanda amana bawu-meni, bisi ditela ni batu bákota mukhanda kikuma kya mukhanda wuna bábayotisa muna lutu yi ku moku ma batu.
EPH 2:12 Muna tangwa dyadina, benu lwákalaku kedi yi Kidisitu; lwákalaku keti muswa wumosi hana kati dya Kiseledi; banzenza lwákala ku bulunda bwa bilangi; benu lwakala zinga konda kivuvu yi konda Nzambi.
EPH 2:13 Kaasi buthwena, mu kimvuka yi Kidisitu Yesu, benu lwákala kyana, lwábwesuka mu nzila ya kimenga kyandi.
EPH 2:14 Mukuma yandi-meni Kidisitu wátunatina ngemba, muna nzila ya kimenga kyandi, mu kubundikisa Bayuta yi batu bana bakondi kala Bayuta, ndangu bakituka mutu mosi. Yandi wámwanga kibaka kya ngyengu kina kyakala bahambula yi kukasa bimbeni.
EPH 2:15 Wámanisa ngolu za mitsiku mya Bayuta, miswa mya myawu yi nzengulu za myawu, ndangu kabakitula mutu mosi wa pha, batu boosu, mwena yandi: bwabuna káyidikila ngemba.
EPH 2:16 Muna nzila ya lufwa lwandi ha kitakani, Kidisitu wábakhundikisa batu boosu mu lutu lumosi yi kuvutula ngemba ha kati dya bawu yi Nzambi; muna nzila ya kitakani, wázangakya kiphala.
EPH 2:17 Musamu wa Bukheti kisa longa Kidisitu, wutadidi ngemba kwena benu lwákala kyana amana wutadidi ngemba kwena babana bákala bela-bela.
EPH 2:18 Kikuma, muna nzila ya yandi, mwamuna twábongila muswa wa kutelama, kwakala betu Bayuta kondilo bana bakondi kala Bayuta, ku thwala ya Nzambi Tata, muna Kitembu mosi.
EPH 2:19 Ihana ni, benu batu lwakonda kala Bayuta, lweku hika banzenza keti batu bátuka kuma kwahika; kaasi buthwena lwekina batu ba kikanda kya Nzambi, lwekina butuka dya Nzambi.
EPH 2:20 Benu, bálutungila ha thandu ya mipfundila mina báyidikila yi bathumwa yi bambikudi; Kidisitu Yesu yandi-meni kenina tadi dya ha sina.
EPH 2:21 Mwena yandi, mwisi zyamina thungidi zoosu ndangu zakituka nzu ya Nzambi yatoma.
EPH 2:22 Mwena yandi, benu phi lwekina thungidi yimosi mu kimvuka yi bakwenu, ndangu lwakituka nzu ya Nzambi mu Kitembu.
EPH 3:1 Kikuma kya bwabuna, meni Pholu, mutu wa boloku wa Kidisitu Yesu kikuma kya benu bana lukondi kala Bayuta...
EPH 3:2 Benu lwáyuka kwenu mboti phila ya kiyeka kina kápheka Nzambi muna khenda zandi kikuma kya benu.
EPH 3:3 Mu nzila ya nzayikusu kátsengwamina kitsweki kya mabanza mandi, bwosu yilusonikinibwa mu khufi.
EPH 3:4 Mu kutangaka mamana, lwalenda bakula ngangu zina yítambula kikuma kya kisalu kya Kidisitu.
EPH 3:5 Muna makula mana máhita, diswekamu dina, Nzambi kásengumunadyoku kwena batu; kaasi buthwena, wusengumunidya kwena bathumwa bandi yi bambikudi, muna nzila ya Kitembu.
EPH 3:6 Diswekamu dyadina dyenina: bana bakondi kala Bayuta bisi tambula kimvwama kimosi yi betu Bayuta; benina phi yi lutu lumosi amana bisi tambula mamboti ma kilangi kimosi, mwena Kidisitu Yesu, muna nzila ya Musamu wa Bukheti.
EPH 3:7 Muna Musamu wa Bukheti meni wuna, mwamuna yíkitukila musadi, bwosu dyenina kabu dya khenda dina kápheka Nzambi, mu buweti bwandi yi ngolu zandi zina zilutini.
EPH 3:8 Kinga kwena meni yenina wa khunda kuhita bakwikidi boosu, báhana kabu dina dya kusamuna Musamu wa Bukheti wa kimvwama kya mvula yi mvula kya Kidisitu, kwena bana bakondi kala Bayuta;
EPH 3:9 amana yilubula ku mwini, kikuma kya batu boosu, mutindu wuna kisi lungisila Nzambi dibanza dya diswekamu dyandi kikuma kya batu boosu. Yandi wáhanga bima byosu, wásweka diswekamu dina muna makula moosu,
EPH 3:10 ndangu mudimu wa Nzambi, muna bitini byandi bya lawu, wazayakana buthwena, mu nzila ya Dibundu, kwena luyalu lwa tsi yi kwena bapfumu bana benina muna mazilu.
EPH 3:11 Bwosu buna mákala mabanza ma mvula yi mvula mana kisi lungisa Nzambi mwena Kidisitu Yesu Pfumu wetu.
EPH 3:12 Mwena Kidisitu yi lukwikilu lwetu mwena yandi, thwenina yi kiphwanza mu kubwesuka ku thwala ya Nzambi yi mbundu mosi.
EPH 3:13 Yilulombini ni lukatulaku kikesa kikuma kya kiwayi kina mbati mona kikuma kya benu: zenina kikuma kya khembu ya benu.
EPH 3:14 Pfukikidini makungulu mama ku mesu ma Tata;
EPH 3:15 kwena yandi kyisi tadila kikanda kyosu, muna mazilu yi hana tsi;
EPH 3:16 ndangu kaluheka, bwosu kyenina kimvwama kya khembu yandi, mu kukala yi kikesa muna moya yi ngolu zina zilutini muna Kitembu kyandi;
EPH 3:17 amana Kidisitu kazingila muna mbundu yenu muna lukwikilu amana lwazyama, lwakala phi ba kutunga mu lungongu.
EPH 3:18 Muna bwabuna ndangu lwalenda mu kubakisa ha kimosi yi bakwikidi, buna kwenina kutoka, dingu, kyana yi kuleya kwa lungongu lwa Kidisitu.
EPH 3:19 Lwazaya phi lungongu lwa Kidisitu -luna lulutini mazaya moosu- amana lwabasa yi kuna kimvwama kyosu kya Nzambi.
EPH 3:20 Kwena wuna walenda kusala mu kimakulu, hana thandu ya mana thwisi lomba holo thwisi banza, mu nzila ya ngolu zoosu zina zisi sala mwena betu,
EPH 3:21 kwena yandi, khembu muna Dibundu mu nzila ya Kidisitu Yesu, muna makula moosu, mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna.
EPH 4:1 Kikesa mbati luheka, meni mutu wa boloku kikuma kya Pfumu: benu kátela, dyatilenu mu mutindu wuna wufwanakani yi mbila meni yayina.
EPH 4:2 Kalenu yi mbundu ya dikulumuna, ya talala yi sipha dya mbundu. Ditambwasenu benu yi benu bwosu lulombini lungongu.
EPH 4:3 Sandakenu mu kubatila kithwadi kina kisi hana Kitembu mu nzila ya ngemba yina yisi lukasa benu yi benu.
EPH 4:4 Lutu lumosi lwenina yi Kitembu mosi, bwosu buna kivuvu kyenina kimosi kina kálutedila Nzambi.
EPH 4:5 Pfumu mosi kenina, lukwikilu lumosi, mbotika yimosi;
EPH 4:6 Nzambi mosi, wuna wenina Tata wa batu boosu, wuna wisi yala ha thandu ya byosu, kisi sala mwena byosu yi muna boosu.
EPH 4:7 Kaasi kosu mutu hana kati dya betu wábonga khenda muna kitesu kya kabu dya Kidisitu.
EPH 4:8 Kikuma kya bwabuna básonikina: «Wátombuka muna malondi, wábanata batu bana bakala mu boloku; wáhana makabu kwena batu.»
EPH 4:9 Kinga, biki disongidila dya mambu mama: «wátombuka»? Disongidila ni wákulumuka phi muna milambu mya mabanda mya ha tsi?
EPH 4:10 Wuna wákulumuka yawuna phi wátombuka mu mazilu ndangu kabasisa tsi yosu.
EPH 4:11 Yandi phi wáhana makabu kwena batu boosu: bahika bathumwa, kwena bambikudi, bakwawu hika, bamwangi ba Musamu wa Bukheti, bakwawu hanga bamvungi holo balongi.
EPH 4:12 Bwosu bwabuna, ndangu kayidika bakwikidi kikuma kya muhangu wa kisyelu kyandi, mu kukodisa lutu lwa Kidisitu,
EPH 4:13 yi kuna twakítwakila betu boosu mutu mosi muna lukwikilu yi muna mazaya ma Mwana wa Nzambi. Bwabuna twakítukila batu bana bakodi kedi, mu kubakila phi mutela wa kyedika wa Kidisitu.
EPH 4:14 Muna bwabuna, twakálaku hika bana ba khunda. Twafwánanaku hika hanga koma ka masuwa kana bisi nata masambwa moosu kwena muphephi wa yanga dya mbuta, mu malongi ma mbi ma mutindu yi mutindu. Batu batúhunaku hika yi bukamvi bwa bawu bwa kutotisila bakwenu.
EPH 4:15 Kaasi mu kuzimbulaka kyedika mu lungongu, twakóla mu mambu moosu yikuna kwena mutu wuna wenina mutwa, Kidisitu.
EPH 4:16 Mwena yandi, lutu lwisi kitukila kima kya ngolu, kya kukhundikisa mu ndambu zoosu yi ngolu zina zifwani. Yi hana ni yuka kosu kitini kyasalaka buna bufwani, lutu lwosu lwisi kola phi mu lungongu.
EPH 4:17 Tala buna nzimbudini yi mana thambwasini kwena Pfumu: khadidi yenu yaswaswana yi yina ya bana bakondi kala bakwikidi, bana bisi dyatila mu mabanza ma bawu mana misiku nata kima.
EPH 4:18 Benina yi ngangu za kaphindi, benina banzenza ku luzingu lwa Nzambi, kikuma kya kukonda kwa mbakisilu ya bawu yi mbundu ya bawu ya tototo.
EPH 4:19 Bátotisa mambu mosu mana ma bukheti amana badihana mu mbongi, ndangu bahangaka mambu ma mvindu ma mutindu yi mutindu yi lukusu lwosu.
EPH 4:20 Kaasi benu, kabwaku buna lwáyuka kikuma kya Kidisitu!
EPH 4:21 Khwikidi mboti ni lwáyuka kwenu mambu moosu mana matadidini yandi, amana bálulonga mambu mandi mu kyedika kina kyenina mwena Yesu.
EPH 4:22 Yihana, lufweti yambula kimutu kyenu kya khulu kina lwakala kyawu theti, kina kyakala yi nzoluka za bukamvi zisi bebisa.
EPH 4:23 Yambulenu kitembu kyenu yi ngangu zenu byakituka bya pha.
EPH 4:24 Amana lwavwata mutu wa pha, wuna wáhangama mu phila ya Nzambi, muna masonga yi kutoma kuna kwisi tuka mu nzila ya kyedika.
EPH 4:25 Yihana ni, yambulenu bukamvi! Amana kosu mutu kazonza yi kyedika kwena khunda wandi, mukuma betu boosu thwenina bitini bya lutu lumosi.
EPH 4:26 Ho lwakala mu khabu, lusumukaku; lunimbaku yi khabu.
EPH 4:27 Lumuhekaku kizika kiphidi-mutu.
EPH 4:28 Mwifi kayibaku hika, kaasi kadihana mu kusala yandi-meni yi moku mandi; ndangu kamona kima kina kasadisila wuna wenina mu phasi.
EPH 4:29 Ka ndinga yimosi ku ya mbi yalubuka muna munwa myenu, kaasi zonzakenu lwesi ndinga za bukheti, zina zisi tunga amana zisi hana khenda kwena babana babati yuka.
EPH 4:30 Lumuyukisaku kyadi Kitembu Kyatoma wuna kalunamika Nzambi hanga kidimbu kikuma kya kilumbu kya luhulusu lwa tsuka.
EPH 4:31 Katulenu mambu moosu ma khadi mana báluhanga, nganzi, khabu, bikalu, ngusi yi mbi za phila yosu.
EPH 4:32 Kalenu bukheti benu yi benu, kalenu yi mbundu ya kyadi; amana dilolulenu benu yi benu bwosu kálulolula Nzambi mwena Kidisitu.
EPH 5:1 Sokululenu mbandu ya Nzambi, mudyambu lwenina bana batondama.
EPH 5:2 Dyatilenu mu lungongu, bwosu buna phi kátuzola Kidisitu, mu kudilambula yandi-meni kwena Nzambi kikuma kya betu, hanga dikabu yi kimenga kya tsudi ya kitoku.
EPH 5:3 Benu lwenina bakwikidi ba Nzambi; yambulenu mbongi, mambu ma mvindu muna mitindu myandi myosu holo lukusu: lusungulamoku keti mbala mosi hana kati dya benu.
EPH 5:4 Ka mboti ku ni lwalubulaka ndinga za khadi, za buzoba holo za mvindu. Kaasi bulungi lwavutulaka matondu kwena Nzambi.
EPH 5:5 Mukuma, zayenu bwoku mboti ni, ka mutu mosi ku wisi dilambula ku kindumba, ku bizumba, ku lukusu -disongidila ni kufukamina nzambi za biteki -wabónga kizika muna Kipfumu kya Kidisitu yi kya Nzambi.
EPH 5:6 Ka mutu ku kaluhuna mu ndinga zakonda mupfunu: kikuma, muna mambu ma mutindu meni wawuna zisi kwisila khabu za Nzambi kwena batu babana.
EPH 5:7 Disongidila, lukalaku keti kima kimosi kya kimvuka yi bawu.
EPH 5:8 Kikuma, theti mu phipha lwákala; kaasi buthwena, mu kikhunda kyenu yi Pfumu, lwekina mwini. Dyatilenu hanga bana ba mwini,
EPH 5:9 mukuma kibundu kya mwini kyenina: buweti, masonga, kyedika.
EPH 5:10 Zayakenu mu kubangumuna mambu mana misi sephidisa Nzambi.
EPH 5:11 Lukotaku mu mihangu mya mu phipha; kaasi benu tungululenumyoku.
EPH 5:12 Kikuma, mambu mana bisi sala mu kitsweki, tsoni menina mu kuzonzilama.
EPH 5:13 Kinga mana moosu, yuka ni matunguluki kedi, hanga malubuki ha tseki.
EPH 5:14 Mukuma mambu moosu mana matungulukini, mekina mwini. Yi hana kazonzidi bwabu: «Tokama, ngeyi wubati nimba, futumuka ha kati dya bafwa, amana Kidisitu kakúkenzula.»
EPH 5:15 Yi hana ni kebenu mu ndyatidi yenu. Lukalaku hanga bazoba, kaasi hanga batu badimuka.
EPH 5:16 Sadilenu bukheti tangwa dina dyenina ku thwala ya benu, mukuma bilumbu bya mbi byenina.
EPH 5:17 Lukalaku hanga bazoba, kaasi syenu ngolu mu kubakisa buna lwenina luzolu lwa Pfumu.
EPH 5:18 Luzelaku vinu, kikuma kwiti dyandi dyisi nata ku mvwalangani; kaasi kalenu babasa yi Kitembu Kyatoma.
EPH 5:19 Dihekenu kikesa benu yi benu mu nzila ya mikunga yi mikunga mya khembu yi mina mya Kitembu; yimbilenu, kumisenu phi Pfumu muna mbundu yenu yosu.
EPH 5:20 Kosu tangwa yi muna mambu moosu, vutulenu matondu kwena yandi wenina Nzambi yi Tata wetu, muna zina dya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu.
EPH 5:21 Dilemvwakilenu benu yi benu kikuma kya bweya mwena Kidisitu.
EPH 5:22 Yi hana ni bakhetu, lemvukenu kwena bayakala benu bwosu lwisi lemvuka kwena Pfumu.
EPH 5:23 Mukuma, yakala kenina pfumu wa mukhetu, bwosu kenina Kidisitu Pfumu wa Dibundu dina dyenina lutu lwandi, amana yandi phi wenina Muhuludi wa dyawu.
EPH 5:24 Disongidila, bulungi bakhetu balemvuka kwena bayakala ba bawu bwosu buna dyisi lemvuka Dibundu kwena Kidisitu.
EPH 5:25 Bayakala, zolenu bakhetu benu bwosu kázola Kidisitu Dibundu, amana wáditambika yandi meni kikuma kya dyawu;
EPH 5:26 ndangu katomisadya, mu kusemisadya mu mamba yi mu Ndinga.
EPH 5:27 Kázola ni Dibundu meni dina dyamonika ku thwala ya yandi, yi khembu, dyakonda mvindu, keti tona, keti kifu kimosi. Kaasi dyakala dyatoma amana dyakonda kifu.
EPH 5:28 Phila mosi ni bayakala bafweti zola bakhetu ba bawu bwosu bisi zola lutu lwa bawu meni. Wuna wazola mukhetu wandi, kisi dizola yandi meni.
EPH 5:29 Kikuma heku mutu wábwisa kedi lutu lwa yandi meni; kaasi kisilwa disa amana kisilwa yidika, bwosu kisibwa sala Kidisitu kikuma kya Dibundu,
EPH 5:30 kikuma betu thwenina bitini bya lutu lwandi.
EPH 5:31 «Yi hana ni yakala kasísa tata wandi yi ngudi wandi ndangu kakhundakana kwena mukhetu wandi, amana bawu bodi bakítuka lutu lumosi.»
EPH 5:32 Diswekamu dimosi dya mbuta dyenina hana; meni nzonzi ni matadidi Kidisitu yi Dibundu.
EPH 5:33 Yi hakana ni, mosi-mosi wa benu kazola mukhetu wandi hanga yandi meni, amana mukhetu kazitisa yakala dyandi.
EPH 6:1 Bana, lemvukenu kwena bibuti byenu bwosu kazodibwa Pfumu, mukuma bwabuna bwenina masonga.
EPH 6:2 «Zitisa tata waku yi ngudi waku» wawuna mutsiku wa theti wenina yi kilangi:
EPH 6:3 «ndangu wakala mu kyesi, wazinga phi luzingu lwa kyesi lawu ha tsi.»
EPH 6:4 Amana benu, batata, bikalulu byenu, binyokunaku bana benu. Kaasi batsasenu mu kubasongisaka yi milongi mina mituki kwena Pfumu.
EPH 6:5 Benu basadi, lemvukenu kwena bapfumu benu hanga mu kimutu yi bweya yi matekita mu kudikulumuna kwa mbundu yenu, bwosu lwisi lemvuka kwena Kidisitu.
EPH 6:6 Lusadilabwoku lwesi ha mesu ma bawu hanga bana bazodi kuditondisa kwena batu; kaasi hanga basadi ba Kidisitu bana bisi lungisa luzolu lwa Nzambi yi mbundu ya bawu yosu.
EPH 6:7 Basadilenu yi luzolu lwa mboti, hanga basadi ba Pfumu kaasi ka basadi ba batu ku.
EPH 6:8 Zayenu ni: kosu mutu, kakala muhika, keku muhika, kabónga lufutu lwandi kwena Pfumu, muna kitesu kya mboti yina kasadila.
EPH 6:9 Kwena benu phi bapfumu, hangenu phila mosi ku thwala ya basadi benu. Syenu ku kabeta tsokisila. Luzayibwa ni benu yi bawu, lwenina yi Pfumu mosi mu mazilu, amana yandi kisiku swasisa batu.
EPH 6:10 Ku tsuka, bongenu ngolu zenu mwena Pfumu yi muna ngolu zandi zina zilutini kitesu.
EPH 6:11 Vwatenu binwaninu byosu bya Nzambi, ndangu lwazyama ku thwala ya bimeka bya kiphidi-mutu.
EPH 6:12 Mukuma, tubatiku nwanisa batu kaasi ngolu za luyalu lwa mbi, bipfumu bina bilutini kitesu yi bitembu byabina byisi yala muna midima; ngolu za bitembu bya mbi bina byenina muna bizika bya mazilu.
EPH 6:13 Yi hana ni vwatenu binwaninu byosu bya Nzambi! Ndangu lubwaku mu bilumbu bya mbi, amana kunima kunwana yi kuna tsuka, lwazyama.
EPH 6:14 Disongidila, zyamenu mboti: kasenu kyedika hanga mukaba muna mbunda zenu, amana vwatenu masonga hanga muledi wa bisengu wuna wisi sweka thulu;
EPH 6:15 vwatenu, hanga tsabatu, Musamu wa Bukheti wuna wanáta ngemba.
EPH 6:16 Muna mambu moosu, vwatenu lukwikilu hanga kibalaka kina kyalúsadisa mu kuzima mbawu ya phunza zina kalútimbwala mbeni.
EPH 6:17 Vwatenu hanga phwa, luhulusu; hanga mbedi ya phoku, ndinga ya Nzambi yina kisi hana Kitembu Kyatoma.
EPH 6:18 Lombilakenu kosu tangwa bilomba bya mutindu yi mutindu muna nzila ya Kitembu. Kikuma kya bwabuna, temunenu mesu amana lulembwaku mu kulombilaka kosu tangwa kikuma kya bakwikidi boosu.
EPH 6:19 Lombilenu phi kikuma kya meni, ndangu muna tangwa dyosu dina yibónga ndinga, Nzambi kaphekaka mihowu mina milungi mu kutungulula yi kikumbwala bitsweki bya Musamu wa Bukheti.
EPH 6:20 Mbatanana buna yenina buthwena mu miyololu, yenina kilolu kya Musamu wa Bukheti meni wuna. Lombilenu ndangu yilongawa yi kikumbwala bwosu buna pfwani yilongilawa.
EPH 6:21 Tisiki, phangi wetu watondama yi nduku wetu wa kisalu kya Pfumu yi musadi wuna thwisi sila mbundu, kalúheka tsangu za meni zoosu ndangu lwazaya mana yisi hanga yi buna yekina.
EPH 6:22 Mbongi lukanu lwa kuluhitika yandi ndangu lwazaya buna thwenina, amana kaluzyamisa.
EPH 6:23 Yambula Nzambi, Tata wetu yi Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu bahana kwena baphangi boosu ngemba yi lungongu ha kimosi yi lukwikilu.
EPH 6:24 Yambula Nzambi kahana khenda zandi kwena babana boosu bisi muzola Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu yi lungongu luna lwisiku nikana.
PHI 1:1 Meni Pholu yi Thimoti, basadi ba Kidisitu Yesu. Kwena bakwikidi boosu benina mwena Kidisitu Yesu kuna Fidiphu, yi batwadisi yi kwena basyelu:
PHI 1:2 Yambula Nzambi Tata wetu yi Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu baluheka khenda yi ngemba.
PHI 1:3 Yisi vutula matondu kwena Nzambi wama muna mbala zoosu zina yisi lusungula.
PHI 1:4 Yisiku lembwa mu kulombilaka yi kyesi muna bilomba byama byosu kikuma kya benu boosu,
PHI 1:5 kikuma kya lusadisu lwenu ku Musamu wa Bukheti, tuka kilumbu kya theti yi buthwena bwabu.
PHI 1:6 Yenina yi kikumbwala ni wuna wáyandika muhangu wa bukheti ha kati dya benu, kalánda tsuka ya wawu yi muna kilumbu kya kwisa kwa Kidisitu Yesu.
PHI 1:7 Bwenina bwa masonga kikuma kya meni ni yikala yi mabanza ma mutindu wawu kwena benu boosu. Kikuma, lwenina muna mbundu yama, benu boosu lwisi khundakana muna kabu dina kaphekini Nzambi, dyakala mu tangwa dina yenina mu miyololu, keti mu tangwa dina yisi zonzila Musamu wa Bukheti ni wa kyedika wenina.
PHI 1:8 Kikuma, Nzambi kenina mbangi wama: yenina yi tsambu ya lawu kikuma kya benu boosu, muna lungongu lwa Kidisitu Yesu.
PHI 1:9 Amana tala mana yisi lomba kwena Nzambi muna bisambu byama: zola dyenu dyavulaka kosu tangwa, dyákala dyabasa muna mazaya yi muna mbakisilu yalunga,
PHI 1:10 bwabuna lwazáyila kubangumuna mambu ma mboti. Ndangu lwakala batu ba kasemi amana bakonda kifu muna kilumbu kya Kidisitu.
PHI 1:11 Lwakála babasa mu mihangu mya masonga mana misi tuka mu nzila ya Yesu Kidisitu, kikuma kya khembu yi lukumu lwa Nzambi.
PHI 1:12 Nzodi ni lwazayabwa, baphangi: mambu mana mambwidiki matomi sadisa mu kumwangana kwa Musamu wa Bukheti.
PHI 1:13 Muna mutindu meni wawuna, batsinzidi boosu muna nganda ya pfumu wa mbanza yi muma mwosu, bazaya ni mu miyololu yenina kikuma kya Kidisitu.
PHI 1:14 Amana miyololu myama mihani kikesa kwena baphangi ba lawu mwena Pfumu, mu kukasa kwa mbundu kikuma kya kulonga Ndinga ya Nzambi konda bweya.
PHI 1:15 Bwa kyedika ni bahika hana kati dya bawu babati samuna musamu wa Kidisitu mu kiphala yi mabanza ma ngyuma, kaasi bakwawu bisiwa samuna yi mabanza ma bukheti.
PHI 1:16 Baba baba babatibwa sadila mu lungongu mukuma bazayi ni yenina hana kikuma kya kuzonzila Musamu wa Bukheti.
PHI 1:17 Bahika babati samuna musamu wa Kidisitu yi mabanza ma kunwanina; mabanza ma bawu ma mbi menina, bisi banza ni bakosikila hika kiwayi hana thandu ya miyololu myama.
PHI 1:18 Ka dyambu ku! Kima kihitini mupfunu mu byosu, keti bweti babati samuna musamu yi mesu ku tsi ya lukaya kondilo ma kyedika, musamu wa Kidisitu babatiwa samuna, amana nsangwadini kikuma kya bwabuna. Yilánda hika mu kusangwala,
PHI 1:19 mukuma nzayi ni mamana moosu mabáluka kikuma kya luhulusu lwama, kikuma kya bisambu byenu yi mu lusadisu luna kisi ndatina Kitembu wa Yesu Kidisitu.
PHI 1:20 Kikuma, muna mana mbati hingila, mana tsidini kivuvu, yikwátukaku tsoni. Kaasi, keti buthwena, keti bilumbu byosu, yi kikumbwala kya lawu yisóngila kutoka kwa Kidisitu muna lutu lwama lwosu, keti mu luzingu lwama, kondilo muna lufwa lwama.
PHI 1:21 Mukuma, kikuma kya meni, luzingu lwenina Kidisitu amana lufwa lwenina lufutu.
PHI 1:22 Kaasi yuka ni kukala mu luzingu lwa kimutu kwapheka hika muswa wa kulungisa muhangu wa mupfunu, hana nzayiku keti biki fwani yisola hika.
PHI 1:23 Mbati nwana yi mambu modi mama mabati tendana: nzodi yikatuka mu luzingu lwalu lwa kimutu ndangu yikala yi Kidisitu, bwabuna buhiti kitoku;
PHI 1:24 kaasi kikuma kya benu, bulungi yinanga hika mu luzingu lwa kimutu.
PHI 1:25 Amana bwosu tsini mbundu muna bwabuna, nzayi ni mu luzingu yikála hika, yinánga hika hakimosi yi benu boosu kikuma kya kulusadisaka ndangu lwakola amana lwakala mu kyesi muna lukwikilu.
PHI 1:26 Ndangu, tangwa yikála hika ha kati dya benu, kyesi kyenu mwena Kidisitu Yesu kyalútuka kuhita kina lwáyuka mu kumbona hika meni.
PHI 1:27 Kima kimosi, lwazingila bwosu buna wulombini Musamu wa Bukheti wa Kidisitu. Ndangu, ata yisi lutala, ata yisiku lutala, yiyukaka ni ludisimbididi mu kithwadi muna kitembu kimosi, lubati nwana hakimosi muna mbundu yimosi kikuma kya lukwikilu luna lwátungila ha thandu ya Musamu wa Bukheti.
PHI 1:28 Amana lubayukaku bweya babana bisi lutendisa; kina kyakála kidimbu kikuma kya kuzangana kwa bawu, amana benu mu nzila ya luhulusu lwenina; kwena Nzambi misi tuka mamana.
PHI 1:29 Mukuma, muna mana matadidini Kidisitu, Nzambi káluhekila khenda, heku ni kikuma kya kukwikila lwesi mwena yandi, kaasi kikuma phi kya kunyokuka kikuma kya yandi.
PHI 1:30 Buthwena, lubati nwana mvita ya mutindu wumosi yi yina lwámbona meni mu kunwana mbala yikwawu, amana yi yayina bwosu luzayini, mbati nwana hika.
PHI 2:1 Kikhunda kyenu hakimosi yi Kidisitu, kikesa kyisi luheka? Lungongu lwandi lwisi lusangumuna? Mu kithwadi lwenina yi Kitembu? Lwenina yi zola yi buweti hana kati dya benu yi benu?
PHI 2:2 Basisenu kyesi kyama mu nzila ya kuyukanaka, kukalaka yi zola dimosi, kukhundakanaka mu mbundu yi mabanza.
PHI 2:3 Luhangaku kima mu mbundu ya kuwila, kondilo mu kusanda lukumu lwa phamba-phamba kaasi mu kudikulumunaka, lwamonaka bakwenu hanga mbedi ni baluhitini benu.
PHI 2:4 Ka mutu ku kasandaka lwesi muluta wa yandi meni, kaasi kosu mutu kabanzilaka phi bakwawu.
PHI 2:5 Hana kati dya benu, banzakenu hanga batu benina bakhundakana kwena Kidisitu Yesu:
PHI 2:6 Yandi wákala Nzambi, kaasi kámonabwoku hanga kima kya kuwila.
PHI 2:7 Kaasi wádiwongumuna mu byosu bina kákala byawu, amana wádikitula hanga musadi. Wákituka mutu hana kati dya batu; kázayakana hanga mutu;
PHI 2:8 wátoma dikulumuna amana wádisongila mutu wa bulemvu yi kuna lufwa, lufwa hana kitakani.
PHI 2:9 Yi hakana phi, Nzambi wámutombula hana kisoka amana wámuheka zina dina dihitini zina dyosu.
PHI 2:10 Ndangu, muna zina dya Yesu, kungulu dyosu dyafukama, muna mazilu yi hana tsi yi muna sina dya tsi,
PHI 2:11 amana munwa wosu wasamuna, muna khembu ya Nzambi Tata: «Yesu Kidisitu kenina Pfumu!»
PHI 2:12 Yi hana ni, baphangi batondama, bwosu buna lwakala lemvuka tangwa dyosu dina yíkala kwena benu, hangenu hika mutindu wumosi buthwena bwabu yeninahoku. Landenu bwabuna mu kusadila luhulusu lwenu, yi luzitu yi kitswi,
PHI 2:13 mukuma Nzambi kabati sala hana kati dya benu, kabati lukitula batu bana balungini mu luzolu yi kulungisa mana mafwanakani yi tsambu ya yandi ya bukheti.
PHI 2:14 Salenu dyambu dyosu konda kunyengalakana keti matendu,
PHI 2:15 ndangu lwakala konda kifu amana ba kasemi, bana ba Nzambi bakonda kifu hana kati dya batu babana ba mbi yi bazangana ba tsi yayi. Lufweti kenzula hanga mwini wa tsi,
PHI 2:16 mu kunataka ndinga ya luzingu. Lwaluna lwakála lulendu lwama muna kilumbu kya Kidisitu: kikuma yítakulaku mu phamba, kondilo yínyokukaku mu phamba.
PHI 2:17 Kaasi keti bweti ni menga mama mafwani kutyakana, hanga kabu dina bakosikidi ku kimenga kikuma kya kisalu kya lukwikilu lwenu; muna bwabuna, mu kyesi yenina amana mbati sangwala hakimosi yi benu boosu.
PHI 2:18 Sangwalenu benu phi, amana sangwalenu hakimosi yi meni.
PHI 2:19 Tsini kivuvu, mwena Pfumu Yesu, mu kuluhitika, ka thama ku, Thimoti, ndangu yibongila kikesa muna mameni ma benu mana kambénikina.
PHI 2:20 Kikuma, heku mutu wa hika walenda bakisa mabanza mama kikuma kya benu, yuka ni ka yandi ku lwesi yi mu kudiyangisaka, kyedika, kikuma kya benu.
PHI 2:21 Boosu babana basadini, ndandu za bawu meni lwesi bisi sanda kaasi bisiku sanda mambu ma Yesu Kidisitu.
PHI 2:22 Kaasi kikuma kya Thimoti, luzayini benu benu mutindu wuna kádihanina kwena meni mu kusala kisalu kya Musamu wa Bukheti, hanga mwana bela-bela yi tata wandi.
PHI 2:23 Amana khwikidi ni yilúhitika yandi tangwa dina yibákisila mutindu wuna mabati kwendila mambu meni meni;
PHI 2:24 amana yenina yi kikumbwala, mwena Pfumu, ni ka thama ku, yikwisa lutala meni meni.
PHI 2:25 Amana, mboni ni bwenina bukheti mu kuluhitika phangi wama Ephafoditi, wenina phi mukwetu wama wa kisalu yi musadi wuna wisi tsadisa mu kunwana muzingu, wuna wenina phi muzika wuna lwátuma benu mu kundatina bima bina yikadi byawu mupfunu.
PHI 2:26 Kikuma kenina yi tsambu mu kulumona hika benu boosu, amana phasi lawu kayukiki ku mbundu kikuma benu lwayuki ni yandi wabela kakadikini.
PHI 2:27 Kikuma, wabela kákala amana kakala lakana; kaasi Nzambi kyadi kámuyukila amana ka kikuma kya yandi lwesi ku, kaasi ndangu phi khalaku mu kyadi kya lawu.
PHI 2:28 Yimutumi hika yi tswasu yosu, ndangu lwasangwala mu kumumona, amana meni meni yikala yi kyadi kya khunda.
PHI 2:29 Yihakana ni, muyambenu yi kyesi kyosu mwena Pfumu. Bazitisakenu batu ba mutindu wuna,
PHI 2:30 mukuma, kazodi kafwa kikuma kya kisalu kya Kidisitu; bwosu lwaléndaku benu mu kwisa tsadisa, yandi wátambwasa mu kusya luzingu lwandi mu kihonza ndangu kisa tsadisa.
PHI 3:1 Mu kumanisa, baphangi bama, sangwalenu mu kukala mwena Pfumu. Bungyeku phasi mu kululandwadila mana yílusonikina kedi, mamana málusadisa mu kulutanina.
PHI 3:2 Kebenu yi bambwa babana, kebenu yi basadi ba mbi, kebenu yi batu bana bisi lulundika mu kudikotisa mukhanda!
PHI 3:3 Mukuma betu thwenina batu babana bákota mukhanda wa mukwandi, betu babana thwisi sadila Nzambi mu nzila ya Kitembu kyandi, thwisi ditsikisila mwena Kidisitu Yesu, amana thwisiku sya kikumbwala mu mambu ma lutu.
PHI 3:4 Kinga, meni phi, yenina mawu mambu mana pfwani yisila kikumbwala muna lutu. Ho ni mutu kabanzaka ni fwani kasya kivuvu mu mambu ma lutu, meni ndungi mu kuhangabwa kuluta.
PHI 3:5 Mu kilumbu kya nana, kunima lubutuku lwama, yíkota mukhanda, yenina mukwa Kiseledi wa mukwandi, muna kanda dya Benzyame, mwisi Hebelu yenina, muna butuka dya Hebelu. Muna mana matadidi mitsiku, Mufwadisi khadikini,
PHI 3:6 muna mana matadidini zangi, yínyokuna Dibundu. Muna mana matadidini masonga mana bisi sanda batu mu nzila ya mitsiku, yíkala konda kifu.
PHI 3:7 Kaasi mambu mana mákhala hanga ndandu, mbatima mona buthwena hanga kima kya phamba kikuma kya Kidisitu.
PHI 3:8 Kaasi mbati tala mambu mana moosu hanga kima kya phamba, kikuma kya mamboti mama mahitini mu kutoka: kuzaya Kidisitu Yesu Pfumu wama, kikuma kya yandi yítambwasila mu kutotisa mambu mana moosu, amana yisi mona moosu hanga tswala, ndangu yibonga Kidisitu
PHI 3:9 amana bisa ngwana mwena yandi. Bangwanaku yi masonga ma meni-meni mana misi tuka ku mitsiku, kaasi mana misi tuka mu nzila ya lukwikilu mwena Kidisitu, masonga mamosi misi tuka kwena Nzambi amana misi yekamina mu lukwikilu.
PHI 3:10 Kima nzodini, kumuzaya Kidisitu yi ngolu za lufutumuku lwandi, kukala mu kithwadi ku phasi zandi yi kufwanana yi yandi muna lufwa lwandi,
PHI 3:11 yi kivuvu ni meni phi yifútumuka ha kati dya bafwa.
PHI 3:12 Heku ni mbongima kedi mambu mana moosu, holo ni moosu mandungidi kedi; kaasi thinu mbati kwenda ndangu yibongama, kikuma Kidisitu Yesu wákhwata kedi.
PHI 3:13 Muna mambu mana mathadidini, baphangi, khwikidiku ni mbongilwa kedi lufutu meni luna; kaasi tsumbi yama yimosi: kuzimbakana mambu moosu mana menina ku manima mama amana yisya ngolu mu mambu mana menina ku thwala.
PHI 3:14 Muna bwabuna, thinu mbati kwenda yi kuna yitudila ku tsuka, ndangu yibonga lufutu luna káthedila Nzambi tuka ku zilu, mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
PHI 3:15 Disongidila, betu boosu babana twenina bakidisitu bakola, tubanzakenu bwabuna. Amana yuka ni mu dyambu dimosi bwabu, lubati banza mutindu wahika, Nzambi kalúsongilabwa wengele.
PHI 3:16 Muna moosu mamana, hana tutudi kedi buthwena, tulandenu mu kukangalaka nzila mosi.
PHI 3:17 Baphangi, landenu mbandu ya meni, amana simbululenu mboti batu babana bisi dyatila mu mutindu wa luzingu luna lwamonini kwena betu.
PHI 3:18 Mukuma, bwosu buna yisi luzimbwala kosu tangwa yi buthwena bwabu, mbati luzimbwala hika yi matsanga muna mesu, ni lawu benina babana benina bambeni ba kitakani kya Kidisitu kikuma kya ndyatidi ya bawu.
PHI 3:19 Tsuka ya bawu yenina kuzangana, nzambi wa bawu kenina kundu dya bawu; amana khembu ya bawu yenina muna mambu mana misi bakwatisa tsoni amana bisi sya mabanza ma bawu muna bima bya tsi.
PHI 3:20 Kaasi kwena betu, thwenina bisi mbanza ya mazilu. Amana tukidila kwakuna, tubati hingila hanga muhuludi, Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu.
PHI 3:21 Yandi wuna wakwisa balumuna lutu lwetu luna lwisi fwa ndangu lwakituka hanga lutu lwandi lwa khembu, muna nzila ya ngolu zina zisi muheka hamu dya kusya bima byosu muna sina dya luyalu lwandi.
PHI 4:1 Yi hakana ni, baphangi bama batondama, benu babana yisi yukila tsambu ya lawu mu kulumona, benu lwenina kyesi kyama yi mukhonzi wama, kalenu bakwikama muna luzingu lwenu yi Pfumu.
PHI 4:2 Yibahekini kikesa Evwodi yi Setiki ni bayukanaka bawu yi bawu mwena Pfumu.
PHI 4:3 Kwena ngeyi phi mukwetu wa kyedika wa kisalu, yikulombini ni wabasadisa, mukuma banwaniki lawu kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti, mu kithwadi yi meni; phila mosi phi yi Kelemasi yi bakwetu bahika ba kisalu, babana básonama mazina ma bawu muna mukanda wa moya.
PHI 4:4 Sangwalakenu kosu tangwa mu kithwadi yi Pfumu; ndanduludibwa hika ni sangwalakenu.
PHI 4:5 Yambulenu buweti bwenu bwazayakana kwena batu boosu. Pfumu wekina bela-bela.
PHI 4:6 Ludiyangisaku kikuma kya kima kimosi, kaasi muna mambu moosu, hanakenu bilomba byenu kwena Nzambi muna nzila ya kubokwadila hakimosi yi makabu ma kuvutula kwa matondu.
PHI 4:7 Amana ngemba ya Nzambi yina yihitini mabanza moosu yalúnda mbundu zenu yi mabanza menu mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
PHI 4:8 Mu kumanisa baphangi bama, mambu moosu mana menina ma kyedika, moosu mana menina ma kitoku, moosu mana menina ma masonga, moosu mana menina ma kasemi, moosu mana misi sephidisa batu, yuka ni ndyambu dimosi dya bukheti dyenina hana, yindulakenu kikuma kya mawu.
PHI 4:9 Mambu moosu mana lwálonguka, lwátambula yi mana lwáyuka kwena meni kondilo mana lwámona kwena meni, sadilenu mamana. Amana Nzambi wa ngemba kakála yi benu.
PHI 4:10 Tsangwadi lawu mwena Pfumu, kikuma tsuka-tsuka, lungyubuki hika. Bwa kyedika ni lumbanziki kedi, kaasi lukadikiku yi phila ya kusongilabwa.
PHI 4:11 Nzonzidibwoku ni kikuma kya kukonda kima, kikuma yílonguka kedi mu kukalaka mu kyesi muna mutindu wuna yenina.
PHI 4:12 Nzayini mu kuzingila mu kiphutu bwosu buna pfwani phi yizingila mu bima bya lawu. Yílonguka mu kukala sangu-sangu kosu tangwa yi muma mwosu, keti ngyukutini, ho loni yenina yi nzala, keti yenina yi bima byafwana, ho loni khondi kima.
PHI 4:13 Pfwani yisala mambu moosu muna nzila ya yandi wuna wisi pheka ngolu.
PHI 4:14 Kaasi bwa buketi luhangini mu kungwaphama mu mambu matadidini biwayi byama.
PHI 4:15 Luzayibwa kwenu bukheti, benu-benu bisi Fidiphu: tangwa yíkatuka ku Masetwani, muna tangwa dina yíyandika kuyadingisa kwa Musamu wa Bukheti, benu lwákala Dibundu dimosi mu kutsadisa, benu lwesi lwákota mambu matadidini phasi zama keti mu kyesi kyama.
PHI 4:16 Mukuma, ha yíkala ku Tesalonika, benu phi lwáphitika hika mu mbala ya zodi bina yíkala byawu mupfunu.
PHI 4:17 Heku ni makabu mbati sanda; kima mbati sanda, lufutu lwa mihangu myenu mya bukheti lwayikama hika kikuma kya benu.
PHI 4:18 Yenina yi bima byosu amana yenina byawu hika lawu, mbongibya byosu bina luphitikiki muna moku ma Ephafoditi. Mana menina mananasi ma mvumba ya kitoku, kimenga kina katambwasini Nzambi, kina kyisi musephidisa yandi.
PHI 4:19 Nzambi wama kabásisa byosu bina luvwini mupfunu, bwosu buna kyenina kimvwama kyandi, muna khembu, mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
PHI 4:20 Khembu yakala kwena Nzambi yi Tata wetu, mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna
PHI 4:21 Hanenu mboti kwena bakwikidi boosu mwena Kidisitu Yesu. Baphangi babana benina ha kimosi yi meni, mboti baluhekini.
PHI 4:22 Bakwikidi boosu, mboti baluhekini; theti-theti basadi bana benina mu nganda ya Khayisala.
PHI 4:23 Yambula khenda za Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu zakala muna kitembu kyenu!
COL 1:1 Pholu, thumwa wa Kidisitu Yesu muna luzolu lwa Nzambi yi phangi Thimoti.
COL 1:2 Kwena batu ba Nzambi, baphangi babana bisi sila mbundu mwena Kidisitu benina ku Kholosayi: Nzambi Tata wetu kaluheka khenda yi ngemba.
COL 1:3 Tuvutudini matondu kwena Nzambi, Tata wa Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu, amana thwisi lombila konda kulembwa kikuma kya benu.
COL 1:4 Kikuma, twayukà mu kuzonzila lukwikilu lwenu mwena Kidisitu Yesu amana yi lungongu luna lwenina lwawu kikuma kya batu ba Nzambi boosu.
COL 1:5 Mukuma, lwisi sya kivuvu mu mana kaluyidikila Nzambi muna mazilu. Tangwa lwayuka ndinga ya kyedika, Musamu wa Bukheti, ha watula kwa benu, wuluzayikisi kivuvu kyakina.
COL 1:6 Musamu wa Bukheti wawu wátula yi kuna lwena benu, bwosu buna wubutini bibundu wuyalanganini muna tsi ya muthu, phila mosi kwena benu, tukidila buna lwáyuka amana lwázaya khenda za Nzambi mu kyedika.
COL 1:7 Musamu wa Bukheti wawu lwabongilawa kwena Ephafwasi, nduku wetu wa kisalu, kenina musadi wa Kidisitu walunga kikuma kya benu.
COL 1:8 Amana, yandi wátumenika mutindu wa lungongu luna káluheka Kitembu.
COL 1:9 Yi hakana, betu phi, tuka kilumbu kina twáyukilabwa, thwisiku lembwa mu kulombila Nzambi kikuma kya benu, mu kulomba phi ni lwakala babasa mu nzayilu ya luzolu lwandi, muna mudimu wosu yi ngangu za mu kitembu.
COL 1:10 Ndangu lwadyatilaka mu mutindu wuna kazodini Pfumu, ndangu twamusephidisaka bwosu buna kyisi zola mu mambu moosu; lwabuta bibundu muna mitindu mya mihangu myosu mya bukheti, lwakola muna nzayilu ya Nzambi.
COL 1:11 Amana lwakituka yi ngolu mu mitindu myosu muna ngolu zandi za khembu, ndangu lwakwaminaka mu kyesi yi sipha dya mbundu ku kimeka kyosu.
COL 1:12 Vutulenu matondu kwena Tata wuna wálukitula batu bana balungini mu kubonga ndambu ya kimvwama kina káswekila batu ba Nzambi muna luyalu lwa mwini.
COL 1:13 Yandi wátukatula ku hamu dya mudima mu kutunata muna luyalu lwa Mwana wandi watondama;
COL 1:14 mwena yandi tuvwidini luhulusu yi ndoluka ya masumu.
COL 1:15 Kidisitu kenina kifwani kya Nzambi wuna wisiku monika; Mwana wa tsomi muna bihangwa byosu.
COL 1:16 Mukuma mwena yandi byáhangamina bima byosu muna mazilu yi hana tsi; bina byisi monika yi bina byisiku monika; biti bya luyalu, bipfumu, ngolu za luyalu lwa mbi, hamu; byosu byáhangamina mwena yandi yi kikuma kya yandi.
COL 1:17 Amana Kidisitu kenina ku thwala ya kima kyosu, amana mwena yandi byisi zyamina bima byosu.
COL 1:18 Yandi kenina mutwa wa lutu, lutu, lwaluna lwenina Dibundu. Kenina luyandiku, mwana wa tsomi hana kati dya bafwa, ndangu kakala wa theti muna bima byosu.
COL 1:19 Mukuma Nzambi kyesi kámonabwa ni bunzambi bwandi bwosu bwakadila mwena yandi Kidisitu
COL 1:20 amana muna nzila ya Mwana wandi, wávutula kithwadi ha kati dya bima byosu yi yandi-meni; byakala bina byenina ha tsi holo phi bina byenina mu mazilu, tangwa kasya ngemba mu nzila ya menga ma Mwana wandi, mana kátyaka hana kitakani.
COL 1:21 Amana kwena benu lwákala theti kyana yi Nzambi, lwákala bambeni bandi muna mutindu wa mabanza menu yi muna mihangu myenu mya mbi.
COL 1:22 Amana buthwena, Nzambi, wávutula kithwadi ha kati dya benu yi yandi, muna nzila ya lufwa lwa mu lutu lwa Mwana wandi, ndangu kalunata benu ku thwala ya yandi: batu ba Nzambi, bakonda kifu, bakonda keti dyambu dya kulufundila.
COL 1:23 Yi hakana ni, yuka lwazingilaka mu lukwikilu, bazyama amana ba kutunga buna bufwanini. Konda kudiyambwadila ni baluhukumuna mu kivuvu kina lwábonga tangwa lwáyuka Musamu wa Bukheti. Musamu wa Bukheti meni wuna básamuna kwena bihangwa byosu bina byisi zingila mu sina dya zilu, amana kuna wawuna, meni Pholu, yíkitwakila musadi.
COL 1:24 Buthwena, mbati sangwala muna minyanga myama mina mbati mona kikuma kya benu. Amana, muna lutu lwa meni, ndungisini kina kikondini ku biwayi bya Kidisitu kikuma lutu lwandi luna lwenina Dibundu.
COL 1:25 Ku Dibundu yíkitwakila musadi, bwosu bwenina kiyeka kina kápheka Nzambi kikuma kya benu: ndangu yisamuna ndinga ya Nzambi buna bufwanini.
COL 1:26 Diswekamu meni dina dyáswekama muna matangwa moosu yi kwena makula moosu, kaasi buthwena, dimonikini kwena bakwikidi.
COL 1:27 Kwena bawu kázola Nzambi kuzayikisa kutoka kwa kimvwama kya khembu kina kitadidini diswekamu meni dyadina kikuma kya bana bakondi kala Bayuta. Amana diswekamu meni dyadina dyenina: kidisitu mwena benu, kivuvu kya khembu.
COL 1:28 Yandi wuna thwisi samuna, mu kulwengisaka mutu wosu yi mu kulongaka kwena mutu wosu, muna mudimu wosu, ndangu twalenda mu kukitula mutu wosu, mutu walunga mwena Kidisitu.
COL 1:29 Kyakina kikuma yisi dihekila phasi, mu kunwaninaka muna ngolu zina zisi tuka kwena yandi, zisi sala mwena meni yi ngolu zoosu.
COL 2:1 Kikuma nzodini lwazaya ni muzingu wa mbuta mbati nwana kikuma kya benu, kikuma kya bakidisitu ba ku Lawodise yi kikuma kya bahika babana khaku kedi bambona mu kimwesa mutu.
COL 2:2 Ndangu babaheka kikesa, bakala kithwadi muna lungongu. Amana bakala boosu babasa mu ngangu, kikuma kya kuzaya diswekamu dya Nzambi, disongidila ni yandi-meni Kidisitu.
COL 2:3 Mwena yandi mwaswamana bima bya thalu byosu bya mudimu yi bya mazaya.
COL 2:4 Nzimbudini bwabuna mu kusya ni baluhunaku kwena mutu mosi mu lengu ndinga.
COL 2:5 Mukuma, ho kyana yenina mu kimutu, mu kitembu, ha kimosi yenina yenu. Mu kyesi yenina, mu kumona ni, kwena benu moosu misi hitila mu ndonga; amana lukwikilu lwenu kwena Kidisitu, lwenina lwazyama ngolu.
COL 2:6 Kikuma, bwosu lutambudini Kidisitu Yesu, Pfumu, dyatilenu mwena yandi.
COL 2:7 Zikenu misodi mwena yandi, amana tungenu luzingu lwenu hana thandu ya yandi. Disyamisakenu muna lukwikilu, muna mutindu wa mamana bálulonga, amana vutulakenu matondu ma lawu kwena Nzambi kosu tangwa.
COL 2:8 Dikengenu, ka mutu ku kalukwata ha mutambu ku nduka za mbi, amana za phamba. Bwenina bukamvi kwandi, bwisi zyamina ku mikuku mya batu, bwosu zenina ngolu za bitembu bya tsi, kaasi bweku mutindu mosi yi mana kazodini Kidisitu.
COL 2:9 Mukuma, mwena Kidisitu mwisi zingila lutu lwa bunzambi bwandi bwosu.
COL 2:10 Amana benu lwenina babasa mwena Kidisitu, yandi wenina mutwa wa kipfumu kyosu yi luyalu lwosu.
COL 2:11 Mwena Kidisitu lwákotila benu phi mukhanda wuna wákonda hangamina ku moku ma batu. Kaasi mukhanda meni wuna mu nzila ya Kidisitu wáhangamina, amana wawuna wulukutumunini benu mu kihika kya lutu lwa masumu.
COL 2:12 Báluzika yi Kidisitu muna nzila ya mbotika, lwáfutumuka phi ha kimosi mwena yandi, muna lukwikilu lwa ngolu zoosu za Nzambi wuna wámufutumuna ha kati dya bafwa.
COL 2:13 Amana benu lwákala bafwa kikuma kya mitsoki myenu, yi kikuma kya bungulungwa bwa lutu lwenu, Nzambi wálufutumuna ha kimosi yi Kidisitu, mu kulolula mitsoki myetu myosu.
COL 2:14 Wáyatawa mukanda wuna wakala tufundaka yi mikuku mya wawu, amana wákatulawa mu kukhokawa hana kitakani.
COL 2:15 Nzambi wáwongumuna bipfumu bya bitembu yi luyalu; wálubulabya ha tseki amana wábulumunabya hanga bakwatami muna kinunga kya Mwana wandi.
COL 2:16 Yi hakana ni, ka mutu ku kalufundisa ku kina lwisi dya yi kina lwisi nwa, kondi loni kikuma kya kyufu kitadidini mukinzi wa ngonda ya pha kondi loni yi mukinzi wa Sabata.
COL 2:17 Byosu bina byenina kininga kya mana menina mu kukwisa, kaasi kyedika kya mawu kibati monikina muna lutu lwa Kidisitu.
COL 2:18 Luyambwadilaku ni balufundisa kwena batu bana bisi sanda mu kudikulumuna mu mambu mana misi monika amana bisi sambila banzyo. Bisi dihana ku ndosi za bawu. Amana mabanza ma bawu ma kimutu misi babasisa mu kimvunya kya phamba;
COL 2:19 amana bisiku simbidila kwena Kidisitu yandi wenina mutwa. Tuka kwena yandi, lutu lwosu lwákhundakanina bwa bukheti muna bikhosu yi muna misuni myisi dikwatila ha kimosi. Nzambi wisi kodisa lutu lwaluna.
COL 2:20 Ho ni lwáfwa kedi yi Kidisitu mu mambu ma bitembu bya tsi, kikuma kya biki lubati zingila hangambedi ni ku moku ma tsi hika lwenina, mu kutambwasaka ni baluhekaka mitsiku mya mutindu wawuna:
COL 2:21 «Wubongaku kyaki», «Wuyedikakyoku», «Wusimbaku kina».
COL 2:22 Bima bina byosu byátangamina mu kuzangana ku manima ma tsadidi ya byawu. Byenina bizila yi malongi ma kimutu.
COL 2:23 Mukyedika, bizila bya mutindu meni wuna, byisi monika hangambedi ni bya kabasi yi mudimu. Mukuma, bulombini ni batu basambila muna mutindu wuna bazodini bawu meni, bakala yi kudikulumuna kwa luvunu; amana badihekaka phasi muna lutu. Kaasi, bizila byabina byeku keti mupfunu, kaka kikuma kya kusephidisaka lwesi tsambu za lutu.
COL 3:1 Amana honi benu lwátokama ku lufwa yi Kidisitu, sandakenu bima bya mu zilu, kwakuna kazakadini Kidisitu kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi.
COL 3:2 Banzakenu ku bima bina byenina mu zilu, kaasi ka byabi ku byenina ha tsi.
COL 3:3 Mukuma benu lwáfwa, amana luzingu lwenu lwaswekama lwenina hakimosi yi Kidisitu mwena Nzambi.
COL 3:4 Kilumbu kamónika, Kidisitu yandi wenina luzingu lwenu, hanga benu phi lumoniki hika yi yandi muna khembu.
COL 3:5 Yi hakana ni, hondenu miza myosu mya ha tsi mina myenina mwena benu: mbongi, mambu ma mvindu, tsambu, nzoluka za mbi yi lukusu luna lwenina kufukamina kwa nzambi za biteki.
COL 3:6 Yi hakana khabu za Nzambi zisi kwisila kwena bandwandwa.
COL 3:7 Theti, benu phi, bwabuna lwakala dyatila, tangwa lwákala luzingu lwenu mu sina dya bima byabina.
COL 3:8 Kaasi, buthwena benu phi, losenu bikalulu bina byosu: khabu, bumbisi, khu, kuhuna misamu, ndinga za khadi zina zilubukini muna munwa wenu.
COL 3:9 Ludihunakaku benu yi benu: mukuma benu lwálosa kedi mutu wa khulu yi mihangu myandi;
COL 3:10 amana lwávwata mutu wa pha, wuna wukitukini wa pha muna nzayilu, bwosu bwenina kifwani kya Muhangi wandi.
COL 3:11 Buthwena, kweku hika ni Mungeleki, keti Muyuta, keti wuna wakota mukhanda, keti ngulungu, keti musenzi, keti mutu wálonguka, keti muhika, keti mutu wa kiphwanza, kaasi Kidisitu kenina wa muthu muna byosu.
COL 3:12 Yi bwabuna ni, benu básola kwena Nzambi, batu ba Nzambi yi batu batondama; vwatenu tsambu ya kyedika, buweti, kudikulumuna, lembami yi sipha dya mbundu.
COL 3:13 Ditambwasakenu benu yi benu; yuka mutu kanyengalakana kikuma kya mukwawu, difwilakenu khenda bwosu buna kálufwila Pfumu khenda. Benu phi, hangenu bwabuna.
COL 3:14 Amana hana thandu ya byosu, vwatenu lungongu, mukuma lwenina zita dya mukwandi dya kikhunda.
COL 3:15 Yambula ngemba ya Kidisitu, yina kálutedila Nzambi mu kukala bitini bya lutu lumosi, yayala muna mbundu zenu. Zayakenu mu kuvutula matondu.
COL 3:16 Yambula ndinga ya Kidisitu yi kimvwama kyandi kyosu yazingila mwena benu. Dilongenu amana dilwengisenu benu yi benu muna mudimu wosu, muna mikunga, muna mikunga mya khembu yi mikunga mya mu kitembu. Muna khenda, muyimbidilenu Nzambi yi mbundu yenu yosu.
COL 3:17 Amana kyosu kima kina luhangini, mu ndinga kondi loni mu mihangu, hangenukya mu zina dya Pfumu Yesu, mu kuvutulaka matondu mu nzila ya yandi kwena Nzambi Tata.
COL 3:18 Bakhetu, lemvukenu kwena bayakala benu, bwosu bulombini mwena Pfumu.
COL 3:19 Bayala, zolenu bakhetu benu, amana lulubulaku phisi kwena bawu.
COL 3:20 Bana, lemvukenu mu byosu kwena bibuti byenu, mukuma yi bwabuna bwisi musephidisa Pfumu.
COL 3:21 Batata, lukwatisaku bana benu khabu, hanga bakatula nana kikesa.
COL 3:22 Basadi, lemvukenu mu byosu kwena bapfumu benu muna kimutu. Luhangilabwoku lwesi mu mesu ma bawu, hangambedi ni kikuma kya kuditondisa kwena batu. Kaasi yi mbundu ya bulemvu, muna bweya bwa Pfumu.
COL 3:23 Kyosu kina lwisi hanga, hangenukya yi mbundu yenu yosu, hangambedi ni kikuma kya Pfumu lubatikya hangila, kaasi ka kikuma kya batu ku.
COL 3:24 Zayenu ni lwatámbula kuvwa hanga lufutu kwena Pfumu. Basadilenu hanga bahika ba Pfumu wa mukwandi, Kidisitu.
COL 3:25 Mukuma wuna wisi yenguna, kafútama muna kayengu kana kahangini, Nzambi kisiku swasisa batu.
COL 4:1 Bapfumu, bahangilenu basadi benu buna bwenina bwa masonga yi bwalunga. Bambukenu ni benu phi, Pfumu mosi lwenina yandi muna zilu.
COL 4:2 Dihanakenu kosu tangwa mu bisambu, kadilakenu mu kitsungila muna nzila ya byawu, muna kuvutula kwa matondu.
COL 4:3 Sambilakenu phi kikuma kya betu, ndangu Nzambi katuyafwadila mwelu kikuma kya kulonga Ndinga. Ndangu twasamuna diswekamu dya Kidisitu. Kikuma kya dyawu dina yenina mu boloku.
COL 4:4 Amana sambilakenu ndangu yizonziladya wengele bwosu buna ndungini mu kuzonzilabwa.
COL 4:5 Dyatilakenu muna mudimu kwena babana bakondi kala Bayuta; sadilenu tangwa.
COL 4:6 Yambula ndinga zenu, kosu tangwa, zakalaka yi khenda yi munzenzu wa mungwa; ndangu lwazaya buna bulungini mu kuvutula mvutu kwena mutu yi mutu.
COL 4:7 Muna mambu mana mathadidini, Tisiki, phangi wenina mwena Pfumu, phangi watondama, musadi wa kusila mbundu, nduku wa kisalu kya kihika, kalúmenikina moosu.
COL 4:8 Yiluhitiki yandi yi tswatsu yosu mu kusya ni lwazaya buna thwenina betu, amana ndangu kalubwisa mbundu.
COL 4:9 Nzila mosi yimuhitikini yi Onezimi phangi watondama, wa kusila mbundu, mutu wa ku hata dyenu. Balúmenikina moosu mana mabati hita kwaku.
COL 4:10 Adisitadiki, mukwetu nduku wama wa boloku, mboti kaluhekini, yi Malaku, kiwutu kya Balanabasi. Lubongikini mikuku mitadidi Malaku: honi kisa lutala, muyambenu bukheti.
COL 4:11 Amana Yesu wuna bisi tela ni Yusitusi, mboti kaluheki phi. Hana kati dya batu bana bákota mukhanda, bawu lwesi bisi yukana yi meni kikuma kya Kipfumu kya Nzambi; bawu baphekiki kikesa kya lawu.
COL 4:12 Ephafwasi wenina mosi wa benu, mboti kaluhekini; muhika wa Kidisitu Yesu, kisiku lembwa mu kunwanaka kikuma kya benu muna bisambu byandi; ndangu lwazyama, lwabasa yi kikumbwala mu kulungisa, buna bulungi, luzolu lwa Nzambi, amana lwatelama bwa bukheti.
COL 4:13 Mbati mutila kimbangi ni kisi diheka phasi lawu kikuma kya benu, kikuma kya bakidisitu ba mbanza ya Lawodise yi kikuma kya bakidisitu ba mbanza ya Yelaphodisi.
COL 4:14 Luka, munganga watondama, mboti kaluhekini yi Temasi, yandi phi.
COL 4:15 Bahekenu mboti baphangi bana benina ku mbanza ya Lawodise, mutindu mosi phi Nimifwa yi Dibundu dina dyenina muna nzu yandi.
COL 4:16 Kilumbu watángama mukanda wawu kwena benu, hangenu phila yosu ni watangama phi ku Dibundu dya mbanza ya Lawodise. Amana benu, mutindu mosi, lwatanga mukanda wuna walúyisila ku mbanza ya Lawodise.
COL 4:17 Muzimbwalenu Adisiphi: «Keba kisyelu kyaki wátambula mwena Pfumu ndangu walungisakya buna bwa bukheti.»
COL 4:18 Mboti yiluhekini, meni Pholu, yi koku dyama: -Sungulakenu ni meni mu miyololu yenina. -Yambula ngemba yakala yi benu.
1TH 1:1 Pholu, Silasi yi Thimoti. Kwena Dibundu dya bisi Tesalonika dina dyenina mwena Nzambi Tata, yi mwena Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu: Yambula khenda yi ngemba byakala yi benu.
1TH 1:2 Thwisi vutula kosu tangwa matondu kwena Nzambi kikuma kya benu boosu, amana thwisi tumbula mazina ma benu konda kulembwa muna bisambu byetu.
1TH 1:3 Thwisi yubuka mu moosu mana malutadidini: muhangu wa lukwikilu, lombu dya lungongu yi kikwamina kyenu mu kivuvu kya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu, ku mesu ma Nzambi wetu yi Tata wetu.
1TH 1:4 Tuzayini, baphangi, ni Nzambi wáluzola amana wálusola,
1TH 1:5 mukuma Musamu wa Bukheti wetu wálutudilaku mu ndinga lwesi, kaasi yi ngolu zina zilutini yi Kitembu Kyatoma yi kikumbwala kya lawu. Amana phi, luzayi keti abweti tukadiki ha kati dya benu, kikuma kya mboti ya benu.
1TH 1:6 Amana benu, lwátusokulula, betu yi Pfumu, mu kutambwasa Ndinga, ha kati dya kiwayi kya lawu, yi kyesi kya Kitembu Kyatoma.
1TH 1:7 Yihana lwákitwakila mbandu mosi kikuma kya bakwikidi boosu muna Masetwani yi mu Akayi.
1TH 1:8 Mukuma ndinga ya Pfumu yáyukalakana kwena benu, amana heku ni ku Masetwani lwesi yi ku Akayi: lukwikilu lwenu mwena Nzambi lwázayakana muma mwosu, mu phila yina yenina ni thweku yi mupfunu wa kuzonzilabwa keti khi kima.
1TH 1:9 Bisi menika, kikuma kya betu, khi mutindu wa kuyamba twáwana kwena benu, abweti lwábaluka kwena Nzambi, mu kubwisaka nzambi za biteki kikuma kya kusadila, hanga bahika, Nzambi mosi wa moya yi wa kyedika
1TH 1:10 yi kikuma kya kuhingila ni Mwana wandi, Yesu, wuna káfutumuna ha kati dya bafwa, kisa vutukisa tuka mu mazilu, yandi watúkatula ku khabu zina zakwísa.
1TH 2:1 Luzayibwa mboti benu-benu baphangi: kukwisa kwetu kwena benu kukadikiku kwa khatu.
1TH 2:2 Kaasi luzayibwa ni, theti bátunyokuna amana bátutukwana kuna mbanza ya Fidiphu. Kaasi twázonza yi kikumbwala mwena Nzambi wetu mu kulusamwana Musamu wa Bukheti wa Nzambi mbatanana kwákala lawu dya mizingu.
1TH 2:3 Mukuma, kikesa kyetu kitukiku mu sunga dya kulutotisa, kondilo mu mambu ma mvindu, keti mu kuhuna.
1TH 2:4 Kaasi kikuma Nzambi wisi tutesa amana wututambwasini kikuma kya kutuheka kiyeka kya Musamu wa Bukheti, tubatiku sanda kikuma kya kusephidisa batu, kaasi kikuma kya kusephidisa Nzambi wuna wisi tesa mbundu zetu.
1TH 2:5 Kikuma, luzayibwa bukheti ni khaniku tuzonza yi lengu ndinga kikuma kya kuhuna batu, amana twákalaku keti sunga dya mbongu, Nzambi kenina mbangi wetu.
1TH 2:6 Tusandikiku lukumu luna lwisi tuka kwena batu, keti kwena benu keti kwena batu bahika.
1TH 2:7 Amana bwosu thwenina bathumwa ba Kidisitu, twakhana lulomba benu mu kunata kizitu kyenu. Kaasi betu twádikulumuna kwetu twakadini hana kati dya benu, hanga buna kisi tsasa ngudi bana ba yandi-meni.
1TH 2:8 Twázola muna kyesi kyetu kikuma kya benu, tuluhekaku lwesi Musamu wa Bukheti wa Nzambi, kaasi yi luzingu lwa betu-betu phi, kikuma lwákituka batondama betu.
1TH 2:9 Kikuma, baphangi, yubukenu lombu dyetu yi kulembwa kwa lutu kwetu: tusadikini phipha yi mwini, amana tubwisikini mu kuyekamina kwena mosi wa benu, yibwabuna tululongikini Musamu wa Bukheti wa Nzambi.
1TH 2:10 Bambangi lwenina benu-benu yi Nzambi phi: tudyatidikini ku thwala ya benu lwisi kwikila mu mutindu watoma, buna bufwani, amana bakonda kifu.
1TH 2:11 Luzayibwa phi ni tukadikini kikuma kya kosu mutu wa benu bwosu kenina tata kwena bana bandi.
1TH 2:12 Tuluhekikini ndongisila yi kikesa, amana tulusikidikisini mu kudyatila muna mutindu wuna wufwani wa Nzambi, yandi wuna wálutela mu kukota muna Kipfumu kyandi yi muna khembu yandi.
1TH 2:13 Amana kikuma kya bwabuna betu phi, tuvutudini matondu kwena Nzambi konda kulembwa: mu tangwa twaluyukisini Ndinga ya Nzambi lwatambwasaya, amana lwátambwasiyoku hanga ndinga yimosi ya kimutu kaasi hanga Ndinga ya Nzambi, yenina kyedika; amana yibwabuna yisi sala mwena benu bakwikidi.
1TH 2:14 Kikuma, baphangi, benu-benu lwásokulula mbandu ya Mabundu ma Nzambi mana menina mu Yuteya amana misi kwikila mwena Kidisitu Yesu. Lwányokuka kwena biwutu byenu bya tsi mosi, bwosu mányokuka Mabundu mana kwena Bayuta.
1TH 2:15 Bawu báhonda Pfumu Yesu yi bambikudi, amana bawu bátunyokuna. Bisiku sephidisa Nzambi amana bawu benina bambeni ba batu boosu.
1TH 2:16 Bisi tukakidikisa mu kuzonza kwena batu bakondi kala Bayuta hanga bahuluka nana. Amana muna bwabuna bisiku lembwa mu kubasisaka mu masumu ma bawu. Kaasi tsuka-tsuka khabu za Nzambi zábabwila.
1TH 2:17 Kwena betu, baphangi, kunima dya kudihambula yi benu mu tangwa dimosi, kyana ku mesu kaasi ka ku mbundu ku, yi lawu dya nzoluka yina twákadi yawu, twahangi mutindu wosu kikuma kya kulumona.
1TH 2:18 Tuzodikini thwisa mbala za lawu mu kulukinda, yi meni-meni Pholu, kaasi Satana wátukakidikisa.
1TH 2:19 Nati si wenina kivuvu kyetu, kyesi kyetu, mukhonzi wetu wa lulendu? Ka benu ku phi, ku mesu ma Pfumu wetu Yesu kilumbu kakwisa?
1TH 2:20 Eeh, benu lwenina khembu yetu yi kyesi kyetu.
1TH 3:1 Amana phi, bwosu twafwanaku hika mu kuhingila, hanga tuzengini twanangina kwetu betu hika ku Ateni,
1TH 3:2 amana tuluhitikini, phangi wetu Thimoti, mukwetu wetu wa kisalu kya Nzambi kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti wa Kidisitu; ndangu kaluzyamisa yi kuluheka kikesa kikuma kya mana matadidini lukwikilu lwenu.
1TH 3:3 Ndangu ka mutu ku kabwa mu kiwayi kyaki lubati mona. Kikuma, benu-benu luzayi mboti ni kyenina ndambu ku mana káyidika Nzambi kikuma kya betu.
1TH 3:4 Tangwa twákala kwena benu, twátekila luzimbwala ni twanyókuka; amana bwabuna phi busalamini bwosu buna luzayidibwa.
1TH 3:5 Yi hakana ni, meni phi bwosu ndendikiku hika mu kusipha mbundu, phitikiki Thimoti mu kubonga tsangu za lukwikilu lwenu. Hanga muhukumuni kalusya nana mu kimeka, amana lombu dyetu dyakala nana dyakhatu.
1TH 3:6 Kaasi buthwena kisi tuvutwakila Thimoti mu kutuka kwena benu; tsangu za bukheti katunatinini zina zitadidi lukwikilu lwenu, lungongu lwenu yi mabanza mamboti mana lwisi kala mawu hika kikuma kya betu. Katusamwani ni tsambu ya lawu lwisi kala yawu ni lwatumona hika, bwosu twisi kala betu phi yi tsambu ya lawu mu kulumona hika benu.
1TH 3:7 Kikuma kya bwabuna, baphangi, hana kati dya biwayi byetu byosu yi minyanga myetu, tubongidini kikesa mwena benu mu nzila ya lukwikilu lwenu.
1TH 3:8 Buthwena tubati zinga hika kikuma bazyama lwenina mu kithwadi yi Pfumu.
1TH 3:9 Abweti tufwanini kuvutula matondu kwena Nzambi kikuma kya benu, kikuma kya kyesi kina kyosu lwisi tuheka ku mesu ma yandi?
1TH 3:10 Phipha yi mwini, thwisi sambila yi ngolu zoosu, ndangu katuyafwadila nzila mu kulumona yi mu kuyika hika kina kikondini muna lukwikilu lwenu.
1TH 3:11 Yambula yandi meni Nzambi, Tata wetu yi Pfumu wetu Yesu batuyidikila nzila tii yi kuna kwena benu.
1TH 3:12 Yambula Pfumu kakódisa amana kavúdisa lawu lungongu luna lwenina lwawu ha kati dya benu yi kwena batu boosu, mu mbandu ya lwalu thwenina betu kikuma kya benu.
1TH 3:13 Pfumu kazyamisa mbundu zenu ndangu lwakala batu ba Nzambi amana bakonda kifu ku mesu ma Nzambi wenina Tata wetu, muna kilumbu kya kwisa kwa Pfumu wetu Yesu yi babana boosu benina ba yandi. Abwabuna!
1TH 4:1 Ku mana masadini, baphangi, lwálonguka kedi kwena betu mutindu wuna lulungini mu kukala yawu kikuma kya kumusephidisa Nzambi; amana phi bwabuna lubati dyatila. Kaasi buthwena, tululombini amana tulubokwadidini, muna zina dya Pfumu Yesu ni dyatilenu hika bukheti kuhita muna bwabuna.
1TH 4:2 Kikuma luzayini khi mutindu wa milongi twáluheka mituki kwena Pfumu Yesu.
1TH 4:3 Luzolu lwa Nzambi lwenina bwabu: lwakala batu ba Nzambi amana lwayambula mbongi.
1TH 4:4 Mosi-mosi wa benu kazaya mu kusola mukhetu muna mutindu wumosi watoma yi wa luzitu;
1TH 4:5 konda kudiyambwadila tsatu za mbi zaluyala, hanga baphani bana bakondi zaya Nzambi.
1TH 4:6 Muna dyambu meni dyadidi, ka mutu ku kasila phangi wandi khoni kondi loni mu kuhuna. Pfumu kisi fundisa ku byosu byabina. Tuluzimbwadikibwa kedi bwabuna amana tulukebisi hika.
1TH 4:7 Mukuma, Nzambi kátutedilaku mu mambu ma mvindu, kaasi muna kuditomisa.
1TH 4:8 Yi hakana ni, wuna wubusini milongi myami kabusiku mutu, kaasi Nzambi kabusini, yandi-meni wuna wisi luheka Kitembu Kyatoma wandi.
1TH 4:9 Kikuma kya mana matadidini lungongu lwa kiphangi, lweku yi mupfunu wa kulusonikina, mukuma, benu-benu, bálulonga kedi kwena Nzambi muna mutindu wa kudizola kwa benu yi benu.
1TH 4:10 Amana bwabuna lwisi hanga kwena baphangi boosu bana benina muna kinzunga kya Masetwani dyosu. Kaasi tuluhekini kikesa, baphangi, ni lwenda hika ku mesu.
1TH 4:11 Kalakenu yi kitya kya kuzingilaka mu ngemba, mu kutadilaka mu mambu mana matadidini benu-benu yi mu kusala bisalu yi moku menu, bwosu tululongisidikibwa.
1TH 4:12 Ndangu lwalenga dyatila buna bwa bukheti ku thwala ya batu ba ku phenza, amana luyekaminaku kwena mutu.
1TH 4:13 Tuzodiku, baphangi, ni lwakala konda kuzaya muna mana matadidini bafwa, ndangu lukalaku mu kyadi hanga batu bahika bana bakondini kivuvu.
1TH 4:14 Kikuma, yuka tukwikidini ni Yesu wáfwa amana wáfutumuka, mutindu wumosi, tukwikidini ni Nzambi kafútumuna phi, ha kimosi yi Yesu, babana bakwisa fwa mu kukwikilu mwena yandi.
1TH 4:15 Kikuma, talenu mana tuluzimbwadini, bwosu yenina ndinga ya Pfumu: betu twakála mu luzingu, twatékidilaku keti koma batu babana bátekila fwa, mu kilumbu kya kwisa kwa Pfumu.
1TH 4:16 Mukuma tangwa wahanama muswa mu ndinga ya ngolu, ndinga ya kaphita wa banzyo yayukalakana, phungi ya Nzambi yabula amana Pfumu yandi-meni katuluka ku zilu; babana bamana fwa mwena Kidisitu batókama batheti.
1TH 4:17 Ku manima, betu thwenina mu luzingu, twazánguka ha kimosi yi bawu muna matuti kikuma kya kutundakana yi Pfumu muna muphephi. Amana bwabuna twakwata kadila yi Pfumu bilumbu byosu.
1TH 4:18 Dihekakenu kikesa benu yi benu muna ndinga zazi.
1TH 5:1 Baphangi, kikuma kya kilumbu yi tangwa, lweku yi mupfunu ni balusonikina.
1TH 5:2 Kikuma, luzayini benu-benu buna bwa bukheti ni kilumbu kya kwisa kwa Pfumu kyakála mu kithulumukina hanga mwifi muna kisuku.
1TH 5:3 Tangwa bazimbula batu: «Ngemba yi talala bikotini», amana kuzangana kwisi kota mu kithulumukina hakana henina bawu, hanga ndunza za kubuta kwena mukhetu wenina ku kifundu. Amana ka mutu ku wafwána mu kuhengamaza.
1TH 5:4 Kaasi benu, baphangi, lweku mu mudima, ndangu kilumbu kyakina kilukadilaku kya kithulumukina hanga mwifi.
1TH 5:5 Mukuma benu boosu lwenina bana ba kikhya yi bana ba mwini. Lweku bana ba phipha keti bana ba mudima.
1TH 5:6 Yi hakana ni, tunimbaku hanga batu bahika, kaasi tukalenu batemuna amana tukalenu ha tambu.
1TH 5:7 Mukuma babana bisi nimba, mu phipha bisi nimba, amana babana bisi dizedisa, mu phipha bisi dizedisa.
1TH 5:8 Kaasi betu thwenina batu ba mwini, tukalenu ha tambu. Tuvwatenu lukwikilu yi lungongu hanga miledi mya bisengu misi sweka thulu, amana kivuvu kya luhulusu hanga phwa.
1TH 5:9 Kikuma Nzambi kátuyidikilaku ku khabu zandi, kaasi kikuma kya kutambula luhulusu mwena Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu;
1TH 5:10 wuna wafwa kikuma kya betu ndangu kalenga tuzingisa ha kimosi yi yandi kilumbu kakwísa, twakala ba moya kondi loni bafwa.
1TH 5:11 Yi hakana, dibwisakenu mbundu muna lukwikilu benu yi benu amana disadisakenu mu kukola mu kimvuka bwosu lwisibwa hangila kedi.
1TH 5:12 Baphangi, tululombini mu kuzitisaka batu babana bisi diheka phasi ha kati dya benu, babana káheka Pfumu kiyeka kya kulutwadisaka yi kya kululwengisaka.
1TH 5:13 Bazitisakenu lawu amana bazolakenu, kikuma kya kisalu kya bawu. Zingilenu mu ngemba hana kati dya benu.
1TH 5:14 Tuluhekini kikesa, baphangi: lwengisakenu batu bakonda luzitu, hanakenu kikesa kwena batu bana beku yi kikesa, sadisenu batu bana balembwa, siphulenu mbundu kikuma kya boosu.
1TH 5:15 Tekikenu matu ni mutu kavutulaku mbela kwena mukwawu; kaasi sandakenu kosu tangwa mu kuhangaka bukheti, benu yi benu yi kwena mutu wosu.
1TH 5:16 Sangwalakenu bilumbu byosu.
1TH 5:17 Sambilakenu konda kulembwa.
1TH 5:18 Vutulakenu matondu mu mambu moosu kwena Nzambi. Yi bwabuna kisi zola Nzambi muna luzingu lwenu mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
1TH 5:19 Lukakidikisaku mihangu mya Kitembu.
1TH 5:20 Lulewulaku misamu mya bambikudi.
1TH 5:21 Zyaminenu bima byosu buna bwa bukheti, kaasi simbidilenu kina kyenina kya bukheti;
1TH 5:22 amana dikandenu ku mbi yi mitindu mya yawu myosu.
1TH 5:23 Yambula Nzambi wa ngemba kalutambika yandi-meni mu luzingu lwenu lwosu. Yambula kimutu kyenu kyosu, kitembu, moya yi lutu byakala konda kifu kikuma kya kilumbu kina kakwísa Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu.
1TH 5:24 Yandi wulutedini kenina wa kusila mbundu, amana kalúngisabwa phi.
1TH 5:25 Baphangi, sambilakenu phi kikuma kya betu.
1TH 5:26 Hanenu mboti mosi yatoma kwena baphangi boosu.
1TH 5:27 Yilubokwadidibwa, muna zina dya Pfumu: tangisenu mukanda wawu kwena baphangi boosu.
1TH 5:28 Yambula khenda za Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu zakala yi benu.
2TH 1:1 Pholu, Silasi yi Thimoti. Kwena Dibundu dya bisi Tesalonika dina dyenina mwena Nzambi Tata wetu yi kwena Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu:
2TH 1:2 Yambula Nzambi, Tata wetu, yi Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu baluheka khenda yi ngemba.
2TH 1:3 Tufweti vutulaka matondu kwena Nzambi kosu tangwa, kikuma kya benu, baphangi; amana bwabuna bwenina bwalunga, mukuma lukwikilu lwenu lubati vula lawu amana lungongu luna lwenina lwawu benu boosu mwena benu yi benu, lwakolaka kosu tangwa.
2TH 1:4 Yi hakana thwenina yi lulendu kikuma kya benu muna Mabundu ma Nzambi, kikuma kya kikwamina kyenu yi lukwikilu lwenu muna minyanga myenu myosu amana yi muna biwayi bina lwisi kwamina.
2TH 1:5 Byabina byenina bidimbu bya pfundusu ya masonga ya Nzambi; ndangu lwamonika balunga mu Kipfumu kya Nzambi kina lunyokwamina.
2TH 1:6 Kikuma, yuka bwa kyedika, Nzambi kenina masonga: kafúta kiwayi muna kiwayi kwena babana bisi luyukisa kiwayi.
2TH 1:7 Amana kwena benu lubati nyokuka, Nzambi kalúheka talala ha kimosi yi betu, kilumbu kamónika Pfumu Yesu ku zilu yi banzyo bandi ba ngolu.
2TH 1:8 Kakwisila muna muleku wa mbawu, mu kuhana ndola kwena babana bazayiku Nzambi yi babana bisiku lemvuka ku Musamu wa Bukheti wa Pfumu wetu Yesu.
2TH 1:9 Babana babónga ndola yina yilungini, kuzangana kwa mvula yi mvula, kyana yi Pfumu yi ngolu za khembu yandi,
2TH 1:10 kilumbu kakwísa kikuma kya kumukembisa kwena batu bandi batu ba Nzambi, amana bamubakula yi ngituka kwena boosu babana bafwana mu kukwikila mwena yandi. Amana benu phi lwakwala muna thalu ya bawu, mukuma lwákwikila musamu wuna twálusamwana.
2TH 1:11 Yi hakana thwisini lombila phi kosu tangwa kikuma kya benu. Ndangu Nzambi wetu kalumona balunga ku mbila yandi. Amana kalungisa, muna ngolu zina zilutini, sunga dyosu dya buweti yi muhangu wosu wa lukwikilu.
2TH 1:12 Mukusya ni, zina dya Pfumu wetu Yesu bakembisiladya mwena benu, amana benu phi mwena yandi. Bwosu zenina khenda za Nzambi wetu yi za Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu.
2TH 2:1 Amana kima tululombini, baphangi, kikuma kya ngisa ya Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu yi lukutakanu lwetu bela-bela yi yandi:
2TH 2:2 yuka mutu kaluzimbwala ni kilumbu kya Pfumu kifwanini, lumukwikilaku, luzakamaku tswatsu, luditanikinaku baluvumwasa mbundu keti kuluyukisa bweya ku mbikutulu, ku musamu kondi loni ku mukanda wumosi wutukini kwena betu.
2TH 2:3 Ka mutu ku kaluhuna keti mu khi mutindu. Mukuma bulungi theti ni batu babwisa malongi ma Kidisitu amana Mutu wa mbi kadimonikisa, yandi wuna wátangama mu kuzangana.
2TH 2:4 Yandu yandu katéndisa kyosu kina bisi fukamina batu, bisi mona phi hanga nzambi. Amana kakwenda kota tii yi muna kikumbu kya Nzambi kikuma kya kuzakala mwamuna yi kudisongila yandi meni hanga Nzambi.
2TH 2:5 Lubatiku yubuka ni yíluzimbwalabwa kedi ha yíkala hika kwena benu?
2TH 2:6 Kinga buthwena, luzayini kima kina kyisi mukwata ndangu kamonika muna tangwa dyandi.
2TH 2:7 Mukuma diswekamu dya Mbi mu kisalu dyenina kedi; bulungini lwesi ni yanduna wuna wisi mukwata buthwena kakatuka.
2TH 2:8 Hanana kakwisa lubula Mbi, wuna kahónda Pfumu Yesu kuna lwanda lwa munwa wandi, kamúkitula kima kya phamba muna khembu ya ngisa yandi.
2TH 2:9 Mbi kakwísa yi ngolu za Satana, kahanga mitindu myosu mya biphadi yi bidimbu yi bithondu bya bukamvi;
2TH 2:10 amana kahánga mbi muna mitindu myosu mya bukamvi kikuma kya kuhukumuna babana bisi kwenda mu kutota kwa bawu. Badítotisa kikuma bátambwasaku lungongu lwa kyedika mukusya ni balenga huluka.
2TH 2:11 Amana kikuma kya bwabuna Nzambi kabahitikidini ngolu zimosi za kuditotisila zina zibati balundika mu kukwikila ku bukamvi.
2TH 2:12 Ndangu babafundisa boosu babana bákwikilaku kyedika, kaasi bábonga tsambu ku kayengu.
2TH 2:13 Kikuma kya betu, baphangi batondama, benu babana katekila zola Pfumu hanga kabu dya theti, tufweti vutulaka matondu kosu kilumbu kwena Nzambi kikuma kya benu. Mukuma Nzambi kálusola kuna luyanduku kikuma kya luhulusu, muna nzila ya kuditambika kwa Kitembu wuna wisi lunatisa luzingu lwatoma yi lukwikilu lwenu mwena kyedika.
2TH 2:14 Muna bwabuna phi kálutedila Nzambi muna nzila ya Musamu wa Bukheti wa betu; ndangu lwabongila khembu ya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu.
2TH 2:15 Yi hakana ni, baphangi, zyamenu ngolu amana simbidilenu mikuku myami tululongini, keti ku ndinga keti loni ku mukanda.
2TH 2:16 Yambula, yandi-meni Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu yi Nzambi, Tata wetu, wuna wátuzola amana wátuheka, muna nzila ya khenda, kikesa kimosi kya mvula yi mvula yi kivuvu kimosi kya bukheti,
2TH 2:17 baluheka kikesa muna mbundu zenu, amana balusyamisa muna mihangu mya bukheti yi muna ndinga za bukheti.
2TH 3:1 Ku tsuka, baphangi, lombilenu kikuma kya betu, ndangu ndinga ya Pfumu yayalangana tswatsu amana bakumisaya bwosu yenina yawu kwena benu.
2TH 3:2 Amana ndangu twakutumuka ku moku ma bandwandwa yi batu ba mbi. Mukuma boosu beku yi lukwikilu.
2TH 3:3 Kaasi Pfumu kenina wa kusila mbundu. Kalúsyamisa amana kalúlema ku moku ma Mbi.
2TH 3:4 Twenina yi kikwamina mwena Pfumu kikuma kya benu ni lubati hanga amana lwahánga hika mana tubati lulomba mu kusala.
2TH 3:5 Yambula Pfumu katwadisa mbundu zenu ku lungongu lwa Nzambi yi ku kikwamina kina kisi hana Kidisitu.
2TH 3:6 Baphangi, tulusendini mu zina dya Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu: diyekulenu yi phangi wosu wuna wisi dyatila mu mvwalangani amana kisiku zitisa mikuku mina twábaheka.
2TH 3:7 Luzayini benu-benu abweti bufwanini mu kulanda mbandu ya betu. Mukuma tuzingidikiku mu luzingu lwa bamolu ha kati dya benu.
2TH 3:8 Tudikiku madya ma mutu mu phamba; kaasi, mu lombu yi kulembwa, tusadikini phipha yi mwini mukusya ni tuyekaminaku kwena mosi wa benu.
2TH 3:9 Heku ni tukadikiku yi muswa, kaasi tuzodikini ni twaluheka mbandu mosi ya kulanda mwena betu-betu.
2TH 3:10 Amana kikuma, ha tukadikini kwena benu, tuluhekikini mulongi wawu: «Honi mutu kazodiku kusala, kadyaku phi.»
2TH 3:11 Kinga tubati yuka ni bamosi hana kati dya benu babati dyatila mu mvwalangani, babatiku sala kima, amana kisalu kya bawu kaka bakotidilaka batu bahika.
2TH 3:12 Kwena batu babana tubati senda amana tubati baheka kikesa muna zina dya Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu: basalaka kisalu muna talala amana badya madya mana balúmbula muna kyusa kya bawu-meni.
2TH 3:13 Kikuma kya benu, baphangi, lulembwaku mu kuhangaka bukheti.
2TH 3:14 Ho ni mutu kalemvukiku ku mama tuzimbudini muna mukanda wawu, musimbululenu bukheti, amana lukalaku yandi hika keti mu kikhunda kimosi, ndangu tsoni zalenga mukwata.
2TH 3:15 Kaasi lumukitulaku hanga mbeni, kaasi mulwengisenu hanga phangi.
2TH 3:16 Yambula Pfumu wa ngemba kaluheka yandi-meni ngemba muna tangwa dyosu, mu mutindu wosu. Yambula Pfumu kakala yi benu boosu.
2TH 3:17 Meni-meni Pholu, tsonikini mboti yayi, dyadina koku dyama muna mikanda myama myosu. Yayina tsonikini yama.
2TH 3:18 Yambula khenda za Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu zakala yi benu boosu.
1TI 1:1 Pholu, thumwa wa Kidisitu Yesu mu kitumu kya Nzambi, Muhuludi wetu, yi Kidisitu Yesu, kivuvu kyetu.
1TI 1:2 Kwena Thimoti mwana wama wa kyedika mu lukwikilu: khenda, kheni yi ngemba bituki kwena Nzambi, Tata, yi kwena Kidisitu Yesu, Pfumu wetu.
1TI 1:3 Bwosu yíkuhekila kikesa ha yíkala ku Masetwani, ni wanangina ku Efesu ndangu wabakandisa batu babana babati longa malongi ma luvunu,
1TI 1:4 amana balandikilaku bingana-ngana keti ndonga ya butuka yakonda tsuka yina yisi nata tendu hana henina kisalu kya Nzambi, kina kibati salama mu lukwikilu.
1TI 1:5 Kisina kya kukebisa meni kuna, kyenina zola dina dyisi tuka ku mbundu ya kasemi, ku katsatsa ka kasemi yi lukwikilu lwakonda bukavungalosi.
1TI 1:6 Ndambu ya batu bahika bátota, amana báditotisa mu mameni ma phamba.
1TI 1:7 Bazodi bakituka balongi ba mitsiku kaasi bisiku bakisa mana bisi zonza, keti mambu mamana bisi tambwasa kya makulu.
1TI 1:8 Eeh, tuzayibwa ni mitsiku myenina mya bukheti, yuka ni twasadilamya mu mutindu wuna wulungini;
1TI 1:9 Tuzayibwa phi ni mitsiku myásalamaku kikuma kya mukwa masonga, kaasi kikuma kya bandwandwa yi bakolami, batu bambi yi basumuki, basafu yi bazangi, bahondi ba batata yi bahondi ba bamama, baba bisi honda batu,
1TI 1:10 bita-mbongi, bayakala bana bisi dinimbisa yi bakwawu bayakala, batu baba bisi sala kikhita kya bahika, bakwa bukamvi, batu baba bisiku zenga ndefi ya masonga yi mambu mahika mama misiku fwanana yi malongi ma kyedika,
1TI 1:11 malongi mafwanana yi Musamu wa Bukheti wa khembu ya Nzambi wa kyesi wuna kápheka meni Pholu.
1TI 1:12 Yimuvutwadi matondu lawu Kidisitu Yesu Pfumu wetu wuna wuphekini ngolu. Mukuma wámbona ni walunga yenina; yi hana katsidini mu kisalu,
1TI 1:13 meni yandu yikala musafula theti, kumunyokuna yi kumutukwana. Kaasi yandi wángyukila kheni, mudyambu yikalaku zaya mambu yikala sala, kukonda kwa lukwikilu.
1TI 1:14 Amana khenda za Pfumu wetu zábasa, hakimosi yi lukwikilu yi zola dina dyenina mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
1TI 1:15 Ndinga yayi yenina ya kyedika, bafweti tambwasaya: Kidisitu Yesu kísa ha tsi yayi kikuma kya kuhulula basumuki; muna kati dya bawu, meni yenina wa mbi kuhyoka boosu.
1TI 1:16 Kaasi kikuma kya bwabuna, muna sipha dya mbundu wángyukila kheni, ndangu mwena meni, yenina wa mbi kuluta boosu, kuna thwala batu balanda mbandu ya meni, bakwikila mwena Kidisitu Yesu, ndangu babonga moya wa mvula yi mvula.
1TI 1:17 Amana kwena Kyamvu wa mvula yi mvula, wuna wisiku fwa, wuna wisiku monika, Nzambi mosi, kabonga luzitu yi lukumu mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna!
1TI 1:18 Kima yikutumi ngeyi mwana wama Thimoti, kituma meni kina kifwanani yi mbikutulu zina batekila samuna kikuma kya ngeyi; ndangu ha walándilaza, wanwana muzingu wa bukheti,
