1TI 1:19 wasimbidilaka lukwikilu lwaku yi katsatsa ka kasemi, kakana bakonda yukila batu bahika amana bamani totisa lukwikilu lwa bawu.
1TI 1:20 Mukati dya bawu thwenina yi Kimeni yi Lekizandi; babana yíbalambula kedi kwa Satana ndangu bazaya ni ka mboti ku mu kulewulaka Nzambi.
1TI 2:1 Kima kya theti yiluhekidini kikesa, lwahanaka bizitu byenu, bilomba, lwabokwadilaka yi kuvutulaka matondu kikuma kya batu boosu,
1TI 2:2 kikuma kya bakyamvu yi kikuma kya boosu babana benina yi biyeka, ndangu twalenga kala yi luzingu lwa talala yi luzitu lwosu muna kuyekamina kwena Nzambi.
1TI 2:3 Bwabuna bwenina bukheti amana kisibwa tambwasa Nzambi, Muhuludi wetu,
1TI 2:4 wuna wisi zola ni batu boosu bahuluka amana balenga tula mu kuzaya kyedika.
1TI 2:5 Mukuma Nzambi mosi kenina, amana phi mukhundikisi mosi kenina hana kati dya Nzambi yi batu, mutu meni wuna kenina Kidisitu Yesu,
1TI 2:6 yandi wádihana yandi-meni hanga thuka kikuma kya batu boosu: kyakina kimbangi kyáhanama muna tangwa dya kyawu.
1TI 2:7 Kyakina bángyadikila meni, yikala mbambala, thumwa yi kiyeka kya kulonga, kwena babana bakondi kala Bayuta, lukwikilu yi kyedika. Nzonzibwa mu kyedika, phuniku.
1TI 2:8 Kikuma kya bwabuna, nzodi ni bayakala boosu balombilaka kosu homa, bathutaka ku zilu moku ma bawu ma kasemi, konda kukalaka yi khabu keti tendu.
1TI 2:9 Kitesu kimosi phi, bakhetu bavwataka mutindu wa bukheti, wa luzitu, konda kudizatisa; badihandaku tsuki, keti bilunga bya wolu yi misanga keti miledi mihiti thalu,
1TI 2:10 kaasi bavwata mihangu mya bukheti, bwosu buna bufwanini kwena bakhetu babana bisi monika ni bisi dihana kwena Nzambi.
1TI 2:11 Bakhetu bafweti yukaka malongi mu talala yi kulemvuka kwosu.
1TI 2:12 Phaniku muswa kwena bakhetu mu kulonga, ho loni kubonga kiyeka ku thwala ya bayakala; bafweti kala talala.
1TI 2:13 Kikuma, Atamu watheti batekila sala, Evwa ku manima nana.
1TI 2:14 Amana ka Atamu ku wáhunakana, kaasi mukhetu, yandi wáhunakana, wákolama ku mutsiku wa Nzambi.
1TI 2:15 Kaasi mukhetu kahúlukila muna bana babana kabúta, ho ni kakwamina muna lukwikilu, muna lungongu yi muna kuditomisa, ha kimosi yi kudikengaka.
1TI 3:1 Ndinga yayi yenina ya kyedika: Honi mutu kasola kukala mutwadisi, kisalu kya kitoku lawu kasodi.
1TI 3:2 Bulungi ni mutwadisi kakala konda kikalu, kafweti kala yakala wákwela mukhetu mosi, kisiku lutikisa kitesu, kadikengaka, kadizitisaka, kayambaka batu, kazaya kulonga,
1TI 3:3 kadihanaku mu kunwa malafu, kakalaku mukwa kingolu-ngolu; kaasi kakala mutu wa talala, mutu wa ngemba, kazolukaku mbongu;
1TI 3:4 katwadisaka bukheti nzu yandi amana bana bandi balemvukaka, mu luzitu lwosu.
1TI 3:5 Amana, honi mutu kisiku twadisa mboti batu benina muna nzu yandi, abweti kalenda twadisila Dibundu dya Nzambi?
1TI 3:6 Kakalaku mukidisitu wa pha; kondilo kaditsikisaka nana mu lulendu hanga ku tsuka kabonga nana ndola bwosu yina ya kiphidi-mutu.
1TI 3:7 Bulungini kakala yi kimbangi kya mboti kwena batu babana bakondi kala bakwikidi, ndangu bamulewulaku amana kabwa nana mu mutambu wa kiphidi-mutu.
1TI 3:8 Basyelu phi mutindu wumosi, bulungini bakalaka batu ba luzitu amana bakalaku batu ba ndinga zodi; balendaku dihanaka ku malafu ata kusosa miluta mya luvunu;
1TI 3:9 bafweti simbidila diswekamu dya lukwikilu muna katsatsa ka kasemi.
1TI 3:10 Babazyamina theti ku thwala ya kusala kisalu, yuka ni bakala batu bakonda kikalu.
1TI 3:11 Mutindu mosi phi, bakhetu bafweti kala bana bisi zitisa, konda mbonzi, bisiku hitikisa kitesu, batu bisi sila mbundu mu mambu moosu.
1TI 3:12 Basyelu bafweti kwela kaka mukhetu mosi amana batwadisaka bukheti bana ba bawu yi nzu ya bawu meni.
1TI 3:13 Mukuma basyelu babana básalakya bukheti kisalu bábazatisa yi kikumbwala kya lukwikilu kina kyenina mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
1TI 3:14 Yikusonikini mukanda wawu yi kivuvu ni ka thama ku, yikwísa kutala.
1TI 3:15 Kaasi honi yizyeta, wazáya khi bikalulu wakadiki byawu mu nzu ya Nzambi, yina yenina Dibundu dya Nzambi wa moyu, yina yenina kunzi amana disi zyamisa mambu ma kyedika.
1TI 3:16 Eeh, bulungi lwazayabwa, diswekamu ditadidini mambu ma kinzambi dyenina dya mbuta: Kidisitu, kisa monika mu lutu lwa kimutu, wádimonikisa mutu wa masonga muna nzila ya Kitembu Kyatoma, amana banzyo bámumona. Batu báyadingisa musamu wa Kidisitu ha kati dya babana bakondi kala Bayuta, bámukwikila kwena batu ba tsi, bámutombula mu khembu ya ku zilu.
1TI 4:1 Kinga Kitembu kazonzibwa wengele: muna matangwa ma tsuka, batu bahika batótisalwa lukwikilu ndangu benda dihana ku bitembu byabina byisi hukumuna yi ku malongi ma bitembu bya mbi,
1TI 4:2 muna mutindu wa kavungalosi ka babana bisi longa mambu ma bukamvi, katsatsa ka bawu meni kenina ka zina ku kisengu kina kisi bema yi mbawu ya kabengi.
1TI 4:3 Batu babana bisi longa ni batu bakwelaku amana bisi bwisa ni badyaku bima byabi kásala Nzambi, kinga Nzambi kásadilabya ndangu, babana benina bakwikidi, bazayi phi kyedika, badyakabya mu kuvutulaka matondu.
1TI 4:4 Kinga bima byosu kásala Nzambi byenina bya bukheti, amana kweku ata kima kimosi bafwani kulosa, yukani badyabya mu kuvutulaka matondu kwena Nzambi.
1TI 4:5 Kikuma byosu byenina byasambuka muna ndinga ya Nzambi yi muna lombilu.
1TI 4:6 Ho wabalongaka baphangi bakidisitu malongi mamana, wakála musadi wa bukheti wa Kidisitu Yesu; wuna wisi longuka ndinga za lukwikilu yi malongi ma bukheti mamana wisi bonga kedi mboti-mboti.
1TI 4:7 Kaasi wutambwasakaku phandi za phamba, mameni ma bambuta ba bakhetu mana matadidiku lukwikilu. Dihanaka theti mu mambu ma kinzambi.
1TI 4:8 Mukuma tsaka za lutu zenina bukheti mu mambu makonda mupfunu, kaasi mambu ma kinzambi menina mupfunu mu mambu moosu: menina yi bilangi bya luzingu, kikuma kya luzingu lwa buthwena yi bilumbu bya ku thwala.
1TI 4:9 Ndinga yayi yenina ya kyedika amana yafwana mu kutambwasa kwena boosu:
1TI 4:10 Kikuma, ho tubati diyangisa yi kunwanaka, mudyambu thwisi sya kivuvu kyetu mwena Nzambi wa moyu, wuna wenina Muhuludi wa batu boosu, batheti bakwikidi.
1TI 4:11 Tala mamana yikusendini mu kulongaka.
1TI 4:12 Ka mutu ku kalewula kingunza kyaku; kaasi ngeyi kala mbandu kwena bakwikidi, muna ndinga, muna khadidi, muna zola, muna lukwikilu yi muna kasemi.
1TI 4:13 Yikuna yikwisila, dihanaka mu kutangaka Masonuku ha mesu ma batu, mu kuhanaka kikesa yi mu kulongaka.
1TI 4:14 Wulewulaku kabu dina wátambula mu nzila ya khenda dina wenina dyawu, dina wábonga muna nzila ya mbikutulu, tangwa bákusya moku kwena kibuka kya bambuta.
1TI 4:15 Simbidila mambu mama, dihana mu kisalu kyaki ndangu babana babati kuyuka bamóna ni kosu kima wubati sala, ku thwala kibati kwenda.
1TI 4:16 Dikengaka ngeyi meni yi muna malongi maku; sikila mwamuna. Mukuma ha wasadiki bwabuna, wadíhulula ngeyi-meni hakimosi yi babana bisi kuyuka.
1TI 5:1 Wukayaku mununu mu khabu, kaasi muheka kikesa hanga mbedi ni tata waku. Basyamisa bangunza hanga baphangi,
1TI 5:2 binunu bya bakhetu hanga bamama, bandumba hanga baphangi ba bakhetu, yi kusema kwosu.
1TI 5:3 Basadisa mboti-mboti bafwidi ba mukwandi.
1TI 5:4 Ho mufwidi kakala yi bana kondilo yi batekulu, bulungi mboti bayandika kusongila bifu bya kinzambi muna kati kya nzu ya bawu amana babasadisaka binunu bya bawu; mukuma bwabuna kisi tambwasa Nzambi.
1TI 5:5 Mufwidi wa mukwandi, yandi wuna wásala yandi hika, wasya kivuvu kyandi mwena Nzambi; kisi kwamina phipha yi mwini muna bizitu byandi yi muna bisambu.
1TI 5:6 Kaasi mufwidi yandu wisi zingila mu tsambu, wafwa kedi mbatanana kisi monika ni moya kenina.
1TI 5:7 Tala mambu mama yikutumini mu kubasonikina, ndangu bakala konda kikalu.
1TI 5:8 Amana ho mutu wisiku sadisa biwutu byandi, theti-theti babana benina mu nzu yandi, wutunilwa lukwikilu, wa mbi lawu kuluta wuna wukondi kala mukwikidi.
1TI 5:9 Mufwidi, ku thwala ya kumusonikisa mu ndonga ya bafwidi, bulungi kakala yi mvula kuluta makumi sambanu, kakala phi mukhetu bákwela kwena yakala mosi;
1TI 5:10 kakala phi yi kimbangi kya mihangu mya bukheti: mutindu wuna kakala tsatsila mboti-mboti bana bandi, kakala yambila batu ku nzu, kakala sukwala bitambi bya batu ba Nzambi, kikuma kya bwabuna kakala yakidila batu babana bákala mu phasi yi mutindu wuna kakala dihanina mu kosu mihangu mya bukheti.
1TI 5:11 Kikuma kya bafwidi baba beku kedi bambuta, lubasonikisaku ku mukanda; kikuma ha bayuka hika tsambu ya kukwela, badihanaku kwena Kidisitu
1TI 5:12 amana dyakala ni babafundisa kikuma kya buna babebisini mutindu wa theti wa kudihana kwena Kidisitu.
1TI 5:13 Dikwawu phi, bwosu benina bamolu, basanda benda kangala mu nzu za lawu, bwosu batsúkinaku lwesi mu kukala bamolu, bazonziki lawu amana bakotiki kosu dyambu, bazonzaka ata mambu mana mafwaniku mu kuzonza.
1TI 5:14 Kikuma kya bwabuna, yizóla ni bangunza ba bafwidi bakwelaka, babuta bana, bakala batwadisi ba bukheti muna nzu za bawu; ndangu bamuheka nana nzila mbeni ya kwenda tuhuna musamu.
1TI 5:15 Mukuma kwenina yi bafwidi bahika baba batoti kedi mu kulanda Satana.
1TI 5:16 Ho mukwikidi mosi wa mukhetu kakala yi biwutu byandi bya bafwidi, kabasadisaka amana Dibundu dibongaku kiyeka, ndangu Dibundu kalenga sadisa lwesi baba benina kyedika bafwidi.
1TI 5:17 Kwena bambuta ba Dibundu bana bisi twadisa bukheti, bulungi babahekaka luzitu mbala zodi, kuluta lawu babana bisi dihana lawu mu Ndinga ya Nzambi yi mu kulonga.
1TI 5:18 Kikuma Masonuku mazonzini: «Wamukasaku munwa ngombi tangwa kabati nika ngenza», amana: «Bulungi musadi kabonga lufutu lwandi.»
1TI 5:19 Wutambwasaku mutu mosi kisa funda mbuta, akolu ni bakala bambangi bodi kondilo batatu.
1TI 5:20 Batu baba basadi masumu, bakaya ku thwala ya batu boosu, ndangu batu bahika bayukaka bweya.
1TI 5:21 Yikusikidikisi ku thwala ya Nzambi, ku thwala ya Kidisitu Yesu yi ku thwala ya banzyo babana básolama, mu kusadila mikuku myami buna bufwani konda kusola mbunzu za batu.
1TI 5:22 Wutsutsaku mu kusya mutu moku. Kalaku mu kithwadi yi mutu wuna wusadi masumu; kala wa kasemi ngeyi-meni.
1TI 5:23 Wunwakaku lwesi mamba; sadilaka phi koma ka vinu, kikuma kya mukati yi buna wisi kuyangisa.
1TI 5:24 Masumu ma batu bahika mazayakani wengele amana misi tekidila mu pfundusu; kwena batu bahika misi landa ku manima.
1TI 5:25 Mutindu mosi, mihangu mya bukheti myisi zayakana: ata myami mya mbi, mina tubatiku mona buthwena, myalendaku swamana.
1TI 6:1 Batu baba benina mu kizitu kya kihika bulungi mboti babazitisaka bapfumu ba bawu, ndangu balewasaku zina dya Nzambi yi malongi mama balonga.
1TI 6:2 Ho bawu bakala yi bapfumu ba bakwikidi, bafwaniku ni babakondaka luzitu mu mvunga ni benina baphangi ba bawu. Kaasi bafweti basadila kuluta, kikuma benina bakwikidi yi biwutu bya bawu bya kutya bisi sadila. Tala mambu mama wufweti longa yi kutuma.
1TI 6:3 Ho mutu kamwangaka malongi mahika konda kulandaka malongi ma kyedika ma Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu yi malongi mana ma kinzambi,
1TI 6:4 kenina mutu wabasa yi lulendu, kazayiku kima; kimbefu kyandi kya kunanama yi ngyuma zitadidi mihowu. Kwakuna kwisi butuka kiphala, matendu, kutukwana, kubongilaka bakwenu mabanza ma mbi,
1TI 6:5 kutendana kwa konda tsuka kwa batu babana benina yi mayedi mazangana, makonda kyedika, bawu bisi dila mu mvunga za kinzambi.
1TI 6:6 Kinga, kinzambi kyenina yi muluta wa lawu, ho wasangwalaka mu kina wenina kyawu.
1TI 6:7 Kikuma, thwisaku yi kima mu tsi, amana twalendaku nata phi keti kima.
1TI 6:8 Muna bwabuna, ho twakala yi madya yi miledi, byabina byatúfwana kwetu.
1TI 6:9 Kaasi batu babana bisi sanda bakituka bamvwama bisi bwa mu kimeka, mu mutambu yi mu tsatu za lawu za buzoba yi za phasi, zisi banata mu kuzangana yi mu lufwa.
1TI 6:10 Mukuma zola dya mbongu dyenina kisina kya mbi zoosu, amana batu bahika bádihana mwamuna, báditotisa kyana yi lukwikilu amana bádinyokuna bawu meni.
1TI 6:11 Kaasi ngeyi, mutu wa Nzambi, hangakaku mambu ma buna. Sandaka masonga, kinzambi, lukwikilu, zola, sipha dya mbundu, lembami.
1TI 6:12 Nwana muzingu wa bukheti wa lukwikilu, simbidila moya wa mvula yi mvula, wuna bákutedila yi kikuma kya bwabuna wátambwasila dyambu ku thwala ya bambangi balawu.
1TI 6:13 Yikuhekini muswa ku thwala ya Nzambi, wuna wisi hulula moya kwena bihangwa byosu yi ku thwala ya Yesu Kidisitu, wuna wáhana kimbangi mu kutambwasa dyambu ku thwala ya Phosi Philatu,
1TI 6:14 mu kusimbidilaka mikuku konda kifu, konda kikalu, tii yikuna kakwisa monikina Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu.
1TI 6:15 Kumonika kwakuna kwa Pfumu wetu kwasálama muna tangwa dina kásila Nzambi wa kyesi yi Pfumu lwesi, Kyamvu wa bakyamvu yi Pfumu wa bapfumu.
1TI 6:16 Yandi wuna lwesi wisiku fwa, mwena yandi mwenina yi mwini wumosi bisiku tala; keti mutu khaniku kamonawa amana kalendawoku mona; kwena Yandi, lukumu yi ngolu zilutini za mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna!
1TI 6:17 Senda kwena baba benina yi bimvwama mu tsi yayi ni bakalaku yi lulendu amana basyaku kivuvu mu bimvwama byakonda kwatakani; kaasi kivuvu kya bawu kyakala mwena Nzambi wuna wisi tuheka byosu bya lawu, ndangu byatuhekaka kyesi.
1TI 6:18 Basenda ni basalaka mambu mamboti, bakalaka bamvwama muna mihangu mya bukheti, bakalaka yi kyesi kya kukabila batu bahika.
1TI 6:19 Balumbikaka bwabuna kimvwama kya bukheti yi kya ngolu kikuma kya tangwa dina dyakwísa, ndangu babonga moya wa kyedika.
1TI 6:20 Muzitu Thimoti, batika bukheti kima kina bákuheka. Wunanamakaku mu phandi za phamba yi za masafu yi phaka za luvunu, zina bisi mona hangambedi ni mazaya.
1TI 6:21 Kikuma, batu bahika, bwosu bázola mu kulanda mazaya meni mamana, bátotisa nzila ya bawu ya lukwikilu. Khenda zakala kwena benu!
2TI 1:1 Meni Pholu, thumwa wa Kidisitu Yesu muna luzolu lwa Nzambi, wuna wápheka kiyeka kya kusamuna moya wuna bátusila kilangi mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
2TI 1:2 Kwena Thimoti, mwana wama watondama: Khenda, kheni yi ngemba kwena Nzambi, Tata, yi kwena Kidisitu Yesu, Pfumu wetu!
2TI 1:3 Mvutudi matondu lawu kwena Nzambi wuna yisi sambila yi katsatsa ka kasemi, bwosu bákala bakhaka bama. Amana phipha, mwini yisiku lembwa mu kulusyaka mu bisambu.
2TI 1:4 Ngyubukini matsanga maku, tsambu ya lawu phi yenina yawu ni yikumona tswatsu, ndangu yibasa mu kyesi.
2TI 1:5 Ngyubukini phi lukwikilu lwa masonga luna wenina lwawu; hanga luna kákala lwawu khaka waku wa mukhetu Loyisi, yi luna lwa ngudi waku Winisi, yenina yi kikumbwala ni wenina lwawu phi ngeyi.
2TI 1:6 Kikuma kya bwabuna, yikubambukisini: tokamisa kabu dya Nzambi dina wábonga ha yikusya moku.
2TI 1:7 Kikuma, Kitembu yandu katuhekini Nzambi kisiku tunatina bweya; kaasi kisi tuheka ngolu, zola yi kudikengila.
2TI 1:8 Wuyukaku tsoni mu kuta kimbangi kya Pfumu wetu, keti kya meni, mutu wandi wa boloku. Kaasi mona phasi hakimosi yi meni kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti, muna ngolu zoosu zina kátuheka Nzambi.
2TI 1:9 Yandi Nzambi wátuhulula amana wátutela mu mbila yatoma, ka kikuma kya mihangu myetu ku, kaasi muna kulanda mabanza mandi mana kádiyidikila kedi, mu khenda zina kátuheka mwena Kidisitu Yesu tuka luyanduku lwa matangwa mamana misiku hwa.
2TI 1:10 Khenda zazi katusongidiza buthwena muna kudimonikisa kwa Muhuludi wetu, Kidisitu Yesu. Yandi wuna wisa zilula ngolu za lufwa amana wumonikisini moya wa mvula yi mvula muna nzila ya Musamu wa Bukheti.
2TI 1:11 Kikuma kya Musamu meni wawu wa Bukheti, meni, bátsikununa yikala mbambala, thumwa yi mulongi.
2TI 1:12 Kikuma kya bwabuna yisi dikumbidila mu phasi zazi; yisibwoku yukila tsoni, mukuma nzayi mwena nani yísila lukwikilu lwama, amana yenina yi kikumbwala ni yanduna kenina yi hamu dya kukeba kina bápheka yi kuna kilumbu meni kyakina.
2TI 1:13 Simbidila, muna lukwikilu yi muna zola dina dyenina mwena Kidisitu Yesu, mbandu ya ndinga zina za bukheti wáyuka kwena meni.
2TI 1:14 Sweka ndinga zoosu za bukheti zina bákuheka mu nzila ya Kitembu Kyatoma wuna wisi zingila mwena betu.
2TI 1:15 Wuzayibwa ni batu boosu ba ku Aziya basala nzukula, mu kati dya batu babana benina Fizyedi yi Edimozyeni.
2TI 1:16 Pfumu káhana khenda zandi muna nzu ya Onezifodi, mukuma kisi pheka kikesa amana káyukaku tsoni za miyololu mya meni;
2TI 1:17 kaasi buna kisa ku Loma, wasya ngolu mu kwenda tsanda amana wámbona.
2TI 1:18 Yambula Pfumu kamusadisa kalenga bonga khenda kwena Nzambi muna kilumbu meni kyakina. Ngeyi meni wuzayi mboti bisalu byosu katsadidi ku Efesu.
2TI 2:1 Kwena ngeyi, mwana wama, kala yi ngolu mu khenda zina zenina mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
2TI 2:2 Amana mamana wángyuka mu kulonga mu mesu ma bambangi balawu, wahanama kwena batu babana bisi sila mbundu, babana benina yi khwakasu ya kulonga phi batu bahika.
2TI 2:3 Nyokuka ngeyi phi, hanga phumbulu wakyedika wa Kidisitu Yesu.
2TI 2:4 Phumbulu wuna wubati yilama kenda ku mvita, kakwendaku sanda kasala mambu ma luzingu, ho kazola ni kamuzatisa pfumu wandi wuna wámukotisa mu kisalu.
2TI 2:5 Amana mutu wuna wisi sala tsaka za kutina thinu, wuna wisiku landa mikuku, kalendaku nunga ho kisiku sadila buna milombini mikuku.
2TI 2:6 Musadi wa bilanga wuna wisi dihana mu kisalu, kafweti kala watheti mu kubonga mbutu yandi.
2TI 2:7 Simbidila mambu mbati kuzimbwala: Pfumu kakúheka ngangu muna mambu moosu.
2TI 2:8 Mubambuka Yesu Kidisitu, mwana wátuka mu khuna ya Tavidi yandu wáfutumuka ku bafwa bwosu wisi longa Musamu wa Bukheti.
2TI 2:9 Kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti meni wawu mbati nyokukina amana batsini mu miyololu hanga mutu wa mbi. Kaasi Ndinga ya Nzambi bakasayoku keti koma!
2TI 2:10 Mukuma kya bwabuna yisi tambwasila phasi zoosu kikuma kya babana kásola Nzambi, ndangu bawu phi babonga luhulusu mwena Kidisitu Yesu, ha kimosi yi khembu ya mvula yi mvula.
2TI 2:11 Ndinga yayi yenina ya kyedika: «Ho twáfwa hakimosi yi yandi, twazínga phi hakimosi yi yandi;
2TI 2:12 ho twakanga mbundu, twayála phi hakimosi yi yandi; ho twamutuna, yandi phi katútuna;
2TI 2:13 ho thweku yi kwikama, yandi kasála wa kwikama, mukuma kaditunaku yandi meni.»
2TI 2:14 Tala mana wabámbukisa boosu amana bakebisa ku thwala ya Nzambi kikuma kya mambu ma ngyuma zina zitadidi mihowu. Ngyuma zina zisiku sadisa keti koma, kaasi zisi bebisa batu bana bisiza yuka.
2TI 2:15 Sya ngolu balenga kutambwasa ku mesu ma Nzambi, hanga musadi wuna wisiku bengisa mesu mu kisalu kyandi amana walongaka, buna bufwani, ndinga ya kyedika.
2TI 2:16 Bwisa phandi za phamba zakonda kala mu kinzambi, mukuma babana bisi dihanamwa bisi yekuka lawu mu kinzambi.
2TI 2:17 Malongi ma bawu menina hanga phuta yavunda yisi wumuna misuni. Bwabuna benina Kimeni yi Fileti:
2TI 2:18 Bayekukini mu nzila ya kyedika amana baningisini lukwikilu lwa batu mu kusamuna ni lufutumuku lwásalama kedi.
2TI 2:19 Kinga mipfundila mya ngolu mina kasya Nzambi myazyama myenina: Ndinga zazi zanama mwamuna: «Pfumu wubazayi batu bandi», amana «kosu mutu wuna watela zina dya Pfumu kafweti bwisa mu kusala mbi.»
2TI 2:20 Muna kati dya nzu ya mbuta, mweku lwesi malonga ma wolu yi ma manzanza; ma mutuma yi ma phophu za miti phi menina. Mamana ma theti yimamana bisi yambila batu ba luzitu, mana mahika kikuma kya kusadilaka bilumbu byosu.
2TI 2:21 Ho mutu kadisemisaka muna mambu mamana yilusamwani, kakála nzungu zina bisi yambila batu ba luzitu, wa kutambika, mupfunu kwena pfumu wandi, kalenda sala kosu kisalu kya mboti.
2TI 2:22 Tinaka tsambu za mbi za kingunza, sandaka masonga, lukwikilu, zola, ngemba, hakimosi yi babana bisi mutela Pfumu yi mbundu ya kasemi.
2TI 2:23 Kaasi bwisaka phaka za phamba yi za buzoba, wazayaka ni zazina zisi buta ngyuma.
2TI 2:24 Kinga bweku bukheti musadi wa Pfumu kayumanaka, kaasi kazolaka batu boosu, kakala mutu walunga mu kulonga amana katambwasaka batu babana bisi mutanga mambu;
2TI 2:25 kafweti balongaka mu malembi batu babana bisi mutendisa, bwalenda kala ni Nzambi kabaheka tangwa dya kusoba mabanza ma bawu amana bazaya kyedika.
2TI 2:26 Balénda dibakisa amana balubuki mu mitambu mya kiphidi-mutu, wuna wábakwata ndangu basalaka luzolu lwa yandi.
2TI 3:1 Wazayabwa mboti: muna matangwa ma tsuka, bilumbu bya phasi byakála.
2TI 3:2 Mukuma, batu bakála yi bwimi, nzoluka ya mbongu, bakwa mitsiki yi bakwa lulendu; bamúsafula Nzambi, balémvukilaku bibuti bya bawu, bakálaku kabanzi amana bakálaku yi luzitu ku mambu matoma;
2TI 3:3 bakála yi mbundu ya zititi, konda kyadi, kukumbaka batu, bakonda kwatakani, bakwa kingolu-ngolu amana bambeni ba mamboti;
2TI 3:4 balámbula bakwawu, batu ba mbundu ya khufi amana lulendu lwabákitula baphofu; bazákama yi tsambu za lutu kuluta Nzambi;
2TI 3:5 bahúnikisa ni benina yi kinzambi, kaasi batúnaza ngolu za kinzambi meni kina. Bafila kunda batu ba mutindu wuna!
2TI 3:6 Mukuma, ha kati dya batu babana, bahika bisi kota mu nzu yi kuhunaka bakhetu, benina yi bizitu bya masumu, muna mitambu mya bawu; bakhetu babana benina yi tsambu za mambu ma mbi ma mutindu yi mutindu;
2TI 3:7 bisi sanda balongukaka kosu tangwa, kaasi bisiku lenda kuzaya kyedika.
2TI 3:8 Bwosu buna phi Yanesi yi Yambelesi bátendana yi Moyize, mutindu mosi phi batu baba babati tendana ku kyedika. Benina batu ba mayedi mazangana yi lukwikilu lwa phamba.
2TI 3:9 Kaasi bakwéndaku kyana kya lawu, mukuma batu boosu babátungulula buzoba bwa bawu, bwosu bwákala bwa Yanesi yi Yambelesi.
2TI 3:10 Kaasi ngeyi wulandiki mboti malongi mama, khadidi, mabanza ma kisalu, lukwikilu, sipha dya mbundu, zola, kikwamina,
2TI 3:11 minyanga yi phasi zazi yímona ku Atyosi, ku Kikonyumi, ku Disiti. Khi minyanga ndatiku! Kaasi muna moosu, Pfumu wákhutumuna.
2TI 3:12 Amana batu boosu bisi sanda kuzingilaka mu kinzambi mwena Kidisitu Yesu banyókuka.
2TI 3:13 Kaasi batu ba mbi yi bakwa bikwaki balánda hika mu kusala mbi, bahúna batu bahika amana babáhuna bawu meni.
2TI 3:14 Kaasi kwena ngeyi, kwamina muna mambu mana wálonguka yi mana wákwikila yi mbundu yosu. Wuzayi kwena nani wálongukama.
2TI 3:15 Amana tuka kimwana kyaku, wuzayima Masonuku Matoma; malenda kuheka mudimu wuna wakúnata ku phulusu muna lukwikilu mwena Kidisitu Yesu.
2TI 3:16 Masonuku moosu másonama mu ngolu za Nzambi, amana menina mupfunu mu kulonga, kubwisa bifu, mu kusungika mbi, mu kulonga mu masonga,
2TI 3:17 ndangu mutu wa Nzambi kalenga kala wayilama buna bulungini amana kakala walunga mu kusala kosu kisalu kya bukheti.
2TI 4:1 Yikusikidikisi ku thwala ya Nzambi yi ku thwala ya Kidisitu Yesu, wuna wabáfundisa batu ba moyu yi bamvumbi, yikulombibwa muna zina dya kudimonikisa kwa Kidisitu yi Kipfumu kyandi:
2TI 4:2 samuna Ndinga ya Nzambi, ata muna tangwa dya bukheti keti dya kakalakanu; bakwikisa, bakaya ho loni baheka kikesa, wabalongaka yi sipha dya mbundu dyosu.
2TI 4:3 Mukuma, tangwa dibati kwisa batu bazólaku kuyuka malongi ma kyedika, kaasi balánda tsambu za lutu lwa bawu amana badíhana kwena balongi ba lawu babásamwana mana bisi zola kuyuka.
2TI 4:4 Bapháta matu ma bawu ndangu bayukaku kyedika, bahúkumuka ku bingana-ngana.
2TI 4:5 Kaasi ngeyi, dikenga mu mambu moosu, tambwasa munyanga, mwangisa Musamu wa Bukheti, lungisa buna bufwanini kisalu kyaku.
2TI 4:6 Kwena meni, beka zola ni bandambula kimenga amana tangwa dyama dya kusisa tsi dilungi.
2TI 4:7 Ndwaniki muzingu wa bukheti, thudini ku tsuka ya thinu, tsimbididilwa lukwikilu.
2TI 4:8 Amana buthwena, mukhonzi wa masonga bátswekilawa: Pfumu, zusi wa masonga, kaphékawa kilumbu meni kyakina, amana ka kwena meni ku lwesi, kaasi yi kwena babana boosu bisi zola kudimonikisa kwandi.
2TI 4:9 Sya ngolu wisa ngwana tswatsu.
2TI 4:10 Kikuma Temasi wáthina, mudyambu dya lungongu lwa mambu ma buthwena ma tsi yayi; wendi ku Tesalonika; Khelesasi kakwénda ku Ngalatiya, amana Titi kakwénda ku Talamati.
2TI 4:11 Luka lwesi yenina yandi. Munata Malaku amana wisa yandi, mukuma mupfunu wa lawu yenina yandi kikuma kya kisalu.
2TI 4:12 Yimutumikini Tisiki ku Efesu.
2TI 4:13 Ha wakwísa, wandatina kazaka kana tsitsiki ku Tholowasi kwena Kadiphusu; amana wandatina phi mikanda, theti-theti mikanda mina báyidikila yi mikanda mya bambisi.
2TI 4:14 Lekizandi wuna wenina mbembu, mbi ya lawu káphanga; Pfumu kamuvutwala bwosu bwenina mihangu myandi.
2TI 4:15 Dikenga kwena yandi, ngeyi phi, mukuma kázolazoku keti koma ndinga zetu.
2TI 4:16 Tangwa yísamba mbala ya theti ha bápfunda, yímonaku mutu wátsadisa: batu boosu bándosila. Yambula Nzambi kabatangilamoku!
2TI 4:17 Kaasi Pfumu wángyakidila amana wápheka ngolu zilutini, ndangu, muna nzila ya meni, Musamu wa Buketi basamunawa buna bufwani amana baba bakondi kala Bayuta boosu bayukawa. Amana wáphulula ku munwa wa thambu.
2TI 4:18 Pfumu kaphúlula hika ku kosu kisalu kya mbi amana kakhótisa konda kifu muna Kipfumu kyandi kya mazilu. Khembu yakala kwena yandi mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna!
2TI 4:19 Muheka mboti Phisikila yi Akilasi, yi nzu ya Onezifodi.
2TI 4:20 Elasiti wusadiki ku Khoditu, amana yimusisikini Thofimi wabela kuna Mile.
2TI 4:21 Sya ngolu wisa buna khaniku kedi disa tangwa dya kyosi kya ngolu. Ebulusu, Phundesi, Dinusi, Koloti yi baphangi boosu mboti bakuhekini.
2TI 4:22 Pfumu kakala yi kitembu kya ngeyi. Khenda za Nzambi zakala yi benu!
TIT 1:1 Pholu, musadi wa Nzambi, thumwa wa Yesu Kidisitu. Yítambula kiyeka kya kunatisa ku lukwikilu babana kásola Nzambi yi kubazayikisa kyedika bwosu lwenina kyenina kinzambi kya bakidisitu,
TIT 1:2 ndangu babonga kivuvu kya luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula. Nzambi, bwosu kisiku huna, yandi wátusila luzingu meni lwaluna ku thwala ya matangwa moosu;
TIT 1:3 amana buna dyálungila tangwa dina kásila, wásongila Ndinga yandi muna musamu wawuna báhana kwena meni yi wawuna yisi longa muna muswa wa Nzambi, Muhuludi wetu.
TIT 1:4 Kwena Titi mwana wama wa kyedika bwosu lwenina lukwikilu lwetu lwa mu kimvuka. Yambula Nzambi Tata yi Kidisitu Yesu Muhuludi wetu baluheka khenda yi ngemba.
TIT 1:5 Kima yíkusisila ku Kheleti, ndangu wámeka kusya mu ndonga mambu mahika mana masadi mu kuyidika amana wasikununa bambuta muna kosu mbanza, bwosu buna yikulongikila meni-meni.
TIT 1:6 Mbuta kafweti kala mutu wakonda kifu, yakala dya mukhetu mosi, wenina yi bana ba bakwikidi bana bakonda kedi funda mu mambu matadidini kisaka-saka keti kukonda kulemvuka.
TIT 1:7 Kikuma, bulungi ni mutwadisi kakala wakonda kifu, kikuma yandi báheka kiyeka kya mambu ma Nzambi, kaditsikisakaku, kakalaku mukwa khabu, kakalaku kinwa malafu, kakalaku lwasa, kasandakaku lufutu mu nzila za mbi.
TIT 1:8 Kaasi kakala mutu wisi yamba batu, wisi zola mamboti. Kakala mutu wa mabanza ma mboti, mutu wa masonga, watoma, mutu wa kukanga mbundu.
TIT 1:9 Kakala mutu wádihana ku Ndinga ya lukwikilu, kisiya sadila phi bwosu buna bálongilaya. Muna bwabuna kakadila yi hamu dya kuhana kikesa muna dilongi dya kyedika amana kalénda songila kifu kya bawu kwena babana babati mutendisa.
TIT 1:10 Kikuma, balawu benina, kuluta hana kati dya bakidisitu babana ba Bayuta, benina bakolami amana bisi zonza mambu makonda mupfunu yi kuhunaka bakwenu.
TIT 1:11 Bulungi kubakangisa munwa. Mukuma nzu za muthu bisi vwadingisa, mu kulongaka mambu mana mafwaniku mu kulonga, kikuma kya lufutu lwa mu nzila za mbi.
TIT 1:12 Mosi hana kati dya bawu, mbikudi, kázimbula: «Bakheleti benina kosu tangwa bahunya misamu, bambisi ba nganzi, babolu bana bisi zola lwesi kudya.»
TIT 1:13 Kimbangi kyaki kyenina kya kyedika. Yihana ni baheka phi bikalu bya ngolu, ndangu bakala ba kasemi mu lukwikilu,
TIT 1:14 amana bayekaminaku hika ku mikhenda mya Bayuta yi ku mikuku mya batu mina misiku landa nzila ya kyedika.
TIT 1:15 Byosu byenina bya kasemi kikuma kya batu babana benina ba kasemi; kaasi heku kima kyenina kya kasemi kikuma kya babana básumuka amana bakonda lukwikilu: ngangu za bawu yi katsasa ka bawu byenina bya mvindu.
TIT 1:16 Bisi tambwasa ni bamuzayini Nzambi, kaasi bisi musuwangana muna mihangu mya bawu. Batu ba nzanzi, bisiku lemvuka amana bisiku lenda kuhanga keti kima kimosi kya bukheti.
TIT 2:1 Kaasi kwena ngeyi, zonza lwesi mambu mana mafwanani yi malongi ma masonga.
TIT 2:2 Zimbula kwena binunu bya bayakala ni bakalaku batu ba kulutisaka kitesu, bawu benina batu ba kuzitisa, benina batu bana bazayini kudibatila mboti-mboti, benina ba kasemi muna lukwikilu, muna zola yi muna kwikama.
TIT 2:3 Phila mosi phi yi kwena binunu bya bakhetu, bakala yi bikalulu bina bilungidini mu kikuma kya bakwikidi; bakalaku batu bisi kwenda mu kukumbaka bakwawu, bakalaku phi bahika ba malafu. Kaasi balongaka mambu ma mboti;
TIT 2:4 ndangu balongaka kwena bandumba ba bangudi mu kuzolaka bayakala ba bawu yi bana ba bawu,
TIT 2:5 bazayaka mu kuditanina mboti-mboti, bakala ba kasemi, badihana mu kusala bisalu bya mu nzu, bakala batu ba mboti, amana balemvukaka kwena bayakala ba bawu, ndangu Ndinga ya Nzambi balewulayoku.
TIT 2:6 Phila mosi phi kwena ngeyi, balongaka masanda ni bazaya kudilunda mboti-mboti
TIT 2:7 mu mambu moosu. Ngeyi meni wakalaka mbandu ya mihangu mya bukheti. Amana malongi maku makala ma kasemi yi mana mabati nata luzitu.
TIT 2:8 Ndinga zaku zakala za masonga, zina balendaku lewula kwena batu, ndangu mutendi kayuka tsoni, kikuma kamónaku dyambu dimosi dya mbi dina kazónza kikuma kya betu.
TIT 2:9 Balonga bahika ni bazitisaka bapfumu ba bawu mu mambu moosu, babasephidisaka, babalumunakaku ndinga za bapfumu ba bawu,
TIT 2:10 babayibakaku keti kima. Kaasi badisongilaka kosu tangwa ni benina batu ba kusila mbundu, kikuma kya kuhana lukumu ku malongi ma Nzambi, Muhuludi wetu.
TIT 2:11 Mukuma, Nzambi wásongila kedi khenda zandi hanga tho ya luhulusu lwa batu boosu.
TIT 2:12 Khenda meni zina zibati tulonga ni twabwisa khadidi ya mbi, twabwisa phi nzoluka za tsi yayi; amana muna tangwa dyadi, twakala batu babana bazayi kudilunda mboti-mboti, batu basungama, yi batu babana bisi zingila mu kinzambi.
TIT 2:13 Bwabuna bufwani kithamina kina tubati hingidila mamboti mana thwisi sila kivuvu, yi kumonika kwa khembu ya Nzambi wa mbuta yi Muhuludi Yesu Kidisitu.
TIT 2:14 Wádilambula yandi-meni kikuma kya betu, ndangu katukula ku mbi yosu amana katukitula kanda dya kasemi, dina dyenina kikuma kya yandi-meni, babana benina babasa yi tsambu ya lawu mu kusala mihangu mya bukheti.
TIT 2:15 Tala mana wufwani mu kulonga, kuhana kikesa kwena bana babati kuhinikina kondilo kubasongisa yi lawu dya hamu. Ka mutu ku kakulewula.
TIT 3:1 Bayubulula bakwikidi ni bafweti bayukila batwadisi yi bapfumu ba luyalu, bafweti balemvukila, amana bakalaka bayilama mu kuhangaka moosu ma bukheti.
TIT 3:2 Balewulaku mutu, kaasi bakalaka batu ba talala yi buweti, amana basongilaka kosu tangwa lembami dya bawu kwena batu boosu.
TIT 3:3 Mukuma, betu phi, twákala theti hanga biyungu, bakolami, twakalaku mu nzila. Twákala bahika ba byesi yi tsambu za mutindu yi mutindu. Twakala zingila mu bundwandwa yi nzoluka. Twakalaku dihekisa luzitu, amana twakala dimenga betu yi betu.
TIT 3:4 Kaasi tangwa kásongila Nzambi Muhuludi wetu buweti bwandi yi lungongu lwandi kikuma kya batu,
TIT 3:5 wátuhulula, heku ni kikuma kya buna twáhanga mihangu mya masonga, kaasi kikuma kya kheni yina kátuyukila. Wátuhulula, wátuheka lubutuku lwa pha. Amana muna nzila ya Kitembu Kyatoma, wátuheka luzingu lwa pha.
TIT 3:6 Mukuma Nzambi wátufwebwala Kitembu Kyatoma hana thandu ya betu, muna nzila ya Yesu Kidisitu Muhuludi wetu;
TIT 3:7 ndangu, muna khenda zandi, kisi tukitula batu ba masonga ku mesu ma Nzambi, amana wátuheka muswa wa kubonga luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula luna thwisi sila kivuvu.
TIT 3:8 Ndinga yina yenina ya kyedika. Nzodi ni wazonzaya yi nziki-nziki, ndangu babana bisi kwikila mwena Nzambi badihana mu kuhangaka hika lawu mihangu mya bukheti. Tala mana menina mboti yi mupfunu kikuma kya batu.
TIT 3:9 Kaasi tina matendu ma buzoba, mambu mana matadidi ndonga ya butuka, ngyuma yi mathata mana matadidi mitsiku: meku mupfunu amana ma phamba.
TIT 3:10 Mutu wuna wisi kotisa ngyengu, muyekula mu Dibundu, ku nima dya kukebisa kwa theti yi kwa zodi.
TIT 3:11 Kikuma, wuzayi ni mutu wa mutindu wawuna wuditotisi kedi, kabati landa kusumuka; amana ndola kabati dizengila yandi-meni.
TIT 3:12 Tangwa yikútumina Aditemasi ho loni Tisiki, sanda phila ndangu wisila kwena meni kuna Nikophodisi, mukuma kwakuna nzengikini kunangina mu kuhitisa tangwa dya kyosi kya lawu.
TIT 3:13 Hanga bwosu bulungi mu kusala kikuma kya kubasadisila mulongi wa mitsiku Zenasi yi Apholosi, mu kitambu kya bawu, yidika ndangu bakondaku keti kima.
TIT 3:14 Bulungi phi baphangi betu bakwikidi balonguka mu kusala mihangu mya bukheti, ndangu balunga mu kusadisa batu babana benina yi mupfunu wa lusadisu. Amana banataku luzingu lwa phamba.
TIT 3:15 Boosu babana benina hakimosi yi meni mboti bakuhitikini. Baheka mboti babana bisi tuzola mu lukwikilu. Yambula khenda za Nzambi zakala kwena benu boosu.
PHM 1:1 Yandu meni Pholu, bákotisa mu boloku kikuma kya Kidisitu Yesu yi phangi Thimoti. Kwena ngeyi Fidimoni, watondama yi musindikidi wetu wa kisalu,
PHM 1:2 yi kwena Aphiya, phangi wetu wa mukhetu, kwena Adisiphi, musindikidi wetu wa mizingu, yi kwena Dibundu dina dyisi khundakana muna nzu yaku:
PHM 1:3 Yambula Nzambi Tata wetu yi Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu baluheka khenda yi ngemba.
PHM 1:4 Mbala zoosu zina yisi vutula matondu kwena Nzambi wama, yisi tumbula zina dyaku Fidimoni muna bisambu byama.
PHM 1:5 Mukuma yisi yuka khululuka ya lungongu lwaku kikuma kya bakwikidi boosu yi lukwikilu lwaku kwena Pfumu Yesu.
PHM 1:6 Yisi lomba kwena Nzambi ni lukwikilu luna wenina lwawu mu kithwadi yi betu, lwakala ngolu mwena ngeyi ndangu lwasongila mamboti mana tufwani mu kulungisa kikuma kya Kidisitu.
PHM 1:7 Kikuma, zola dyaku, phangi, dipheki kyesi kya lawu yi kikesa, mukuma wusyamisini mbundu ya bakwikidi.
PHM 1:8 Yihana ni, mbatanana yenina yi muswa mu kithwadi yi Kidisitu mu kukusenda mana wulungini mu kuhanga,
PHM 1:9 kaasi nzodi yikulomba kima kimosi muna zina dya lungongu. Bwosu yekina, meni Pholu, kinunu, amana phi buthwena mu boloku yenina kikuma kya Kidisitu Yesu,
PHM 1:10 mbati kulomba lusadisu kikuma kya Mwana wama Onezimi. Yandi Kenina mwana wama wuna mbutidini muna boloku.
PHM 1:11 Theti, kákalaku mupfunu kwena ngeyi, kaasi buthwena bwabu, mupfunu katuyekina kwena ngeyi yi meni.
PHM 1:12 Buthwena, yikuvutwadi yandi, yandi wenina hanga ndambu ya meni meni.
PHM 1:13 Yizodi ni kakala bela-bela yi meni ndangu katsadisaka ha kifulu kya ngeyi, muna tangwa dyadi yenina mu boloku kikuma kya Musamu wa Bukheti.
PHM 1:14 Kaasi nzodikiku ni yihanga kima konda wapheka nzila, ndangu wuhangaku mambu mu kingolu-ngolu kaasi yi mbundu ya bukheti.
PHM 1:15 Ngatu Onezimi káyekukila kwena ngeyi kikuma kya tangwa dya khunda, ndangu kakuvutwakila kyamakulu,
PHM 1:16 kakalaku hanga muhika wa ngeyi, kaasi wekina kuhita muhika: phangi mosi watondama. Mukuma kenina kwena meni, hanga phangi watondama, kakálabwa hika kwena ngeyi phi phangi watondama, hanga mutu, hanga phi phangi mwena Kidisitu.
PHM 1:17 Yuka ni wisi mbongila hanga nduku waku, mubonga yandi phi bwosu wisi mbongila meni.
PHM 1:18 Yuka ni mbi kákuhanga, kondi loni pfuka yaku kenina yawu, syabya mu mutwa wa meni.
PHM 1:19 Yi koku dya meni meni mbati sonikina mambu mama: Meni Pholu, yikúvutwalabya. Nzodiku yikuyubululabwa ni ngeyi pfuka ya meni wenina yawu, luzingu lwaku yáta.
PHM 1:20 Kyedika, Phangi wama, tsadisa bwabuna kikuma kya lungongu lwa Pfumu: ndembika mbundu mukuma ngeyi yi meni kima kimosi thwenina mwena Kidisitu.
PHM 1:21 Tsini mbundu ni muna tangwa dyadidi mbati kusonikina, wahánga kuhita hika buna yikulombini. Nzayi mboti ni wahángabwa hika kuluta.
PHM 1:22 Amana muna mbala mosi, yikulombi hika ni wangidikila mwanza, mukuma yenina yi kikwamina ni muna bisambu byenu nzila yakhángwakila ndangu yisa luvutwakila hika.
PHM 1:23 Ephafwasi, yandi wenina hakimosi yi meni mu boloku kikuma kya Kidisitu Yesu, mboti kakuhekini;
PHM 1:24 Malaku, Adisitadiki, Temasi yi Luka, basindikidi bama ba kisalu, bawu phi mboti bakuhekini.
PHM 1:25 Yambula khenda za Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu zakala yi kitembu kyenu!
HEB 1:1 Muna tangwa dya khulu, Nzambi kakala zonza kwena batata betu mbala za lawu amana mu mitundu mya lawu muna nzila ya bambikudi,
HEB 1:2 kaasi buthwena, mu bilumbu byabi bya tsuka, kátuzonzila mwena Mwana wandi mosi wuna kásikununa swana wa byosu, muna nzila ya yandi wuna káhangila tsi.
HEB 1:3 Mwana meni wuna kenina mutsyenzya wa khembu ya Nzambi amana kenina kifwani kya mukwandi kya buna kenina Nzambi, amana ndinga ya yandi ya hamu yisi zyamisa tsi. Ku manima ma kusemisa batu ku masumu ma bawu, wázakala kuna koku dya kitata dya kipfumu kya Nzambi, muna bisoka bya mazilu.
HEB 1:4 Bwosu kákituka mbuta kwena banzyo Nzambi wámuheka zina dihitini dina dya bawu.
HEB 1:5 Mu kyedika, keti kwena mosi wa banzyo Nzambi kázimbwala kedi: «Ngeyi wenina Mwana wama, tuka lelu dyadi, meni yikubutini.» Amana khaniku kazimbula kwena wanzyo mosi: «Tata yikála kikuma kya yandi amana kakála Mwana kikuma kya meni.»
HEB 1:6 Kaasi mu tangwa káhitika Mwana wandi wa tsomi muna tsi, wuzimbudini: «Banzyo ba Nzambi boosu bamufukamina.»
HEB 1:7 Kikuma kya banzyo, kázimbula: «Nzambi, banzyo bandi, kisi bakitula bitembu amana basadi bandi kisi bakitula mileku mya mbawu.»
HEB 1:8 Kaasi Nzambi kázimbula kikuma kya Mwana wandi: Wenina Nzambi, «Kiti kyaku kya luyalu kyásikila mvula yi mvula. Koka dya masonga maku dyenina koka dya luyalu lwaku.
HEB 1:9 Wisi zola masonga, amana wámenga mbi, yi hakana Nzambi, Nzambi waku, kákusodila mu kukusita mafuta ma thumbama, amana wákusola kuhita bakwenu khunda.»
HEB 1:10 Kázimbula hika: «Ngeyi, Pfumu, wátunga tsi muna luyandiku, amana mazilu menina muhangu wa moku maku.
HEB 1:11 Byosu byabina byazíluka, kaasi ngeyi wenina. Tsi yi zilu byakúlwakila hanga miledi mya khulu;
HEB 1:12 wavúngabya hanga muzaka wumosi, amana byasóba hanga muledi wumosi phi. Kaasi ngeyi wenina phila mosi kaka, amana luzingu lwaku lweku yi tsuka.»
HEB 1:13 Amana Nzambi kázimbulaku kedi keti kwena mosi wa banzyo bandi: «Awisa sikuka ku kitata kyama, yi kuna yikítwala bambeni baku kidyatilu kya bitambi byaku.»
HEB 1:14 Aketi banzyo benina bitembu, bana byenina mu kisalu kya Nzambi: Nzambi kisi batuma kikuma kya kusadisaka batu babana bakwisa vwa luhulusu.
HEB 2:1 Yi hakana betu tufweti simbidila buna bufwani ku musamu wuna twáyuka, hanga twaditotisa nana nzila.
HEB 2:2 Kikuma, honi musamu wuna kázonza Nzambi mu nzila ya banzyo wawu wálungila, amana wosu wuna wazítisawoku kondi loni walémvukilawoku, kabonga ndola yina yilungini.
HEB 2:3 Amana abweti twalenda mu kuhenga ndola yina ho twalewula luhulusu lwa mbuta lwaluna? Yandi-meni Pfumu watekilalwa samuna. Amana phi, babana báyuka mu kuzonzila luhulusu meni lwenina kwena Pfumu bátukwikisalwa.
HEB 2:4 Nzambi wásikununa kimbangi kya bawu ni kya kyedika muna nzila ya bidimbu, muna bithondu, yi mu biphadi bya mutindu wosu, yi muna kabu dina kátyakila Kitembu Kyatoma kwena mosi-mosi wa bawu muna luzolu lwandi.
HEB 2:5 Kikuma, heku ni kwena banzyo káhana Nzambi, kiyeka kya tsi yina yakwísa yina tubati zonzila.
HEB 2:6 Kinga, mutu mosi kázimbula muna Masonuku: «Nati kenina mutu ndangu ngeyi wamuyubukaka? Nati kenina mwana wa mutu ndangu ngeyi wamukebaka?
HEB 2:7 Muna tangwa dya khunda, ngeyi wamusila mutu muna sina dya banzyo, wámuvwatisa mu khembu yi luzitu,
HEB 2:8 wasya byosu muna sina dya bitambi byandi.» Yuka ni Nzambi káhana kiyeka kya bima byosu kwena mutu, disongila, kásisaku kima kina kimutadiku. Kinga buthwena, tubatiku mona ni byosu mu kiyeka kya mutu byenina.
HEB 2:9 Kaasi tumoni ni Yesu bámukitula koma, muna sina dya banzyo mu tangwa dimosi bwabu, amana wávwata mukhonzi wa khembu yi luzitu kikuma kya lufwa luna kányokukina. Amana muna buweti bwa Nzambi, kisa fwila kikuma kya batu boosu.
HEB 2:10 Kikuma muna nzila ya yandi Nzambi yi mwena yandi byosu byisi zingila, kázola mu kunatisa ku khembu bana balawu. Káhanga bwabuna mu kumukitula Yesu mutu walungila muna nzila ya minyanga myandi, yandi wenina kisina kya luhulusu lwa bawu.
HEB 2:11 Mukuma, Yesu wisi semisa batu ku masumu ma bawu amana babana benina ba kasemi boosu kwena Tata mosi batukini. Yi hakana yandi keku yi tsoni za kubatedila baleki bandi.
HEB 2:12 Tangwa kazimbudini Yesu: «Yisámuna zina dyaku kwena baphangi bama, yikútsikisa hana kati dya kimvuka.»
HEB 2:13 Wuzimbudi phi: «Yisya mbundu yama mwena Nzambi.» Amana phi: «Awu meni, meni yi bana babana kaphekini Nzambi.»
HEB 2:14 Kikuma bana babana boosu benina kima kimosi yi yandi muna menga yi mu lutu, yandi phi luzingu lumosi kázinga yi bawu. Yi hakana ni muna lufwa lwandi wátusuna kiphidi-mutu, wuna wakala simbidila ngolu za lufwa,
HEB 2:15 amana wákula boosu babana meni bákala bakwatama mu kihika kya bweya bwa lufwa muna luzingu lwa bawu lwosu.
HEB 2:16 Kikuma, kyedika ka kwena banzyo ku kisi kwisa mu kusadisa, kaasi ku butuka dya Bulahami kisi kwisa sadisa.
HEB 2:17 Yi hakana kálunga mu kukituka kitesu kimosi mu moosu kwena baphangi bandi. Bwabuna ndangu kakituka mbuta-nganga mosi wabasa yi buweti yi kuhwila mwani muna kisalu kya Nzambi, kikuma kya kulolula masumu ma batu.
HEB 2:18 Mukuma bwosu kányokuka yandi-meni tangwa káhita mu kimeka, wulungini mu kuyakidila babana benina mu kimeka.
HEB 3:1 Amana phi baphangi batu ba Nzambi, bakwetu khunda ba mbila ya Nzambi, talenu kwena Yesu, yandi thumwa wa Nzambi amana Mbuta-Nganga wa lukwikilu lwalu tubati samuna.
HEB 3:2 Kikuma, Yesu wáhwila mwani kwena wuna wámusikununa bwosu kákalabwa Moyize muna nzu yosu ya Nzambi.
HEB 3:3 Kaasi Yesu kenina yi khembu ya lawu kuhita yayi ya Moyize hanga mutu wuna wutungini nzu kenina yi lukumu lwa lawu kuhita yawu-meni nzu.
HEB 3:4 Kosu nzu, mu kyedika, mu nzila ya mutu yisi tungamina; amana, wuna wátunga bima byosu, kenina Nzambi.
HEB 3:5 Amana Moyize wáhwila mwani muna nzu ya Nzambi yosu hanga musadi, kikuma kya kuta kimbangi kya mana kakala zonza Nzambi.
HEB 3:6 Kaasi Kidisitu keninabwa hanga Mwana wa kusikununa, mutwa wa nzu ya Nzambi. Kinga nzu ya yandi yi betu, ho twalema kikumbwala yi lulendu luna thwisi sila kivuvu.
HEB 3:7 Yi hakana ni, bwosu kazimbudibwa Kitembu Kyatoma: «Lelu, ho luyukini ndinga ya yandi,
HEB 3:8 luzitikaku mbundu, bwosu mu kilumbu kina batu bámubalwakila Nzambi, mu tangwa dya kimeka muna tseki ya khatu;
HEB 3:9 Kwakuna bakhaka benu bátsokila muna kimeka kimosi mbata nana bámona mihangu myama.
HEB 3:10 Muna mvula makumaya. Yi hakana yíyukila khabu kikuma kya batu ba tangwa meni dyadina, amana nzimbudini: "Bisi ditotisa kosu tangwa muna mbundu ya bawu, bámonazoku nzila zama."
HEB 3:11 Yidya ndefi muna khabu zama: Bakótamwoku muna tsi yina yíbayidikila kikuma kya kulembwila!»
HEB 3:12 Kebenu baphangi, ka mutu ku hana kati dya benu kakala yi mbundu yimosi ya mbi, mbundu ya ngolu amana yamuyekulaka kwena Nzambi wa moya.
HEB 3:13 Kaasi disyamisakenu benu yi benu kosu kilumbu buna fwanini mu kuzonzila «lelu», ndangu keti mosi wa benu kahunanaku ku disumu amana kakituka yi mbundu ya tadi.
HEB 3:14 Kikuma, tukituki basindikidi ba Kidisitu, tufweti tomalunda kikumbwala yi kuna tsuka bwosu kyákala ku luyandiku.
HEB 3:15 Bwosu mazimbudi Masonuku: «Ho luyukini ndinga ya yandi lelu, luzitikaku mbundu zenu bwosu mu kilumbu kina batu bámubalwakila Nzambi.»
HEB 3:16 Banati babana báyuka ndinga ya Nzambi amana báhakuka kikuma kya yandi? Ka bawu ku boosu babana kálubula Moyize mu Ngiphiti?
HEB 3:17 Amana kwena banati kásidikila Nzambi muna mvula makumaya? Ka kikuma kya babana ku báhola masumu amana bakala fwa muna tseki?
HEB 3:18 Amana kwena ba nati kádila Nzambi ndefi yayi: «bakótamwoku muna tsi yina yíbayidikila kikuma kya kulembwila», ka babana ku bamana hakuka?
HEB 3:19 Amana tumonini buna bwa bukheti ni, bálendamwoku kukota kikuma kya kukonda kwa bawu kwa lukwikilu.
HEB 4:1 Nzambi wátusisila kilangi kimosi kya kukota muna kilembwadi. Tukebenu ni hana kati dya benu, hakala nana yi mutu wabánza ni mu tsukinina kenina.
HEB 4:2 Mukuma betu mutindu wumosi yi kwena bakhaka betu twáyukawa Musamu wa Bukheti. Kaasi, ndinga yina báyuka bawu, yábasadisaku mukuma bátambwasayoku yi lukwikilu.
HEB 4:3 Kaasi kwena betu twákwikilaya, tukotini muna kilembwadi bwosu kázimbula Nzambi: «Yidya ndefi muna khabu zama: Keti bwe, bakótakumwoku muna kilembwadi kyama!» Kinga, mihangu myandi myámanisa kedi tukidila mu kuhangama kwa tsi.
HEB 4:4 Mukuma, kázimbula homa hamosi kikuma kina kitadidini kilumbu kya tsambwadi: «Amana Nzambi wálembwa muna mihangu myandi myosu.»
HEB 4:5 Amana muna nzila yayi wuzimbudi hika: «Keti bwe, bakótaku muna kilembwadi kyama.»
HEB 4:6 Kikuma bwáyilama kwena batu bahika mu kukota, amana babana báyuka theti Musamu wa Bukheti, bákotamwoku kikuma kya kukolama kwa bawu. Yi bwabuna, phila yenina hika kikuma kya batu ba hika mu kukotamwa.
HEB 4:7 Nzambi wusini kilumbu kya hika kina katedi ni «lelu». Kázonzilakya hika kyakina lawu, muna nzila ya Tavidi, muna kitini kina tutangi kedi: «Ho luyukini ndinga ya Nzambi lelu, luzitikaku mbundu yenu».
HEB 4:8 Wadi ni Yoswa kabanatisaka mu kilembwadi, wadi Nzambi ku manima kakhaniku zonzila hika kilumbu kikwawu.
HEB 4:9 Disongidila ni, kilembwadi kimosi kya sabata kisadini kikuma kya kanda dya Nzambi.
HEB 4:10 Mukuma, wuna wukotini mu kilembwadi kya Nzambi wulembwini ku mihangu myandi bwosu kálembwa Nzambi ku mihangu mya yandi meni.
HEB 4:11 Tusyenu tswatsu mu kukota mu kilembwadi kyakina; ndangu mutu kabwaku hanga bakhaka betu bábwisa mu kulemvuka.
HEB 4:12 Mukuma ndinga ya Nzambi yenina ya moya amana ya ngolu. Yisi tapha hanga mbedi mosi ya phoku. Yisi kota yi kuna byákhundakanina moya yi kitembu, bikhosu yi miluku amana yihambudibya. Yisi fundisa masunga yi mabanza ma mbundu ya mutu.
HEB 4:13 Amana kweku kima kyáswamana ku mesu ma yandi, kaasi kyosu kyenina ha tseki amana kya kuyengika ku mesu ma yanduna wuna, betu boosu, twámenikina zimbu.
HEB 4:14 Bwosu twenina yi mbuta-nganga wuna wádimbuka mazilu, Yesu, Mwana wa Nzambi, tusimbidilenu ngolu ku lukwikilu luna thwisi samuna.
HEB 4:15 Mukuma mbuta-nganga yandu thwenina yandi kenina wuna wufwanini mu kunyokuka hakimosi yi betu muna malebakani metu: kábwa mu kimeka hanga betu muna bima byosu, kaasi konda kuhola disumu.
HEB 4:16 Yi hakana ni, tubwesukenu yi kikumbwala ku kiti kya kipfumu kya Nzambi yandu wabasa yi khenda; mu kunona kheni yi khenda, ndangu kalenga tuyakidila muna tangwa dya phasi.
HEB 5:1 Kaasi mbuta-nganga wosu, bisi musola hana kati dya batu, bamusikununi kikuma kya batu muna kisalu kya Nzambi; ndangu katambikaka milambu yi bimenga kikuma kya masumu.
HEB 5:2 Bufwani ni kakala yi mbakisilu kikuma kya babana bazayiku mambu yi babana bisi ditotisa. Mudyambu yandi meni wáhitila muna lebakani.
HEB 5:3 Amana kikuma kya lebakani dyadina, kafweti tambika bimenga kikuma kya masumu ma yandi meni yi kikuma kya masumu ma batu bahika.
HEB 5:4 Kinga ka mutu ku wufwani mu kudiheka lukumu yandi meni, ho bámutediku kwena Nzambi, bwosu kákalabwa Loni.
HEB 5:5 Phila mosi, Kidisitu ka yandi meni ku wádiheka lukumu lwa kimbuta-nganga. Kábongilalwa kwena Nzambi wuna wámuzimbwala: «Wenina Mwana wama, yandika lelu, meni yikubutini.»
HEB 5:6 Amana mwahika wuzimbudini: «Wenina nganga Nzambi mu kimakulu muna ndonga ya Medikiseteki.»
HEB 5:7 Muna bilumbu bya luzingu lwandi ha tsi, Yesu wátambika bisambu, kubokwadila yi matsanga kwena Nzambi wuna wakhana muhulula ku lufwa. Amana Nzambi wámuyuka kikuma kya bulemvu bwandi.
HEB 5:8 Keti bweti kákala kwandi Mwana wa Nzambi, wálonguka mu kulemvuka muna nzila ya bina kányokwakina.
HEB 5:9 Amana bwosu buna, Nzambi kámukitula mutu walunga, wákituka kisina kya luhulusu lwa konda tsuka kikuma kya mutu wosu wuna wisi mulemvwakila.
HEB 5:10 Nzambi wámusikununa mbuta-nganga muna mutindu wa Medikiseteki.
HEB 5:11 Mambu lawu thwenina mawu mu kuzonza matadidini dyambu dyadi, kaasi phasi mu kulutendwala, mukuma lwekina yi makokwa mu kubakula.
HEB 5:12 Tukidila thama wadi lwakituka kedi balongi, kaasi bafweti lulonga hika bikuma bya theti bya luyandiku bya ndinga za Nzambi. Kyadi kwena benu, mukuma yi lelu dyadi, mu kuyema lwenina kaka hana lwáfwana mu kudya madya ma ngolu.
HEB 5:13 Wosu wuna wisi zoluka mu kunwa mayeni mwana wa khunda kwandi kenina, kafwaniku kutenda mu kikuma kitadidini masonga.
HEB 5:14 Kaasi madya ma ngolu menina kikuma kya bambuta, kikuma kya babana benina yi katsatsa ka kuswasikisa, muna luzingu lwa kosu kilumbu, mambu mana menina ma mboti yi mana menina ma mbi.
HEB 6:1 Yi hakana ni, tuzakukenu muna bikuma bya theti bya malongi matadidini Kidisitu. Tuvutukilaku hika malongi mana ma kisina hanga tsobuka ya mbundu ku mambu matadidini mihangu myafwa yi lukwikilu mwena Nzambi,
HEB 6:2 malongi matadidini mbotika yi kuthetika kwa moku, pfutumuka ya bafwa yi pfundusu ya kimakulu.
HEB 6:3 Amana bwabuna twahánga, ho Nzambi kazolabwa.
HEB 6:4 Kikuma batu babana bábayinika ku mwini wa Nzambi mbala yikwawu, bálekita ku kabu dya ku zilu, bátambula Kitembu Kyatoma hakimosi yi bakwawu,
HEB 6:5 Bálekita ndinga ya bukheti ya Nzambi yi ngolu zilutini za tsi yina yakwísa.
HEB 6:6 Babwini muna luzingu lwa bawu lwa khulu! Bwalendakanaku mu kubanata ku tsobuka ya pha ya mbundu. Mukuma, Mwana wa Nzambi babati vutula hika ha kitakani amana babati mulewula ha mesu ma batu.
HEB 6:7 Kikuma, yuka ni mvula kakotaka mu mafu kosu tangwa, amana kamenisaka miti mya mupfunu kwena babana bakunimya, disongidila ni mafu mamana, Nzambi wásakumunama.
HEB 6:8 Kaasi ho mamenisa bivunza bya tsaku yi kisoma, mákalaku mupfunu; amana ka thama ku babundilama kwena Nzambi amana tsuka tsuka kuyokama.
HEB 6:9 Yi hakana, keti bweti, tuzonzi bwabuna kaasi baphangi bama batondama, tusini mbundu ni kima kimosi kya tsambu kibati luhingila, luhulusu.
HEB 6:10 Kikuma Nzambi keku kayengu. Amana kazímbakanaku muhangu wenu, keti lungongu luna lusongidini kikuma kya zina dyandi, ha lwádikotisa mu kusadila bakwikidi tuka thama yi buthwena bwabu.
HEB 6:11 Kaasi tuzodi ni kosu mutu wa benu kasongila tsambu meni zazina tii yi kuna tsuka, ndangu kivuvu kyenu kyamonika kyabasa.
HEB 6:12 Ndangu lukitukaku bamolu, kaasi sokululenu babana bisi bonga kuvwa kuna kásila Nzambi muna lukwikilu yi kikwamina.
HEB 6:13 Tangwa kásila Nzambi kilangi kwena Bulahami, bwosu kwákalaku zina dya mutu wa mbuta mwena dina káfwana mu kudila ndefi, yi hana kádila ndefi muna zina dya yandi meni.
HEB 6:14 Wázimbula: «Kyedika, yikúsakumuna buna bufwani amana yivúdisa butuka dyaku.»
HEB 6:15 Yi hakana ni Bulahami mu kikwamina, wánona kina kásila Nzambi.
HEB 6:16 Kinga, batu ha bisi dya ndefi muna zina dya mutu wuna wubahitini bawu mu lukumu, amana ndefi yayina yisi tabula tendu dyosu.
HEB 6:17 Muna phila yayina, Nzambi kázola ni kasongila wengele kwena babana bafwana mu kubonga mamboti ma kilangi ni ndefi yandi yisiku katuka; yi hakana kádila ndefi ku kilangi kyandi.
HEB 6:18 Yi hakana, muna mambu modi mafwaniku mu kusoba, bwalendakanaku kwena Nzambi mu kuhuna. Yi hakana ni, thwenina yi kikesa kya lawu, betu baba thwenina yi kiswaminu kimosi: kubonga kivuvu kina bátusila.
HEB 6:19 Kivuvu kyakina kikuma kya betu kyenina hanga kikokolu kya ngolu yi kya mukwandi kya moya wetu. Kyisi lobuka amana kihiti kibwiku kya kizika kyatoma hedila.
HEB 6:20 Yi hakana meni kákotila Yesu ku thwala ya betu yi kikuma kya betu, mu kuyata kanga ku mesu ma betu, wákituka mbuta-nganga mu kimakulu muna kanga dya Medikiseteki.
HEB 7:1 Medikiseteki meni yandina kyamvu wa tsi ya Salemi kákala yi nganga-Nzambi wa Nzambi Kahungu. Kenda mu kuhukulula Bulahami, muna tangwa dina kákala mu kuvutwakisa, yandi Bulahami, ku muzingu wuna kábedisila bakyamvu amana Medikiseteki wámusakumuna.
HEB 7:2 Bulahami kwena yandi káhana mulambu wa kimosi kya kumi kya muluta wuna kábonga ku mvita. Kinga ho twabindula zina dya Medikiseteki, theti-theti, disongidila «kyamvu wa masonga»; amana phi, kenina kyamvu wa tsi ya Salemi, disongidila «kyamvu wa ngemba.»
HEB 7:3 Bamuzayidiku keti tata, keti ngudi, keti kisina kya butuka; luzingu lwandi lweku keti luyandiku keti tsuka. Kisi fwanakana yi Mwana wa Nzambi, kenina nganga-Nzambi wa mvula yi mvula.
HEB 7:4 Mutalenu buna kenina wa mbuta mutu yandu, kwena yandi wuna káhana keti khaka Bulahami kimosi kya kumi kya muluta wuna kábonga ku mvita!
HEB 7:5 Bwosu wenina muna mitsiku, bana ba Lefi bawu benina mu tsadidi ya banganga-Nzambi, benina yi muswa wa kulambwasa kimosi kya kumi kya bima byosu kwena kikanda kya Kiseledi, disongila kwena baphangi ba bawu kibeni, kinga bawu phi mu vumu dya Bulahami benina.
HEB 7:6 Medikiseteki yandi keku mu butuka dya Lefi, kaasi wálambwasa kimosi kya kumi kwena Bulahami, amana hika, wámusakumuna wuna básila bilangi kwena Nzambi.
HEB 7:7 Kinga, kweku keti tendu, mbuta wisi sakumuna muleki.
HEB 7:8 Batekulu ba Lefi, babana bisi lambwasa kimosi kya kumi, benina batu bisi fwa, kaasi mu dyambu ditadidini Medikiseteki, Masonuku masongidi ni kenina mutu wuna wisi zinga.
HEB 7:9 Ndangu mu kuzimbula moosu, muna nzila ya Bulahami, keti Lefi wuna wisi lambwasa kimosi kya kumi, yandi phi wálambula kimosi kya kumi kwena Medikiseteki.
HEB 7:10 Mukuma keti bweti Lefi kákalaku kedi wabutuka, hana kákala muna menga ma khaka wandi Bulahami muna tangwa dina kisa mutundakana Medikiseteki.
HEB 7:11 Kinganga-Nzambi kya kilefi kyákala ha sina dya mitsiku mina káhana Nzambi kwena kanda dya Kiseledi. Kinga, wadi kinganga-Nzambi kya balefi kyanatisaka batu mu kutoma, wadi kukhaniku kala hika mupfunu wa kulubula ndonga yahika ya kinganga-Nzambi mu kanga dya Medikiseteki; kaasi ka mu kanga dya Loni ku.
HEB 7:12 Mukuma ho kinganga-Nzambi kisobukini, mitsiku phi mifweti sobuka.
HEB 7:13 Amana Pfumu wetu, wuna zitadidi ndinga zazi, kenina mu butuka dya hika, dyadina dyeku keti mutu mosi wáhanga kedi kisalu kya mesa ma kimenga.
HEB 7:14 Mukuma wázayakana kedi, tukidila lubutuku, ni Pfumu wetu mu vumu dya Yuta kenina, hahana Moyize kakonda zonzila kima kitadidini kinganga-Nzambi.
HEB 7:15 Bwabuna bwekina wengele: nganga-Nzambi wuna wulubukini muna kanga dyadina wufwanini yi Medikiseteki.
HEB 7:16 Kakitukiku nganga-Nzambi mu nzila ya mutsiku wa butuka dya kimutu; kaasi mu nzila ya hamu dya luzingu lumosi luna lwakonda tsuka.
HEB 7:17 Mukuma, Masonuku mamutidini kimbangi: «Wenina nganga-Nzambi kyamakulu muna ndonga ya Medikiseteki.»
HEB 7:18 Bwabuna wákumwakina mukuku wa khulu, kikuma wákalaku walunga amana wákalaku mupfunu;
HEB 7:19 mukuma mutsiku wa Moyize, wánatisaku mu kutoma. Ndambu yi kwawu, kivuvu kimosi kya bukheti kyátuhanamina, amana kibinga kwena kivuvu kyakina, tufwanini mu kubandakana kwena Nzambi.
HEB 7:20 Amana, bwabuna bwáhangamina muna nzila ya kudya kwa ndefi kwa Nzambi. Bahika bákituka banganga-Nzambi konda ndefi ya mutindu wuna.
HEB 7:21 Kaasi Yesu, yandi, kákituka Nganga-Nzambi mu nzila ya ndefi, kwena Nzambi wuna wámuzimbwala: «Pfumu wádya ndefi, kazósululaku hika: ''Wenina Nganga-Nzambi kyamakulu."»
HEB 7:22 Muna bwabuna, Yesu wákituka Nganga-Nzambi wuna wisi hana tsikiningi ya bulunda bwa bukheti kuluta.
HEB 7:23 Kuhita, banganga-Nzambi bádilandikisa mu thalu ya lawu, kikuma lufwa lwábakakidila mu kulanda kisalu kya bawu.
HEB 7:24 Kaasi Yesu bwosu kisi zinga mvula muna mvula amana kiyeka kyandi kya kinganga-Nzambi kyásikila kyamakulu.
HEB 7:25 Yi hakana phi kyenina kyafwana mu kuhulula kyamakulu babana bisi kokuluka kwena Nzambi mu nzila ya yandi, mukuma bilumbu byosu wa moya kenina muna kulombilaka Nzambi kikuma kya bawu.
HEB 7:26 Yesu kenina Nganga-Nzambi wa mbuta yandi wuna wáfwana kikuma kya betu. Kenina watoma, konda kifu, konda disumu; wa kuhambula yi basumuki amana Nzambi wámulumisa lawu kuhita mazilu.
HEB 7:27 Keku yi mupfunu wa kuyokaka kimenga theti kikuma kya masumu mandi yi kikuma kya mamana ma kanda hanga bambuta banganga bahika. Bwabuna káhangabwa mbala yimosi lwesi kikuma kya moosu, mu kuditambika yandi-meni hanga kimenga.
HEB 7:28 Mutsiku wa Moyize wisi sikununa bambuta banganga batu bana benina yi lebakani. Kaasi ndefi ya Nzambi, yina yázonzama ku manima ma mitsiku, yámusikununa, hanga mbuta nganga kyamakulu, Mwana wuna wenina watoma.
HEB 8:1 Kinga tala dyambu dya mupfunu wa lawu thwisi zimbula, thwenina yi Mbuta-Nganga wa bwabuna, yandi wuna wázakala muna mazilu kuna koku dya kitata dya kiti kya kipfumu kya Nzambi.
HEB 8:2 Mu kisalu kenina kya kikumbu kya Nzambi, disongidila ni sombolu dya kyedika dina dyátungamina kwena Pfumu amana ka kwena mutu ku.
HEB 8:3 Mukuma mbuta-nganga wosu bisi musikununa kikuma kya kutambika makabu yi bimenga; yi hakana meni mupfunu wenina ni mbuta-nganga wa betu yandi phi kavwa kima kimosi mu kutambika.
HEB 8:4 Kinga wadi kakalaka ha tsi, kakhanaku kukala phi keti nganga-Nzambi, kikuma kwenina yi bahika bisi tambika kedi makabu bwosu bwenina muna mitsiku mya Moyize.
HEB 8:5 Kinga, banganga-Nzambi babana bisi sala kisalu muna kikumbu meni kina, bisikya sala mu kifwani yi kininga kya kikumbu kya ku zilu. Mamana mafwananini yi mutindu wuna kázonza Nzambi kwena Moyize tangwa kazola katunga sombolu dya lukutakanu: «Wasímbulula mu kusya ti kisalu kyaku kyafwanana yi mbandu yina yíkusongila ha mongu.»
HEB 8:6 Kaasi buthwena, Nzambi wámuheka Yesu kisalu kya mbuta kuhita, yandi wenina mukhundingisi wa bulunda bumosi bwa mbuta, bwátungamina ha bilangi bya mbuta bya bukheti.
HEB 8:7 Wadi bulunda bwa theti bwákalaka konda kifu, kwakhanaku kala yi mupfunu wa kuhingisa bwahika bwa zodi.
HEB 8:8 Kaasi byenina bikalu kabati songisa Nzambi kwena kanda dyandi, tangwa kabati zimbula: «Bilumbu byisini, kazimbudini Pfumu, bina yita bulunda bumosi bwa pha yi kanda dya Kiseledi yi kanda dya Yuta.
HEB 8:9 Bwakálaku hanga bulunda buna yita yi batata ba bawu kilumbu kina yíbasimba ku koku kikuma kya kubalubula ku tsi ya Ngiphiti. Kikuma bawu-meni bákwaminaku muna bulunda bwama bwabuna, meni phi yisiku diyangisa hika kikuma kya bawu, kazimbudini Pfumu.
HEB 8:10 Kinga tala bulunda buna yíta yi kanda dya Kiseledi ku manima ma bilumbu byabina, kazimbudini Pfumu: Yisya mitsiku myama muna ngangu za bawu, yisónikamya muna mbundu ya bawu,: Nzambi wa bawu yikadiki amana bawu bakadiki kanda dyama.
HEB 8:11 Ka mutu ku wakála yi mupfunu wa kulonga kwena mukwenu kondi loni keti kwena phangi wandi, kámuzimbwala: muzaya Pfumu! Mukuma boosu banzáya, yandikila mwana wa khunda yi kuna mutu wa mbuta hana kati dya bawu.
HEB 8:12 Mukuma, yibáfwila khenda kikuma kya mitsoki mya bawu amana yiyúbukamoku hika masumu ma bawu keti koma.»
HEB 8:13 Mu kuzonzila bulunda bwa pha, Nzambi wákitulabwa buna bwa khulu mu bulunda bwa theti; kinga, kina kyekina kya khulu amana kinunini kyekina mu kutota.
HEB 9:1 Bulunda bwa theti bwákala yi mikuku mitadidi bisambu yi kikumbu kyandi kya ha tsi.
HEB 9:2 Kikuma, sombolu dya theti dyatekila tungama. Muna ndambu ya theti ya mukati, bisi tela kizika kyahedila, mwákala yi muzanga wa mwinda, mesa yi mapha ma kutambika kwena Nzambi.
HEB 9:3 Ku manima ma kibwiku, kwákala yi ndambu yikwawu ya sombolu, yina bakala tela ni Kizika Kyatoma lawu.
HEB 9:4 Kwákala yi mesa ma pfwabidi ma kutunga mu wolu yi mukunzu wa bulunda wátungama wosu mu wolu. Muna mukunzu wamuna mwákala yi bangwa dya wolu dina dyakala sweka maana, koka dya Loni dina dyábufula bifulu yi bitini bya matadi bya bulunda. Mwákala hika yi bitini bya matadi bina bánamika ndinga za bulunda.
HEB 9:5 Hana thandu ya mukunzu hákala yi banzyo bana bisi tela ni syedibe babana bakala songila khembu ya Nzambi. Bakala yalumuna mahela ma bawu hana thandu ya munoku wa mukunzu wa bulunda. Kaasi buthwena kadyaku tangwa dya kutongutuna byosu byabina.
HEB 9:6 Byabina byosu ho ni biyilamini, banganga-Nzambi bisi kota kosu kilumbu muna kitini kya theti kya sombolu kikuma kya kulungisa kisalu kya bisambu bya bawu.
HEB 9:7 Kaasi muna kyakina kya zodi, mbuta-nganga lwesi wisimwa kota, mbala mosi muna mvula. Homa hana, kisiha kotila kikuma kya kutambika menga ma kibulu kikuma kya mitsoki mya yandi meni yi kikuma kya mitsoki mya kanda.
HEB 9:8 Kitembu Kyatoma kasongidini bwabuna ni nzila ya kizika kyatoma lawu yáfwanaku kedi mu kukanguka bwosu buna dibati zinga sombolu dya theti.
HEB 9:9 Kyakina kyenina kingana kikuma kya tangwa dyadi. Kisi tendula ni makabu yi bimenga bya bibulu bina bisi lambula kwena Nzambi bilungiku mu kusemisa katsatsa ka wosu wuna wisibya sadila.
HEB 9:10 Byabina byenina bizila bitadidini lwesi bima bya kudya, bya kunwa yi mambu mahika matadidini kudisemisa. Yákala tsadidi ya kimutu tii yi kuna tangwa dina kásobisila Nzambi mambu.
HEB 9:11 Kaasi Kidisitu kísa hanga Mbuta-Nganga wa bima byabi bidiyenina kedi. Wádimbuka sombolu dya mbuta mbuta yi dyalungila, dina dyakonda tungamina kwena batu, disongila ni dyeku dya tsi yayi yáhangama.
HEB 9:12 Kidisitu kákota mbala mosi lwesi muna kizika kyatoma lawu, kálambulaku menga ma bakhombu yi ma bana ba bangombi; menga ma yandi meni lwesi kálambula yi bwabuna kátusumba kyamakulu ku masumu metu.
HEB 9:13 Kikuma ho ni menga ma bakhombu yi ma miluma mya bangombi yi mbombi ya ngombi wa kibuti, mana bisi mwanginina hana thandu ya batu babana básumuka, mabatomisaka yi mu kubasemisaka lutu,
HEB 9:14 abweti menga ma Kidisitu máhitilaku mu ngolu? Muna nzila ya Kitembu wa mvula yi mvula, Kidisitu yandi wákala konda kifu, wáditambika yandi meni kwena Nzambi hanga kimenga kyakonda kifu. Menga mandi masémisa katsatsa ketu ka mihangu mina myisi natisa ku lufwa, ndangu twalenga fukamina Nzambi wa moya.
HEB 9:15 Yi hakana, Kidisitu kenina mukhundingisi wa bulunda bwa pha, ndangu babana kátela Nzambi balenga bonga kuvwa kwa mvula yi mvula kuna kásila Nzambi. Disongidila ni batu meni babana benina balunga mu kubonga kuvwa meni kuna; kikuma lufwa lwa mutu mosi lwáyakidila mu luhulusu lwa mitsoki mya batu mina myáhangama muna bulunda bwa theti.
HEB 9:16 Mukuma hakana básisa ndinga, bulungi ni lufwa lwa yanduna wásisaya lwazayakana.
HEB 9:17 Kikuma, ndinga ya mutu wafwa yisiku kwatakana bwosu kenina mu luzingu mukwa yawu wuna wázonzaya; yisi kwatakana ku manima ma lufwa ma yanduna lwesi.
HEB 9:18 Yi hakana ni bulunda bwa theti bwawu meni bwákalaku kedi bwa kusikununa konda menga.
HEB 9:19 Tangwa kásamuna Moyize kwena kanda dyosu kosu mukuku bwosu wenina muna mitsiku, wábonga menga ma bana ba bangombi yi ma bana ba bakhombu yi mamba. Wásophulabya hana mukanda wa mitsiku yi kikanda kyosu kuna sophu dya muhandi wa yizophi yi koma ka muphungu wa kabengi.
HEB 9:20 Kázimbula: «Mama menina menga ma bulunda buna káta Nzambi kikuma kya benu.»
HEB 9:21 Kunima, wásophula hika sombolu yi menga yi bilekwa byosu bya kisalu bitadidini bisambu.
HEB 9:22 Kinga, bwosu milombini mitsiku, kima kyosu bisikya semisa yi menga, amana ndoluka ya masumu yisi hanamina kaka yuka ni menga matyakanini.
HEB 9:23 Bifwani bya bima bya ku zilu byálomba ni basemisabya muna mutindu meni wawuna; amana bina byenina ku zilu, byawu meni, byisi lomba bimenga bya phwena.
HEB 9:24 Mukuma Kidisitu kákotaku mu kikumbu kyátungama ku moku ma batu, kifwani kya kikumbu kya kyedika. Wákota muna kati dya zilu, kwakuna kenina buthwena watelama kuna mesu ma Nzambi kikuma kya betu.
HEB 9:25 Heku ni kikuma kya kuditambika yandi meni kosu tangwa bwosu kisi kota mbuta-nganga muna kikumbu ku manima ma kosu mvula yi menga mana meku ma yandi meni.
HEB 9:26 Wadi kabwaku, wadi kakhana nyokuka mbala za lawu tukidila ku luyandiku lwa tsi. Kaasi buthwena, thwenina ku tsuka ya tangwa, kálubuka mbala ya yimosi lwesi mu kukumuna disumu muna nzila ya kimenga kina kaditambiki yandi meni.
HEB 9:27 Amana bwosu bwátangamina kwena batu mu kufwa mbala yimosi lwesi, ku manima hanana yakwisa pfundusu ya Nzambi,
HEB 9:28 yi bwabuna phi, Kidisitu káditambikila mu kimenga mbala ya yimosi, ndangu kakumuna masumu ma lawu dya batu. Kamónika hika mu mbala ya zodi, ka mu kikuma ku hika kya kutala mambu ma masumu, kaasi kikuma kya babana bisi muhingila kikuma kya kubonga luhulusu.
HEB 10:1 Mitsiku mya Moyize myenina lwesi kifwani kya bima bina byakwísa; kaasi myeku kininga kya mukwandi kya mambu meni mamana. Yi hakana milungiku mu kutomisa batu babana bisi bwesuka kwena Nzambi mu nzila ya bimenga meni byabina bisi landulula kosu mvula.
HEB 10:2 Wadi ni babana bisi sambila Nzambi yi kutambikaka bima bya mutindu wuna basemaka muna mbala yimosi lwesi ku mitsoki mya bawu, wadi bisiku kala yi katsasa ka disumu.
HEB 10:3 Kinga, muna bimenga meni byabina, batu bisi yubuka masumu ma bawu mvula muna mvula.
HEB 10:4 Mukuma bwalendakanaku ku menga ma miluma mya bangombi yi ma miluma mya bakhombu mu kukatula masumu.
HEB 10:5 Yi hakana ni Kidisitu, mu kukota muna tsi, kázimbula: «Keti kimenga, keti mulambu, wázolabyoku. Kinga wángidika lutu.
HEB 10:6 Keti kimenga kya kuyoka kya muthu, keti bimenga kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu; byosu, wázolabyoku.
HEB 10:7 Yihanga nzimbudini: "Awu meni, mukuma, kikuma kya meni básonikina muna mukanda wa kuvunga: yisini, oh Nzambi mu kuhanga luzolu lwaku.»
HEB 10:8 Wuzimbudi theti: «Wázolaku keti kimenga kya kuyoka kya muthu, keti milambu mya kuyoka, keti bibulu bya kuyoka ha mutalaka, keti bimenga bya ndoluka ya masumu, keti kimosi wásephilaku kyawu muna byosu.» Kinga makabu mamana moosu bisima tambika bwosu buna myenina mitsiku.
HEB 10:9 Hanga wukosikidi: «Awu meni, yisini mu kuhanga luzolu lwaku.» Muna bwabuna, Kidisitu wákumuna mutindu wa theti wa kubwesuka kwena Nzambi amana wáhingisiwa ku mutindu wuna wa zodi.
HEB 10:10 Muna luzolu lwaluna, mwamuna twátomina betu muna nzila ya kimenga kya lutu lwandi luna kátambika mu mbala mosi.
HEB 10:11 Kaasi nganga-Nzambi wosu kosu kilumbu kisi telama kikuma kya kusala kisalu kyandi; kisi tambika kosu tangwa bimenga byabina, bina bifwaniku mu kukatula masumu.
HEB 10:12 Kaasi Kidisitu, yandi, kátambika kimenga kimosi lwesi kikuma kya masumu, amana kuna koku dya kitata dya Nzambi, kisi zakadila mvula muna mvula.
HEB 10:13 Buthwena, kwakuna kabati hingidila ni Nzambi kabakitula bambeni bandi kidyatilu kya yandi.
HEB 10:14 Amana, muna mulambu wumosi lwesi, mwamuna kábalungisila, mvula muna mvula, batu babana kátomisa.
HEB 10:15 Bwabuna Kitembu Kyatoma phi kabati tutila kimbangi. Mukuma, kazimbudi theti:
HEB 10:16 «Talenu bulunda buna yita yi bawu ku manima ma bilumbu byabina, kazimbudini Pfumu: Yisónika mitsiku myama muna mbundu ya bawu, yinámikamya muna kitembu kya bawu.»
HEB 10:17 Amana wukosikidini: «Yisúngulaku hika masumu ma bawu yi mitsoki mya bawu.»
HEB 10:18 Kinga, ho masumu maloluki kedi, kweku hika yi bimenga kikuma kya masumu.
HEB 10:19 Bwabuna, baphangi, thwekina yi muswa wa kukotila muna kizika kyahedila lawu, muna nzila ya menga ma Yesu.
HEB 10:20 Yesu wátuyafwadila nzila ya pha yi ya moya; yandi meni wátekila lutila mwamuna: muna nzila ya kibwiku kina kya mu nzu ya Nzambi ya Bayuta, disongila muna nzila ya lutu lwa yandi meni.
HEB 10:21 Amana thwenina yi Mbuta-Nganga mosi wuna básikununa mbuta wa nzu ya Nzambi.
HEB 10:22 Disongidila ni tubwesukenu kwena Nzambi yi mbundu ya kyedika yi lukwikilu luna lwa mukwandi, mbundu ya kasemi ku byosu byisi hana katsatsa ka mbi yi lutu lwa kuyebisa yi mamba ma kukenza.
HEB 10:23 Tusimbidilenu ngolu kivuvu kyetu kina thwisi samuna, mukuma Nzambi kisi hwila mwani ku bilangi byandi.
HEB 10:24 Tukalenu yi kitsungila betu yi betu kikuma kya kudihekaka kikesa ku zola yi mihangu mya bukheti.
HEB 10:25 Tutinaku mabundu metu bwosu báyikanabwa batu bahika, kaasi tudihekakenu kikesa betu yi betu, bwosu tubati mona kilumbu kya Pfumu kibwesukini.
HEB 10:26 Mukuma ho thwisi hola masumu mu luzolu ku manima ma kubonga nzayilu ya kyedika, kweku hika kimenga kikuma kya masumu.
HEB 10:27 Kaasi henina yi pfundusu ya Nzambi yi ngolu za mbawu yina yayóka bandwandwa.
HEB 10:28 Wosu wuna wakúlula mitsiku mya Moyize kafwa konda kumuyukila kheni, mu kimbangi kya batu boodi kondi lo batatu.
HEB 10:29 Khi mutindu wa ndola kabónga yanduna waléwula Mwana wa Nzambi? Wuna wasáwula menga ma bulunda, muna mamana bámutomisina? Yi wuna watúkwana Kitembu wa khenda? Banzenu khi lawu dya lombu kakúkula!
HEB 10:30 Mukuma, tuzayi ni yanduna wuna wázimbula: «Meni yivútula mbela, meni yisi futa kwena mutu wosu bwosu byenina bisalu byandi.» Amana kázimbula hika: «Pfumu kafúndisa kanda dyandi.»
HEB 10:31 Keba, wakúluka, ho ni wabwa mu moku ma Nzambi wa moya!
HEB 10:32 Yubukenuti bilumbu bya theti bina, ku manima ma kubonga mwini wa Nzambi: lwázyandama muzingu wuna wa mbuta yi wa phasi.
HEB 10:33 Matangwa mahika, lwákwatuka tsoni ku ngusi yi minyanga ha mesu ma batu boosu. Matangwa mahika, bakala luwaphama kwena batu bahika babana bátekila mona phasi meni zina.
HEB 10:34 Lwákota mu boloku hanga lutambwasini yi kyesi kya kulubotula bima, kikuma luzayi ni lwenina yi kuvwa kwa bukheti kuna kwa mvula yi mvula.
HEB 10:35 Kaasi lutotisaku kikumbwala kyenu: kina kyenina yi lufutu lumosi lwa mbuta.
HEB 10:36 Kaasi lwenina yi mupfunu wa kikwamina, ndangu ku nima dya kulungisa luzolu lwa Nzambi, lwabonga kina kásila.
HEB 10:37 Mukuma, bwásonama: «Muna tangwa dya khunda, dya khunda hika, amana yandi wuna wulungini mu kukwisa, kakwísa; amana kazingidilaku.
HEB 10:38 Kinga, Nzambi kazimbudini, mutu wa masonga ku mesu ma meni, mu lukwikilu kazíngila, kaasi ho kavutuka ku manima, yikálaku yi tsambu ya yandi.»
HEB 10:39 Betu, thweku batu babana bisi vutuka ku manima balenga ditotisa. Betu thwenina batu ba lukwikilu kikuma kya kuhulula moya myetu.
HEB 11:1 Kinga lukwikilu, lwenina kikumbwala mu kubonga kedi kina bisi sila kivuvu, kyenina kusya mbundu muna bima bina byisiku monika hangambedi ni hana byenina.
HEB 11:2 Kikuma kya lukwikilu Nzambi kábatambwasila bambuta bakhulu.
HEB 11:3 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, tubati kwikila ni tsi yáhangamina ku ndinga ya Nzambi, mu phila ni tsi yayi yisi monika kisina kya yawu ka byabi ku thwisi mona.
HEB 11:4 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Abelu kátambikila mukhayilu wa lukumu lwa lawu kwena Nzambi, kuhita wuna wa Khayina. Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Nzambi wámutila kimbangi ni mutu wa masonga kákala, kikuma yandi meni Nzambi wátambwasa makabu mandi. Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Abelu kisi zonza hika mbata nana kenina wafwa.
HEB 11:5 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Noki bámunata kwena Nzambi konda kafwa. Keti mutu kámumonaku, kikuma Nzambi wámunata kwena yandi meni. Masonuku mazimbudi ni ku thwala ya kumutombula, bámutila kimbangi ni Nzambi kásephidisa.
HEB 11:6 Kinga, konda lukwikilu, ka mutu ku wasephidisa Nzambi. Kikuma, wuna wisi khundakana kwena Nzambi kafweti kwikila ni Nzambi kenina amana kisi bafuta babana bisi musanda.
HEB 11:7 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, káyukila Nowa, ngwisi za Nzambi kikuma kya mambu mamana máfwana mu kusalama kaasi khaniku kedi masalama. Kálewulazoku ngwisi zazina amana wátunga nzasa ndangu kahulwasila nzu yandi. Muna bwabuna kázengila mukanu wa batu ba tsi amana wámutambwasa hanga mutu mosi wa masonga Nzambi wámutambwasa kikuma kya lukwikilu lwandi.
HEB 11:8 Mu nzila ya lukwikilu, Bulahami kálemvwakila ku mbila ya Nzambi: wátambwasa mu kukwenda ku tsi yina kakhana muheka Nzambi. Mbatanana kákonda zaya kuna kakala kwenda.
HEB 11:9 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, kázingila hanga munzenza mosi muna tsi yayina kámusila Nzambi kilangi. Kakala nangina muna masombolu, yi Yizaki yi Yakobi bawu bátambula kilangi kimosi kya Nzambi.
HEB 11:10 Mukuma Bulahami kakala hingila mbanza yina yenina yi mipfundila mya ngolu, yayina káyidika, kátunga phi yandi meni Nzambi.
HEB 11:11 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu Sala, yandi phi mbatanana bukhobu bwandi yi kinunu kyandi, kábongila hamu dya kubuta bana. Kikuma wásya mbundu ni kilangi kina kásila Nzambi kyakhana lungila.
HEB 11:12 Yi hakana ni kwena mutu mosi lwesi, wákala mununu bela-bela yi kufwa, kwábutukila lawu dya mabutuka hanga bathetimbwa muna zilu yi tsekengi kuna kabeta ka yanga dya mbuta, balendaku mu kutanga.
HEB 11:13 Batu babana boosu muna lukwikilu bámana fwila. Konda kubonga bima bina kásila Nzambi, kaasi bámonabya amana báhekabya mboti muna kyana. Bátambwasa hana mesu ma boosu ni banzenza bákala yi bakangadi ba nzila hana tsi.
HEB 11:14 Mukuma babana bisi zonza bwabuna basongidini wengele ni tsi babati sanda.
HEB 11:15 Wadi ni bakalaka yi dibanza dya kuyananaka tsi yina bálubuka, wadi bakhana mona phila ya kuvutwakilaya.
HEB 11:16 Amana mu masonga, tsi mosi yihitina kitoku bakala sanda, disongila tsi ya ku zilu. Yi hakana ni Nzambi keku yi tsoni za ku mutela Nzambi wa bawu; kikuma, tsi mosi kábayidikila.
HEB 11:17 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Bulahami kátambikila Yizaki mu kimenga tangwa kámusya Nzambi mu kimeka. Mwana wandi mosi kwandi kakhana tambika, mbatanana kákala yi kilangi kya Nzambi
HEB 11:18 wuna wámuzimbwala: «Muna nzila ya Yizaki, mwamuna wávwila butuka dyaku dina yíkusila.»
HEB 11:19 Bulahami kakala banza ni Nzambi kákala yi hamu dya kufutumuna mvumbi, yi hakana kámuvutwala yandi Mwana hanga mbedi ni kidimbu kya lufutumuku kákala.
HEB 11:20 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna Yizaki kásakwamina Yakobi yi Kizawu kikuma kya mambu ma bawu mana mákwisa.
HEB 11:21 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Yakobi mu tangwa dya kufwa, kásakwamina kosu mwana wa Yozefu, amana wázyaminina kuna tsongi ya koka dyandi mu kufukamina Nzambi.
HEB 11:22 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Yozefu, ha kátula mu kufwa, kásamwana ni bana ba Kiseledi balúbuka ku Ngiphiti amana wáhana muswa mu mana matadidini bifufwa byandi.
HEB 11:23 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna Moyize mu lubutuku lwandi, bámuswekila ngonda tatu kwena bibuti byandi. Mukuma bámona ni mwana wa kitoku kakála, amana báyukaku keti bweya mu kukolama ku mukuku wa kyamvu.
HEB 11:24 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna Moyize, tangwa kákituka mbuta, kábusila ni bamutelakaku mwana wa mwana mukhetu wa Fwalawo.
HEB 11:25 Wátambwasa mu kunyokuka yi kanda dya Nzambi kuluta mu kukala mu tsambu za tangwa dimosi za disumu.
HEB 11:26 Kámona ni kulewuka hanga Masiya kuhiti kimvwama kya mbuta kya Ngiphiti, mukuma mesu mandi mákala ma kutadisa kuna lufutu luna lwakwísa.
HEB 11:27 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, Moyize wákatuka ku Ngiphiti konda kuyuka bweya bwa khabu za kyamvu; wázyama ngolu, hanga mbedi ni kakala mumona Nzambi wuna wisiku monika.
HEB 11:28 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna Moyize kátila mukinzi wa Phaki yi kusophula kwa menga muna mwelu mya nzu, ndangu wanzyo wa lufwa kahondaku bana ba batsomi ba bisi Kiseledi.
HEB 11:29 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna bana ba Kiseledi bálabwakila yanga dya mbuta dya Kabengi hanga mu mafu mamosi máyumuka; kaasi Bisi Ngiphiti ha bámeka mu kulabuka bwabuna meni, mamba mábazyondisa.
HEB 11:30 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna bibaka bya Yediko byáwulumukina, amana bana ba Kiseledi bázyetabya bilumbu tsambwadi.
HEB 11:31 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna Lahabi, ndumba-leta, káfwilaku yi bambeni ba Nzambi, kikuma kya buna kábayamba bukheti ba mbambala ba Kiseledi.
HEB 11:32 Biki hika yizónza? Tangwa dyakhónda mu kuzonzila Zeteyo, Balaki, Samisoni, Zefite, Tavidi, Samwela, yi bambikudi.
HEB 11:33 Kibinga, muna nzila ya lukwikilu, bánungina bipfumu, báhangila masonga amana bábongila bilangi bina kásila Nzambi. Bákasa munwa mya bathambu,
HEB 11:34 bázima mbawu za ngolu, báhuluka ku lufwa lwa mbedi ya phoku. Maladi mábazokisa amana ku nima ngolu zábavutwakila; muna tangwa dya mvita, kikesa kyábavutwakila amana bákukwasa bibuka bya basuta ba banzenza.
HEB 11:35 Muna nzila ya lukwikilu, mwamuna bakhetu bámonina bamvumbi ba bawu mu kufutumuka amana bávutwakila luzingu. Batu bahika bábanyokuna mu kuthaba; kaasi bábwisa mu kubasula, ndangu balenga bonga kutokama kwa bukheti kwa ku lufwa.
HEB 11:36 Batu bahika bákala baseya, bakwawu bákala bazyatula mafimbu, bakwawu hika mu miyololu amana bábatimbula mu boloku.
HEB 11:37 Bahika bábahondila ku matadi, bahika kubabukununa ho lo kubahondila ku mbedi ya phoku. Amana bakwawu hika bakala kwenda homa hamosi yi hakwawu. Bakwawu bakala vwata mikanda mya mikoku kondi lo mya bakhombu hanga miledi. Bakwawu bákala bahwa-dya-hwa. Bakwawu bakala banyokuna yi kubamonisaka minyanga.
HEB 11:38 Bámonika ku mesu ma batu hangambedi ni bakalaku balunga mu kuzingila mu tsi yayi. Bakala ngata muna tseki za khatu yi muna myongu, muna bitadi yi mabulu bakala zingila.
HEB 11:39 Nzambi wábatambwasa boosu kikuma kya lukwikilu lwa bawu; mbatanana bábongabyoku bina kásila Nzambi.
HEB 11:40 Kikuma, Nzambi káyidikila kima kimosi kya mbuta kikuma kya betu. Yi hakana ni byakhanaku lungila kedi konda betu.
HEB 12:1 Kikuma kya betu, bátuzyeta kwena mulumba-lumba wa bambangi. Tulosenu kizitu kyosu kya masumu kina kyisi kakidikisa wenzi wetu, amana tutsyakulenu yi kuna tsuka za thinu zazi batusidini.
HEB 12:2 Mesu metu ma kutadisa kwena Yesu, yandi wenina kisina yi tsuka ya lukwikilu lwetu. Wátambwasa mu kufwa hana kitakani, konda kutala mutindu wa tsoni za lufwa meni lwaluna, kikuma kákala mona mutindu wa kyesi kina kyátangamina kikuma kya yandi. Amana buthwena kuna koku dya kitata dya kiti kya Nzambi kisi zakadila.
HEB 12:3 Banzenu kwena wuna wákwamina ku matendu ma basumuki; ndangu lukatulaku kikesa.
HEB 12:4 Mukuma, muna muzingu wenu wutadidini disumu, khaniku kedi lunwana tii yi kuna lufwa.
HEB 12:5 Luzimbakanaku ndongisila zina káluheka Nzambi hanga kwena bana: «Mwana wama, wulewulaku tsungika ya Pfumu, amana wukatulaku kikesa mu tangwa kabati kukaya.
HEB 12:6 Mukuma Pfumu kisi sungika wuna kisi zola, kisi beta wosu wuna kisi mona hanga mwana wandi.»
HEB 12:7 Tambwasakenu tsungika ya Nzambi, kikuma kisibwa hanga bwosu tata kwena mwana wandi. Khi mwana yandina bisiku beta kwena tata wandi?
HEB 12:8 Ho ni Nzambi kisiku lubeta hanga bana bandi, zonza ni lweku bana bandi ba kubuta, lwenina bana ba makangu.
HEB 12:9 Mukuma thwenina yi batata mu kimutu: bisi tusungika amana twakala balemvukila. Yi hakana twafweti lemvukilaka Tata wetu wa ku zilu, kikuma kya kubonga luzingu kwena yandi.
HEB 12:10 Kaasi batata betu bakala tusungikaka kikuma kya koma ka bilumbu, bwosu buna bámoninabwa bukheti. Kaasi Nzambi kisi tusungika kikuma kya bukheti bwetu, ndangu kalenga tuheka kutoma kwandi.
HEB 12:11 Ha batusungikini, muna tangwa meni dyadina, dyisiku kala dyambu dya kyesi kaasi dya kyadi. Kaasi tsuka tsuka, babana babongini milongi myamina myisi banatina ngemba yi luzingu lwa masonga.
HEB 12:12 Yi hakana ni thutenu moku mamana mazokini, amana zyamisenu makungulu menu mamana mabati tekita!
HEB 12:13 Yidikenu nzila zasungama kikuma kya bitambi byenu, ndangu batu babana bisi tinguna badibunda-bundaku mu bikhosu, kaasi bakola.
HEB 12:14 Sandakenu lwakalaka mu ngemba yi mutu wosu yi mu kudisemisaka; mukuma, konda bwabuna, ka mutu ku wamóna Pfumu.
HEB 12:15 Kebenu ni ka mutu ku kakonda mu kubonga khenda za Nzambi amana ka musodi wumosi ku wa khadi wamena, hanga wadikila nana batu ba lawu.
HEB 12:16 Kebenu mu kusya ni hakalaku yi bita-mbongi hana kati dya benu, zitisenu bima byahedila; luhangabwoku hanga buna káhanga Kizawu, kikuma kya ndya yimosi, wásumbisa kimbuta kyandi kya butuka.
HEB 12:17 Mukuma, luzayibwa ni ku manima, tangwa kázola mu kubonga lusakumunu lwa tata wandi, bámulosila. Kámonaku keti phila ya kusobila mambu, mbatanana nyengi dyandi yi matsanga mandi.
HEB 12:18 Benu tangwa lwábwesuka kwena Nzambi, lwábwesukaku ku mongu wumosi bafwanini mu kusimba, wuna wakala lema mbawu; lwábwesukaku keti ku mudima, keti ku phipha, keti ku pfunzi,
HEB 12:19 keti muhungu wa phungi, keti khololu ya ndinga. Bisi Kiseledi ha báyukaya ndinga meni yayina, bábusa mu kuyuka keti ndinga yimosi hana thandu.
HEB 12:20 Mukuma, bálendaku mu kusipha mulongi meni wawuna: «Yanduna wasímba mongu, keti abweti kenina mbisi, bamúhonda mu kumutimbwala kwa matadi.»
HEB 12:21 Bwákala bweya bwa lawu mu kumona dyambu meni dyadina kázimbula Moyize: «Mbundu yimvumukini yi tsula!»
HEB 12:22 Kaasi benu lwábwesuka ku mongu wa Siyoni yi ku mbanza ya Nzambi wa Moya, Yelusalemi dya ku zilu, mafunda yi mafunda ma banzyo bandi kwakuna benina mu mukinzi.
HEB 12:23 Amana kuna dingumba dya bana batsomi ba Nzambi lwákokuluka, babana básonama mazina ma bawu muna mazilu. Benu lwákokuluka kwena Nzambi zusi wa batu boosu, amana lwákokuluka ku bitembu bya batu basungama babana bákituka batu balunga.
HEB 12:24 Kwena Yesu hika lwákokuluka benu, yandi wenina mukhundingisi wa bulunda bwa pha buna kata Nzambi yi betu, amana menga mandi mana mátekuka misi zonza buna bufwani kuhita menga ma Abelu.
HEB 12:25 Kebenu! Lubusaku mu kuyuka yanduna wisi luzonzisa. Bawu bábusa mu kuyuka wuna wakala baheka ndongisila ha tsi, báhengaku ku ndola ya Nzambi. Twaléndaku mu kuhengaya ho ni betu twámufila kunda yanduna wisi zonza kwena betu muna mazilu.
