HEB 12:26 Ndinga yina kátekila zonza Nzambi yátekitisa mafu; kaasi buthwena Nzambi wutusidi hika kilangi kyakina: «Yitékitisaya hika, ka tsi ku lwesi, kaasi yi zilu phi.»
HEB 12:27 Mihowu myami «mbala yayi hika» mibati songila ni bima bina byáhangama byaníngana amana byazíluka, ndangu byananga lwesi bima bina byisiku ningana.
HEB 12:28 Tukalenu kabanzi, kikuma tubongi luyalu lumosi luna lwisiku ningana. Tusongilenu kabanzi meni kakana mu kusadilaka Nzambi muna mutindu wuna wisi muhekila tsambu, mu luzitu yi kubanga.
HEB 12:29 Mukuma, Nzambi wetu kenina mbawu yina yisi vukula.
HEB 13:1 Yambulenu kiphangi kyazinga hana kati dya benu.
HEB 13:2 Luzimbakanakaku mu kuyambaka babana bisi kwisa ku nzu zenu. Mukuma, henina yi bamosi báhangilabwa kinga báyamba banzyo konda kuzayakabwa.
HEB 13:3 Sungulakenu batu ba boloku, hangambeni ni mu boloku lwenina yi bawu. Sungulakenu batu babana bisi nyokuna, hangambedi ni hakimosi lubati nyokuna bawu.
HEB 13:4 Mutu wosu kazitisalwa longu amana basumunayoku thangi ya longu. Nzambi kafúndisa bita-mbongi yi bakwa kisanda.
HEB 13:5 Ndyatidi yenu yikalaku yi nzoluka ya mbongu; sephilakenu ku bina lwenina byawu, mukuma Nzambi kázimbula bwabu: «Yikúsisaku, yikúlosilaku keti bweti.»
HEB 13:6 Amana ba kabasi yi kikumbwala twalenda mu kuzimbula: «Pfumu kenina lusadisu kikuma kya meni, amana yiyúkaku bweya, Biki kaphánga mutu kwena meni?»
HEB 13:7 Sungulakenu bambuta ba dibundu benu babana bisi lulonga ndinga ya Nzambi. Simbululenu bikalulu bya bawu buna bámanisina luzingu amana sokululenu lukwikilu lwa bawu.
HEB 13:8 Yesu Kidisitu kenina mutindu wumosi, mukolu, lelu yi mvula muna mvula.
HEB 13:9 Lulandakaku malongi moosu ma luvunu: mana mafwananiku yi lukwikilu lwa betu. Bulungi ni mbundu zenu zazyaminaka mu khenda za Nzambi, kaasi ka kikuma kya bizila bya madya ku; bwásadisaku keti babana bisi dyatila muna bwabuna.
HEB 13:10 Betu thwenina yi mesa ma kimenga, amana banganga-Nzambi ba bayuta beku yi muswa wa kudya bina bitukini ku mesa meni mamana. Mukuma, bawu, mu sombolu bisi sambila bisambu.
HEB 13:11 Mwamuna, mbuta-nganga kisi nata menga ma bambisi muna kizika kyahedila lawu kikuma kya kukatula disumu, amana misuni mya bambisi meni babana ku phenza ya mbanza bisimya yokila.
HEB 13:12 Yi hakana Yesu, yandi phi, káfwila ku phenza ya mbanza, kikuma kya kusemisa batu ku masumu ma bawu yi menga ma yandi meni kibeni.
HEB 13:13 Amana tulubukenu twenda tundakana yi yandi kuna phenza ya mbanza, amana twazíta ngusi zazina kitesu kimosi yi yandi.
HEB 13:14 Mukuma, ha tsi haha, thweku keti mbanza yimosi yina yisi zinga mvula muna mvula, kaasi mbanza yimosi tubati sanda yina yakwisa kala ka thama ku.
HEB 13:15 Muna nzila ya Yesu, tulambulenu konda kulembwa kwena Nzambi lukumu lwetu hanga kimenga, disongidila mulambu wuna wisi lubuka muna malebu wisi kumisa zina dyandi.
HEB 13:16 Luzimbakanakaku mu kuhangaka mambu ma bukheti amana disadisakenu muna kiphangi, mukuma byabina yi bimenga byisi musephidisa Nzambi.
HEB 13:17 Lemvukenu kwena bayadi benu amana bayukilakenu. Kikuma bawu bisi tadikina moya myenu kosu tangwa, zayenu ni yi bawu bisi luhanina meni kwena Nzambi. Hangakenu mu kusya ni balungisa kiyeka kya bawu mu kyesi konda nyengi, kondi loni bwabuna bwalúkadilaku keti muluta.
HEB 13:18 Sambilakenu kikuma kya betu. Kikuma tusini mbundu mu kukala yi katsatsa ka bukheti, mukuma thwisi zola ni twazingilaka bukheti muna mambu moosu.
HEB 13:19 Amana hika, yilubokwadidi mu kulombila ndangu Nzambi kakhángwala nzila mu kuvutuka yi tswatsu kwena benu.
HEB 13:20 Yambula Nzambi wa ngemba, wuna wátokamisa ha kati dya bafwa, kalema wa mbuta wa mikoku, Pfumu wetu Yesu; muna nzila ya menga ma bulunda bwa mvula yi mvula,
HEB 13:21 kalulonga mu kuhanga mambu mamana menina ma bukheti mu kuhanga luzolu lwandi. Katuhangila buna bumuyenina bwa bukheti muna nzila ya Yesu Kidisitu, khembu yakala kwena yandi muna mvula yi mvula! Abwabuna.
HEB 13:22 Mbati lusyamisa, baphangi: tambwasenu ndinga ya kikesa yayi yi sipha dya mbundu. Kikuma mu khufi yilusonikini.
HEB 13:23 Zayenu ni phangi wetu Thimoti wulubukikini mu boloku. Ho ni katula mwa tswatsu, nzila yimosi yikwéndayandi mu kulumona.
HEB 13:24 Bahekenu mboti basadi benu boosu yi bakwikidi boosu. Baphangi ba ku tsi yina bisi tela ni Kitadi mboti baluhekini.
HEB 13:25 Yambula khenda za Nzambi zakala yi benu boosu!
JAM 1:1 Meni Zyaki, musadi wa Nzambi yi wa Pfumu Yesu Kidisitu. Mboti zama kwena makanda kumi yi modi mámwangana muna tsi yamuthu.
JAM 1:2 Baphangi bama, ha lutundakanini phasi za mutindu wosu kikuma kya lukwikilu, kalenu mu kyesi kya lawu.
JAM 1:3 Mukuma, luzayibwa ni yuka lukwikilu lwenu lwakala lwazyama muna tangwa dya phasi, lwisi lumbula kikwamina.
JAM 1:4 Kinga bulungini ni kikwamina kyenu kyazyama yi kuna tsuka, ndangu lwakala bakodidila, bafwana muna mambu moosu amana bakonda kifu.
JAM 1:5 Amana ho mosi wa benu kakonda nduka, kalombaza kwena Nzambi. Yandi kamúhekaza; mukuma Nzambi kisi hana yi kyesi kwena boosu konda mulandu, amana zamúhanamina.
JAM 1:6 Kaasi bulungini kalombaza yi lukwikilu, konda kuketyanisa; mukuma mutu wuna wisi ketyanisa wufwanani yi mahuwa ma yanga dya mbuta mamana kisi hulumuna pfunzi amana wuhungudima ku kabeta kahika.
JAM 1:7 Mutu yanduna kadifwataku ni kima kabónga kitukini kwena Pfumu.
JAM 1:8 Kenina mutu mosi wa mbundu zodi amana keku yi kwatakani muna mambu mana kisi hanga.
JAM 1:9 Amana Phangi wuna wa luzingu lwa mu sina kaditsikisila muna bina kamútombwala Nzambi.
JAM 1:10 Amana mvwama kaditsikisila muna bina kamúkulwamina Nzambi. Mukuma mvwama kalúta hanga kifulu kya khangu.
JAM 1:11 Ha kalúbuka tangwa, mwini wandi balabala wayúmwasa khangu; kifulu kyandi kibwini amana phisi yandi yihwini. Bwabuna katóta mvwama hana kati dya bisalu byandi.
JAM 1:12 Kyesi kwena mutu wuna wisi zita mu kimeka; mukuma ku manima ma kusongila kuzyama kwandi mu kimenga, kabónga mukhonzi wa luzingu luna kásila kwena babana bisi muzola.
JAM 1:13 Ka mutu ku ho ni kahukumukini, kazimbula: «Nzambi yandina wuphukumunini.» Mukuma Nzambi fwaniku bamuhukumuna, amana yandi-meni phi kisiku bwisa mutu mu phukumunu.
JAM 1:14 Kaasi, kosu mutu, yandi meni wisi dibwisa mu phukumunu muna tsambu zandi za mbi, zisi mulundika amana zisi mukwatisa ha mutambu;
JAM 1:15 ku manima, tsambu ya mbi yosu yisi kodidila amana yibuti disumu; amana disumu ha dikodidini dyosu, dibuti lufwa.
JAM 1:16 Ludizimbikisaku, baphangi bama batondama:
JAM 1:17 mambu moosu ma bukheti yi kabu dyosu dina dyalungila, byisi tuyisila tukidila ku zilu. Byabina, kwena Nzambi byisi tuka, yandi wuna wenina Tata wa mwini, yandi wuna kisiku soba hanga buna kyisi soba kivula ku matangwa.
JAM 1:18 Kikuma, Nzambi muna luzolu lwa yandi meni kátubutila muna nzila ya Ndinga ya masonga, ndangu twakala muna ndonga ya theti ya bihangwa byandi byosu.
JAM 1:19 Zayenu, baphangi bama batondama: kosu mutu kakala tswatsu mu kuhinikina, kaasi malembi mu kuzonza, malembi phi mu kuyuka khabu.
JAM 1:20 Mukuma mutu wuna wenina mu khabu kahángaku mambu ma masonga ku mesu ma Nzambi.
JAM 1:21 Yi hakana, losenu mvindu yosu yi khu yosu yina yihitakani. Tambwasenu, yi kudikulumuna, ndinga yina kakunini Nzambi muna mbundu zenu wufwanini mu kuluhulula.
JAM 1:22 Kitukenu basadi ba ndinga buna bufwanini, kaasi lukalaku bahinikini lwesi mu kudihunaka benu benu.
JAM 1:23 Mukuma mutu wuna wisi hinikina ndinga konda kusadilaya wufwananini hanga mutu wuna wubati simbulula, ku kiphelu, mbunzu yandi yina kábutwakila.
JAM 1:24 Ku manima ma kudisimbulula, wendi kwandi amana muna mbala mosi, wuzimbakani buna kakadini.
JAM 1:25 Kaasi wuna wisi yekamina ku mitsiku myalungila, myamina myisi kutumuna, kisi hwila mwani mu kudihanaka kuna mitsiku meni myamina; kisi hinikina ndinga, kisiku zimbakanaya amana kisi hanga bwabuna bulombini mutsiku. Mutu yanduna kyesi kakála kyawu muna mambu mamana kisi hanga.
JAM 1:26 Ho mutu wisi dibanzila muna mbundu ni musambidi kenina amana kazayiku kusimbulula lulaka lwandi, kaasi kisi dihuna yandi-meni: bisambu byandi bya khatu.
JAM 1:27 Bisambu byenina bya kasemi amana byakonda mvindu ku mesu ma Nzambi, Tata, byabina byisi kinda bana ba batsona yi bafwidi muna kiwayi kya bawu, yi mu kudikenga konda kifu ku bima bya tsi.
JAM 2:1 Baphangi bama, benu lwákwikila mwena Pfumu wetu Yesu Kidisitu, yandi wabasa yi khembu, luhangilakaku batu kayengu.
JAM 2:2 Mu mbandu: ho mwisa kota mutu mosi muna dingumba dyenu, wavwata ndamba yimosi ya wolu muna mulembu yi miledi misi kedyamina; amana mwisa kota phi muwayi mosi mu masengi;
JAM 2:3 ho luhungwadini mesu kwena yanduna wuvwatikini miledi myisi kedyamina amana lumuzimbwadini: «Ngeyi sikuka haka, homa ha lukumu!» Kaasi lwisi zimbula kwena muwayi: «Ngeyi, kala kwaku wa mutendendi, kondi loni sikuka kwaku haha, hana tsi, ha malu ma meni.»
JAM 2:4 Yuka ni bwabuna dyenina, lwisi swasisa mambu ha kati dya benu amana lukituki bazusi ba mabanza ma mbi.
JAM 2:5 Hinikinenu, baphangi bama batondama: Nzambi wásola bawayi ku mesu ma batu ba tsi ndangu bakituka bamvwama muna lukwikilu yi baswana ba mambu ma Kipfumu kyakina kásila kwena babana bisi tonda.
JAM 2:6 Kaasi benu, lwisi lewula muwayi! Kinga bamvwama bisi lutusuna amana balubulumuni ku mesu ma bazusi, kabwaku?
JAM 2:7 Aketi yi bawu bisi lewula zina dya bukheti dina lwisi sungamina.
JAM 2:8 Ho mu kyedika, lwisi lungisa mutsiku wa Kipfumu, bwosu buna mazimbudi Masonuku: «Wazóla khunda waku hanga ngeyi-meni, bukheti lwisi hanga.»
JAM 2:9 Kaasi ho lwasongilaka kayengu, luhodi disumu amana mutsiku wulufundisini hanga bakuludi ba mutsiku.
JAM 2:10 Mukuma mutu wuna wisi landa mitsiku myosu kaasi ho kadikhukula ku dyambu dimosi lwesi, wekina mukuludi wa mitsiku myosu.
JAM 2:11 Mukuma, Nzambi kázimbula: «Wukalaku muta mbongi», kázimbula phi: «Wuhondaku mutu.» Amana ho weku kwaku muta mbongi kaasi ho wuhondi mutu, hana wekina mukuludi wa mitsiku.
JAM 2:12 Zonzakenu amana zingakenu hanga batu babana bátangama mu kufundisama bwosu bwenina muna mutsiku wuna wisi kutumuna.
JAM 2:13 Mukuma, mu kilumbu kya pfundusu, Nzambi kakálaku yi kheni kikuma kya babana báyukilaku bakwawu kheni. Kaasi kheni yisi nunga ku pfundusu.
JAM 2:14 Baphangi bama, khi mupfunu kwena mutu mu kuzimbula: «Yenina yi lukwikilu», ho kasongidilwoku mu mihangu? Kyedika lukwikilu lwaluna lwalenda mu kumuhulula?
JAM 2:15 Ho phangi mosi wa yakala kondi loni phangi wa mukhetu wukondi muledi wa kuvwata keti madya ma kosu kilumbu;
JAM 2:16 amana ho mosi hana kati dya benu kabazimbwala: «Alwendenu mu ngemba, lungwalenu amana dyenu lwayukuta!» Konda kubaheka bina bibafwani kikuma kya lutu, khi wawu si mupfunu?
JAM 2:17 Kitesu kimosi phi yi lukwikilu: ho lumonikiku muna mihangu, lwenina kwalwawu lwafwa lwosu.
JAM 2:18 Kaasi, ho mutu kazimbula: «Ngeyi wenina yi lukwikilu, meni yenina yi mihangu. Tsongileti lukwikilu lwaku konda mihangu! Amana meni yimúsongila lukwikilu lwama muna mihangu.»
JAM 2:19 Wisi kwikila ni Nzambi mosi lwesi kenina? Nunga kwaku. Bitembu bya mbi byisi kwikilabwa phi amana byisi tekita yi bweya.
JAM 2:20 Ngata! Amana wuzodini wazaya, ni lukwikilu lukondini mihangu lweku mupfunu?
JAM 2:21 Bulahami tata wetu, abweti bámutambwasila hanga mutu wa masonga: ka kikuma kya mihangu myandi ku, ha kátambika mwana wandi Yizaki hana mesa ma kimenga?
JAM 2:22 Wumoni ni lukwikilu lwakala monika muna mihangu myandi: amana muna nzila ya mihangu myamina lukwikilu lwandi lwálungila lwosu.
JAM 2:23 Amana yi bwabuna málungidila mana mazimbudi Masonuku: «Bulahami kákwikila mwena Nzambi, amana Nzambi wámunungisa hanga mutu wa masonga.» Ku manima bámutela ni nduku wa Nzambi.
JAM 2:24 Lumonibwa ni, mutu mu nzila ya mihangu, kisi tangamina hanga mutu wa masonga kwena Nzambi; heku ni kikuma kya lukwikilu lwesi.
JAM 2:25 Phila mosi phi kikuma kya Lahabi ndumba-leta: muna nzila ya mihangu Nzambi kámutambwasila hanga mutu wa masonga. Mukuma wáyamba bambambala ba kanda dya Kiseledi amana wábatinisina mu nzila yimosi ya hika.
JAM 2:26 Kikuma, phila mosi, konda lwanda lwa moya, lutu lwenina lwafwa, phila mosi phi, konda mihangu, lukwikilu lwenina lwafwa.
JAM 3:1 Baphangi bama, ludikitulaku benu boosu balongi, mukuma zayenubwoku ni batúfundisa buna bwenina kuhita batu bahika.
JAM 3:2 Thwisi dikhukula lawu betu boosu mu mitindu mya lawu, ho mutu wudikhukudiku mu lulaka, kenina mutu mosi walunga, wafwana mu kuzita lutu lwandi lwosu.
JAM 3:3 Amana ho tubati kasa munwa mya baphunda kikuma kya kutulemvwakila, tubati natisa phi lutu lwa bawu lwosu.
JAM 3:4 Talenu phi masuwa: musyetebengi nana menina, pfunzi nana ya ngolu, ku phaka-phaka ya khunda bisima yendisila, misi kwenda kuna dyenina sunga dya muyendisi.
JAM 3:5 Phila mosi, bwosu lwenina lulaka ndambu yimosi ya khunda ya lutu, kaasi mambu ma mbuta lwisi hanga. Talenu kukeya kwa mbawu, kaasi yisi yoka musitu wumosi wa mbuta.
JAM 3:6 Kinga, lulaka lwenina mutindu wumosi yi mbawu. Lwenina tsi ya mambu ma mbi, ndambu yimosi ya lutu lwetu, lwisi zanga lutu lwosu. Lulaka lwisi yoka luzingu lwetu, tukidila ku lubutuku tii yi kuna lufwa; mbawu meni yayina ku bilungi yisi tuka.
JAM 3:7 Mutu kalenda mu kulemvula mutindu wosu wa bambisi, ba musitu, banuni, bambisi babana bisi landanda yi bambisi ba mu mamba.
JAM 3:8 Kaasi keti mutu heku walenda mu kulemvula lulaka: lwisiku lembwa kosu tangwa yi mambu mambi, lwabasa yi ndikila yina yisi honda.
JAM 3:9 Thwisilwa sadila lulaka kikuma kya kukumisina Pfumu, Tata wetu; amana phi yi lulaka meni, lwaluna thwisi singila batu babana benina mu kifwani kya Nzambi.
JAM 3:10 Muna munwa wumosi mwisi lubuka lusakumunu yi masingu. Baphangi, bufwaniku bwabuna bwakala.
JAM 3:11 Kweku tho yimosi yifwanini kulubula mamba ma tuluu yi mamba ma khadi muna mudidi wumosi.
JAM 3:12 Baphangi, kweku keti miti wa fiki wumosi wufwanini mu kuha bibundu bya Olive, kweku keti vinu dimosi difwanini mu kuha bibundu bya fiki. Kitesu kimosi, tho yimosi yalubulaku mamba ma mungwa yi mana ma tulu.
JAM 3:13 Nati wenina nduka yi ngangu hana kati kya benu? Kasongilabwa muna kikalulu kyandi kya bukheti, muna mihangu, muna kudikulumuna yi muna nduka.
JAM 3:14 Kaasi ho lwakala muna mbundu zenu yi kiphala kimosi kya mbi, yi kitembu kya kudimonikisa; luditombulaku ni nduka lwenina, luhunaku ni bukamvi bwenu bwenina kyedika!
JAM 3:15 Nduka za bwabuna zisiku tuka ku zilu; kaasi nduka za ha tsi, za kimutu amana za kiphidi-mutu.
JAM 3:16 Kikuma hakana henina kiphala yi kitembu kya kudimonikisa, henina phi yi mvwalangani yi mihangu mya mbi myosu.
JAM 3:17 Kaasi nduka za ku zilu zisi kala theti za kasemi, kunima zisi nata ngemba, zisi kala talala amana zisi khundikisa, za kabasi mu kiwayi yi mu mihangu mya bukheti; zeku kayengu yi kavungalosi.
JAM 3:18 Kibundu kya masonga muna ngemba bisikya kunina kwena babana bisi hanga mihangu mya ngemba.
JAM 4:1 Ku biki kwisi tuka ngyuma yi mvita hana kati kya benu? Aketi kuna tsambu zenu zazina zisi nwana muna mbundu yenu.
JAM 4:2 Lwisi neka kaasi lwisiku bonga; lwenina bahondi amana lwabasa yi kiphala, yi hakana lwisiku bongila; ludikotisi mu ngyuma yi mu mvita. Lweku yi bina lwisi zoluka, kikuma lwisibyoku lomba kwena Nzambi.
JAM 4:3 Ho lwisi lomba, lwisiku bonga, kikuma sunga dyenu dya mbi; lwisi lomba lwesi kikuma kya kusephidisa tsambu zenu za mbi.
JAM 4:4 Bita-mbongi! Luzayiku ni kukala yi zola dya mambu ma tsi, kukituka mbeni wa Nzambi? Yanduna wuzodini mu kukala nduku wa tsi wudikitudi mbeni wa Nzambi.
JAM 4:5 Kondi loni, zayenu ni Masonuku mazonzidiku mu phamba: «Nzambi kisi sangwala yi tsambu ya lawu mu Kitembu wuna kasya mwena betu.»
JAM 4:6 Kaasi khenda zina kisi tuheka za lawu hika zenina, mukuma Masonuku mazimbudini: «Nzambi kisi kakidila bakwa lulendu, kaasi kisi hana khenda kwena batu badikulumuna.»
JAM 4:7 Lemvukilenu Nzambi; kaasi muzyandaminenu kiphidi-mutu amana kalútina kyana.
JAM 4:8 Kokulukenu kwena Nzambi amana yandi kakókuluka kwena benu. Benu basumuki, semisenu moku menu; amana benu batu ba keti-keti, semisenu mbundu zenu!
JAM 4:9 Bakisenu buwayi bwenu, syenu khondu, dilenu amana kolulukenu; kiseyu kyenu kyakituka mu kitsanga, amana kyesi kyenu mu kiwayi.
JAM 4:10 Dikulumunenu ku mesu ma Pfumu amana kalútombula.
JAM 4:11 Baphangi, lukumbakaku bakwenu. Yanduna wisi zonzila mukwawu phangi mu mbi, wukituki zusi wandi amana wukituki phi zusi wa mitsiku. Muna bwabuna, wudikitudi zusi wa mitsiku hana bulungini mu kusadilamya.
JAM 4:12 Kinga, Nzambi lwesi wisi hana mitsiku, yandi phi wisimya fundisa; yandi wuna fwanini mu kuhulula yi kutotisa. Amana ngeyi nati wenina mu kufundisaka mukwenu?
JAM 4:13 Ngyukenu benu lwisi zimbula: «Lelu kondi loni mbasi twakwénda ku mbanza yimosi, twanángakwa kwakuna mvula mosi, twata kikhita amana twavwa mbongu.»
JAM 4:14 Benu batu luzayiku mambu ma kilumbu kya mbasi luzingu lwenu keti abweti lwakála! Kikuma, lwenina hanga mbuki yina yisi lubuka kikuma kya koma ka tangwa kumanima yitotini!
JAM 4:15 Bulungini ni lwazimbulaka: «Ho Pfumu kazolabwa, twazínga amana twahánga kyaki kondi loni kina.»
JAM 4:16 Kaasi mu kuzonza kwa bukheti, lwisi ditsikisila muna ndinga zenu za bukamvi. Lulendu lwosu lwa mutindu wawuna lwenina lwa mbi.
JAM 4:17 Ho mutu wuzayi kuhanga mambu ma bukheti, amana kahangimoku; wuhodi masumu.
JAM 5:1 Kwena benu bamvwama, ngyukenu buthwena! Dilenu amana kolulukenu kikuma kya biwayi byabina byalúyisila hana thandu ya benu!
JAM 5:2 Kimvwama kyenu kivundini amana miledi myenu mimani yatuka kwena bathaka.
JAM 5:3 Wolu dyenu yi mbongu zenu zihangi mboku, mboku ya byawu yakála kimbangi kikuma kya benu; Yavúkula misuni myenu hanga mbawu. Lulumbikiki bima bya thalu ku tsuka ya tangwa!
JAM 5:4 Taleti lubwisi mu kufuta lufutu lwa basadi babana bákatula mbongu muna bilanga byenu. Nyengi dya bawu yi kiwolu kya bawu biyukalakani tii yi muna matu ma Nzambi, Pfumu mukwa ngolu zoosu.
JAM 5:5 Muna luzingu lwenu lwa ha tsi, lwázingila muna muzandu yi muna tsambu. Lwakala disa bukheti lutu lwenu, luyukutini hanga bibulu bina bisi disa kikuma kya kilumbu kya kubahonda.
JAM 5:6 Lwázengila ndola amana lwáhondisa mutu wa masonga; kázyandamaku.
JAM 5:7 Baphangi disongidila, siphenu mbundu tii yi kuna ngisa ya Pfumu. Talenu mukuni wa kilanga, kisi sipha mbundu mu kuhingila tii yi kuna kanonina bibundu bya bukheti byabina byalúbuka mu mafu: yandika bina bya ndendi yi kuna bina byakódidila.
JAM 5:8 Siphenu mbundu, benu phi, zyamisenu mbundu zenu, mukuma ngisa ya Pfumu yibwesukini.
JAM 5:9 Lunyengalakanakaku kikuma kya bakwenu, baphangi, ndangu Nzambi kalufundisaku. Talenu yandi zusi, awuna muna mwelu watelama!
JAM 5:10 Muna mambu matadidini munyanga yi sipha dya mbundu, baphangi, bongenu mbandu ya bambikudi bázonzila mu zina dya Pfumu.
JAM 5:11 Talenu, tusamunini kyesi kwena batu babana bákwamina. Lwayukini buna bisi zonzila kikwamina kya Yobi, amana luzayini bina kámuheka Pfumu kuna tsuka. Mukuma, Pfumu wa kabasi mu khenda yi mukwa buweti.
JAM 5:12 Theti, baphangi bama, ludyaku ndefi: keti muna zilu, keti muna mafu, keti muna mutindu wahika. Ni «Eeh» dyenu dyakala eeh, amana «loni» dyenu dyakala loni, ndangu lubwaku mu pfundusu ya Nzambi.
JAM 5:13 Mosi hana kati dya benu wenina mu munyanga? Kasambila. Mutu wenina mu kyesi? Kayimbila mikunga mya lukumu.
JAM 5:14 Mutu wenina wabela hana kati dya benu? Katela bambuta ba Dibundu; amana bawu bamúsita masi ku manima basámbila kikuma kya yandi muna zina dya Pfumu.
JAM 5:15 Amana kisambu kya lukwikilu kyahúlula mbefu: Pfumu kamútelamisa, amana ho masumu kahodikini Nzambi kamúlolulama.
JAM 5:16 Fungunakenu masumu menu benu yi benu amana lwadisyaka mu bisambu benu yi benu, ndangu lwalenga kola mu bimbefu byenu. Kisambu kya mutu mosi wa masonga kyenina yi hamu dya lawu.
JAM 5:17 Diya kákala mutu mosi wafwanana mu lutu hanga betu; muna kisambu, wásambila yi hamu mu kusya ni mvula kanokaku, amana kwánokaku mvula mu mafu muna mvula tatu yi ngonda sambanu.
JAM 5:18 Amana phi wisa lombila hika mbala yikwawu; hanga zilu dyánokisa mvula amana mafu málumbula mbutu yandi.
JAM 5:19 Baphangi, honi mutu mosi hana kati dya benu wudizimbikisi nzila, wekina kyana yi masonga, amana phangi mosi wa hika wuna wulendini mu kumuvutula,
JAM 5:20 zayenu ni yanduna wavútula musumuki mosi muna nzila yayina kádizimbikisila, kahúlula moya wa mutu yanduna ku lufwa amana mutu yanduna kahuludini kabónga ndoluka ya masumu mana mahitini kitesu.
1JO 1:1 Mamana mákala tuka ku luyandiku, mamana twáyuka, mamana twámona yi mesu metu, mamana twátala, amana moku metu masimbini; yi yawu Ndinga yisi hana luzingu.
1JO 1:2 Mukuma luzingu meni luna lwámonika, thwisilwa tila kimbangi amana tulusamwanilwa luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula, luna lwakala kwena Tata amana lwisa monika kwena betu
1JO 1:3 mamana twámona yi mamana twáyuka, tulusamwanima benu phi ndangu lwakala phi mu kithwadi yi betu. Kinga kithwadi kyetu kyenina yi Tata amana hakimosi yi Mwana wandi, Yesu Kidisitu.
1JO 1:4 Amana, betu, tusonikima, ndangu kyesi kyetu kyakala kyalungila.
1JO 1:5 Musamu wuna twáyuka kwena yandi amana tulusamwani: Nzambi kenina mwini, amana mwena yandi mwisiku kala keti mudima.
1JO 1:6 Ho twazonza ni twenina mu kithwadi yi yandi, kuna yi kudyatilaka muna mudima, bingumba thwenina amana tusadiku mana menina kyedika.
1JO 1:7 Kaasi yuka ni tubati dyatila mu mwini bwosu kenina yandi meni mu mwini, hana mu kithwadi thwenina betu yi betu, amana menga ma Yesu, Mwana wandi, mabati tusemisa muna masumu moosu.
1JO 1:8 Yuka twazonza ni tweku yi masumu, tutoti betu betu, amana kyedika kyeninamwoku mwena betu.
1JO 1:9 Kaasi yuka ni twafunguna masumu metu, yandi kenina masonga amana walunga: katúlolula masumu amana katúsemisa mu kukonda kwa masonga.
1JO 1:10 Yuka twazonza ni tuhodiku masumu, tumukwati kingumba, amana ndinga yandi yeninamwoku mwena betu.
1JO 2:1 Bana bama, mbati lusonikina bwabuna ndangu lusumukaku. Kaasi yuka ni mutu wusumukini, thwenina yi Nganzi mosi ku mbela ya Tata, Yesu Kidisitu, yandi wenina mukwa masonga.
1JO 2:2 Yandi meni wisa ditambika hanga kimenga kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu metu; ka masumu ma betu lwesi ku, kaasi yi masumu ma tsi yosu.
1JO 2:3 Muna mutindu meni wawuna thwisi muzayila; yuka ni twalundaka mikuku myandi.
1JO 2:4 Yuka mutu kazimbulaka: «Yimuzayini», kaasi kisiku lunda mikuku myandi, kingumba kenina, amana mwena yandi mwakonda kyedika.
1JO 2:5 Kaasi wuna wisi lunda Ndinga yandi, mu kyedika, lungongu lwa Nzambi lwenina mwena yandi. Muna bwabuna, twalenda zayila ni mwena yandi thwenina.
1JO 2:6 Wuna wisi zonza ni mwena yandi kisi nangina, kafweti dyatila bwosu buna kádyatila yandi.
1JO 2:7 Baphangi batondama, heku ni mukuku wa pha yilusonikini, kaasi mukuku wa khulu, wawuna lwátambula tuka mu luyandiku; mukuku meni wawuna wa khulu, wenina ndinga yina lwatekila yuka.
1JO 2:8 Kinga, mukuku wa pha mbati lusonikina; kyedika kina kyenina mwena Yandi, kyenina phi mwena benu. Kikuma, phipha yibati kwenda amana mwini wa kyedika wutwi kedi.
1JO 2:9 Wuna wisi zimbula ni mu mwini kenina kuna yi kumengaka phangi wandi, yanduna, mu phipha kenina.
1JO 2:10 Wuna wisi tonda phangi wandi, mu mwini kisi nangina, amana mwena yandi, mwakonda kisinza kya kubwila.
1JO 2:11 Kaasi wuna wisi menga phangi wandi, yanduna, mu phipha kenina; mu phipha kisi dyatila amana kazayikwoku kuna kisi kwenda kikuma phipha yamufidinga mesu.
1JO 2:12 Mbati lusonikina, bana bama kikuma masumu menu maloluki kikuma kya zina dya Yandi.
1JO 2:13 Mbati lusonikina batata, kikuma lumuzayini wuna wisi kala tuka ku luyandiku. Mbati lusonikina, bandumba yi masanda, kikuma lwámununga kiphidi-mutu.
1JO 2:14 Yilusonikini, bana bama, kikuma lumuzayini Tata. Yilusonikinini, batata, kikuma lumuzayini Wuna wisi kala tuka ku luyandiku. Yilusonikinini bangunza, kikuma lwenina yi ngolu, ndinga ya Nzambi yisi zingila mwena benu amana benu lwámununga kiphidi-mutu.
1JO 2:15 Luzolaku tsi, keti bima bina byenina mu tsi. Yuka ni mutu wisi zola tsi, lungongu lwa Tata lweninamwoku mwena yandi;
1JO 2:16 mukuma, kyosu kina kyenina mu tsi: nzoluka ya lutu, nzoluka ya mesu amana bwabuna nzoluka ya kulumbika bima bya ha tsi. Byabina byosu byisiku tuka kwena Tata, kaasi bima bya ha tsi.
1JO 2:17 Kinga tsi yibati hita, yi nzoluka yandi phi; kaasi wuna wisi hanga luzolu lwa Nzambi kisi zinga mu kimakulu.
1JO 2:18 Bana bama, dyekina tangwa dya tsuka; lwáyuka kuzonzila ni mutendi wa Kidisitu kabati kwisa, amana henina yi lawu dya batendi ba Kidisitu: bwabuna tuzayidi ni dyadi tangwa dya tsuka.
1JO 2:19 Kwena betu bálubwakila, kaasi bákalaku ba betu; mukuma, wadi ni bákala ba betu, wadi bakhana zingila hakimosi yi betu; kaasi muna bwabuna, bubati monika ni ka mosi ku wa bawu wenina wa betu.
1JO 2:20 Benu bátomika kwena Kitembu Kyatoma, benu boosu luzayi.
1JO 2:21 Yuka ni mbati lusonikina, heku ni kikuma luzayiku kyedika, kaasi kikuma luzayikya, kikuma phi kya buna ni ka bukamvi bumosi ku butukini ku kyedika.
1JO 2:22 Amana nati wenina kingumba? Yuka ni ka wuna ku wisi suwangana ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu. Yandi wuna mutendi wa Kidisitu: yandi kisi suwangana, muna mbala mosi, yi Tata yi Mwana.
1JO 2:23 Wosu wuna wamusuwangana Mwana, yandi keku phi yi Tata; wuna wisi tambwasa Mwana kenina phi yi Tata.
1JO 2:24 Kwena benu, yambula mana lwáyuka tuka ku luyandiku mazingila mwena benu. Yuka ni mana lwáyuka tuka ku luyandiku mananginaka mwena benu, lwanángina, benu phi, mwena Mwana yi mwena Tata.
1JO 2:25 Amana kilangi kátusila yandi, kyenina kya luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula.
1JO 2:26 Yilusonikinini bwabuna, kikuma kya mana matadidini batu bana bisi lutotisa.
1JO 2:27 Kwena benu bátomika kwena Kitembu Kyatoma, lweku yi mupfunu ni mutu kalulonga; kaasi bwosu buna Kitembu Kyatoma kálulongila muna mambu moosu, kyedika kálulonga, kálulonga bukamvi. Yi hakana ni hangenu mana kálulonga: nanginakenu hakimosi mwena Yandi.
1JO 2:28 Amana buthwena bwabu, bana bama, nanginakenu hakimosi mwena Kidisitu, ndangu twakala babasa yi kikumbwala tangwa kakwisa monika amana tukwatukaku tsoni ku thwala ya yandi mu kilumbu kya kukwisa kwandi.
1JO 2:29 Yuka lwazaya ni mukwa masonga kenina, zayenu ni wosu wuna wenina yi masonga mwena Nzambi kábutukila.
1JO 3:1 Tala mutindu wa kuzola kuna kátuzola Tata! Lungongu lwandi lwenina muna mutindu wuna bisi tutedila betu bana ba Nzambi. Hahana tsi yikondi tuzayila: Tsi yámuzayaku Nzambi.
1JO 3:2 Banduku bama, buthwena, thwekina bana ba Nzambi, amana buna twakwisa kala khaniku kedi buzayakana; kaasi tuzayi ni kosu tangwa dina kakwisa dimonikisa, twafwánakana yi yandi, kikuma twamúmona bwosu buna kenina.
1JO 3:3 Wosu wuna wasya kivuvu kya mutindu wuna mwena yandi-meni, wudisemisini, bwosu buna kenina yandi-meni wa kasemi.
1JO 3:4 Wosu wuna wisi sumuka, mutsiku kisi tendisa, mukuma disumu dyenina kutendisa mutsiku.
1JO 3:5 Luzayibwa ni Yesu Kidisitu kísila kikuma kya kukatula masumu amana mwena yandi, mwakonda disumu.
1JO 3:6 Yi hakana ni, wosu wuna wanangina mwena yandi kisiku sumuka. Wosu wuna wusumukini, kisi songila ni kámumonaku, kámuzayaku phi.
1JO 3:7 Bana bama, ka mutu ku kalutotisa! Wuna wisi hanga mambu ma masonga kenina yandi meni mukwa masonga, bwosu buna kenina yandi meni Kidisitu mukwa masonga.
1JO 3:8 Wuna wisi landa mu kuhola disumu kenina wa kiphidi-mutu, mukuma kiphidi-mutu wásumuka tuka ku luyandiku. Mwana wa Nzambi kísila lwesi kikuma kya kuzanga mihangu mya kiphidi-mutu.
1JO 3:9 Wosu wuna wábutuka mwena Nzambi wáyambula mu kuhola disumu, mukuma mbutu ya Nzambi yenina mwena yandi; bwosu buna Nzambi kenina Tata wandi, kafwaniku hika ni kasumuka.
1JO 3:10 Tala mana misi baswaswanisa bana ba Nzambi yi bana ba kiphidi-mutu: wosu wuna wisiku hanga mambu ma masonga, kondilo kisiku zola phangi wandi, keku wa Nzambi.
1JO 3:11 Kikuma, tala musamu wuna lwáyuka tuka ku luyandiku: tudizolenu betu yi betu.
1JO 3:12 Tukalaku hanga Kayina: kákala wa kiphidi-mutu amana wáhonda myaki wandi. Amana biki kámuhondila? Kikuma mihangu mya Kayina mbi myákala, kinga mina mya myaki wandi mya masonga myákala.
1JO 3:13 Luyitukaku, baphangi, yuka ni batu ba tsi yayi balumenga.
1JO 3:14 Betu tuzayi ni twáhitila tuka ku lufwa yi kuna luzingu; kikuma thwisi bazola baphangi. Wuna wisiku zola, mu lufwa kisi nangina.
1JO 3:15 Wosu wuna wayúkila phangi wandi kikudi-kudi, yandi kenina mukwa khengu. Kinga luzayibwa ni heku keti mukwa khengu mosi wenina yi kifulu kya kunangina muna luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula mwena yandi-meni.
1JO 3:16 Tala buna thwisi zayila lungongu: Yesu Kidisitu wálambula luzingu lwandi kikuma kya betu. Betu phi, tufweti lambula luzingu lwetu kikuma kya baphangi betu.
1JO 3:17 Yuka ni mutu wenina yi kuvwa kwa ha tsi kamona phangi wandi wuna wenina yi mupfunu wa kima kaasi wumukasidi mbundu, abweti lungongu lwa Nzambi fwani lwanangina mwena yandi?
1JO 3:18 Bana bama, tuzodilaku lwesi ha lebu yi lengu ndinga kaasi mu mihangu yi kyedika.
1JO 3:19 Tala buna twazáyila ni ku kyedika thwisi yekamina. Bwabuna mbundu yetu yalenda diyuka ni yalunga yenina ku thwala ya Nzambi.
1JO 3:20 Kikuma, ata mbundu yetu yituhekini kibela, tuzayini ni Nzambi wa mbuta kenina kuhita mbundu yetu amana yandi wuzayini moosu.
1JO 3:21 Amana banduku bama, yuka ni mbundu yetu yituhekiku kibela, twalenda kala babasa yi kikumbwala ku thwala ya Nzambi.
1JO 3:22 Thwisi tambula kwena yandi byosu bina thwisi lomba, kikuma thwisi lemvuka ku mikuku myandi amana thwisi hanga mana misi musephidisa yandi.
1JO 3:23 Tala mukuku wandi: bulungi twakwikila muna khumbu ya Mwana wandi Yesu Kidisitu amana phi twazolana betu betu, bwosu buna wenina mukuku wandi.
1JO 3:24 Wuna wisi lunda mikuku mya Yandi kisi nangina mu kithwadi yi Nzambi amana yandi Nzambi muna kenina mwena yandi. Tala buna thwisi zayila ni Nzambi muna kenina mwena betu: muna lusadisu lwa Kitembu wuna kátuheka
1JO 4:1 Baphangi batondama, lukwikilakaku mwena kosu kitembu; kaasi simbululakenu bitembu mu zayila yuka ni byenina bya Nzambi, mukuma bambikudi ba bukamvi lawu bamwangani mu tsi.
1JO 4:2 Tala buna lwazayila yuka ni Kitembu kya Nzambi wuna: kitembu kyosu kina kyatámbwasa ni Yesu Kidisitu kisa mu kimutu kyakina kyenina kya Nzambi.
1JO 4:3 Kaasi wosu wuna wubwisini mu kutambwasa Yesu bwosu buna kenina, yandi keku wa Nzambi, kaasi kenina kitembu kya Mutendi wa Kidisitu: lwáyuka ni wuna wáfwana mu kukwisa amana buthwena wekina kedi muna tsi.
1JO 4:4 Kaasi benu, bana bama, Nzambi wuluvwini amana phi lwábanunga bambikudi ba bukamvi; mukuma Wuna wenina mwena benu kenina wa mbuta kuhita wuna wenina mwena babana bavwini kwena tsi.
1JO 4:5 Batu meni babana, tsi yibavwini. Yihakana ni nzonzidi ya bawu yenina ya mutindu wa batu ba tsi amana tsi yisi bayukila.
1JO 4:6 Kaasi betu, Nzambi wutuvwini. Mutu wuna wumuzayini Nzambi kisi tuyukila; wuna kondi kala wa Nzambi kisiku tuyukila. Bwabuna twalenda zayila Kitembu wa kyedika yi kitembu kina kyisi totisa.
1JO 4:7 Banduku bama batondama, tudizolenu betu yi betu, mukuma lungongu kwena Nzambi lwisi tuka. Wosu wuna wisi zola mukwenu, mwena Nzambi kábutukila amana phi wumuzayi Nzambi.
1JO 4:8 Wuna wisiku zola kábutukilaku mwena Nzambi, mukuma Nzambi kenina lungongu.
1JO 4:9 Tala Nzambi buna kásongila lungongu lwandi kikuma kya betu: Yandi wátuma Mwana wandi mosi muna tsi, mu twavwila luzingu lwa mwana Yandi.
1JO 4:10 Amana lungongu meni lwaluna lwenina bwabu: heku ni betu twámuzola Nzambi, kaasi yandi wátuzola; wátuma Mwana wandi wuna wádilambula hanga kimenga kikuma kya ndoluka ya masumu metu.
1JO 4:11 Banduku bama, yuka ni bwabuna kátuzodila Nzambi, tufweti dizola phi betu yi betu.
1JO 4:12 Heku mutu wámumona kedi Nzambi. Yuka ni twadizolaka betu yi betu, Nzambi kenina mwena betu, amana lungongu lwandi lwisi lungidila mwena betu.
1JO 4:13 Muna bwabuna, tuzayi ni mwena yandi thwisi nangina, hanga yandi mwena betu: yandi wátuheka Kitembu wandi.
1JO 4:14 Amana betu, twámona amana tubati ta kimbangi ni Tata kámuhitika Mwana wandi hanga Muhuludi wa tsi.
1JO 4:15 Wuna wisi tambwasa ni Yesu kenina Mwana wa Nzambi, Nzambi kisi nangina mwena yandi, bwosu yandi mwena Nzambi.
1JO 4:16 Amana betu, tuzayilwa lungongu luna kenina lwawu Nzambi kikuma kya betu, amana thwisi kwikila ni Nzambi kisi tuzola. Nzambi kenina lungongu; wuna wisi nangina mu lungongu, mwena Nzambi kisi nangina, amana Nzambi kisi nangina mwena yandi.
1JO 4:17 Yuka ni lungongu lwakala lwalungila mwena betu, hahana nana twakádila babasa yi kikumbwala muna kilumbu kya pfundusu; bwosu buna kenina Yandi, bwabuna thwenina betu phi mu tsi yayi.
1JO 4:18 Muna lungongu mwisiku kala yi bweya; lungongu lwa mukwandi lwisi katula bweya. Bweya bwádikasa yi kuhingila kwa ndola amana wuna wenina yi bweya keku walungila muna lungongu.
1JO 4:19 Kwena betu, thwisi zola, kikuma yandi wátekila tuzola mutu wa theti.
1JO 4:20 Yuka ni mutu kazonzaka: «Nzambi yisi muzola» amana kamengaka phangi wandi, kenina kingumba. Kikuma, yuka ni kisiku muzola phangi wandi yandi kisi mona, kalendaku muzola phi Nzambi wuna kisiku mona.
1JO 4:21 Amana tala mukuku kátuheka: wuna wisi zola Nzambi kafweti zola phi phangi wandi.
1JO 5:1 Wosu wuna wukwikidini ni Yesu kenina Kidisitu wuna wábutuka mwena Nzambi, amana wosu wuna wisi buta, kisi muzola phi wuna wubutukini mwena Nzambi.
1JO 5:2 Muna mambu meni mamana, tuzayi ni thwisi bazola bana ba Nzambi: tangwa thwisi muzola Nzambi amana thwisi sadila bwosu buna myenina mikuku myandi.
1JO 5:3 Mukuma lungongu lwa Nzambi, lwenina ni twalunda mikuku myandi. Amana mikuku myandi myeku phasi,
1JO 5:4 kikuma kyosu kina kyábutukila mwena Nzambi kyenina yi kinunga mu mambu matadidini tsi; amana kinunga kina kyánunga tsi, kyenina lukwikilu lwetu.
1JO 5:5 Nati wánunga tsi? Yuka ni ka wuna ku lwesi wisi kwikila ni Yesu kenina Mwana wa Nzambi.
1JO 5:6 Yandi, Yesu Kidisitu, wisila muna mamba yi menga; heku ni mu mamba lwesi, kaasi yi mamba yi menga; amana Kitembu wisi ta kimbangi, kikuma Kitembu kenina kyedika.
1JO 5:7 Mukuma bambangi batatu benina:
1JO 5:8 Kitembu, mamba yi menga, amana bawu boosu benina yi kimbangi kimosi.
1JO 5:9 Yuka ni twatambwasaka kimbangi kya batu, kimbangi kya Nzambi kihitini mu kutoka; mukuma kimbangi kya Nzambi kyenina ni kata kimbangi kikuma kya Mwana wandi.
1JO 5:10 Wuna wisi sya lukwikilu lwandi mwena Mwana wa Nzambi kenina yi kimbangi muna mbundu ya yandi meni; wuna wisiku kwikila, kingumba kisi mukitula Nzambi, kikuma kya buna kakondi kwikila mu kimbangi kina kata Nzambi kikuma kya Mwana wandi.
1JO 5:11 Kimbangi meni kina kyenina bwabu: Nzambi wátuheka luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula amana luzingu meni luna, lwenina mwena Mwana wandi.
1JO 5:12 Wuna wenina yi Mwana, luzingu kenina lwawu; kaasi wuna wukondi kala yi Mwana wa Nzambi wukondi luzingu.
1JO 5:13 Yilusonikinini mambu mana ndangu lwazaya ni luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula lwenina lwawu benu babana lwisi kwikila mu zina dya Mwana wa Nzambi.
1JO 5:14 Kikumbwala kina thwenina kyawu ku thwala ya yandi kyenina ni yuka twalomba kyosu kina mu luzolu lwa yandi, kisi tuyukila.
1JO 5:15 Amana yuka thwisi kumbwala ni kisi tuyukila, muna moosu mana twálomba kedi, tuzayi phi ni tutambudima kedi.
1JO 5:16 Yuka ni mutu wumoni ni phangi wandi, disumu kahodini dina dyisiku nata ku lufwa, bulungini kasambila amana Nzambi kahána luzingu kwena phangi meni wuna. Mambu mama matadidini batu babana bisi hola masumu mana misiku nata ku lufwa. Kaasi henina yi disumu dimosi dyisi nata ku lufwa, amana heku ni kikuma kya disumu dya mutindu wuna ndobidi mu kusambila.
1JO 5:17 Kukonda kwa masonga kwosu kwenina disumu amana henina yi disumu dimosi dina dyisiku nata ku lufwa.
1JO 5:18 Tuzayi ni wosu wuna wábutukila mwena Nzambi kisiku hola disumu; mukuma Mwana wa Nzambi kisi mutala amana kiphidi-mutu kamúhangaku kima.
1JO 5:19 Tuzayibwa ni bana ba Nzambi thwenina amana ni tsi ya muthu yenina mu luyalu lwa kiphidi-mutu.
1JO 5:20 Kaasi tuzayi phi ni Mwana wa Nzambi wisa amana wátuheka ngangu zina zisi tusadisa mu kuzayila Wuna wenina wa kyedika. Thwisi nangina ha kimosi kwena Wuna wenina wa kyedika mwena Mwana wandi Yesu Kidisitu. Yandi Nzambi wa kyedika, yandi luzingu lwa mvula yi mvula.
1JO 5:21 Bana bama, dikengenu ku nzambi za biteki!
2JO 1:1 Meni mbuta wa dibundu, kwena Ngudi wuna wásolama yi kwena bana bandi bana yisi zola muna kyedika kyosu. Ka meni ku lwesi yisi luzola, kaasi boosu phi babana bazayini kyedika,
2JO 1:2 kikuma, mwena betu kyedika kyisi nangina amana kyazíngila mwena betu mvula yi mvula.
2JO 1:3 Yambula Nzambi Tata yi Yesu Kidisitu, Mwana wa Tata, batuheka khenda, kyadi yi ngemba muna kyedika yi lungongu.
2JO 1:4 Yenina yi kyesi mu kumona bana baku babana bisi dyatila mu kyedika, bwosu buna wenina mukuku wuna twátambula kwena Tata.
2JO 1:5 Amana buthwena, Ngudi watondama, yikulombini bwabu: tudizolenu betu yi betu. Heku ni mukuku wa pha wawuna mbati kusonikina; wawuna twátambula tuka ku luyandiku.
2JO 1:6 Amana lungongu lulombini kuzingila bwosu myenina mikuku meni mina. Wawuna mukuku wuna wulufwani mu kudyatila, bwosu buna lwáyukilabwa tuka ku luyandiku.
2JO 1:7 Kikuma, bakwa bukamvi lawu bamwangani mu tsi; bisi bwisa mu kutambwasa ni Yesu Kidisitu wisa mu kimutu. Mwamuna bwisi lubukila bukamvi bwa bawu, Mutendi wa Kidisitu.
2JO 1:8 Dikengenu benu benu, ndangu lutotisaku kibundu kya kisalu kyetu, kaasi lwatambula lufutu lwenu buna bufwanini.
2JO 1:9 Wosu wuna wakonda nangina muna malongi ma Kidisitu, kaasi kabati hitikisa, keku mu kithwadi yi Nzambi. Wuna wisi nangina muna malongi mamana kenina mu kithwadi yi Tata yi Mwana.
2JO 1:10 Ho mutu kisa kwena benu amana kalunatiniku malongi mama, lumutambwasaku kuna nzu yenu amana bwisenu phi mu kumuheka mboti;
2JO 1:11 mukuma wuna wamúheka mboti kakítuka kima kimosi yi mihangu myandi mya mbi.
2JO 1:12 Mbatanana yenina yi mambu ma lawu ma kulusonikina, nzodikiku ni yihangilabwa ku kisyati yi kazasa. Yenina yi kivuvu kya kukwisa kwakuna mu kimwesa mutu, ndangu kyesi kyetu kyakala kyalungila.
2JO 1:13 Bana ba phangi waku wa Mukhetu, wuna phi wásolama, mboti bakuhekini.
3JO 1:1 Meni, Mbuta wa dibundu, kwena muzitu Kayusi wuna yisi zola yi kyedika kyosu.
3JO 1:2 Muzitu, kilomba kyama kyenina ni moosu makala kitoku kikuma kya ngeyi amana wakala phi yi lutu lwa kitoku bwosu bwenina muna moya waku.
3JO 1:3 Kikuma baphangi batudiki amana batiki kimbangi kitadidini kyedika kina kyenina mwena ngeyi yi mutindu wuna wisi dyatila ngeyi mu kyedika. Kyesi kya lawu ngyukikini.
3JO 1:4 Heku kima kifwani kyapheka kyesi kya lawu, ho ka kuyuka ku ni bana bama babati dyatila buna dyenina kyedika.
3JO 1:5 Muzitu watondama, muna moosu mana wisi hanga kikuma kya baphangi keti kikuma kya banzenza, bwabuna bwisi songila lukwikilu lwaku.
3JO 1:6 Bakutidini kimbangi kya lungongu lwaku ku thwala ya Dibundu. Yihakana ni basadisa mu kulanda kitambu kya bawu buna bufwani muna mutindu wa Nzambi.
3JO 1:7 Kikuma, babwi mu nzila kikuma kya kisalu kya zina dya Kidisitu, konda kutambwasa kima ku moku ma batu ba hika.
3JO 1:8 Disongidila ni tufweti basadisa batu ba mutindu wuna, ndangu twasala ha kimosi mu kumwangisa kwa kyedika.
3JO 1:9 Kisyati kya khufi yisonikini kwena Dibundu; kaasi Thyotefi, yandi wisi zola mu kutwadisaka byosu, kisiku simbidila keti dyambu dimosi muna mamana yisi zimbula.
3JO 1:10 Yi hakana, tangwa yikwísa, yítungulula mbi yina babati hanga, yandi wuna wubati huna mambu yi kuzonzaka mambu ma mbi kikuma kya betu. Kaasi ka moosu ku: kisiku zola ni kayambaka baphangi, yi bana bazodi mu kubatambula, yandi kabati bakakidila mu kubanwanisaka yi kubalubulaka mu Dibundu.
3JO 1:11 Muzitu wama, sokululaku mambu ma mbi kaasi mana menina ma bukheti. Wuna wisi hanga mambu ma mboti kenina wa Nzambi; wuna wisi hanga mambu ma mbi kamuzayiku Nzambi.
3JO 1:12 Boosu babati ta kimbangi kya Temetidiyosi. Kyawu-meni kyedika kibati ta kimbangi kikuma kya yandi. Betu phi, kimbangi kya bukheti tubati ta kikuma kya yandi amana wuzayibwa ni kimbangi kyetu kyenina kya kyedika.
3JO 1:13 Yilenda kala yi mambu ma lawu mana pfwani yikusonikina kaasi yilendamoku sonika ku kisyati yi kazasa.
3JO 1:14 Tsini kivuvu ni ka thama ku yikṵ́mona amana twaménasana ha munwa munwa.
3JO 1:15 Yambula ngemba yakala ha kimosi yi ngeyi. Banduku baku mboti bakuhekini. Hana mboti kwena banduku, kosu mutu muna zina dyandi.
